40001001	A Zezi Krista, a Daviid biiga, a Abraam biiga roog sebre.
40001002	A Abraam n doga Izaak. A Izaak n doga Zakoob, a Zakoob n doga Zɩɩda ne a yaopa,
40001003	a Zɩɩda n dog a Fares ne a Zara, tɩ b ma yaa Tamar, a Fares n dog a Esrom, a Esrom n dog a Aram,
40001004	a Aram n doga Aminadab, a Aminadab n dog a Naason, a Naason n dog a Salmon,
40001005	a Salmon n dog a Booz, a ma la a Raab, a Booz n dog a Zobɛɛd, a ma la a Rut, a Zobɛɛd n dog a Zese,
40001006	a Zese n dog dĩm a Daviid. A Daviid n dog a Salomo, a ma a Uri paga,
40001007	a Salomo n dog a Roboam, a Roboam n dog a Abia, a Abia n dog a Asa,
40001008	a Asa n dog a Zozafat, a Zozafat n dog a Zoram, a Zoram n dog a Oziyas,
40001009	a Oziyas n dog a Zoatam, a Zoatam n dog a Akaz, a Akaz n dog a Ezekiyas,
40001010	A Ezekiyas n dog a Manase, a Manase n dog a Amon, a Amon n dog a Zoziyas,
40001011	a Zoziyas n dog a Zekoniyas ne a yaopa. Bãmb wakatẽ la b vʋk Israyɛl kamb n kẽng Babilon.
40001012	Babilon yembd poore, a Zekoniyas n dog a Salatiyɛl, a Salatiyɛl n dog a Zorobabɛl,
40001013	a Zorobabel n dog a Abiud, a Abiud n dog a Eliakim, a Eliakim n dog a Azor,
40001014	a Azor n dog a Sadok, a Sadok n dog a Akim, a Akim n dog a Eliyud,
40001015	a Eliud n doga Eleazar, a Eleazar n dog a Matan, a Matan n dog a Zakoob,
40001016	a Zakoob n dog a Zozɛf, a Maryam sɩda la a Maryam n dog a Zezi, sẽn boond tɩ Krista.
40001017	Dẽnna yaab rãmba ne b rot sõta woto: a Abraam n taa Daviid, yaa rot piig la a naase. A Daviid n ta Babilon yembdo, yaa rot piig la a naase. Babilon yembdo n ta Krista yaa rot piig la a naase.
40001018	A Zezi Krista dogma kibar la woto: a ma, a Maryam, da ya a Zozɛf pʋg-bila. La a Maryam sẽn waa n nan ka kul a Zozɛf, a mikame, tɩ ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng raabo, a lebga zɩsgo.
40001019	A sɩda, a Zozɛf, sẽn da ya nin-tɩrgã, pa tʋlg n gom tɩ yi yɩng ye a tʋlgame bal n soos n bas a Maryam.
40001020	La rẽ sẽn waa n be a yamẽ, la a sẽn yãe Soaala malɛk a zãmsdẽ, sẽn yeel-a: «Zozɛf, Daviid biiga, da zoe rabeem n deeg f pʋg-bila, a Maryam, f zakẽ ye, tɩ biig ning sẽn sig a pʋgẽ wã yita a Vʋʋsem Sõng nengẽ.
40001021	Bi-ribl la a na n doge la f na n pʋda a yʋʋr a Zezi: tɩ yaa yẽ n na n sɩd yiis a buuda neba yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ.»
40001022	La yella yɩɩ woto, n taas Soaala sẽn da togs ne bãngdba noore:
40001023	Pa-kul na n dɩka pʋga n dog biiga, la b na n pʋda a biigã tɩ Emmanwɛl, dat n yeelame tɩ Wẽnd bee d sʋka.
40001024	A Zozɛf sẽn neke, a maana wala malɛka sẽn wilgi, a peega a paga, a zakẽ,
40001025	la a tol n doga a biigã tɩ b pa bãng taab ye; la a Zozɛf pʋda biiga yʋʋr a Zezi.
40002001	A Zezi doga Bɛtelyɛɛm, Zɩɩde tẽnga, dĩm a Erod naamẽ, la ade, neb sẽn bʋgd ãds yii yaanga n wa Zerizalɛɛm
40002002	n sok woto: «Zʋɩf rãmb dĩma sẽn dog paalma bee yɛ? Tõnd yãenda b ãdg sẽn puki tɩ d wa n na n waoog-ba.»
40002003	B sẽn wʋm dẽ, dĩm a Erod ne Zerizalɛɛm tõre yɛɛsame.
40002004	Dĩma tigma maan-kʋʋdba kãsem dãmba ne sẽn karem-ba n sikã la a sok-b lame n bãng Wẽnd Nedã sẽn na n dog zĩig ninga.
40002005	«Yaa Bɛtelyɛɛm, Zɩɩde tẽnga, tɩ bãngda gʋlsame:
40002006	Zɩɩda tẽn-peelmẽ Bɛtelyɛɛm, ka foo la tẽn-bil Zɩɩda ye, tɩ dĩm ning sẽn na n gũ m buuda Israyɛl, na n yila f pʋgẽ.»
40002007	A Erod soos n boola ãdsa bagbã n na n bãng wakat bʋg taki la ãdga puk-ba,
40002008	la a tees-b la Bɛtelyɛɛm sore n yetẽ: «Kẽng-y n tɩ sok-y biiga yelle, la y sã n bãng vẽenega, bɩ y lɛɛg n wa togs-ma tɩ m me kẽng n tɩ waoog-a.»
40002009	Ãdsa bagba sẽn paam dĩma koɛɛga, b rɩka sore; b le yãee ãdgã t'a kẽnd b taoore la a waa n tɩ yalsa sus biiga sẽn da be zĩig ningã.
40002010	B sẽn yãe ãdgã b sũur yɩɩ noog wʋsgo.
40002011	B kẽe roogã n yãend biiga ne b ma, a Maryam, la b wõgemdame n waoog-ba; b pagsa b kogendo n yiis b kũuni n kõ-ba: sãnem, tɩdare, ne tɩ-kaam sẽn tar yũ-noogo.
40002012	Dẽ poore b bãnga b zãmsdẽ tɩ b ka tõe n leb n tũ a Erod nengẽ ye, la b bao sor a to n leb b tẽngẽ.
40002013	Bãmb loogr poore, Soaala malɛk lika a Zozɛf a gũeemẽ n yeel-a: «Yik n dɩk biiga ne a ma n zoe n kẽng Ezipt tẽnga la f pa be n ta wakat ning m sẽn na n wilg fu; a Erod na n baoo biigã n kʋ.»
40002014	A Zozɛf yika ne yʋngo n dɩk biiga ne a ma n zoe n kẽng Ezipt tẽnga,
40002015	la a paa be n tãag a Erod kaalem. Woto la Soaala koɛɛg tõog n taase: M boola m biiga Ezipt tẽnga.
40002016	A Erod sẽn mik tɩ bagba belg-a lame, a sũur puuga al wʋsgo, dẽ la a tʋm tɩ b kẽng Bɛtelyɛɛm la Bɛtelyɛɛm weoogo n kʋ kamb niyns fãa yʋʋm sẽn pa yɩɩd a yiibu, wala neba sẽn da mak n wilgã.
40002017	La woto yɩɩ bãngd a Zeremi koɛɛg taasgo:
40002018	Kɛleng n kelem Rama yãbr la waasgo n waas be: ya a Rasɛl n yãbd a kamba la a tõt belegre tɩ b le ka ket ye.
40002019	La a Erod kũum poore, Soaala malɛk lika a Zozɛf a gõeemẽ, Ezipt tẽnga,
40002020	n yeel-a: «Yik n dɩk biiga ne a ma n leb Israyɛl tẽnga tɩ sẽn da baood-b biigã n na n kʋ wã fãa kiime.»
40002021	A Zozɛf yikame n dɩk biiga ne a ma n leb Israyɛl tẽnga.
40002022	A sẽn wʋm t'a Arkelawus n dɩt naam Zɩɩda tẽn-peelmẽ, a ba, a Erod, zĩigẽ, a Zozɛf zoe rabeem ne be lebre, la a sẽn paam koɛɛg a zãmsdẽ, a zãagame n tees Galile baobgo,
40002023	a waa n kẽe tẽng a ye sẽn boond tɩ Nazarɛt. Woto me la bãngda koɛɛg tõog n taase: B na n bool-a lame tɩ Nazarɛt daoa.
40003001	Rao n da kõt soobo, a yʋʋr a Zã; a waa n bee Zɩɩda weoogẽ n karemd neba
40003002	n yetẽ: «Tuub-y y yel-wẽna tɩ Wẽnd Rĩung kolgame.»
40003003	Ad-y yaa yẽ yell la bãngd a Izai da gomda: Sẽn moond-a weoogẽ wã koɛɛg la woto: segl-y Soaala sor, kɩt-y tɩ b so-bugsa lebg tɩrse.
40003004	A Zã ra yera fuug sẽn wʋg ne yʋgem kõbdo la a ra sẽga gãndo. A rɩɩb da yaa sʋya la weoog sɩɩdo.
40003005	Zerizalɛɛm ne Zɩɩda la Zʋrdẽ baobga rãmb fãa gill da kẽnda a nengẽ.
40003006	B ra togsda b yel-wẽna n deegd soobo, Zʋrdẽ koomẽ.
40003007	A Zã sẽn yãend Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba tɩ b wat wʋsgo n na n deeg soobo, a yeel-b lame: «Wag-bi buudu, ãnda n wilg yãmb tɩ y zoe n põs Wẽnd beem sẽn wat y zutu?
40003008	Bɩ y tʋm tʋʋm sõma n wilg tɩ y teema zʋgo,
40003009	la y ra saag n yeel y sũurẽ: ‹Tõnd yaa a Abraam kamb ye.› M yet-y lame tɩ kuga sẽn dɩgã, Wẽnd tõe n yiisa a Abraam kamb b pʋsẽ.
40003010	Lar zoe n dɩga tɩɩga sɛɛga; tɩɩg ninga fãa sẽn pa womda bi-sõma, b na n kɛɛg-a lame n yõog bugum.
40003011	Mam yẽ kõt-y la soob koomẽ y zʋg tekr yĩnga la mam sẽn deng a soab taoorã yɩɩda maam; paam n lodg a neodr gĩs menga looga maam; yẽ na n soo yãmb ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng la bugum.
40003012	A zãada kaorg a nugẽ n na n yelg a kood zɛɛgẽ; ka-bɛɛla na n suii baoorẽ, la fɩɩba na n yõoga bugum ning sẽn ka kiida pʋgẽ.»
40003013	A Zezi yii Galile n wa Zʋrdẽ kʋɩlga, a Zã nengẽ, n na n deeg soobo.
40003014	A Zã ra pa rat n sak ye, n yetẽ: «Yaa maam n tog n deeg soob yãmb nengẽ, tɩ yãmb baas n wat mam nengẽ!»
40003015	A Zezi leok-a lame: «Bas tɩ m maan woto nanda tɩ yaa woto la d tog maan tɩ fãa zemse.» T'a Zã yaool n na n sak.
40003016	A Zezi sẽn deeg soob n yit koomẽ, la saaga pilg a gãongo, la b yãee a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn sigd a Zezi zugu wa walle,
40003017	la koɛɛg me n sãd yĩngri: «Ada yaa mam bi-nongre, mam yam kẽe-a la zãnga!»
40004001	A Vʋʋsem Sõng talla a Zezi n kẽ we-raoogẽ tɩ Sʋtãan kʋɩɩb-ba.
40004002	B maana rasem pisnaase la yʋnd pisnaase n ka rɩ, n ka yũ ye.
40004003	Dẽ la kʋɩɩbda kolg n yeele: «Fo sã n ya Wẽnd Biiga bɩ f kɩt tɩ kug kãensa lebg buri.»
40004004	A Zezi leok-a lame: «B gʋlsame: Ninsaal ka rɩlgd a meng ne bur bal ye, yaa ne koɛɛg ning fãa sẽn yit Wẽnnaam noorẽ.»
40004005	La Sʋtãan tall-b lame n kẽ Zerizalɛɛm n dʋʋs-b wẽnd dooga zugu,
40004006	n yeel-ba: «Fo sã n ya Wẽnd Biiga bɩ f yɩk n tiimd tẽnga, tɩ b gʋlsame: B na n kõ-la b malɛgsa noore tɩ b põk foom b nugẽ tɩ f naoor da sɩɩs kugr ye.»
40004007	A Zezi leok-a Sʋtaana: «B le gʋlsame: Da kʋɩɩb Wẽnnaam, f Soaala ye.»
40004008	Sʋtãan tall-b lame n dʋ tãn wok zugu n wilg-b dũni wã ne a zɩɩri,
40004009	n yeel-ba: «M na n kõ-f la woto fãa, f sã n wõgemd m taoore n waoog maam.»
40004010	Dẽ la a Zezi yeel-a: «Looge, Sʋtãana! Tɩ b gʋlsame: Wẽnnaam, f Soaala, bal taoore la f na n wõgemd Bãmb bal la f na n waooge.»
40004011	Sʋtãan bas-b lame n looge tɩ malɛgsa kolg n na n ges b yelle.
40004012	A Zezi sẽn wʋm tɩ b yõka a Zã, b leba Galile.
40004013	B yii Nazarɛt tẽnga n wa kẽed Kafarnaom, Tiberiyad mogr noore, Zabulõ la Neftali satmẽ.
40004014	Woto la bãngda Izayi toagsga taasyã:
40004015	Zabulõ tẽnga, Neftali tẽnga, mogr sorẽ dãmba, Zʋrdẽ rʋʋnd dãmba, Galile bu-zẽmb rãmba!
40004016	Baad-y likẽ dãmba yãee vẽenem kãsenga, vẽenem n bui lik la kũum sẽn da reeg tẽns niyns n yãmbã.
40004017	A Zezi sɩnga marsã n karemd neba n yetẽ: «Teem-y zʋgo tɩ Arzãn Rĩung kolgame.»
40004018	A Zezi waa n looda Galile mogra noore, n yãe ned ne a yao: a Simo, b sẽn boond a soab t'a Piyɛr, ne a Andre, a ba-biiga; b ra lobda b zulumsi tɩ b da yaa zĩm yõgdba.
40004019	B yeel-b lame: «Pʋg-y maam tɩ m na sõng-y tɩ y paam ninsaalba.»
40004020	La bãmb wẽneg n basa b zulumsa be n pʋg a Zezi.
40004021	B sẽn ta taoore, b le yãee ned a to ne a yao, a Zak la a Zã, a Zebede kamba, tɩ b be koglg pʋgẽ ne b ba, n manegd b zulumsi;
40004022	b bool-b lame. Bãmb me basa b ba la b zulumsi n pʋg a Zezi.
40004023	A Zezi ra saada Galile tẽnse n maand karengo pʋʋsg rotẽ, n wilgd Wẽnd Rĩung Kibar noogã, la b sãoogd bãas la pa-keem buud fãa.
40004024	B yʋʋr yiime n ta Siri zamaana; tẽng fãa ra wata ne b nimbãan dãmba la b bãad dãmb buud toɛ toɛyã, wala sẽn yikd-b kisenkiiri, zut sẽn lebg rãmba, nao sẽn ki rãmba. B ra wata ne-ba t'a Zezi sãoog ba.
40004025	Sɩd yɩɩ zãma kãseng n sɩng b pʋgbo; neb sẽn yit Galile la Tẽns piig sẽn tot taaba, n yit Zerizalɛɛm la Zɩɩda la Zʋrdẽ rʋʋnde.
40005001	A Zezi sẽn yãe zãma wã, b rʋʋ tãnga zugu. B zĩndame tɩ b karen-biisa na n kolg-ba.
40005002	A Zezi kõ-b la koɛɛga n yetẽ:
40005003	«Sũ-noog rãmba la sẽn teeg-b Wẽnd bala tɩ Wẽnnaam Rĩunga yaa bãmb soolem.
40005004	Sũ-noog rãmba la nin-bʋgse tɩ tẽnga na n yɩɩ bãmb soolem.
40005005	Sũ-noog rãmba la sũ-beed sẽn tar b rãmba, tɩ b na n paama belgda.
40005006	Sũ-noog rãmb la sẽn yãbd-b sõmblem kom la ko-yũudu, tɩ b na n tɩgame.
40005007	Sũ-noog rãmb la sẽn zoet-b b taab nimbãanega, tɩ b na n zoee bãmb me nimbãanega.
40005008	Sũ-noog rãmb la pʋ-peelem dãmba tɩ b na n yãee Wẽnnaam.
40005009	Sũ-noog rãmb la sẽn mi-b sugri, tɩ b na n boola bãmb tɩ Wẽnd kamba.
40005010	Sũ-noog rãmba la sẽn sakd-b namsgo b tʋʋm sõma yĩnga, tɩ Wẽnd Rĩunga yaa bãmb soolem.
40005011	Yãmb la sũ-noog rãmba b sã n wa tʋʋsd-y la b namsd-y la b rõt-y rõadg buud fãa mam tũudma yĩnga.
40005012	Noog-y y sũuri la y kɩdem tɩ y pʋɩɩr na n yɩɩ kãseng arzãna. Ad-y yɩɩ boto la bãngdba nams pĩnda.
40005013	Yãmb yaa mooga yamsem. Yamsem sã n sãbge, bõe n tõe n le wa ne a noosem? A ka le be yõod ye la a sẽn tog yaa b lob-a yɩnga tɩ neb tabe.
40005014	Yãmb yaa dũni vẽenem; tẽng sẽn zao tãng zug ka tõe n solg a meng ye.
40005015	Fitil ka widigdi n dɩk koglg n lill-a ye, b ningd-a la zĩig ninga a sẽn na n tõog n kõ zaka rãmb vẽenem.
40005016	Woto me yãmb vẽenema tog n yãga y taab nini tɩ b yãe y tʋʋm sõma n tõog n pẽg y Ba sẽn be arzãna.
40005017	Da ning-y y yamẽ tɩ m waame n na n sɛɛs Noora ne bãngdbã sẽn wilga ye; m waame n na n maneg n baase.
40005018	Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ gomde, gomd pɛdg meng kõn zĩnd Wẽnnaam noora pʋgẽ n pa taase tɩ saaga la tẽnga ket n be b zĩigẽ ye.
40005019	Dɩlla ned ning fãa sẽn na n tõdg-a, ba noor sẽn ya bilfu, Wẽnnaam noya sʋka la a wilg a taab tɩ b tõdg wa yẽnda, b na ges yẽ soab me wa nin-bila, Wẽnd Rĩunga pʋgẽ. Ned ninga sẽn na n deeg-ba la a zãms a taab tɩ b maan wa yẽ, b na ges yẽ soab wa nin-kãsenga Wẽnnaam Rĩunga pʋgẽ.
40005020	M yet-y lame, tɩ y sõmblem sã n pa yɩɩd sẽn karen-ba-n-sikã la Farizẽ rãmba rẽnna, y kõn kẽ Arzãn ye.
40005021	Y wʋmame tɩ b yeela pĩnd dãmba: da kʋ ned ye, la sẽn kʋ-a a to bɩ b kẽes-a bʋʋdo; la mam yet-y lame tɩ ned ning fãa sẽn na n puuga sũuri ne a to, dẽ seka bʋʋd kẽesgo.
40005022	La ned sã n yeel a to tɩ yalma, dẽ sekda a wa bʋʋd-bɛda rãmb taoore. La a sã n yeel-a tɩ pʋlum-sãamda, yẽ soab paalgda a meng bugum bʋʋdo.
40005023	Dɩlla fo sã n wa ne f kũuni maanda zĩigẽ, n tẽeg tɩ bũmb n be foo ne f to sʋka,
40005024	bɩ f bas f kũuna maanda zĩigẽ la f lɛɛg tɩ y tɩ zems taaba tɩ f na yaool n wa kõ f kũuna.
40005025	Fo sã n seg f zabd-n-taaga, bɩ f ning pãng tɩ y zems taaba sora zugu, sã n ka rẽ a wat n bool-f la bʋʋdo tɩ bʋʋda soab paalg-f ne gũudã, tɩ gũuda yõk fo n pag roogo.
40005026	Sɩd-sɩda, mam yet-f lame tɩ f kõn tõog n yi roogã, samd pɛdg meng sã n ket f zug ye.
40005027	Yãmb wʋmame tɩ b yeelame: Da ro f to pag ye.
40005028	La mam yet-y lame: Ned ninga sẽn gesa a to pag ne raabo, a soab zoe n yoo ne-a a sũurẽ.
40005029	F rɩtg nif sã n kʋɩɩbd-fo, bɩ f kɩdg-a n lob yɩɩga; fo yĩnga wilg a ye bõne, são yĩnga tõr sẽn na n lob bugmẽ.
40005030	F nug rɩtg sã n kʋɩɩbd-fo, bɩ f kʋʋg-a n lob yɩɩga; fo yĩnga wilg a ye bõne, são yĩnga tõr sẽn na n lʋɩ bugmẽ.
40005031	B yeelame yɛsa: Ned ninga sẽn yiisa pag tog n kõ-a-la a rigb sebre.
40005032	Mam yet-y lame tɩ sã n ka pagã n bao ned a to, ned ninga sẽn yiis-a wã wilgd-a-la yoob sore. Ned ninga me sẽn na n dɩk pʋg kãnga, yaa yoob la a maanda.
40005033	Yãmb le wʋma b sẽn yeel pĩnd dãmbã: Da sãam f pʋlong ye, la pids kãabg ning fãa f sẽn kãab Soaalã.
40005034	Mam yet-y lame: da wẽen ba bilfu, da wẽen ne yĩngr tɩ yaa Wẽnd zaoore.
40005035	Da wẽen ne tẽnga tɩ yaa Wẽnd nao palgr zĩiga. Da wẽen ne Zerizalɛɛm tɩ yaa Na-kãseng tẽnga.
40005036	Da wẽen ne f zugu tɩ f ka tõe tɩ f zoobg a ye pelg bɩ sob ye.
40005037	Y sã n tog n leok tɩ N-yẽe! Bɩ y leok tɩ N-yẽe! Sã n tog n leok tɩ Ayoo! Bɩ yɩ Ayoo! Sẽn zʋʋg rẽ yita yam-beeda soab nengẽ.
40005038	Yãmb wʋmame tɩ b yeelame: Nif n dond nifu, yẽnd n dond yẽnde.
40005039	Mam yet-y lame tɩ y ra rok y sũur ne y bɛ ye. Ned sã n wẽ f rɩtg yɛgdg pɛka bɩ f wẽneg f goabgã n tees-a;
40005040	a sã n dat n kẽes-f bʋʋdo n deeg f fu woko, bɩ f paas-a f fu taoko.
40005041	Ned sã n modg-f tɩ f yãag-a naoyakem tusr bala, bɩ f yãag-a naoyakem tus a yiibu.
40005042	Ned sã n kos foo bɩ f kõ-a; a sã n dat n peng bɩ f ra zãgs ye.
40005043	Yãmb wʋmame tɩ b yeela pĩnda: Nong f zoa la f kisg f bɛyã.
40005044	Mam yet-y lame: nong-y y bɛɛba la pʋʋs-y sẽn namsd-b yãmba yĩnga.
40005045	Woto yãmb na n yɩɩ Ba ning sẽn be-a arzãna kamba, tɩ b basda b wĩndg t'a pukd nin-sõma la nin-wẽnse, la b basda b saaga t'a niid nin-sõma la nin-wẽns yĩnga.
40005046	Yãmb sã n nong sẽn nong-b yãmb bala, bõe rolb la y na n le gũ yɛsa? Sẽn deesd-b fadga ka maan dẽ sɩda?
40005047	Yãmb sã n pʋʋsd y saam-biisa bala, bõe la toogo, bu-zẽmba ka maand boto sɩda?
40005048	Yãmb me modg n yɩ sõma wa y yĩngr Ba wã sẽn ya sõmb zãngã.
40006001	Gũus-y n da maan y tʋʋm sõma neb a taaba taoore nagr yĩng bal ye. Ka rẽ y kõn paam dolbo y Ba sẽn be arzãna nengẽ ye.
40006002	Fo sã n na n yols ned nimbãanega bɩ f ra yi n moon yɩnga wa ninsaan-kazukem kẽere sẽn maand pʋʋsg rotẽ la sotiisẽ n baood neb pẽgr ye, tɩ m togsd-y la vẽenega, bãmb dãmb zoe n paama b rolbo.
40006003	Fo sã n dat n yols ned nimbãanega bɩ f ra sak tɩ f goabg bãng f rɩtg sẽn maand bũmb ning ye.
40006004	Woto ned kõn bãng fo sẽn maan-a ye la f Ba Sõng sẽn ne likẽ wã na rol-fo.
40006005	Y sã pʋʋsdẽ bɩ y ra maan wa zãmb rãmba sẽn maanda ye; bãmb sã n na n pʋʋse, b baooda zĩig ning neb wʋsg sẽn tõe n yãend-ba, pʋʋsg roto la sobadse. M yet-y lame tɩ b zoe n paama b rolbo.
40006006	Fo sã n pʋʋsdẽ bɩ f kẽ f roogẽ n lɛɛg n pag f kʋɩlenga la f pʋʋs f Ba, lillẽ, tɩ f Ba sẽn ne likẽ wã na rol-fo.
40006007	Y pʋʋsg pʋgẽ bɩ y ra baam wala bu-zẽmba ye; b tẽedame tɩ b sã n gomd n pa yɛɛdẽ la Wẽnd kelgd b pʋʋsgo.
40006008	Da maan-y wa bãmb bada, tɩ y Ba zoe n mii y sẽn tar bũmb ning tʋʋmde tɩ y nan ka yaag y noor ye.
40006009	Dẽ yĩngã pʋʋs-y woto: ‹Tõnd Ba sẽn be arzãnẽ, y yʋʋr paam pẽgre,
40006010	tɩ y Rĩung yalse, tɩ b maan y yam tẽng zug, wẽnd b sẽn maand arzãna.
40006011	Kõ-y tõnd dũnna d beoog-beoog fãa rɩɩbo.
40006012	Kõ-y tõnd d yel-wẽna sugri wẽnd d sẽn kõt d taab sugri,
40006013	la y ra bas tɩ d lʋɩ kʋɩɩbg pʋgẽ ye la y fãgd-d wẽnem soaba nugẽ.›
40006014	N-ye! Yãmb sã n kõ y taab sugri, y Ba sẽn be arzãna me na kõ yãmb sugri.
40006015	La yãmb sã n pa kõ y taab sugri, y Ba wã me kõn bas-y taal ye.
40006016	Y sã n loet y noor bɩ y ra gãnem y neng wa zãmb rãmba sẽn maanda ye; b takda b nenga tɩ neba tõog n yãe tɩ b sɩd maanda no-loeere. M yet-y lame tɩ b zoe n paama b rolbo.
40006017	Fo sã n loet f noore bɩ f zɛ f zug kaam la f pek f nenga,
40006018	woto ned kõn bãng tɩ f loee noore sã n ka f Ba wã bal sẽn yɛs lillẽ wã, la bãmb sẽn ne likẽ wã na rol-fo.
40006019	Tẽng zug ka, bɩ y ra tigs arzɛk ye tɩ bugd la zũnzũur dɩtame, tɩ wagdb pood roto n zuuda.
40006020	Tigs-y y arzɛka arzãnẽ, tɩ be, bugd la zũnzũur ka n dɩtẽ ye la wagdb me ka pood n zuud ye.
40006021	F arzɛk sẽn be zĩig ninga, be me la f sũura na n zĩndi.
40006022	Nif la yĩnga fitila. Fo nif sã n ya sõmbo, fo yĩnga fãa bee vẽenemẽ.
40006023	La f nif sã n sãame, f yĩnga zãng bee likẽ. Fo vẽenem sã n lebg lika, fo lik yɩta a wãna?
40006024	Ned ka tõe n maan zu-soaben-dãmb a yiib raab ye, f na kisga a ye, n nong a ye, f na n basa a ye n tũ a ye. Yãmb me ka tõe n pʋg Wẽnnaam la y pʋg Ligd ye.
40006025	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet-y: da bʋ-y y vɩɩma poorẽ, n sokd-y y sẽn na n dɩ bũmb ning ye; la y ra bʋ y yĩnga poorẽ n sokd-y y sẽn na n yeelg fuug ning ye. Vɩɩma ka yɩɩd dɩɩbo la yĩnga ka são fuugu?
40006026	Ges-y luiili sẽn yɩgd yĩngri: b ka bʋte, b ka kẽebde, b ka suiid baoorẽ ye, la y Ba sẽn be arzãna dɩlgd-b lame. Yãmb pa yɩɩd bãmb sɩda?
40006027	Yãmb sʋka ãnda n tõe n zĩnd n bʋ n paas a vɩɩma woglem kãntɩɩg a ye?
40006028	La fut poorẽ, bõe yĩng la y na n bʋ? Ges-y pʋt puudu: ges-y b sẽn yit toto, b pa namsde, b ka wĩid lamdo.
40006029	La m yet-y lame t'a Salomo ne a zɩɩra sẽn yɩ a soaba, ka tõog n paam fu neer wa bãmb dẽnda buud n yeelg ye.
40006030	Wẽnd sã n yeelgd pʋt mood woto, bũmb sẽn be rũnna n na n yɩ bugum dɩɩb beoogo, b kõn maan tɩ yɩɩg boto yãmb yĩnga, tẽeb kɩdg rãmba?
40006031	Da bʋ-y n yetẽ: d na n dɩɩ bõe la d na n yũu bõe la d na n yeelga bõe ye,
40006032	tɩ bu-zẽmbã n zĩi n bʋʋd boto. Yãmb Ba sẽn be yĩngrã miime tɩ y tara rẽ fãa tʋʋmde.
40006033	Deng-y n bao-y arzãn Rĩungã ne a sõmblem tɩ sẽn keta fãa b na kõ-y rẽ wa lɛnga.
40006034	Da sũk-y beoog poorẽ tɩ beoog na baoo a rẽnna. Daar fãa ne a zɩɩbo, sekd-a lame.
40007001	Da kao-y y taab bʋʋdo tɩ b kõn kao y me bʋʋd ye.
40007002	Y sẽn kaood y taab bʋʋda toto, boto me la b na n kao yãmb bʋʋdo. Makr ning y sẽn makd n kõt y taaba, makr kãng me n yɩt yãmb dẽnna.
40007003	Bõe tɩ f get mooga sẽn be f to nifẽ? Fo yaool n ka ne ra-giiga sẽn be f nifẽ ye.
40007004	Fo na n yɩɩ wãna n yeel f to: ‹Yaas tɩ m yiis moogo f nifẽ,› tɩ ra-giig yaool n be f rẽnnẽ?
40007005	Zãmb soaba, deng n yiis ra-giiga f nifẽ tɩ f na tõog marsã n yãe moogã n yãk f to nifẽ.
40007006	Da rɩk-y maand nemd n kõ baag ye, da rɩk-y kĩndfu n lob kurkuy taoor ye: b wat n tab-a lame n yaool n lɛɛg n kẽ yãmba, n na n wãb yãmb.
40007007	Kos-y tɩ b na kõ-y, bao-y tɩ y na yãe. Kabs-y tɩ b na pak tɩ y kẽ.
40007008	Sẽn kota n paamde, sẽn baooda n yãete, sẽn kabsda la b pakda.
40007009	Yãmb sʋka ãnd n be t'a biig sã n kos-a buri bɩ a kõ-a kugri?
40007010	Ka rɩll bɩ a kos-a kʋɩl-zẽoogo t'a kõ-a waafo?
40007011	Dɩlla yãmb ne y wẽnema, y sã n mii y kamb bõn-sõma kũuni, bãng-y tɩ Ba Sõng na maan neere n yɩɩd ne neb niyns sẽn bõsd-b bãmba.
40007012	Yãmb sẽn dat tɩ y taab maan bũmb ninga y yĩnga, bɩ y maan boto ne y taaba: dẽ n be Noora sebrẽ la bãngdba me rẽnnẽ.
40007013	Tũ-y so sẽka n kẽ. Menesg sor tuka yalenga, tɩ wʋsg rɩkd-a.
40007014	Vɩɩma sor tuka sẽka la a tãagda kʋɩleng sẽn pa yalem t'a yãetb sõor ya bilfri bala.
40007015	Gũus-y ne zirẽ-be-bãngdba. B sã n be yãmb sʋka, bãng-y piis sẽn ka tar b toorẽ yell ye, mik yaa digd-n-yĩid-toose.
40007016	B tʋʋma n na n wilg yãmba b sẽn ya bũmb ninga. Sib na wob gõaag zugu? La kankam na tõs kãgrẽ?
40007017	Ade, tɩ-sõng faa womda bi-sõma la tɩ-wẽng fãa womda bi-wẽnse.
40007018	Tɩ-sõng pa tõe n wom bi-wẽns ye la tɩ-wẽng me ka tõe n wom bi-sõng ye.
40007019	Tɩɩg ninga fãa sẽn ka womda bi-sõma, b kɛɛgd-a lame n yõog bugum.
40007020	Dɩlla b tʋʋmẽ wã la y na n bãng-b n bake.
40007021	Ka sẽn boond-a maam: ‹Soaala, Soaala,› n kẽed arzãn ye, yaa sẽn maand-a m Ba sẽn be arzãna yamleoogo.
40007022	Wʋsg wat n yeela maam daar a ye: ‹Soaala, Soaala, tũu ne yãmb maasem tɩ d paam n wilg sẽn na n yaool n wa, la d dig sʋtãamba, la d maan bõn-bãna.›
40007023	La m kõn zoe b nif n leok-b ye: ‹Mam zɩ n bãng yãmb ye, yi-y m taoore, tʋʋm yood dãmba!›
40007024	Ned ninga sẽn na n kelg goam niyns m sẽn togs mars marsã la a maand boto, m tõe n mak-a la ne sɩlem soaba sẽn me a roog kugr kegemd zugu.
40007025	Saag niime, koom fõdame, sob-raoog yikame tɩ b fãa tãag-a la a pa lʋɩ ye, b sẽn me-a kugra zug yĩnga.
40007026	Ned ning me sẽn wʋmd-a mam koɛɛga la a pa maand wa m sẽn datã, b tõe n maka yẽ soab ne gãeenga sẽn me a roog bĩsr zugu.
40007027	Saag niime, koom waa ne pãnga, sob-raoog yikame tɩ b tãag-a la a lʋɩɩme la a wãab ka yɩ bilfr ye!»
40007028	A Zezi sẽn gom n sɛ, la zãma wã sẽn wẽ siri b karenga poorẽ; sɩda a Zezi pa gomd wa sẽn karen-ba-n-sika ye,
40007029	b gomda wa naab sẽn gomd ne a soolem dãmba.
40008001	A Zezi siga tãngã tɩ neb wʋsg sɩng b pʋgbo.
40008002	Yĩng soab a ye n waa n wõgemd b taoore n yeel-ba: «Yãmb sã n dat waa, m Soaala, y tõe n sãoog-m lame.»
40008003	B tẽega b nus n sɩɩs-a n yetẽ: «Sãoog tɩ m nonga rẽ.» Wakat kãng bala a yĩnga yɩlgame.
40008004	T'a Zezi na n yeel-a: «Sõng n da gom tɩ neb wʋm ye, kẽng tɩ maan-kʋʋda yãend-fo la f kɩs kũun ning a Moyiiz sẽn yet tɩ b kɩs a soaba tɩ yɩ f sãoogr kaseto.»
40008005	B sẽn kẽ Kafarnaom tẽnga la tãnsoab a ye sẽn bʋʋg-ba n na n kos-b bũmbu. A yeelame:
40008006	«Soaala, m dakõor n gãe yiri, a nus la a nao kiime la a namsda wʋsgo.»
40008007	A Zezi yeel-a lame: «M na kẽng n tɩ sãoog-a!»
40008008	Tãnsoaba leokame: «Soaala, m zema bõe tɩ y na n kẽ m zakẽ? Yeel-y gomd a ye bala tɩ m dakõora na sãooge.
40008009	Ade, maam ne m sẽn pa na-kãsengã, m soo tãb-biisi, m sã n yeel a ye: kẽnge! A kẽngdame, m sã n yeel a to: wa! A watame; m sã n yeel m dakõorã: maan woto! A maandame.»
40008010	A Zezi wʋma gomdã la kẽ-la b sũurẽ tɩ b yeel b poorẽ dãmba:
40008011	«Mam yeta yãmba, m pa yãend tẽeb a woto buud Israyɛl kamb sʋk ye. Wʋsg na n yii yaanga la taoore n wa paam tɩgra roog n kẽ ne a Abraam, a Izaak la a Zakoob arzãn Rĩung pʋgẽ,
40008012	tɩ Rĩunga kamb mens na n yaool n pa yɩnga, likẽ, n yãbd tɩ b yẽn kẽrsdẽ.»
40008013	B yaool n yeela tãnsoabã: «Dɩk f sore, la Wẽnd na kõ foom f sẽn tẽede.» Wakat kãng bala dakõora paama laafi.
40008014	A Zezi sẽn kẽ a Piyɛr zakẽ, a mikame tɩ yẽ reem-poak gãeeme n pa keemẽ.
40008015	B sɩɩsa reem-poaka nug la a sãoogame la a yikame n segl-ba.
40008016	Zĩig sẽn waa n sobge, b talla neb wʋsgo n wa b taoore; sʋtãamba n da be b pʋsẽ; b yiisa gomd bala n dig sʋtãamba, la bãad dãmb sãoogame.
40008017	La yɩɩ woto la bãngd a Izayi gomda taasyã: A rɩka tõnd komslem, tõnd bãase n tʋk a menga.
40008018	A Zezi mikame tɩ sẽn pʋgd-b bãmbã da yaa wʋsgo tɩ b na n kõ noor tɩ b rʋʋg kʋɩlgã.
40008019	Sɛb-mit a ye kolg-b lame n leok-ba: «Soaala, y sẽn dabd zĩig ning fãa m na tũ-y lame.»
40008020	T'a Zezi yeel-a: «Waas tara b roto, tɩ yĩngr luiili tar b tʋgdo; Ned Biiga bala n ka tar gãag zĩiga.»
40008021	B karen-biig a ye n waa n yeele: «Soaala, m kota sor n deng n tɩ solg m ba.»
40008022	La a Zezi leok-a lame: «Tũ maam la f bas kɩɩmsa ti b mum taaba.»
40008023	Dẽ poore b kẽe koom koglg ne b karen-biisi.
40008024	Ko-wiis rãmba bɛd-bɛda tɩ koglga rat n lisi. Dẽ t'a Zezi gõeeme.
40008025	Karen-biisa kolgame n nek a Zezi n yeel-ba: «Soaala, wa-y tɩ d na n kiime!»
40008026	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Bõe yĩng la y zoet dabeem, tẽeb bilf rãmba?» B sẽn yiki, b tãsa mogrã ne sobgã la bũmb fãa lebga sɩɩ.
40008027	Neba pɛleng yɩkame tɩ b yeele: «Nin-kãnga la a bõe tɩ sobd la mogr meng deegd a noore?»
40008028	A Zezi sẽn dʋʋg mogrã n ta Gadar tẽnga la neb a yiibu, sẽn tar Sʋtãan b pʋsẽ, yi yaadẽ n seg-ba. B ra yaa nin-toose al wʋsgo, al tɩ ned ba a ye ra pa le saagd n tũ sor ning sẽn yegd-a be wã ye.
40008029	B sɩnga moonego: «Wẽnd Biiga baooda bõe ne-do? A wat n na n zoe n nams-d lame tɩ wakat nan ka yao?»
40008030	Sẽn vẽsg be bilfu, kurkuy wʋsgo n da wãbd yamdo.
40008031	Sʋtãamba yeela a Zezi: «D kotame tɩ f sã n dig-d ka n yiis bɩ d tɩ kẽ kurkuya!»
40008032	B yeel-b lame tɩ b kẽnge la b yiime n tɩ kẽ rũmsã tɩ b kaoog vugr bala n sig n kẽ mogrã tɩ kooma rɩ-b gilli.
40008033	Rũm-kɩɩmba ninga tĩiga n ta n togs tẽnga rãmba rũmsa sãoongo la neb a yiiba sãoogre.
40008034	Tẽnga tõr yiime n na n seg a Zezi; b sẽn yãend-ba, b kos-b lame tɩ b yi b tẽngẽ.
40009001	B kẽe koom koglg yɛsa n dʋʋg kʋɩlgã n leb b tẽngẽ.
40009002	B talla põor n wa b taoore. Põora da gãe a gãag zugu. A Zezi sẽn yãend neba tẽebã, b yeela põorã: «Da le bʋ ye, m biiga, tɩ f paama f yel-wẽna sugri.»
40009003	Sɛb-mitba kẽer yeela b sũurẽ: «Yãoã yaa wẽn-tʋʋsa.»
40009004	A Zezi sẽn mi b sũur tagsgã leoka woto: «Bõe yĩng la y bilgd wẽng y sũurẽ?
40009005	Gomd bʋg togsg la naana n yɩɩda: f paama f yel-wẽna sugri, bɩ: yik n kẽne?
40009006	Sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ y bãng tɩ Ned Biiga tara tõog n kõ yel-wẽnd sugr, tẽng zug ka, ade, põore, m yet-f lame: tik n yik, dɩk f gãaga, leb f yiri!»
40009007	Põora yikame n dɩk a gãaga n leb a zakẽ.
40009008	La rẽ kẽesa rabeem kãsenga neb niyns sẽn yãend-ba sũurẽ, la b pẽga Wẽnnaam b sẽn kõ ninsaalb tõog a woto buudu.
40009009	A Zezi waa n yiime n loogdẽ, n yãe ned sẽn zĩ fadg reesg zĩigẽ, n boond tɩ Matiye. A Zezi yeel-a lame: «Tũ maam!» La a yik n tũ-b lame.
40009010	B sẽn ta a zakẽ n sɩng rɩɩbo la fadg rɛɛsdb ne yel-wẽn-maandb wʋsg sẽn waa n naag a Zezi ne b karen-biisã.
40009011	La rog-n-mika tũudba, Farizẽ rãmba, sẽn yãend rẽndã, b yeela karen-biisã: «Yaa wãn tɩ yãmb karen-saamba dɩt ne fadg rɛɛsdb la yel-wẽn-maandba?»
40009012	Mik a Zezi meng ra wʋmame tɩ b na n yeele: «Ka sẽn tar-b laafi n baood tɩɩm soab zĩig ye, yaa sẽn bẽed-ba.
40009013	Kẽng-y n tɩ zãms-y gomd kãnga võore: nimbãan-zoeer la m nong n yɩɩd maoongo. Ka nin-sõma wã la m waa n na n boole, yaa yel-wẽn-maandbã.»
40009014	Dẽ poore a Zã karen-biisa kolg-b lame n sok-ba: «Bõe yĩng la tõnd ne Farizẽ rãmba loet noore tɩ yãmb karen-biisa pa loetẽ?»
40009015	T'a Zezi na n leok-ba: «Pʋg sɩd zo-rãmb tõe n gãnema b nens wa ku-biisi tɩ pʋg-sɩda ket b sʋk bɩ? Wakat ning n wat n zĩndi tɩ b na n loog ne pʋg-sɩdã, wakat kãng la b na n loe b noore.»
40009016	Ned ka rɩkd peen-paalg sẽn ka wẽ koasla n sũk fu-kʋɩdg ye. Peen-paalga na n zɩsga fuugã t'a le kẽeg n paase.
40009017	Woto me waoog sẽn kʋdg ka rɩkd n sui dã-paalg ye. Ning tɩ pusgi, tɩ rãam daage, tɩ waoog yɩ bõne. Wao-paalg la b suiid dã-paalga, woto bõne ka ye.
40009018	B sẽn da ket n gomd la nin-naab a ye sẽn kolge n wõgemd b taoore n yeel-ba: «Ad-y m bi-pugl n ki mars-mars noogã, wa-y n tik-a ne y nugu t'a na vʋʋge.»
40009019	La a Zezi yikame n tũ-a, bãmb ne b karen-biisã.
40009020	Pag a ye sẽn da bẽed mende al yʋʋm piig la a yiibu, kolga b poorẽ n sɩɩs b fuuga noore.
40009021	A ra gomda a sũurẽ: «M sã n sɩɩs b fuugã, m na n paama laafi.»
40009022	A Zezi sẽn wẽneg b poorẽ b yãend-a lame n yeel-a: «Teeg maam, m biiga, tɩ f tẽeb fãag-f lame.» La wakat kãng bala paga wẽneg n paama laafi.
40009023	B sẽn ta nin-naaba zakẽ, b yãee neb sẽn peeb-d wɩɩse la neb wʋsg sẽn gũmi, tɩ zak wulumdi.
40009024	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yi-y tɩ bi-pugla nan ka ki ye, a gõeeme bala. Neba da laad-b lame.»
40009025	La b sẽn yiis neba yɩnga, a Zezi kẽeme n gãd bi-pugla nugu, t'a yik.
40009026	La kibara sãaga tẽnga fãa.
40009027	A Zezi sẽn yik tɩ b loogda, la zoeens a yiib sẽn sɩng pʋgbo la b moonẽ: «Daviid biiga, zoe-y d nimbãanega!»
40009028	B sẽn ta yiri, la zoeensã sẽn kolg-ba tɩ b na n sok-ba: «Yãmb tẽedame tɩ m tõe rẽnna?» Tɩ b leoke: «N-yẽe, Soaala!»
40009029	Tɩ b na n sɩɩs b nina la b yetẽ: «Bɩ yɩ wa y sẽn tẽede!» B nina pukame.
40009030	T'a Zezi na n leok-b pãr pãre: «Maan-y gũusgu, tɩ ned da bãng ye!»
40009031	Zoeensa sẽn yi, pa kaoos ye, b sɩnga b yʋʋra yelegr beelẽ baobgã.
40009032	Bãmb sẽn looge, ka kaoos ye, tɩ b tall ned a ye n wa la Sʋtãan-muk n da be a pʋgẽ.
40009033	B sẽn dig Sʋtãana la neda sẽn sɩng goama. Zãma wã pɛleng yɩkame tɩ b yetẽ: «Ned zɩ n yãe woto taar Israyɛl tẽng ye.»
40009034	Farizẽ rãmba yẽ ra yetame: «Ad-y yaa ne Sʋtãamba naab pãnga la a rigd sʋtãamba.»
40009035	A Zezi ra kẽeda tẽn-bɛd la tẽn-bõonese, n maand karengo pʋʋsg rotẽ, n togsd Rĩunga kibar noogã la b sãoogd bãag la pa-keem buud fãa.
40009036	A Zezi gesa zãma wã n wẽ siri tɩ b ra yɛɛ zãnga, tɩ b nensa surẽ wa piis sẽn pa tar pe-kɩɩma.
40009037	Dẽ la b yeel b karen-biisi: «Kooda sẽn ta kɛɛba labsa, la kɛɛdba sõor paooda.
40009038	Kos-y pʋʋga soaba t'a tʋm ka-kɛɛdba a pʋʋgẽ.»
40010001	B boola b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã la b kõ-b-la tõog tɩ b rig Sʋtãamba la b sãoog bãag la pa-keem buud fãa.
40010002	Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã yʋy la woto: pipi yaa a Simo, b sẽn boond a soab tɩ Piyɛr; yẽ poore, a yao, a Andre, n paas a Zak ne a yao, a Zã, bãmb ba la a Zebede;
40010003	le yaa a Filip, a Bartelemi, a Toma, a Matiye, yẽ da reegda fadgo; le paasa a Zak, a Alfe biiga ne a Taade,
40010004	n paas a Simo a to: yẽ la m sũur bee ne buuda bɛ fãa; n baasd ne a Zɩɩda, Iskariyot tẽng neda; yẽ n sõng a Zezi bɛɛba tɩ b paam-ba n yõke.
40010005	Bãmb piig la a yiibã la a Zezi yeel tɩ b saag n ges tẽnsã, n sagl-b woto: «Da tũ-y bu-zẽmba sor ye, la ra kẽ-y Samari rãmb tẽngẽ ye.
40010006	Pʋg-y Israyɛl kamba sẽn kẽ-b weoog wa piisã.
40010007	Sor zug bɩ y moon tɩ Wẽnd Rĩung kolgame.
40010008	Sãoog-y bãad dãmba, vʋʋg-y kũum, tõog-y yĩng bãase, dig-y Sʋtãamba. B kõo yãmb zaalem, bɩ yãmb me kõ zaalem.
40010009	Da bao-y sãnem bɩ wanzurf ye, da sui-y bõonego y gɩfẽ ye.
40010010	Da bob-y korgo n kẽnd ye, da zɩ-y fut a yiib ye, da widi neooda ye, da zã-y dasaar ye. Tʋʋm-tʋmd toga ne yaoodo.
40010011	Y sã n kẽ tẽn-bil bɩ tẽn-kãsenga, bɩ y kos tɩ b wilg-y nin-sõng zaka tɩ y yõg gãag-sobend be, n ta y loogr daare.
40010012	Y sã n wa kẽed zaka pʋga bɩ y kãab-a laafi,
40010013	la a sã n sɩd tog ne-a, y laafi na sig a pʋgẽ, la y laafi kõn sig-a, a sã n pa tog ne-a ye.
40010014	Ned sã n mong-y gãag-sobendo, a sã n zãgs y koɛɛg kelgre, bɩ y yi a zakẽ, bɩ a tẽngẽ, la y fugumd y neooda tom.
40010015	La m yet-y lame tɩ bʋʋda raare, Sodom la Gomor nimbãanega kõn zeng tẽn-kãng rẽnd ye.
40010016	Ad-y m tʋmd-y-la wa pe-yãans digd-n-yĩids sʋka, bɩ y sɩlem yɩ waaf sɩlem, la y yɩ neb sẽn ka tar b toorẽ yelle wa walle.
40010017	Maan-y gũusgu ne ninsaalba; b na n kẽes-y-la bʋʋdo bʋ-kaood bɛda taoore, b na n pãb-y la ne kaase, b pʋʋsg rotẽ.
40010018	Mam yĩnga, b na n vu-y lame n kẽng dĩm dãmb la kombɛɛmba taoore, tɩ m datame tɩ y yɩ m kaset dãmba, bãmb la bu-zẽmba taoore.
40010019	La b sã n wa yõg-y bɩ y ra nams y menga n bao y sẽn na n leok to-to, bɩ y sẽn na n togs bũmb ning ye; y sẽn na n togs bũmb ningã, y na bãng-a wakat kãng bala,
40010020	tɩ ka yãmb n na n gome, yaa y Ba wã Vʋʋsem n na n gom y zĩigẽ.
40010021	Ned na n kɩsa a ba-biiga, tɩ b kʋ, tɩ ba na n kɩs a meng bi-roaka, tɩ kamb na n yik ne b ba rãmba, n kʋ-ba.
40010022	B fãa na n kisga yãmb, mam yĩnga, la ned ninga sẽn na n kell n modga a yõor tɛka, yẽ soab n na n paam fãagre.
40010023	B sã n digd yãmb tẽn kãngã, bɩ y zoe n kẽ tẽng a to, b sã n pʋg-y be, bɩ y zoe n kẽ tẽng a to; la m yet-y lame tɩ y kõn saag Israyɛl tẽnsã n sɛ, tɩ Ned Biiga nan ka wa ye.
40010024	Karen-biig pa yɩɩd a karen-saamb ye, la rakõor pa yɩɩd a zu-soab ye.
40010025	Karen-biig sã n Wẽnd a karen-saamba, tɩ dakõor wẽnd a zu-soaba, sekame. B sẽn bool zak soab t'a Beelzebul, bõe la b ka n a n yeel a zaka rãmb poorẽ?
40010026	Da zoe-y neba ye. Sẽn solg na n pukame la sẽn lud fãa na n lakame. M sẽn togs yãmb bũmb ning fãa likẽ, bɩ y yi n moon yɩnga,
40010027	la m sẽn walem-y bũmb ning y tʋbrẽ bɩ y rʋ roog zugu n pãr-a.
40010028	Da zoe-y lɛ-lɛ sẽn tõe n kʋ-b yĩngã n yaool n pa tõe n kʋ sɩɩga ye. Zoe-y bala, ned ning sẽn tõe n lub bugmẽ sɩɩga la yĩngã.
40010029	Yirsa yiib yɩɩda tãma sɩda? La yirg ba a ye ka lʋɩt tẽnga tɩ y Ba zɩ tiir ye.
40010030	Dɩlla yɩta a wãn ne yãmba. Ad-y y zoobda fãa, Wẽnd tara b sõore!
40010031	Da bʋ-y ye, tɩ yãmb sãoo luin-sugri.
40010032	Ned ninga sẽn na n yeel-a neb taoore t'a kẽeda maam, m Ba sẽn be arzãna taoore, mam me na yeel tɩ m kẽeda a soaba.
40010033	Ned ninga sẽn na n yeel-a neb taoore t'a ka mi maam, mam me na yeele, m Ba sẽn be arzãna taoore, tɩ m ka mi-a ye.
40010034	Da tẽ-y tɩ m talla laafi n wa tẽng zug ye, ka laafi la m tall n wa, yaa zabr sʋʋga.
40010035	M waame n na n zablg ned ne a ba, bi-pugl ne a ma, pag ne a bi-paga.
40010036	Fo bɛɛba na n yii f buudẽ.
40010037	Sẽn nong-a a ba bɩ a ma n yɩɩd maam, ka tog ne maam ye; sẽn nong-a a bi-ribl bɩ a bi-pugl n yɩɩd maam, yẽ soab ka tog ne maam ye.
40010038	Sẽn ka rɩkd-a a pika n pʋg maam, ka tog ne maam ye.
40010039	Sẽn baood-a a yõore na n menes-a lame; la sẽn menesa a yõor mam yĩnga, na n le paam-a lame.
40010040	Sẽn deegd-a yãmb sãando, yaa maam la a reegda; sẽn deegd-a maam sãando deegda ned ning sẽn tʋm-a maam.
40010041	Ned ninga sẽn maand-a bãngd sãando a sẽn ya bãngda yĩnga, yẽ soab na n paama bãngd dolbo. Ned ning sẽn maand-a nin-sõng sãando a sẽn ya nin-sõnga yĩnga, yẽ soab na n paama nin-sõng dolbo.
40010042	Ned ninga sẽn na n kõ m kom-bãmba nin-yend ko-maasg wamde, a sẽn ya m karen-biiga yĩnga, m yet-y lame t'a kõn kong a rolb ye.»
40011001	A Zezi sẽn waa n sagl b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã n sɛ, b yiime n kẽ tẽnsã n le sɩng zãmsgo.
40011002	Mik a Zã zĩnda bi-bees roogẽ n wʋm Wẽnd Neda tʋʋma yelle.
40011003	A yiisa a karen-biis tɩ b tɩ sok a Zezi: «Yãmb la sẽn tog n waa soaba bɩ d tog n gũ-la a to?»
40011004	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Tɩ togs-y y karen-saamb a Zã y sẽn wʋme la y sẽn yãe bũmb ninga:
40011005	Zoeens neeme, wobs kẽndame, wãoob sãoogdame, wʋms wʋmdame, sẽn ki-b vʋʋgdame, la b togsda Koe-noogã naong rãmba;
40011006	zu-noog soaba la sẽn ka lakd-a maam wa sor zug kugri n lʋɩ.»
40011007	A Zã sẽn tʋm b rãmba sẽn lɛɛg n kuiisẽ la a Zezi sẽn leok woto a Zã poorẽ: «Bõe la y tɩ yãe weoogẽ, tɩ-pol sobg sẽn lengde?
40011008	Bõe la y tɩ yãend sẽ? Ned sẽn yer faong fuugu bɩ? Ad-y sẽn yer-b faong futa vɩɩ nanams zagsẽ.
40011009	Bõe la y tɩ yãend sẽ, y tɩ yãee bãngda? N-ye! La m yet-y lame: yɩɩda bãngda.
40011010	Ad-y yaa yẽ poorẽ la b gʋlsyã: M na n yiisa ned n ning m taoore t'a maneg sor ning m sẽn na n tũ wã.
40011011	Sɩd-sɩda, m yet-y lame tɩ pagba kamb sʋka, ned ka yɩɩd a Zã, rao ning sẽn kõta sooba ye, la ne rẽ fãa sẽn ya-a yao zʋʋg Arzãn Rĩunga pʋgẽ, yɩɩd-a lame.
40011012	A Zã sẽn sɩng sooba tɛka n dabd marsã, Arzãn Rĩunga waa ne wɩsg-m-menga, lebga sẽn tara pãng tus n kẽ.
40011013	Sebr sõng la bãngdba talla wilgri, n tãag a Zã.
40011014	La sã n yaa a Zã, m ka mi y sã na n deega m goama, ad-y yẽ la Eli ning sẽn na n lɛɛg n wa wã.
40011015	Sẽn tar-a tʋbr bɩ a wʋm!
40011016	Bõe la m na n yãe n mak zamaan kãnga? A wẽnda yãas sẽn kõ taab sɛk tẽnga tẽnsʋka, n na n gom taab beedo,
40011017	n yetẽ: ‹Tõnd peeba wɩɩse, tɩ y zãgs saooga, tɩ tõnd kelem kʋʋre, tɩ y zãgs y yãoog toosgo!›
40011018	A Zã sɩd waame n pa rɩtẽ la a pa yũud ye, tɩ b yet tɩ Sʋtãan n be a pʋgẽ.
40011019	Ned Biiga waame, n dɩtẽ la a yũuda, tɩ b yet tɩ b baad dɩ-rɩta la rã-yũuda, tɩ b baad fadg rɛɛsdba la yel-wẽn-maandba zoa. La b tʋʋm sõma wã waa n kõo kaseto tɩ Yam Pidunga soab bee ne-ba.
40011020	Dẽ poore b yika zabre ne tẽns niyns sẽn yãend-b bõn-bãna n yɩɩd tẽns a taaba n yaool n ka tek b zʋgã.
40011021	Yel-beed ne foo, Korozein tẽnga! Yel-beed ne foo, Bɛtsayid tẽnga! Wẽnd makr niyns sẽn maan yãmb pʋgẽ sã n da maanẽ Tir la Sidõ, yaa daar zãr la be rãmba yeelgẽ sũ-pa-noang futu la b bilmẽ b mens tompɛglemẽ, n teemẽ zʋgo.
40011022	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet-y: bʋʋda raare, Tir ne Sidõ sɩbgr kõn ta y rẽnd ye.
40011023	La foo, Kafarnaom, fo tẽedame tɩ f na n lugame n tãag saaga? Ade, bʋg-tẽng la f na n sirg n lʋɩ. Bãng tɩ bõn-bãn-niyns sẽn maan f pʋgẽ sã n da maanẽ Sodom tẽnga, a ket n yɛsẽ la rũnna.
40011024	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet-fo: bʋʋda raare, a Sodom sɩbgr kõn ta f rẽnd ye.»
40011025	A Zezi waa n zẽka b koɛɛg n gom woto: «M Ba, yĩngr la tẽng Soaala, m pʋʋsd-y la barka y sẽn solg woto sɩlem dãmba la yam dãmba n yaool n togs nin-bõonese.
40011026	N-ye! Woto n sɩd yɩ y raabo, m Ba sõngo!
40011027	M sẽn tar fãa yaa m Ba n kõ-ma. Ned ka mi Biiga sã n ka Ba, la ned me ka mi Ba sã n ka Biigã, bɩ ned ninga sẽn paam-a Biiga wilgri.
40011028	Wa-y m nengẽ, yãmb fãa sẽn tar-b pɛta la sẽn zɩt-b zɩɩb n yõrdẽ, tɩ m na yols y fãa.
40011029	Tʋk-y m zɩɩbã la lebg-y m karen-biisi, tɩ m yaa ned sẽn ka mi sũ-toog la zẽk-m-menga, la y sɩɩga zu-loees na paam yolsgo.
40011030	Bãng-y tɩ m sẽn na n tʋk-y zɩɩb ninga yaa faasga la tʋʋsga bʋgsa.»
40012001	Sibr daar a ye, a Zezi waa n loogda kood sẽn bɩ sʋka. Kom da tara b karen-biisã tɩ b kũus ka-zut n tẽg n wãbe.
40012002	Farizẽ rãmb yãeeme n yeel-ba: «Yãmb karen-biisa maanda sẽn kis vʋʋsg daare!»
40012003	T'a Zezi na n yeel-ba: «Dɩlla yãmb pa karen a Daviid sẽn maan bũmb ninga, kom sẽn waa n yõk-a, yẽnda ne a tũud-n-taase?
40012004	Ad-y b kẽe wẽnd doogẽ n dɩ buri niyns sẽn da rɩk n kõ Wẽndã. Yẽ ne a tũud-n-taasa yaool n da pa tõe n dɩ bur kãens ye, tɩ maan-kʋʋdba bal n da tar sor n dɩ-ba.
40012005	Bũmb a to, y pa karem Noora sebrẽ tɩ vʋʋsga daare maan-kʋʋdba tʋmda wẽnd doogẽ tɩ ka yel-wẽnd bɩ?
40012006	M yet-y lame: sẽn yɛs-a yãmb taoorã yɩɩda wẽnd doogã.
40012007	Yãmb sã n dag n wʋme gomd kãnga võore: m nonga nimbãan-zoeere n yɩɩd maoongo, y kõn sak n ningẽ taale neb sẽn ka maan yel-wẽnd ye.
40012008	Bãng-y tɩ Ned Biigã n so vʋʋsga daare.»
40012009	B sẽn looge, pʋʋsga roogẽ la b tɩ kẽ.
40012010	Zemsg neere, nug kɩɩng a ye soab n da be be la Farizẽ rãmba soka a Zezi: «Bãad tõe n sãooga vʋʋsga daar bɩ?» B soka woto n na n kẽes a Zezi yellẽ.
40012011	Dẽ la a Zezi leok-ba: «Yãmb sʋka, ãnd n tar pe-yãang a ye tãa, t'a lʋɩ bokẽ vʋʋsga daare t'a zãgs a tɩ gãd-a n yiisi?
40012012	Y mi tɩ ninsaal yɩɩda pesg al zĩig sẽn zãre. Dẽnna bõn-sõng maaneg ka kis vʋʋsga daar ye.»
40012013	Dẽ poore b yeela koamsã: «Tẽeg f nug.» A tẽega a nugu, nuga vʋʋgame n ya kɛgeng wala a yembrã.
40012014	Farizẽ rãmba yiime la b yẽsa ne taaba b sẽn na n maanega n paam a Zezi n kʋ.
40012015	B sẽn bãng rẽ, a Zezi yiime. Wʋsg tũ-b lame.
40012016	B sãooga koms rãmba fãa la b yeel-b lame tɩ b ra gom tɩ ned wʋm ye.
40012017	Woto taasa bãngda Izayi gomde:
40012018	Ad ned ning m sẽn yãk m tʋʋmda yĩnga. Yaa m zoa nongre, m yam kẽe-a la zãnga. M na n sika m Vʋʋsem a zugu, t'a wilg bu-zẽmba sõmblem la sɩd sore.
40012019	A kõn yɩ zab baooda la bʋrg soab ye. Ned kõn wʋm a koɛɛg sotiisẽ ye.
40012020	Tipol sẽn kaooge, a kõn kũk-a n baas ye fitil laong sẽn ket n nukd bug-zõose, a kõn kiis-a n baas ye al n wa tõog tɩ sɩd la sõmblem reeg zĩig zãng n yãmbe.
40012021	Yẽnda la dʋni rãmba fãa na n maan b teegda.
40012022	Sʋtãan n da kẽ neda t'a soaba ya zoanga la muka la b tall-a lame n wa a Zezi taoore la bãmb sãoog-a lame t'a gomd la a neẽ.
40012023	Zãma wã yɛɛsame n yetẽ: «Nin kãnga kaa Daviid biigã?»
40012024	Farizẽ rãmba wʋmame n leoke: «A sã n digd sʋtãamba, yaa ne Sʋtãamba naab, a Beelzebul, pãnga.»
40012025	A Zezi sẽn mi b pʋga yeel-b lame: «Rĩung buud fãa sẽn welg sagse, rĩung kãng baooda a wãabo. Tẽng a ye rãmba bɩ zak a ye rãmb sã n welg taaba, tẽng kãng bɩ zak kãng ka tõe n yals ye.
40012026	Sʋtãan sã n digd a sʋtãan taaga, a welga a yiibu, a naam na n yɩɩ wãn n vigli?
40012027	Sã n yaa ne a Beelzebul pãng la mam digd Sʋtãamba, yãmb neba rigd-b la ne ãnda rẽnna? Dɩlla bãmb n na n kao y bʋʋdo.
40012028	La sã n ya ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng pãng la m digd sʋtãamba, bɩ y bãng tɩ Wẽnd Rĩunga taa yãmba.
40012029	Bũmba to yɛsa: ned yɩta a wãn n kẽ gãndaoog zakẽ n zɛ a teedo, a sã n ka reng n yõk-a n sẽbe? Sẽbdame n yaool n zɛ teedo.
40012030	Sẽn ka-a mam zoa, yaa mam bɛyã, sẽn ka suiid-a mam sẽn suiidẽ, sẽegdame.
40012031	Yaa rẽ la m yeta: ninsaalba na n paam b yel-wẽnd la wẽn-tʋʋr buud fãa sugri la a Vʋʋsem Sõng tʋʋda kõn paam sugr ye.
40012032	Sẽn tʋʋs-a Ned Biiga na paam sugri, la sẽn tʋʋs-a Vʋʋsem Sõngo kõn paam sugr dũni kãnga la dũni ninga sẽn pʋgda ye.
40012033	Tɩ-sõngo womda bi-sõma. Tɩ-yoog biis me na yɩ yoodo. Tɩɩg biig n wilgd a sã n yaa sõng bɩ yoogo.
40012034	Wag-bi buudu, y goama yɩta a wãn n yɩ sõma tɩ y mens ya wẽnse? Sẽn pid sũuri n wat noorẽ!
40012035	Nin-sõng yiisda bõn-sõma tɩ bõn-sõma la a bĩng a baoorẽ, la nin-wẽng sẽn bĩng bõn-wẽnsã, yiisda bõn-wẽnse.
40012036	M yet-y lame, gomd yaalg buud fãa ned sẽn na n yiis a noorẽ, b na sok-a bʋʋda raare.
40012037	Yaa f sẽn yiis f noorẽ n na n yiis foo bʋʋdẽ bɩ n na n paalg-fo.»
40012038	Noor sebra mitba la Farizẽ rãmb kẽere yeel-b lame: «Soaala, d tʋllame tɩ y maan bõn-bãnd tɩ d yãende.»
40012039	B leok-b lame: «Zãmb la yoob zamaan kamba rata wẽnd makre la b ka na n paam wẽnd makr a to ye; a Zonas makra bal la m na n kõ-ba.
40012040	Wala a Zonas sẽn pa mogra Bõn-nind pʋg rasem a tã la yʋnd a tã, wotome Ned Biiga na n paa tẽng pʋgẽ rasem a tã la yʋnd a tãabo.
40012041	Bʋʋda raare, Niniv rãmb na n yika ne rũnna zamaana rãmba la b na n mong-b-la bʋʋm, tɩ bãmb sẽn wʋm a Zonas koɛɛga, b sɩbga b mense; sẽn yɛs-a ka wã yɩɩda a Zonas.
40012042	Bʋʋda raare, tẽn-zãorgẽ Dĩmpoaka na n yika ne rũnna zamaana rãmba la a na n mong-b-la bʋʋm tɩ yẽ yii al Mooga sɛtmẽ n wa kelg gom-minim naab, a Salomo, la sẽn be-a ka wã yɩɩda a Salomo!
40012043	Sʋtãan dẽgd sã n yi n bas a sẽn da kẽ a soaba, a gõoda weoogo n baood vʋʋsg zĩiga n ka yãetẽ ye.
40012044	A yeta a sũurẽ: m na n leba m zĩ-kʋdgẽ. A watame n mik t'a yaa vɩʋʋgo, mik tɩ b maneg pɩɩs-a lame, tɩ bũmb fãa be a zĩigẽ.
40012045	T'a na n lɛɛg n wa ne a sʋtãan taas a yopoe sẽn yɩɩd yẽ ne wẽnem, tɩ b wa kẽ-a. Bãng-y tɩ nin-kãng yell lebgda wẽng n yɩɩg pĩnda. Dũnna zamaan yooka yell na n yɩɩ boto.»
40012046	A Zezi ra ket n sõsda ne zãma wã la b ma ne b saam-biisa waa n bee yɩng n dat n gom ne-ba. [
40012047	Ned a ye n wilgi: y ba la y ma n be dignoorẽ la b rat n leok-y la bũmbu.]
40012048	A Zezi yeela sẽn waa n togsa wã: «Ãnda la mam ma, la m saam-biisi?»
40012049	La b zẽka b nug n tees b karen-biisã, n yetẽ: «Ad m ma la m saam-biisi.
40012050	Ned ninga sẽn maand-a m Ba sẽn be arzãna yam, yẽ yaa saam-biiga, la tão, la ma, m yĩnga.»
40013001	A Zezi yii yiri n kẽng mogra noore n tɩ zĩi.
40013002	Neb wʋsg sɩnga bãmb gũbgri tɩ b kong n kẽ n zĩnd koglg pʋga, tɩ zãma wã be kʋɩlga noore.
40013003	B goma bũmb wʋsg yell ne-ba la ra yaa ne yelbũna. Ad-b sẽn da yete: «Bʋt n yi n na n bʋde,
40013004	la a sẽn waa n bʋtẽ, bõn-buuda kẽer lʋɩɩ sor noor la luiili waa n dɩgs-b-la zãnga n dɩ.
40013005	Kẽer lʋɩɩ kug zĩigẽ, n ka paam n bus neer ye; la b sẽn ka paam n bus neerã b pa kaoos yiib ye.
40013006	La wĩntoog sẽn puki, a waolga yõog-b lame. La b sẽn ka tar yẽgen yĩnga, b kʋɩɩme.
40013007	Kẽer me lʋɩɩ gõosẽ la gõosa tobame n wulumd-ba n kʋ.
40013008	Kẽer lʋɩɩ zĩ-sõngẽ n wom biisi, kẽer koabg-koabga, kẽer pisoobsoobe, kẽer pistã-tã.
40013009	Sẽn tar-a tʋbr bɩ a wʋm!»
40013010	Karen-biisa kolgame n sok-ba: «Bõe yĩng la y gomd ne yelbũna?»
40013011	Tɩ b leoke: «Sã n ya yãmba, yãmb paamame n bãng Wẽnd Rĩungã yel-soalma la neb a taaba ka paam dẽ ye.
40013012	Sẽn zoe n tar-a, b na n kõ-a lame n paas a paoongo, la sẽn ka tar-a wʋsgo, a sẽn tar-a zãng la b na n deege.
40013013	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m gomd ne neb a taaba ne yelbũna: tɩ b neeme la yaa waa b pa ne ye; b wʋmdame la yaa waa b pa wʋmde, wa ka kẽed b yamẽ ye.
40013014	Bãmb me taasa bãngda Izayi koɛɛga: Y na n kelgame la y kõn wʋm fɩ, y na n gesame la y kõn yãe fɩ.
40013015	B yam lebga lika; b paga b tʋba la b nini tɩ b pa rat tɩ b nin yãe, tɩ b tʋbr wʋm, tɩ b yam deeg tɩ b teem tɩ m kõ b laafi ye.
40013016	Yãmb yẽ, yãmb yaa zu-noog rãmba tɩ y tara nin sẽn ne la tʋb sẽn wʋmde.
40013017	Sɩd-sɩda, m yet-y lame tɩ bãngdb wʋsgo la nin-sõma tʋlgame n yãe y sẽn yãete, la b ka paam ye, n wʋm y sẽn wʋmde la b ka paam dẽ ye!
40013018	Bɩ yãmb kelg bʋta yelbũndã.
40013019	Ned sã n kelg Wẽnd Rĩunga gomde n ka wʋm a võore, wẽnema naab kẽeda a sũurẽ n vaag a sẽn wʋm-a n looge. Yẽ soab makr la sor noorẽ bõn-buudã.
40013020	Bõn-buud ninga sẽn lʋɩ-a kuglaagẽ makda ned ninga sẽn wʋm-a koɛɛgã n deeg-a tao tao ne sũ-noogo.
40013021	La a sẽn ya ned sẽn ka tar yẽgna, ned sẽn ka tar a meng võorã, toog sã n wa bɩ b sã n namsd-a, Gomda yĩnga, tao tao t'a pãs n lʋɩɩme.
40013022	Bõn-buud ninga sẽn lʋɩ-a gõosẽ makda ned ninga sẽn wʋmd-a Koɛɛgã la a bas tɩ dũni zu-loeese la arzɛk tʋlsem wulumd-a t'a ka tõe n wom biis ye.
40013023	Bõn-buud ninga sẽn lʋɩ-a zĩ-sõngẽ makda ned ning sẽn wʋm-a Koɛɛgã a tʋbrẽ la a yamẽ; yẽ soab womda biisi, yẽ soab n womd koabg-koabga, pisoobsoobe, pistã-tã.»
40013024	B le wẽe yelbũnd a to: «Arzãn Rĩunga wẽnda ned sẽn bʋd bõn-buud sõng a pʋʋgẽ.
40013025	La neb sẽn waa n kẽ gõeem, a bɛ yiime n tɩ fẽeg bõn-buud yoogo n bas n looge.
40013026	Kooda sẽn waa n tob vãado la b wek biisi la b sẽn yẽnd bõn-buud yoog me.
40013027	Woto rakõapa tɩ yeela pʋʋga soaba: ‹Zu-soaba, ka bõn-buud sõng la y bʋd y pʋʋgẽ laa? Tũu ne bõe tɩ bõn-buud yoog me wa beẽ?›
40013028	Pʋʋga soab leok-b lame: ‹Yaa bɛ nina n maan dẽ.› Tɩ rakõapa le sok: ‹Y ka rat tɩ d kẽng n tɩ võ ba?›

40013030	Bas-y tɩ b bɩ n ta ka-kɛɛrã la ka-kɛɛra wakato m na yeel kɛɛdba: deng n tigs-y kood yoogã n kals n yõog bugmẽ. Dẽ poor marsã y na kẽeb buud sõngã n sui m baoẽ.› »
40013031	B le paasa yelbũnd a to: «Arzãn Rĩunga wẽnda tɩɩg a ye biisi, seneve tɩɩga, b sẽn dɩk n bʋd pʋʋgẽ.
40013032	Tɩɩsa biis sʋka seneve rẽnd n paood n yɩɩda la a sã n yi, yẽ n zʋʋgd zẽed tɩɩs a taaba la a wat n tol n lebga bedre tɩ luiili wat n soond a wilẽ.»
40013033	B le wẽe yelbũndi: «Arzãn Rĩunga wẽnda rabɩll pag sẽn dɩk n ning zom moena a tã pʋgẽ tɩ fãa wuki.»
40013034	A Zezi goma woto ne yelbũna. B pʋs n dag n ka gomda tɩ ka ne yelbũn ye.
40013035	Yaa woto la bãngda gomd tõog n taase: «M na n yaaga m noor n wẽ yelbũna, m na n puka yɛla sẽn solg al dũni sɩngrẽ.»
40013036	B basa nebã n leb yiri. B karen-biisa kolgame n kose: «Wilg-y tõnd vẽenega bõn-buud yooga yelbũnda võore.»
40013037	B yeel-b lame: «Sẽn bʋt-a bõn-buud sõnga yaa Ned Biigã.

40013039	Bɛyã sẽn bʋd bõn-buud yooga yaa Sʋtãana. Ka-kɛɛra yaa dũni sɛɛbo. Ka-kɛɛdba yaa malɛgse.
40013040	Wala b sẽn kɛɛd nadẽnse n yõogd bugma, dʋni wã sɛɛb me na n yɩɩ boto.
40013041	Ned Biiga na n tʋma malɛgs tɩ b kẽ b Rĩunga pʋgẽ n wʋk ye-lwẽna la yel-wẽn-maandba fãa
40013042	n lob bug-toaagẽ tɩ b be be n yãbd, tɩ b yẽn kɛɛd taaba.
40013043	Wẽnd kãng la nin-sõma wã na n yãg wa wĩntoogo, b Ba Rĩunga pʋgẽ. Bɩ sẽn tar-a tʋbr fãa wʋm!
40013044	Arzãn Rĩunga wẽnda arzɛk sẽn bus pʋʋgẽ tɩ ned wa buk-a. A le lɛɛg n bus-a lame la a kula ne sũ-noogo n tɩ koos a sẽn tar fãa n dɩk n da pʋʋgã.
40013045	Arzãn Rĩung wẽnda toanda sẽn baood muizãan neba.
40013046	A waa n yãenda a ye sẽn ya sõmb wʋsgo t'a kẽng n tɩ koos a sẽn tar fãa n paam n da-a.

40013055	Ka yẽ la ra-wãada biig laa? Ka yẽ ma la a Maryam, t'a Zak, a Zozɛf, a Simo la a Zɩɩd yaa a saam-biis laa?
40013056	A saam-bi-pogsa ka ket n be d sʋk laa? Yɛ la a paam woto fãa?»

40014001	Komber, a Erod, waa n wʋmdame tɩ b tar a Zezi yʋʋra pẽgre
40014002	t'a yeel a sõsd-n-taase: «Ad-y yaa Zã ning sẽn da kõt-a soobã; a vʋʋga kɩɩms sʋka, la rẽ n so la a maand wẽnd makr dãmba.»
40014003	Sɩd me, a Erod n da kɩt tɩ b yõk a Zã n balg bãnga, n pag roogo. Yɩ-la a Erodiad, a Filip paga, poorẽ,
40014004	t'a Erod n da rɩk a yao, a Filip, paga t'a Zã yet tɩ rẽ pa segd ye.
40014005	A Erod tʋlgame meng n kʋ a Zã la a zoe neba nifu, tɩ b ra geta a Zã wa bãngda.
40014006	A Erod waa n tẽega a rogem daare n maan kibsa. A Erodiad bi-pugl waa n saoo neere neba fãa nifẽ n noog a Erod sũuri al wʋsgo.
40014007	Dẽ la a kãab bi-pugla t'a sẽn na n kos bũmb ning fãa a na paame.

40014010	la a tʋmame tɩ b kẽng bi-bees roogẽ, n tɩ fiuug a Zã zugu.
40014011	B sɩd talla a Zã zuga ne laag n wa kõ bi-puglã t'a reeg n kõ a ma.
40014012	A Zã karen-biisã n waa n dɩk a Zã yĩngã n tɩ mum, n lɛɛg n wa wilg a Zezi.
40014013	A Zezi wʋma a Zã kaalem, n kẽ koglg, n vẽsge, n tees weoogo. Neba bãnga rẽ n yi b tẽnsẽ ne nao n bʋʋg-ba.
40014014	A Zezi sẽn yet tɩ b yit koglgã, b yãee neb ka tɛka, tɩ b nimbãaneg na n yõk-ba. La b sãooga bãad dãmba fãa.
40014015	Zĩig sẽn sobge b karen-biis kolg-b lame n yeele: «Ade, ka yaa weoogo la lebga zĩ-sobdo. Bas-y neba tɩ b le b tẽnsa pʋgẽ n tɩ ra rɩɩb n dɩ.»
40014016	Dẽ la a Zezi leok-ba: «Ka modgre tɩ b leb tẽng pʋgẽ ye, y mens y toore bao rɩɩbã n kõ-ba.»

40014018	«Tall-y n wa-y yã.»
40014019	B kɩtame tɩ b zĩndig nebã, moodẽ, n dɩk bur a nu wã la kʋɩl-zẽed a yiibã n zẽk b neng yĩngri, n pʋʋs bark pʋʋsgo, n wes burã n dɩk n kɩs karen-biisã tɩ b pʋɩ zãma wã.
40014020	B fãa rɩɩme n tɩge. B wʋka burã neba sẽn dɩ n kellã la pet piig la a yiibu la b pids yã.
40014021	Bãng-y tɩ rɩtba sõor da taa tus a nu, pagba la kom-bõonega toog sẽn ka ye.
40014022	Dẽ poore b modga b karen-biisã tɩ b kẽ koglg n deng taoore, tɩ b meng yaas n kuls nebã.
40014023	B sẽn waa n kuls nebã n sɛ, a Zezi rʋʋ tãnga zugu, kɛɛnga, n na n pʋʋse; yʋng waa n paam-b-la be.
40014024	Dẽ tɩ karem-biisa koglgã da paam n taa ko-sʋka tɩ ko-wiis lengd-a, tɩ sobg wẽed lebende.
40014025	Beoog sẽn waa n kolg vẽegre, a Zezi kẽna kooma zugu n babs-ba.
40014026	B sẽn yãend t'a Zezi kẽnd kooma zugu, rabeem yõka karen-biisã; b tẽeme tɩ yaa kɩɩma, n na n sɩng kɛlenga.
40014027	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Bas-y yam-yoaaga, yaa mam menga, da zoe-y rabeem ye!»

40014030	La sobga sẽn da vũud wʋsg yĩnga rabeem yõk-a lame t'a sɩng lisbu, n na n kelem: «Soaala, fãag-y-ma.»
40014031	A Zezi wẽneg n tuda b nugu n gãd-a, n yeel-a: «Tẽeb kɩdg soaba, f yam yooda bõe yĩnga?»
40014032	B sẽn kẽ koglga pʋga la sobga sẽn yõke.

40015001	Zerizalɛɛm Farizẽ rãmbã la sẽn karen-ba-n-sikã kolga a Zezi n sok-ba:

40015016	T'a Zezi yeele: «Yãmb yama ket n ka puk ba bilfu la?

40015019	Yaa sũurẽ la tʋls wẽns yita, n paas nin-kʋʋr, yoobo, yoob nonglem, wagdem, kaset-zirẽ, taab yʋʋr sãoongo.
40015020	Yaa yell kãens n dẽgemd ninsaala. La ka pek nus n yaool n sɩng rɩɩbo, ka tõe n dẽgem ninsaal ye.»
40015021	A Zezi sẽn yi be, b kẽnga Tir la Sidõ baobgo.
40015022	La ade, Kanaã pag n da yi a tẽngẽ n wa yɛs n moonẽ: «Zoe-y m nimbãaneg wɛ, Soaala, Daviid biiga! Ad-y Sʋtãan n tar m biiga n yaannẽ.»

40015028	T'a Zezi na n yeel marsã: «Paga, f tẽeb labsa, bɩ yɩ wa f sẽn date.» La wakat kãng bala a bi-pugla paama laafi.
40015029	A Zezi yii be n leb Galile mogr noore. B rʋʋ tãng zug n zĩndi.
40015030	Neb wʋsg babs-b lame ne wobse, ne zoeense, ne mugs la koms rãmb buud a taaba, n dɩgl-ba a Zezi taoore la a Zezi sãoog-b lame.
40015031	Neba wẽe siri b sẽn wʋm tɩ mugs gomda la b ne koms rãmba sẽn paam pãnga, tɩ wobs kẽnd tɩrga tɩ zoeens neẽ la neba pẽga Israyɛl Wẽnnaam.
40015032	A Zezi boola b karen-biisã n yeel-ba: «Nin-bãmba nimbãaneg tar-m lame, yaa rasem a tãab rũnna la b ka serg mam taoore la b pa tar sẽn na n dɩ ye. M pa rat n kuls-b ne kom ye; kẽer wat n lʋɩɩ sorẽ.»
40015033	Tɩ karen-biisa na n yeele: «La we-raoogẽ ka, d yãeta bur yɛ n kõ zãma a woto t'a rɩ n tɩge?»
40015034	La b sokame: «Bur a wãn la y tara?» Tɩ b leok tɩ yaa bur a yopoe la kʋɩl-zẽ-bõoneg bilf bala.
40015035	A Zezi kõo neba noor tɩ b zĩnd tẽnga.
40015036	B rɩka bur a yopoe wã la kʋɩl-zẽedã, n maan pʋʋsgo, n wes-ba, n dɩk n kɩs tɩ b pʋɩ nebã.
40015037	B fãa rɩɩme n tɩge la b wʋka gɩrsa sẽn kellã n pid pet a yopoe.
40015038	Bãng-y tɩ sẽn dɩ-ba yɩɩ tus a naase, pagb la kamb toog sẽn ka ye.
40015039	A Zezi kulsa nebã n yaool n kẽ koom koglg n wa Magadan tẽnga.
40016001	Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba sẽn da rat n bẽd-ba n yõk, kolgame n yeel a Zezi tɩ b sõng-b ne Wẽnd makre sẽn yit yĩngri.
40016002	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Zĩ-sobdo yãmb yetame: saag ka ye tɩ wĩntoog yaa moomd yʋdʋd.
40016003	Yibeoogo, yãmb yetame: yĩngr lobda sabla, dɩlla saag na n nii rũnna. Woto, tẽng zug yɛlã, yãmb mi-b lame la y tara b võore, zamaan paalga yɛl bala la y pa tar b võore!
40016004	Nin-yaals la yoaadb buudu, y rata makre la ya a Zonas makra bala la m na n kõ yãmba.» La b loogame n bas-ba.
40016005	B sẽn dʋʋg kʋɩlgã, karen-biisa yãeeme tɩ b ka zɩ bur ye.
40016006	A Zezi sẽn yaool n yeel-bã: «Puk-y y nini la y gũus ne Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba rabɩlle,»
40016007	b tẽe b yamẽ tɩ yaa b sẽn ka zɩ burã yĩnga.
40016008	A Zezi bãnga b tagsgo n yeel-ba: «Tẽeb kɩdg rãmba, bõe la y tagsd tɩ yaa y sẽn ka zɩ burã?
40016009	Y ket n nan pa wʋmde? Y pa tẽr bur a nu wã sẽn dɩlg neb tus a nu, la y pa tẽr peta sõore b girsã sẽn pids laa?
40016010	Y pa le tẽr bur a yopoe wã sẽn dɩlg neb tus a naase la y pa tẽr peta sõore b kɛla sẽn pids laa?
40016011	Yaa a wãna tɩ y ka ne tɩ ka bur yelle la m dat n gome? Gũus-y, wala m sẽn leokd yãmbã, ne Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba rabɩlle.»
40016012	B yaoolame marsã n wʋm tɩ b yeel-b lame tɩ b gũus ne Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba zãmsgo, ka yet tɩ b gũus ne rabɩll sẽn tar n wẽed bura ye.
40016013	B sẽn ta komber a Filip tẽng sẽn boond tɩ Sezare, a Zezi soka b karen-biisã: «Neba yeta me tɩ Ned Biiga yaa ãnna?»
40016014	Tɩ b yeele: «Kẽer nengẽ b ya a Zã ning sẽn da kõta soobã, kẽer nengẽ b yaa Eli, kẽer nengẽ b yaa Zeremi bɩ bãngdba nin-yende.»
40016015	T'a Zezi paas: «La sã n ya yãmba, y yetame tɩ maam la a bõe?»
40016016	A Piyɛr leokame: «Yãmb la Wẽnd Nedã, Wẽnnaam vɩɩga Biigã.»
40016017	T'a Zezi na n yeel-a: «Fo yaa zu-noog soaba, Simo, Zonas biiga, tɩ f bãngrã, ka ninsaal nengẽ la f paam-a ye, yaa m Ba sẽn be arzãna nengẽ.
40016018	La ade, m yet-f lame tɩ f yaa Kugri la kug kãng zug la m na n me m Tigungu, la kũuma ne a pãngã kõn maan daood a taoor ye.
40016019	M na n kõ-f la arzãn Rĩung kʋɩlem-biisi. Fo sẽn na n loe bũmb ning fãa tẽng zug, bõn-kãng me na n loe arzãnẽ. Fo sẽn na n lodg bũmb ning fãa tẽng zugu, bõn-kãng me na n lodga arzãnẽ.»
40016020	B yaool n sagla b karen-biisã tɩ b ra wilg ned ba a ye tɩ bãmb la Krista ye.
40016021	Badaare tɛka a Zezi sɩngame n wilg b tũud-n-taasã tɩ wat n yɩɩ tɩlɛ ne bãmba tɩ b kẽng Zerizalɛɛm, n yãe toogo wʋsgo, nin-kẽemsã, maan-kʋʋdba kãsem dãmba la Sẽn karen-ba-n-sikã nengẽ, tɩlɛ tɩ b ki menga la b vʋʋg dasm a tãab daare.
40016022	A Piyɛr veoog-b lame, n zabd ne-ba, n yetẽ: «Wẽnd na laas-y ne rẽ fãa, Soaala, ayoo, dẽ kõn tõog ye!»
40016023	A Zezi wẽnegame n yeel a Piyɛr: «Leb poorẽ, Sʋtãana! Fo lebga m lakr kugri, fo tagsga yaa ninsaal dẽnna, ka Wẽnnaam tagsg ye.»
40016024	Dẽ poore b yeela b karen-biisã: «Sẽn data n pʋg maam, bɩ a ra bao a meng ye, a tʋk a pik n tũ maam.
40016025	Ned ninga sẽn dat-a n ligl a yõore na n kiime la sẽn na n ki-a mam yĩnga na n vɩɩndame.
40016026	Dũni wã soogre manegda ned wãn wãna, f vɩɩm sã n tũ rẽ n sãam? Bõe la ned tõe n tek ne a vɩɩm?
40016027	Bãng-y tɩ Ned Biiga na n lɛɛg n waa ne a Ba zɩɩri n lebs ned kam fãa a vɩɩm sẽn tog ne.
40016028	La m yet-y lame tɩ yãmb sʋka, kẽer beeme n ka na n wʋm kũum yũugu tɩ b pa reng n yãend Ned Biiga tɩ b wat ne b Rĩunga ye.»
40017001	Dasem a yoob sẽn maane, a Zezi peega a Piyɛr, a Zak, la a yao, a Zã, bãmb b naasa bala; b zãaga ne zãma wã, tãn-wok zugu.
40017002	La a Zezi tedga bãmb nifẽ: b nenga ra yãgda wa wĩntoogo, tɩ b fut pɩnda.
40017003	La a Moyiiz ne a Eli waa n sõsda ne-ba.
40017004	A Piyɛr zẽka a koɛɛg n yeele: «Soaala, tõnd sẽn be ka wã yaa-d-la noogo, y sã n data m na ti rot a tãabo, n kõ yãmb a yembre, a Moiz a ye, a Eli me a ye.»
40017005	A Piyɛr pa yãee n gom n sɛ la sawad-pɛɛlg sẽn waa n bui-ba, tɩ koɛɛg zĩnd sawadga pʋga n moone: «Nin-kãnga yaa m Bi-nongre, m yam kẽ-b la zãnga, kelg-y-ba.»
40017006	Karen-biisa sẽn wʋm goama la b sẽn lʋɩ b yãnvabga n digd dabeem.
40017007	A Zezi kolgame n sɩɩs-ba n yeel-ba: «Yik-y la y bas rabeem!»
40017008	Karen-biisa puka b nini, b pa le yãend neda to n paas a Zezi ye.
40017009	B sẽn waa n sigd tẽn-nabrẽ, a Zezi kõ-b-la noor kãngã: «Da gom-y likr kãnga yelle tɩ Ned Biiga nan pa vʋʋg ye.»
40017010	Karen-biisa sok-b lame: «Bõe marsã la sẽn karen-ba-n-sikã yet t'a Eli n na n deng wa?»
40017011	Tɩ b yeele: «N-ye, a Eli na n deng n wa, n wa lebs bũmb fãa a zĩigẽ.
40017012	La m yet-y lame, a Eli zoe n waame la neba pa bãng tɩ yaa yẽ ye, n zã-a wa b sẽn date. Dẽ n so tɩ Ned Biiga me na n yãe toogo.»
40017013	Karen-biisa wʋmame marsã tɩ yaa Zã ning sẽn da kõta sooba yell la b gom yã.
40017014	B sẽn leb zãma wã sʋka la nin-yend sẽn kolg n yĩgimd b taoore n yeel-ba:
40017015	«Soaala, zoe-y m biiga nimbãanega t'a bẽeda kisenkiiri la yaa toogo. Naoor wʋsgo, a lʋɩta bugmẽ, n lʋɩt koomẽ.
40017016	M tall-a lame n wa y karen-biisa nengẽ la b pa tõog t'a sãoog ye.»
40017017	T'a Zezi yeel: «Wẽn-kɩɩsdb la nin-yaals buudu, m na n paa ne yãmb n ta wakat bʋgo? Tall-y bãadã n wa ka!»
40017018	A Zezi tãsa Sʋtãana la a yiime n bas biigã tɩ laafi wẽneg n wa.
40017019	Karen-biisa kolga a Zezi la nebã sẽn waa n looge, b sok-b lame tɩ yaa bõe yĩng la bãmb pa tõog n dig Sʋtãana n yiisi.
40017020	Tɩ b na n leoke: «Ya y tẽebã sẽn ya bilfra yĩnga; sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ yãmb tẽeba bedrem sã n ta seneve biiga, y na yeel tãnga sẽn tõndã: ‹Luk ka n ta ka.› A na luk a zĩigẽ la bũmb ba a ye kõn yɩ toog ne y ye. [
40017021	Sʋtãamb a woto buud ka tõe n dig n yiis tɩ pʋʋsg la no-loeer ka naag ye.]»
40017022	Daar a ye, a Zezi ne b karen-biisa ra bee Galile t'a Zezi yeel-ba: «Ned Biiga na n lʋɩɩ ninsaalb nusẽ,
40017023	la b na n kʋ-b lame la dasm a tãab daare b na n vʋʋgame.» La rẽ sãama karen-biisa sũur wʋsgo.
40017024	B taa Kafarnaom tɩ sẽn deesda wẽnd dooga ligd kolg a Piyɛr n sok-a: «Yãmb karen-saamba yẽ pa yaood wẽnd dooga yaood la?»
40017025	T'a leoke: «A yaoodame sẽ!» B sẽn ta yiri, a Zezi yɩɩ tao n yeel a Piyɛr: «Fo yetame tɩ wãna, Simo? Tẽnsa nanams reegda ligda bɩ fadgã ãnd dãmb nengẽ: b kambã n yaood bɩ yaa neb a taabã?»
40017026	B leokame tɩ ka b zaka rãmb nengẽ la b reegd ligd ye. T'a Zezi yeel: «Dɩlla zaka kamb pa yaood ye.
40017027	Baasg zãnga, m sẽn pa rat tɩ b yeel tɩ m pa maand wa neb a taaba, kẽng kʋɩlgẽ n tɩ lob f loɛɛga; gãd pipi zĩifã f sẽn na n yõkã, yaag a noorã tɩ f na yãe ligdi maam ne foom yaood yĩnga, tɩ f kɩs fadg a soaba.»
40018001	Karen-biisa waa n kolga a Zezi n sok-ba: «Arzãn Rĩunga pʋgẽ, ãnda n lʋɩt a taab taoore?»
40018002	B boola bi-bilfu n yals-a sʋka n yeele:
40018003	«Sɩd-sɩda, y sã n ka põd n lebg yãase, y kõn tõog n kẽ Arzãn Rĩunga pʋg ye.
40018004	Sẽn na n lʋɩ-a a taab taoor Arzãn Rĩunga pʋgẽ, yaa sẽn na n lebg-a bi-bilfu wa ad-a.
40018005	Ned ninga sẽn na n ges bi-bilf wa bi-kãnga yelle mam yĩnga, yaa mam meng yell la a ges yã.
40018006	Ned ninga me sẽn na n kɩt tɩ kom-bõonesã maan wẽnga, ad-y sãoo ne a soaba, tɩ b bao kugri wa neguug kugri, bõeensa sẽn gilgd ne kugr ning n werd zoma, n loe nin-kãng yubla, n tus-a n lub mogrẽ, tɩ kooma rɩ-a.
40018007	M yãbd dũni rãmba, b sẽn kʋɩɩbd taab yĩnga! M mi tɩ kʋɩɩbg ka tõe n ka zĩnd ye la m yãbd ned ninga sẽn ya-a kʋɩɩbda.
40018008	F nug bɩ naoor sã n lubd foo yell pʋgẽ, bɩ f fiuug-a n lob yɩɩga; fo sã n ya nug fiungu bɩ kar fiungu n paam vɩɩm, são b sẽn na n lob-f ne nus a yi bɩ ne nao a yi, bugum sẽn ka kiid pʋgẽ.
40018009	Sã n yaa f nif n lubd foom yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ, kɩdg-a n lob yɩɩga, tɩ f sã n ya ni-feoogo n kẽ vɩɩm zĩigẽ, são f sẽn na n lʋɩ ne f nin a yiibu bugum sẽn ka kiid pʋgẽ.
40018010	Da sak-y n paoog bi-bilfu ba a ye tɩ m yet-y lame tɩ arzãnẽ, b malɛk rãmb yɛsa wakat buud fãa, m Ba wã taoore. [
40018011	Ned Biiga waa n fãaga sẽn da menem-ba.]
40018012	Yãmb yamẽ, ned na n maana a wãna, a sã n tar pe-yãans koabga t'a ye wa menem? A kõn bas piswɛ la a wɛ wã tãnga zugu la a saa n gẽes sẽn menem-a wã sɩda?
40018013	A sã n yãend-a, m yet-y lame t'a sũur na tos kaam a poorẽ n yɩɩd piswɛ wã sẽn ka menem-ba.
40018014	Woto me, y Ba ninga sẽn be arzãnẽ ka rat tɩ kom-bãmba nin-yend menem ye.
40018015	F to sã n beege, babs-a, la yẽnda, a ye, taoore, wilg-a a kongre. A sã n kelg foom, f manega a yelle.
40018016	A sã n ka reege, bɩ f bao nin-yend bɩ neb a yiibu n paase tɩ yella kʋʋb paam neb a yiib bɩ neb a tãab kaseto.
40018017	A sã n zãgs b kelgre bɩ f togs Tigungu. A sã n zãgs Tigungu kelgre, bɩ f ges-a marsã wa bu-zẽnd la fadg rɛɛsda.
40018018	Sɩdem sɩdem, y sẽn loe bũmb ning fãa tẽng zug, bõn-kãng loee yĩngri me. Y sẽn lok bũmb ning fãa tẽng zug, loka yĩngri me.
40018019	M le togsd-y lame tɩ sɩd-sɩda, neb a yiibu, yãmb sʋka, sẽn na n naag taaba, tẽng zugu ka, n kos bũmb ning fãa, m Ba sẽn be arzãna na kõ-ba.
40018020	Neb a yiib bɩ a tãab sã n tigim taaba, mam yĩnga, mam meng bee b sʋka.»
40018021	A Piyɛr kolgame n yeel a Zezi: «M to sã n beeg-ma, naoor a wãn la ya tɩlɛ tɩ kõ-a sugri? M na yaa n ta naoor a yopoe bɩ?»
40018022	T'a Zezi na n leoke: «M pa yet tɩ naoor a yopoe bal ye, yaa naoor pisopoe la a yopoe.
40018023	Ad-y Arzãn Rĩung wẽnda dĩm sẽn tʋlg t'a sõgen-kamb wa, t'a pʋg a arzɛk nao.
40018024	Gɛɛlga sẽn sɩnge, b waa ne ned a ye sẽn tar dĩma samde, la samda yaa sãnem gil sẽn ta neb tus piig zɩɩbo.
40018025	A sẽn da ka tar n na n yao yĩnga, dĩma yeelame tɩ b koos yẽ ne a pag la a kamba la a sẽn tar fãa, tɩ samda tõog n yao.
40018026	Sõgna wa-la a zu-soaba taoore n vabende, n yeel-a: ‹Bas-y tɩ yɩ bilf tɩ m na bao n yao fãa.›
40018027	A zu-soaba zoe-la a nimbãanega n bas-a, n tol kiis a samda zãnga.
40018028	Nin-kãng yiime n seg a tũud-n-taag a ye sẽn da tar samde; Yẽ samda zemsa neb koab zɩɩbo. A soga a kokoɛ wã n wẽoogdẽ, n na n sãr-a la a yetẽ: ‹Wa ne f sẽn tog n kõ maama gilli.›
40018029	T'a tũud-n-taaga me yĩgimd a taoore n yeel-a: ‹Bas tɩ yɩ bilfu, tɩ m na bao n yao.›
40018030	A zãgsame n kɩt tɩ b kẽes-a roogo, n gũud t'a yao samda zãnga.
40018031	Dẽ la tũud-n-taas a taaba sũur sãam wʋsgo tɩ b tɩ togs b zu-soaba rao kãng manesma.
40018032	Tɩ zu-soaba na n bool-a n yeel-a: ‹Sõgen yoogo, fo sẽn da tog n yao bũmb ningã, m basa fãa taale, f sẽn kosa yĩnga.
40018033	Mam sẽn zoe fo nimbãanega, fo me ra tõee lame n zoe f tũud-n-taaga nimbãanega.›
40018034	Zu-soaba sũur puuga wʋsgo la a kɩtame tɩ b yõk-a n kɩs kambõe naaba tɩ b nams-a tɩ samda wa yao zãnga.
40018035	Yaa woto la m Ba sẽn be arzãna na n maan ne yã, yãmb me sã n ka kõt y taab sugri ne pʋ-peelem.»
40019001	B sẽn kõ b koeesa Galile rãmb n sɛ, a Zezi yii be n dʋʋg Zʋrdẽ kʋɩlga n kẽ Zɩɩda soolmẽ,
40019002	Neb wʋsg pʋg-b lame la b sãoog-b la beenẽ.
40019003	Farizẽ rãmb kolgame n sok-ba la b sokra ra yaa bẽdgo: «Ned tõeeme n yiis a pag yaar bɩ?»
40019004	Tɩ b leoke: «Dɩlla yãmb pa karem tɩ sɩngrẽ Wẽnnaam naana rao ne paga
40019005	la b yeelame: ‹Raoã tog n basa a ba la a ma n zĩnd ne a paga la b yiiba tog n lebga bõn-yɛnga?›
40019006	B pa leb n ya yĩns a yiib ye, b yaa yĩng a ye. Bãng-y tɩ Wẽnd sẽn lagem bũmb ningã, ninsaal ka tog n welg-a ye.»
40019007	Farizẽ rãmba le sokame: «Yaa bõe yĩng marsã la a Moyiiz kõ noor tɩ b sã n na n yiis paga bɩ b kɩs-a a yiisg sebre?»
40019008	T'a Zezi yeele: «Yaa y tʋb-pa-wʋmdma yĩnga la a Moiz kõ-y sor tɩ y yiis y pagba; la baad-y da ka boto sɩngrẽ ye.
40019009	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet yãmba, tɩ sã n ka b mikame tɩ b zĩnd-n-taara yaa kisgu, rao ning sẽn dig a paga, n lɛɛg n dɩk a to, maanda yoob bala.»
40019010	Karen-biisa yeel-b lame: «Rao ne pag yell sã n ya a woto, dẽnd f sẽn ka kẽed kãadem n são!»
40019011	Tɩ b leoke: «Ka neb fãa n wʋmd dẽ ye, yaa Wẽnd sẽn kõ b rãmb bala.
40019012	Neb kẽer beeme n pa tõe n kẽ kãadem ye, tɩ b roga boto; kẽer beeme n pa tõe n kẽ kãadem tɩ Zamaana rãmb n wa ne gɩdgr kãnga; kẽer beeme n pa tõe n kẽ kãadem ye la yaa bãmb n tʋlg rẽ ne b yamleoogo, Arzãn Rĩunga yĩnga. Sẽn tõe-a n wʋm, bɩ a wʋm!»
40019013	Kom-bõoneg la b tall n wa a Zezi taoore tɩ b ning-b barka; b tẽega b nus b zutu n pʋʋs b yĩnga. Karen-biisa da rigda kambã.
40019014	Dẽ la a Zezi yeel-ba: «Bas-y kom-bõonegã tɩ b wa m nengẽ la y da rig-b ye tɩ yaa sẽn wẽnd-b bãmb bala n na n soog Arzãn Rĩungã.»
40019015	B tẽega b nus b zutu n yaool n le rɩk b sore.
40019016	Ade, ned n kolg a Zezi n sok-ba: «Karen-saamba, bõn-sõng bʋg la m na n maane, n paam vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ?»
40019017	T'a Zezi yeel-a: «Bõe yĩng la f sokd maam bõn-sõng poorẽ? Nin-yend bal la sõngo. F sã n dat n kẽ vɩɩmẽ, deeg Wẽnnaam noyã.»
40019018	T'a na n yeele: «Noy bʋse?» T'a Zezi leoke: «Da kʋ ye, da yo ye, da zu ye, da maan kaset-zirẽ ye,
40019019	waoog f ba la f ma, n paas yɛsa: nong f to n wẽnd f menga.»
40019020	Tɩ bi-bɩɩga na n yeele: «Mam deega rẽ fãa al m yãadmẽ. Bõe n ket marsã?»
40019021	T'a Zezi yeele: «Fo sã n dat n yɩ sõng zãnga, bɩ f kẽng n tɩ koos f sẽn tar fãa n pʋɩ naong rãmba tɩ f na paam dolb arzãnẽ, la wa pʋg maam.»
40019022	A sẽn wʋm dẽ, rasãnga looga ne sũ-sãanga t'a ra yaa rakãagre.
40019023	A Zezi yaool n yeela b karen-biisã: «Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ arzãn kõom na yɩ toog ne arzɛk soaba.
40019024	N-yẽe, m le togsd-y lame n paas tɩ yʋgemd sẽn na n tũ supĩim yõorẽ n looge yaa naana n yɩɩd arzɛk soaba sẽn na n kẽ Wẽnd Rĩunga pugẽ.»
40019025	Karen-biisa yɛɛsame, n yetẽ: «Sã n ya woto ãnda n na n põse?»
40019026	T'a Zezi ges-ba n yeel-ba: «Dẽ wẽnda toog ne ninsaala la Wẽnnaam nengẽ, bũmb pa toog ye.»
40019027	A Piyɛr goma woto: «Tõnd basa fãa n pʋg yãmba, bõe n na n yɩ tõnd dolbo?»
40019028	T'a Zezi yeele: «Sɩd-sɩda m yeta yãmb fãa sẽn pʋg maama, tɩ dũni tekr wakato, Ned Biiga sẽn wat n zĩnd a zɩɩr goeela zugu, yãmb me na zĩnd n yegl-ba, goeels piig la a yiib zutu, n kao Israyɛl sags piig la a yiiba bʋʋdo.
40019029	Ned ninga fãa sẽn na n bas a yiri, a yaopa, a tãopa, a ba, a ma, a kamba bɩ a pʋto, mam yĩnga, a na paam sẽn yɩɩd rẽnna, a na paam vɩɩm sẽn ka tar sɛɛbo.
40019030	Pipi rãmba wʋsg na n lebga poorẽ dãmba tɩ yaoolem dãmb wʋsg lebg pipi rãmba.
40020001	Arzãn Rĩunga wẽnda koaag soaba sẽn sãd beoogo n bao tʋʋm-tʋmdba sẽn na n fãs a bugsuntung sõng biisi.
40020002	Tɩɩsa soab yẽsa ne tʋʋm-tʋmdba t'a na n yao-b la waki koɛɛnga, raar a ye, n yaool n yeel-b marsã tɩ b kẽng tʋʋmna.
40020003	Sõor sẽn zẽke, a yãee neb a taaba sẽn zĩ zaalem tẽnga sʋka,
40020004	t'a yeel-ba: ‹Yãmb me kẽng tʋʋmna tɩ m na yao-y wa sẽn segde.›
40020005	B kẽngame. A le yii wĩnto-sʋka la zĩig sẽn maage n sed ne neb a taab me.
40020006	Wĩndg sẽn waa n kɩlle, a le yiime n tɩ yãe neb tɩ b zĩ, t'a yeel-ba: ‹Bõe yĩng tɩ y zĩ al beooga sẽn vẽegã n ka tʋm fɩ?›
40020007	B leoka woto: ‹Ned ba a ye ka rɩk tõnd tʋʋmd ye.› Tɩ tʋʋmda soab na n yeele: ‹Bɩ y me kẽng m tʋʋmna.›
40020008	Tʋʋmda sẽn sigi, bugsuntunga soab yeela sẽn gesa tʋʋmna: ‹Bool tʋʋm-tʋmdbã n kõ ned kam fãa a yaood, la sɩng ne yaoolem dãmbã n wat tõd-beoogẽ dãmbã.›
40020009	Sẽn yaool-b waoongã kolgame n deeg b wakɩr koɛɛnga.
40020010	Sẽn waa n ta pipi rãmbã, b tẽeme tɩ b na n paamame n yɩɩg b taaba, mik yaa koɛɛng a ye la bãmb me na n deege.
40020011	Dẽ la b reeg b wakirã la b guglumd ne tɩɩsa soaba:
40020012	‹Sẽn yaool n wa-ba tʋma wakat a ye bala la b paama wa tõnd sẽn sɩng yibeoogo, n nams tʋʋlgo.›
40020013	Tɩ bugsuntunga soab na n yeel bãmb nin-yende: ‹M zoa, m ka maan f zãmb ba bilfu; tõnd da seda wakɩ-koɛɛng daar a ye.
40020014	Deeg f wakirã n looge. Maam n dat la m kõ sẽn yaool-b waoongã wala foom;
40020015	fo yetame tɩ m ka tõe n maan m sẽn dat ne m sẽn so bɩ? Mam sẽn ya sõngã n wa ne fo sũ-kiiri bɩ?›
40020016	Ad-y yaa woto la pipi rãmba na n lebg poorẽ dãmba, tɩ poorẽ dãmba lebg pipi rãmba.»
40020017	Waa n yɩɩ tɩlɛ t'a Zezi leb Zerizalɛɛm tɩ b na peeg Tʋʋm-tʋmdba bala; la sor zugu b yeel-b lame:
40020018	«Tõnd dabda Zerizalɛɛm; b na n yõka Ned Biigã n kõ Maan-kʋʋdba kãsem dãmba la Noora sebr Mitba; bãmb na n kao-la b bʋʋdo n yeel tɩ b toga ne kũum.
40020019	B na n bas-b-la ne bu-zẽmbã, tɩ bu-zẽmba na n yaal ba, n pãb-b ne kaase, n ka-b pika. La b kũum dasm a tãab rare, b na n vʋʋgame.»
40020020	A Zebede kamba ma waa a Zezi taoore n wõgemd n na n kos bũmbu.
40020021	A Zezi sok-a lame: «Yaa bõe la f rata?» A yeelame: «Ad-m kamb a yiibã, sõng-y t'a ye zĩnd y rɩtgo, a ye y goabga, y Rĩunga pʋgẽ.»
40020022	Dẽ la a Zezi leok-a: «Yãmb ka mi y sẽn kot bũmb ning ye. Wamd ning mam sẽn na n tuglã, yãmb tõe n tugl-a lame bɩ?» B leokame: «N-yẽe! D tõeeme.»
40020023	T'a Zezi me na n paase: «Dɩlla y na yũ mam sẽn na n yũ bũmb ningã la kella a ye zĩnd m dɩtgo, a ye zĩnd m goabga, dẽ ka be me maam ye, tũuda m Ba sẽn kãab b rãmba.»
40020024	Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piiga kelga goama la b sũur puuga ne a Zebede kamb a yiibã.
40020025	A Zezi kosame tɩ b fãa kolge la b kõ-b-la koɛɛga: «Y miime tɩ bu-zẽmba nanams nongame n soog b nebã la b wẽoog-b kẽnkẽ.
40020026	Pa tog n yɩ boto yãmb nengẽ ye. Sẽn dat-a naam yãmb sʋka bɩ a yɩ yãmb sõgne.
40020027	Sẽn dat-a n yɩ pipi soab yãmb sʋka, bɩ a lebg yãmb yamba.
40020028	Dẽ n so tɩ Ned Biiga ka wa n na n dɩ naam, a waame n na n yɩ sõgne la a rɩk a vɩɩm n kõ neb wʋsgo, n fãag-ba.»
40020029	A Zezi waa n yita Zeriko tɩ neb wʋsg pʋgd-ba.
40020030	La ade, zoeens a yiib n da zĩ sora noore; b sẽn bãng tɩ yaa a Zezi n loogdã, b mooname: «Soaala, Daviid biiga, zoe-y d nimbãanega!»
40020031	Neba tãs-b lame tɩ b bas bʋʋre, tɩ bãmb na n nadg pãng n paas: «Soaala, Daviid biiga, zoe-y d nimbãanega!»
40020032	A Zezi yaasame; b bool-b lame n yeel: «Bõe la y rat tɩ m maan y yĩnga?»
40020033	Tɩ b yeele: «Soaala, kɩt-y tɩ d nina puki.»
40020034	B nimbãanega yõka a Zezi tɩ b rɩk b nug n sɩɩs b nina. Nina puka zĩ kãng bala tɩ b na n sɩng a Zezi pʋgbo.
40021001	B sẽn waa n kolg Zerizalɛɛm n ta Bɛtfaze la bala, Oliviye tãnga zug, a Zezi tʋma neb a yiibu.
40021002	B yeel-b lame: «Kẽng-y tẽnga sẽn tondã, tɩ y na yãe bõang b sẽn loe t'a biig yɛs a sɛɛgẽ; lok-y ba la y tall-b n wa kõ-ma.
40021003	B sã n sok-y bɩ y yeele tɩ yaa Soaala n tar b tʋʋmde, tɩ b na bas tɩ y loog ne-ba.»
40021004	B maana woto n na n taas bãngda koɛɛga:
40021005	«Yeel-y Siõ bi-pugla, ad-f dĩm sẽn wat f nengẽ, a sẽn ka baood faongã, a zomba bõanyãanga, a zomba zɩɩb-zɩt biiga.»
40021006	Sẽn tʋm b rãmba kẽngame.
40021007	B tɩ waa ne bõangã ne a biigã, wala Soaala sẽn togs-bã.
40021008	Karen-biisa rɩka b fut n palg bõeensã t'a Zezi zomb. Neb wʋsg sɩngame n yɛdg b fut sora zugu, tɩ kẽer kɛɛd tɩɩs wila n tʋɩt sorã.
40021009	Sẽn da be-b a Zezi taoor la b poorẽ da naaga taab n moonẽ: «A Daviid biiga paam pẽgre, kilill! Wẽnd sẽn tʋm a soaba paam pẽgre, b pẽgr kul sa-gãndo! Kilill!»
40021010	B sẽn poog Zerizalɛɛm la tẽnga sẽn wulumd ne bʋʋre tɩ ned kam fãa sokdẽ: «Yaa ãnda?»
40021011	Tɩ zãma wã na n leoke: «Yaa bãngd a Zezi, Galile Nazarɛt Zezi.»
40021012	A Zezi kẽe wẽnd doogẽ n dig sẽn da be-b be n koosdẽ la b raadẽ. B tusa sẽn da tekd-b ligda te-roagensã n lubi, n lub sẽn da koosd-b wala goeelse.
40021013	B yeelame: «B gʋlsa me: mam dooga na n boolame tɩ pʋʋsg roogo, la yãmb dɩk-a lame n maand fãadb roogo.»
40021014	Zoeens la wobs me waa n bʋʋg-b la wẽnd dooga pʋga la b sãoog-b lame.
40021015	Maan-kʋʋdba kãsem dãmba la Sɛb-mitba yãee bõn-bãna la b wʋma kom-bõonegã sẽn moonde: «A Daviid biiga paam pẽgre!» B sũur puuga wʋsgo.
40021016	B yeela a Zezi: «Y wʋmda kom-bãmba sẽn togsd bũmb ningã?» B leokame: «M wʋmda neere, la bas-y tɩ m soke, yãmb nan ka karem sẽn gʋlsa ye: ‹Pẽgr neerem yita kom-bõoneg la sẽn yẽsemd-b bĩisim noorẽ?› »
40021017	La a Zezi bas-b lame n kẽng Betani n tɩ gãand.
40021018	Yibeoog pĩnda b yii Betani n lebd Zerizalɛɛm, tɩ kom tar-b.
40021019	Tɩ b yãend kankang sora noore n bʋdg n ges-a, n mik tɩ yaa vãad bal la a yɛs ne. B yeela kankangã: «Fo kõn le wom biig bada.» Zĩig pʋgẽ bala, kankanga wẽneg n kʋɩɩme.
40021020	Dẽ yɛɛsa karen-biisã tɩ b sok tɩ maana a wãn tɩ kankanga wẽneg n kʋɩ vugr bala?
40021021	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ y sã n tar tẽeb sẽn ka mi sãmbg ba bilfu, ka mam sẽn maan kankanga bal la y na n tõog n maan ye; ba y sã n yeel tãngã sẽn tondã: ‹Yɩk n lʋɩ koomẽ wã›, na n yɩɩ boto.
40021022	Bũmb ning fãa y sẽn na n kos ne tẽeb kãsenga, y na n paam-a lame.»
40021023	A Zezi kẽe Wẽnd doogẽ n zãmsd nebã tɩ maan-kʋʋdba la tẽnga nin-kẽemb babs-b be n yeel-ba: «Sor bʋg la y paamyã n maand y sẽn maandã? Ãnda n kõ yãmb sorã?»
40021024	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Yaas-y tɩ m me sok-y bũmbu, bũmb a ye bala, la y sã n leok maam, mam me na wilg-y m sẽn paam sorã zĩig ninga n maand m sẽn maandã:
40021025	A Zã sooba yita yɛ? Wẽnnaam nengẽ bɩ ninsaalb nengẽ? Tɩ b na n yeel b sũurẽ: ‹Tõnd sã n leok t'a yita Wẽnnaam nengẽ, b na n sokame tɩ yaa bõe yĩng marsã la tõnd pa tẽ a Zã.
40021026	D sã n leok t'a yita ninsaal nengẽ, zãma wã beem na rɩ-do, tɩ neba fãa geta a Zã wa bãngda.›
40021027	Dẽ la b kong n yeel a Zezi tɩ b pa mi ye.» A Zezi leok-b lame: «Mam me kõn togs yãmba m sẽn paam ned ning sor ye.»
40021028	«Togs-y maam yãmb me sẽn tagsde: ned n da tar a kamb a yiibu. A yeela pipi soaba: ‹M biiga, kẽng rũnna n tɩ tʋm m pʋʋgẽ.›
40021029	T'a leoke: ‹M pa rabd ye.› La sẽn yɩ bilfu, a mikame tɩ ka neere, n tuubi, la a kẽnga pʋʋgẽ wã.
40021030	Ba wã goma ne a yiib soaba, tɩ yẽ leok: ‹M dabdame, m zu-soaba› n yaool n pa kẽng ye.
40021031	Bãmb b yiiba sʋka, ãnda n maan a ba raabo?» Tɩ b leoke tɩ yaa pipi biigã. A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yaa sɩd la m sẽn togsdã: fadg rɛɛsdba la pʋg-yoaadb na n lʋɩɩ y taoor Wẽnnaam Rĩunga pʋgẽ.
40021032	Ade, a Zã waa yãmb sʋk ne sõmblem la y pa tẽe-a ye, tɩ fadga rɛɛsdb la pʋg-yoaadb yaool n tẽe-a. Bãmb manes-sõnga ka kẽes tuubg bilfr menga y sũurẽ tɩ y sak n tẽ ye.
40021033	Kelg-y yelbũnd a to. Ned n da tar a pʋʋgo n sel bugsuntung sõngo, n wẽ yãgr n gũbg tɩɩsã, n maneg zĩig ning b sẽn na n wẽkd tɩɩsa biis tɩ lebg rãam, n ning gũudb ro-lug-lug a ye sʋka, n bao neb n gũnug pʋʋgã n bas n tog sore.
40021034	Tɩɩsa biis sẽn waa n kolg tõsbo, tɩɩsa soab tʋma a rakõapa tɩ b wa reeg biis n wa.
40021035	Sẽn get-b pʋʋga yõka rakõor a ye n pãbe, n kodg a ye, n lab a ye ne kuga.
40021036	Pʋʋga soab le tʋm a zak kamb a taaba; b sõor yɩɩga pipi rãmbã, la b maana ne bãmb wa b sẽn maan ne pipi rãmbã.
40021037	A kong n tʋma a meng biiga n yet a sũurẽ: ‹B na waoog m bigã.›
40021038	Mik bãmb sẽn yãe pʋʋga soab biiga, b yeelame: ‹Yẽ n na n soog a ba raboogo, dɩlla wa-y tɩ d kʋ-a n soog a paoongo.›
40021039	B yõka biigã n lob-a yãgra poore n kʋ-a.
40021040	Pʋʋga soab sã n wa, a na n maana a wãn ne gũudbã?»
40021041	Tɩ b leoke: «A na kɩt tɩ b ki kũ-toogo la a na bao neb a taab n gũnug a pʋʋgã, neb sẽn na n wa ne a pʋɩɩre, wakat fãa sẽn ta.»
40021042	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yãmb zɩ n karem sebr sõng pʋgẽ: ‹Kugr ning metba sẽn bas kɛɛngã, kug kãng n lebg rooga sũuri. Dẽ yaa Wẽnnaam tʋʋmde, la d neeme t'a toga ne pẽgre.›
40021043	M yet-y lame tɩ Wẽnd Rĩunga tʋʋmde, b na n deeg-a-la y nugẽ n kõ neb a taaba sẽn na n sõng t'a wom biisi. [
40021044	B sẽn gom kugr ninga yellã, f lʋɩɩ a zugu, f bũmb na kao, a lʋɩɩ f zugu bũmb na bedse.]»
40021045	Maan-kʋʋdba la Farizẽ rãmba sẽn wʋm goama, b bãngame tɩ yaa bãmb poorẽ la b togs boto.
40021046	B ra baood n na n yõk-b lame la b ra zoeta zãma wã, tɩ neba ra geta a Zezi wa bãngda.
40022001	A Zezi le sɩnga b yelbũna wẽebo:
40022002	«Arzãn Rĩung wẽnda dĩm a ye sẽn maan kibsa, a biig yikãadem yĩnga.
40022003	A yiisa sõgen-kamba tɩ b saa n bool neb tɩ b wa yikãadma la b sẽn bool b rãmba pa tʋlg waoong ye.
40022004	A tʋma kamb a taab yɛsa la a goma ne b woto: ‹Yeel-y m sẽn bool b rãmbã: Ade, kibsa rɩɩb seglame: lolse la dũm-wubdsa koodame, bũmb fãa beeme, wa-y yikãadma!›
40022005	B sẽn bool b rãmba maana wa b toog ka ye. Kẽer kẽng a b pʋtẽ, tɩ kẽer kẽng leebgo.
40022006	Kẽer yõga sõgen-kambã n nams-ba, n kʋ-ba.
40022007	Dĩma sũur puugame t'a yiis tãb-biisi tɩ b kʋ bãmb me la b yõog b tẽnga.
40022008	A yaool n yeela sõgen-kambã: ‹Dɩɩba segl n sɛɛme, la m sẽn bool b rãmba yɩɩ nin-yoodo.
40022009	Kẽng-y sotiisẽ, n kãas y sẽn yãe b rãmb fãa tɩ b wa kibsã.›
40022010	Sõgen-kamba yiime, n wool b sẽn paam b rãmb fãa sor zugu, nin-sõma la nin-wẽnse, n pids roogã.
40022011	Dɩma kẽe rɩɩba roogẽ n na n ges nebã la a mika ned a ye sẽn pa yeelg a sẽn tog n yeelg fuug ninga ye. A yeel-a lame:

40022014	Yaa kʋʋnga zãng la b boonda la bilfr bala n na n paam n kẽ b sẽn tũus b rãmba sʋka.»

40022017	Y ka bak nin-bedr ne nin-bil ye, dẽ la d kot tɩ y leok-do: togame bɩ ka toge tɩ d yao Rom naaba yaoodo?»

40022019	Wilg-y maam yaooda ligdi!» B kɩs-b la wakɩr koɛɛng a yembre.

40022022	A Zezi leokra ling-b lame tɩ b na n bas ba n looge.

40022024	«Soaala, a Moyiiz yeela woto: ‹Ned sã n ki n ka bas biiga, bɩ yaoã rɩk a kẽema pag n dog biig n kõ a kẽema.›
40022025	Ade, tõnd zamaanẽ wã neb a yopoe n zĩndi n da ya ba-biisi. Pipi soaba yii kãadem ne paga la a kiime n pa rog biig ye, n bas paga ne a ba-biig a yiib soabã.

40022028	Vʋʋgra raare, paga paada ne bʋgo, b fãa yɩla a sɩdb rãmb la?»
