40022030	Bãng-y tɩ vʋʋgr poore rao pa le rɩkd paga, la pag ka le kuiis rao ye, b vɩɩ wa malɛk rãmba sẽn vɩ toto arzãnẽ.
40022031	La yĩnsa vʋʋgr poorẽ, y pa karem gomd ning Wẽnd sẽn kõ-y wã la? B yeelame:
40022032	‹Maam la a Abraam Wẽnnaam, a Izaak Wẽnnaam, a Zakoob Wẽnnaam?› B pa kiid n pa vʋʋgdẽ rãmb Wẽnnaam ye, b yaa sẽn vɩ-b Wẽnnaam.»
40022033	A Zezi zãmsga pãng yɛɛsa sẽn wʋm-bã.
40022034	B sẽn wʋm t'a Zezi kʋɩdga Saduseẽ rãmba, Farizẽ rãmba me sũu taaba n wa.
40022035	B nin-yend soka a Zezi la sokra yɩɩ no-baoor meng-menga:
40022036	«Soaala, bʋg la no-kãsenga Wẽnnaam noya sʋka?»
40022037	T'a Zezi yeel-a: «Yaa nong Wẽnnaam, f Soaala, ne f sũur fãa, ne f sɩɩg fãa, nef yam fãa.
40022038	Yẽ la no-kãsenga la pipi soaba.
40022039	Sẽn pʋgda yẽ wẽnd-a lame, yaa nong f to wala f menga,
40022040	Noora la bãngdba sẽn togsa waa n soga noy bãmba b yiibã pʋgẽ.»
40022041	A Zezi sẽn mik tɩ Farizẽ rãmba ra tigma taab wʋsgã, bãmb me sok-b lame:
40022042	«Yamb yetame tɩ bõe, Wẽnd Nedã poorẽ? B yaa ãnda biiga?» Tɩ b leoke: «A Daviid biiga.»
40022043	Dẽ la a Zezi yeel yã: «Sɩngame tɩ bõe marsã t'a Daviid sẽn gomd ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng vẽnegr baas n boond-b tɩ Soaala:
40022044	‹Zu-soaba yeela m Soaala, zĩnd m dɩtgo tɩ m wa zõneg f bɛɛba fãa f taoore tɩ f teeg-b ne f nao?›
40022045	A Daviid sã n boond-b t'a Soaala, bãmb na n yɩ-la a wãn yɛsa n le yaa a Daviid biiga?»
40022046	Ned ba a ye ka tõog n leok-b tɩ bũmb ye. Badaar tɛk me, b pa le saag n bao b noor ye.
40023001	A Zezi yeela zãma wã la b karen-biisã:
40023002	«Noora Mitba la Farizẽ rãmba reega a Moyiiz karen-boko.
40023003	Dɩlla b sẽn yet bũmb ninga bɩ y reeg la y maan boto, b menga manesma bala la y ka tog n tũ. B yetame tɩ woto n toge la b ka maand ye.
40023004	B loeta zɩɩb bɛd n zɩlgd b taab bãgdo, la b menga nug-bil ka sɩɩsd-b ye.
40023005	B sẽn maand bũmb ninga fãa yaa sẽn na yɩlẽ tɩ neba yãend-b bala. Yaa woto la b loet b rĩir bɩ b kamse sɛb gãna, la basd b futa zerd wogd-wogdo.
40023006	B baooda pipi zĩiga, rɩɩb rotẽ la pʋʋsg rotẽ.
40023007	B nongame tɩ neb waoog-b kʋʋng sʋka, b nongame tɩ b bool-b tɩ karen-saamba.
40023008	Yãmb da saag n bas tɩ b bool-y tɩ karen-saamb ye, tɩ yãmb karen-saamb ya a ye bala la y fãa yaa ba-biisi.
40023009	Da bool-y ned ba a ye tɩ y ba tẽng zugu, tɩ y ba ya a ye tãa la yaa Ba ninga sẽn be-b arzãna.
40023010	Da saag-y n bas tɩ b bool-y tɩ zu-soab ye, tɩ yãmb tara zu-soab a ye tãa: yaa Krista.
40023011	Sẽn yɩɩd-a a taab yãmb sʋka na n yɩla a taab sõgne.
40023012	Sẽn zẽkd-a a menga, b na n sik-a lame. Sẽn sulgd-a a menga, b na n zẽk-a lame.
40023013	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, tɩ y pagda arzãn Rĩung neba taab yĩnga; yãmb n pa kẽede la y pa na n bas sẽn dat-ba me tɩ b kẽ ye. [
40023014	Yell na pak yãmba, Noora sebr mitba la yãmba, Farizẽ rãmba! Yãmb n pʋʋsde n ka yɛɛdẽ ye n yaool n sɛɛsd pʋg-kõap paoongo. Dẽ me la y sɩbgr na n zʋʋg y taab rẽnna.]
40023015	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, tɩ y rʋʋgda kʋɩlse la y saagda moog tõre n na n bao karen-biiga, la y sã n wa paam-a, y kɩtdame t'a tog ne bugum n yɩɩd yãmb naoor a yi.
40023016	Yell na pak yãmba, so-wilgdb sẽn ya zoeense, tɩ y yetame tɩ f sã n wẽen ne wẽnd doogo, ka ye, la f sã n wẽen ne wẽnd dooga sãnem, yaa moodgr tɩ f pids f pʋlemde.
40023017	Yam koees rãmba la zoeense, bõe n yɩɩde: sãnema bɩ wẽnd doogã sẽn kɩt tɩ sãnema lebg Wẽnd bũmbã?
40023018	Yãmb yetame yɛsa tɩ f sã n wẽen ne maan-kugri, ka ye, la f sã n wẽen ne maoongã sẽn dɩg a zugã, lebga pakre tɩ f pids f pʋlemde.
40023019	Zoeense, bõe n yɩɩde, maoongã bɩ maan-kugrã sẽn kɩt tɩ bũmb ning sẽn waa a zugu bɩ a lebg Wẽnd kũuna?
40023020	Fo sã n wẽen ne maan-kugrã, fo wẽena ne bũmb ning fãa sẽn dog a zugu.
40023021	Fo sã n wẽen ne wẽnd doogo, fo wẽena ne doogã la ne Wẽnd menga sẽn be a pʋgẽ.
40023022	Fo sã n wẽen ne yĩngri, f wẽena ne Wẽnnaam zaoorã la ne Wẽnnaam meng sẽn zao a zugu.
40023023	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, yãmb sakd n kɩta dʋr a ye piig zugu, y zẽ-vãad la y zẽ-biis sẽn tar yũ-noodo n yaool n basd Noora sẽn wilg bũmb niyns wa pakre n yɩɩdã, wala zemsgo, nimbãan-zoeere la pʋ-peelem. Dẽ n segdẽ pipi tɩ sẽn keta yaool n wa paasẽ.
40023024	Zoeens sẽn dat n wilg sore, ad-y y venda sẽn zem yʋgʋmde n yaool n yoogd zõaag n lobda.
40023025	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, yãmb nedgda wamd la lengr poore, t'a pʋg yaool n pid ne wagdem la yão-beed dẽgdo.
40023026	Zoeense, deng-y n pek-y wamda la lengra pʋga, n yaool n tõog n pẽg a poora neerem.
40023027	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, yãmb wẽnda yaad sẽn fẽ goore, yɩnga b yaa neere, la pʋgẽ wã b pida ne kõab la yũugu buud fãa.
40023028	Yãmb me yaa boto: yɩnga, neb nifẽ, yãmb wẽnda nin-tɩrse, la pʋgẽ, yãmb pida ne zãmbo la rẽgdo.
40023029	Yell na pak yãmba, Sɛb-mitba la Farizẽ, zãmb rãmba, yãmb meta bãngdba yaado la y manegd nin-sõma wã rẽnna,
40023030	n yetẽ: ‹Tõnd sã n da vɩɩnẽ d yaab rãmba wakato, d kõn naagẽ bãmb n daag bãngdba zɩɩm ye.›
40023031	La woto wã, y meng y toore n togs tɩ y yaa sẽn kʋ-b bãngdba yagense.
40023032	Aya! Modg-y n yɩɩg y saam-dãmba ne wẽnem!
40023033	Wiisi la wag-bi buudu, yãmb yɩta a wãn n põs bugum sɩbgre?
40023034	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m sẽn tʋmd y nengẽ bãngdba, sɩlem dãmba la sɛb-mitba; yãmb na n kʋʋ kẽere, n ka kẽer pika, n pãb kẽer pʋʋsg rotẽ, n dig-b tɩ b kẽ tẽng a ye tɩ y ta be n yis-ba.
40023035	La woto y na rɩ zɩɩm ning fãa sẽn daag tẽng taale, sẽn sɩng a ka-yell-soab a Abɛl zɩɩm, n ta a Zakari, a Baraki biigã, y sẽn kʋ wẽnd doogẽ, maan-kugra taoore.
40023036	Sɩd-sɩda, m yet-y lame, y zamaana na rɩ zɩ kãng fãa taale!
40023037	Zerizalɛɛm, Zerizalɛɛm sẽn kʋʋd bãngdba la f labd ne kuga b sẽn tʋm a soab fãa f nengẽ, m tʋlga naoor yaka n tigs f kamba wa noaag sẽn põgend a kamba, la kamba pa sak ye.
40023038	Ad-y y roogã na n lebga ro vɩʋʋgo.
40023039	M yet-y lame tɩ y kõn le yãend-m yɛsa n tãag y sẽn na n moon daare: ‹Wẽnd sẽn tʋm a soaba paam pẽgre!› »
40024001	A Zezi sẽn yi wẽnd doogẽ wã n looda, la b karen-biisa sẽn kolg n yeel-b tɩ b ges wẽnd dooga sẽn me to-to.
40024002	T'a Zezi leoke: «Y ka gesa rẽ fãa neer la? Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ kugr kõn pa kugra to zug ye, fãa na n sirgame.»
40024003	B sẽn waa n zĩ Oliviye tãnga zugu, a Zezi karen-biisa bal kolg-b lame n le sok-ba: «Soaala, d kotame tɩ y togs-do sẽn ya wakat ning la rẽ fãa na n yɩ la bũmb ning bũmb ning sẽn na n wilg y waoongo la dũni wã sɛɛbo.»
40024004	T'a Zezi na n yeel-ba:
40024005	«Maan-y gũusgu tɩ b ra wa tudg-y ye. Wʋsg na n zuka mam yʋʋre n wa yeelyã: ‹Mam la Wẽnd Nedã,› tɩ wʋsg na n tudg n tẽ.
40024006	Y na wʋm tɩ b gomd zabr yelle, zabr rãamde na lʋɩ y tʋbrẽ, la ra bas-y tɩ b bondg y yam ye.
40024007	Dẽ fãa na n sɩd zĩndame la nan ka rẽ la dũni sɛɛb ye. Tẽns na n yika zabr ne taaba, tɩ rĩung wulumd ne rĩung; kom na n lʋɩɩ ka la a lʋɩ ka, tẽng na n miimame,
40024008	la rẽ fãa nan yaa dogma waasg sɩngr bala.
40024009	B na n yõga yãmb n namse, n yõg-y n kʋ. Mam yĩnga dũni wã ninsaalb fãa na n kisg-y lame.
40024010	Wakat kãng la wʋsg na n lʋɩ. Wʋsg na n zãmba taaba la b na n dɩɩ beem ne taaba.
40024011	Zirẽ bãngdba na n yɩɩ ka tɛka n tudg neb wʋsgo.
40024012	Yel-wẽna sẽn paasd n dabd yĩnga, taab nonglem na n wooga wʋsg sũurẽ.
40024013	La sẽn na n modg-a n ka tol n lʋɩ, yẽ soab na põse.
40024014	Wẽnd Rĩunga Koe-noogã na n moana dũni fãa pʋgẽ, ninsaalb fãa yĩnga. Dẽ poor bala la dũni wã na n sɛ.
40024015	Y sã n wa ne Yel-yoog ninga a Daniyɛl sẽn goma t'a be wẽnd dooga pʋga (sẽn karemda ning pãng ne wʋmbo),
40024016	bɩ Zɩɩde rãmb zoe n dʋ tãmse;
40024017	sẽn be-a roog zugu bɩ a ra sig a roogẽ n nog a teed ye;
40024018	sẽn be-a pʋʋgẽ me ra lɛɛg n wa bao a fuug ye!
40024019	Yell na pak pagb niyns sẽn tʋt-b, bɩ sẽn tar b kamba sẽn ket bĩsrẽ wakat kãnga.
40024020	Pʋʋs-y tɩ y zoees da seg waood bɩ vʋʋsg daar ye.
40024021	Yel-beed ninga sẽn na n wa, wakat kãngã, wẽnem na n yɩɩga yel-beed niyns fã sẽn wa-b al dũni sɩngre n ta rũnna la b kõn le yãend a taar ye.
40024022	B sã n da ka boogẽ dasem kãens sõore, ned ba a ye kõn põsẽ ye, la nin-sõma wã yĩnga, daara sõor na n boogame.
40024023	Ned sã n yeel yãmba: ‹Ade, Krista bee ka,› bɩ: ‹Ade, b bee ka sẽnẽ,› bɩ y ra tẽ ye.
40024024	Zirẽ-be-krist rãmba la zirẽ-be-bãngdba na n yikame n maan makre la bõn-bãn wʋsgo sẽn na n tudgẽ nin-sõma wã mense, dẽ sã n da tõẽ.
40024025	Ade, m wilg-y la woto tɩ y bãng tiiri.
40024026	Dɩlla b sã n yeelyã: ‹Ned Biiga bee weoogẽ bɩ y ra kẽng ye.› B sã n yeele: ‹B soonda ka,› bɩ y ra tẽ fɩ.
40024027	Wala saag bugum sẽn yãngd yaanga n wẽneg n ta taoore, Ned Biiga waoong na n yɩɩ boto.
40024028	Ad-y kɩɩng rɩgr kõn solg yibreg ye.
40024029	Yel-beed kãens poore, wĩntoog na n sobame, kiuug ka na n le kõ vẽenem ye, ãds na n dʋʋgame, bũmb fãa na n yogsa a zĩigẽ yĩngri.
40024030	Wakat kãng la Ned Biiga makr na n puk yĩngri tɩ Adem biig fãa tood a yãoogo. B na yãend Ned Biiga tɩ b zao sawato n sigd ne pãng la zɩɩr kãsenga.
40024031	B na n yiisa b malɛk rãmba ne tõntõog sẽn kũmd wʋsgo tɩ b tigim dũni wã taoor la a yaang nin-sõma zãnga.
40024032	Kelg-y kankang yelbũndi. A sã n tãood wil poala la a tobd vã-miinim, y miime tɩ tʋʋlg kolgame.
40024033	Woto-me y sã n yãe yell kãensa fãa bɩ y bãng tɩ Ned Biiga wata a naam dɩɩbo.
40024034	M yet-y lame tɩ zamaan kãnga kamb kõn loog tɩ m sẽn wilga fãa ka taas ye.
40024035	Yĩngr la tẽng na n loogame, la mam sẽn togsa na n yalsame.
40024036	Dũni sɛɛb daare la a wakato ned ba a ye ka mi ye, sã n ka Ba: ned ka mi, malɛk ka mi, Ned Biiga ka mi.
40024037	Sẽn zĩnd a Nowe wakatã n na n wilg-d Ned Biiga waoong sẽn na n yɩɩ a soaba.
40024038	Sa-kẽenga sẽn waa n dag n nan ka ni wã, b ra rɩtame la b yũuda, tɩ rap rɩgsd pagba, tɩ pagb kuiis rapa. Yɩɩ woto n tãag a Nowe sẽn kẽ koom koglg kẽenga raare.
40024039	Neba ra pa tẽed tɩ bũmb na maan ye, n tãag sa kẽengã sẽn wa n loog ne b fãa gilli. Ned Biiga waoong me na n yɩɩ boto.
40024040	Rap a yiib na n kooda pʋʋgẽ, tɩ b yãk a ye n bas a ye;
40024041	pagb a yiib na n werda neerẽ, tɩ b yãk a ye n bas a ye.
40024042	Maan-y gũusgu tɩ y ka mi y Zu-soaba waoong raar ye.
40024043	Tags-y neer tɩ zak soab sã n da miẽ sẽn ya wakat ning la wagdr na n waẽ yʋngo, a kõn gũsẽ ye, a kõn basẽ tɩ b poog a roog ye.
40024044	Yãmb me, bob-y n dõbẽ tɩ yaa wakat ning yãmb sẽn pa tẽedã la Ned Biiga na n wa.
40024045	M ba bõe la sõgen sõngo la yẽesenga, t'a zu-soaba rɩk a zak n gũnug-a, t'a kõt zaka rãmb rɩɩbo, wakat sẽn ta?
40024046	Zu-noog soab la sõgen kãnga, a zu-soaba sã n yi sor n wa mik t'a maanda boto.
40024047	Sɩda m yet-y lame t'a na gũnug-a a paoong fãa.
40024048	La Sõgna sã n ya sõgen yoogo, n yeel a sũurẽ: ‹M zu-soaba kaoosda waoongo›,
40024049	t'a na n yik n pãbd a taaba, n na n dɩtẽ la a tɩgd rãam ne rã-yũudba,
40024050	yaa daar ning la wakat ning a sẽn pa tẽedã la a zu-soaba na n wa;
40024051	a na yiis-a, a na tɩ naag-a ne zãmb rãmba; be yaa yãbre la yẽn kẽrsg zĩiga.
40025001	Arzãn Rĩung na n wẽnega pʋg-sɛdb piig sẽn yi ne b fitils n na n tɩ seg yikãad paalga.
40025002	Bãmb sʋka, pʋg-sɛdb a nu n ya yalemse, t'a nu ya yẽesense.
40025003	Yalemsa dɩka b fitils la b pa tẽeg n sui kaam n zɩ ye.
40025004	Yẽesensã dɩka b fitils la b tẽeg n zɩɩ kaam, la-bõones pʋga.
40025005	Pʋg-sɩd sẽn kaoos waoongo, b fãa sɩnga suusgu, n wa baas ne gõeem.
40025006	Yʋn-sʋka, b wʋmame tɩ b moonda: ‹Ad pʋg-sɩda, yik-y tɩ d seg-a.›
40025007	Pʋg-sɛdba fãa nekame tɩ ned kam fãa na n yõgen a fitila.
40025008	Yalemsa yeela yẽesensã: ‹Sõng-y-d ne kaam tɩ d fitilsa kiidame!›
40025009	Tɩ bãmb na n leok-ba: ‹Kaama ka tõe n sek tõnd ne yãmb ye, kẽng-y raagẽ n tɩ ra.›
40025010	Bãmb me sẽn kẽng raabo la pʋg-sɩda sẽn ta, tɩ sẽn tar-b kaama naag n kẽ kibsa roogẽ, tɩ kʋɩleng wẽneg n page.
40025011	Yalemsa lɛɛg n waame n yetẽ: ‹Soaala, soaala, pak-y tɩ d kẽ!›
40025012	T'a na n zĩnd pʋgẽ n leoke: ‹Mam ka mi yãmb ye.›
40025013	Sõng-y n da gũs ye tɩ y ka mi raare la wakat ye.
40025014	Yaa wala ned sẽn togd sore n bool a rakõapa n dɩk a laog n gũnug-ba.
40025015	A kɩsa a ye, sãnem gil a nu, a to wã a yiibu, a tãab soaba a ye: ned kam fãa ne a dabaar sẽn tõe to-to la a loogame. La ka yãee n kaoos ye,
40025016	sẽn deeg-a sãnem gil a nu wã tɩ leebame n dok a nu.
40025017	Sẽn deeg-a a yiibã maana rabaare a me roka a yiibu.
40025018	Sẽn deeg-a a ye wã tɩ tuka boko n bus zu-soaba ligdi.
40025019	Sẽn waa n kaoose, zu-soaba lɛɛg n waame la b zĩndame n maan b geelse.
40025020	Sẽn dag n deeg-a a nu wã n dogl a nu wã kolg n yeelame: ‹M zu-soaba, yãmb da basa ne maam sãnem gil a nu la ade, m paama a nu n paase.›
40025021	Tɩ zu-soaba na n leok-a: ‹Yaa neere, sõgen sõng la ka mi kʋɩɩm soaba, fo sẽn ka maan kʋɩɩm ne sẽn pa zem bũmbã, bũmb wʋsgo la m na n gũnug-fu; wa naag f zu-soabã n kɩdme.›
40025022	Sãnem gila yiiba soab n pʋge la a yeelame: ‹M zu-soaba, y da basa ne-m sãnem gil a yiibu, la ade, m paama a yiib n paas.›
40025023	Zu-soaba leok-a lame: ‹Yaa neere, sõgen sõng la ka mi kʋɩɩm soaba, fo sẽn pa maan kʋɩɩm ne sẽn pa zem bũmbã, bũmb wʋsg la m na n gũnug-fu; wa naag f zu-soabã n kɩdme.›
40025024	Sẽn deeg-a a ye wã me waame n yeel: ‹M zu-soaba, m paam n bãnga yãmb neere wala ned sẽn baood ne a sũuri; yãmb kẽebda y sẽn pa bʋdẽ, la y wʋkda y sẽn pa yedgẽ.
40025025	Dẽ n kɩt tɩ m zoe rabeem n dɩk y sãnema n bus tẽnga, la ade, deeg-y y soolem.›
40025026	Dẽn la zu-soaba leok yã: ‹Nin-yoogo la kʋɩɩm daolgo, fo ra mii tɩ m kẽebda m sẽn pa bʋdẽ, la m wʋkda m sẽn pa yɛdgẽ,
40025027	bõe yĩng la f pa rɩk m ligdã n bas ligd tɛkd nengẽ, woto m sẽn waẽ wã, m deegdẽ la m dẽnd zugu tɩ roaglg le paas.
40025028	Deeg-y nin-kãnga sãnem gilgã n kõ sẽn tar-a piiga soaba.
40025029	Sẽn tar-a, b kõt-a lame t'a pʋɩɩr fɩɩge, la sẽn ka tar-a wʋsgo, b na reeg bilfrã a sẽn tarã.
40025030	La yõk-y bõn-yaalgã n lob yɩnga, likẽ, yãbr la yẽn kẽrsg zĩigẽ.›
40025031	Ned Biiga wat n siga ne zɩɩr kãsenga, t'a malɛk rãmb yãagd-a. Wakat kãng la b na n zĩnd b naama zaoor zugu.
40025032	Ninsaalb fãa na n tigma b taoore tɩ b welg-ba wa rũm-kɩɩm sẽn bakd pe-yãans ne boeese.
40025033	B na n ninga pe-yaansa rɩtgo, n ning boeesã b goabga.
40025034	Dĩma na n yeela sẽn beb rɩtgã: ‹Wa-y wɛ, m Ba sẽn bark b rãmba, n deeg pʋɩɩr b Rĩunga pʋgẽ, Rĩung ning b sẽn segl y yĩng al dũni sɩngrẽ.
40025035	Ade, kom yõka maam la y rɩlg-m lame, ko-yũud yõk-m lame la y kõ-m lame tɩ m yũ; m yɩɩ sãana la y maan-m la sãando.
40025036	M yɩɩ m zaala la y kõ-m la fuugu, m yɩɩ bãada la y waa n pʋʋs-m la tarem; b kẽes-m la roogo la y wa n ges-m lame.›
40025037	Wakat kãnga nin-sõma na n leok-b lame: ‹Soaala, da-bʋr la tõnd mik tɩ kom tar yãmba tɩ d kõ-y rɩɩbo, tɩ ko-yũud tar-y, tɩ d kõ-y koom,
40025038	tɩ y ya sãana tɩ d maan-y sãando, tɩ ya y zaala tɩ d yeelg-y fuugu,
40025039	bãad bɩ bi-bees roogẽ neda tɩ d wa ges yãmba?›
40025040	La dĩma na n yeelame: ‹Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ y bãng tɩ y sẽn maan dẽ ne m yaopa fãa yao zʋʋga, yaa mam meng la y maan yã.›
40025041	Dẽ poore b na n yeela b goabg rãmbã: ‹Zãag-y ne maam, ka bark rãmba, n lʋɩ bugum sẽn ka kiid abada pʋgẽ, b sẽn segl Sʋtãana la a tũud-n-taas yĩnga.
40025042	Ade, kom yõka maam la y pa kõ-m tɩ m dɩ ye, ko-yũud yõk-m lame la y pa kõ-m tɩ m yũ ye,
40025043	m yɩɩ sãana la y pa maan-m sãand ye, m yɩɩ m zaala la y pa kõ-m fuug ye, m yika pa-keem, la b pag-m la roogo la y pa lɩk n ges-m ye.›
40025044	Dẽ la b me na n sok-ba: ‹Soaala, wakat bʋgo la y tall kom la ko-yũudu, la y yɩ sãan, la y zĩnd y zaal, la y yik pa-keem bɩ b kẽes-y la roogo, tɩ tõnd pa tol n sõng yãmba?›
40025045	B na n leok-b lame: ‹Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ y sẽn pa maan bũmb ning fãa ne mam yaopa yao zʋʋg ba a ye, yaa mam meng la y mong yã.›
40025046	La bãmb na n kẽnga namsg sẽn ka sɛt zĩigẽ tɩ nin-sõma wã kẽng vɩɩm sẽn ka sɛɛb zĩigẽ.»
40026001	A Zezi sẽn gom woto n sɛ la b sẽn yeel b karen-biisã:
40026002	«Y miime tɩ pak keta rasem a yiibu, la b na n yõka Ned Biiga n kɩs tɩ b ka-b pika.»
40026003	Maan-kʋʋdba kãsem dãmba la tẽnga nin-kẽemba tigma taaba maan-kʋʋd kãseng a Kaif zakẽ.
40026004	B yẽsa ne taaba sɩlem ning b sẽn na n sɩlem n paam n yõk a Zezi n kʋ.
40026005	B yalsa woto: «Ka tog tɩ yɩ kibsa pʋgẽ ye tɩ tẽnga na n wa naag n wulumdame.»
40026006	A Zezi da bee Betani, wãoor a Simo zakẽ.
40026007	La pag n kolg-b ne a yubla, kug peesem yubl neere; yaa kaam sẽn tar yũ-noog wʋsgo la sẽn koosd toogo n da be a pʋgẽ. Paga sudga kaama a Zezi zug. Wakat kãng tɩ b ra rɩtame.
40026008	Karen-biisa yãee rẽ n puug b sũuri n yetẽ: «Yaa bõe tɩ b sãamd bõn-sõng a woto?
40026009	B ra tõe n koosa kaama n paam ligd wʋsgo n kõ naong rãmba.»
40026010	A Zezi wʋmame n yeel-ba: «Bõe tɩ y maan mo-beed ne pʋg kãngã? Yaa tʋʋmd sõng la a tʋm mam yĩnga.
40026011	Y na kell n yãe naong rãmb y sʋka la mam ka na n kell n pa y sʋk ye.
40026012	Paga sẽn daag yũ-noogã m zugã, yaa mam mumb la a sɩɩl n wilgi.
40026013	Sɩd-sɩda m yet-y lame tɩ zĩig ning fãa kibar kãnga sẽn na n taẽ, dũni wã fãa pʋgẽ, b na tẽeg n gom n pẽg paga sẽn maam marsã wã.»
40026014	Yaa wakat kãng la Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiiba nin-yend sẽn boond t'a Zɩɩda, Iskariyot tẽng neda, kẽng maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb nengẽ n tɩ yeel-ba:
40026015	«Bõe la y na n kõ-m tɩ m yõk-ba n kõ yãmba?» B kõ-a-la wakɩ koeems pistã.
40026016	Dẽ tɛka a sɩng n baooda a sẽn na n bẽd bũmb ning n yõk-b n kɩse.
40026017	Bur sẽn ka le ningd bɩlla pipi raare, la karen-biisa waa n sok a Zezi: «Y ratame tɩ d segl pak rɩɩb yɛɛlẽ?»
40026018	B leokame: «Kẽng-y tẽnga pʋgẽ, a Zagl nengẽ n yeel-a: ‹Zagla, Soaala tɩ d wilg-fu: Mam wakat taame, la yaa fo zakẽ la m na dɩ pak rɩɩbo ne m karen-biisã.› »
40026019	Karen-biisa kẽngame n maan wa a Zezi sẽn yeele la b segla pakã.
40026020	Zaabr taame tɩ b kẽ ne b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã n na n dɩ.
40026021	Rɩɩba wakato b yeelame: «Sɩd la m togsda, yãmb nin-yend n na n yõk maam n kõ m bɛɛba.»
40026022	Sũ-sãang bondga b Tʋʋm-tʋmdba yam tɩ b na n sok, a yeyn-ye: «Soaala, na n yɩɩ maam bɩ?»
40026023	Tɩ b leoke: «Sẽn naagd-a maam n tʋmd laagẽ wã, yaa yẽ n na n zãmb-ma!
40026024	Ned Biiga lebre na n yɩɩ wa b sẽn gʋlse la yell na pak ned ning sẽn na n zãmba wã. A sẽn ka waẽ moogo n sãoẽ a yĩnga!»
40026025	Sẽn waa n ta a Zɩɩda, ned ning sẽn na n yõk-b n kɩs bɛɛbã, yẽ me sokame: «Wat n yɩɩ maam bɩ, Soaala?» La a Zezi leok-a lame: «Fo togs n sɛɛme.»
40026026	B sẽn waa n dɩtẽ, a Zezi rɩka buri, n pʋʋs bark pʋʋsgo, n wes burã n kõ b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã n yetẽ: «Deeg-y n dɩɩ-y, woto yaa mam yĩnga.»
40026027	Dẽ poore yaa laog neer la b rɩk yã la b sẽn pʋʋs barka, b kɩs-a-la b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã n yetẽ:
40026028	«Yũ-y, yãmb fãa, tɩ woto yaa m zooda zɩɩm, zood sẽn yõg ne zɩɩma m sẽn daag neb fãa yĩnga, b yel-wẽna sugr yĩnga.
40026029	La sɩd wa m sẽn yetã, m kõn leb n yũ bugsuntung sõng biis rãam n tãag raar ning m sẽn lebd n wa yũ a rã-paalgã ne yãmba, m Ba Rĩunga pʋgẽ.»
40026030	B sẽn yɩɩl n sɛ, b rɩka Oliviye tãng sore.
40026031	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yʋnga bala m na n yɩɩ kugr ninga y fãa sẽn na n lak n lʋɩ. B gʋlsame: ‹M na n wẽe pe-kɩɩma la piisa fãa na n sẽegame.›
40026032	La m vʋʋgr poore, m na reng-y Galile tẽnga.»
40026033	A Piyɛr yeelame: «Ba b fãa gill sã n na n lak yãmb wa kugr n lʋɩ, kõn yɩ maam ye.»
40026034	T'a Zezi na n leok-a: «Sɩd wa m sẽn yetã, yʋnga bala, no-raoog sẽn wat n nan ka kelem dẽ tɩ f yeela naoor a tã tɩ f ka mi maam ye.»
40026035	T'a Piyɛr na n leoke: «Ba m na naag yãmb n ki, m kõn yeel tɩ m ka mi-y ye.» Taaba fãa me yeela boto.
40026036	B waa n taa zĩig a ye sẽn boond tɩ Zɛtsemani t'a Zezi yeel b karen-biisã: «Yaas-y ka tɩ m ta taoor n pʋʋs.»
40026037	B boola a Piyɛr la a Zebede kamb a yiibã. Wakat kãnga sũ-sãang la yĩnsirg yõk-b lame,
40026038	tɩ b yeele: «Sũ-sãang n na n kʋ-ma, yaas-y ka n pak-ma.»
40026039	B sẽn zãag bilfu, b lʋɩɩ b yãnvabga n sɩng pʋʋsg woto: «M Ba, sã n tõe, bɩ y kɩt tɩ tooga zãag ne maam. La ade, ka mam daab n so taoor ye, yaa yãmb dẽnna.»
40026040	B sẽn leb b karen-biisa nengẽ, b mikame tɩ b gõe, tɩ b yeel a Piyɛr: «Woto yãmb pa tõog n pak maam wakat yɛng menga?
40026041	Bas-y gõeem la y pʋʋs n da lʋɩ ye tɩ ninsaal sũur data la a pãng paooda.»
40026042	B le zãagame yɛsa n na n pʋʋse: «M Ba, tooga sã n ka tõe n zãag tɩ m pa yũ-a bɩ yɩ wa y sẽn date.»
40026043	B le lɛɛg n waame n le mik tɩ karen-biisa gõe: b nina ra zɩsga ne gõeem.
40026044	B bas-b lame n le zãag n na n pʋʋs, naoor a tãab soaba, wala b sẽn da zoe n pʋʋse.
40026045	Dẽ poore b lɛɛgame n wa yeel-ba: «Y tõe n gũsame marsã, n vʋʋse. Ned Biiga sẽn na n lʋɩ yel-wẽn-maandba nusẽ wakat taame.
40026046	Yik-y tɩ d looge tɩ sẽn na n kɩta tɩ b yõk maama waame bala!»
40026047	A Zezi ka paam n gom n sɛ ye, t'a Zɩɩda, Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiiba nin-yende, wẽneg n poog ne neb ka tɛka sẽn zãad sʋʋs la rasaba; yaa maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb la tẽnga nin-kẽembã n da yiis-b.
40026048	Zãmbda ra kõ-b-la makr kãngã: «M sẽn na n mobg a soab wala m zoa wã, yaa yẽnda, yõk-y yẽe.»
40026049	A sɩd kolga a Zezi n yetẽ: «Soaala, m pʋʋsda!» La a mobg-b lame,
40026050	t'a Zezi yeel-a: «M zoa, maan f tʋʋmde.» Tɩ neba na n kolg marsã n yõk-ba.
40026051	A Zezi tũud-n-taasa nin-yend taka a sʋʋg n wõog, la a kɛɛ maan-kʋʋd kãsma sõgen a ye tʋbre n fiuug.
40026052	T'a Zezi na n yeel-a: «Lebs f sʋʋga a wʋʋgẽ tɩ sẽn zãada sʋʋg fãa, sʋʋg n kʋʋd-a.
40026053	F tẽedame tɩ m ka tõe n yõk m Ba sɛɛga, tɩ b ko maam mars-marsã bala, malɛk rãmb sẽn taẽ tus kobs-yopoe la a yi?
40026054	La sẽn gʋls tɩ kall tɩ yɩ boto wã maandẽ-la a wãn n taase?»
40026055	B lɛɛg n goma ne zãma wã: «Mam yaa so-gɩt laa, tɩ y yi ne sʋʋs la rasaba n na n yõk ma? Beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa m da zĩi wẽnd doogẽ n zãmsd-y la y ka yõk-m ye.
40026056	Yɩɩ woto tɩ sẽn gʋls Sebr pʋgẽ tõog n pidsi.» Wakat kãnga karen-biisa fãa bas-b lame n zoe.
40026057	Sẽn yõk-ba a Zezi wã tall-b lame n kẽng maan-kʋʋd kãseng a Kayif nengẽ; be, Sɛb-mitba la nin-kẽembã waa n tigma taaba.
40026058	A Piyɛr da pʋgda yɩɩg-yɩɩga n wa ta maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yiri; a tol n kẽe pʋgẽ n zĩnd ne sõgen-kambã n na n ges yella sẽn na n baas to-to.
40026059	Bãng-y tɩ maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb ne bʋʋda rãmba da baooda rõadga n na n dõd a Zezi n paam n kʋ-ba la ra ka naana ye.
40026060	Sẽn wa-ba yaool n yɩɩ wʋsgo. Baasgo neb a yiibu n ta
40026061	n togs woto: «Nin-kãnga yeelame: ‹M tõeeme n wã wẽnd doogã n lebs n me-a ra-yɩten-daare.› »
40026062	Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yikame n yeel a Zezi: «Fo ka leokd tɩ bũmbu, bõe la b yet tɩ foo n maane?»
40026063	T'a Zezi sĩnd b noore. Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yeel-b lame: «M kot-f lame tɩ f togs-do sã n yaa foom la Krista, Wẽnnaam Biigã.»
40026064	A Zezi leok-a lame: «F togs n sɛɛme, la m yet-y lame tɩ y na n yãee Ned Biiga t'a zĩ Wẽnnaam pãng soab rɩtgo, n zao sawadgo n sigd tẽnga.»
40026065	Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga kẽesa a fut n yetẽ: «A tʋʋsa Wẽnde, d le baooda kaset dãmb n na n maan bõe? Yãmb sẽ n ka wʋme, a tʋʋsa Wẽnde.
40026066	Y yetame tɩ bõe?» B naaga taab n leoke: «A toga ne kũum.»
40026067	B sɩngame n tʋbsd b neng kolkoodo la b pãbd-b pegse; kẽer da soosd n pãbd-b lame la b yetẽ:
40026068	«Bãng wɛ, Wẽnd Nedã, ãnda n wẽ foom?»
40026069	A Piyɛr da zĩi zakẽ tɩ yem-poak a ye kolg n sok-a: «Foo, fo ra ka be ne Galile Zezi wã?»
40026070	A Piyɛr kɩɩsa neba fãa taoore n yetẽ: «Ad mam ka mi fo sẽn dat n yeel tɩ bũmb ning ye.»
40026071	A Piyɛr sẽn serge n lebd dignoorẽ, la yem-poak a to sẽn yãe-a n yeel neb a taaba: «Ad-y nin-kãnga ra bee ne a Zezi, Nazarɛt Raoã.»
40026072	La a Piyɛr le kɩɩsame la a wẽnnẽ: «Mam pa mi nin-kãnga ye.»
40026073	Sẽn yɩ bilfu, zaka noor dãmb kolga a Piyɛr n yeel-a: «Kɩɩsg ka ye, fo ra tũud-a lame, fo goama bal n lukd f bãongo.»
40026074	T'a Piyɛr tar kɩɩsgo la wẽenego: «Mam ka mi nin-kãnga ye.» La no-raoog wẽneg n kelmame.
40026075	A Piyɛr tẽega Krista sẽn da yeelã: «Noaag ne a na n kelem tɩ f yeela naoor a tã tɩ f ka mi maam ye.» La a yiime la a kiigd nintãm.
40027001	Beoog sẽn vẽege, maan-kʋʋdba la nin-kẽemba le tigma taaba la yaa b yẽsgã na baas ne a Zezi kũum bala.
40027002	B sẽba a Zezi n tall-ba n tɩ bas ne a Pilat tɩ yẽ n da ya kombere.
40027003	Zãmb soab a Zɩɩda sẽn bãng tɩ b paalga a Zezi bʋʋdo, a zaba ne a menga n tall sãnem wakɩ pistã wã n wa lebs maan-kʋʋdba la tẽnga nin-kẽembã,
40027004	n yetẽ: «Ade, m kongame n kɩt tɩ b na n daag ned sẽn ka tar a toorẽ yell zɩɩm.» La b yeel-a lame: «Dẽ ka pak tõnd ye, foo n na bãnge.»
40027005	T'a na n lob ligda wẽnd doogẽ la a yi n tɩ luul.
40027006	B sẽn wʋk ligdã, la maan-kʋʋdba sẽn yeele: «Ligd kãnga ka tõe n yɩ wẽnd doog ligd ye, t'a yaa zɩɩm ligdi.»
40027007	B yẽsa ne taaba la b rɩka ligdã n da yagda pʋʋgo n na n mumd sãamba.
40027008	Yaa rẽnd me yĩnga la al ba rũnna b ket n boonda pʋʋgã tɩ «Zɩɩm pʋʋgo.»
40027009	Woto taasa bãngda Zeremi gomde: B rɩka wakɩ pistã wã, Israyɛl kamb sẽn da saag sẽn zʋʋga saagrã
40027010	la b raa yagd pʋʋgo, wala m Soaala sẽn wilg-ma.
40027011	B talla a Zezi n ta kombera taoore tɩ yẽ na n sok-ba: «Yaa foo la Zʋɩf rãmba dĩma bɩ?» T'a Zezi na n leok-a: «Fo togsame.»
40027012	Maan-kʋʋdba kãsẽm-dãmb la nin-kẽemba ra rõt-b lame tɩ b sĩnda.
40027013	Dẽ la a Pilat le sok-ba: «Fo ka wʋmd b sẽn togsd f poorẽ laa?»
40027014	La a Zezi ka leok-a tɩ bũmb ye, al t'a Pilat yɛɛs wʋsgo.
40027015	Yʋʋmd-yʋʋmd fãa, kibsa yĩnga, a Pilat da mii n yiisda bi-bɛɛg a ye roogo, la yaa tẽnga rãmb sẽn kos tɩ b yiis a soaba.
40027016	Mik bi-be-maasr a ye n dag n be roogẽ yʋʋmd kãnga t'a yʋʋr boond tɩ Barabas.
40027017	Dẽ la a Pilat sok zãma wã: «Bʋg la y rat tɩ m yiis roog n base, a Barabas bɩ a Zezi, b sẽn boond a soab tɩ Krista?»
40027018	A yaool n mii neere tɩ yaa sũ-kiir yĩng bala la b yõk a Zezi.
40027019	A Pilat paga tʋmame tɩ b wa yeel-a bʋʋda zĩigẽ: «Da lʋɩɩs f toog yell kãnga pʋgẽ ye tɩ yaa nin-tɩrga; yʋngẽ m zãmsa a poorẽ la ka yɩ-m noog ye.»
40027020	Maan-kʋʋdba kãsẽm-dãmb la tẽnga nin-kẽemba sagla zãma wã tɩ b kos a Barabas la b kɩt tɩ b kʋ a Zezi.
40027021	Dẽ la Kombera sok-ba: «Ãnda la y rat tɩ m base?» B leokame t'a Barabas.
40027022	A Pilat yeel-b lame: «La a Zezi, b sẽn boond a soab tɩ Krista, m maanda yẽ soab bõe?» Tɩ b fãa leoke: «Ka-y yẽe pika!»
40027023	T'a Pilat me leok ba: «Bõe la a maanyã tɩ ya wẽnga?» La b naaga taab n moon tɩ yɩɩd pĩnda: «Ka-y yẽe pika.»
40027024	A Pilat sẽn mik t'a makda zaalem la bʋʋra bal n wulumd n dabda, a rɩka koom n nudg a nus neba fãa nifẽ la a yetẽ: «M yiisa m toog zɩ kãnga raagrẽ, yãmb n na bãnge.»
40027025	B le naaga taab n yeele: «Bɩ a zɩɩma taal pa d zug la d kamba zugu.»
40027026	A Pilat kong n basa a Barabas; a kɩtame tɩ b pãb a Zezi la a kõo neba sore tɩ b ka-b pika.
40027027	A Pilat tãb-biisa talla a Zezi n kẽ bʋʋdba sikẽ la neb sẽn ta kobs-yoob gũbg-b lame.
40027028	B yeega b fuugã n yeelg-b fu miuugu, n gõd gõos gʋle n teeg b zugu; n bao kãnkãr n ning b nugẽ, (wa naam dasaare) n yĩgimd b taoor marsã n laad ba:
40027029	«Y zĩig be neere, Zʋɩf rãmb dĩma!»
40027030	B ra tʋbsda b nenga kolkoodo la b mii n deeg kãnkãrã n va b zugu.
40027031	B sẽn waa n yaal-ba n tɩge, b yeega fu-miuugã n yeelg-b b meng fuugu, la b tall-b lame n na n tɩ ka pika.
40027032	B sẽn waa n dabda, b sega Sirɛn ned a ye, a yʋʋr a Simo, la b modg-a lame t'a sõng a Zezi n zɩ b pika.
40027033	B sẽn ta Golgota (zu wang tãnga) b kalma rãam ne rũng yam n kõ-b tɩ b yũ.
40027034	La b sẽn lembe, b pa tʋlg n yũ ye.
40027035	B sẽn ka a Zezi n sɛ, b pʋɩɩ taab b futu, ned kam ne a zu-noog sẽn tʋʋg-a soaba.
40027036	B ra zĩi woto marsã n gũudẽ.
40027037	B ra gʋlsa bũmb n yagl a Zezi zugẽ, n na n wilg sẽn ya bũmb ning n wa ne b kʋʋbo; ra gʋlsa woto: «Wã la a Zezi, Zʋɩf rãmb dĩma.»
40027038	Naaga so-gɩtba a yiib me n ka, a yembre b rɩtgo, a yembre b goabga.
40027039	Neba ra loogda pika tẽngre n yĩgsdĩ la b tʋʋsd-b.
40027040	B ra yetame: «Sẽn tõe-a n wã wẽnd doogã la a lebs n me-a ra-yɩten-daar soaba, fãag f menga, f sã n ya Wẽnnaam Biiga la f sig pika zugu.»
40027041	Maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb me ra laad-b lame; b me naaga Sɛb-mitba la tẽnga nin-kẽemba n yetẽ:
40027042	«A fãaga a taaba n yaool n ka tõe n fãag a meng ye. A yaa Israyɛl Dĩma: bɩ a sig pika marsã tɩ d na tẽe-a!
40027043	A yet t'a teega Wẽnd la, Wẽnd sã n geta yelle, bɩ b fãag-a. Ka yẽ meng n yeele: ‹Mam yaa Wẽnd Biiga!› »
40027044	So-gɩtba sẽn da ka pika me ra naagame n tʋʋsd ba.
40027045	Wĩnto-sʋk n ta zafare, zĩiga lebga lika.
40027046	Zafare, a Zezi tãsa ne pãnga: «Eli, Eli! Lema Sabaktani.» La rẽ rat n yeelame: M Wẽnnaam, m Wẽnnaam! Bõe yĩng la y bas-ma?
40027047	Neb kẽer sẽn zĩnd be n wʋm b goama ra yetame: «Nin-kãnga boondaa Eli!»
40027048	Dẽ la nin-yend wudg n dɩk bũmb sẽn fõogd koom n los rã miisg pʋgẽ, n yaag n loe tãnwĩiga n kõ-b tɩ b yũ.
40027049	La neb a taaba yeel-a lame: «Yaas tɩ d ges a Eli na wa n fãag-a sɩda!»
40027050	A Zezi le tãsame la b kiime.

40027054	Sã n ya tãnsoaba la neb niyns sẽn da be-b pika sɛɛga n gũud a Zezi wã, b sẽn yãend tẽnga miuungu la yɛl a taaba, b pɛlens yɩkame tɩ b yeele: «Ad-y nin-kãnga sɩd da yaa Wẽnd Biiga.»
40027055	Pagb wʋsg ra yɛsa yɩɩga n getẽ. Yaa pagb niyns sẽn da pʋgd-b al Galile tẽnga la b ra get b yelle,
40027056	wala Magdala Mari, n paas a Mari a Zak la Zozɛf ma, n paas a Zebede kamba ma.

40027060	la a mum-a-la a meng yaoogẽ, a sẽn nan tuk paalem kugsẽoogẽ. A baoo kug bedre n pag yaooga noor la a kuli.
40027061	Sã n yaa Magdala Mari la Mari a to wã bãmb waa yaoogẽ wã n da zĩi n get-a.

40027063	«Dĩma, d tẽegame tɩ zirẽ-be-neda sẽn waa n ket n vɩ, a yeelame: ‹M kũum dasm a tãab poore, m na n vʋʋgame.›
40027064	Dɩlla kɩt-y tɩ b gũ yaooga dasm a tã, sã n ka rẽ, a karen-biisa wat n soos n dɩka a yĩnga n yaool n yeel neba t'a vʋʋgame, la ziri kãng wẽnem na n yɩɩga pipi soabã.»
40027065	A Pilat yeel-b lame: «Ad tãb-biisi, tɩ yals-y-ba tɩ b gũ wa y sẽn datã.»
40027066	Tao-tao bala b kẽngame n tɩ ges yaoogã, n ning makre a linga zugu la b yals gũudba n gilg.
40028001	Sibra raar sẽn looge t'a vẽkembeoog sõor nan pukdẽ, Magdala Mari ne Mari a to wã waame n na ges yaoogã.

40028006	b ka le ket ka ye, b vʋʋgame, wala b sẽn da yeele. Waa-y n ges-y b sẽn da gãneg-b zĩig ninga.

41002020	B sẽn wat n bak pʋg-sɩda ne bãmb daare, la b na n loe b noore.
41002021	Ned pa rɩkd peen-paalga sẽn ka wẽ koasla n sũk fu-kʋdg ye. Peend paalga na n yõbame n tak kʋdgã t'a pãrg n paase.
41002022	Ned pa suiid rã-paalg wao-kʋdg pʋg ye, rãama na n pusga waoogã tɩ lebg bõne. Woto yĩnga rã-paalg suiida wao-paalsẽ.»

41002026	A pa kẽ wẽnd doogẽ, maan-kʋʋd, a Abiatar, wẽnnẽ, n dɩk wẽnd dooga bur n wãb bɩ? A ra yaool n miime tɩ yaa maan-kʋʋdba bala n da tõe n wãb bur kãense. A pa saag n kõ a tũud-n-taasa tɩ b rɩ bɩ?»

41003001	Vʋʋsg daar a to, a Zezi le kẽe pʋʋsg roogẽ. Nug-kɩɩng soab a ye n da be be
41003002	la neba fãa ra gũusdame n na n ges a Zezi sã n na n sãoog-a-la vʋʋsga raare, n paam yell n dogl b zugu.
41003003	A Zezi yeela nug-kɩɩngã: «Yik n wa sʋk ka.»
41003004	Dẽ poore b soka nebã: «Maan neer vʋʋsg daar pa são wẽng maaneg bɩ? Vɩɩm kũun vʋʋsg daar n são bɩ yõor yãkre n são?» Ned ba a ye pa leok-b tɩ bũmb ye.
41003005	A Zezi karg n ges-b lame tɩ b sũur kɛɛd ne-ba, b sẽn pa tar nimbãan-zoeer ba bilfã la b yeela raoã: «Tẽeg f nugã!» Tɩ raoã sɩd tẽege la a nuga wẽneg n sãoogame.
41003006	B sẽn yi, tao-tao bala, Farizẽ rãmba yẽsa ne a Erod kẽedbã n baood b sẽn na n yãend dabaar ninga n sãam a Zezi yelle.
41003007	A Zezi yii ne b karen-biisã n tees mogra sẽne; zãma kãseng n da yi Galile la Zɩɩda soolmẽ n tũ-ba.
41003008	Neb wʋsg me sẽn da wʋm a Zezi bõn-bãna kibare da yita tẽns wʋsg n wat b nengẽ, wala Idume tẽnse, Zʋrdẽ kʋɩlg rʋʋnde, Tir la Sidõ.
41003009	A Zezi yeela b karen-biisã tɩ b bao koglg bil a yembre n pẽneg yam-yam bãmb meng yĩnga, tɩ neba ra pẽdgd-b lame tɩ looge.
41003010	A Zezi ra sãooga bãad-dãmb wʋsgo, dẽ yĩnga bãad-dãmba fãa ra pẽdgdame n dat n sɩɩs-ba.
41003011	Sʋtãamba sẽn da be b rãmb pʋsẽ da kolgda a Zezi n wõgemdẽ la b moonẽ: «Yãmb yaa Wẽnnaam Biiga!»
41003012	La a Zezi ra tãsd-b lame tɩ b sĩndi la b ra moon b yʋʋra woto ye.
41003013	Dẽ poore a Zezi dʋʋ tãng a ye. B sẽn da rat neb kẽere, b bool-b lame la b waame.
41003014	Bãmb piig la a yiib la b tũusyã tɩ b na yɩ b Tũud-n-taase n tʋm b tʋʋmde: Koe-nooga moonego.
41003015	B kõ-b-la tõog tɩ b rig Sʋtãamba.
41003016	Piig la a yiiba sẽn yãkã yʋy la woto: a Simo, b pʋda yẽ yʋʋr a Piyɛr, Kugri,
41003017	n paas a Zebede kamba: a Zak ne a yao a Zã. B kõo bãmb yʋ-kãnga: Bonarzes (sa-tãs kamba)
41003018	Le paasa a Andre, a Filip, a Bartelemi, a Matiye, a Toma, a Alfe biig a Zak, a Tade, a Simo, yẽ la a ka yogd ne buuda bɛ,
41003019	la a Zɩɩda, Iskariyot tẽng neda, a Zezi zãmbdã.
41003020	A Zezi lɛɛg n waa yiri la zãma kãseng tũ-b lame yɛsa, al tɩ b ra pa tar zĩig n na n zĩnd n dɩ ye.
41003021	A Zezi doagdba sẽn wʋm dẽ, b kẽngame n na n tɩ yõk-ba tɩ b ra yetame: «Ad-a zuga lebgame.»
41003022	Mitb n yi Zerizalɛɛm n wa n yetẽ: «Yaa Sʋtãan a Beelzebul n be nin-kãnga pʋga, la yaa ne Sʋtãamba naab pãnga, la a yiisd Sʋtãamba.»
41003023	A Zezi wẽe yelbũndi n yetẽ: «Sʋtãan na n yɩ wãn n dig Sʋtãana?
41003024	Rĩung a ye neb sã n wẽneg n zabd ne taaba, rĩung kãng na n yɩɩ wãn n ka wã zãnga?
41003025	Yir a ye neb sã n wẽneg n zabd ne taaba, yi kãng kõn wã sɩda?
41003026	Sʋtãan sã n zabd ne a menga, a sã n welg ne a menga, a pa tõe n yals yĩngr yɛs ye. Yẽ yell sɛɛme.
41003027	M yeta yãmba tɩ ned ka tõe n kẽ nin-daoog zakẽ n wʋk a teed t'a pa reng n yõk-a n sẽb ye.
41003028	Sɩd-sɩda m yeta yãmba tɩ Adem biisa yel-wẽna la b wẽn-tʋʋra na paam sugri, ba b sõora sẽn zem bũmb ninga.
41003029	La ned ninga sẽn na n tʋʋs-a Vʋʋsem Sõngo, yẽ soab kõn paam sugr abada. Yel-wẽnda na n paa ne-a, raar fãa.»
41003030	Yaa Farizẽ rãmba sẽn da yet tɩ Sʋtãan n be a Zezi pʋgẽ yĩngã la b gom woto.
41003031	A Zezi ma la b buuda neb waa n yaasa yɩnga n tʋm tɩ b bool a Zezi n kõ-ba.
41003032	Neb wʋsg da zĩ-la a Zezi sɛɛgẽ, wakat kãnga. B yeela a Zezi: «Ad-y y ma la y saam-biisi, rap la pagba n be yɩnga n baood-y.»
41003033	A Zezi leokame: «Mam ma la ãndã, m saam-biis la ãnd dãmba?»
41003034	La a Zezi gesa neb niyns sẽn da be-b bãmb sɛɛgẽ n yeele: «Ad-m ma, ad-m saam-biisi.
41003035	Ned ninga fãa sẽn maand-a Wẽnnaam yam, yẽ soab la m yao, m tão la m ma.»
41004001	A Zezi da leb n sɩnga neba zãmsgo mogra noore. Neb wʋsg ra tigma taab b sɛɛgẽ. La neba sẽn da ya wʋsg yĩnga, b kongame n kẽ koglg a ye pʋga, n ta ko sʋka. Nebã n pa tẽnga, mogra noore.
41004002	A Zezi zãms-b la bũmb wʋsg ne yelbũna. B zãmsg pʋgẽ b ra yetame:
41004003	«Kelg-y yelbũndi. Ned a ye n da yii n na n bʋd a pʋʋgo.
41004004	A sẽn waa n bʋtẽ, bõn-buud kẽer dʋʋga sora noore la luiili wẽneg n dɩgs-b la zãnga.
41004005	Kẽer lʋɩɩ zẽgdg zugu, la bʋgsem sẽn da ka be wʋsg yĩnga, b yika tao-tao.
41004006	Wĩndg sẽn waa n wɩnge, bãmb wẽneg n kiime, tɩ b ra ka kɩ yẽgen wʋsg ye.
41004007	Kẽer lʋɩɩ gõos sʋka la gõos wulumd-b lame n kʋ tɩ b pa paam n wom biis ye.
41004008	Kẽer lʋɩɩ zĩ-sõngẽ la bãmb yikame n wom biis wʋsgo, kẽer pistã-tã, kẽer pisoobsoobe, kẽer koabg-koabga.»
41004009	A Zezi da yetame: «Ned ninga sẽn tar-a tʋba n na kelg bɩ a yoog a tʋb n kelge.»
41004010	A Zezi waa n bee kɛɛnga tɩ b sõsd-n-taasa ne Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã na n sok-b b yelbũna poorẽ.
41004011	Dẽ la b ra yet woto: «Sã n ya yãmba, yãmb paamame tɩ b wilg-y Wẽnd Rĩunga yɛla. Sã n ya ne sẽn be-b yɩngã, yaa ne yelbũn la b gomd ne bãmba,
41004012	sẽn na n yɩla tɩ b sã n get neere me bɩ b ra yãe ye; b sã n kelgd neer me bɩ b ra wʋm ye, ka rẽ, raar a ye b wat n teemame n paam sugri.»
41004013	A Zezi yeela bãmba: «Yãmb sɩd ka wʋmd yelbũnd kãnga võore? La sã n ya woto, yãmb na n maana a wãn n wʋm a taaba võore?
41004014	Bʋta sẽn bʋtã, yaa Wẽnd Gomdã.
41004015	Sẽn be-b Gomda sẽn bʋd sor ninga noorã, la sẽn wʋm-b Gomdã tɩ Sʋtãan wẽneg n yiis-a b sũurẽ.
41004016	Zĩ kʋɩgdgẽ dãmba yaa neb niyns sẽn wʋm-b Gomdã n deeg-a tao-tao ne sũ-noogo.
41004017	La b meng sẽn ka kɩ yẽgna, yaa wakat yɛng bala la b ya rapa. La b sã n seg toog bɩ namsgo, Koe-nooga yĩnga, b kongda raoodo n pãs n lʋɩ.
41004018	Gõosẽ dãmbã, yaa neb niyns sẽn wʋm Gomdã
41004019	n yaool n bas tɩ dũni zu-loeese, arzɛgs tʋlsem, tʋls wẽns buud fãa, wulumd-ba, tɩ Gomda sẽn bʋda pa tõe n wom biis ye.
41004020	Sẽn lʋɩb zĩ-sõngẽ, makda sẽn kelgd-b la b reegd Gomdã n paam n womd biisi, pistã-tã, pisoobsoobe, koabg-koabga.»
41004021	B ra leb n yet-b lame: «Fitil yõgendame n lud ne koglg bɩ n solg gãag tẽngr bɩ? Ka roagendga zuug la b ningd-a?
41004022	Bũmb ka be sẽn solg likẽ, tɩ b ka na n wa ne a vẽenemẽ ye. Sẽn sogl fãa tara a pukr daare.
41004023	Sẽn tar-a tʋb fãa n na n kelge, bɩ a kelg.»
41004024	A Zezi ra yet-b lame yɛsa: «Gũus-y ne y sẽn wʋmde! Yãmb sẽn na n dɩk makr ninga n mak n kõ y taaba, yãmb me rẽn na n maka boto la pʋs n na yɩɩg rẽnd me.
41004025	Sẽn zoe n tar-a wã la b na n kõo n paase. Sẽn ka tar-a wã, bilfra a sẽn tarã la b na deege.»
41004026	A Zezi ra yet-b lame yɛsa: «Wẽnd Rĩunga wẽnda bõn-buud ned sẽn bʋd a pʋʋgẽ.
41004027	A gõeeme bɩ a neeme, yaa wĩntoog bɩ yaa yʋngo, bõn-buuda bundame n yi a toore t'a ka miẽ ye.
41004028	Tẽnga meng n wat ne a yõodo: pipi yaa vãado, a yiib soaba yaa ka-zugu, la rẽ poore yaa biisi.
41004029	La kood sã n bɩ n sɛ, yaa kɛɛbo tɩ kooda bɩɩme.»
41004030	A Zezi le yeelame: «Mam na n maka Wẽnd Rĩunga ne bõe? M na n wẽe yelbũnd bʋgo n mak-a tɩ y wʋme?
41004031	Wẽnnaam Rĩunga wẽnda seneve tɩɩg biiga, a bʋdb wakato, a yaa bilfr wʋsgo bõn-buud a taab fãa sʋka.
41004032	La b sã n bʋd-a t'a yi n sɛ, a lebgda tɩ kãsenga al n tão wil bɛda tɩ yĩngr luiili wat n vʋʋsd a maasmẽ.»
41004033	Yaa ne yelbũn wʋsg woto la a Zezi ra gomd ne nebã n zãmsd-ba b sẽn tõe n wʋm bũmb ninga.
41004034	La a Zezi ra ka gomd ne bãmb tɩ ka ne yelbũn ye la b sã n da yaool n be ne b karen-biisa bala, b ra wilgda bãmb yelbũna võore.
41004035	Baraare, zĩig sẽn waa n sobgdẽ, a Zezi yeela b tũud-n-taasã: «Wa-y tɩ d dʋʋg mogrã.»
41004036	B basa nebã la b talla a Zezi ne koglg ning b sẽn da be a soab pʋgẽ wã n dʋʋge. Koom kogend a taab me yãag-b lame.
41004037	Wakat kãng la sob-kãseng yik yã al tɩ ko-wiisa da rãmbd wʋsgo n buiid koglgã t'a rat n pidi.
41004038	A Zezi menga ra bee poorẽ n kʋgl b zug zu-kʋka n gõe; karen-biisa nek-b lame n yeel-ba: «Soaala, yãmb pa ne tõnd sẽn na n ki wã la, n maand wa y toog ka be?»
41004039	A Zezi sẽn neke, b zaba ne sobgã la b kõo mogra noor n yetẽ: «Yɩ sɩɩ la f bas bʋrga!» Sobga yõka vugr bala tɩ mogra zãng lebg sɩɩ.
41004040	A Zezi yaool n yeela b karen-biisã: «Yaa bõe yĩng la y zoet dabeem woto? Yaa bõe tɩ y pa tar tẽebo?»
41004041	Dabeem kãseng yõka bãmb fãa tɩ b ra yet taaba: «Nin-kãnga yaa Ãnda tɩ sobg la mogr deegd b noore?»
41005001	A Zezi sẽn ta mogra rʋʋnde, Gadar tẽnga.
41005002	B sẽn sig koom kogenda bala, la ned a ye sẽn yi yaadẽ n zoet n segd-ba. Yaa Sʋtãan n da be nin-kãng pʋgẽ.
41005003	A ra gãee yaad pʋsẽ la neba ra ka ne bõn-zaadg ning b sẽn na n tall n zaa-a ye, ba ya bãeense.
41005004	Naoor wʋsgo b yõk-a lame n balg, n sẽb-a ne bãeense t'a kao bãeensã ne rabõangã; ned ba a ye ra ka tõe-a ye.
41005005	Wakat fãa, yʋng la wĩntoogo, a ra bee yaadẽ bɩ tãmsa zut n wiisdẽ la a bogd a meng ne kuga.
41005006	A sẽn yãe a Zezi tɩ b be yɩɩg n watẽ, a zoe n seg-b lame, n wõgemd b taoore n moon wʋsgo:
41005007	«Y rat-m la ne bõe, Zezi, yĩngr Wẽnda Biiga? M kot-y la ne Wẽnde, tɩ y ra maan-m bũmb ye!»
41005008	La rẽ yaa a Zezi sẽn da yeel-a: «Sʋtãan yoogo, yi nin-kãnga pʋgẽ.»
41005009	A Zezi sok-a lame: «Fo yʋʋr la a bõe?» T'a leoke: «M yʋʋr la a Kʋʋma, tɩ sɩda, d sõor yaa wʋsgo.»
41005010	Sʋtãan yõka sɛɛga tɩ b ra rig-a n yiis tẽnga pʋgẽ ye.
41005011	Kurkuy wʋsgo n da be tãng a yembr zug be, n wãbd yamdo.
41005012	Sʋtãana kosa a Zezi: «Bɩ y bas do tɩ d kẽ kurkuya pʋsẽ.»
41005013	A Zezi kõ-b la sore, la b sẽn paam dẽ, b yiime n tɩ kẽ kurkuya tɩ b kaoog n zoet n sigd tãngã n digd mogrã. Rũmsa sõor da taa tus a yiibu la b fãa lʋɩɩ mogrẽ tɩ kooma rɩ-ba.
41005014	Rũm-kɩɩmba zoee tao-tao n tɩ togs kibara tẽnga pʋga la tẽn-kɩremsa fãa. Tẽnga rãmb zoeeme n wa ges yellã sẽn yɩ to-to.
41005015	B sẽn ta, b yãenda Sʋtãana sẽn da kẽ-a soabã t'a zĩ a Zezi sɛɛgẽ n yer fuug la a gomd neere. B yãend-a lame tɩ rabeem kẽ-ba tɩ yaa sʋtãamb wʋsgo n sɩd da be nin-kãng pʋgẽ.
41005016	Neb niyns sẽn zĩnd-b be n yãend yella sɩngre, togsa b taaba bũmb ning fãa sẽn maane ne raoã la ne kurkuya.
41005017	Tɩ b naag taab n kos a Zezi tɩ b yi b tẽngẽ.
41005018	A Zezi sẽn yet tɩ b kẽed koglgã, la ned ninga sẽn paam-a sãoogra kos sor n na n tũ-ba.
41005019	A Zezi pa sak ye; b yeel-a lame: «Kul f yiri, f buud neb sʋka, la togs bãmb kibarã; gom ne-ba, nimbãan-zoeer tʋʋm niyns Soaala sẽn sak n maan f yĩnga.»
41005020	Raoã sɩd kulame la a saaga Tẽns piiga sẽn tot taabã n moond a Zezi sẽn maan bũmb ning ne yẽnda. Neba fãa pẽgame.
41005021	A Zezi rʋʋga kʋɩlgã ne koglgã la zãma kãseng waa n gũma be.
41005022	Yaa wakat kãng la pʋʋsg roog a ye naab sẽn boond t'a Zayir pɩʋʋg be.
41005023	A sẽn yãend a Zezi, a wõgemda b taoore n kot-b ne pẽdgre: «M bi-pugl n be yiri n ka laafi ye, la a pãnga sɛɛ fãa, m kotame tɩ y wa tẽeg y nug a zugu t'a paam laafi la a ra ki ye.»
41005024	T'a Zezi sɩd na n tũ n kuli. Neb wʋsg kaoogame n pʋgd a Zezi n tol n lagsd b nao.
41005025	Pag a ye n da bẽed mende, al yʋʋm piig la a yiibu.
41005026	Pʋg-kãnga namsa wʋsgo tɩt rãmba buud toor-toor nusẽ. A sãama ligd wʋsgo la a ka paam laafi ye. A bãaga da paasdame n dabda.
41005027	A sẽn wʋm tɩ b gomd a Zezi yelle, a soos n pʋga poorẽ n kẽ neba sʋka, n sɩɩs a Zezi fuugu.
41005028	A ra tagsda a sũurẽ: «M sã n paam n sɩɩs a fuuga bala, m na n paama laafi.»
41005029	Vugr bala zɩɩma yõkame tɩ paga bãng t'a sãoogame.
41005030	Tao-tao bala, a Zezi me bãngame tɩ pãng n yi b nengẽ n sãoog neda. B wẽnegame n sok sẽn da pʋgd-b bãmbã: «Yaa ãnda n sɩɩs m fuugã?»
41005031	Tɩ b karen-biisa na n leoke: «Neb pẽdgd yãmb woto tɩ y le sokd tɩ ãnda n sɩɩs yãmba?»
41005032	A Zezi ra ket n geta b sɛɛgẽ, n baood ned ninga sẽn sɩɩs-a bãmbã.
41005033	Paga sẽn mi tiirã, rabeem yõk-a lame t'a rigda. A kolgame n wõgemd a Zezi taoore n togs a pʋga.
41005034	A Zezi yeel-a lame: «M biiga, fo tẽeba fãag-f lame. Kẽng ne laafi, f bãaga sẽn da yaand fooma na n kell n sãooga zãnga.»
41005035	A Zezi ra ket n gomda ne pagã, la neb n yi naaba yiri n wa togs naaba: «Fo biiga konga pãnga, ra nams Soaala zaalem ye!»
41005036	A Zezi sẽn wʋm b goama leoka naabã: «Da zoe rabeem ye, fo ye n tẽ bala.»
41005037	B gɩdga neba tɩ b ra le pʋg-b ye, sã n ka a Piyɛr la a Zak ne Zã bala.
41005038	B rɩka naaba yir sore; b sẽn ta yiri b yãee neb wʋsg sẽn yãbd la b kaasdẽ.
41005039	A Zezi kẽeme n sok nebã: «Yaa bõe tɩ y yãbda la y maand bʋʋr woto? Biiga ka ki ye, a gõeeme bala.»
41005040	Tɩ neba na n la a Zezi. A Zezi rig-b la zãnga, n peeg biiga ba ne a ma la b karen-biisã n kẽ bãada roogẽ.
41005041	B gãda biiga nug n yeel-a: «Talita koum!» Dat n yeelame: «Bi-pugla, m yet-f lame, yiki!»
41005042	Tao bala bi-pugla yikame n kẽnda. A ra tara yʋʋm piig la a yiibu. Dabeem kẽe nebã wʋsgo.
41005043	A Zezi kõo noor tɩ b modg tɩ yella ra yi kɛɛng ye. B paasame tɩ b bao rɩɩb n kõ biiga t'a rɩ.
41006001	A Zezi yii be n kẽng Nazarɛt, b ba-yiri. Karen-biisa me tũume.
41006002	Vʋʋsg daare b kẽe pʋʋsg roogẽ n na n zãms neb karengo. Neb wʋsg wʋma b goama la b pɛleng yɩkame tɩ b yetẽ: «B zãmsa woto fãa yɛ? Ya ãnna kõ-b yam la tõog kãngã tɩ b maand bõn-bãna?
41006003	Ka bãmb la ra-wãada laa? Ka bãmb la a Maryam biiga laa? Ka a Zak, a Zoze, a Simo, a Zɩɩd saam-biig la bãmb laa. B saam-bi-pogsã ka vɩ ne tõnd bɩ?» B poorẽ da yaa no-koeemde.
41006004	A Zezi ra yet-b lame bala: «Bãngd buud fãa ka tõe n paam waoogr a tẽngẽ ye, a pa tõe n paam waoogr a tẽnga kamba nengẽ la a zakẽ ye.»
41006005	Beelẽ a Zezi ra ka maan wẽnd-makr dãmb wa zĩis kẽer ye. B tẽega b nus koms-rãmb kẽer zug bala, n kõ-b laafi.
41006006	A Zezi meng ra ka wʋmd neba sẽn pa tẽeda võor ye. Rẽ poore a Zezi sɩnga tẽn-kɩremsa saabo, neba zãmsg yĩnga.
41006007	A Zezi boola b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã la b tʋm-b la a yiib-yiibu; b ra kõ-b la tõogo tɩ b yiis sʋtãamba neb pʋsẽ.
41006008	B kõ-b la noore tɩ b sã n dabd b tʋʋmna bɩ b ra zɩ bũmb sã n ka rasaar bala. B yeel-b lame tɩ ra zɩ sor dɩɩbo, bɩ korgo, bɩ ligd b gɩfẽ ye.
41006009	B yeel-b lame tɩ b wid gãndalsa, la b ra yeelg fut a yiib ye.
41006010	B ra yet-b lame yɛsa: «Yãmb sẽn na n ta zĩig ning fãa bɩ y kẽ zak a yembre la y pa be n ta y loogre.
41006011	Yãmb sẽn ta zĩig ninga tɩ b pa reeg yãmb la b pa sak n kelg yãmb zãmsgo, bɩ y yi n bas tẽn-kãnga. La y sã n yita bɩ y pĩng y nao tom, n ning tẽnga rãmb taale.»
41006012	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba kẽngame n zãms nebã tɩ b tuub b yel-wẽna.
41006013	B riga sʋtãamb wʋsgo la b zɛɛ bãad-dãmb wʋsg ne kaam n sãoog-ba.
41006014	Dĩm a Erod wʋma a Zezi kibare, tɩ b yʋʋra ra yii wʋsgo. B ra yetame: «Zã ning sẽn da sooda neba kooma vʋʋga kɩɩms sʋka la yaa rẽnd yĩnga la a wẽn-makr dãmba ka be sõor ye.»
41006015	Neb kẽer da yetame: «Yaa a Eli» tɩ neb kẽer me yetẽ: «A yaa bãngda wa bãngdba a taabã.»
41006016	A Erod me ra wʋmda b yelle la yẽ ra yetame: «Yaa Zã ning m sẽn fiuug a soab zugã, n vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka!»
41006017	Sɩd me a Erod n da kɩt tɩ b yõk a Zã, n sẽb-a, n kẽes-a roogo. A Erod da rɩka, a yao paga, a yao, a Filip, paga, a Erodiad, n maan a paga.
41006018	A Zã me ra yeta a Erod: «Pa segd tɩ yãmb dɩk y yao paga n maan y pag ye.»
41006019	A Erodiad sũur da puuda ne a Zã, al t'a da rat a kũum, la a ra pa tõe n kʋ-a ye,
41006020	t'a Erod meng ra zoeta a Zã, a sẽn da ya nin-tɩrga la nin-sõngã, la a ra pa rat tɩ ned maan-a bũmb ye. A Zã goama bal n wa n kɩt t'a le ka mi a sẽn na n maanega. Baasg fãa, a ra ket n kelgda a Zã ne sũ-noogo.
41006021	Waa n sega daar a ye, t'a Erod maand a rogem daar tẽegr kibsa. A ra boola nanams bɛda, tãnsoabẽn-dãmb la Galile soolem nanamse.
41006022	Dẽ la a Erodiad bi-pugla kẽ rɩɩba roogẽ n sao, al t'a Erod ne sẽn da rɩt-ba fãa sũur yɩ noogo t'a na n yeel bi-puglã: «Bɩ f kos maam f sẽn dat bũmb ning fãa, tɩ m na kõ-fo.»
41006023	A tol n paasame ne wẽenego: «Fo sẽn na n kos maam bũmb ninga fãa, ba yaa m rĩunga pʋɩ-sʋka, f na n paamame.»
41006024	Bi-pugla yiime n zoe n tɩ sok a ma: «M ma, m na n kosa naab bõe?» A ma wã leokame: «Kos a Zã zugu.»
41006025	Bi-pugla zoe lomb-lombe, n wa naaba nengẽ n wilg a kosgã: «M kotame tɩ y ning a Zã zugã laag pʋgẽ n kõ maam mars-marsã bala.»
41006026	Naaba sũur sãama al wʋsgo, la a wẽenega yĩnga, n paas neba me yĩnga, a pa tõog n zãgs ye.
41006027	Tao bala, a kõo tãb-biisa noor tɩ b fiuug a Zã zug n wa.
41006028	Tãb-biisa kẽnga bi-beesa roogẽ n tɩ fiuug a Zã zug n ning laagẽ, n wa kɩs bi-puglã. La bi-pugla talla zugã n tɩ kɩs a ma.
41006029	A Zã tũud-n-taas sẽn wʋm woto, b waa n dɩka a yĩngã n solg yaoogẽ.
41006030	Karen-biisa yii b sorã n le wa bãmb sɛɛgẽ. B togsa b sẽn maan bũmb ninga, la b sẽn zãms bũmb ninga.
41006031	La a Zezi yeel-b lame: «Bɩ d tũ taab n zãag zĩig bilfu n paam n vʋʋse.» Neba ra pɩʋʋmda taab zĩ kãng al wʋsgo, tɩ b ra ka tõe n paam vɩʋʋg n dɩ meng ye.
41006032	Bãmb ne b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã bal kẽe koom koglgo, n dʋʋg n ta neb sẽn da ka be zĩig ninga.
41006033	Neba yãee b sẽn dʋʋg mogrã n digd weoogẽ wã, la b sẽn da zoe m mi b sẽn dabdẽ, wʋsg yii tẽnsa fãa pʋsẽ ne nao bala, n deng bãmb be.
41006034	A Zezi sẽn ta rʋʋnde, b yãee neb wʋsg sẽn da tigim taab beene. B sẽn yãe nebã, b zoe b nimbãanega. B ra wẽnda piis sẽn ka tar pe-kɩɩm ye. La b sɩngame n zãms-ba n kaoose.
41006035	Karen-biisa sẽn mik tɩ zĩiga ra zʋʋgame, b kẽng n tɩ wilg a Zezi: «Ka, tõnd bee weoogẽ, la zĩig me zʋʋgame.
41006036	Bɩ y bas neba tɩ b kẽng pʋtẽ la tẽnsa pʋsẽ n da rɩɩb n dɩ.»
41006037	Dẽ la b leok ba: «Bɩ yãmb mens bao rɩɩbo n kõ-b wɛ!» Tɩ karen-biisa yeele: «Na yaa n yɩ pakr tɩ d yiis wakɩ koeems sẽn ta kobsi n da bur n kõ-b tɩ b rɩ?»
41006038	La a Zezi wẽneg n sok-b lame: «Yaa bur a wãna la y tara, tɩ sõd-y n gese.» Karen-biisa sẽn tɩ gese, b waa n togsame tɩ yaa bur a nu la kʋɩl-zẽed a yiib n kete.
41006039	A Zezi kõ-b la noore tɩ b welg rɩt-n-taasa bal bale, mo maasa zugu.
41006040	La bãmb kɩtame tɩ neba zĩnd sak saka, koabg koabga, pisnu-nu.
41006041	A Zezi deega bur a nu wã la kʋɩl-zẽed a yiibã, la b zẽka b neng yĩngr n maan bark pʋʋsgo n yaool n wes burã n kõ Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã tɩ b pʋɩ nebã. B pʋɩ neba zĩm a yiiba me.
41006042	Neba fãa paamame n dɩ n tɩge.
41006043	Karen-biisa wʋka bura girse la kʋɩl-zẽedã sẽn kellã n pid pet piig la a yiibu.
41006044	Sẽn da rɩba fãa sõor taa tus a nu.
41006045	Neba sẽn dɩ n sɛ bala, a Zezi modga b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã tɩ b kẽ koom koglga pʋga n deng bãmb rʋʋnde, Bɛtsayid sẽnẽ. Bãmb meng paame n na n yõdg n kuls nebã.
41006046	B sẽn kuls nebã n sɛ, b kẽnga tãng a yembr zugu n tɩ pʋʋse.
41006047	Zĩig waa n sobgame, la koglga me ra zoe n taa mogra sʋka, tɩ bãmb b ye bal ket b zĩigẽ.
41006048	B sẽn yãe tɩ sobg ra segda Tʋʋm-tʋmdba tɩ b namsd wʋsg ne koglga rʋgsgu, tõd-beoog pĩnda, b yikame n kẽn kooma zug n babs-ba. B maana wala b da rat n loog-b lame.
41006049	La bãmb sẽn yãe ned sẽn kẽnd koom zug woto, b yeela taaba: «Ad-y yaa kɩɩma!»
41006050	B ra maanda bʋrga tɩ bãmb fãa sẽn yãe woto, rabeem yõk-b lame. A Zezi goma ne bãmba n yetẽ: «Keng-y y pelse, tɩ yaa maam; da zoe-y rabeem ye.»
41006051	La a Zezi meng kẽe b koglga pʋga. Wakat kãng bala sobga yõka vugr n lebg sɩɩ. Rabeem kãsenga da ket n bee ned kam fãa sũurẽ.
41006052	Bãmb da pa wʋm bura fɩɩr võor ye, da ket n yaa wa b bee likẽ.
41006053	B sẽn dʋʋg mogrã, b tɩ kolga Zenezarɛt n yaase.
41006054	B sẽn yi koglga pʋg n sɛ, neba bãnga tao-tao bal tɩ yaa a Zezi.
41006055	Neba zoe n saaga tẽnga fãa n tʋk bãad-dãmb ne b gãase n wa a Zezi nengẽ. B sẽn da be zĩig ning fãa, neba ra watame.
41006056	B sẽn da wʋm t'a Zezi bee zĩig ninga fãa, a Zezi sẽn ta tẽng ning fãa, tẽn-bõonego, tẽn-bɛda la tẽn-kɩremse, fãa ra tigimda b bãad-dãmba, tẽnga sɛk zĩigẽ, la b ra kota a Zezi tɩ b sak tɩ bãad-dãmb sɩɩs b fuuga zerd bala. La neb niins fãa sẽn da paam-ba n sɩɩs a Zezi fuuga ra sãoogdame.
41007001	Farizẽ rãmba ne Mitba yii Zerizalɛɛm n tigim taab n wa a Zezi nengẽ.
41007002	B yãe e Zezi karen-biisa kẽer sẽn da rɩt ne rẽgdo, dat n yeelame: ne nus sẽn ka peke.
41007003	Farizẽ la Zʋɩf rãmba fãa da pa rɩt rɩɩbo n pa reng n pek b nus n tãag kãntɩɩs ye. Dẽ yaa b rog-n-mik.
41007004	B sã n da yi raagẽ n wa b soodame n yaool n dɩ. B ra tara yɛl a taab wʋsgo, b rog-n-mika pʋgẽ, wala wama ne yʋya nedegre, yõg-laasa pekre.
41007005	Yaa rẽ la Farizẽ ne mitba sok a Zezi: «Bõe yĩng tɩ yãmb karen-biisã pa rɩt wala rog-n-mika sẽn date? Yaa bõe yĩnga tɩ b rɩt ne nus rẽgdo?»
41007006	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Zãmb rãmba, a Izayi n bãng n gom y yelle n gʋls woto: ‹Nin-bãmba waoogda maam ne noor bala, b sũya zãra ne maam.
41007007	B waoogr pa waoogd-m ye. B zãmsga tekda ninsaal sẽn mi bala.›
41007008	Yãmb basa Wẽnnaam noya n tũud neb rog-n-miki.»
41007009	A Zezi ra yet-b lame yɛsa: «Sɩd-sɩda yãmb kɩtame tɩ yãmb dog-n-mik reeg Wẽnnaam noya zĩiga.
41007010	A Moyiiz da yeelame: ‹Waoog f ba la f ma la ned ning sẽn sãbsda a ba la a ma, a soab toga ne kũum.›
41007011	Yãmb nengẽ y gomdame: ‹Ned sã n yeel a ba bɩ a ma: ad-m sẽn da tõe n dɩk bũmb ning fãa n sõng foo lebga Wẽnd dẽnna›,
41007012	yãmb pa le sakd t'a sõng a ba bɩ a ma ye.
41007013	Woto wã, yãmb dog-n-mika kɩtame tɩ Wẽnnaam goama lebg zaalem la yãmb maanda bũmb wʋsgo sẽn wẽnd boto.»
41007014	Dẽ poore, a Zezi le boola neba yɛsa n yeel-ba: «Yãmb fãa, bɩ y kelg mam sẽn na n togs-y bũmb ninga neere.
41007015	Bũmb ka be yɩnga sẽn tõe n kẽ ned pʋgẽ n dẽgem-a ye. Yaa f mengẽ la rẽgda yita n dẽgemd-f. [
41007016	Ned ninga sẽn tar-a tʋb n tõe n wʋm bɩ a wʋm!»]
41007017	B sẽn waa n bas nebã n kẽ roogẽ, b karen-biisa sok-b lame n na n bãng b gomda võore.
41007018	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Yãmb me yam ket n paooda woto laa? Yãmb ka mi tɩ bũmb ning fãa sẽn zĩnd yɩnga n kẽ ninsaal pʋgẽ ka tõe n dẽgem-a bɩ?
41007019	Baad-y bõn-kãng ka kẽed a sũurẽ ye. Bõn-kãng kẽeda a pʋgẽ n yaool n le yi a sã n kẽng we-kɛɛnga.» Woto me la b wilg yã tɩ fãa tõe n yɩɩ rɩɩbo.
41007020	A Zezi yeelame yɛsa: «Ya bũmb ning sẽn yit ninsaal sũurẽ, yaa bõn-kãng n dẽgemd-a.
41007021	Yaa ninsaal pʋgẽ, yaa a sũurẽ la tʋlg f to ne wẽng yita, n paas yoobo, wagdem, nin-kʋʋre,
41007022	to pag baoobo, arzɛk wʋsg baoobo, pu-toogo, zãmbo, reem yoodo, sũ-kiiri, to yʋ sãoongo, nagre, yẽs-põasa.
41007023	Bõn-wẽens kãensã yita ninsaal sũurẽ la yaa bãmb n dẽgemd-a.»
41007024	A Zezi yii b sẽn da be zĩig ningã n kẽng Tir tẽnga. B kẽe yir a ye; b ra ka rat tɩ neba bãng ye la b ka tõog n solg b meng ye.
41007025	B sẽn ta bala, la pag a ye sẽn wʋm b yelle n zoe n wa wõgemd b taoore. Paga bi-pugla la Sʋtãan da kẽ n yãmbe.
41007026	Pʋg-kãng ra yaa bu-zẽna, Sirofenisi rãmb neda. A kosa a Zezi tɩ b yiis Sʋtãana sẽn da kẽ a bi-puglã.
41007027	A Zezi ra yet-a lame: «Bas tɩ kamba reng n dɩ n tɩge, tɩ pa segd tɩ b rɩk kamb dɩɩbo n kõ ba-bi ye.»
41007028	Paga leok-b lame: «Rẽ yaa sɩda, Soaala, la yaa sɩd me tɩ ba-bi wã tõe n dɩgsa dɩ-zeremsã kamba sẽn basd tɩ rʋʋgd tẽngã.»
41007029	A Zezi yeel-a lame: «Fo gomd kãnga yĩnga bɩ f kẽng tɩ Sʋtãana yiime n bas f biigã.»
41007030	La paga yikame n kuli, la sɩda, a tɩ mikame tɩ Sʋtãana yiime n bas a bi-pugla t'a gãe a gãag zugu.
41007031	Wẽnd kãnga, a Zezi yii Tir tẽnga n tũud Sidõ soolme, n tees Galile Mogrã, n digd Tẽns piiga sẽn tot taabã.
41007032	La b sẽn waa n loogdẽ, neb n tall bãad a ye sẽn ya muk la wʋnga n wa b taoore. B kos-b lame tɩ b tẽeg b nug a zugu n sãoog-a.
41007033	A Zezi taka bãadã n yi kɛɛnga la b rɩka b nus-bi n tʋm a tʋbẽ la b sɩɩs a zelemdã ne kolkoodo.
41007034	B naka b neng yĩngri n wẽ siri n yetẽ: «Efata» dat n yeelame: tʋba, pak-y.
41007035	La vugr bala a tʋba yoogame la a zelemd lakame t'a gomd neere.
41007036	A Zezi wilg-b lame tɩ b ra gom ne ned ye; la a Zezi sẽn da kos-b bũmb ningã, bãmb pa tõog b noor ye; b da wãgda a Zezi yʋʋr n yɩɩd pĩnda.
41007037	Neba pɛlens ra yɩgda wʋsgo tɩ b yetẽ: «B sẽn maan fãa yaa sõma: b kɩtame tɩ wʋms wʋmnẽ, tɩ mugs gomda.»
41008001	Wakat kãnga neb kʋʋng da leb n tigma taab a Zezi sɛɛgẽ. La b sẽn da ka tar dɩɩb sẽn na n dɩ yĩnga, a Zezi boola b tũud-n-taase, n yeel-ba:
41008002	«Mam zoeta bãndurba nimbãanega. Yãmb ne tɩ yaa rasma a tã rũnna la b be ne maam, la b pa tar dɩɩb n na n dɩ ye.
41008003	Mam sã n kuls-b woto tɩ b pa rɩ, wʋsg na n paa sorẽ. Bãmb kẽer yii al zĩig sẽn zãrẽ.»
41008004	B karen-biisa leokame: «D na n yãee bur yɛ tɩ sek nin-bãmba, we-raoogẽ ka?»
41008005	A Zezi sok-b lame: «Yãmb tara bur dãmb a wãna?» Tɩ b leoke: «Yaa a yopoe.»
41008006	A Zezi kɩtame tɩ neba fãa zĩnd tẽnga; dẽ marsã la b reeg bur a yopoe wã n pʋʋs bark pʋʋsgo n yaool n wes n kɩs b karen-biisã tɩ b pʋɩ nebã, la b maana boto.
41008007	Kʋɩl-zẽ-bõoneg bilf me n da kete. B ninga rẽ me barka n yet tɩ b pʋɩ nebã.
41008008	Neba fãa dɩɩme n tɩge la b sẽn wʋk girsã b pidsa pet a yopoe.
41008009	Neba sõor da taa tus a naase; la a Zezi yaoolame marsã n kuls-ba.
41008010	Dẽ poore, a Zezi ne b karen-biisa le kẽe koglgo n dʋʋg mogrã n kẽng Dalmanuta tẽnga.
41008011	Farizẽ rãmb waame n wẽ no-koeemd ne a Zezi, la b da kota bãmba bõn-bãn sẽn yit yĩngri n na n ges b sã n sɩd tõeme.
41008012	A Zezi wẽe siri n yetẽ: «Bõe yĩng la nin-bãmba kot wẽnd makre? Sɩd-sɩda m yeta yãmba tɩ m pa na n maan wẽnd makr zamaan kãnga neba yĩng ye.»
41008013	A Zezi yikame n bas-ba la b le kẽe koglg yɛsa, n dig rʋʋnde.
41008014	Karen-biisã ra yĩmame n pa zɩ bur ye. Da yaa bur a yembr tãa n da be b nengẽ, koglga pʋga.
41008015	A Zezi yaool n da sagend-b la woto: «Puk-y y nini la y gũus ne Farizẽ la a Erod kẽedba rabɩlle.»
41008016	Tɩ bãmb na n lɛɛg n leok taaba: «Daare yaa d sẽn ka zɩ burã la b gomd woto.»
41008017	A Zezi bãngame n yeel-ba: «Yaa bõe tɩ yãmb tagsd tɩ m gomda y sẽn pa zɩ burã? Yãmb ket n pa wʋmd laa? Y pa wʋmd m goama võore? Yãmb sũya bee zond pʋgẽ.
41008018	Yãmb tara nini la y ka ne ye, y tara tʋba la y ka wʋmd ye. Yãmb pa le tẽr laa?
41008019	Mam sẽn wes bur a nu n kõ neb tus a nu wã, y wʋka gɩrsa pet a wãna?» Tɩ b leok tɩ yɩɩ piig la a yiibu.
41008020	«Mam sẽn waa n wes bur a yopoe n kõ tus a naasã, yɩɩ pet a wãna la y wʋk gɩrsã?» Tɩ b leoke: «A yopoe.»
41008021	Tɩ b na n yeel-b marsã: «Y yam ket n nan pa vẽnege?»
41008022	A Zezi ne b karen-biisa taa Bɛtsayid. Beene b talla zoang n wa a Zezi nengẽ la b kos-b lame tɩ b sɩɩs-a ne b nugu.
41008023	A Zezi gãda zoanga nugu n tak-a n yi kɛɛnga la b taaga a nina ne kolkoodo. Dẽ poore b tẽega b nus zoanga zugu, n sok-a a sã n nee bũmbu.
41008024	Zoanga sẽn da sɩng yãeeba, yeelame: «Mam nee neba, mam nee sẽn kẽnda, la wẽnda wa tɩɩse.»
41008025	A Zezi le sɩɩsa zoanga nini ne b nusi la rẽ poore, a yãee vẽenega la a sɩngame n paam laafi. A ra yãeta bũmba fãa vẽenega la a ra nee yɩɩg me.
41008026	A Zezi kʋls-a lame n yetẽ: «Da wɩɩg n kẽ tẽnga pʋgẽ meng ye.»
41008027	Dẽ poore a Zezi ne b karen-biisa rɩka Sezare sore, komber a Filip soolmẽ. A Zezi sok-b la sokr kãnga: «Neba yetame tɩ mam yaa ãnna?»
41008028	Karen-biisa leok-b lame: «B yetame tɩ yaa Zã ning sẽn da kõta soobã; kẽer me yetame tɩ yãmb yaa a Eli, kẽer tɩ yãmb yaa bãngdba nin-yende.»
41008029	«La yãmba, yãmb yetame tɩ mam yaa ãnna?» A Piyɛr leok-b lame: «Yãmb yaa Krista, Fãagdã.»
41008030	La a Zezi kõ-b la noore tɩ b ra sak n gom ne ned bãmb yell ye.
41008031	A Zezi sɩnga b karen-biisa zãmsgo n yeel-b tɩ yaa pakre tɩ Ned Biiga nams wʋsgo; tɩ nin-kẽemba, maan-kʋʋdba kãsẽm dãmba la Sɛb-mitba na n yi-la b poorẽ, n bas tɩ b kʋ-ba, la yaa tɩlɛ tɩ b vʋʋg b kũuma rasma tãab raare.
41008032	A Zezi wilga bãmb yell kãnga vẽenega neba fãa sʋka. A Piyɛr boola a Zezi n yi kɛɛnga la a sɩngame n zabd ne-ba, n yet tɩ b ra gom woto ye.
41008033	A Zezi kedgame n ges b karen-biisã la b zaba ne a Piyɛr: «Kẽng n leb poorẽ, Sʋtãana. Fo tagsgo ka Wẽnnaam tagsg ye, fo tagsda wala ninsaal bala.»
41008034	B kɩtame tɩ zãma wã ne b karen-biisa kolge tɩ b yeele: «Ned ning fãa sẽn dat-a n tũ maam, bɩ a soab sãbs a menga la a rɩk a pika n pʋg maam.
41008035	Ned ning sẽn dat-a n fãag a yõore, na m menes-a lame, la sẽn na n menes-a a yõore, maam la Koe-nooga nonglem yĩnga, na n fãag-a lame.
41008036	Ba ned sã n da tõeẽ n soog dũni wã gilli, rẽnda nafdẽ-la yẽnda wãn-wãna, a sɩɩga yell sã n sãam?
41008037	Bõe la ned na n dɩk n tek ne a sɩɩgã?
41008038	Ned ning fãa sẽn zoe-a yãnd ne mam tũudem la m zãmsgo, dũni nin-wẽnsa taoore, Ned Biiga me kõn saag n yeel tɩ b mii yẽ soaba, b sã n wa lɛɛg n wa ne b Ba ziiri tɩ b malɛgs sõma yãagd-b.»
41009001	A Zezi ra gomda woto ne nebã: «Sɩd-sɩda mam yeta yãmba, yãmb neb kẽer pa na n ki tɩ b pa yãend Wẽnd Rĩunga sẽn wat ne pãng la ziir ye.»
41009002	Dasem a yoob dẽ poore, a Zezi peega a Piyɛr, a Zak ne a Zã, n yi kɛɛnga, tãn-lug-lug a ye zugu. A Zezi tedga zãng fas bãmb taoore.
41009003	B futa ra pɩndame la tẽng zug ka, pɛgd-mit zɩ n tõog tɩ fuug paam bãmb dẽnda peelem ye.
41009004	A Eli ne a Moyiiz likame n gomd ne a Zezi.
41009005	T'a Piyɛr na n zẽk a koɛɛg n gom ne a Zezi: «Karen-saamba, tõnd sẽn be ka wã, d sũur yaa noogo. Tõnd na n tii zãn a tãabo: a ye yãmb yĩnga, a yembre, a Moyiiz yĩnga, a yembre, a Eli me yĩnga.»
41009006	Yẽ ra goma woto t'a ra ka mi a sẽn na n yeel bũmb ning ye. Rabeem yõk-b la wʋsgo.
41009007	Sawadg a yembr maasem luda bãmba. La Koɛɛg yii sawadgẽ wã n yetẽ: «Bãmb yaa mam Bi-nongre, bɩ y kelg-ba.»
41009008	B wẽnesame n ges la b pa le yãend ned a to n paas a Zezi ye.
41009009	B sẽn waa n sigd tãngã, a Zezi kõ-b la noore tɩ b ra sak n togs b taabã b sẽn yãend bũmb ninga ye, al tɩ Ned Biiga wa vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka.
41009010	Karen-biisa reega saglgã, n baas n sokd b mense: «Vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka» sẽn dat n yeel tɩ bũmb ninga.
41009011	B waa n soka a Zezi woto: «Bõe yĩng la sɛb-mitba yet t'a Eli n na n deng n wa?»
41009012	T'a Zezi leok-ba: «Sɩda, a Eli n dengd taoore n lebs bũmb fãa a sõmb zĩigẽ. Maana a wãn tɩ b gʋls marsã Ned Biiga poorẽ tɩ b na n namsame la b na n paama paoogr wʋsgo?
41009013	Mam yeta yãmba t'a Eli zoe n waame, la wala sẽn da gʋlse, neba maana b sẽn dat bũmb ning fãa, ne-a,»
41009014	B sẽn leb karen-biis a taaba nengẽ, b yãee zãma kãseng sẽn da tigmi. Sɛb-mitba me ra bee sʋka tɩ ya sogsgo ne sogsgo.
41009015	Neba yãenda a Zesi tɩ zĩiga wulumd tɩ ned kam fãa zoet n kolgdẽ n na n pʋʋs-ba.
41009016	A Zezi sok-b lame: «Yaa bõe koees la y ra leokd taaba?»
41009017	Ned a yembre zĩnda sʋka n yeele: «Karen-saamba, mam talla m biig n wa y nengẽ, la yaa Sʋtãan n be a pʋgẽ n kɩt t'a lebg muka.
41009018	Sʋtãana yõkd-a-la a sẽn paamẽ fãa, n lubd-a tẽnga, t'a tãntãmpuuda yita. A kẽrsda a yẽna la a yĩnga fãa tirdame. Mam kosa yãmb karen-biisã la b pa tõog n sãoog-a ye.»
41009019	A Zezi leokame: «Kɩɩsdb buudu, m na n paa ne yãmba n ta da-bʋre? M na n tõoga m sũur ne yãmb, n ta da-bʋre? Bɩ y tall y bãadã n wa!»
41009020	B talla bãadã n wa a Zezi taoore. La Sutãana sẽn yãend a Zezi la a sẽn kɩt tɩ biiga yĩnga vɩgda. Biiga waa n tol n lʋɩɩ tẽnga, n gãe n bilimdẽ la a lasd tãntãmpuudu.
41009021	A Zezi soka biiga ba: «Yaa sẽn ta yʋʋm a wãna la a ya woto?»
41009022	Tɩ ba wã na n yeele: «Yaa al a yãadme. Naoor wʋsgo Sʋtãana lubd-a-la bugmẽ bɩ koomẽ n dat n kʋ-a. Yãmb sã n tõe bɩ y zoe d nimbãanega la y sõng-do.»
41009023	T'a Zezi na n leoke: «Bõe tɩ f yet: sã n tõe? Ned ninga sẽn tẽeda, a sẽn dat fãa pitame.»
41009024	Tao-tao bala biiga ba mooname: «Mam tẽedame la bɩ y sõng-ma tɩ m tẽeba paoodame.»
41009025	A Zezi sẽn yãe tɩ neba zoet n watame b tãsa Sʋtãana: «Sʋtãan muk la wʋnga, m kõt-f la noor tɩ f yi bi-kãnga pʋgẽ la f ra leb n kẽ-a yɛs ye.»
41009026	Biiga ra tara kaasgo t'a yĩnga wils vɩgd ne pãnga tɩ Sʋtãana na n loog n bas-a t'a gãe wa kũum la neba sɩd da gomda woto: «A kiime!»
41009027	La a Zezi gãda biiga nug n yik-a yĩngri.
41009028	A Zezi kẽe zakẽ tɩ b karen-biisa na n kolg n sok-ba: «Yaa bõe yĩng tɩ tõnd yẽ pa tõog n yiis Sʋtãana?»
41009029	T'a Zezi leoke: «Sã n pa ne pʋʋsg bala, Sʋtãan kãnga buud ka tõe n dig ye.»
41009030	A Zezi yii yirã n pãrgd Galile la b ra pa rat tɩ neba bãng ye.
41009031	Dẽ tɩ b ra tara b karen-biisa zãmsgo la b ra yet-b lame: «Neb na n yõka Ned Biiga la b na n kʋ-a lame. La b sã n kʋ-a, dasma a tãab poore, a na n vʋʋgame.»
41009032	B ra pa wʋmd b gomda võor ye. La sokr dabeem da tar-b lame.
41009033	B taa Kafarnaom, la b sẽn kẽ zakẽ, a Zezi soka b karen-biisã: «Yaa bõe no-koeemde la y da wẽed sora zugu?»
41009034	Tɩ b fãa sĩnda, tɩ sor zugu b da wẽeda no-koeemde ne taaba n na n bãng bãmb taoor soaba la ãnda.
41009035	Dẽ la a Zezi zĩnd yã n bool b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã n yeel-ba: «Ned sã n dat n yɩ pipi soaba bɩ a pa a taab fãa poorẽ n yɩ a taab fãa sõgne.»
41009036	Dẽ poore b gãda biig a ye n tak-a n yaas sʋka, n mobg-a la b yetẽ:
41009037	«Ned ninga sẽn na n sak n deeg bi-bilf a woto mam yʋʋr yĩnga, yaa mam meng la a reeg yã. La ned ning sẽn na n deega maam, pa maam la a soab reegr ye, yaa sẽn tʋm-a maama.»
41009038	A Zã yeela a Zezi: «Karen-saamba, tõnd yãee ned a ye sẽn digd Sʋtãamba, yãmb yʋʋr yĩnga, la a sẽn pa tũud tõndã, tõnd da rat n dig-a lame.»
41009039	A Zezi leokame: «Bɩ y ra rig a soab ye tɩ ned pa tõe n maan wẽnd makr mam yʋʋr yĩnga n le wẽneg n gom wẽng mam poorẽ ye.
41009040	Ned ninga fãa sẽn ka-a tõnd bɛ, yaa tõnd zoa.
41009041	Ned ning sẽn na n kõ-a yãmb koom ne wamde tɩ y yũ y sẽn kẽed Krista yĩnga, sɩda, mam yeta yãmba tɩ yẽ soab kõn kong a rolb ye.
41009042	La ned ning sẽn na n sãam-a bi-bilf a yembr bal sẽn tar tẽeb sɩɩga, ad-y sãoo ne yẽ soaba, b sã n dɩk bõeensã sẽn bilgd kugr ning n werd zoma n loe a yubla n tus-a n lub mogr pʋga.
41009043	Fo nug sã n kɩt tɩ f lʋɩ yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ bɩ f fiuug-a tɩ fo sẽn na n kẽ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ pʋgẽ ne nug yende, rẽ sãoo fo sẽn na n kẽ bugum sẽn ka kiid pʋgẽ ne f nus a yiibã. [
41009044	Be zũnzũur ka kiidi, be bugum me ka kiid ye.]
41009045	Fo naoor sã n kɩt tɩ f lʋɩ yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ bɩ f kʋʋg naoorã, tɩ fo sã n kẽ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ pʋgẽ ne nao yende, sãoo fo sẽn na n lʋɩ bugmẽ ne f naoa yiibu. [
41009046	Be zũnzũur ka kiidi, be bugum me ka kiid ye.]
41009047	Fo nif sã n kɩt tɩ f lʋɩ yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ bɩ f kɩdg f nifã. Fo sã n kẽ Wẽnd Rĩung pʋgẽ ne nifr a ye, sãoo fo sẽn na n kẽ ne f nin a yiibã bug-toaagẽ.
41009048	Beenẽ zũnzũur pa kiidi, la yaa wakat fãa la bugma me wita.
41009049	Bugma na n kẽe nemsã wala yamsem.
41009050	Yamsem yaa bõn sõngo, la a sã n sãbge, yaa bõe n na n le wa ne a noosem? Tall-y yamsem y pʋsẽ la y vɩɩma ne taab yɩ laafi vɩɩm.»
41010001	A Zezi sẽn yi be, b waa Zɩɩda soolmẽ, Zʋrdẽ kʋɩlga rʋʋnde. Be me, zãma tigma b sɛɛgẽ. A Zezi le sɩngame n zãmsd nebã wa rasem kam.
41010002	Farizẽ rãmba kolgame n sok a Zezi: «Rao tara sor n yiis a pag bɩ?» Bãmb da sokda a Zezi pʋto-sokre n dat n fɛɛs-ba.
41010003	A Zezi leok-b-la woto: «A Moyiiz kõo yãmb no-bʋg yell kãnga poorẽ?»
41010004	Tɩ b yeele: «A Moyiiz kõo sore tɩ b gʋls kãadma welgr sebre la b yaool n yiis pagã.»
41010005	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Yaa y sũura sẽn kɩʋʋlma, la a Moyiiz gʋls no-kãng y yĩnga.
41010006	Dũni sɩngrẽ, Wẽnd n zĩndig rao la paga.
41010007	Yaa rẽ yĩng la rao na n bas a ba la a ma n zĩnd ne a paga,
41010008	la raoã ne pagã na n lebga yĩng a ye.
41010009	Woto yĩnga, Wẽnnaam sẽn lagem bũmb ninga, pa tog tɩ ninsaal welg-a ye.»
41010010	A Zezi sẽn waa n le kẽ zakẽ, karen-biisa sok-b-la yell kãnga poorẽ.
41010011	A Zezi leok b lame: «Ned ning sẽn yiisd-a a paga n le kẽ ne pag a to, yaa yoob la a maanda.
41010012	Sã n ya pag n yi n bas a sɩda n tɩ rɩk rao a to, yaa yoob bal la a maanda.»
41010013	Neb wʋsg waa ne b kom-bõonego a Zezi nengẽ n kot-ba tɩ b sak n sɩɩs-ba. La karen-biisa zaba ne-ba.
41010014	A Zezi sẽn yãe woto, b sũur puugame tɩ b yeele: «Bas-y kom-bõonegã tɩ b wa mam nengẽ la y ra rig-b ye. Yaa neb niyns sẽn wẽnd-b bãmba n na n soog Wẽnd Rĩungã.
41010015	Sɩd-sɩda, mam yeta yãmba tɩ ned ninga fãa sẽn ka reegd-a Wẽnd Rĩunga wala bi-bilfu, a soab kõn kẽ a pʋgẽ ye.»
41010016	Dẽ poore, a Zezi mobga kambã, n tik ned kam fãa zug ne b nugu, n ning-b barka.
41010017	A Zezi sẽn dɩk sore, la rao a yembre sẽn zoe n seg-ba n wõgemd b taoore, n sokdẽ: «Karen-saamb sõngo, mam na n maana a wãn n paam vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ?»
41010018	A Zezi yeel-a lame: «Yaa bõe yĩng la fo boond maam tɩ karen-saamb sõngo? Sã n pa Wẽnnaam b ye bala, ned ka be n ya sõng ye.
41010019	Fo mii Wẽnnaam noya la: da kʋ ned ye, da yo ye, da zu ye, da kõ kaset ziri ye, da wẽg f to ye, waoog f ba la f ma.»
41010020	La daoã leokame: «M zu-soaba, mam sɩng n maanda rẽ al m yãadmẽ.»
41010021	A Zezi ges-a-la ne nonglem, n yeel-a: «Bũmb a ye bala n paoog foo marsã: fo sẽn tar bũmb ning fãa, bɩ f rɩk n koos n kõ naong rãmba tɩ f na paam arzɛk arzãnẽ. Dẽ poore, bɩ f wa tũ maam.»
41010022	La raoã sẽn wʋm woto, a sũur sãamame t'a gãnem a neng n looge t'a ra tara laog wʋsgo.
41010023	A Zezi gesa sẽn da be-b bãmb sɛɛgẽ wã la b yeela b karen-biisã: «Wẽnnaam Rĩung pugẽ kõom na n yɩɩ toogo ne neb niyns fãa sẽn tar-b arzɛka!»
41010024	Gomda yɩka karen-biisa pɛlenga t'a Zezi na n le yeel-ba, n paase: «M kamba, ad-y Wẽnnaam Rĩunga pugẽ kõom na n yɩɩ toogo ne arzɛk rãmba!
41010025	Yʋgemd sẽn na n tũ supĩim yõore n loog yaa naana n yɩɩd arzɛk soab sẽn na n kẽ Wẽnnaam Rĩungã pugẽ.»
41010026	Tɩ bãmb na n le yɛɛs n paas la b yet taaba: «Sã n ya woto, ãnda n na n paam fãagre?»
41010027	A Zezi ges-b-la pem, n yeel-ba: «Yaa toog ne ninsaalba, la ka toog ne Wẽnd ye tɩ bãmb tõee fãa.»
41010028	A Piyɛr yeela a Zezi: «Ges-y, tõnd basa bũmba fãa n tũ yãmba.»
41010029	A Zezi leokame: «Sɩd-sɩda, mam yeta yãmba, tɩ ned ning fãa sẽn sak-a n bas a yiri, a yaopa, a tãopa, a ma la a ba, a kamba bɩ a pʋto, mam yĩnga la Koe-nooga yĩnga,
41010030	yẽ soab na n paama naoor koabga, marsã menga, doto, yaopa, tãopa, ma rãmba, kamba la pʋto. Namsg yẽ na naage, la zamaan ning sẽn pʋgdã, na n yɩɩ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ.
41010031	Wʋsgo sẽn da ya pipi rãmba na n lebga poorẽ dãmba tɩ poorẽ dãmb na n lebg pipi rãmba.»
41010032	B ra rɩka sor n dabd Zerizalɛɛm. A Zezi meng ra lʋɩɩ bãmb taoore la b fãa ra kẽnda ne pɛlen-yɩka, b fãa ra pʋgda ne yɛɛsgo. A Zezi baka Piig la a yiibã la b sɩngame n wilgd-b yɛl niyns sẽn na n paam bãmb menga:
41010033	«Ade, tõnd dabda Zerizalɛɛm la b na n yõka Ned Biigã n kɩs maan-kʋʋdba nanamse la Sɛb-mitba; bãmb n na n kao b kũum bʋʋdo, n bas-b bu-zẽmba nusẽ,
41010034	tɩ b na n yaal-ba, n sẽnes b neng kolkoodo, n pãb-b ne kaase, n kʋ-ba, la dasma a tãab poore, b na n vʋʋgame.»
41010035	A Zebede kamba, a Zak la a Zã, kolga a Zezi n yeel-ba: «Karen-saamba, d kotame tɩ y kõ-d d sẽn na n kos-y bũmb ningã.»
41010036	T'a Zezi yeel-ba: «Yaa bõe la y rat tɩ m maan y yĩnga!»
41010037	B leokame: «Y zɩɩra zĩigẽ, bɩ y sõng tɩ d nin-yend zĩnd y rɩtgo, t'a to wã zĩnd y goabga.»
41010038	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yãmb pa mi y sẽn kot bũmb ning ye. Yãmb tõe n yũu wamd ning b sẽn na n tugl-ma la y so koom ning b sẽn na n so-ma?»
41010039	B leok-b lame: «Tõnd tõeeme.» La a Zezi yeel-b lame: «Mam sẽn na n yũ wamd ningã yãmb me na yũ-a. Mam sẽn na n so soob ninga, yãmb me na so.
41010040	La sã n kella mam goabg la rɩtg zĩigã, mam pa tõe n kõ yãmb rẽ ye. Zĩ-kãens yaa b sẽn segl b rãmb yĩnga.»
41010041	Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piiga sẽn wʋm a Zak la a Zã goama b sũur puuga ne-ba.
41010042	A Zezi boola bãmb fãa n yeel-ba: «Yãmb miime tɩ bu-zẽmba nanams rɩta naam b soolma rãmb zutu la b nin-bɛda maand-b la pãnga.
41010043	Pa na n yɩ boto ne yãmb ye, ayoo! Yãmb sʋka, ned sã n dat n lebg nin-kãsenga, bɩ a reng n yɩ yãmb sõgne.
41010044	La ned ninga sẽn dat-a n yɩ pipi soaba, yãmb sʋka, bɩ a soab reng n yɩ yãmb fãa yamba.
41010045	Ned Biiga meng ka wa tẽng zugu n dat tɩ neb maana a yam ye; a waame n na n maan neb a taab yam, la a kõ a meng vɩɩm neb wʋsg fãagr yĩnga.»
41010046	B taa Zeriko. La bãmb sẽn waa n yit be ne b karen-biisã la zãma kãsengã, a Bartime, a Time biiga, sẽn ya zoanga, ra zĩi sora noor n bõsdẽ.
41010047	A sẽn wʋm tɩ b gomd tɩ yaa Nazarɛt Zezi, a mooname: «Zezi, Daviid biiga, zoe-y mam nimbãanega.»
41010048	Neb wʋsg da zabda ne-a, n yet t'a sĩnd a noore. La yẽ da moondame n yɩɩd pĩnda: «Daviid biiga, zoe-y mam nimbãanega.»
41010049	A Zezi yaasame n yeel: «Bool-y zoangã!» Tɩ b bool-a n yeel-a: «Keng f pɛlga, yik tɩ b boond-f lame.»
41010050	La zoanga loba a fuug n wudg n ta a Zezi taoore.
41010051	A Zezi sok-a lame: «Fo ratame tɩ m maan-f bõe?» Tɩ zoanga yeele: «Karen-saamba, sõng-y tɩ m nina puki!»
41010052	La a Zezi yeel-a lame: «Bɩ f kẽng tɩ f tẽeb fãag-f lame.» La tao-tao bala, a nina pukame, t'a ra tũud a Zezi.
41011001	B sẽn waa n kolg Zerizalɛɛm, Bɛtfaze la Betani sẽn ta la bala, Oliviye tãnga pennẽ, a Zezi tʋma b karen-biis a yiibu.
41011002	B yeel-b lame: «Bɩ y kẽng tẽng ning sẽn tond y taoorã; y sã n ta, y na n yãe bõn-bil sẽn loe; ned ba a ye nan pa zomb-a ye. Bɩ y lok-a n wa ne.
41011003	Ned sã n yeel yã: ‹Yaa bõe la y maand woto?› bɩ y yeel: ‹Yaa Soaala n tar a tʋʋmde, la a na bas-y tɩ y wa ne a.› »
41011004	B kẽngame la b yãee bõn-bil sẽn loe, yir sɛɛgẽ la sor noore, la b lok-a lame.
41011005	Neb niyns sẽn da pẽ-ba sok-b lame: «Yaa bõe yĩng la y lokd bõn-bilã?»
41011006	Karen-biisa leokame wala a Zezi sẽn togs bãmbã la neba bas-b lame tɩ b looge.
41011007	B talla bõangã n wa a Zezi nengẽ, b palga bõangã b futu, t'a Zezi yaool n zomb-a.
41011008	Neb wʋsg yɛdga b fut sora zugu la kẽer me kɛɛ vãad, pʋtẽ, n gãneg sorã.
41011009	Neb niyns sẽn da lʋɩ-b a Zezi taoore la sẽn da pʋgd-b poorẽ, fãa ra moondame: «Kilill! Sẽn wata Soaala yʋʋr yĩnga paam barka!
41011010	D kils naam sẽn wate, d kils d ba a Daviid Naama! Kilill, Yĩngr soaba paam pẽgre!»
41011011	A Zezi kẽe Zerizalɛɛm, wẽnd dooga pʋga, b gesa bũmb ning fãa sẽn da be wẽnd doogẽ wã, la zĩig sẽn da zoe n sɩng sobgr yĩnga, b yii ne b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã n dɩk Betani sore.
41011012	Beoog sẽn vẽege, t'a Zezi yit Betani, tɩ kom tar-ba,
41011013	b yãee kankang a yembr yɩɩg ne vãado; b kolgame n na n ges b kõn yãend kankam a zugu. B sẽn ta, b pa yãend bũmb sã n pa vãad bala. Da pa kankam wakat ye.
41011014	A Zezi goma ne kankangã: «Dũnna tɛka ned ba a ye kõn le rɩ fo biig ye.» La b Tʋʋm-tʋmdba ra kelgdame.
