41014008	Pʋg kãnga maana a sẽn da tõe n maan bũmb ninga. A sẽn zɛ mam yĩnga ne kaama, a zoe n beoolame n segl m mumbu.
41014009	Sɩd-sɩda mam yeta yãmb tɩ dũni wã fãa pʋgẽ, b sẽn na n togs Kibar nooga zĩig ning fãa, b na gom pʋg kãnga sẽn maana me yelle.»
41014010	Dẽ poore, piig la a yiiba nin-yend sẽn boond tɩ Zɩɩda, Iskariyot tẽng neda, kẽngame n tɩ yẽs ne maan-kʋʋdba nanamse n yet t'a na yõk a Zezi n kõ-ba.
41014011	B sẽn wʋm woto, b sũur yɩɩ noog wʋsgo tɩ b kãab-a ligdi. A Zɩɩda ra baooda marsã, wakat ning a sẽn na n yõk a Zezi.
41014012	Bura sẽn pa le ningd bɩlla sɩngr daare, pe-bila kʋʋb daare, karen-biisa soka a Zezi: «Yãmb datame tɩ d segl pak rɩɩb yɛɛlẽ?»
41014013	A Zezi tʋma bãmb neb a yiibu: «Kẽng-y tẽnga pʋgẽ tɩ y na seg rao a ye sẽn zɩt yʋʋre ne koom.
41014014	Bɩ y pʋg-a n kẽ a sẽn na n kẽ zĩig ningã la beene, y na yeel zaka soaba: ‹Soaala n tʋm tõndo tɩ d wa sok yãmba n ges yaa do-bʋgo la b na n paam n dɩ pak rɩɩbo ne b karen-biisã?›
41014015	A na n wilg-y-la do-kãsenga sẽn dog a to zugu la sẽn be neere. Do-kãng pʋg zoe n manegame n sɛ. Segl-y paka rɩɩb be.»
41014016	Sẽn tʋm b rãmba yii n loogame la b yãee fãa w-a a Zezi sẽn pĩn n togsã la b segla paka rɩɩbo.
41014017	Zaabr sẽn ta, a Zezi waa ne b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã.
41014018	B sẽn waa n dɩtẽ, a Zezi yeel-b lame: «Ade m yeta yãmba tɩ yãmb nin-yend n na n zãmb maam. Yẽ soab rɩta ne maam marsã.»
41014019	Bãmb fãa ra zĩi ne sũ-sãanga la ned kam fãa ra sokdame: «Soaala, yaa maam bɩ?»
41014020	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yaa yãmb piig la a yiibã nin-yende, yaa ned sẽn naaga maam n tʋmd a nug laagẽ.
41014021	Ned Biiga sɩd na n looga wa b sẽn da pĩnd n gʋls a poorẽ, la yell na pak Ned Biiga zãmbdã. Nin-kãng sã n da pa rogẽ n são.»
41014022	B sẽn waa n dɩtẽ, a Zezi rɩka bur n ning-a barka n wes n pʋɩ b karen-biisã n yetẽ: «Deeg-y tɩ woto yaa mam yĩnga.»
41014023	B rɩka laog neere ne rãam n pʋʋs bark pʋʋsgo n yaool n dɩk n kõ-ba. Ned kam fãa reegame n yũ.
41014024	A Zezi yaool n yeel-b lame: «Woto yaa m zooda zɩɩm, Zooda sẽn yõg ne zɩɩma m sẽn daag neb fãa yĩnga.
41014025	Sɩd-sɩda mam yeta yãmba tɩ m kõn leb n yũ bugsuntung sõng biis rãam n tol n ta raar ning m sẽn na n leb n wa yũ a rã paalga Wẽnd Rĩunga pʋga.»
41014026	B sẽn yɩɩl bark yɩɩl n sɛ, b yiime n dɩk Oliviye tãng sore.
41014027	A Zezi waa n yeel-b lame: «Yãmb fãa na n basa raood ne mam pʋgbo tɩ b gʋlsame: M na pãba pe-kɩɩma la pe-yãansa na n sẽegame.
41014028	La m sã n wa vʋʋge, m na reng yãmb Galile.»
41014029	T'a Piyɛr na n leok-ba: «Ba m taaba fãa sã n na kɩɩs tɩ b ka mi yãmba, kõn yɩ maam ye.»
41014030	A Zezi yeel-a lame: «Sɩd la m sẽn yet fooma: yʋnga bala no-raoog kõn kelem naoor a yiibu tɩ foom, a Piyɛr, pa kɩɩs naoor a tã tɩ f ka mi-m ye.»
41014031	La a Piyɛr le yeela ne pãnga n yɩɩd pĩnda: «Ba m na naag yãmba n ki, m kõn yeel abada tɩ m ka mi yãmb ye.» La karen-biis a taaba me yeela wa a Piyɛr.
41014032	B taa zĩig a ye sẽn boond tɩ Zɛtsemani la beene a Zezi yeela b karen-biisã: «Zĩnd-y ka tɩ m zãag n pʋʋs la m wa.»
41014033	B peega a Piyɛr, a Zak ne a Zã n zãag bilfu. Wakat kãnga sũ-sãang la yɩɩr yõk-b lame.
41014034	Dẽ la b yeel b karen-biisã: «Sũ-sãang n tar maam la sũ-sãanga seka m kũum. Bɩ y zĩnd ka la y ra gũs ye.»
41014035	B zãaga bilfu n lʋɩ tẽng n sɩng pʋʋsgo, n kotẽ tɩ namsga wakata zãag ne-ba, sã n tõe.
41014036	B ra pʋʋsda woto: «M Ba, bũmb ka be n ya toog ne yãmb ye. Y sã n dat bɩ y zãag namsg kãnga ne maam, la baasg fãa, bɩ y maan y sẽn dat la y ra tũ mam daab ye.»
41014037	Dẽ poore b le waa b karen-biisa nengẽ la b mikame tɩ b gõe. A Zezi neka a Piyɛr n yeel-a: «Piyɛr, fo gõeeme laa? Fo ka tõe f meng wakat a ye pʋgẽ bal n ka gũsi?
41014038	Bas-y gõeem la y pʋʋse n da wa lʋɩ kʋɩɩbg pʋgẽ ye. Ninsaal wɩɩda pãng a raabẽ, la yĩngẽ wã, a pãng paooda.»
41014039	B leba b pʋʋsga zĩigẽ la b pʋʋsame n le togs pĩnd goama.
41014040	B sẽn le lɛɛg n wa karen-biisa nengẽ, b le mikame tɩ b ket n gõe. Gõeem da tar-b la wʋsgo la b ra ka mi b sẽn leokd bũmb ning ye.
41014041	A Zezi le waa b nengẽ naoor a tãab soaba la b yeel-b lame: «Y sã n dat bɩ y gũs marsã la y vʋʋse tɩ fãa sɛɛme. Wakata taame; yaa marsã la b na n yõk Ned Biiga n kɩs yel-wẽn-maandba.
41014042	Aya! Yik-y tɩ d loog tɩ sẽn na n zãmba Ned Biiga kolgame.»
41014043	A Zezi da ket n gomdame t'a Zɩɩda wẽneg n ta ne neb ka tɛk sẽn zãad sʋʋs la rasaba. Yaa tẽnga kãsem dãmba la maan-kʋʋdba nanamse n da tʋm-ba.
41014044	Zãmbda ra pĩnd n kõ-b la makre: «Mam sẽn na n mobg ned ningã, yaa yẽ, bɩ y yõk-a la y tall-a ne gũusgu.»
41014045	A Zɩɩda sẽn ta bala, a wẽneg n kolga a Zezi n yetẽ: «Soaala, m pʋʋsda yãmba.» La a mobg-b lame.
41014046	La neba yõka a Zezi.
41014047	Ned a yembr sẽn da be a Zezi sɛɛgẽ wõoga a sʋʋga n kɛ maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sõgen tʋbre n fiuugi.
41014048	La a Zezi goma ne nebã n yetẽ: «Yãmb waa ne sʋʋse n na n yõk maam, wala mam yaa so-gɩta.
41014049	Daar fãa mam da bee wẽnd doogẽ n zãmsd neba, la yãmb pa yõk maam wakat kãng ye. Dẽ fãa yaa sẽn na yɩla tɩ bãngdba gʋlsg tõog n taase.»
41014050	Wakat kãnga karen-biisa fãa basa a Zezi n zoe.
41014051	Bi-bɩɩg a yembr n da pʋgd a Zezi. Yaa fu-goabg bal la a ra pil yã. Tãb-biisa sẽn yõk-a,
41014052	a fãagame n zoe a bɩlgemde, n bas fu-goabga bãmb nusẽ.
41014053	B talla a Zezi n kẽng maan-kʋʋd kãseng yiri. Maan-kʋʋdba nanamse, tẽnga kãsem-dãmb la Sɛb-mitba fãa ra tigma be.
41014054	A Piyɛr pʋg-b la yɩɩga n wa tol n kẽ kãsma zakẽ n tɩ zĩ ne tãb-biisã n woot bugum.
41014055	Maan-kʋʋdba nanamse la tẽnga kãsem dãmba ra baooda yell sẽn na n dogl a Zezi zugu n yaool n tõog n kao b kũum bʋʋdo, la b ra pa yãet fɩ.
41014056	Kaset-zirẽ dãmb wʋsg waa be, la b toagsga ra pa segd taab ye.
41014057	Neb kẽer yikame n yagd zirẽ n yetẽ:
41014058	«Tõnd wʋma a sẽn yeele: mam na n wãa wẽnd do-kãnga, neb nus sẽn me, la dasma a tãab pʋgẽ bala m na lebs n me a to sẽn pa na n yɩ ninsaal nug tʋʋmd ye.»
41014059	Yell kãnga poorẽ me b yelsma da pa zemsd taab ye.
41014060	Dẽ la maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yik a toore neba sʋka n sok a Zezi: «Y pa leokd tɩ bũmb laa? Yaa bõe kaset la b kõt yãmb poorẽ woto?»
41014061	A Zezi sĩnda b noore n pa leok tɩ bũmb ye. Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yeela a Zezi: «Yaa foom la Wẽnnaam sẽn tʋm a soba bɩ?»
41014062	A Zezi leokame: «N-yẽe! Yaa mam menga. La yãmb na yãend Ned Biiga t'a zĩ Wẽnnaam pãng soab rɩtgo, la a yit sawat zug n watẽ.»
41014063	Dẽ la maan-kʋʋd kãsenga kẽes a fut n yetẽ: «Tõnd tara kaset dãmb tʋʋmd yɛs bi?
41014064	Yamb wʋma a sẽn tʋʋs Wẽnnaam yʋʋre, yãmb tagsdame tɩ bõe?» La b fãa yeelame t'a toga ne kũum.
41014065	Neb kẽer sɩngame n tʋbsd a Zezi neng ne kolkoodo. B pila b neng ne pɛɛla n pãbd-b pegse n yetẽ: «Bɩ f bãng sẽn ya ned ninga n wẽ fooma!» Naab ka loog ka rãmba pãb-b la wʋsgo.
41014066	A Piyɛr sẽn waa n be zakẽ wã, maan-kʋʋd kãseng zakẽ, bi-pugl n wa be.
41014067	A yãenda a Piyɛr sẽn da zĩi n woot bugma, a gesa a neng n yetẽ: «Fo me ra bee ne a Zezi, Nazarɛt nedã.»
41014068	A Piyɛr kɩɩsame n yetẽ: «Mam pa mi-a ye. Mam pa wʋmd fo sẽn dat n yeel tɩ bũmb ning ye.» A Piyɛr yiime n leb zãongẽ, la wakat kãnga no-raoog kelmame.
41014069	Bi-pugla sẽn paam n ges neere, a yeela neb niyns sẽn da be-b be wã: «Ad-a sɩd yaa bãmb neda.»
41014070	La a Piyɛr le kɩɩsame. Sẽn yɩ bilfu rẽ poore, sẽn da be-b be wã fãa yeela a Piyɛr: «Sã n ya sɩda, fo yaa bãmb neda, fo yaa Galile neda.»
41014071	La a Piyɛr sɩngame n kãabd a meng la wẽene: «Mam ka mi ned ning yãmb sẽn gomd a soab yella ye.»
41014072	La wakat kãng bala no-raoog kelma naoor a yiib soaba. A Piyɛr tẽega a Zezi sẽn da yeel yẽnd gomd ninga: «No-raoog kõn kelem naoor a yiibu tɩ fo pa kɩɩs maam naoor a tãab ye.» La a sɩnga yãbre.
41015001	Beoog sẽn waa n vẽege, maan-kʋʋdb nanamse, tẽnga kãsem dãmba, Sɛb-mitba la bʋ-kaoodba tigma taaba n na n ges b sẽn na n maan bũmb ninga. B kɩtame tɩ b sẽb a Zezi ne wĩyã n tall-ba n kẽng a Pilat nengẽ.
41015002	A Pilat soka a Zezi: «Yaa foom la Zʋɩf rãmba dĩma bɩ?» T'a Zezi leoke: «Yãmb meng yeelame.»
41015003	Maan-kʋʋdba nanams rõda a Zezi ne rõadg buud fãa.
41015004	A Pilat soka a Zezi yɛsa: «Fo pa leokd tɩ bũmb laa? Ges b sẽn dõt foo ne rõadg ning wɛ!»
41015005	La a Zezi kell n pa leok tɩ bũmb ye, al t'a Pilat pɛleng ra yɩgda.
41015006	Zʋɩf rãmba sã n da mii n maand kibs kãseng fãa, a Pilat da mii n yiisda roogo bi-bɛɛg ninga neba sẽn da kot-a t'a yiisi.
41015007	Zemsame tɩ wakat kãnga neb wʋsg tigma taab n kos a Pilat t'a yiis bi-bɛɛg a yembre, waa a sẽn mii n maand yʋʋmd fãa.
41015008	Bi-bɛɛg a yembre n da be bi-beesa roogẽ, t'a yʋʋr boond tɩ Barabas. Yẽ n da naag a tũud-n-taas n kʋ ned, zabr sẽn yik tẽnga pʋgẽ.
41015009	A Pilat sok-b lame: «Yãmb datame tɩ m yiis Zʋɩf rãmba dĩm n kõ-y bɩ?»
41015010	A Pilat meng ra miime tɩ yaa sũ-kiir yĩnga la maan-kʋʋdba nanams ra yõk a Zezi n wa yẽ nengẽ.
41015011	Maan-kʋʋdba nanams sagla neba tɩ b kos a Barabas yiisgu.
41015012	A Pilat soka neba yɛsa: «La mam maanda bõe ne yãmb sẽn boond a soab tɩ Zʋɩf rãmb dĩma?»
41015013	La neba mooname yɛsa: «Bɩ y ka-a pika.»
41015014	A Pilat sok-b lame: «A maana bõe sẽn ya wẽnga?» Zʋɩf rãmba mooname n yɩɩd pĩnda: «Bɩ y ka-a pika.»
41015015	A Pilat sẽn da rat n noog neba sũur yĩnga, a yiisa a Barabas n kõ-ba, dẽ poore, a kɩtame tɩ b pãb a Zezi ne kaase la a kõ-b la sor tɩ b ka-b pika.
41015016	Tãb-biisa talla a Zezi n kẽ zaka yaanga la b boola tãb-biisa fãa sẽn da beb be tɩ b wa tigim.
41015017	Dẽ poore, b yeelga a Zezi fu-miuugu la b kãama gõos gʋlle n teeg a Zezi zugu.
41015018	B ra pʋʋsd-b lame n yetẽ: «M pʋʋsda yãmb, Zʋɩf rãmba dĩma.»
41015019	B ra pãbda a Zezi zug ne tãnwĩiga la b sẽnesd b neng ne kolkoodo. B ra wõgemda b taoore n pʋʋsd-ba.
41015020	B sẽn wa n yaal a Zezi n tɩge b yeega fu-miuugã n le pil-b b meng fuugu.
41015021	Dẽ poore, b talla a Zezi n na n tɩ ka-b pika. Sor zugu, b sega rao a yembre sẽn yi a weoogẽ n kuiisẽ, a yʋʋr la a Simo. A da yaa Sirɛn neda, a Aleksãndr la a Rufus baaba. B modg-a lame t'a reeg a Zezi pikã n zɩ.
41015022	B talla a Zezi n kẽng zĩig a yembr sẽn boond tɩ Golgota. Dat n yeelame tɩ zu-waanga.
41015023	B kõ-la a Zezi rãam sẽn pul tɩdare la b pa sak n yũ ye.
41015024	B ka a Zezi pika, la b rɩka b futã n pʋɩ taaba. B poeesame n na n bãng fuug fãa soaal sẽn na n yɩ a soaba.
41015025	B sẽn waa n ka a Zezi n sɛ, dẽ tɩ yaa wĩnto-sʋka
41015026	la b da gʋlsame n wilg b sẽn lʋɩɩs bũmb ning taoore n na n kʋ a Zezi: «Zezi, Zʋɩf rãmba dĩma.»
41015027	B ra kaa wagda a yiibu n naag ne a Zezi, a yembre a Zezi rɩtgo, a yembre b goabga. [
41015028	Yaa woto la sẽn gʋls Sebra pʋgẽ tõog n taase: b sõd-a la nin-wẽens sʋka.]
41015029	Sẽn da loogdeb be wã fãa ra tʋʋsda a Zezi la b gird b zutu n yetẽ: «Aya! Fo sẽn tõe n wã wẽnd doogã n le me-a rasem a tãab pʋgẽ wã, aya! Sig pika marsã n fãag f menga.»
41015030	Maan-kʋʋdba nanamse, Sɛb-mitba ra laada ne taaba n yetẽ:
41015031	«A fãaga a taaba la a pa tõe n fãag a meng ye.
41015032	Wẽnnaam Tʋʋm-tʋmda la Israyɛl dãmba dĩma, sig pika zug marsã tɩ d yãend n yaool n tẽ.» Ba b sẽn da naag neb niyns n ka pika ne a Zezi wã, bãmb me ra laad-b lame.
41015033	Wakat a yoob soab sẽn ta, lik bui tẽnga zãnga, al tɩ ta zaabre.
41015034	Zafare, a Zezi moona ne koɛɛg kãsenga: «Eloi, Eloi, lema sabaktani?» (Eli, Eli, yaa bõe yĩng tɩ y basd maam?)
41015035	Neb kẽer sẽn da pẽ wʋma a Zezi goama la b yeela taaba: «Ad-a boonda a Eli.»
41015036	La ned a yembr wudgame n dɩk bũmb sẽn fõogd koom n los rã-miisgẽ n sel-a tãnwĩig n kõ a Zezi tɩ b yu. B ra yetame: «Bas woto tɩ d gese a Eli na waa n sik-a.»
41015037	La a Zezi zẽka b koɛɛg n moon ne pãnga la b kii wakat kãnga.
41015038	Wakat kãng bala, wẽnd doog peen-kãsenga kẽegame, al yĩngri n ta tẽnga.
41015039	Tãnsoab n da yɛs pika tẽngre. A sẽn yãe t'a Zezi kiime a yeelame: «Sɩd-sɩda nin-kãnga ra yaa Wẽnnaam Biiga.»
41015040	Pagb kẽer da yɛsa yɩga n getẽ. A Mari Madelɛn, a Mari, a Zak la a Zozɛf ma, n paas a Zebede kamba ma, ra bee bãmb sʋka.
41015041	A Zezi sẽn waa n be Galile, yaa bãmb n da tũud-b la b ra sõngd-b. Pʋs n yɩɩ pagb wʋsgo n da tũ ba n wa Zerizalɛɛm.
41015042	Zĩiga da zoe n sobgame, la sẽn da ya vʋʋsg ket tɩ beoog seglg yĩnga,
41015043	Arimati ned a yembre sẽn boond t'a Zozɛf, da yaa nin-kãsenga bʋʋdba sʋka. Yẽ ra gũuda Wẽnd Rĩunga waoongo la yẽ n keng a sũuri n kẽng a Pilat nengẽ n tɩ kos a Zezi yĩnga.
41015044	A Pilat pɛleng yɩka a sẽn wʋm t'a Zezi zoee n kiime t'a bool tãnsoabã n sok-a n bãng kũuma sẽn yɩ sasa ninga.
41015045	A sẽn paam tãnsoaba leokre, a kɩsa kũuma a Zozɛf.
41015046	A Zozɛf raa peende la a sika a Zezi yĩnga n vil-a ne peende n yaool n gãneg-a yaoog sẽn tuk pĩigẽ. Dẽ poore, a bilga kug bedre n pag yaooga noore.
41015047	A Mari Madelɛn la a Mari, a Zozɛf ma, da geta b sẽn gãnegd a Zezi zĩig ningã.
41016001	Sibri daar sẽn looge, a Mari Madelɛn la a Mari, a Zak ma, n paas a Salome, daa yũ-noog kaam n na n tɩ zɛ a Zezi yĩnga.
41016002	Ata daar yibeoogo, wĩndg sẽn puk paalem, b waa yaoogẽ wã.
41016003	Bãmb da gomda ne taaba: «Yaa ãnna n na n bilg yaooga kugr n kõ-do?»
41016004	La b sẽn doog b nenga b yãeeme tɩ kugra billgame n dɩg kɛɛnga. Kugra ra bɛdma al wʋsgo.
41016005	B kẽe yaoogẽ wã la b yãee bi-bɩɩg sẽn da zĩ rɩtgo n yer fu pɛɛlga la rabeem kãseng yõk-b lame.
41016006	Daoa yeel-b lame: «Da zoe-y rabeem ye! Yãmb baooda a Zezi, Nazarɛt nedã b sẽn da ka pika, b vʋʋgame, b ka le be ka yɛs ye, ad-b sẽn da gãneg bãmb zĩig ninga.
41016007	La bɩ y kẽng n tɩ wilg b tũud-n-taasã la a Piyɛr n yɩɩda, tɩ b na n denga bãmb Galile, la yaa beene la y na n yãend-ba, wa b meng sẽn pĩnd n wilgi.»
41016008	B sẽn yi yaoogẽ wã, b zoeeme n zãag. Bãmb fãa ra rigdame, la b ra pa le so b meng yɛs ye. Dabeem sẽn da tar-b yĩnga, b pa sak n gom ne ned ba a ye. [
41016009	A Zezi vʋʋga ata raar yibeoogo la b reng n lika a Mari Madelɛn.
41016010	Yaa yẽ pʋgẽ la a Zezi ra yiis Sʋtãamb a yopoe. A kẽngame n tɩ togs kibarã a Zezi tũud-n-taasã. Bãmb fãa sũr da sãamame al tɩ b ra ket n yãbda.
41016011	Bãmb sẽn wʋm t'a Zezi vʋʋgame la a Mari Madelɛn yãend-b lame, b pa sak n tẽ ye.
41016012	Dẽ poore, yaa bãmb neb a yiibu la a Zezi lik sor zugu ne yĩng sẽn da ka le wẽnd pind dẽnda; nin-bãmb da rabda b weoogẽ.
41016013	Bãmb lɛɛg n wa togsa kibarã b taaba la b pa sak n tẽ bãmb me ye.
41016014	Dẽn zugẽ yɩɩ Tʋʋm-tʋmb piig la a yembrã la a Zezi likyã. Bãmb da zĩi n dɩta wakat kãnga. A Zezi sãbsa bãmb me b sũ-keelma yĩnga la b sẽn pa sak n tẽ wã yĩnga. Bãmb pa tẽ neb niyns sẽn da yãend-b a Zezi sẽn yi kɩɩms sʋk ye.
41016015	A Zezi yeela b Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã: «Bɩ y kẽng dũni fãa pʋgẽ n zãms neb Kibar noogã.
41016016	Ned ninga sẽn na n saka n tẽ, la sẽn na n saka n deeg soobo, yẽ soab na n paama fãagre. La ned ning sẽn na n zãgsa tẽebo, yẽ soab na palga a menga.
41016017	Ad sẽn na n tẽbã sẽn na n maam bõn-bãn niynsi: mam yʋʋr yĩnga, b na n diga sʋtãamba. B na n goma bu-zẽmb goama.
41016018	Bãmb na n yõga wiis ne b nusi, la b sã n wa yũ zẽnem me, a kõn maan-b bũmb ye. B sã n sɩɩs bãad-dãmb ne b nusi, b na n paama laafi.»
41016019	A Zezi sẽn waa n gom ne bãmb n sɛ, b yɩkame n dʋ yĩngri. B zĩi Wẽnnaam dɩtgo.
41016020	La Tʋʋm-tʋmdba saaga zĩis fãa n zãms Kibar noogã, la Soaala ra sõngd-b lame, la b da maanda wẽnd makr dãmba n paasdẽ.]
42001001	Ad-y yɛl niyns fãa sẽn maan tõnd sʋka, neb wʋsg n yik n na n gʋls ba,
42001002	n gʋls-b tɩ tũ wala pipi Koe-nooga moandb sẽn yãend ne b nini.
42001003	Bãmb nao la m pʋgyã, n le vɛɛs yɛla fãa, al b sɩngrẽ n na n gʋls-b fo yĩnga, m nin-sõngo Teofil.
42001004	La woto wã f na bãng tɩ f sẽn paam zãmsgo ninga ka naag ne zirẽ lɛ-lɛ.
42001005	Zɩɩde naab a Erod zamaanẽ, maan-kʋʋd a ye n da be, a Abia sakẽ, n boond t'a Zakari, t'a pag sẽn boond t'a Elizabɛt yaa Aarõ yagenga.
42001006	Bãmb b yiiba da yaa nin-sõma Wẽnnaam taoore n da tũud Soaala noya la b raaba fãa, tɩ wɩdg ka ye.
42001007	B ra pa tar biig ye, t'a Elizabɛt ra yaa pɩg-kiiri; la bãmb b yiiba fãa ra kʋʋlame.
42001008	Sẽn waa n beẽ, maan-kʋʋra tʋʋmd gilgame n ta a Zakari saka. B poeesa wala b sẽn mii n maandẽ,
42001009	la lʋɩɩ yẽ zug, t'a kẽ Sõmblem Naab meng roogẽ n yõog wisdu.
42001010	Wisda yõogr wakato, zãma wã paa yɩnga n pʋsdẽ.
42001011	La Soaala malɛka lika a Zakari, wisda maan-kugra rɩtgo.
42001012	A Zakari sẽn yãe-a, a yɛɛsame la rabeem yõk-a lame.
42001013	Tɩ malɛka yeel-a: «Ra zoe rabeem ye, Zakari, tɩ f pʋʋsg reegame, fo pag na n doga biig n kõ-fo la f na n pʋda a yʋʋr a Zã.
42001014	A rogma na n pidsa fo menga la neb wʋsgo ne sũ-noog la na yɩ kɩdengo.
42001015	A Zã na n yɩɩ nin-kãseng Soaala taoore; a kõn yũ rãam la toos ye. A na n pida ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo t'a ket a ma pʋgẽ.
42001016	A na n talla Israyɛl kamb wʋsgo tɩ b lɛɛg n wa kẽ Soaala, bãmb Wẽnnaam.
42001017	A na n lʋɩɩ Soaala taoore ne a Eli yam la a pãnga; a na wẽnemda ba rãmb la kamba sũur n tees taaba. A na n kõo kɩɩsdba nin-sõma wã yam sõngo, la woto a na n segl buud sõngo n kõ Soaalã.»
42001018	A Zakari yeela malɛkã: «Bõe n na n sõng-m tɩ m bãng rẽnna? M yaa nin-kẽema, m pag me kʋʋlame.»
42001019	La malɛka leok-a lame: «Mam la a Gabriyɛl sẽn yɛs Wẽnnaam taoore, la b tʋm-m lame tɩ m wa gom ne foo la m togs-f koe-noog kãnga.
42001020	La ade, fo na n lebga muka, fo kõn le tõog n gome, n tol n tãag yɛl kãensa fãa taasg raare, fo sẽn pa tẽ m goama yĩnga, la b yaool n na n pidsame, b raara sã n ta.»
42001021	La neba fãa yaool n da gũuda a Zakari, tɩ b pɛlens yɩgda a sẽn kaoosd wẽnd doogẽ wã.
42001022	A sẽn waa n yi, a makame t'a na n gom ne nebã, n konge. Dẽ la b bãng t'a paama likr wẽnd doogẽ. Yẽ menga ra kong n bilgda ne nugu, la a kell n yɩɩ muka.
42001023	A Zakari sẽn maan a tʋʋmna n pids a raare, a leba a yiri.
42001024	Sẽn yɩ bilf rẽ poore, a paga, a Elizabɛt, dɩka pʋga; a solga a meng kiis a nu. La yẽ meng n waa n gomda:
42001025	«Ad-y Soaala yaa n maana bũmb m yĩnga. Yaa n ta-la b raabo tɩ b rok m yãnd ninsaalb sʋka!»
42001026	Kiis a yoob sẽn sõd dẽ poore, Wẽnnaam tʋma malɛk a Gabriyɛl Galile tẽng a ye sẽn boond tɩ Nazarɛt,
42001027	bi-pugl a yembr nengẽ, b sẽn da kõ sɩd sẽn boond t'a Zozɛf n yaa a Daviid buud neda. Bi-pugla yʋʋr da boondame tɩ Maryam.
42001028	La malɛka sẽn kẽ a nengẽ, a yeelame: «M pʋʋsda yãmba, pid ne kũun soaba! Soaala bee ne yãmba, yãmb paama barka, pagba fãa sʋka.»
42001029	La a Maryam sẽn wʋm gomdã, a yɛɛsame; a ra bilgdame n baood pʋʋsg a woto võore.
42001030	Malɛka yeelame: «Da zoe-y rabeem ye, Maryam, yãmb paama bark Wẽnnaam taoore.
42001031	Ade, yãmb na n dɩka pʋga, yãmb na n doga bi-ribla la y na pʋda a yʋʋr a Zezi.
42001032	Bãmb na n yɩɩ nin-kãsenga, la b na n bool-b lame tɩ yĩngr soab Biiga. Wẽnnaam na n kõ bãmba b saamba, a Daviid, zaoore,
42001033	la b na n dɩ naam a Zakoob zakẽ daar fãa la b naam kõn zĩnd sɛɛb ye.»
42001034	A Maryam soka malɛkã: «Dẽ na n yɩ-la a wãna, tɩ m ka mi rao ye?»
42001035	Malɛka leokame: «A Vʋʋsem Sõng na n siga yãmb zugu la yĩngr soab pãng na n bui yãmba. Dẽ n so tɩ sõmblem biiga yãmb sẽn na n dogã, b na n bool-b lame tɩ yĩngr soab Biiga.
42001036	Bɩ y gese! Yãmb doagda, a Elizabɛt, dɩka pʋga n na n dog biig a kʋʋlem pʋgẽ, lebga kiuusa yoob marsã, b sẽn da ket n boond-a tɩ pʋg-kiiri;
42001037	tɩ bũmb ka be sẽn yɩɩd Wẽnnaam nug ye.»
42001038	La a Maryam yeelame: «Mam yaa Soaala yem-poaka, bɩ kell n yɩ ne maam wala yãmb sẽ yeelã.» La malɛka bas-a lame n looge.
42001039	A Mariyam waa n yika ne yãgbo n tees tẽng a yembre, Zɩɩda tãmsẽ.
42001040	A tɩ kẽe a Zakari yiri n pʋʋs a Elizabɛt.
42001041	A Elizabɛt sẽn wʋm a Maryam pʋʋsma, biiga sẽn da be a pʋgẽ wã yĩng sidgame. La a Elizabɛt pida ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo,
42001042	t'a zẽk a koɛɛg n moonẽ: «Fo paama barka, pagba fãa sʋka, la f pʋgẽ biiga me paama barka.
42001043	Mam bee yɛ, tɩ m Soaala ma wat m nengẽ?
42001044	Ade, fo pʋʋsma sẽn lʋɩ m tʋbrẽ la m biiga yĩng sẽn sidgi, sũ-noog keelem yĩnga.
42001045	Foom la zu-noog soaba, tɩ fo tẽeme tɩ gomna b sẽn leok foom, Soaala yʋʋr yĩnga, na n taasame.»
42001046	La a Maryam yeelame: «Mam sɩɩga pẽgda m Soaal,
42001047	la m sũur kɩdemda sũ-noogo, Wẽnnaam m Fãagda yĩnga.
42001048	Bãmb gesa b biiga paoodlem. Ad marsã tɛka ninsaal buud fãa na n boola maam tɩ zu-noog soaba.
42001049	Tɩ Pãng soab maana yɛl kãsens mam yĩnga, la b yʋʋr yaa sõngo.
42001050	Dũni sẽn yet t'a yaa dũniya, b nimbãan-zoeer bee sẽn zoet-b bãmb zutu.
42001051	B wilga b kang pãnga. B riga wakr dãmba n sẽege.
42001052	B sika pãens rãmb b zaoorẽ, b zẽka talse.
42001053	Kom sẽn tar b rãmba, b tɩgs-b la ne kũuni, tɩ arzɛk rãmb yaool kul zaalem.
42001054	B kogla b biig, a Israyɛl; tɩ b tẽega b nimbãan-zoeerã
42001055	n na n pids zamaan woo zamaana b sẽn da kãab d saam-dãmba, a Abraam ne a kamba!»
42001056	A Maryam zĩnda ne a Elizabɛt sẽn zems kiis a tã n yaool n kul a yiri.
42001057	A Elizabɛt dogem taame; a roga bi-ribla.
42001058	A yags la a buud dãmb wʋmame tɩ Soaala zoe-la a nimbãanega, tɩ b lagem ne-a, n kɩdemnẽ.
42001059	Dasem a nii daare, b kẽesa bi-pɛɛlga bãongo. B pʋd-a la a ba yʋʋre: Zakari.
42001060	T'a ma yeele: «Ayoo! A Zã la b na n bool-a.»
42001061	Tɩ b yeel-a: «Fo buudẽ wã, ned ka be sẽn pʋd yʋ-kãng ye.»
42001062	La b bilsa ne nus n sok biiga ba a sẽn dat tɩ b pʋd biiga yʋʋr ninga.
42001063	A Zakari kosa walga n gʋls woto: «A yʋʋr la a Zã.» La b fãa pɛleng yɩkame.
42001064	Wakat kãng bala, a Zakari yaaga a noor t'a zelemd lak t'a na n gom n pẽg Wẽnnaam.
42001065	Dabeem yõka a yagsa fãa. A Zɩɩda soolma fãa tɛka, neba sõasg ra yaa yell kãnga.
42001066	La neb niyns fãa sẽn wʋm-ba, yella kɛ-la b sũurẽ tɩ b ra yetẽ: «Bi-kãnga na n wa yɩɩ bõe?» Sɩd me Wẽnnaam nug ra tika biiga zugu.
42001067	La biiga ba, a Zakari, ra pida ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo, t'a gom bãngr goama n yeele:
42001068	«Soaala, Israyɛl Wẽnnaam, paam pẽgre, tɩ b waa n gesa b buudu n fãag-a.
42001069	Tõnd yĩnga b yiisa Fãagda, Pãng soaba, b biiga Daviid zakẽ.
42001070	Wala b sẽn da pĩnd n togs ne tẽn-kʋdem wẽnnẽ bãngdb sõma noore,
42001071	yaa Fãagd sẽn na fãag tõndo d bɛɛba la sẽn kis-b tõnda nusẽ.
42001072	Yɩɩ woto la b maan b nimbãan-zoeere ne d yaab rãmba. B tẽega b bark zoodã,
42001073	b tẽega kãabg ningã, b sẽn da kãab d ba, a Abraam.
42001074	B kãabame tɩ b na zãag-d ne d bɛɛba, n zãag-d ne rabeem buud fãa, tɩ d tõog n waoog-ba,
42001075	ne sõmblem la pʋ-peelem, bãmb maasmẽ, la d vɩɩma tõre.
42001076	La foom, bi-pɛɛlga b na bool foom tɩ Yĩngr soab no-rɛɛsa, tɩ foom n na n lʋɩ Soaala taoore n segl b soya;
42001077	n kɩt tɩ buuda bãng t'a na n paama fãagre ne a yel-wẽna yẽesgo,
42001078	tõnd Wẽnda sũuri pida ne nimbãan-zoeer bala, b nimbãan-zoeer yĩnga, b yĩngr Ãdga
42001079	na puki la a vẽneg sẽn zĩ-b likẽ sẽn zĩ-b kũum maasmẽ tɩ b nao wa paam n dɩk laafi so-tɩrga.»
42001080	Biiga ra bɩtame t'a yam da paasdẽ. A zĩnda weoogẽ n tãag daar ning a sẽn vẽneg a meng a Israyɛl kamba.
42002001	Wẽnd kãnga, dĩma, a Ogust, yiisa sebre tɩ b sõd dũniya neba fãa.
42002002	Sõadg kãng n yɩ pipi sõadg la b maana-a-la a Kirinus, Siri kombera zamaanẽ.
42002003	Ned kam fãa ra lebda a tẽngẽ tɩ b sõd-a be.
42002004	A Zozɛf me yika Nazarɛt, Galile tẽnga, n kẽng Zɩɩda tẽng a ye sẽn boond tɩ Bɛtelyɛɛm, t'a ra ya a Daviid buuda neda.
42002005	La be la a tɩ sõde, yẽ ne a paga, a Maryam, sẽn da tʋte.
42002006	B sẽn waa n be Bɛtelyɛɛm, a Maryam dogem daar taame.
42002007	A doga a sãdem-biiga, n vil-a ne pɛɛla, n gãneg-a b sẽn kẽesd rũmsa zĩig ning n kõt b rɩɩbo, tɩ b ka paam weer sãamba dotẽ ye.
42002008	Pe-kɩɩmb n da be tẽnga noor n gũd b rũmsi ne yʋngo,
42002009	Soaala malɛk wa n pẽneg-b lame tɩ Soaala zɩɩra vẽenem bui-ba la rabeem kãseng yõk-b lame.
42002010	Malɛka yeel-b lame: «Da zoe-y rabeem ye tɩ yaa Kibar noog la m tara, yãmb la buuda fãa yĩnga:
42002011	dũnna, a Daviid tẽngẽ, Fãagda doga yãmb yĩnga; bãmb la Wẽnd Nedã la Soaalã.
42002012	Yaa ne makr kãnga la y na n bãng-ba: y na n yãee bi-pɛɛlg t'a gãe b sẽn kẽesd rũmsa zĩig ning n kõt-b rɩɩbã.»
42002013	Vugr bala yĩngr tãb-biisa ka tɛka wa n naaga malɛkã tɩ b pẽgd Wẽnd woto:
42002014	«Wẽnnaam paam pẽgr yĩngri la b yamleooga sẽn kẽ b rãmba paam laafi tẽng zugu!»
42002015	Malɛk rãmba bas-b lame n leb yĩngri tɩ pe-kɩɩmba yeel taaba: «Bɩ d ta Bɛtelyɛɛm n ges bũmb ning sẽn maane tɩ Soaala wilg tõndã.»
42002016	B kẽnga tao n tɩ mik a Maryam ne a Zozɛf la bi-pɛɛlg t'a gãe b sẽn kẽesd rũmsa zĩig ning n kõt-b rɩɩbã.
42002017	Pe-kɩɩmba yãenda ne b nifu, tɩ bãmb me na n sɩng n togs marsã, malɛka sẽn da zoe n wilg bãmb biiga poorẽ.
42002018	Ned ning fãa sẽn kelg-a, ra zĩi ne pɛlen-yɩka.
42002019	A Maryam ra bĩngda yɛl bãmb a sũurẽ, n bʋgsd-ba a yamẽ.
42002020	Pe-kɩɩmba lebgame n kilsdẽ la b pẽgd Wẽnnaam b sẽn yãend la b sẽn wʋm yĩnga. Fãa sɩd yɩɩ wala b sẽn da togs-bã.
42002021	A rogem dasm a nii yĩnga, b kẽesa biiga bãongo, n pʋd biiga t'a Zezi, yʋʋr ninga malɛka sẽn pind n pʋde tɩ b ma nan ka tʋd b pʋgã.
42002022	B sẽn waa n segl b mens n taas daar ning Noora sẽn yalsã, b talla biigã n kẽng Zerizalɛɛm n tɩ rɩk-b n kõ Wẽnde,
42002023	tɩ woto n be Soaala Noora sebrẽ: Bi-ribl fãa sẽn doge n yaa a ma pipi biiga, b rɩkd-a lame n kõ Soaala tɩ b sooge,
42002024	la wala Soaala Noor sẽn le rat yɛsa, yaa malwal a yiibu bɩ wal a yiibu la b kɩs tɩ b kʋ maoongo.
42002025	La ade, dao a ye n da be Zerizalɛɛm n boond t'a Simeõ. A ra yaa nin-tɩrga, nin-sõngo; a da gũuda Israyɛl yolsgo la a Vʋʋsem Sõng ra bee ne-a.
42002026	A Vʋʋsem Sõng ra vẽneg-a lame t'a bãng t'a kõn ki t'a ka reng n yãe Krista, Wẽnd Neda ye.
42002027	A Vʋʋsem Sõng kɩtame t'a kẽng wẽnd doogẽ. La biig a Zezi ba rãmb sẽn tall-b wakat ninga n wa pids noorã,
42002028	a reeg-b la a nusẽ la a pẽga Wẽnnaam n yetẽ:
42002029	«Soaala, wala y sẽn wilg y yambã, y tõeeme marsã n kõ-a sor t'a loog ne laafi;
42002030	tɩ m nini yãe-la y fãagre,
42002031	y sẽn seglg ninsaalb buud fãa yĩnga.
42002032	A yaa vẽenem n vẽnegd bu-zẽmbã, a yaa yãmb buud, a Israyɛl, zu-zẽkre.»
42002033	Biiga ma ne a ba pɛleng yika b sẽn da gomd b yell woto wã yĩnga.
42002034	A Simeõ ning-b la barka la a yeela a Maryam, biiga ma: «Ade, bi-kãnga waa ne neb wʋsgo sãoong la neb wʋsg manegre, Israyɛl pʋgẽ. A na n yɩɩ wa bõn-bãnde n wa ne no-koeemde.
42002035	La yãmb menga, yaa sʋʋga n na n kõs yãmb sũuri n kɩt tɩ y tũ rẽ n bãng sẽn be neb wʋsg rẽnnẽ.»
42002036	Bãngd poak a ye me n da be be, a An, a Fanuwɛl biiga, a Azɛr buudẽ; a ra kʋʋla wʋsgo; a sẽn yi kãadem a pʋg-sademnẽ, a zĩnda ne a sɩda yʋʋm a yopoe bala,
42002037	la a kell n paa pʋg-kõto t'a yʋʋm wa ta pisnii la a naase; a ra pa viigd wẽnd doogẽ ye; a ra waoogda Wẽnnaam yʋng la wĩntoogo, ne no-loeere la pʋʋsgo.
42002038	A An me waa wakat kãng bala n pẽgd Wẽnnaam la a gomd biiga yelle ne neb niyns fãa sẽn da gũud-b Zerizalɛɛm fãagre.
42002039	B sẽn maan fãa n sɛ wala Soaala noor sẽn date, b leba b tẽngẽ, Nazarɛt, Galile soolem.
42002040	La Biiga ra bɩtame, t'a pãng paasdẽ, la a ra tara yẽesem, la Wẽnnaam yam da kẽe-a lame.
42002041	Yʋʋmd-yʋʋmd fãa, b ba ne b ma da kẽnda Zerizalɛɛm, pak kibsa yĩnga.
42002042	Biiga yʋʋm sẽn waa n ta piig la a yi, b kẽnga Zerizalɛɛm, wala b sẽn yib n maand kibs kãng wẽnde.
42002043	Tigra rasem sẽn looge tɩ b lɛɛg n kuiisẽ, biiga paa Zerizalɛɛm tɩ b ba la b ma ka bãng ye.
42002044	Bãmb sẽn da tẽed tɩ b bee ne so-toagdb a taaba, b kẽna daar a ye kẽnde n yaool n na n sɩng baoobo, b roagdba la b mitba sʋka
42002045	la b ka yãend-b ye tɩ b leb Zerizalɛɛm n tar b baoobo.
42002046	Sẽn maam dasem a tã, b yaool n tɩ yãend-b la wẽnd doogẽ tɩ b zĩ karen-saam-dãmb sʋka n kelgd-b la b sokd-b.
42002047	La sẽn wʋm-b bãmba fãa da yɛɛsdame, b yẽesma la b leoba yĩnga.
42002048	B ba ne b ma sẽn waa n yãend-ba, b pɛleng yɩkame. B ma yeel-b lame: «M biiga, yaa bõe yĩng la fo maan tõnd woto? Gese! Ad-f ba ne maam, tõnd da saad n baooda foo ne sũ-sãanga.»
42002049	La b leokame: «Bõe yĩng la y baood maam? Yãmb da ka mi tɩ yaa pakr tɩ m tʋm m ba tʋʋmd laa?»
42002050	La b sẽn gom woto wã, ba rãmba pa wʋm a võor ye.
42002051	La a Zezi yik n tũ-b lame n kul Nazarɛt la b ra sakda b noore. B ma ra bĩngda yɛla fãa a sũurẽ.
42002052	La biiga ra bɩtame tɩ b yam la sõmblem da paasdẽ, Wẽnnaam la ninsaalb nifẽ.
42003001	A Tiber sẽn deeg Rom naam tɩ yʋʋm piig la a nu, t'a Põs Pilat so Zɩɩde, t'a Erod ya Galile naaba, t'a yao, a Filip, ya Iture la Trakonitid kombere, t'a Lizanias ya Abilɛn naaba,
42003002	maan-kʋʋr kãsẽm-dãmb a An la a Kaif zamaanẽ, a Zakari biig a Zã, wʋma Wẽnnaam koɛɛg weoogẽ.
42003003	Dẽ la a wa Zɩɩde baobga fãa n moon sũur tekr soobo, yel-wẽna sugr paoong yĩnga,
42003004	wala b sẽn gʋls bãngd a Izayi sebrẽ: «Sẽn moond-a weoogẽ wã koɛɛg la woto: segl-y Soaala sore, maneg-y b soya n demse!
42003005	Tãn-long fãa sĩdi! Sarem-y tãmsa la kunkuba fãa! Rems-y so-golomse! So-rʋda legb saalse!
42003006	Tɩ woto ninsaal fãa na yãend Wẽnnaam fãagre.»
42003007	A Zã ra yeta zãma wã sẽn da wat a nengẽ t'a so-bã: «Wag-bi buudu, ãnna n wilg yãmb tɩ y zoe n põs sũ-puur ning sẽn watã?
42003008	Wom-y biis sẽn be yõodo, sũ-tekr biisi la y ra saag n yeele: ‹D ba la a Abraam ye.› Mam yeta yãmba tɩ Wẽnnaam tõe tɩ kugã sẽn digã, dog kamb n kõ a Abraam.
42003009	Marsã lar zoe n dɩga tɩɩs yẽgnẽ, tɩɩg ning sẽn pa womd-a bi-sõma fãa, b kɛɛgd-a lame n lob bugmẽ.»
42003010	Zãma wã ra sokd-a lame: «D na n maana bõe?»
42003011	T'a leok-ba: «Sẽn tara fu-yord a yi bɩ a kõ sẽn pa tar-a, la sẽn tar-a sẽn na n dɩ bɩ yẽ me kõ sẽn pa tar-a!»
42003012	Sẽn deesd-b yõor yaood me waame t'a so-ba. B me sokame: «Karen-saamba, d na n maana bõe?»
42003013	T'a leok: «Da reeg-y bũmb n dogl b sẽn kõ noor tɩ y reeg ye.»
42003014	Tãb-biisa me sok-a lame: «La tõnd yẽ, d maan bõe?» T'a yeel-ba: «Bɩ y ra maan ned ba a ye pãng ye, da luk-y ned bãong zaalem ye, la y ra tʋlg bũmb n zʋʋg y yaood ye.»
42003015	Zãma wã ra gũuda Fãagdã. Dẽ la ned kam fãa ra yet, a pʋgẽ: sãnd kaa a Zã la Wẽnd Nedã?
42003016	Dẽ la a Zã leok-b fãa: «Mam sooda yãmb koom; la ned n wate, tɩ b pãng yɩɩd maam; mam pa zem bũmb n na n lok b gãndalsa gĩs ye. Bãmb na n so-y la ne Vʋʋsem Sõngo la bugum.
42003017	B zãada kaorg b nugẽ, la b na n pɩɩga b zɛɛga n wʋk biisã n sui baoorẽ, la b yõog fɩɩba bugum sẽn ka kiid pʋgẽ.»
42003018	A Zã ra togsda neba Koe-noogã la a wɩngd b sũuri ne saglgo buud toor toore.
42003019	A Zã ra yika zabre ne naab a Erod. Zabra yɩ-la a Erodiad poorẽ. A Erodiad da yaa a Erod yao, a Filip, paga. Zabra yɩ-la a Erod tʋʋm wẽns a taaba me poorẽ.
42003020	Dẽ kɩtame t'a Erod paas bõn-wẽng a to: a kɩtame tɩ b paga Zã roogo.
42003021	A Zã waa n soo nebã n sɛ, t'a Zezi meng tol n deeg soobo. A Zezi sẽn waa n ket n pʋʋsdẽ la arzãn sẽn pake,
42003022	tɩ Vʋʋsem Sõng sig b zug ne bũmb wẽnego, ne wall wẽnego. Koɛɛg n yi yĩngr n yetẽ: «Fo yaa mam bi-nongre, mam n dog foo rũnna bala.»
42003023	A Zezi yʋʋm da zemsa pistã, b sẽn waa n sɩng b tʋʋmde. Sã n ya neba sẽn tẽedã, b ba yɩla a Zozɛf, a Eli biiga,
42003024	a Matat biiga, a Levi biiga, a Melki biiga, a Zamayi biiga, a Zozɛf biiga,
42003025	a Matatiyas biiga, a Amos biiga; a Nawum biiga, a Esli biiga, a Nagayi biiga,
42003026	a Maat biiga, a Matatiyas biiga, a Semeyin biiga, a Zozɛf biiga, a Zoda biiga,
42003027	a Zoanan biiga, a Resa biiga, a Zorobabɛl biiga, a Salatiyɛl biiga, a Neri biiga,
42003028	a Melki biiga, a Addi biiga, a Kosam biiga, a Elmadam biiga, a Ɛr biiga,
42003029	a Zezi biiga, a Eliezɛr biiga, a Zorim biiga, a Matat biiga, a Levi biiga,
42003030	a Simeõ biiga, a Zɩɩda biiga, a Zozɛf biiga, a Zonam biiga, a Eliakim biiga,
42003031	a Melea biiga, a Menna biiga, a Matata biiga, a Natam biiga, a Daviid biiga,
42003032	a Zese biiga, a Zobɛɛd biiga, a Booz biiga, a Sala biiga, a Naason biiga,
42003033	a Aminadab biiga, a Admin biiga, a Arni biiga, a Esrom biiga, a Farɛs biiga, a Zɩɩda biiga,
42003034	a Zakoob biiga, a Izaak biiga, a Abraam biiga, a Tara biiga, a Nakor biiga,
42003035	a Seruk biiga, a Ragawu biiga, a Falɛk biiga, a Ebɛr biiga, a Sala biiga,
42003036	a Kayinam biiga, a Arpaksad biiga, a Sem biiga, a Nowe biiga, a Lamɛk biiga,
42003037	a Matusala biiga, a Enok biiga, a Zarɛt biiga, a Maleleyɛl biiga, a Kayinam biiga,
42003038	a Enos biiga, a Sɛt biiga, a Adem biiga, Wẽnnaam biiga.
42004001	A Zezi ra pida ne Vʋʋsem Sõngo. B yii Zʋrdẽ kʋɩlgã n lɛɛg n wa. A Vʋʋsem Sõng waa n le kẽes-b la we-raoogẽ wã;
42004002	b maana rasem pisnaas be la Sʋtãan kʋɩɩb-b lame. Dasem kãense, b pa rɩ fɩ; la dẽ me la kom waa n yõk-ba.
42004003	Ad Sʋtãana sẽn leok-ba: «Yãmb sã n ya Wẽnnaam Biiga, bɩ y yeel kugr kãnga t'a lebg buri.»
42004004	La a Zezi leok-a lame: «B gʋlsame: ‹Ka bur bal n dɩlgd ninsaal vɩɩm ye.› »
42004005	La Sʋtãan sẽn dʋʋs-b yĩngri bilfu, a wilg-b la vugr bala dũni wã rĩund zãnga,
42004006	n yeel-ba: «M na kõ-f tẽn-bãmba fãa ne b pãng la b zɩɩri tɩ b yaa m soolem, la m kõt-b la m sẽn dat a soaba.
42004007	Fo sã n wõgemd n waoog maam, f na soog-b zãnga.»
42004008	A Zezi leok-a lame: «B gʋlsame: ‹Pʋʋs Soaala, f Wẽnnaam, la f waoog bãmb bala.› »
42004009	Sʋtãana le tɩ rʋʋs-b la Zerizalɛɛm wẽnd dooga zugu, zĩig ninga sẽn lug n yɩɩd a taabã, n yeel-ba: «Fo sã n ya Wẽnnaam Biiga, bɩ f yɩk ka n tiimd tẽnga,
42004010	tɩ b gʋlsame: ‹Wẽnnaam na n kõo malɛk rãmb noore n yeel-b tɩ b gũ fo.›
42004011	Woto me n le paase: ‹B na n kok-f-la b nusẽ, tɩ f naoor da wa lak kugr ye.› »
42004012	A Zezi leok-a lame: «B yeelame: ‹Da fɛɛs Soaala, f Wẽnnaam ye.› »
42004013	Sʋtãana sẽn kʋɩɩb-b n sɛ, a bas-b lame n looge n gũud a zu-noog raar a to.
42004014	A Vʋʋsem Sõng pãng taasa a Zezi Galile tẽnga; beelẽ b yʋʋr yii zĩig zãnga.
42004015	B ra karemda neba pʋʋsg rotẽ la neba fãa ra pẽgd-b lame.
42004016	B kẽnga Nazarɛt, b sẽn wub tẽng ninga; vʋʋsg daare, b kẽe pʋʋsg roogẽ wala b sẽn da yib n maanẽ; b yikame n na n karem,
42004017	tɩ b kɩs-b bãngda, a Izayi sebre. B sẽn lak sebrã, sega sẽn gʋls woto:
42004018	«Wẽnd Vʋʋsem bee m zugu, tɩ b zɛɛ maam ne kaam sõngo, tɩ m tɩ togs naong rãmba Koe-noogo; b tʋm-m lame tɩ m moone n wilg yemse tɩ b tɩlga ne yembdo, la zoeense, tɩ b paama nini, la b sẽn tar b rãmb toogã tɩ b leb b zagsẽ ne laafi,
42004019	la b moon tɩ Soaala bark yʋʋmd vẽkame.»
42004020	Dẽ poore b paga sebrã n lebs karen-saamba la b zĩndame. Dooga neba fãa ra tees n geta bãmba.
42004021	Tɩ b na n sɩng goama, n yeele: «Sebr sõng gomdã yãmb sẽn wʋm mars-marsã taasa rũnna.»
42004022	La b fãa ra kõta kaseto la b pẽgd goama sẽn da yit b noorẽ. B ra yetame: «Ka yẽ la a Zozɛf biiga wɛɛ?»
42004023	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Mam mi tɩ yãmb na wẽ-m yelbũn kãnga: ‹Tɩɩm soaba, reng n sãoog f menga. Wẽnd makr dãmba fãa sẽn maan Kafarnaom tɩ d wʋmnẽ wã, bɩ f maan-b ka me, fo ba-yiri.› »
42004024	B tol n le paasame: «Sɩda, mam n togsd-y: bãngd buuda fãa zɩɩ n paam waoogr a ba-yir ye.
42004025	Yaa sɩda la m sẽn togsd yãmbã, pʋg-kõapa ra waooga Israyɛl tẽnga, a Eli zamaanẽ, saag sẽn waa n pa tol n ni yʋʋm a tã la kiis a yoobe,
42004026	b yaool n pa tʋm a Eli ned ba a ye nengẽ sã n pa pʋg-kõor a ye sẽn da be Sarepta, Sidõ soolmẽ.
42004027	Wãooba me ra waooga Israyɛl tẽnga, bãngd a Elize wẽnnẽ, la baasgo bãmb ned ba a ye ka paam tɩ b sãoog-a, sã n ka Siri neda, a Naama bala.»
42004028	Pʋʋsga roogẽ, b fãa sũur puuga al wʋsgo, b sẽn wʋm boto.
42004029	B yikame n tus-ba tɩ b yi b tẽngẽ; b tẽnga da tii tãng zugu. Woto b tall-b lame n ta tãnga rĩ-sɩlengẽ n na n tus-ba n lub vɩʋʋgẽ.
42004030	La a Zezi pɩʋʋga bãmb sʋk n looge.
42004031	A Zezi kẽnga Kafarnaom, Galile soolmẽ, la b ra karemda nebã vʋʋsg daare.
42004032	B karenga yɩka neba pɛlenga, tɩ b ra gomda wa ned sẽn tar naam la tõogo.
42004033	Dao a ye n da be pʋʋsga roogẽ n tar Sʋtãan a pʋgẽ, a kelma ne pãnga:
42004034	«Ey! Y bõe toog n be ne tõndo. Mam mii yãmb sẽn yaa a soaba: Wẽnnaam Nin-sõngo!»
42004035	A Zezi tãs-a lame: «Sĩnd f noore, yi la f bas daoã!» La Sʋtãana tusa raoã n lub neba sʋka, n bas-a n yi la bũmb pa maan-a ye.
42004036	Dabeem yõka neba fãa tɩ b ra tar ne taaba: «Yɛ ned n gomd woto? A kõta sʋtãan-yood noor ne tõog la pãnga la b yitame.»
42004037	A Zezi yʋʋra sɩd yii zĩig zãnga.
42004038	A Zezi yii pʋʋsga roogẽ n kẽng a Simo yiri. A Simo reem-poaka yĩns ra wɩnga bas-base la b yõka a Zezi sɛɛga tɩ b sõng-a.
42004039	A Zezi zõondame n tãs yĩn-wɩngrã la a sigame. Paga yika zĩig pʋgẽ n segend-b.
42004040	Wĩndg sẽn kẽ, b talla bãad-dãmb ka tɛka n wa a Zezi nengẽ. B tẽega b nus bãmb ned kam fãa zugu n sãoog-ba.
42004041	Sʋtãamba ra yita neb wʋsg pʋsẽ n kelemdẽ la b moonẽ: «Yãmb yaa Wẽnnaam Biiga.» La a Zezi ra tãsd-b lame. B ra pa sakd tɩ b gome, tɩ sʋtãamba ra miime tɩ b yaa Wẽnd Nedã.
42004042	Zĩig sẽn yẽege, b yii n kõsa weoogo. Zãma wã saame n bao-ba, n wa yãend-ba, n da rat n gõog-ba tɩ b ra loog n bas-b ye.
42004043	La a Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yaa modgr tɩ m tɩ togs tẽns a taaba me, Wẽnd Rĩung Koe-noogã, tɩ b tʋm-m la rẽnd yĩnga.»
42004044	B ra zãmsda neba Galile pʋʋsg rotẽ.
42005001	Daar a ye, Zãma wã ra pẽdgda a Zezi, Zenezarɛt mogra noor, n na n kelg Wẽnnaam gomde. La mogra noore,
42005002	b yãenda koom-kogend bõones a yiibu. Kʋɩl-zẽ-yẽedba da yi n pegda b zulumsi.
42005003	A Zezi kẽe koglg a ye, a Simo rẽnna, n kos tɩ b zãag mogra noor bilfu la b zĩnda koglga pʋg n zãmsd nebã.
42005004	B sẽn gom n sɛ, b yeela a Simo: «Ta-y ko-sʋka n lob y zulumsã n yẽ zĩma.»
42005005	T'a Simo leoke: «Karen-saamba, tõnd namsa yʋnga tõre n pa yõk bũmb ye la y sẽn yeela yĩnga, m na lob zulumsã.»
42005006	La b sẽn lobe, b yõga kʋɩl-zẽed wʋsgo al tɩ zulumsa ra pãrsdẽ.
42005007	B kamsa b tũud-n-taase sẽn da be koglg a to pʋga, tɩ b wa sõng-ba. B waame la b vaagame n pids kogend a yiibã tɩ b rat n lisi.
42005008	La a Simo sẽn yãe rẽ, a wõgemda a Zezi taoore n yeel-ba: «Zãag-y ne maam, Soaala, tɩ m yaa yel-wẽn-maanda.»
42005009	Rabeem kãseng yõk-a lame, yẽ ne a tũud-n-taase, kʋɩl-zẽeda sẽn yõg wʋsga yĩnga.
42005010	Rabeem me kẽ-la a Zak la a Zã, a Zebede kamb a yiibã, sẽn da tʋmd ne a Simo. T'a Zezi na n yeel a Simo: «Da zoe rabeem ye tɩ marsã tɛka, yaa neb la f na n paame n kõ-ma.»
42005011	B lɛɛg n waa ne kogendã mogra noore la b basa fãa n tũ a Zezi.
42005012	A Zezi waa n bee tẽng a yembre tɩ rao a ye sẽn da bẽed wãoodo yãend-ba, n wõgemd b taoore n fõgna a neng tẽnga, n pʋʋs-ba: «Soaala, yãmb sã n data, y tõe n sãoog-m lame.»
42005013	A Zezi tẽega b nug n sɩɩs-a n yeele: «Mam datame, sãooge!» La zĩig pʋgẽ bala, a wãooda sãoogame.
42005014	Tɩ b na n kõ-a noore t'a ra togs ned ba a ye la b le paasame: «Kẽng n tɩ wilg f meng maan-kʋʋda la f sẽn sãooga yĩnga, kɩs kũuni, wala a Moyiiz noor sẽn date tɩ yɩ kaset b yĩnga.»
42005015	A Zezi yʋʋr da yit n paasdame tɩ zãma wã sɩng n tigimd ka tɛka, n na n kelg-ba la b paam b bãas sãoogre.
42005016	Bãmb da nong n paa weoogẽ n pʋʋsdẽ.
42005017	A Zezi ra karemda neba daar a ye, tɩ Farizẽ la noora karen-saam-dãmb da lagem n zĩ be; b ra yii Zɩɩde la Galile la Zerizalɛɛm tẽn-toose. Soaala pãng ra bee ne a Zezi tɩ b sãoogd nebã.
42005018	La ade neb n da zɩt b põor ne a gãaga, n baood n na n sik-a bãmb taoore.
42005019	La b sẽn da ka mi b sẽn na n tũ zĩig ning n kẽ ne bãadã, zãma wã yĩnga, b rʋʋ bɛoongã n kɩbg võore n sik-a ne a gãagã, a Zezi taoore.
42005020	A Zezi yãenda b tẽebo n yeel: «Daoa, fo paama f yel-wẽna sugri.»
42005021	Farizẽ rãmba ne Sɛb-mitba tagsa b sũurẽ: «Yãoo yaa ãnna n mamesd a meng ne Wẽnde? Anna n tõe n kõ yel-wẽnd sugri, sã n ka Wẽnnaam b ye?»
42005022	A Zezi bãnga b sũur tagsgo la b yeel-b lame: «Yaa bõe tagsgo la yãmb tagsda y sũur pʋgẽ?
42005023	Yelsem bʋg la naana: fo paama f yel-wẽnd sugri, bɩ: yik n kẽne?
42005024	Sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ y bãng tɩ Ned Biiga tara tõog tẽng zugu, n kõ yel-wẽnd sugri, põore, maam n kõt f noore: yiki! Tʋk f gãag n kul f yiri!»
42005025	La Zĩig pʋgẽ bala, a yika bãmb nifẽ, n tʋk a gãag n kuiis a yiri la a pẽgd Wẽnnaam.
42005026	Neba fãa pɛleng yɩkame tɩ b ra pẽgd Wẽnnaam; rabeem da tar-b lame tɩ b yetẽ: «Dũnna tõnd yãee yel-soalma.»
42005027	Dẽ poore a Zezi yiime la b yãee rao a yembre sẽn boond t'a Levi, t'a zĩ a tʋʋmd zĩigẽ, fadg reesg tʋʋmde, tɩ b yeel-a: «Tũ maam!»
42005028	A Levi basa fãa n yik n tũ-ba.
42005029	A Levi maana kibs kãseng a yiri, n segl dɩɩbo. Sẽn deesd-b yõor yaoodã yɩɩ wʋsgo la neb a taab me waa n paasame, tɩ b ra zĩi n dɩtẽ.
42005030	Farizẽ rãmba la Sɛb-mitba guglumame la b yeela a Zezi karen-biisã: «Yaa bõe yĩng la yãmb lagemd sẽn deesd-b yõor yaoodã la yel-wẽn-maandbã n dɩtẽ la y yũuda?»
42005031	T'a Zezi na n leok-ba: «Sẽn zĩ-a ne laafi ka tar tɩɩm soab tʋʋmd ye, yaa sẽn pa keem-bã n tar a tʋʋmde.
42005032	Mam ka wa nin-sõma boolg ye, yaa yel-wẽn-maandba la m wa n na n bool tɩ b tuub b yel-wẽna.»
42005033	Nim-bãmb n lɛɛg n yeel a Zezi: «A Zã karen-biisa loeta b noor naoor wʋsgo. Farizẽ rãmba karen-biis me maanda boto. Yãmb karen-biisa bala n nong n dɩtẽ la b yũuda.»
42005034	T'a Zezi leok-ba: «Pʋg-sɩd zo-rãmb tõe n loee noore tɩ pʋg-sɩd nan ket ne bãmb bɩ?
42005035	Daar n wate. B sẽn loog ne pʋg-sɩdã raare, b na loe noore.»
42005036	B wẽ-b la yelbũnd a ye: «Fu-paalg kõ kẽeg n lisg fu-kʋɩds ye, peen-paalg la kʋɩds pa zemsd taab ye.
42005037	Ned me kõn sui rã-noodo, ko-wao kʋtẽ ye, tɩ rãama na n pusa ko-waoosã n daage la ko-waoosa na n yɩɩ bõne.
42005038	B suiida rã-noodo ko-wao paalẽ.
42005039	Ned pa yũud rãam sẽn kũmi n dat rã nood ye. B tol n wẽe yelbũnd kãnga: rã kũmdi la noogo.»
42006001	Vʋʋsg daar a ye, a Zezi ra pɩʋʋgda pʋto tɩ karen-biisa ra tẽgd kasãna n wãbdẽ.
42006002	Farizẽ rãmb kẽer yeel-b lame: «Yaa bõe la yãmb maand y sẽn pa tar sor n maan vʋʋsg daare?»
42006003	A Zezi leok-b lame: «Yãmb pa karem a Daviid sẽn maan bũmb ninga, kom sẽn waa n yõk-a, yẽ ne a tũud-n-taasa la?
42006004	A ka kẽ wẽnd doogẽ n yãk bur b sẽn da kõ Wẽnnaam, n dɩ bɩ? A pa tol n kõ a poorẽ dãmb tɩ bãmb me rɩ bɩ? Yaool n yaa maan-kʋʋdba bal n tõe n dɩ bur kãnga.»
42006005	La b yeelame: «Ned Biig n so al ba vʋʋsg daare.»
42006006	Vʋʋsg raar a to, b kẽe pʋʋsg roogẽ n da karemd neba la rao a ye n da be be t'a rɩtg nug ya kɩɩnga.
42006007	Sɛb-mitba ne Farizẽ rãmba da gũusda a Zezi, n na n gese b sã n na n sãooga bãada, vʋʋsg daare tɩ b paam n ning-b taale.
42006008	A Zezi da mii b tagsgo, dẽ la b yeel nug-kɩɩngã: «Yik n yaas sʋka.» Tɩ raoã yik n yaase,
42006009	la a Zezi yeelame: «Mam sokda yãmba: vʋʋsg daare, d tara sor n maan neer bɩ d tara sor n maan wẽnga? D tara sore n fãag ned bɩ d tara sor n bas-a t'a ki?»
42006010	B yaas n gesa b fãa gilli n yaool n yeel raoã: «Tẽeg f nugu!» Tɩ raoã tẽeg a nug la a nuga vʋʋgame.
42006011	Neba sũur puuga al vʋsgo tɩ b ra yẽsd ne taaba n na n bãng b sẽn na n maan a Zezi bũmb ninga.
42006012	Wa n segame tɩ sasa kãnga a Zezi da rʋʋ tãng zug n na n pʋʋse. La yʋnga tõre yii pʋʋsg bala.
42006013	Zĩig sẽn yẽege b boola b karen-biisã n tũus bãmb sʋka neb piig la a yi, n bool-b tɩ b Tʋʋm-tʋmdba.
42006014	Yɩla a Simo, b sẽn pʋd a soab t'a Piyɛr (kugri) la a ba-biig a Andre, n paas a Zak, a Zã, a Filip, a Bartelemi;
42006015	a Matiye, a Toma; a Alfe biig a Zak; a Simo, yẽ la m sũur be ne buuda bɛ;
42006016	a Zak biig a Zɩɩd; a Zɩɩda, Iskariyot tẽng dao, sẽn yɩ a zãmb soabã.
42006017	B sẽn sigd tãngã, b tees n yaasa a lʋgrẽ; karen-biisi la zãma ka tɛk n da tigim be; b ra yii Zɩɩde la Zerizalɛɛm, ne Tir la Sidõ sẽn be mogr noore.
42006018	Bãmb fãa ra waame n na n kelg-ba la b paam b bãas sãoogre; Sʋtãan yood sẽn da tar b rãmb n namsdẽ wã fãa da paamda yolsgo.
42006019	Zãma wã ra baood n sɩɩsa bãmba tɩ pãng n da yit b nengẽ n sãoogd bãmb fãa.
42006020	A Zezi zẽka b neng n ges b karen-biisã n yeele: «Sũ-noog rãmba la yãmba, naong rãmba, tɩ yãmb n so Arzãn Rĩungu.
42006021	Sũ-noog rãmb la yãmba, sẽn kũmd-b kom dũnna wã, tɩ yãmb n na n tɩge. Sũ-noog rãmb la yãmba, sẽn yãbd-b rũnna, tɩ yãmb n na n la n kaase.
42006022	Yãmb la sũ-noog rãmba neb sã n wa kis yã, Ned Biiga yĩnga, la b yiisd yãmb buudẽ, la b tar y tʋʋre la b sãbsd y yʋʋrã wa a yaa yʋ-beoogo.
42006023	Wakat kãng bɩ y noog y sũuri la y kɩdem tɩ yãmb dolb na n yɩɩ wʋsg arzãnẽ. Yɩɩ woto la yaab rãmba da kis bãngdbã.
42006024	Yãmb la zu-bʋk rãmba, arzɛk rãmba, tɩ yãmb zoe n tara sẽn na noog y sũuri.
42006025	Yãmb la zu-bʋk rãmba sẽn tɩgd-b rũnna wã tɩ yãmb la kom na n yõk beoogo. Zu-bʋk rãmba la yãmb sẽn mi laad rũnna wã, tɩ yãmb n na n kelem kʋʋre la y yãb yãb-toogo.
42006026	Yãmb la zu-bʋk rãmba neb sã n gomd y yelle n pẽgd yã. Ad-y yɩɩ woto la yaab rãmba maan ne zirẽ bãngdba.
42006027	Yãmb fãa sẽn kelgd maama, m yet-y lame: Nong-y y bɛɛba; sẽn tugd-b beem ne yãmbã, bɩ y maan-b yel sõmde.
42006028	Sẽn kãabd-b yãmb wẽnga bɩ y kãab-b kãab-noogo la y pʋʋs n kõ sẽn sãamd-b yãmb yʋʋrã.
42006029	Ned wẽ f yɛgdg a ye pɛka bɩ f wẽnemd f yɛdg a to wã n tees-a. Ned yẽeg fo n deeg f fu-taoko, da mong-a f fu-wok ye.
42006030	Sẽn bõs-a foom, kõ-a; sẽn dɩka fo bũmbu bɩ f ra sok-a n deeg ye.
42006031	Yãmb sẽn dat tɩ ned maan yãmb bũmb ningã, maan-y boto ne y taaba.
42006032	Yãmb sã n nong sẽn nong-b yãmba bala, yell sõng la bʋgo? Yel-wẽn-maandba me maanda boto.
42006033	La sã n ya sẽn maand-b yãmb neer bala la y maand neere, yell sõnga la bʋgo? Yel-wẽn-maandba me maanda boto.
42006034	Yãmb sã n penge, n mi tɩ y sẽn peng b rãmba na n wa lebs-y lame, yell sõnga la bʋgo? Yel-wẽn-maandba me pengda b taaba n na n wa reeg b sẽn kɩsa zugu.
42006035	Sã n ya yãmba, nong-y yãmb bɛɛba, maan-y yel-sõma la y peng n da saag bũmb ye tɩ woto yãmb dolbo wat n yɩɩ wʋsgo la yãmb yɩta Yĩngr Ba wã kamba tɩ bãmb maanda yel-sõm-zɩtb la nin-wẽns neere.
42006036	Dẽ yĩnga yɩ-y nimbãan-zoetba, wala Ba wã sẽn ya nimbãan-zoetã.
42006037	Da kao-y ned bʋʋd ye, tɩ b kõn kao yãmb me bʋʋd ye. Da ning-y ned taale tɩ b kõn ning yãmb me taal ye. Kõ-y sugri tɩ b na kõ yãmb me sugri.
42006038	Kõ-y tɩ b na kõ yãmb me. Y na n kolemda y fuug tɩ b kiig-y wamd pidungu, wamd sẽn yegs yegse n pĩ tɩ baas n sẽegdẽ. Yãmb sẽn dɩk wamd ning n mak n kõ y taabã, wamd kãng la b rɩkd n mak n kõ yãmb me.»
42006039	A Zezi wẽ-b la yelbũna: «Zoang sã n tat a zon-taaga b yiiba fãa kõn tɩ far n lʋɩ longẽ sɩda?
42006040	Karen-biig ka yɩɩd a karen-saamb ye, karen-biig karm n siki, a yɩta waa a karen-saamba.
42006041	Bõe yĩng tɩ fo ne moog sẽn sor f saam-biiga nifu, n yaool n pa ne ra-bed kẽemdã sẽn sel f nifẽ?
42006042	Fo yɩta a wãn n yeel f saam-biiga: yaas tɩ m lɩk mooga sẽn sorg f nifu? Zirẽ-be-neda! Deng n feoog da-bed kẽenga sẽn sel fo nifẽ wã tɩ f na paam nini n lɩk mooga sẽn sorg f saam-biiga nifã.
42006043	Tɩ sõng zɩ n wom bi-wẽns ye la tɩ wẽng me zɩ n wom bi-sõma ye!
42006044	Tɩɩg fãa bãngda a biisẽ; kankam kõn fãs gõosẽ ye, la sib ka tõsd kãgrẽ ye.
42006045	Nin-sõng sẽn pid sõmblem kẽeda a sũurẽ n yiis yel-sõma, tɩ nin-wẽng sẽn pid wẽnem kẽed a sũurẽ n yiisd sẽn pa sõmbe. F sũur sẽn pid ne bũmb ninga la f noor tar n gomda.
42006046	Yaa bõe tɩ y boond-m tɩ y zu-soaba la y yaool n pa maand m sẽn togsd yãmba?
42006047	Sẽn wat-a mam nengẽ, sẽn kelgd-a mam goama la a tũud-ba, yaas-y tɩ m togs a sẽn wẽnd a soaba.
42006048	Yaa wa ned sẽn met roogo; a tuudame n yẽeg bog zulunga n sɩng rooga pĩig zugu. Sakoom wa yã, a zoee ne pãnga n wẽ roogã la a pa tõog n dĩms-a ye t'a meeb yaa sõmbo.
42006049	Sẽn kelgd-a la a pa tũudẽ, yaa wa ned sẽn me roog tẽn-nabrẽ, bĩisri zugu, koom kaoogame n zoe n wẽ-a ne pãnga, vugr bala doog sirgame la yɩɩ sirgr kãsenga.»
42007001	B sẽn togs neba b koeesã, a Zezi yikame n kẽng Kafarnaom.
42007002	Tãb-biis koabg tãnsoab n da tar a yem-daoogo la a ra nong-a-la wʋsgo. Yem-daooga yika pa-keem n dat n ki.
42007003	A sẽn wʋm a Zezi yelle, tãnsoaba tʋma Zʋɩf rãmb nin-kẽems b nengẽ n dat tɩ b kudg kãntɩɩga tɩ b wa sãoog a nedã.
42007004	B sẽn ta a Zezi nengẽ, b kos-b la ne b sũur fãa n yetẽ: «Togame tɩ y maan bũmb a yĩnga,
42007005	t'a nonga tõnd buudu la a tol n me d pʋʋsg roogã n kõ-do.»
42007006	La a Zezi tũ-b lame la b sẽn waa n kolg yiri, tãnsoaba tʋma a zo-rãmba tɩ b wa yeel-ba: «M zu-soaba, ra nams-y y meng woto ye, tɩ ka tog tɩ y wa kẽ m zakẽ ye.
42007007	M tagsame tɩ m paooda ne m wa m toore n seg yãmba. Yeel-y gomd a ye bala la m yamba na n sãoogame.
42007008	Mam menga tara zu-soaben-dãmba la m soo tãb-biisi. M yeel bãmb nin-yende: Kẽnge, a kẽndame. M yeel a to: Wa! A watame. M yeel m yambã: Maan woto! A maandame.»
42007009	A Zezi sẽn wʋm woto, b pẽga tãnsoaba la b wẽnega b poorẽ n yeel zãma wã sẽn da pʋgdã: «Sɩda m yeta yãmba, al ba Israyɛl pʋgẽ, mam nan pa yãe tẽeb kãseng a woto ye.»
42007010	Sẽn tʋm b rãmba sẽn ta zakẽ b mikame tɩ yamba bee laafi.
42007011	Dẽn sẽn looge, a Zezi waa n dabda tẽng a ye sẽn boond tɩ Nayim, tɩ b karen-biisa la zãma kãseng ra pʋgd-ba.
42007012	B sẽn ta tẽnga noore, segame tɩ b tʋka biig sẽn ki n dabd mumbu; biiga ra yaa a ma-bi-yende la ma wã da yaa pʋg-kõore; tẽnga neb wʋsg da yãagd-a lame.
42007013	Soaala sẽn yãe pagã, b kũma a nimbãanega la b yeel-a lame: «Da yãb ye!»
42007014	La b kolg n sɩɩsa kũuma; tɩ sẽn tʋk-ba yaase la a Zezi yeelame: «Biiga m kõt-f la noore, yiki!»
42007015	Kũuma yikame n sɩng goama t'a Zezi lebs-a a ma.
42007016	Dabeem kãseng yõka nebã tɩ b fãa pẽgd Wẽnnaam n yetẽ: «Bãngd kãseng lika tõnd sʋka la Wẽnnaam waa n gesa b buudu.»
42007017	Pẽgra taa Zɩɩde soolmẽ la tẽn-kɩremsa fãa n sãage.
42007018	A Zã karen-biisa tɩ wilg-a-la rẽ fãa.
42007019	Dẽnd la a Zã bool a karen-biis a yiibu n tʋʋm-ba tɩ b tɩ sok a Zezi: «Yaa yãmb la b sẽn da gũud a soab waoongã bɩ yaa ned a to?»
42007020	B sẽn ta a Zezi nengẽ, karen-biisa yeelame: «A Zã n tʋm tõndo tɩ d wa soke: yãmb la neba sẽn da gũud a soab waoongã bɩ yaa ned a to?»
42007021	Wakat kãng t'a Zezi ra sãoogda bãad-dãmb wʋsgo la koms rãmba, la zĩn dãmba la b pukd zoeens nini.
42007022	B yeelame: «Kẽng-y n tɩ togs a Zã y sẽn yãe la y sẽn wʋme: zoeens le paamda nini, wobs kẽndame, wãoob sãoogdame, kũum vʋʋgdame la b togsda naong rãmba Koe-noogã.
42007023	Zu-noog soaba la sẽn ka na n lak-a maam wa bɛooga n lʋɩ.»
42007024	A Zã sẽn tʋm b rãmba sẽn looge, a Zezi yeela zãma wã: «Bõe la yãmb kẽng n tɩ maag y meng n ges weoogẽ? Tãnwĩig sobg sẽn lengd bɩ?
42007025	Yaa bõe la yãmb kẽng n tɩ gese? Ned sẽn yer fʋ-neeb bi? Sẽn yer-b fʋ-neeba la sẽn yãet-b naare bee nanams zagsẽ.
42007026	Yaa bõe la yãmb tɩ gese? Bãngd bɩ? N-yẽe! Maam n yeele, la yɩɩda bãngda.
42007027	Yaa yẽ soab yelle la b sẽn gʋlse: Mam tʋmda n tʋʋm-tʋmda t'a reng taoore n segl f soya.
42007028	Mam yeta yãmba tɩ pagba kamb fãa sʋka sẽn yɩɩd a Zã ka ye. La ade, sẽn yaa yao-zʋʋg Wẽnd Rĩungẽ wã yɩɩd-a lame.
42007029	Zãma wã la fadga rɛɛsdba sẽn kelg a Zã koɛɛga n sak t'a ko-b soobã, bãmb manesma tũu Wẽnd sẽn date.
42007030	Farizẽ la noor karen-saam-dãmba sẽn zãgs a soobã, ad-y b kɩtame tɩ Wẽnnaam sẽn da tʋlg bũmb ninga vaale.
42007031	Mam makda zamaan kãnga kambã ne ãndãmba?
42007032	B wẽnda kamb sẽn zĩ raagẽ n zabd taaba: ‹Tõnd peeba wɩɩse la yãmb pa sao warb ye, d pʋda kʋʋr yɩɩla la yãmb pa kũm ye.›
42007033	A Zã waame n zãgs t'a kõn dɩ rɩɩbo la a kõn yu rãam ye tɩ yãmb yet t'a zug ka ye.
42007034	Ned Biiga waame n dɩtẽ la a yũuda tɩ yãmb yet t'a yaa yão-be-neda la rã-yũuda, sẽn deesd-b fadgã la yel-wẽn-maandba zoa.
42007035	La Wẽnd kamb naaga taab gilli n kõ kaseto tɩ tʋʋma tũu Wẽnd yam zulunga sẽn yalse.»
42007036	Farizẽ n bool a Zezi tɩ b wa rɩ ne yẽnda, t'a Zezi kẽ a zakẽ tɩ b sɩng rɩɩbo.
42007037	La ade pag a ye n da ya tẽnga pʋg-yoaada; a bãngame t'a Zezi rɩta Farizẽ wã yiri,
42007038	t'a wa ne a yubl sẽn pid ne yũ-noog kaam, a yalsa poorẽ, a Zezi nao wã sẽn tẽesẽ. A ra yãbdame, n madgd a Zezi nao ne a nintãm, n yẽesd-b ne a zoobdo la a zɛɛd-b ne kaama.
42007039	Farizẽ ninga sẽn bool a Zezi wã sẽn yãend rẽ, yeela a sũurẽ: «Yãoo sã n da yaẽ-la bãngda, paga sẽn sɩɩs-a wã, a na bãngẽ tɩ yaa yel-wẽn-maanda.»
42007040	La a Zezi leok-a lame: «Simo, m dat n togsa yãmb koɛɛga.» T'a yeele: «Karen-saamba, togs-y.»
42007041	Neb a yiibu n da tar ned a ye samde: pipi soaba yaa sãnem gil a nu, a to wã wakɩ koeems pisnu bala.
42007042	B sẽn da pa tar n yaood b samda yĩnga, a bas-b la b yiiba fãa taale. Anna n na n nong-a n yɩɩda?
42007043	A Simo leokame: «M tẽedame tɩ yaa ned ninga samd sẽn yɩɩd a to wã t'a bas taalã.» A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yãmb togsa sɩda.»
42007044	B wẽnega b poorẽ n ges pagã n yeel a Simo: «Yãmb yãee pagã? Mam kẽe yãmb zakẽ la y pa kõn-m koom tɩ m waas m nao ye la yẽ zãgsa m nao ne a nintãm n yẽes-b ne a zoobdo.
42007045	Yãmb ka mok m yɛgd ye, la yẽ sẽn kẽ tɛka a mogsda m nao n ka basdẽ ye.
42007046	Yãmb ka sõog m zug kaam ye la paga zɛɛ m nao ne yũ-noog kaam.
42007047	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet yãmba t'a paama a yel-wẽna sẽn ya wʋsga sugri, a nonglem sẽn yɩ wʋsga yĩnga. B sẽn bas a soab bõn-bilfr taale, yẽ soab nonglma zemsame bala.»
42007048	B yeela pagã: «Fo paama f yel-wẽna sugri.»
42007049	Sẽn da rɩt-b ne bãmba yeela b sũuri: «Yãoo yaa ãnna, n kõt ba yel-wẽnd sugri?»
42007050	La a Zezi yeela pagã: «Fo tẽeba fãag-f lame, kẽng ne laafi.»
42008001	Dẽ poore a Zezi da saada tẽn-bɛd la tẽn-bõonego n gomd Wẽnd Rĩung yelle la b moond b Koe-noogo. Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã n da tũud-ba,
42008002	n paas pagb kẽere. Yaa sʋtãan dẽgd la b ra yiis b pʋsẽ, bɩ yaa b bãas la b ra sãoog yã, wala a Mari b sẽn da boond a soab t'a Madelɛn; Sʋtãamb a yopoe la b yiis a pʋgẽ,
42008003	wala a Zan, a Erod ligd naab a Kuza paga, la pagb a taab wʋsgo sẽn da sõngd-b ne b paoongo.
42008004	Neb kʋʋng tigma taaba n waa a Zezi nengẽ tɩ b na n tão-b yelbũndi:
42008005	«Bʋt a ye n yi n na n tɩ bʋd a pʋʋgo. A sẽn waa n fẽedã a bõn-buudã, bɛɛl kẽer lʋɩɩ sor zugu; neb tab-b lame, yĩngr luiili rɩ-b lame.
42008006	Kẽer lʋɩɩ zĩ-kʋɩgdgẽ, b sẽn yi, b wẽneg n kiime, tɩ b ra pa tar bʋgsem ye.
42008007	Kẽer lʋɩɩ gõosẽ la b sẽn yi gõosa sʋkã, gõosa wulumd-b lame tɩ b ki.
42008008	Kẽer lʋɩɩ zi sakdgẽ, bãmb yiime n wom biisi, a ye fãa koabg koabga.» A Zezi sẽn yeel woto, b mooname: «Sẽn tar-a tʋb n tõe n wʋm bɩ a wʋm!»
42008009	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba sok-b la yelbũnda võore,
42008010	tɩ b leok-ba: «B kõo yãmb tɩ y bãng Wẽnd Rĩunga yɛl-solgdi la sã n ya neb a taabã, yaa ne yelbũna la b gomd ne bãmba, sẽn na yɩlẽ ‹tɩ b sã n getẽ bɩ b ra neẽ ye, tɩ b sã n kelgdẽ bɩ b ra wʋm võor ye.›
42008011	Ad yelbũnda võore: bõn-buuda yaa Wẽnnaam Gomde.
42008012	Sẽn lʋɩ-b sora zugu makda sẽn kelg-ba tɩ Sʋtãan yaool n wa yiis Gomdã b sũurẽ, tɩ b ra wa tẽ n fãag b mens ye.
42008013	Sẽn lʋɩ-b zĩ-kʋɩgdgẽ wã makda sẽn kelg-b Wẽnnaam Gomdã n deeg-a ne sũ-noogo la b pa kɩ yẽgen ye, b tẽeda wakat yɛng bala; kʋɩbg sã n wa, b basda raoodo.
42008014	Sẽn lʋɩ-b gõos sʋka makda sẽn kelg-b Gomdã, la sora zugu, zu-loees buud fãa, arzɛka la dũni wã bõn-nooda tʋlsem wulumd-b lame tɩ b ka tõe n bɩ n taas ye.
42008015	Sẽn lʋɩ-b zĩ-sakdgẽ wã makda sẽn kelg-b Gomdã ne yẽesem la sũ-tɩrga, la b reeg-a ne sũ-keelem t'a womd biisi.
42008016	Ned kõn yõgen fitila n dɩk rʋk n fõgen-a bɩ n dɩgl-a a gãag tẽngr ye; a dogend-a-la a zĩigẽ, tɩ sẽn kẽed-b fãa yãe a vẽenem.
42008017	Sẽn lill ka be sẽn ka na n puk ye, sẽn solg ka be sẽn ka na n wa por yɩng ye.
42008018	Dẽnd yĩnga, bɩ y modg ne kelegre, tɩ sẽn tar-a, b na n paas-a lame la sẽn pa tara b na n deega a sẽn tẽed t'a tara bũmb ningã.»
42008019	A Zezi ma ne b saam-biis waame, la b ka tõog n ta b nengẽ, zãma wã yĩnga.
42008020	Tɩ b wa yeel-ba: «Y ma la y saam-biis n be yɩnga n baood yãmba.»
42008021	Tɩ b leoke: «Mam ma, mam saam-biisi, yaa neb niynsi sẽn kelgd-b Wẽnnaam Gomde la b reegd-a.»
42008022	Daar a ye a Zezi kẽe koom koglgo ne b karen-biisi. B yeel-b lame: «Wa-y tɩ d kẽng mogra rʋʋnde.» La b looga ko-sʋka.
42008023	B sẽn waa n dabda, a Zezi gũsame. Mik sob-raoog kaooga mogra zugu, tɩ koglga kẽed koom, tɩ rabeem beẽ.
42008024	La karen-biisa kolga a Zezi n nek-ba n yetẽ: «Karen-saamba, Karen-saamba, d na n ki wɛ!» B nekame, n tãs sobga la ko-wiisã tɩ b yõke, tɩ fãa lebg sɩɩ.
42008025	Tɩ b na n yaool n yeel-ba: «Yãmb tẽeba bɛɛ?» Dabeem kãseng yõk-b lame tɩ b pɛleng yɩk; la b ra yeta taaba: «Bãmb yaa ãnna n kõt al ba sobg la mogr noor tɩ b sakdẽ?»
42008026	B taa Gadar dãmb tẽnga sẽn tot ne Galile.
42008027	A Zezi sẽn yi koglga pʋga, tẽnga rao a yembre n wa n seg-ba. Sʋtãamb wʋsgo n da be nin-kãng pʋgẽ. Al daar zãra a ra pa le yeelgd fuug ye, a ra ka gãe yir ye, dẽnd yaadẽ.
42008028	A sẽn yãe a Zezi la a sẽn kelme, n wõgemd b taoore n zẽk a koɛɛg n moon woto: «Bõe n be maam ne yãmb sʋka, Zezi, Wẽnnaam Yĩngr soab Biiga? Y sugri la y ra nams-m ye!»
42008029	Dẽ t'a Zezi ra kõta Sʋtãan dẽgda noore t'a yi la a bas raoã. Sɩda, yaa naoor yaka la a ra yõk daoã, tɩ b mii n sẽb-a n gãneg ne wĩ la bãeense, la a kaooda fãa. Sʋtaana ra kẽesd-a la weoogo.
42008030	A Zezi sok-a lame: «Fo yʋʋr la a bõe?» T'a leok: «Kʋʋma» tɩ yaa Sʋtãamb wʋsgo n da kẽ raoã pʋgẽ.
42008031	Sʋtãamba yõka a Zezi sɛɛg tɩ b ra yiis ba n lebs-b bog zulungẽ wã ye.
42008032	Kurkuy ka tɛk n da wãbd yamdo tãnga zugu; Sʋtãamba kosa a Zezi sore n na n yi n kẽ kurkuya; tɩ b kõ-b sore.
42008033	Sʋtãamba basa raoã n yi n kẽ kurkuya la kurkuya zãnga siga tãnga n wudg n tɩ lʋɩ mogra pʋga, n pa koomẽ.
42008034	Sẽn da gũud-b kurkuya sẽn yãe yellã, b zoe n tɩ togsa tẽnga pʋgẽ la tẽn-kɩremsã.
42008035	Neba yiime n wa ges yella sẽn maana. B taa a Zezi nengẽ n mik Sʋtãamba sẽn yi n bas rao ninga t'a zĩ a Zezi taoor ne laafi n yeer fuug la a mi a nenga. La rabeem yõk-b lame.
42008036	Sẽn yãend-b yellã togsa raoã sẽn paam a menga toto.
42008037	Gadar tẽng rãmb fãa sũu taaba n kos a Zezi tɩ b loog n yi b tẽngẽ. Rabeem kãseng da tar-b lame. A Zezi kẽe koom koglgo n lebe b sẽn yiẽ.
42008038	Sʋtãamba sẽn yi n bas rao ninga yõka a Zezi sɛɛg n na n pa ne bãmba; a Zezi kʋls-a lame n yete:
42008039	«Leb f yiri la f tɩ togs Wẽnnaam sẽn maan bũmb ning ne foo.» Daoã kẽngame n tɩ moon tẽnga fãa a Zezi sẽn maan bũmb ning a yĩnga.
42008040	A Zezi lɛɛg n waame. Neb kʋʋng reeg-b lame tɩ b ra gũud-b lame
42008041	la ade, rao a ye n wa. A ra boondame t'a Zayir, n ya pʋʋsg roog naaba. A wõgemda a Zezi taoore n yõk b sɛɛga tɩ b wa kẽe a zakẽ.
42008042	A ra tara a bi-pugl yende sẽn zems yʋʋm piig la a yi. Biiga ra yaa bãada la bãaga ra lebga toogo. A Zezi rɩka a zaka sore, tɩ neba sɩng b pẽdgre.
42008043	Pag a ye me n da bẽed mende, yʋʋm piig la a yiibu; ned ba a ye ka tõog n sãoog-a ye.
42008044	A kolga poorẽ n sɩɩs a Zezi fuug zerdo. Zĩig pʋgẽ bala a zɩɩma yõkame.
42008045	La a Zezi sokame: «Anna n sɩɩs maam?» La ned ba a ye pa saag n yeel tɩ yaa yẽ ye. T'a Piyɛr leok-ba: «Karen-saamba, zãma wã n sũ taaba n dɩdgd yãmba.»
42008046	T'a Zezi yeele: «Ned n sɩɩs maam, tɩ m bãngame tɩ pãng n yi m nengẽ.»
42008047	Paga sẽn mik t'a yella pukame, a waame n digda, n wõgemd a Zezi taoore la a togsame tɩ neb fãa wʋm a sẽn sɩɩs-ba võore, la a sẽn wẽneg n sãoog zĩig pʋgẽ balã. A Zezi yeel-a lame:
42008048	«M biiga, fo tẽeb fãag-f lame, kẽng ne laafi.»
42008049	B sẽn da ket n gomda la ned yi naaba yiri n wa yeele: «Y biiga kiime, da le nams-y karen-saamb ye.»
42008050	La a Zezi ra wʋmame tɩ b na n yeel pʋʋsga roog naaba: «Da maan-y rabeem ye, yãmb ye n tẽ bala, biiga na n tɩlgame.»
42008051	B sẽn ta yiri, b pa sak tɩ ned ba a ye tũ bãmb n kẽ sã n kaa a Piyɛr la a Zã, la a Zak, n paas bi-pugla ba la a ma.
42008052	B fãa ra yãbdame la b tood b yãoogo, kũuma yĩnga. T'a Zezi yeele: «Da yãb-y ye, biiga pa ki ye, a gõeeme.»
42008053	Neba ra laada a Zezi tɩ bãmb yẽ ra miime t'a kiime.
42008054	A Zezi yõka biiga nugu, n zẽk b koɛɛg n yeele: «Biiga yiki!»
42008055	Biiga vɩɩm le waame; vugr bala a yikame. A Zezi yeelame tɩ b kõ-a rɩɩbo.
42008056	Bi-pugla ba ne a ma yɛɛsame; a Zezi sagl-b lame tɩ b ra togs ned ba a ye yella sẽn maana ye.
42009001	A Zezi boola b Tʋʋm-tʋmdb piig la a yiibã n kõ-b pãng la tõogo tɩ b rig sʋtãamba la b sãoog bãad-dãmba fãa.
42009002	B tʋm-b lame tɩ b sa n moon Wẽnd Rĩungã la b yols bãad-dãmba.
42009003	B yeel-b lame: «Da zɩ-y bũmb sor zug yĩng ye. Da zɩ-y dasaare bɩ korgo la rɩɩbo bɩ ligd ye. Ned ba a ye ra zɩ fu-yord a yiib ye.
42009004	Y sẽn kẽ yir ninga bɩ y kell n pa be n tãag y loogre.
42009005	B sẽn pa reeg yãmb zĩig ning fãa, y sã n yit b tẽngẽ bɩ y pĩng y gãndalsa tom tɩ rẽ n yɩ zood kaoob kaseto la taal ningri.»
42009006	Tʋʋm-tʋʋmdba kẽngame, b saaga tẽnsa fãa n moon Koe-noogã la b sãoogd bãad-dãmb zĩis fãa.
42009007	A Erod wʋma a Zezi sẽn maan fãa la a ra ka mi a sẽn na n tags bũmb ning ye tɩ kẽer da gomdame: «Yaa a Zã n vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka.»
42009008	Kẽere: «A Eli n le wa.» Kẽere: «Tẽn-kʋdem-wẽnnẽ bãngd a ye n vʋʋge.»
42009009	La a Erod da yetame: «Sã n ya a Zã, mam n kɩt tɩ b fiuug a zugu. B sẽn gomd rao ning yelle tɩ m wʋmnẽ wã marsã, yẽ la ãnna?» Dẽ la a ra baood n na n yãend a Zezi.
42009010	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba sẽn lɛɛg n wa, b togsa a Zezi bãmb sẽn maan fãa. A Zezi peeg-b lame n yi kɛɛnga; b teesa tẽng sẽn boond tɩ Bɛtsayid.
42009011	Zãma wã bãngame la b rɩka b nao. A Zezi sakame n gom ne-ba, Wẽnd Rĩunga yelle; b sãooga sẽn da tʋl-b laafi wã fãa.
42009012	Wĩndg sẽn waa n dat n kẽ, piig la a yiibã kolg n yeela a Zezi: «Kuls-y neba tɩ b leb Bɛtsayid la pʋtẽ wã n bao gãag zĩiga la b paam dɩɩb n dɩ tɩ d sẽn be ka wã yaa weoogo.»
42009013	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Yãmb meng n tog n kõ-b rɩɩb tɩ b rɩ.» Dẽ la b leok yã: «Bur a nu la kʋɩl-zẽed a yiib bal la d tara. Woto wã d na n kẽnga tẽnga pʋgẽ d toore n tɩ ra rɩɩb n wa, tɩ ka rẽ zãma wã labsa.»
42009014	Daopa sẽn da be be sõor da tõe n taa tus a nu. B yeela b karen-biisã: «Zĩndg-y neba pisnu-nu.»
42009015	B reega noore, n kɩt tɩ neba zĩndi.
42009016	A Zezi reega bur a nu wã ne kʋɩl-zẽed a yiibã n zẽk b neng n tees yĩngri n pʋʋs bark pʋʋsgo. B yaoolame n wes burã n kõ b karen-biisã tɩ b pʋɩ zãma wã.
42009017	B fãa rɩɩme n tɩge n tol zɩ pet piig la a yi, n kuli, pet sẽn pid ne bura girs sẽn kellã.
42009018	A Zezi ra yii kɛɛng, raar a ye, n pʋʋsdẽ. B karen-biisa bal n da be ne ba. B sok-b lame: «Zãma wã yetame tɩ maam la a bõe?»
42009019	Tɩ b leoke: «Kẽer yetame t'a Zã, kẽer t'a Eli. Kẽer tɩ tẽn-kʋdem-wẽnnẽ bãngd a ye sẽn vʋʋge.» T'a Zezi yeel-ba:
42009020	«La yãmb yẽ, yãmb yetame tɩ m yaa ãnna.» A Piyɛr n leoke: «Krista, Wẽnd Nedã!»
42009021	A Zezi kõ-b la noore tɩ b ra saag n togs ned ye.
42009022	B yeelame: «Yaa pakr ne Ned Biiga tɩ b nams wʋsgo, tɩ nin-kẽemba, maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb la sɛb-mitba yiis-b buudẽ la b kʋ-ba; la b na n vʋʋga dasem a tãab daare.»
42009023	B yaool n yeela b fãa: «Ned sã n dat n dɩk mam nao, bɩ a bas a meng yamleoogo la a tʋk a pika, beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa, n tũ maam.
42009024	Sɩd me sẽn tʋll-a n fãag a meng vɩɩm na n menes-a lame la sẽn menesd-a a meng vɩɩm mam yĩnga, na n fãag-a lame.
42009025	Bõe yõod la ned rokda a sã n paam dũni wã zãng fãa n sooge, n yaool n kẽ moogo la a sãam a meng yelle?
42009026	Sẽn yeela tɩ maam ne m goama yãnd tar-a lame, Ned Biig me na yeel yẽ soaba t'a yãnd tar-b lame, b sã n lɛɛg n wa ne zɩɩri, ne b Ba la malɛgs sõma pẽgre.
42009027	Sɩd ne sɩda, mam yeta yãmba tɩ kẽer n be ka n ka na n wʋm kũum yũugu tɩ b pa reng n yãe Wẽnd Rĩunga ye.»
42009028	Dẽ loogr poore, sẽn maan dasm a nii, a Zezi peega a Piyɛr la a Zak, la a Zã. B tɩ rʋʋ tãng n pʋʋsdẽ.
42009029	Pʋʋsga wakato, a Zezi neng tedgame. B futa lebga peelse n pɩnda.
42009030	Ade, neb a yiibu n da sõsd ne bãmba: da yaa a Moyiiz la a Eli n lik ne zɩɩri.
42009031	B da gomda b kũuma sẽn na n yɩ a soab Zerizalɛɛm.
42009032	Dẽ t'a Piyɛr ne a tũud-n-taasa ra zuka gõeem tɩ gõeema ra tar-b la wʋsgo. B sẽn neke b yãenda a Zezi zɩɩrã ne rapa yiibã sẽn da be-b ne bãmbã.
42009033	Nin-bãmb sẽn waa n loogdẽ, a Piyɛr yeelame: «Karen-saamba, tõnd sẽn be ka wã, d sũur yaa noogo. D tilg zãn a tãabo, a ye yãmb yĩnga, a to a Moyiiz yĩnga, a tãab soaba a Eli yĩnga.» A ra ka tar a goama nao ye.
42009034	La a sẽn waa n gomdã, sawadg n waa n lud bãmba tɩ lebg likã, tɩ b yɛɛsdẽ.
42009035	La koɛɛg n yi sawadga pʋgẽ n yetẽ: «Bãmb yaa mam Bi-nongre, kelg-y-ba!»
42009036	B wʋma koɛɛgã la dẽ pore b mikame t'a Zezi lebga b yembre. Karen-biisa me tõoga b noore wakat kãng n pa togs ned ba a ye b sẽn yãend bũmb ninga ye.
42009037	Vẽkembeoogo, b sẽn sig tãngã la zãma wã sẽn pooge.
42009038	Ade, dao a ye n zĩnd zãma wã sʋka n kelme: «Karen-saamba, m yõkd-y-la sɛɛga, ges-y m biiga yelle tɩ yaa m bi-yende.
42009039	Sʋtãan a ye n mii n yõk-a t'a tar kɛlenga. Wakat ninga sʋtãana lubd-a la tẽnga t'a yĩnga vɩgda, t'a noor lasd tãntãnpuudu; a pa yit n bas-a naana ye. A rengd n sɛɛsa a pãnga zãnga.
42009040	Mam kosa y karen-biisa tɩ b rig-a la b pa tõog ye.»
42009041	A Zezi yeelame: «Kɩɩsdb la bi-bees buudu, mam na n kaoosa ne yãmb la m tõog m sũurã n ta da-bʋre? Tall f biigã n wa ka.»
42009042	Biiga sẽn wa n kolgdẽ, sʋtãana lub-a-la tẽnga t'a gãe n vigd ne pãnga. A Zezi tãsa sʋtãan dẽgda, n sãoog biigã n lebs-a a ba.
42009043	B fãa yãenda Wẽnnaam pãngã tɩ b pɛleng yɩke. Ned kam sẽn da pẽgd a Zezi sẽn maana yĩnga, bãmb yeela b karen-biisi:
42009044	«Yok-y y tʋbre n kelg m goama: B na n yõka Ned Biiga n ning ninsaalb nusẽ.»
42009045	La karen-biisa pa wʋmd gomda sẽn lebdẽ ye, t'a Zezi pa tʋlg tɩ yɩ vẽenega tɩ b wʋma võor ye; la soka Zezi b gomda võor da yaa rabeem ne-ba.
42009046	B yika no-koeemd ne taaba n na n bãng, bãmb sʋka, ãnna n yɩɩd a taaba.
42009047	A Zezi sẽn da mi b sũur tagsgo, b zĩndga bi-bilf b sɛɛgẽ n yeel-ba:
42009048	«Sẽn deeg-a bi-bilfã reega mam menga, sẽn deeg-a maam deega sẽn tʋmeb maama. La sẽn yaa yao-zʋʋg yãmb sʋka yẽ n yɩɩd a taaba.»
42009049	A Zã yeelame: «Karen-saamba, tõnd yãee dao a yembre sẽn digd sʋtãan yãmb yʋʋr yĩnga la tõnd gɩdg-a lame t'a pa lagem ne tõnd n tũud yãmb ye.»
42009050	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Bɩ y ra rig-a ye! Sẽn pa zabd-a ne yãmba bee yãmb poorẽ.»
42009051	B daara sẽn waa n kolge tɩ b na n yi dũni kãnga, a Zezi kenga b pɛlga n dɩk Zerizalɛɛm sore.
42009052	Neb la b tʋm tɩ b reng taoore. B rɩka sore la b tɩ kẽe Samari tẽng a ye n na segl b waoongo.
42009053	B sẽn ta, be rãmb pa reeg-b neer ye, tɩ b yãeeme tɩ yaa Zerizalɛɛm la b da rabda.
42009054	A Zak ne a Zã sẽn yãend woto b yeelame: «Yãmb datame tɩ d kõ noor tɩ saag bugum sig n yõog bãmba bɩ?»
42009055	A Zezi wẽneg n ges-lame m sãbs-ba.
42009056	La b yiime n kẽ tẽng a to.
42009057	B sẽn waa n be sorẽ, ned n yeel bãmba: «Mam na n tũu yãmba, y sẽn na n kẽng tẽng ning fãa.»
42009058	A Zezi leoka yẽ soaba: «Waas tara b bogdo tɩ yĩngr luiili tar b tʋgdo. Ned Biiga yẽ pa tar zĩig n gãnegd b zug ye.»
42009059	B yeela ned a to: «Tũ maam!» T'a soab leoke: «Kõ-y maam sore tɩ m deng n tɩ mum m ba.»
42009060	La a Zezi yeel-a lame: «Bas kɩɩmsa tɩ b mum taaba; la foom, kẽng n tɩ moon Wẽnd Rĩungu.»
42009061	Ned a to me n yeel-ba: «M na n pʋga yãmba, Soaala, la bɩ y kõ sore tɩ m deng n tɩ pʋʋs m neba wẽnd na taas la m yaool n wa.»
42009062	T'a Zezi leok-a: «Ned sã n gãd wãka n zõond n na n ko, n wẽneg n ges a poorẽ, a soab ka tog ne Wẽnd Rĩung ye.»
42010001	Dẽ poore Soaala le tũusa karen-biis pisopoe la a yiibu n tʋm ba tɩ b reng bãmb taoore, b yiib-yiibu, zĩis fãa la tẽns niyns fãa bãmb meng sẽn dag n na n kẽngẽ.
42010002	B ra yet-b lame: «Ka-kɛɛra waooga la ka-kɛɛdba sõor paoodame. Pʋʋs-y Tigsga Naaba tɩ b yiis tʋʋm-tʋmdba ka-kɛɛra yĩnga.
42010003	Kẽng-y! La ade, m tʋmda yãmb wa pe-bi digd-n-yĩids sʋka.
42010004	Da zɩ-y korg bɩ waoog ye, bɩ neodr ye la y ra yaas n pʋʋs ned sor zugu ye.
42010005	Yãmb sẽn kẽed zak ninga, reng-y n yeel-y: ‹Laafi sig yi-kãnga!›
42010006	Laafi biig sã n be a pʋgẽ, yãmb laafi na sig a zugu, sã n pa rẽ, a lebda yãmba.
42010007	Bɩ y kell n pa yir kãnga n dɩtẽ la y yũud b sẽn kõt-y bũmb ning fãa, tɩ tʋʋm-tʋmd toga ne yaoodo. Bɩ y ra sa yir woo yir ye.
42010008	Yãmb sẽn kẽ tẽng ning fãa tɩ b reeg yã, bɩ y rɩ la y yũ b sẽn na n tẽgen y taoore.
42010009	Sãoog-y tẽnga bãad-dãmba la y yeel nebã: ‹Wẽnd Rĩung pẽe yãmba.›
42010010	La yãmb sẽn kẽ tẽng ninga tɩ b pa reeg yã, kẽng-y b sɛk zĩigẽ la y yeele:
42010011	‹Al ba yãmb tẽnga tom sẽn tabend tõnd nao, tõnd pĩmsd-a lame n bas ne yãmba, la baasg fãa bãng-y tɩ Wẽnnaam Rĩung kolgame.›
42010012	M yeta yãmb tɩ bʋʋda raare, Sodom sɩbgr toolem kõn zeng tẽn kãng rẽnn ye.
42010013	Na pak foom Korozein! Na pak foom Bɛtsayid! Tɩ wẽnd makr dãmb sẽn maan yãmb sʋka sã n da maanẽ Tir la Sidõ, b ra pĩn n yeelgẽ sũ-pa-noang futu la b bilmẽ tompɛglem n kos sugri al daar zãra.
42010014	Dẽ yĩnga, bʋʋd kaoob daare, Tir la Sidõ rãmb sɩbgr toolem kõn kolg yãmb dẽn ye.
42010015	La foom, Kafarnaom, fo zẽkd f meng n tãag saag me, b na n sika foom al n tɩ tãag bʋg-tẽnga.
42010016	Sẽn kelgd-a yãmb kelgda maam; sẽn zãgs-a yãmb zãgsa maam; sẽn zãgs-a maam, zãgsa sẽn tʋm-a maama.»
42010017	Karen-biis pisopoe la a yi wã lebg n waa ne sũ-noog n yeele: «Soaala, al ba sʋtãamba reegda tõnd noore, yãmb yʋʋr yĩnga.»
42010018	A Zezi yeel-b lame: «Mam da nee sʋtãan sẽn da yit yĩngri n lʋɩt wa saag sʋʋga.
42010019	Ade, mam kõo yãmb tõog, tɩ y tab wiis la namse la bɛyã ne a pãnga fãa kõn tõog n maan y bũmb ye.
42010020	La baasgo bɩ y ra noog y sũuri sʋtãamba sẽn deegd y noor yĩng ye, noog-y sũuri yãmb yʋy wã sẽn gʋls arzãnẽ yĩnga.»
42010021	Wakat kãnga Wẽnd Vʋʋsem kɩtame tɩ b yeele: «Mam pẽgd-y lame, Ba, yĩngr la tẽng Soaala, yãmb sẽn solg yell bãmba, yam dãmda la yẽesem dãmba, n yaool n wilg-b kom-bõonego. N-yẽe! M Ba, woto la yãmb tʋlgre ne y nimbãan-zoeerã.
42010022	M Ba rɩka bũmb fãa n kõ maam, ned ba a ye ka mi m Ba sẽn yaa a soaba, sã n ka Biigã, la Biiga sẽn sak n wilg a soaba.»
42010023	La b wẽneg n gesa b karen-biisã n yeel-ba, bãmb ne taab bala: «Sũ-noog rãmba la nin sẽn yãet yãmb sẽn yãete!
42010024	Mam yeta yãmba: bãngdba la nanamse tʋlg n yãee yãmb sẽn yãetã, la b pa yãe ye, la b wʋm yãmb sẽn wʋmd bũmb ningã, la b pa wʋm ye.»
42010025	La ade, noor karen-saamb a yembre n yik n na n bẽd-ba, n sok-ba: «Karen-saamba, bõe la m tog n maan n paam vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ?»
42010026	T'a Zezi leok-a: «Noor sebre pʋgẽ b gʋlsa bõe? Bõe la y karemda?»
42010027	T'a leoke: «Nong Soaala, f Wẽnnaam ne f sũur fãa, ne f pɛlg fãa, ne f pãng fãa la ne f yam fãa, la f nong f to n wẽnd f menga.»
42010028	A Zezi yeelame: «Yãmb leoka neere! Maan-y woto tɩ y na paam Vɩɩm.»
42010029	Karen-saamba sẽn da rat n kõ a meng bʋʋm, a soka a Zezi: «La m to yaa ãnna sẽ?»
42010030	T'a Zezi leok-a: «Ned n da yi Zerizalɛɛm n dabd Zeriko n tees n lʋɩ fãadb nusẽ tɩ b rees a teeda fãa n pogl-a, n bas-a t'a rat n ki.
42010031	Maan-kʋʋd a ye n waa n tũud so kãnga n yãend-a la a bas-a lame n looge
42010032	maan-kʋʋd sõangd a ye n waa n yãend-a, n bas-a n looge.
42010033	La Samari dao a yembre n da togd sore n wa lood be. A sẽn yãend-a, a zoe-la a nimbãanega,
42010034	la a kolgame n dɩk rãam ne kaam n pek a noadã, n vil ne pɛɛla, n zombg-a a meng bõanga, n tall n kẽng a gãag soab yiri, n tɩbs-a.
42010035	Vẽkembeoogo, a yãka wakɩ koeems a yiibu n kõ a gãag soaba n yeele: ‹Tɩbs-y neda neere, la y sẽn na n sãam ligd ning n paase, m sã n lɛɛg n wa, m na lebs yãmba.›
42010036	Bãmb b tãaba sʋka, sã n ya ne yãmba, ãnda n ges raoã sẽn lʋɩ fãadba nusẽ wala a to?»
42010037	Tɩ karen-saamba leok: «Yaa sẽn zoe-a raoã nimbãanega sẽ.» T'a Zezi yeel-a: «Bɩ y kẽnge, la yãmb me maan boto.»
42010038	A Zezi sẽn dɩk sor ne b karen-biisi, b tɩ kẽe tẽng-a ye tɩ pag a ye sẽn boond t'a Mart reeg-b sãando, a yiri.
42010039	A Mart da tara yao sẽn boond t'a Mari, la yao wã ra zĩi Soaala taoore n kelgd b goama.
42010040	A Mart da yãgda ne rɩɩba seglgo la ragend tʋʋm a taaba; a waa n yaasa a Zezi taoore n yeele: «M yao wã sẽn bas maam tɩ m segend m yembrã ka pak yãmb ye? Soaala, yeel-y m tão wã t'a yik n wa sõng-m wɛ!»
42010041	Soaala leok-a lame: «Mart, Mart, fo maanda yɩɩre, la fo sũkda bũmb wʋsg poorẽ,
42010042	la yaool n yaa bũmb a ye bala n pake. A Mari sẽn yãk pʋɩɩr ningã n são, la b kõn deeg n bas-a ye.»
42011001	Daar a ye, a Zezi da bee zĩig a ye n pʋʋsdẽ. B sẽn pʋʋs n sɛ, b karen-biig a yembr yeel-b lame: «Soaala, zãms-y tõnd pʋʋsgo wala a Zã sẽn zãms a karen-biisi.»
42011002	A Zezi yeelame: «Yãmb sã n pʋʋsdẽ, yeel-y woto: ‹Ba, y yʋʋr yi ne pẽgre, y naam wa.
42011003	Kõ-y tõnd beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa, d daara rɩɩbo.
42011004	Kõ-y tõnd d yel-wẽna sugri, tɩ tõnd me kõta sẽn beeg-b tõnda fãa sugri la y ra bas tɩ kʋɩɩbg yõk-d ye.› »
42011005	B le yeel-b lame: «Yãmb sʋka, ned sã n tar-a zoa t'a bʋʋg-a yʋn-sʋk n yeel-a: ‹M zoa, peng-m bur a tã,
42011006	tɩ m zoa a to n yi sor n wa, tɩ m ka tar bũmb n na n kõ-a ye.›
42011007	Tɩ yãoo soaba zĩnd roogẽ n leoke: ‹Bas-m laafi tɩ m doog pagame, maam ne kamba kẽe gãaga, ad-m ka tõe n yik n bao n kõ-f ye.›
42011008	Mam yeta yãmba, t'a zoa wã sã n pa yik n kõ-a, b zooda yĩng me, pẽdgra yĩnga, a na yik n kõ-a wala a sẽn dat tɛka.
42011009	La mam yeta yãmba: kos-y tɩ b na n kõ-y lame, bao-y tɩ y na n yãeeme; kabs-y tɩ b na pak tɩ y kẽ.
42011010	Sɩd me, sẽn bõsd-a paamdame, sẽn baood-a yãetame la sẽn kabsd-a, b pakd n kõ-a lame.
42011011	Yãmb sʋka, roagd a bõe n be t'a biig kos-a kʋɩl-zẽoogo, t'a bas kʋɩl-zẽegã n kõt-a waafo?
42011012	Bɩ a kos-a la gelle, t'a kõ-a nanga?

42011014	A Zezi ra yiisda Sʋtãan sẽn da kẽ neda t'a lebg muka. Sʋtãana sẽn yi, muka gomame, tɩ neb pɛleng yɩke.
42011015	La neb kẽer yeelame: «Ad-y yaa ne sʋtãamb naab a Beelzebul pãnga la a yiisd sʋtãamba.»
42011016	La kẽer me da rat n bãnga b pãnga, n kos-b bõn-bãnd a ye sẽn yit yĩngri.
42011017	A Zezi sẽn da mi b tagsgo, b yeel-b lame: «Rĩung a ye rãmb sã n welg n maan beem ne taaba, b wãada b rĩungã t'a rot lʋɩ n bʋʋg taaba.
42011018	Sʋtãana sã n welg la a maand beem ne a soolem dãmba, a rĩung na n le zĩnda wãna? Yãmb sẽn yet tɩ yaa ne a Beelzebul pãnga la m yiisd sʋtãamba,
42011019	la mam sã n digd sʋtãamba ne a Beelzebul pãnga, yãmb digd-b la ne ãnd pãng marsã? Woto yĩnga, yãmb meng n kaood y bʋʋdo.
42011020	La mam sã n digd sʋtãamba ne Wẽnnaam nug pãnga, dẽnna Wẽnd Rĩunga sɩd waa yãmb sʋka.
42011021	Gãndaoog bob a zab teed n gũud a zaka, a sẽn tar fãa, bũmb kõn maan ye.

42011024	Sʋtãan dẽgd sã n yi ned pʋgẽ, a gõoda zĩ-peen-daagẽ n baood vʋʋsgo n kongdẽ. Dẽ la a wat n yeele: ‹M leb roog ninga mam sẽn yii wã.›
42011025	A sã n le wa kẽe, a mikdame tɩ b pɩɩsa sagda n maneg-a neere;
42011026	t'a kẽng n le tɩ wa ne sʋtãamb a yopoe wẽnem sẽn yɩɩd yẽnda, tɩ b fãa kẽ be n maag b meng n zĩndi tɩ nin-kãng yell sãam n yɩɩd pĩnda.»
42011027	A Zezi sẽn gom woto, la pag a ye sẽn zĩnd bãndurba sʋka n zẽk a koɛɛg n yeele: «Sũ-noog soaba la pag ning sẽn tʋda y pʋga tɩ y yẽsem a bĩisim!»
42011028	La a Zezi leokame: «Yeel-y tɩ sũ-noog rãmba n yɩɩda la sẽn kelgd-b Wẽnnaam gomde la b reegd-a.»
42011029	Zãma wã ra yaa wʋsgo tɩ wa lebg pẽdgre t'a Zezi na n yeele: «Zamaan kãnga yaa zamaan yoogo; a bolgda wẽnd makre la a kõn paam makr a to n zʋʋg a Zonas rẽnda ye.
42011030	Wala a Zonas sẽn yɩ makre Niniv rãmb yĩnga, woto me Ned Biigã na n yɩɩ makre zamaan kãnga yĩnga.
42011031	Bʋʋda raare, dĩm-poaka sẽn yi tẽn-zãorgẽ wã na n yik n bʋʋ zamaan kãnga bʋʋdo n mong-a bʋʋm, tɩ yẽ yii al dũni wã sɛtmẽ, n wa kelg yam soab a Salomo goama; la sẽn yɩɩda a Salomo n be ka.
42011032	Bʋʋda raare, Niniv rãmb na n yikame n bʋ zamaan kãng bʋʋdo la b na n mong-a la bʋʋm tɩ b sẽn wʋm a Zonas saglgo, b tuuba b yel-wẽna; la ade: sẽn be-a ka wã yɩɩda a Zonas.
42011033	Ned kõn yõgen fitila n solg-a bɩ n fõgen-a rʋk ye; a dogend-a-la roagendga zugu tɩ sẽn kẽedba fãa yãe vẽenem.
42011034	Fo nif la a f yĩng fitila, fo nif sã n ya sõmbo fo yĩnga fãa tara vẽenem; a sã n pa sõmbe, fo yĩnga zãng fãa zĩi ne lika.
42011035	Ges f sẽn tar vẽenem ninga sã n ka lebg lika!
42011036	Ad-f yĩnga fãa sã n tara vẽenem t'a wilg ba a ye ka be likẽ, a zãng faa na n yɩɩ vẽenem wala f fitil sẽn vẽnegd-f ne a vẽenem.»
42011037	A Zezi sẽn da waa n gomdã, Farizẽ a yembre n waa n kos tɩ b wa rɩ a yiiri. Tɩ b kẽ n sɩng rɩɩbo.
42011038	Farizẽ wã yãee ne pɛlen-yɩka tɩ b pa reng n nudg b nus n yaool n sɩng rɩɩb ye.
42011039	La Soaala yeel-a lame: «M nong rẽ! Yãmb Farizẽ rãmba nedgda laag la wamd poore tɩ y menga yaool n pid ne wagdem la wẽnem.
42011040	Gãeemse! Sẽn naana poore, ka bãmb n naan pʋg la?
42011041	Dɩk-y y sũura sẽn gãd bũmb ningã n maan wẽn-kosgo tɩ sẽn keta fãa na yɩ yɩlgemde y yĩnga.
42011042	La na pak yãmba, Farizẽ rãmba! Yãmb yãkda y zẽ-vãadã la y zẽ-biisa sẽn tar yũ-noogã n kõtẽ, dʋr a ye piig zugu, n yaool n yãk y toog ne pʋ-peelem la Wẽnnaam nonglem: y tog n pidsẽ la boto, la woto me ra ka togẽ n pa sãoog ye.
42011043	La na pak yãmba, Farizẽ rãmba! Tɩ pʋʋsg rotẽ yãmb nong n zĩnda taoore, waoor zĩigẽ, y nonga pʋʋs-bɛda kʋʋng zĩigẽ, sɛk zĩigẽ.
42011044	Na pak yãmba, Farizẽ rãmba! Tɩ yãmb wẽnda yaad sẽn sarem tɩ neb tabd n pa mii ye!»
42011045	Noor karen-saamb a ye leokame: «Yãmb sẽn gom woto wã, y sãbsda tõnd me.»
42011046	La a Zezi leokame: «Na pak yãmb me, Noor karen-saam-dãmba! Tɩ yãmb tʋkda ninsaalba, zɩɩb b sẽn pa tõe n tʋke, tɩ yãmb menga nug-bil yaool n pa sɩɩsd bũmb ye.
42011047	Na pak yãmba! Tɩ y manegd n meta bãngdba yaado la yaool n yaa y yaab rãmb n kʋ bãngdbã.
42011048	Dẽnd yĩnga yãmb ne bãmb yaa kaset yɛnga: Bãmb n sɩd kʋ, tɩ yãmb, b kamba, tẽeda tɩ y roka b yãnde, n manegd bãngdba yaado!
42011049	Yaa woto la yell kõ-ling-m Wẽnda beool n yeele: M na n tʋm-b la bãngdba la tʋʋm-tʋmdba, b na n kʋʋ kẽere, n dig kẽere,
42011050	sẽn na n yɩ-la tɩ b wa sok zamaan kãnga kamba, bãngdba faa zɩɩm sẽn daag al dũni sɩngre,
42011051	sẽn sɩng ne a Abɛl zɩɩm n tãag a Zakari, b sẽn kʋ a soaba maan-kugr la Wẽnd doog sʋka. Sɩd wa m sẽn yetã, zamaan kãnga na rɩ zɩ-kãng fãa taale!
42011052	Na pak yãmba, Noor karen-saam-dãmba! Yãmb looga ne bãngra roog kʋɩlen-bila, yãmb meng n pa kẽede la y yaool n digda sẽn dat-ba me kõom.»
42011053	A Zezi sẽn yi be, Sɛb-mita la Farizẽ rãmba sɩng n dat-b la ne wẽnga la b pẽdgd bãmb ne sokr dãmb wʋsgo, bũmb wʋsg poorẽ.
42011054	B ra gãnegd-b-la bẽdgo, n dat tɩ b meng noor yiis gomd sẽn na n paalg-ba.
42012001	Wakat kãnga, zãma ka tɛk tigmame n gũbg a Zezi n tabd taaba, tɩ b na n sɩng n yeel b karen-biisã: «Gũus-y y meng ne Farizẽ rãmb rabɩlle, ne b zãmbã.
42012002	Sẽn lud ka be tɩ b ka na n wa puk-a ye. Sẽn solg me ka be tɩ b ka na n wa bãng-a ye.
42012003	Dẽ n so tɩ yãmb sẽn togs bũmb ning fãa yʋngo, b na wʋm-a wĩnto-sʋka, la y sẽn kẽed roog n walm bũmb ning tʋbrẽ, b na rʋ bɛoongo n moon-a.
42012004	Mam yeta yãmba, m zo-rãmba, da zoe-y sẽn kʋʋd-b yĩnga n yaool n pa tõe n paas bũmb a to ye.
42012005	Yaas-y tɩ m wilg yãmba, y sẽn tog n zoe a soaba. Zoe-y sẽn kʋʋda la a leb n tõe n kẽes yãmb bugmẽ. N-yẽe! Mam yeta yãmba, yẽ soab la y tog n zoe.
42012006	Yirs a nu ka koosd tãm a yiib wɛɛ? Ne rẽ fãa Wẽnnaam pa yĩmd bãmb ba a ye yell ye.
42012007	Al ba yãmb zug zobdo, b sõd-b-la zãnga. Bɩ y ra maan rabeem ye, yãmb bee yõod n yɩɩd yirs ka tɛka.
42012008	M yeta yãmba, sẽn yeel-a ninsaalb taoore t'a mii maam, Ned Biiga me na yeel Wẽnnaam malɛk rãmb taoore, tɩ b mii yẽ soaba.
42012009	La sẽn kɩɩsda neb taoore t'a ka mi maam, mam me na kɩɩs Wẽnnaam malɛk rãmb taoore tɩ m ka mi-a ye.

42012012	A Vʋʋsem Sõng n na n wilg yãmb wakat kãng bala y sẽn tog n yeele.»
42012013	Ned n zĩnd zãma wã sʋka n yeel a Zezi: «Karen-saamba, yeel-y m ba-biiga t'a pʋɩ d ba sẽn bas laog ningã, n kõ-m m dẽnna.»
42012014	Tɩ b na n leok-a: «Daoa! Ãnda n kõ-m sore tɩ m bʋ yãmb bʋʋdo la m pʋɩ yãmb laogo?»
