44004034	Bũmb da ka paoogd ned ba a ye. Sẽn da tar-b pʋto la teed a taaba da koosd-b lame n wat ne ligdã
44004035	n dɩgend Tʋʋm-tʋmdba taoore. Dẽn marsã la b ra tõe n kõ ned kam fãa wala a zu-loɛɛga yolsg sẽn dat tɛka.
44004036	Sɩnga ne a Zozɛf; yẽnda la b sẽn pʋd t'a Barnabe, a mi sagl n gãneg sũuri; a yaa Levi buud neda la a ra yita Sɩpr tẽnga.
44004037	A ra tara pʋʋgo, a koos-a lame n tall ligdã n wa kɩs Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã.
44005001	A Anani me ne a pag, a Safir, waa n koosa b pʋʋgo.
44005002	A Anani seda ne a paga n yãk ligdã n yaool n tall sẽn keesã n wa kɩs Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã.
44005003	Dẽ la a Piyɛr yeel-a: «Anani, bõe yĩng la f sak tɩ Sʋtãan kẽ f sũurẽ tɩ f wedg pʋʋga ligdi n na n tudg Wẽnd Vʋʋsem?
44005004	F Pʋʋga sẽn da waa n ket f soolmẽ, da yaa pakr tɩ f koos-a bɩ? La f sẽn koos-a wã, ka foo n so a ligdã n tõe n maan f sẽn dat ne-a bɩ? Maana a wãna tɩ soos n kell n yet tɩ kɩsa zãnga waa f yamẽ? Ad ka ninsaalb la f yag zirẽ ye, yaa Wẽnd menga.»
44005005	A Anani sẽn wʋm gomdã, a lʋɩɩme n kell n ki. Rabeem kãseng me yõka sẽn wʋm-b kibarã.
44005006	Kom-bɩɩb n wa n pil-a fuugu n dɩk-a n tɩ mum.
44005007	Wakat a tãabo sẽn looge, a paga sẽn da ka mi tɩ yell n maana me waame, la a sẽn kẽ,
44005008	a Piyɛr yeel-a lame: «Yɩɩ woto tɛk la y sẽn koos y pʋʋga bɩ?» Tɩ yẽ leoke: «N-ye! Yɩɩ boto.»
44005009	T'a Piyɛr na n yeel-a: «Yãmb yɩɩ wãn n sed ne taaba, n na n belg a Vʋʋsem Sõngo? Ade, sẽn yɛs-b rignoorẽ wã yaa sẽn tɩ mum-f sɩdã, la fo me la b waa n na n dɩke.»
44005010	Nif kamsg pʋgẽ, a Anani lʋɩ-la a Piyɛr taoore n be kũum. Kom-bɩɩba sẽn kẽ wã mikame t'a kiime tɩ b tall-a n loog n tɩ mum-a n yegl a sɩda.
44005011	Rabeem kãseng yõka Tigingã zãnga la sẽn wʋm-b kibara fãa.
44005012	Zãma wã sʋka, yaa bõn-bãna la wẽnd makr dãmb ka tɛka la Tʋʋm-tʋmdba ra maanda.
44005013	B ra zemsa taab n paad a Salomo zãongẽ wã. Ned ba a ye ra ka saagd n yi kɛɛnga n wa lagem ne-b ye. Zãma wã da tara b pẽgr bala.
44005014	Tẽedba sõor da tara paasgo, pagb la rapa,
44005015	al tɩ b ra wat n dɩgend bãad-dãmba ne b gãas, gãas paal wala kʋda, soya zutu, tɩ ba na yɩ nin-yend, bɩ a Piyɛr maasma bui-a a sã n wa looda.
44005016	Zãma wã ra yita Zerizalɛɛm tẽn-toosa meng n wat ne b bãad-dãmba la Sʋtãan yood sẽn kẽ b rãmba la b fãa ra paamda laafi.
44005017	Sega maan-kʋʋd kãsenga waoongo, yẽ ne a poorẽ dãmba la Saduseẽ rãmba. Fãa sũur da pida ne beem bala,
44005018	tɩ b na n yõg Tʋʋm-tʋmdba n sui bi-bees roogẽ.
44005019	La Soaala malɛk waa yʋngo n pags bi-beesa roog kʋɩlemse tɩ b yi t'a yeel-ba:
44005020	«Dig-y wẽnd doogẽ wã n tɩ wilg zãma wã bũmb ning fãa sẽn get fãagra yelle.»
44005021	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba reega malɛka noore la b tõda beoog n kẽ wẽnd doogẽ wã, n sɩng zãmsgo. Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga waa ne a poorẽ dãmba, n bool bʋ-kaoodba bʋʋda zĩigẽ, ne Israyɛl buuda nin-kẽemse la b yeelame tɩ b tɩ yiis Tʋʋm-tʋmdba bi-beesa roogo n tall n wa.
44005022	Sẽn kẽng-ba n na tɩ yiis-b bi-beesa roogã ka tɩ yãend-b ye tɩ b lɛɛg n wa yeele:
44005023	«D tɩ mikame tɩ bi-beesa roog kʋɩlens paga neere, d yãenda gũud fãa a zĩigẽ. La d sẽn pake d pa yãend b sẽn yõk b rãmba pugẽ ye; ned ba a ye.»
44005024	B sẽn wʋm woto, gũudba naaba la maan-kʋʋd kãsenga yɛɛsame la b fãa ra baooda yella võore.
44005025	Wakat kãng la ned waa n yeel-ba: «Yãmb sẽn da kẽes b rãmb roogã, ad-y b bee wẽnd doogẽ n karemd nebã.»
44005026	Tɩ gũudba kãsma ne a neba na n leb wẽnd doogẽ wã, n tɩ wa ne-ba. B ka maan b pãng ye; b ra zoeta zãma wã, b ra zoeta b na n wa lab-b ne kuga.
44005027	B sẽn wa, b kẽes-b la bʋ-kaoodb bɛda bʋʋdo tɩ Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga na n sok-ba:
44005028	«Tõnd da ka yeel yãmb tɩ y ra saag n pʋd Neda yʋʋr laa. Yaool n yaa zãms kãng la y yelg n pid Zerizalɛɛm tõre! Yãmb datame tɩ d dɩ a zɩɩma taal bɩ bõe?»
44005029	Ta Piyɛr na n leoke ne a taabã: «Yaa Wẽnd noora la d tog n sake n yɩɩd ninsaal dẽnna.
44005030	D yaab rãmba Wẽnnaam n vʋʋg Zesi ninga y sẽn da ka pik n kʋ wã.
44005031	Zezi kãng la b zĩndg b rɩtgo n kɩt t'a lebg Dĩm la Fãagda, sẽn na n yɩlẽ t'a Israyɛl paam, bãmb maasmẽ, a yel-wẽna tuubgu la b sugri.
44005032	Tõnd tara yell kãens fãa kaseto, tõnd ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo, b sẽn kõt sẽn kẽed-b bãmbã.»
44005033	B ra kelgda a Piyɛr goama tɩ b sũur fõta, tɩ b kaool b kũum.
44005034	Dẽ la Farizẽ a ye sẽn boond tɩ Gamaliyɛl yik bʋʋda zĩigẽ. Da yaa Noora karen-saamba, neba fãa sẽn da waoogde. A kosame tɩ b zãag ne Tʋʋm-tʋmdba bilfu,
44005035	la a yeela bʋ-kaoodbã: «Israyɛl buudu, gũus-y y sẽn dat n maan bũmb ning ne nin-bãmba wã.
44005036	Bãng-y tɩ raar sẽn vẽsg bilfu a Tewudas yikame n yet tɩ yẽ yaa raoa, tɩ neb na ta kobs-naas yik n pʋg-a. B kʋ-a lame t'a poorẽ dãmba sẽege, la bũmb ka kell ye.
44005037	Yẽ poore, sõadga wakato, yaa Galile rao a Zɩɩda, n paam tɩ neb sũ a poorẽ. Yẽ me kiime tɩ sẽn da pʋgd-b yẽnda wã sẽege.
44005038	Dũnna wã, m yet-y lame, bas-y nin-bãmba, da lʋɩɩs-y y toog ye. B goama wala b tʋʋma sã n yit ninsaal nengẽ, b na n menema b toore.
44005039	La sã n sɩd yaa Wẽnd nengẽ la b yita, y kõn tõog n sãam fɩ. Woto wã da saag-y n wa lebg Wẽnd bɛɛb ye.» Fãa reega a saglgo.
44005040	B le talla Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã n wa sʋka. B pãb-b la ne kaase, n yeel tɩ b ra saag n pʋd a Zezi yʋʋr ye la b bas-b lame.
44005041	B yii bʋʋda zĩigẽ la b ra kɩdemda sũ-noogo b sẽn paam paoogre a Zezi Yʋʋr yĩnga.
44005042	Beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa, wẽnd doogẽ wã bɩ b zagsẽ, b ra ka vʋʋsd ne a Zezi Krista Koe-nooga mooneg ye.
44006001	Tẽedba sõor sẽn da tar paasg yĩnga, wakat n zĩndi tɩ sẽn gomd-b grɛka guglem ne Ebre rãmbã. B ra yetame tɩ beoog-beoog pʋɩɩra wakato, b wẽgda bãmb pʋg-kõapa.
44006002	Dẽ me la Tʋʋm-tʋmdba tigim karen-biisa zãnga n yeel-ba: «Ka segd tɩ tõnd bas Koe-nooga moonego n ges rɩɩba pʋɩɩr ye.
44006003	Ges-y yãmb sʋka n yãk neb a yopoe sẽn tar yʋ-noogo, tɩ Wẽnd me pids-b ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng vẽenem, tɩ d kõ-b tʋʋmd kãnga.»
44006004	Sã n ya tõndo, tõnd tʋʋmd na n yii pʋʋsgo la Koe-nooga moonego.
44006005	Koɛɛga taa neba fãa yam tɩ b na n yãk a Etiyɛn ned sẽn pid ne tẽeb la ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsem, n paas a Filip, a Prokor, a Nikanor, a Timon, a Parmenas la a Nikola, Zʋɩf kẽed paalg sẽn yit Antiyos
44006006	B tall-b lame n wa Tʋʋm-tʋmdba taoore tɩ bãmb pʋʋse la b tẽeg b nus b zutu.
44006007	Wẽnd Gomda ra paamda moonego. Karen-biisa sõor da paasda wʋsg Zerizalɛɛm la maan-kʋʋdba wʋsg mens da sak n lebga tẽedba.
44006008	A Etiyɛn sẽn da pid ne sõmblem la pãnga, ra bee b sʋk n maand wẽnd makr dãmba la bõn-bãna.
44006009	La neb n waa n yiki n na n wẽ no-koɛɛm ne a Etiyɛn. Yaa pʋʋsg roog a ye rãmba sẽn yɩ yem-daad Rom la sẽn paam b mens n lɛɛg n wa. Le paasa Sirɛn neba, ne Aleksãndri, Silisi la Azi rãmba.
44006010	B ra pa tõe n lub a Etiyɛn ye. A tara yam vẽenem sẽn pa paoode la a Vʋʋsem Sõng da gomda ne a noore.
44006011	B kong n bao ligd n kõ neb tɩ b wa yeele: «D wʋmame t'a gomd n tʋʋsd a Moyiiz la a tʋʋsd Wẽnde.»
44006012	B rãmba Zãma wã, nin-kẽemsã la Noora karen-saam-dãmbã. B soos n yõk-a lame n wa bʋʋda zĩigẽ.
44006013	Be me b waa ne kaset ziri dãmba sẽn yeele: «Nin-kãnga ka vʋʋsd ne wẽnd dooga la Noora sãbsg ye.
44006014	D wʋma a noorẽ tɩ Nazarɛt Zezi wã na n wãa wẽnd do-kãnga la a teem a Moyiiz rog-n-mikã.»
44006015	Sẽn da be-b bʋʋda zĩigẽ fãa da geta a Etiyɛn laa ra wẽnda malɛka.
44007001	Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sokame: «Sẽn togsa yaa boto bɩ?»
44007002	T'a Etiyɛn leoke: «M ba rãmba, m saam-biisi, Wẽnd ninga sẽn tog ne pẽgrã lika d yaaba a Abraam, a sẽn da waa n ket Mezopotami. A ra nan ka ti a zak Arã tẽng ye.
44007003	La ad-b sẽn yeel-a: Bas f ba-yiri la f buuda neba la kẽng tẽng ning m sẽn na n wilg-fu.
44007004	A Abraam yii Kalde tẽnga n wa kẽ Arã. Yaa a ba wã kũum poore la Wẽnd yiis-a be n tɩ kẽes-a y sẽn be tẽng ninga marsã wã.
44007005	A pa reeg vẽenem tẽn-kãnga, ba sẽn zems nao-pʋg yalem. A paama Wẽnd kãabgo bala, tɩ yẽ n na n soog tẽngã, la yẽnda yagense, yẽnda loogr poore; la rẽ t'a rag n nan ka rog biig ye.
44007006	Yaa woto la Wẽnd gom yã: ‹A buuda na n paa tẽn-zẽngẽ, b na n kẽes-a-la yembdo la yʋʋm kobs naas tõre, a na n yãee toogo.
44007007	La Buud ninga sẽn na n kẽes-b yembdã, maam n na n kao a bʋʋdo, maam, Naaba-Wẽnde. Dẽn poore, m na n yiis-b la be n wa kẽes ka la ka la m na n waoog-ma.›
44007008	B waa n yõg zoodo. La zood kãng kaset la bãong kẽesgo. Yɩɩ woto la a Abraam kẽes a biig a Izaak bãongo, a rog tɩ rasem a nii. A Izaak me maana boto ne a Zakoob, t'a Zakoob maan boto ne a kamb piig la a yiibã.
44007009	Yaab rãmba maana sũ-kiir ne a Zozɛf n koos-a, tɩ b tall-a n loog Ezipt tẽnga. La Wẽnd da pʋgda a poore.
44007010	Beelẽ b yiis-a la a zu-loees fãa pʋgẽ n kõ-a bark la yam pidungu, Ezipt naaba zakẽ. Ezipt naaba kõ-a la kãsengo Ezipt tẽnga la a meng zakẽ.
44007011	Kom kãsenga la fare n yaool n wa lʋɩ Ezipt la Kanaã. Rɩɩb ra ka bee n dɩtẽ ye.
44007012	Yaab rãmb sẽn wʋm tɩ bũmb ket n tõe n paama Ezipt, a Zakoob tʋm-b-la be: dẽ yɩɩ pipi kẽnde.
44007013	B kẽnd a yiib soabã la a Zozɛf lik a menga a kẽem-dãmba la rẽ me la Ezipt naaba bãng a sẽn yitẽ.
44007014	A Zozɛf tʋmame tɩ b tɩ wa ne a ba, a Zakoob, la a ba wã zaka rãmba; b zãng ra yaa pisopoe la a nu.
44007015	A Zakoob tʋga Ezipt, n tol n tɩ pa be, yẽnda ne d yaab rãmbã.
44007016	B yĩnsã la b tall n wa Sikɛm, yaoog ning a Abraam sẽn daa a Emmor kamba nengẽ; a Emmor la a Sikɛm ba.
44007017	Wẽnd sẽn da wẽen ne b meng n kãab a Abraam bũmb ninga pidsg ra kolgdame. Buuda waa n fɩɩga zembal Ezipt tẽnga.
44007018	Dĩm paalg me n waa n dɩt Ezipt tẽng naam la yẽ ka bãng a Zozɛf ye.
44007019	Dĩm kãnga yãenda rabaar buud toor-toore n nams d yaab rãmba. Yẽ n tol n kɩt tɩ b fãsd kambã b ma nusẽ n basd-b tɩ b kiidẽ.
44007020	Wẽnd kãng la a Moyiiz wa moogo, la Wẽnd meng pẽga a neerma. Kiisa tã la a paa a ba zakẽ.
44007021	La b sẽn waa n kong n lob-a, yɩɩ Ezipt naaba bi-pugl n dɩk-a, n wub-a waa a meng biiga.
44007022	Yɩɩ woto la b wub a Moyiiz, n weka yama wa Ezipt biiga la a yɩɩ ned sẽn pid zãnga a goamẽ la a tʋʋmẽ.
44007023	A yʋʋm sẽn waa n digd pisnaase, a kõ-la a meng yam n na n gilg n ges a saam-biisã, Israyɛl kambã.
44007024	A sẽn yãend tɩ b namsd bãmb nin-yende, a kʋʋ Ezipt raoã sẽn da namsd-a wã.
44007025	A ra tẽedame t'a buuda rãmb na bãng tɩ yaa Wẽnd n tʋm-a t'a wa fãag-ba. B ka wʋm dẽ ye.
44007026	Woto wã beoog a to sẽn vẽege, a yãenda neb a yiib sẽn zabd taab t'a yet t'a na n paas-ba, n yeel-ba: ‹M zo-rãmba, yamb yaa saam-biisi, bõe tɩ y namsd taaba?›
44007027	Sẽn tara pãnga lebsa a Moyiiz kɛɛnga n yetẽ: ‹Ãnd yeel-f tɩ f soog-do la f kao d bʋʋdo?
44007028	Sãnd f ka rat n kʋ maam wala f sẽn kʋ Ezipt biiga zaamẽ wã?›
44007029	A Moyiiz kong n zoeeme n dig Madiã tẽnga. Bee, a roga kamb a yiibu.
44007030	Yʋʋm pisnaas dẽ poore, Sinayi tãnga zugu, we-raoogẽ, malɛk n lik-a kãgrẽ la yaa kãgr sẽn wit bugum.
44007031	A Moyiiz da ka tar yell kãnga võor ye. La a sẽn da kolgd n na n paam n yãend neere, la a sẽn wʋm Soaala koɛɛga:
44007032	‹Maam la f yaab rãmba Wẽnde, a Abraam, a Izaak la a Zakoob Wẽnde.› T'a Moyiiz yɛs n digda, n pa le saagd gesg ye.
44007033	Tɩ Soaala na n yeel-a: ‹Piid f neooda wã, tɩ f sẽn yɛs zĩig ninga yaa zĩ-sõngo.

44007035	Moyiiz ning b sẽn zãgs Ezipt tẽnga, b sẽn waa n sok-a: ‹Ãnda n yeel-f tɩ f yɩ d kãsma la d bʋ-kaooda?› Moyiiz kãng la Wẽnd kõ-ba, wala b naaba, b fãagda; la rẽ la malɛka lik kãgrẽ wã n togs-a.
44007036	Ya a Moyiiz n yiis-b Ezipt. La tũu ne bõn-bãna la yɛl-soalma a sẽn maan Ezipt tẽnga la Mog Miuugẽ; we-raoogẽ wã yɩɩ yʋʋm pisnaase.

44007038	B sẽn waa n ti b sika we-raoogẽ, yẽ n da be zĩis a yiibu: yẽ n da be Sinayi tãnga zugu n kelgd malɛka sẽn da gomd ne-a, yẽ n da be ne d ba rãmbã, b sikẽ. Yẽ n deeg Vɩɩma koees n taas-do.

44007040	tɩ b na n yeel a Aarõ: ‹Naan wẽnd dãmba n kõ-do tɩ d lʋɩɩs d taoore tɩ d ka mi yell ning sẽn paam a Moyiiz, rao ninga sẽn yiisa tõnd Ezipt tẽnga ye.›
44007041	B yika wẽnd kãnga n maan nag-bila; b kʋʋ maoong n waoog b bõn-naande, b maana sũ-noog kibsa, b nus sẽn yaga soaba yĩnga.
44007042	Wẽnd me zabame n bas-ba. B sẽn teeg b rãmb marsã lebga yĩngr ãdse, wala sẽn gʋls bãngdba sebr pʋgẽ: ‹Maanda buud toɛ-toɛ wã sʋka, maoong bʋg la y kʋʋ m yĩnga, yʋʋm pisnaas pʋgẽ, we-raoogẽ wã, Israyɛl kamba?
44007043	Y yaool n tii roog n kõ a Molok. Y yaga bõn-yood n togs y wẽn-faoogo, y wẽnd a Refa, ãdga; y yag-a lame n na n waoog-a; la rẽ me yĩng la m na n tall-y n kẽng yembd Babilon yaanga.›
44007044	We-raoogẽ, d yaab rãmba ra tii roogo tɩ zooda kaset bĩngd a pʋgẽ. Rooga ra tii wala Wẽnd sẽn da gom n wilg a Moyiiz, n yet t'a modg tɩ wẽneg a sẽn yãend a soabã.
44007045	La d yaab rãmba waa n baasa rooga ne a teedã n tall ba, a Zozuwe zamaanẽ, n tɩ kẽ tẽns niyns Wẽnd sẽn dig b soaalba tɩ b yii n bas vɩɩdã. Yɩɩ woto n tãag a Daviid.
44007046	Wẽnd yam sẽn da kẽe-a yĩnga, a Daviid kosa sore n na n me Roog a to a Zakoob Wẽnda yĩnga.
44007047	Yɩla a Salomo n me roogã.
44007048	D yaool n miime tɩ yĩngr Soaala ka kẽed doog neb nus sẽn me ye. Bãngd a ye n sɩd yeele:
44007049	‹Saaga la m naam zaoore. Tẽnga yaa m nao palgr zĩiga. Dẽn la Soaala sokda: ro bʋg la y na n me m yĩnga? Zĩ-bʋg n na n yɩ m vʋʋsg zĩiga?
44007050	Ka mam nug tʋʋmd la rẽ fãa laa?›
44007051	Yubl sẽn ka gõmsd dãmba, tʋb kɩd la sũ-rẽgd dãmba, wakat fãa y zãgsda a Vʋʋsem Sõngo! Y ba rãmba sẽn yɩ bũmb ninga, yãmb me boto!
44007052	Bãngd a bõe la y ba rãmba ka namse? B kʋʋ sẽn wilgb fãa tɩ Nin-sõnga na n waame. La ka yɩɩd dasma a wãna, Nin-sõnga yẽnẽ la y sẽn zãmbe n yõk n kʋ wã.
44007053	Noorã y sẽn paam ne malɛk rãmb wilgrã, y ka reeg-a ye.»
44007054	Neba sẽn wʋm woto b sũura fõda wʋsgo ne a Etiyɛn al tɩ b yẽna ra kẽrsdẽ.
44007055	A Etiyɛn sẽn da pid ne Vʋʋsem Sõngo dooga a neng yĩngri la Wẽnd lik-a la ne b ziiri, t'a Zezi yɛs yingri, b rɩtgo.
44007056	A yeelame: «Ad-y m nee saag sẽn pake tɩ Ned Biiga yɛs yĩngri Wẽnnaam dɩtgo.»
44007057	B kaasame, n yẽd b tʋba, la wala nin-yende, b kẽe a Etiyɛn.
44007058	B tus-a lame n yi tẽngã la b sɩnga a labr ne kuga. Kaset zirẽ dãmba da yeesa b futã n dɩgl bi-bɩɩg a ye naoẽ, a Sol naoẽ.
44007059	B sẽn waa n labd a Etiyɛn a ra pʋʋsda woto: «Soaala Zezi, reeg-y m sɩɩgã.»
44007060	A sẽn yigimdi a kelmame: «Soaala, da ning-y-b taal m kũuma yĩng ye.» La a sẽn gom woto a kiime.
44008001	Sã n ya a Sol, yẽ ra tagsdame t'a Etiyɛn kʋʋba zemsame. Baraar bala b yikame n na n sãam Zerizalɛɛm Tigengã sãoong wẽnga. Sã n ka Tʋʋm-tʋmdba bala, tẽedba fãa zoeeme n sẽeg Zɩɩde la Samari weto.
44008002	Nin-sõma n waa n dɩk a Etiyɛn n tɩ mum la b kelem a kʋʋre.
44008003	A Sol da tara Tigenga wãabo; a ra kẽeda zak woo zaka, n yiisd pagb la rapa n suiid doogo.
44008004	Tẽedba sẽn da sẽegã ra saada tẽng-tẽnga n moon Koe-noogã.
44008005	Woto a Filip sẽn da tɩ kẽ Samari tẽnga ra moonda Krista beelẽ.
44008006	Zãma wã ra pʋgda lame n deegd a zãmsgo. B fãa ra wʋmdame tɩ b gomd la b yãet ne b nini, yel-bãna a sẽn da maande.
44008007	Sʋtãan yooda ra yit n basda neb wʋsgo. B ra yitame la b kaasdẽ. Wobs la koms-rãmb wʋsg me paama laafi.
44008008	Tẽnga rãmb sũ-noog yɩɩ wʋsgo.
44008009	Ned n yaool n da reng a Filip beelẽ. Yaa a Simo. A ra maanda yel-bãna n yɩkd neb pɛlense. A ra geta a meng wa nin-kãsenga.
44008010	Dẽ me la neba fãa, bɛd la bõonego, ra pʋgd-a. B ra yetame: «Nin-kãnga pãnga yaa Wẽnd pãn-kẽoongo.»
44008011	B ra pʋgd-a lame tɩ yaa al daar zãr la a ra yɩkd b pɛlens ne a yel-bãna.
44008012	Neba sẽn waa n tẽ Wẽnd Rĩunga la a Zezi Krista Koe-noogã, a Filip sẽn waa n wilg-bã, b sakame tɩ b kõ-b soobo, pagb la rapa.
44008013	A Simo menga waa n tẽeme n deeg soobo, n da ka le rat n serg n bas a Filip ye t'a ra nee yel-bãna la wẽnd makr dãmba sẽn da maand a nifẽ.
44008014	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba sẽn da ket Zerizalɛɛm wʋmame tɩ Samari rãmb saka tẽebo tɩ b tʋm a Piyɛr la a Zã beelẽ.
44008015	B kẽe Samari rãmb tẽnga la b pʋʋsa b yĩnga, n kos a Vʋʋsem Sõng t'a sig bãmba,

44008017	A Piyɛr la a Zã ra tẽegda b nus b zutu tɩ b paamd a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.
44008018	A Simo sẽn yãende t'a Piyɛr la a Zã tẽegda b nus t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng sigda, a bao ligdi n kõ-ba.
44008019	A yeelame: «Kõ-y maam me y pãngã tɩ m nusa sẽn na n tẽeg ned ning fãa zugu bɩ a me reeg a Vʋʋsem sõngo.»
44008020	T'a Piyɛr na n yeel-a: «Wẽnd na sãam foo ne f ligdã, f sẽn tẽed tɩ Wẽnd kũun tõe n daa ne ligdã!
44008021	Wẽnd nifẽ, f sũura ka tɩrg ye la yõod kõn zĩnd f yĩnga, rũnna wala beoog ye.

44008023	F sũura pida ne tɩɩsem tɩ f yĩnga za ne wẽnem gadre.»

44008026	Soaala malɛk yeela a Filip: «Yik n tũ goabg sorã n yek sor ninga sẽn yit Zerizalɛɛm n dabd Gaza. Neb ka waoog so-kãng zug ye.»
44008027	A Filip yikame n tɩ yek sorã. La ade, Etiopi ned n da kẽng Zerizalɛɛm n lɛɛg n kuiisẽ. Da yaa Etiopi dĩm-poaka sõgen kãsenga, a kamb naaba la a laoga fãa gũuda.
44008028	A ra lɛɛg kuiisame, n zao bilim-bilm n karemd a Izayi sebre.

44008040	Yaa Azot tẽng la b le wa yãend a Filip. A ra kẽnda a kẽnde n moon Koe-noogã a sẽn ta tẽng ning fãa, n wa tãag Sezare.
44009001	A Sol yẽ sẽn da mi, yaa kẽes tẽedba rabeem la a kʋ-b bala. Dẽ la a tɩ yãend maan-kʋʋd kãsengã

44009003	A sɩd dɩka sore n kolgd Damas; la vugr bala vẽenem tãoo yĩngr n bu-a.

44009009	Maana rasem a tãabo t'a ka ne fɩ, n ka rɩtẽ la a ka yũud fɩ.
44009010	Karen-biig a ye n da be Damas n boond t'a Anani. Soaala waa n lika b meng yẽnda n yeel-a: «Anani!» Tɩ yẽ sake: «Soaala, m bee ka.» Tɩ Soaala lɛɛg n yeel-a:
44009011	«Kẽnge, rɩk sor ning sẽn pʋd tɩ Tɩrgã, n sok a Zɩɩda zaka. Beelẽ f na sok Tars rao a Sol yelle. Nin-kãng pʋʋsdame marsã,
44009012	la nin-kãng nee ned sẽn boond tɩ Anani. A nee a Anani sẽn kẽed n na n tẽeg a nus a zug t'a nina le puki.»
44009013	A Anani leokame: «Soaala, m wʋma neb ka tɛk sẽn gom nin-kãnga yelle. Neba fãa togsda wẽng ning a sẽn maan ne Zerizalɛɛm tẽedbã.
44009014	A sẽn wa kaalẽ wã menga, a waa ne Maan-kʋʋd kãsensa noore n na n sog bãeense neb niyns fãa sẽn pʋt y yʋʋre.»
44009015	Soaala me yeel-a lame: «Kẽng m sẽn tʋm-f zĩig ningã tɩ nedã, maam n yãk-a ne yamleoogo, t'a moon m yʋʋra bu-zẽmbã, dĩm dãmba la a Israyɛl buudu.
44009016	Mam meng m toore n na n wilg-a a sẽn na n nams bũmb ning fãa, mam yʋʋra yĩnga.»
44009017	A Anani sak n loogame, a kẽe zakẽ, a tẽega a nus a Sol zug n yeel-a: «Sol, Sol, m saam-biiga, sẽn tʋm-a maama, yaa nin kãng n lik foo f sora zugu la a tʋm-m lame tɩ m wa puk f nini la f reeg a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.»
44009018	Zĩig pʋgẽ bala yɩɩ wa pagdo n yi a nina n dʋʋg tẽnga. A nina wẽneg n pukame la a reega soobo.
44009019	A sẽn paam dɩɩbo, a rɩɩme n le paam pãnga. A Sol maana dasem a wãn ne Damas karen-biisã.
44009020	A sɩngame n wilgd pʋʋsg rotẽ t'a Zezi yaa Wẽnnaam Biiga.
44009021	Sẽn da kelgdba fãa ra yɛsa ne pɛlen-yɩka la b maanẽ: «Ka rao kãnga n da yik Zerizalɛɛm n maan beem ne sẽn da pʋt-b Nin-kãnga Yʋʋra laa? La a sẽn wa ka wã, a ka wa bal n na n yõg-b n tɩ kɩs maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb wɛɛ?»
44009022	Ad a Sol da paamda pãnga beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa n gomd n lubd Damas Zʋɩf rãmbã, n wilgd-b vẽenega t'a Zezi sɩd yaa Krista.
44009023	Yʋʋm sẽn maan a wãna, Zʋɩf rãmba seda ne taaba n na n kʋ a Sol.
44009024	A Sol bãngame tɩ bũmb la b rat n maane, tɩ b ra tol n ninga gũudba tẽnga noor kʋɩlensẽ, tɩ b be be wĩndg la yʋngo, sẽn na yɩlẽ n paam-a n kʋ.
44009025	Woto wã, yʋng a ye, karen-biisa seda ne taaba n sagl-a peoog pʋga n sik-a lalg poore.
44009026	A Sol sẽn ta Zerizalɛɛm, a makame n na n fãoog a meng ne karen-biis a taabã la b fãa ra zoeta rabeem; b ra pa tẽed t'a sɩd kẽe Krista ye.
44009027	A Barnabe n kong n peeg-a, n tall-a n ta Tʋʋm-tʋmdba nengẽ la a wilg-b bũmb ning sẽn maan Damas sor zugu: a yãenda Soaala la Soaala goma ne-a. A wilg-b-la a Sol sẽn moon, ne sũ-keelem ninga a Zezi Krista yʋʋr Damas tẽnga.
44009028	Dẽ marsã la b ra tũud taab n yit la b watẽ, Zerizalɛɛm pʋgẽ, la b kõt Soaala kaseto tɩ rabeem kaẽ ye.
44009029	A Sol da sõsda ne Zʋɩf niyns sẽn gomd-b grɛkã, tɩ b wẽed no-koɛɛm ne taaba. La b fãa ra soos n baooda a kũum.
44009030	Karen-biisa sẽn bãng rẽ b tall-a lame m leb Sezare, n wa tɩ yi be n dig Tars tẽnga.
44009031	Sã n ya Zɩɩde, Galile la Samari, bãmb da tara laafi. Tigenga ra kɩɩda yẽgna. B ra zoeta Wẽnde. A Vʋʋsem Sõng sõngr yĩnga, b ra pida ne sũ-noogo.
44009032	A Piyɛr da kẽeda tẽnsa fãa; a waa n taa nin-sõma wã nengẽ Lida.
44009033	A yãenda ned be sẽn boond tɩ Ene, la yaa yʋʋm a nii la a gãe a gãag zugu: a ra lebga põore.
44009034	A Piyɛr yeel-a lame: «Ene, a Zezi Krista n kõt-f laafi. Yik la f maneg f gãaga f toore.» A wẽneg n yikame.
44009035	Lida neba fãa la sẽn be-b Saron bãooga, yãend-a lame la b tẽe Soaala.
44009036	Zope karen-biisa sʋka pag a ye n da boond tɩ Tabita, tɩ Grɛk rãmb boond tɩ Dorkas (Yãka). A sẽn da sẽbg kall ningã yaa maan tʋʋm sõma la a yols naong rãmb nimbãanega.
44009037	A waa n lʋɩɩ pakeem n wẽneg n maan kaalem. B sẽn so-a koom b rʋʋ yĩngr doogã n gãneg-a.
44009038	Lida ne Zope tẽns ra ka zãr taab ye, woto b sẽn bãng t'a Piyɛr bee Zope, karen-biisa tʋma neb a yiibu sẽn tɩ yeel-a: «Wa d nengẽ la ra kaoos ye.»
44009039	A Piyɛr yik n tũ-b lame n loog. A sẽn ta, a dʋʋ yĩngri doogã. Pʋg-kõapa sẽn da tigim be wã gũbg-a lame n wilgd-a fut buud toor toore a Dorkas sẽn da wʋgda, a sẽn da waa n ket b sʋka.
44009040	A Piyɛr kɩtame tɩ b fãa yi la a yĩgimdame n pʋʋse. A waa n wẽnemd n gesa pagã n yeel-a: «Tabita, yiki!» A puka a nini, n yãend a Piyɛr, n yik n zĩndi.
44009041	A Piyɛr gãda a nug n yik-a yĩngri. Yaa nin-vɩɩga la a Piyɛr bool nin-sõma wã la pʋg-kõapã n wilgi.
44009042	Zope tõr wʋma kibarã, tɩ wʋsg na n kẽ Soaalã.
44009043	A Piyɛr kaoosa bilf Zope, zapa a ye yiri, zapa yʋʋr la a Simo.
44010001	Ned n da be Sezare n boond tɩ Kornɛy. A ra yaa tãb-biis koabg taoor soaba, la Kornɛy tãnsoben-dooga neb da yita Itali.
44010002	Yaa ned sẽn da mi Wẽnd waoogre: ne a sẽn ya bu-zẽna, yẽ ne a zak rãmb fãa da gãda Zʋɩf rãmba tẽebo. A ra kõta Zʋɩf rãmba kũun bɛda. A ra ka vʋsd ne pʋʋsg ye.
44010003	A waa n paama likri. Daar a ye, zafare, a yãenda ne a nif menga, Wẽnd malɛk sẽn kẽ a zakẽ n bool-a: «Kornɛy!»
44010004	A sẽn ges-a, a yɛɛsame. A sokame: «Yaa bõe, Soaala?» Malɛka leokame: «Ad-f pʋʋsgã la f wẽn-kosgã yel-sõmda yɛsa Wẽnd taoore, tɩ Wẽnd tẽr f yelle.
44010005	Dɩlla marsã bala tʋm neb Zope tɩ b tɩ wa ne a Simo, b sẽn boonda soab t'a Piyɛr.
44010006	A yõga zap a ye gãag-sobendo. Zapa me yʋʋr yaa Simo la a yira bee mogra noore.»
44010007	Malɛk ning sẽn da gomda wã sẽn looge, la a Kornɛy sẽn bool a rakõap a yiibu n paas tãb-biig a ye sẽn kẽ Wẽnde la a sẽn da yãk n gũnug a menga.
44010008	A sẽn wilg-ba b sẽn da tog n bãnge, a tʋm-b la Zope.
44010009	Vẽkembeoogo b taame. Zemsa wĩnto-suka, zemsa a Piyɛr sẽn dʋ rooga zug n na n pʋʋse.
44010010	Kom waa n yõk-a lame t'a rat bũmb n ning a noorẽ. B sẽn waa n segend dɩɩbã, a yama fʋsga a yĩngã.
44010011	A yãenda saaga sẽn pake tɩ peen kãseng sẽn loe a noy a naas sigd tẽng wa zãnega.
44010012	Zãnega ra pida ne rũms sẽn tar nao a naase la bõn-vuudi la yĩngr luiili.
44010013	La koɛɛg n wẽneg n yeel-a: «Aya! Piyɛr, kʋ n wãbe.»
44010014	T'a Piyɛr yeele: «Ayo! Soaala, bũmb sẽn ya rẽgdo, t'a sɩɩsg meng kisa, zɩɩ n kẽ m noorẽ ye.»
44010015	Koɛɛga le yeel-a lame, naoor a yiib soaba: «Wẽnd sẽn yɩlg bũmb ningã bɩ f ra saag n bool tɩ rẽgd ye.»
44010016	Yella maana woto naoor a tãabo. Dẽ poore, fãa leba a zĩigẽ, yĩngri.
44010017	A Piyɛr ra ket n yɛsa ne yɩɩre la a sokd a menga a sẽn yãenda võore. Wakat kãng la a Kornɛy sẽn tʋm b rãmba poog dignoorẽ.
44010018	B reng n sokame n bãng a Simo zaka, n bãng rao ning sẽn boond t'a Piyɛr sã n sɩd siga be.
44010019	Dẽ t'a Piyɛr ra ket n baooda likra võore la a Vʋʋsem Sõng yeel-a lame: «Ad neb n baood-fo.
44010020	Yiki, sig n tũ-ba n looge tao-tao tɩ yaa maam n tʋm-ba.»
44010021	A Piyɛr sigame n sok nebã: «Bõe n wa ne y ka?»
44010022	Tɩ b na n leok: «Yaa Tãnsoab a Kornɛy, yaa nin-sõng sẽn sak Wẽnd tẽebo tɩ Zʋɩf rãmba pẽgd-a, yaa yẽ n paam tɩ malɛk sõng wilg-a t'a bool-f tɩ f waa a nengẽ la a kelg koees niyns f sẽn na n kõ-a.»
44010023	T'a Piyɛr na n bas-b tɩ b kẽ la a maan-b gãag-sobendo. Beoog sẽn vẽege, b naaga taab n dɩk sore; Zope saam-biis kẽer yãag-b lame.
44010024	Da-yɩten-daar la a ta Sezare. A Kornɛy ra tigsa a buudu la a zo-rãmba n gũud-a.
44010025	A Piyɛr sẽn kolg zaka noor la a Kornɛy sẽn yi n seg-a n wõgemd a taoore.
44010026	A Piyɛr doog-a lame n yetẽ: «Yik tɩ mam me yaa ned wa foom.»
44010027	B sɩnga sõasg la b kẽedẽ. Yaa zãma n da tigim zaka pʋga.
44010028	A Piyɛr yeel-b lame: «Wala y sẽn mi wã, maan zood ne bu-zẽn la f kẽe a zakẽ, yaa kisgu ne Zʋɩf. La ade, Wẽnd Wilg-m-la sẽn ka yɩɩd rasem a wãn bala tɩ m ka tog n bool ninsaal ba a ye tɩ rẽgdo, bɩ n yeel t'a sɩɩsg kisame ye.
44010029	Yaa rẽnd me yĩnga la y sẽn bool-ma m pa yaas n tadg ye. M kot-y lame tɩ y togs-ma: yaa bõe yĩng la y bool-ma?»
44010030	A Kornɛy leokame: «Yaa rasem a tãab rũnna la m da be m zakẽ n pʋʋsd zafar pʋʋsgo la ned n waa n yals m taoore ne fut peelem sẽn tʋʋsd nini.
44010031	Raoã yeel-m lame: ‹Kornɛy, f pʋʋsga reegame, Wẽnd tẽega f wẽn-kosga yel-sõmde.
44010032	Tʋm neb Zope tɩ b wa ne a Simo sẽn boond tɩ Piyɛr. A bee zap a Simo zakẽ, zak sẽn be mogra noore.›
44010033	M wẽneg n kɩtame tɩ b babs-fo, la f sẽn wa wã f maana neere. Ad-d fãa sẽn yɛs f taoore n dat n wʋm Wẽnd sẽn kõ-f noor ningã.»
44010034	A Piyɛr yeelame: «M neeme tɩ Wẽnd ka welg ninsaal ne a to ye.
44010035	Fo buuda sẽn yaa soaba, f sã n zoet Wẽnde la f maand sẽn zemse, b pʋgda f poore.
44010036	Yaa Israyɛl kamba la b gom ne, n gom laafi ning Dũni zãng Soaala, a Zezi Krista, sẽn wa ne a soabã.
44010037	Y tẽra bũmb ning sẽn maan Zɩɩde ween-vɩʋʋgẽ. Y tẽra Nazarɛt Zezi wã yelle. Y tẽra b sɩngr Galile, a Zã sooba poore.
44010038	Y tẽra Wẽnd sẽn pids-b ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo la b pãnga. Y tẽra me tɩ Wẽnd sẽn da be ne-bã, b sẽn pɩʋʋg zĩig ning fãa b maana neere la b sãooga Sʋtãan sẽn da kẽ b rãmb fãa.
44010039	Sã n ya tõndo, d yɩɩ b vɩɩma kaset dãmba, Zʋɩf rãmb tẽngẽ la Zerizalɛɛm. Yaa bãmb la b saag n ka pika zugu n kʋ.
44010040	La Wẽnd vʋʋg-b la rasem a tãab daare tɩ b na lik b menga.
44010041	Ka neba fãa la b lik b meng ye, yɩɩ Wẽnd sẽn beool n yãk b rãmba. Yɩɩ tõnd sẽn dɩ la d yũ ne bãmba, b vʋʋgra poore.
44010042	Bãmb n kõ tõnd noor tɩ d moon la d wilg tɩ bãmb la Wẽnd yals yã tɩ b na n kao sẽn vɩ-ba la sẽn ki-ba bʋʋdo.
44010043	Yaa bãmb yelle la bãngdba fãa gomda n yet tɩ sẽn tẽed-a bãmb fãa na paam a yel-wẽna yẽesgo bãmb yʋʋr yĩnga.»
44010044	A Piyɛr ra ket n gomdame la a Vʋʋsem Sõng siga sẽn da kelgd-ba fãa.
44010045	Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn da tũ a Piyɛr n wa wã yɛɛsame tɩ b yãendame t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng me siga bu-zẽmbã.
44010046	B ra wʋmdame tɩ b wɩlemd bu-zẽn goama n pẽgd Wẽnnaam. Dẽ la a Piyɛr yeel yã:
44010047	«D tõeeme n mong soobo, neb sẽn paam a Vʋʋsem Sõng wala tõnd bɩ?»
44010048	La a kõo noor tɩ b so-ba, a Zezi Krista yʋʋr yĩnga. B kosa a Piyɛr t'a pa ne-ba dasem a wãn yɛsa.
44011001	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba ne Zerizalɛɛm saam-biisa waa n wʋmame tɩ bu-zẽmba me reega Wẽnd gomde.
44011002	Woto a Piyɛr sẽn ta Zerizalɛɛm, Zʋɩf rãmba yika ne-a:
44011003	«Bõe yĩng la f saag n kẽ bu-zẽmb zagsẽ la f zĩnd n dɩ ne-ba?»
44011004	T'a Piyɛr na n dɩk yella nao n wilg-ba:
44011005	«Ad-y m da bee Zope n pʋʋsdẽ, tɩ m yama wa fʋsg m yĩngã; m paama likri. Bũmb n da yit yĩngri sigd m taoore: peen kãseng sẽn loe wa zãnega.
44011006	M nina yõka gesgo n ka kamsdẽ ye la m yãenda tẽng zug rũms sẽn tar nao a naase, we-rũmsi, bõn-vuudi la yĩngr luiili.
44011007	La m wẽneg n wʋma koɛɛga: ‹Aya! Piyɛr, kʋ n wãbe.›
44011008	La m leokame: ‹Ayo! Soaala, bõn dẽgd la bũmb sɩɩsg sẽn kis zɩɩ n kẽ m noorẽ ye.›
44011009	Koɛɛga zĩnda yĩngri n le yeel-ma: ‹Da saag n ges wa rẽgdo Wẽnd sẽn yɩlg ye.›
44011010	Bũmba maana woto naoor a tãabo n yaool n wa leb yĩngri.
44011011	Zemsa neb a tãab sẽn wa. B waa n yalsa tõnd sẽn da beẽ la Sezare ned n da tʋm-ba.
44011012	A Vʋʋsem Sõng wilg-m lame tɩ m da maan sãmbg ye la m tũ-ba. M saam-biis a yoobã sẽn zĩ wã me tũu maam la d kẽe zapa yiri.
44011013	Yẽ me togsa tõndo malɛka sẽn lik-a n yeel-a: ‹Tʋm Zope tɩ b wa ne a Simo, b sẽn boonda soab t'a Piyɛr.
44011014	Yẽnda n na n kõ foo koɛɛg sẽn na n fãag foo ne f zakã.›
44011015	M sẽn sɩng bal tɩ m na n gome la a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn sig bãmba, wala b sẽn sig tõnd sɩngrẽ wã.
44011016	Wakat kãng la m tẽeg Soaala gomde: A Zã kõo soob ne koom, la sã n ya yãmba y na n soo ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.
44011017	Wẽnd sã n kõ bãmb wala b sẽn kõ tõnd sẽn tẽ Soaal a Zezi Krista, maam la a bõe n na n gɩdg Wẽnde.»
44011018	Gom kãensa maaga b sũuri la b pẽga Wẽnd n yetẽ: «Wẽnd kõo bu-zẽmba me tuubg ning sẽn wat ne vɩɩma.»
44011019	Neb niyns sẽn da sẽeg-b, a Etiyɛn namsga wakato, sãag n taa Fenisi, Sɩpr la Antiyos; la yaa Zʋɩf rãmba bal la ra moond Koe-noogã.
44011020	Sɩpr la Sirɛn tẽng rãmb n yaool n zĩnd bãmb sʋka. B sẽn ta Antiyos b sak n goma ne bu-zẽmbã n moon Soaal a Zezi Krista Koe-noogã.
44011021	Wẽnd da pʋgda b poor ne b pãnga. Woto sẽn sak-b tẽeb n lebg Soaala karen-biis yɩɩ ka tɛka.
44011022	Rẽ lʋɩɩ Zerizalɛɛm dãmba tʋbrẽ tɩ b tʋm a Barnabe Antiyos.
44011023	Yẽ me waame; a yãenda Wẽnd kũuna sẽn yɩ a soaba; a sũur yɩɩ noogo la a sẽn mi saglg yĩnga a kõ-b-la pãnga tɩ b da le bak ne Soaala ye.
44011024	A Barnabe ra yaa nin-sõngo n pid ne tẽebo la ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo. Sɩd yɩɩ neb ka tɛk n wa n kẽ Soaalã.
44011025	A Barnabe babsa a Sol Tars tẽnga.
44011026	A sẽn yãend-a, a peeg-a lame n wa Antiyos. B paa ne taab yʋʋmd tõre ne Antiyos Tigenga rãmba. Yɩɩ neb ka tɛk yam la b vẽneg yã. Yɩɩ Antiyos la b sɩng n boond karen-biisa tɩ «kristneba».
44011027	Bãngdba n waa n yi Zerizalɛɛm n wa Antiyos.
44011028	B nin-yend sẽn boond tɩ Agabus yika ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng vẽnegre n moon tɩ kom kãsenga n na n lʋɩ tẽnga tõre. Kom kãng la sẽn zĩnd a Klod zamaanẽ.
44011029	Karen-biisa yalsame tɩ ned kam fãa na n maana a sẽn tõe n tool sõngre Zɩɩde saam-biisã.
44011030	B sakame n tool nin-kẽemsa bũmbu la a Barnabe ne a Sol n na n tall-a n taas.
44012001	Yaa rẽ sasa la a Erod yõg Tigenga neb kẽere n namse.
44012002	A kɩtame tɩ b kʋ ne sʋʋga a Zã kẽema, a Zak.
44012003	Rẽ taa Zʋɩf rãmba yam t'a na n kɩt tɩ b yõk a Piyɛr me. Sega bur sẽn pa lobd bɩlle wakato,
44012004	t'a na n kong n sui-a roogo n gũud Paka poore n na kẽes-a bʋʋdo, buuda gill taoore.
44012005	A Piyɛr sẽn kẽ roogo la Tigenga me sẽn yõk pʋʋsg a yĩnga n ka vʋʋsdẽ ye.
44012006	Ra zoe n lebga yʋngo, ra keta beooga vẽeg tɩ b kẽes a Piyɛr bʋʋdo. A ra paam n gõee tãb-biis a yiib sʋka la bãng n da sog-a ne tãb-biig fãa. B ra ninga gũudb me rooga noore.
44012007	Soaala malɛk siga vugr bala tɩ bi-beesa roog na n yãng ne vẽenem. Malɛka tika a Piyɛr lʋgre t'a yiki. A yeel-a lame: «Yik yĩngr tao!» Bãeensa foosa a nusẽ n dʋʋg tẽnga.
44012008	Malɛka yeelame: «Sẽbg f sẽbdga la ning f gãndalsa.» T'a Piyɛr maan boto. Malɛka le paasame: «Rɩk f fu taokã n palg f bãoko la f pʋg maam.»
44012009	A Piyɛr yiime n pʋgd-a. A ka mi tɩ yella yaa sɩd ye. A bas n tẽedame t'a zãmsdame.
44012010	B yõsga pipi gũudba zĩiga, n le yõsg a yiib soaba, n wa ta tẽnga noor kut kʋɩlenga sẽn paka toore tɩ bãmb looge. B kẽname n tɩ yek sor a to la malɛka wẽneg n bas-a lame.
44012011	Dẽ marsã la a yama leb a zĩigẽ t'a yeele: «Marsã la m ne vẽenega tɩ Soaala tʋma b malɛk t'a wa fãag-ma a Erod nusẽ la a fãag-m ne Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn da gũud bũmb ningã.»
44012012	A Piyɛr bãnga a sẽn be zĩig ninga t'a na n tees a Mari zaka. Pʋg kãng ya a Zã ma la a Zã me le boondame tɩ Mark. Neb wʋsgo n da tigim zakã, n da pʋʋsdẽ.
44012013	A Piyɛr sẽn vẽ kʋɩlengã la zak bi-pugl a ye, sẽn boond tɩ Rodɛ, waa n na n ges sẽn yaa soaba,
44012014	n wʋm a Piyɛr koɛɛg, n kɩdem sũ-noogo n yĩm kʋɩlenga pakre, n wudg n leb pʋgẽ n na n wilg tɩ ya a Piyɛr n be dignoorẽ.
44012015	Pʋgẽ dãmba yeel-a lame: «Ad-f zuga lebgame.» La yẽ ra wẽendame tɩ yaa sɩda. Tɩ b le paase: «Ad yaa Malɛka!»
44012016	A Piyɛr ra ket n tara kʋɩlenga kogsgo. B sẽn waa n pake b sɩd mikame tɩ yaa yẽnna tɩ rabeem na n kẽ-ba.
44012017	A Piyɛr kams-b la ne nug tɩ b bas bʋʋre; a wilg-b la Soaala sẽn yiis-a rooga toto la a paasame: «Tɩ wilg yã a Zak la saam-biisã.» A sẽn yi, a kẽnga zĩig a to.
44012018	Zĩig sẽn yẽege, tãb-biisa nengẽ wulumdame: a Piyɛr kẽe yɛ? A kẽe yɛ?
44012019	A Erod sẽn tʋm tɩ b wa ne-a, b pa yãend-a ye. A kɩtame tɩ b sogs gũudbã, a kɩtame tɩ b kʋ ba. A Erod yii Zɩɩde n leb Sezare la a paa be.
44012020	A Erod ne Tir la Sidõ rãmba ra ka zemsd taab ba bilfu. B waa n tɩ yõka sõgen kãseng, a Blastus, sɛɛga t'a tall-ba n taas dĩma taoore tɩ b yẽs laafi yẽsgo. B tẽnsa sõngr da yita dĩma nẽngẽ.
44012021	Daara sẽn ta, a Erod yeelga a naam futu. A rʋʋ bũmb sẽn zẽke n yɛs n gomda.
44012022	Zãma wã sɩnga kaasgo: «Ad-y ka ninsaal n gomd ye, yaa wẽnde!»
44012023	Zĩig pʋgẽ bala, Soaala malɛk wẽe-a lame t'a ka gom n pẽg Wẽnd ye. Zãnzũy n wẽneg m kẽe a nemsã t'a ki.
44012024	Wẽnd gomda ra paamda moonego tɩ tẽedba me sõor tar paasgo.
44012025	A Barnabe ne a Sol pidsa b tʋʋmna Zerizalɛɛm. B lɛɛg n waa Antiyos ne a Zã, b sẽn boonda soab me tɩ Mark.
44013001	Bãngdba la karen-saam-dãmba n da be Antiyos Tigenga pʋga. Ad-a Barnabe, a Simeõ, sẽn boond tɩ Sablga, ad Sirɛn Lusiyus, ad-a Manaɛn, kombera, a Erod, deem-n-taaga n paas a Sol.
44013002	Daar a ye b waa n naaga taab n pʋʋsdẽ la b loet b noore t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng yeele: «Welg yã a Barnabe ne a Sol toore tɩ tʋʋmd la m na n kõ-ba.»
44013003	Pʋʋsga la no-loeera sẽn sɛ b tẽega b nus b zutu tɩ b yik n loog b tʋʋmde.
44013004	B sɩnga tʋʋmd ning b sẽn deeg a Vʋʋsem Sõng nengẽ. Dɩlla b yii Zerizalɛɛm n tees Selewusi, n yi be n kẽ koom koglg n dig Sɩpr.
44013005	B taa Salamin n sɩng Koe-nooga moonego Zʋɩf rãmb pʋʋsg rotẽ. A Zã n da pʋgd n sõngd-ba.
44013006	B saaga Sɩpr n ta Pafos, la be b sega yel-bãn soaba, Zʋɩf sẽn ya zirẽ-be-bãngda, n boond tɩ Bar Zezi.
44013007	A ra yaa sõsd-n-taar ne Komber a Serziyus Pawulus, ned sẽn pid ne sɩlem. Kombera kɩtame tɩ b bool a Barnabe ne a Sol t'a da rat n wʋma Soaala Koɛɛg.
44013008	Yel-bãn soab, a Elimas, da ningda gɩdgre, t'a ra pa rat kombera ne tẽeb ye.
44013009	Rẽ marsã la a Sol – b boond-a lame yɛs t'a Pol – yik ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng pãnga n gẽen-a,
44013010	n yeel-a: «Nin-yoog sẽn pid ne zãmb la wẽnem buud fãa, Sʋtãan biiga, zemsg buud fãa bɛyã, wakat bʋg la f na vʋʋs ne Wẽnd so-tɩrsa kedbgo?
44013011	Soaala na n zɩsga b nug f zug marsã. F na n lebga zoanga, la rasem a wãn pʋgẽ f kõn le yãend wĩntoog vẽenem ye.» La zĩig pʋgẽ bala fãa lebga yʋng la lik a yĩnga t'a ra wẽnesed goabg la rɩtgo n baood tata.
44013012	Kombera sẽn yãe woto, a saka tẽebo la sɩda Soaala Zãmsga yɩka a pɛlenga.
44013013	Pafos tẽnga, a Pol ne a tũud-n-taasa le kẽe koom koglg n ta Perze sẽn be Pãnfili tẽn-peelmẽ. Zĩ kãng la a Zã bas-ba n leb Zerizalɛɛm.
44013014	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba yẽ kell n sãaga Perze n ta Antiyos a to sẽn be Pisidi. Vʋʋsga raare b kẽe pʋʋsga roogo n zĩndi.
44013015	Noora la bãngdba sebr kareng poore, pʋʋsga roog nanams tʋmame tɩ b yeel-ba: «Saam-biisi, y sã n tar Koɛɛg n na n kõ zãma wã n le paas a raoodo bɩ y leoke.»
44013016	A Pol yikame n kabs ne a nug la a yeelame: «Israyɛl kamba la yãmb fãa sẽn pʋgd Wẽnde, m kotame tɩ y kelg-ma.
44013017	Tõnd sẽn be buud ninga tẽngẽ wã Wẽnde, a Israyɛl Wẽnd, n tũus d yaab rãmbã la bãmb n kɩt t'a neba sõor fɩɩg zembala Ezipt tẽnga, b pa-weer tẽnga. Bãmb n yiis-b tẽn kãng ne b kang pãnga.
44013018	Bãmb n zã-b yʋʋm pisnaas we-raoogẽ.
44013019	Bãmb n sɛɛs buud a yopoe Kanaã, n deeg b soolma n kõ-ba.
44013020	Bãmb meng b toore n ges b yell yʋʋm kobs-naase la pisnu. Dẽ poore b kõ-b la Bʋ-kaoodba n tãag bãngd a Samwɛl.
44013021	Ba rãmba waa n yikame n kos dĩma, tɩ Wẽnd na n kõ-b a Sis biig, a Sol, a Bẽzame buudẽ, la a soog-b la yʋʋm pisnaase.
44013022	Wẽnd waa n lebsa yẽ kɛɛnga n kõ-b dĩm a Daviid; la ad-b sẽn yeel a Daviid poorẽ: ‹M yãenda a Zese biig a Daviid tɩ m yam kẽe-a. Yẽnda n na n pids m daaba fãa.›
44013023	Ya yẽnda buudẽ la Wẽnd pids b kãabgã n yiis a Zezi wala a Israyɛl Fãagda.
44013024	A Zã n lʋɩ taoore n segl b waoongo, n wilg a Israyɛl buud tɩ soob n be n ya sũur tekr soobo.
44013025	A Zã sẽn waa n na n looge, a ra yetame: ‹Yãmb sẽn tẽed tɩ m yaa ned ningã, ad-y ka maam la yẽ soab ye. B na n waa mam poorẽ la m ka tog n yɩ b sõgen meng ye.›
44013026	M saam-biisi, a Abraam yagense, la yãmb fãa sẽn be ka la y pʋgda Wẽnde, yaa yãmb fãa yĩng la Fãagr Koɛɛga moon yã.
44013027	Zerizalɛɛm taoor dãmba pidsa ne yĩdgu, bãngr koees niyns d sẽn karemd sibr daar fãa.
44013028	Ne b sẽn pa yãend b nengẽ bũmb sẽn sek b bʋʋd paalgre, b baas n kosa a Pilat t'a kʋ-ba.
44013029	B sẽn taas bũmb ning fãa sẽn gʋls b poorẽ, b sika b yĩnga n mum yaoogẽ.
44013030	Wẽnd vʋʋg-b lame.
44013031	La rasem sõor sẽn ka paood pʋgẽ b lika neb niyns sẽn yi-b ne bãmb Galile n wa Zerizalɛɛm la nin-bãmb la buuda fãa kaset rãmb marsã.
44013032	Tõnd kõt-y-la Koe-noogo. Tõnd yet-y lame tɩ Wẽnd sẽn kãab bũmb ning d yaab rãmbã,
44013033	b pids-a-la tõnd ned kamb fãa yĩnga, n vʋʋg a Zezi. B kãab-b-la tõnd woto Yɩɩla sebrẽ: Fo yaa mam biiga, rũnda la m dog foo.
44013034	D sẽn gãd bũmb ning n mi tɩ Wẽnd vʋʋg-b la kɩɩms sʋka, tɩ b na n tɩlg põogre, yaa b sẽn da yeelã: m na n pidsa kãab-sõma niyns m sẽn da kãab a Daviid wala bũmb sẽn ka tõe n vaale.
44013035	Yaa rẽ me yĩng la b le yet zĩig a to: F kõn bas f nin-sõngã t'a bãng põogr ye.
44013036	D miime t'a sẽn baas tʋʋmd ning Wẽnd sẽn wilg-a, a Daviid kiime tɩ b mum-a la a bãnga põogre.
44013037	Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋg a soaba yẽ tɩlga põogre.
44013038	Dɩlla, m saam-biisi, bãng-y tɩ yaa yẽ soab yʋʋr yĩnga la b moond yel-wẽn yẽesgo. Sõmblem ning a Moyiiz Noora sẽn ka tõog n kõ yãmb a soabã,
44013039	ned ning fãa sẽn tẽeda bãmb paamd-a lame.
44013040	Gũus-y tɩ bãngdba sẽn yeela ra wa taas ye:
44013041	‹Gesyã, ka mi to pẽgr dãmba. Yɛɛs-y n menem! Bũmb la m na n maan yãmb sʋka m na n maan-a lame ti y ket n vɩ, la ned sã n da yiẽ kɛɛnga n wa togs yã, y kõn deegẽ ye.› »
44013042	Pʋʋsga sẽn sɛ, b kosa a Pol la a Barnabe tɩ b le wa rɩk b rũnna koɛɛgã sibr ning sẽn pʋgdã.
44013043	Tigsga sɩnga sẽegre la Zʋɩf rãmb wʋsgo ne Kẽed paalse tũ-la a Pol ne a Barnabe. Bãmb me ra sõsda ne-ba n kot-b tɩ b ra bas tɩ Wẽnd kũuna lʋɩ vɩʋʋgẽ ye.
44013044	Vʋʋsg raar ninga sẽn pʋgã, yɩɩ tẽnga zãng la bala n waa n na n kelg Wẽnd Gomdã.
44013045	Zʋɩf rãmba me sẽn yãend rẽnna b yika sũ-kiiri n leood a Pol la b naagd ne wẽn-tʋʋre.
44013046	Dẽ me la a Pol ne a Barnabe keng b sũuri n yeel-ba: «Yaa yãmb la d da togẽ pipi n moon Koe-noogã. La yãmb sẽn pa sakã, la y pa kẽes y mens vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ kamba sʋka, ade, tõnd na n wẽnemda d neng n tees bu-zẽmbã.
44013047	No-kãng me la d paam Wẽnd nengẽ: ‹M yals-f la wa bu-zẽmba vẽenem, m yeel-f lame tɩ f taas fãagra Koe-noog dũni wã sɛtmẽ.› »
44013048	Bu-zẽmba sẽn wʋm dẽ, b sũur yɩɩ noogo tɩ b na n pẽg Koe-noogã. Sẽn paam-b Wẽnd zelemd noogã, vɩɩm sẽn ka be sɛɛb kãabgã, faa saka tẽebo.
44013049	Woto la Soaala koɛɛg me paam n moon Pisidi tẽn-peelmẽ.
44013050	Zʋɩf rãmba maana sũdum ne nin-bɛda pagba sẽn da waoogd Wẽnde la ne tẽnga taoor dãmba tɩ b na n yik beem ne a Pol la a Barnabe, n dig-ba n yiis b tẽngẽ.
44013051	Bãmb me pĩmsa b nao wã tom la b teesa Ikoniyom.
44013052	Karen-biisa yẽ ra pida ne sũ-noogo la ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.
44014001	B sẽn ta Ikoniyom, b le kẽe Zʋɩf rãmba pʋʋsg roogẽ la b sẽn gom goam niynsa kɩtame tɩ bu-zẽmba, wala Zʋɩf rãmba, sak tẽebo.
44014002	Zʋɩf rãmb kẽer me zãgsa tẽebo n tus b taab tɩ b yik n maand beem ne saam-biisã.
44014003	A Pol ne a Barnabe kong n kaoosa beelẽ. B sũur da kegmame tɩ Soaala ra yãagda Koe-nooga moonego rãmba ne wẽnd makr dãmba la yel-bãna b sẽn da maande.
44014004	Tẽnga waa n welga sags a yiibu: bãmb dãmb kẽed Zʋɩf rãmbã tɩ bãmb dãmb kẽed Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã.
44014005	Zʋɩf rãmba ra yikame, bãmb ne b taoor dãmba n baood n na n nams Tʋʋm-tʋmdba la b lab-b ne kuga.
44014006	B bãngame n tɩ soond Likaoni tẽnsẽ: Listr, Derbe la b tẽn-toose.
44014007	Be me b sɩnga Koe-nooga moonego.
44014008	Listr tẽnga b yãee ned sẽn zĩ n ka tõe n yals a nao zug ye. A sẽn dog tɛka a zɩɩ n kẽn ye.
44014009	A kelga a Pol karengo. A Pol me ges-a lame la a sẽn mik t'a tẽeba sekame,
44014010	a zẽka a koɛɛg n yeel-a: «Yik n yaas tɩrga f nao zugu!» A sɩd yika vugr n sɩng kẽnde.
44014011	B sẽn yãenda Pol sẽn maana, neba kelma ne Likaoni tẽng rãmb goama: «Ad-y wẽnd dãmb n dɩk ninsaal wẽneg n sig d sʋka!»
44014012	B ra boonda a Barnabe t'a Zewus, n boond a Pol t'a Ermɛs, yẽ sẽn da so goama yĩnga.
44014013	Tẽnga noore, b ra mee roog b wẽnd a Zewus yĩnga la a Zewus maan-kʋʋdba waa ne lolse. B ra zoe n kãama puud n pid lolsã la yaa maoong kʋʋb la b ra naag zãma wã n segendẽ.
44014014	A Pol ne a Barnabe sẽn bãng rẽnna, b kẽesa b futu la b wudg n kẽe zãma wã sʋka la b kaasdẽ:
44014015	«D Zo-rãmba, yaa bõe la y maand woto? Tõnd me yaa ninsaalb wa yãmba. D waame bala n na n kos-y tɩ y bas y wẽn-yaalsa pʋgbo la y wẽnemd y nenga n tees Wẽnd vɩɩgã, sẽn naana yĩngr la tẽnga, mogra ne a pʋgẽ teed fãa.
44014016	Zamaan niyns sẽn looge Wẽnd basa buud kam fãa t'a tũ a sore;
44014017	b yaool ka kong b zãab sõnga kaset ye tɩ b zĩnda yĩngr n tool-b saase, n kõ-b sigr sõngo, n tɩgs-b ne koodo la b pids b sũur ne sũ-noogo.»
44014018	Gom bãmba pa tõog wʋsgo n lak b yama ne maoonga kʋʋb ye.
44014019	Zʋɩf rãmb n yaool n yi Antiyos la Ikoniyom n wa la zãma wã kelg-b lame. Woto wã b laba a Pol ne kuga n vu-a n yiis tẽngã, n tẽed t'a kiime.
44014020	Karen-biisa waa n gũbg-a lame n getẽ la a tik n yikame n kẽ tẽnga pʋga. Vẽkembeoogo a looga Derbe tẽng ne a Barnabe.
44014021	B sẽn moon Koe-nooga beelẽ n paam karen-biis zembala, b lɛɛg n tuda Listr, Ikoniyom la Antiyos.
44014022	B ra kengda karen-biisa sũuri n sagend-b tɩ b kell n gãd b tẽebã la a ra yet-b lame: «Wẽnd Rĩunga pʋgẽ pa kẽede tɩ f pa reng n yãe toog ye.»
44014023	B kõo Tigeng fãa a kãsem-dãmba. La b maana pʋʋsg sẽn naag ne no-loeere, n yaool n dɩk-ba n gũnug ne Soaala b sẽn teeg a soabã.
44014024	B sãaga Pisidi n ta Pãnfili,
44014025	b moona Koe-nooga Perze n yi be n dig Atali,
44014026	n le tɩ yi be n kẽ koom koglg n tees Antiyos, b pipi tẽnga. Saam-biisa ra yãagd-b la ne Wẽnd bark pʋʋsgo b tʋʋm sõma wã yĩnga.
44014027	B sẽn ta Antiyos b boola Tigengã n wilg Wẽnd sẽn sõng-b tɩ b maan bũmb ning fãa, n wilg tẽeba sor sẽn pak bu-zẽmba yĩnga.
44014028	B kaoosa beelẽ ne karen-biisã.
44015001	Neb kẽer n da yi Zɩɩde n wa zãmsd saam-biisã woto: «Y sã n ka kẽ bãong wala a Moyiiz Noora sẽn date, fãagr nan ka ye.»
44015002	Bʋʋr la no-koeemd yika bãmb ne a Pol la a Barnabe sʋka. B waa n yeelame tɩ b na n tʋma a Barnabe ne bãmb neb kẽer tɩ b leb Zerizalɛɛm, Tʋʋm-tʋmdba nengẽ tɩ b welg yellã.
44015003	Tigenga sõng-b la ne sor zug rɩɩbo tɩ b na n pãrg Fenisi la Samari, la b togsd bu-zẽmba sẽn lebg tẽedba tɩ rẽ noogd saam-biisa sũur al wʋsgo.
44015004	B sẽn ta Zerizalɛɛm, Tigengã, Tʋʋm-tʋmdba la nin-kẽemsã, reeg-b la neere la bãmb me togsa b sẽn maan bũmb ning ne Wẽnd sõngre.
44015005	Farizẽ rãmba neb kẽer da saka tẽebo. Bãmb n yik n yeele tɩ rẽnd b yeel bu-zẽmba tɩ b kẽ bãongo la b reeg a Moyiiz Noorã.
44015006	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba la nin-kẽemsã tigma taab n ges yellã.
44015007	B wẽe no-koeemde n kaoos la a Piyɛr wa n yikame n yeele: «Y miime, m saam-biisi, tɩ sɩngrẽ wã maam la Wẽnd yãk yã. B yãk-m lame tɩ bu-zẽmba wʋm m noorẽ Koe-noogã la b tẽ.
44015008	Wẽnd sẽn ne ninsaal sũuri kõo kaset tɩ b ka bas-b kɛɛng ye: b sika a Vʋʋsem Sõngo b zugu wala b sẽn sig tõndã.
44015009	B ka welg-b ne tõnd ye, n pek-b ne tẽeb kũuni.
44015010	Yaa bõe tɩ y rat n fɛɛs Wẽnde, bõe tɩ y rat n zɩlg karen-biisã zɩɩbo, d yaab rãmb la tõnd mens sẽn ka tõog n tʋke?
44015011	Ad-y yaa Krista maasmẽ la tõndo, wala bãmba, tẽed fãagre.»
44015012	Zãma wã yɩɩ sɩɩ. B le kelga a Barnabe ne a Pol sẽn maan wẽnd makr la yel-bãn niynsi ne Wẽnd sõngre, bu-zẽmba sʋka.
44015013	B sẽn gom n sɛ la a Zak sẽn yik n yeele: «Kelg-y ma, m saam-biisi;
44015014	a Simeõ wilg-y lame Wẽnd sẽn tʋlg al sɩngrẽ n sʋk buud sẽn na yɩ b rẽnna.
44015015	‹La rẽ me n be bãngdba sebrẽ:
44015016	M na n lɛɛg n waame m na n yika a Daviid ro-wãoongo m na n yika a raboogo; sẽn lʋɩ wã na n le yalsa yĩngri,
44015017	woto la sẽn ket-ba na n bao Soaalã, la na n yɩɩ boto me ne bu-zẽmb niyns m sẽn welg toore: yaa Soaala n yeele,
44015018	bãmb n yals rẽ al zamaan woko.›
44015019	Yaa rẽnd me yĩnga la ma me tagsda tɩ b ra nams bu-zẽmb niyns sẽn lebg tẽedbã ye.
44015020	B kos-b bala tɩ b vẽ ne maanda bũmbu, ne yoobo, ne gɩf la zɩɩm.
44015021	Rẽ wã yaa vẽeneg ne ba tɩ yaa al daar zãra la a Moyiiz Noora tar karen-saamb tẽng fãa pʋgẽ t'a karemd-a noora pʋʋsg rotẽ, sibr daar fãa.»
44015022	Tʋʋm-tʋmdba, nin-kẽemsã la Tigenga gill zemsa taaba n yãk bãmb neb kẽere n tum-b Antiyos ne a Pol la a Barnabe. Yɩ-la a Zɩɩd, b sẽn boond t'a Barsabas la a Silas, neb sẽn da ya sʋk neba.
44015023	Ad sebr ning b sẽn ning b nugẽ: «Tʋʋm-tʋmdba la nin-kẽemsã, yãmb saam-biisi, n toond pʋʋsem saam-biis niyns sẽn be-b Antiyos, Siri la Silisi, bu-zẽmba tẽn-peelmẽ.
44015024	D wʋmame tɩ neb n yi ka n wa y nengẽ la tõnd yaool n ka tʋm-b ye, la b waa n gomame n yɛɛs yã la b kalem yɛlã y yamẽ.
44015025	Dẽ me la d zĩnd ne taaba n zems taaba n tũus neba n tʋm-b yãmb nengẽ ne d zo-rãmb a Barnabe la a Pol,
44015026	neb sẽn dɩk b vɩɩm zãnga n kõ Soaala Zezi Krista.
44015027	D tʋm-y-la a Zɩɩd la a Silas la b na togs-y ne noore sẽn be sebra pʋga.
44015028	Tõnd naaga a Vʋʋsem Sõng n yalse tɩ d ka na n zɩlg-y zɩɩb a to n zʋʋg sẽn pak bala
44015029	tɩ y vẽ ne maand nemdo, ne zɩɩm, ne gɩfo la ne yoobo. Modg-y n gũus-y ne rẽ. Wẽnd na taas!»
44015030	B sẽn pʋʋs taaba n sɛ, sẽn tʋm b rãmba looga Antiyos. B sẽn ta bal la b sẽn tigim tẽedbã n kɩs-b sebrã.
44015031	B reeg-a lame n karem la b sũur yɩɩ noog t'a waa n kenga b raoodo.
44015032	A Zɩɩd ne a Silas ra yaa bãngdba, bãmb me goma ne saam-biisã n kaoos n le keng b sũya.
44015033	Dasem sẽn maan a wãna, saam-biisa lebs-b la sẽn tʋm-ba nengẽ ne laafi toaala. [
44015034	A Silas yẽ zãgsame t'a kõn loog ye.]
44015035	Sã n ya a Pol ne a Barnabe, bãmb me paa Antiyos. B ra naaga neb wʋsgo n zãmsdẽ la b moon kiba-noogã, Soaala Koe-noogã.
44015036	Sẽn yɩ bilf dẽ poore, a Pol yeela a Barnabe: «D leb n kaag saam-biisã tẽns niyns d sẽn zoe n moon Soaala koɛɛgã n ges b tũudma sẽn be zĩig ninga.»
44015037	A Barnabe da ratame t'a Zã, b sẽn boond a soab t'a Mark, tũ-ba.
44015038	A Pol da pa rat t'a tũ ye, tɩ Pãnfili, a ra lɛɛg n bas-b lame la a ka naag bãmb n tʋm ye.
44015039	Waa n lebga zabre, tɩ b na n kong n welg taaba. A Barnabe ne a Mark kẽe koglg n tees Sɩpr.
44015040	A Pol me looga ne a Silas la b saam-biisa rengame n yõk Soaala sɛɛg b yĩnga.
44015041	A Pol pɩʋʋga Siri la Silisi, n maneg n zĩndig Tigengu.
44016001	Dẽ poore a taa Derbe la Listr. Karen-biig a ye n da be be n boond t'a Timote. A ma yaa Zʋɩf poak sẽn sak tẽebo la a ba yaa Grɛk.
44016002	Listr la Ikoniyom saam-biisa ra gomda a yell ne pẽgre.
44016003	Dẽ me la a Pol yeel t'a na n lebga a tũud-n-taaga la a kẽes-a-la bãongo tɩ Zʋɩf rãmb da bee be la b ra miime t'a Timote ba yaa bu-zẽna.
44016004	B sẽn ta tẽng ning fãa b ra wilgda Tʋʋm-tʋmdba la nin-kẽemsa sebrã n sagennẽ tɩ b modg n tũ.
44016005	Tigeng fãa pʋgẽ tẽeba ra kɩɩda yẽgna la tẽedba sõor da paasda beoog sẽn vẽege.
44016006	B saaga Frizi tẽn-peelem la Galat rãmb tẽnga. B ka paam a Vʋʋsem Sõng sore n moon Koe-nooga Azi tẽng ye.
44016007	B waa n taa Mizi sɛtmẽ, n tʋlg n kẽ Bitini la a Vʋʋsem Sõng ka pak sor ye.
44016008	Woto wã b pɩʋʋga Mizi n lɛɛg n sig Troas.
44016009	Yʋng sẽn ta, a Pol zãmsame. A yãenda Masedoan ned a ye, t'a yɛs yĩngr n kot-a: «Tũ Masedoan, wa fãag-do!»
44016010	Likra poore, d tʋlgame n ta Masedoan, tɩ d da kõ-la d mens yam tɩ Wẽnd n boond tõndo Koe-nooga yĩnga.
44016011	D sẽn kẽ koglg Troas d teesa Samotras. Vẽkembeoogo d teesa Neyapolis,
44016012	d yii be n dig Filip tẽnga. Yaa tẽn kãseng Masedoan tẽnsa fãa sʋka la Rom dãmb n da waa n kẽed-a. D maana rasem a wãn tẽn kãng pʋgẽ,
44016013	la vʋʋsg daare d yii tẽnga kɛɛnga; kʋɩlg n da be be, la yaa kʋɩlga noor la b ra yãk pʋʋsg zĩiga. D zĩndame la d yãenda koɛɛg n kõ pagba sẽn da tigma.
44016014	Bãmb nin-yend n da kelgd neere: a yʋʋra la a Lidi, a ra koosda monom Tiyatir pʋgẽ, a ra waoogda Wẽnde; Wẽnd kõ-a-la vẽenegre la a Pol karengã kɛla a sũurẽ.
44016015	Yẽ ne a zak rãmb sẽn deeg soobo, a kos-d la woto: «Y sã n get-m wa Soaala neda, bɩ y wa zĩnd m zakẽ,» la yɩɩ wala modgre.
44016016	D waa n dabda pʋʋsg daar a yembre, n seg yem-pog-bil a ye sẽn da bʋgd bagre. A bãgra ra kõta a zu-soaben-dãmba ligd wʋsgo.
44016017	A Sɩngame n pʋgd tõnd ne a Pol la a gomda: «Nin-bãmba yaa Yĩngr Wẽnda tʋʋm-tʋmdba, yaa fãagra sor la b wilgd-y.»
44016018	A pʋg-d la woto rasem a wãna. A Pol waa n yɛɛme n wẽneg n yeele: «A Zezi Krista yʋʋr yĩnga, m kõt-f la noore, Sʋtãana, tɩ f yi la f bas pagã.» La a sɩd wẽneg n yiime n bas-a.
44016019	A zu-soaben-dãmba sẽn mik tɩ b rɩɩba sor menemame, b tɩ yõka a Pol la a Silas n tall-ba n taas tẽnga rãmb sɛk zĩigẽ, bʋ-kaoodb taoore.
44016020	B yeela tẽnga taoor dãmba: «Nin-bãmba waa n dãmbda tẽngã, yaa Zʋɩf rãmba.
44016021	B wata ne noe tõnd Rom dãmba sẽn ka tõe n deeg la d tũ ye.»
44016022	Neba yika ne-ba. Taoor dãmba kɩtame tɩ b yees b futã la b pãb-b-la ne kaase.
44016023	B Pãb-b la sõmbo n yaool n kẽes-b roogo. B kosa ro-gũudã t'a maan a ni.
44016024	Ro-gũuda me sẽn wʋm dẽ, a kẽes-b la pʋgẽ doogã n loe b nao wã ne rabõanga.
44016025	Yʋn-sʋka, a Pol ne a Silas ra pʋʋsdame la b pẽgd Wẽnd ne yɩɩla.
44016026	Tẽnga waa n yika vugr bal n tar miuungu tɩ ya wa rooga na n lukame. Kʋɩlensa fãa pagsa vugri tɩ bãeensa sẽn da sog bi-beesa foos n dʋʋg.
44016027	Ro-gũuda nekame n yãe tɩ kʋɩlensa pagsame t'a wõog a sʋʋga n na n kʋ a menga t'a ra tẽedame tɩ bi-beesa fãa loogame.
44016028	A Pol tãs-a lame: «Da pogl f meng ye tɩ tõnd fãa keta ka.»
44016029	Ro-gũuda kosame tɩ b widg bugum t'a zoetẽ la a rigda n tɩ wõgemd a Pol ne a Silas taoore.
44016030	A yiis-b la roogo la a yeel-b lame: «Soaala, yaa bõe la m tog n maan n fãag m sɩɩga?»
44016031	B leok-a lame: «Tẽ Soaal a Zezi tɩ foo ne f zaka na paam fãagre.»
44016032	B wilg-a-la Soaala Koe-noogã, yẽ ne a zak rãmba.
44016033	Yɩɩ zĩig pʋgẽ bala la ne yʋngo la a peeg-ba n tɩ peks b noadã la yẽ ne a zaka rãmb fãa deega soobo.
44016034	A tall-b lame n kẽes a zakẽ, n bao rɩɩb n kõ-ba la a naaga a zak rãmb n kɩdem sũ-noogo, b sẽn lebg tẽedba yĩnga.
44016035	Zĩig sẽn yẽege, tẽnga taoor dãmb tʋma rapoy-bi tɩ b wa yeel ro-gũuda: «Yiis-y nin-bãmba roogo.»
44016036	Ro-gũuda me taasa a Pol b goama: «Tẽnga taoor dãmb tʋmame tɩ b wa yeel tɩ b bas-y tɩ y looge. Dẽnd yĩnga yi-y n loog-y.»
44016037	Dẽ me la a Pol yeel Dapoy-bi wã: «B kɩtame tɩ b pãb tõnd neba fãa taoore, tõnd ne d sẽn ya Rom tẽngen-bi-taase; b kẽesa tõnd bi-bees roogẽ. La marsã b ratame n soos n yiis-du! Bada! B mens wa b toore n yiis-du.»
44016038	Dapoy-bi wã taasa tẽnga taoor dãmb b goama. B sẽn wʋm t'a Pol ne a Silas yaa tẽngen-bi-taar ne Rom dãmba, b yɛɛsame.
44016039	Tẽnga taoor dãmb n sɩd wa b toore n kos-b tɩ b maan yãgbo la b yi tẽngã.
44016040	B sẽn yi roogo a Pol ne a Silas leba a Lidi zakẽ. B le sega saam-biisa be n le keng b tẽeb n yaool n loog.
44017001	B kẽe Amfipolis n sãag Apoloni n ta Tesalonik. Beelẽ Zʋɩf rãmba ra tara b pʋʋsg roogo.
44017002	La wala a sẽn maand dasem kam, yaa beelẽ la a Pol tɩ yãend-ba. Vʋʋsga raar tong taaba a tã b sẽn gãneg b sõasgã sebr sõng zugu.
44017003	A Pol ra gomda ne-ba n wilgd-b tɩ Krista ra tog n namsame la b vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka, la a ra yetame: «Krista la a Zezi, m sẽn moond a soabã.»
44017004	Bãmb sʋka neb kẽer paamame n yi b likẽ n lebg tũud-n-taar ne a Pol la a Silas. La tõe n paas a Zʋɩf rãmb kẽed-paalse la bu-zẽmba la nin-bɛd pagb ka tɛka.
44017005	Zʋɩf rãmba yika sũ-kiiri, n kẽ raagẽ wã n wool nin-yaalse sẽn gũm taaba n tar bʋʋr tẽnga pʋga. B ta a Zason yiri n baood a Pol la a Silas n na kẽes-b bʋʋd tẽnga soaalba taoore.
44017006	B ka yãend-b be ye la b kora a Zason la saam-biis kẽer n ta kombɛɛmba nengẽ la b kaasdẽ: «Nin-bãmba n leebd ãndũni rãmba zutu, la ad-b sẽn ta ka me.
44017007	La ad-a Zason sẽn deeg-b a zakẽ. Nin-bãmba tõdgda Rom naaba noore, n moonẽ tɩ dĩm a to n be: a Zezi.»
44017008	B bʋʋra yɛɛsa zãma wã la kombɛɛmbã.
44017009	B yeela a Zason la neb a taabã tɩ b wa ne ligdi tɩ b yaool n bas-ba.
44017010	Zĩig sẽn sobge, saam-biisa kɩtame t'a Pol ne a Silas loog Bere tẽnga. B sẽn ta be b tɩ kẽe Zʋɩf rãmba pʋʋsg roogẽ.
44017011	Bãmb da tara zʋg sõngo n yɩɩd Tesalonik rãmbã. B reega Koɛɛga tao-tao. Beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa b ra karemda Sebr Sõngo n get bõe n ka zems a Pol dãmb toagsgẽ.
44017012	Bãmb wʋsg saka tẽebo, la bu-zẽmba sʋka, nin-bɛd pagba, la rap me.
44017013	Tesalonik Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn wʋm t'a Pol moona Bere tẽnga Wẽnd koɛɛgã b le waa n dãmba nebã.
44017014	Dẽ la Saam-biisa me kɩt t'a Pol yi n tees mogrã. A Silas la a Timote yaool n paa be.
44017015	Sẽn da yãagd-ba a Pol yãag-a lame n ta Atɛn n yaool n lɛɛg ne a Pol koɛɛg, a Silas la a Timote yĩnga: tɩ b bʋʋg-a be tao tao.
44017016	A Pol ra gũuda a Silas la a Timote Atɛn la a sũura ra kɛɛda wa bugum, a sẽn mik tɩ tẽnga pida ne wẽn-naandse.
44017017	Woto a sõasga ra welga sags a yiibu. A Ra sõsda pʋʋsga roogẽ ne Zʋɩf rãmba la sẽn da tũud-b Wẽnde; n sõsd tẽnga rãmb sɛka zĩigẽ ne sẽn wat-b be.
44017018	Neb sẽn da karem n sik meng n da mii n wat a nengẽ, wala bãng sẽn noom f yĩnga rãmba, la kũum dabeem ka tar-m dãmba. Bãmb kẽer da sokdame: «Luiin-bag kãnga yetame tɩ bõe?» Tɩ kẽer me yetẽ: «Ad-y yaa bu-zẽnd wẽnd dãmb sor la a wilgda.» La rẽ me yaa b sẽn da wʋmd Zezi yʋʋre la kũum vʋʋgre.
44017019	B talla a Pol n zãag bilfu n sokd-a: «D tõeeme n bãng f zãms paalsa bɩ?
44017020	Fo sẽn leokd tõnd koees niynsa yaa koe-sãamse, dẽ la d dat n wʋm b võore.»
44017021	Atɛn tẽng rãmba la sãamba sẽn waa n nok-bã sɩd da ka tar tʋʋmd a to n zʋʋg kibar paalg yelgre bɩ kelgr ye.
44017022	A Pol yik n yalsa yĩngr bãmb sʋka n yeele: «Atɛn dãmba, m neeme tɩ y yaa neb sẽn mi wẽnd waoogre n yɩɩd buuda taaba.
44017023	M saagame n gilg y tẽngã, la m gesa neere y sẽn me y wẽnd dãmba yĩnga. M tol n yãenda maan-kugri b sẽn gʋls a zug woto: ‹D sẽn ka mi wẽnd ninga rẽnna›. Ad-y yaa yãmb sẽn waoogd n yaool n ka mi a soaba la mam wat n na n wilg yãmba.
44017024	Wẽnd ning sẽn naana dũnia la bũmb ning fãa sẽn be a pʋgẽ, yĩngr la tẽng Soaala, ad-y b ka kẽed ninsaal sẽn me rot niynsa ye.
44017025	Ka ninsaal nug n na n yiis bũmb n kõ-ba, wala bũmb n paoog-b tɩ b rat ye, tɩ yaa bãmb n kõt vɩɩm, vʋʋsem la paoong fãa.
44017026	B tʋlgame tɩ ninsaalba fãa sẽn be tẽng zugã yɩ yẽgr a ye wila. B yalsa bũmb fãa a zĩigẽ, n yals bũmb fãa a toaaga la a wakato.
44017027	La b raaba yaa b fãa bao la b paam Wẽnd belem kaseto, wala b sẽn tõe, ba sã n na yɩɩ wala ne bablgo, tɩ Wẽnd pa zãr ne tõndo, b pa zãr ne ned kam fãa ye.
44017028	Sɩda yaa bãmb maasmẽ la d vɩ la d kẽnda la d yaa d sẽn yalã. Pʋs n yaa woto la yãmb neb kẽer yeel yã: ‹D yaa buud a ye ne Bãmba.›
44017029	Tõnd ne Wẽnd sã n ya buud a ye, d ka tog n mams-ba wala sãnem, wanzurfu bɩ kugr, ninsaal minim la a bãngr sẽn yag ye.
44017030	Wẽnd basa sẽn looga taale, bãngr kaoolga taale, n yik marsã n na n wilg ninsaalba, b sẽn ya zĩig ning fãa neba, tɩ b teem zʋgo.
44017031	B bãng tɩ b yãka raare n na n kao ne zemsgo ninsaalba fãa bʋʋdo. B yãka bʋ-kaoodã, la kaset ning b sẽn kõt tɩ bãmb n yãk yẽ soabã, yaa b sẽn vʋʋg-a kɩɩms sʋkã.»
44017032	Atɛn dãmba sẽn wʋm t'a Pol gomd sẽn ki vʋʋgr yellã, kẽer pusga laado. Kẽer me yeelame: «D na kelg gomd kãnga nindaare.»
44017033	Boto me la a Pol paam n yi b sʋka.
44017034	Neb kẽer lebga b tũud-n-taase la b saka tẽebo. A Denis zĩnda b sʋka. Pag a ye me n zĩnd be n boond tɩ Damaris. Neba taab me n paase.
44018001	Dẽ sẽn looge, a Pol zãaga ne Atɛn n dig Korẽnt.
44018002	A yãenda Zʋɩf a ye be sẽn boond tɩ Akilas, yaa Põ tẽn-peelmẽ neda la a nan waa paalem, yẽnda ne a pag a Prisil. Itali la b yii n wa Korẽnt tɩ dĩm a Klod da kõo Zʋɩf rãmba noore tɩ b yi Rom. A Pol lebga zood ne bãmba,
44018003	b nug tʋʋmd sẽn da ya tʋʋm yɛnga. Yaa bãmb la a tɩ noke tɩ b naag taab n tʋmnẽ. Yaa pɛɛl sẽn tar n tiid doto la b ra wʋgda.
44018004	Sibr daar fãa a Pol da maanda kareng pʋʋsga roogẽ n na n vẽneg Zʋɩf rãmba la bu-zẽmba.
44018005	A Silas ne a Timote sẽn yi Masedoan n wa tɛka, a Pol tʋʋmda lebga moon Koe-noogã n wilg Zʋɩf rãmbã t'a Zezi la Wẽnd sẽn tʋm a soabã.
44018006	A sẽn mik tɩ b pa rat n kelge la b gomd n tʋʋsda Wẽnde, a Pol fugumda a fut b taoore n yetẽ: «Y kɩɩsga sẽn wãad yãmba taal pa ne yã. Sã n ya maam, taal ka m zug ye la marsã tɛka yaa bu-zẽmba la m na n babse.»
44018007	A Pol yii be n dig a Zustus yiri; nin-kãng ra pʋʋsda Wẽnde la a zaka ra yega ne pʋʋsga roogo.
44018008	Pʋʋsga roog naab ra boondame tɩ Krispus. Yẽnd me saka tẽebo. Korẽnt neba pʋs n yɩɩ wʋsgo sẽn sak tẽeb la b reeg soobo.
44018009	Yʋng a ye Soaala lika a Pol n yeel-a: «Da zoe rabeem ye, da vʋʋs ne Koɛɛga mooneg ye, da sĩnd ye.
44018010	M bee ne foo la ned kõn sɩɩs-fo n maan-f wẽng ye, kaalẽ m tẽeda neb wʋsgo m Tigenga yĩnga.»
44018011	A Pol paa Korẽnt yʋʋmd la kiis a yoobe, n tar Koɛɛga mooneg bala.
44018012	A Galiõ sẽn waa n ya Akayi kombere, Zʋɩf rãmba yika wa nin-yɛnga n na n maan zabr ne a Pol. B kẽes-a la bʋʋdo,
44018013	n yetẽ: «Nin-kãnga sagenda neba tɩ b waoog Wẽnd ne waoogr sẽn pa tũud Noorã.»
44018014	A Pol sɩngame t'a na n gome la a Galiõ leoka Zʋɩf rãmbã: «M na n kelgẽ-la y koɛɛgã sã da yaẽ la ned bũmb la a sãam yã, bɩ sã n da yaẽ la yel-yood la a maanyã, tɩ rẽ segdame.
44018015	La sã n kella no-koɛɛm goam biis poorẽ, bɩ yʋy poorẽ, bɩ y meng Noora poorẽ, yãmb n na bãnge, mam yẽ kõn lʋɩɩs m toog ye.»
44018016	A Yiis-b-la bʋʋda zĩigẽ.
44018017	B fãa yii n gãda a Sostɛn, pʋʋsga roog naaba, la b sɩnga a pãbr, bʋʋda zak noor bala, t'a Galiõ sɩd sĩnd waa toog ka ye.
44018018	A Pol kell n paa rasem a wãn Korẽnt la a waa n basa a saam-biisã n kẽ koglgo, n tees Siri. A Prisil ne a Akilas yãag-a lame. A Pol ra põnga a zug Sẽnkre tɩ pʋleng la a ra pʋlm yã.
44018019	B waa n siga Efɛɛz. Beelẽ a welga ne a tũud-n-taasã. A sẽn tɩ kẽ pʋʋsg roogẽ a sõsa ne Zʋɩf rãmba.
44018020	Bãmb kos-a lame t'a ra yãg loogr ye, t'a ka sak ye.
44018021	B sẽn waa n pʋʋsd Wẽnd na taas la a yeel-b: «M na n lɛɛg n wala y nengẽ, Wẽnd sã n data.» A yii Efɛɛz.
44018022	A Sẽn sig Sezare, a tɩ pʋʋsa Tigengã n yaool n tees Antiyos.
44018023	A maana rasem a wãn beelẽ n le yi n dɩk a sor n digd Galat la Frizi rãmb tẽnga, n kengd karen-biisa tẽebo.
44018024	Zʋɩf a ye sẽn boond tɩ Apolos, n yit Aleksãndri baobgo, waa Efɛɛz. Yaa ned sẽn da mi goama la ned sẽn da vẽen ne Sebr sõngo.
44018025	A ra paam n zãmsa sor ning sẽn boond tɩ Soaala sorã la a ra pelga a sũuri n moonẽ la a gomd a Zezi yell tɩ tũud tɩrga, la yaool n ya a Zã soobã la a so yã.
44018026	A yika pʋʋsga roogẽ n gomd t'a sũur pa kiuusdẽ ye. A Prisil la a Akilas kelga a goama la b peeg-a lame n tɩ vẽneg-a Sora zãnga.
44018027	A Apolos da rat n kẽnga Akayi, tɩ saam-biisa yeel-a t'a maan dẽ, a maan neere, la b gʋlsa karen-biisa tɩ b reeg-a neere. Sɩda a sẽn ta be, ne Wẽnd sõngre, tẽedba rɩ-la a yõod zembala.
44018028	A ra leoodame n lubd Zʋɩf rãmbã, neba fãa nifẽ, n wilgd ne Sebr sõngo t'a Zezi la Wẽnd sẽn tʋm a soabã.
44019001	A Apolos sẽn waa n be Korẽnt, dẽ t'a Pol saaga tẽns niyns sẽn zao tãmsa zutu n sig Efɛɛz. A mika karen-biis kẽere.
44019002	A yeel-b lame: «Yãmb sẽn sak tẽebã wakato, y paama a Vʋʋsem Sõng bɩ?» Tɩ b leoke: «Tõnd nan ka wʋm meng tɩ b gomd t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng beeme ye.»
44019003	T'a Pol le sok-ba: «Yãmb sẽn deeg soob ninga la bʋgo?» Tɩ b yeele: «A Zã soobo.»
44019004	Dẽ la a Pol yeel yã: «Yaa sũur tekr soob la a Zã ra kõta la a yet zãma wã tɩ b tẽ ned ninga sẽn na n wa yẽnda poorẽ wã: a Zezi.»
44019005	B sẽn wʋm dẽ b reega soob Soaal a Zezi yʋʋr yĩnga.
44019006	A Pol sẽn tẽeg a nus b zutu la a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn sig-ba tɩ b sɩng n wɩlemd bu-zẽn goam la b gomd bãngr goama.
44019007	B ra yaa bãmb piig la a yiibu.
44019008	A Pol tɩ kẽe pʋʋsga roogẽ la kiis a tã sẽn pʋg taaba a ra gomda ne raoodo. A Sõasga ra yaa Arzãn Rĩunga yelle n dat tɩ kẽ b sũurẽ.
44019009	Kẽer n zĩnd be n da pa reegd saglg ye tɩ b sũura ra kɩʋʋlmame. Bãmb dãmb n da sãbsd Wẽnd sorã, neba fãa taoore. A welga ne bãmb dãmba. A sʋka karen-biisã. Beoog-beoog fãa a ra maand-b la kareng a Tiranos karen-doogẽ.
44019010	Kell n talla boto yʋʋm a yi la rẽ me la Azi rãmba, Zʋɩf bɩ bu-zẽmba tõog n wʋm Soaala Koɛɛgã.
44019011	Wẽnd kõ-la a Pol pãng t'a maand wẽnd makr dãmb sẽn da yɩkd pɛlense.
44019012	Sã n dɩk peend buud fãa sẽn sɩɩs a Pol n lɛɛg n sɩɩs bãad-dãmba, b bãasa wẽnegd n sãoogame, bɩ Sʋtãamba yit n loogame.
44019013	La ade, Zʋɩf rãmb kẽer me n da saad n sãoogd neba. Bãmb me makame n pʋd Soaala Zezi yʋʋr n na n sãoog Sʋtãan sẽn da kẽ b rãmba. B ra yetame: «M kot-y lame tɩ y yi, Zezi ninga yʋʋr yĩnga, Zezi ning a Pol sẽn gomd a soab yellã!»
44019014	Da yaa a Seva kamb a yopoe n da maand woto la a Seva meng ra yaa Zʋɩf rãmb maan-kʋʋd kãsenga.
44019015	Sʋtãan a ye lɛɛg n yeel-b lame: «Sã n ya a Zezi, mam mii bãmba, Sã n ya a Pol, mam mii yẽ me. La yãmba, yãmb la a bõe rãmba?»
44019016	La Sʋtãana yiime n wudg n kẽ bãmba, n lubd-ba, a yembr-yembre, n pogend-ba tɩ b na n zoe n yi yɩnga, b bɩlma, la ne sãmpoaga.
44019017	Efɛɛz rãmb fãa, Zʋɩf bɩ bu-zẽmb wʋma yellã. Rabeem yõka b fãa, la Soaala Zezi yʋʋr paama pẽgre.
44019018	Sẽn sak-b tẽeba waa zembala n deeg b kongre la b wilg bãmb me sẽn da maande.
44019019	Sẽn da zãms-b rabaar buud toor toore n tʋmnẽ n yɩkd neba pɛlensã, waa ne b rabaara sɛba la b yõog-b la neba fãa taoore. B geela b sɛba yõodo. Seka neb tus pis nu daar a ye tʋʋmd yaoodo.
44019020	Ad-y Soaala Koe-nooga ra paamda moonego la a ra kɩɩda yẽgen sẽn tar pãnga.
44019021	Dẽ loogr poore a Pol ninga a yamẽ t'a na n le tũu Masedoan la Akayi n leb Zerizalɛɛm. A ra yetame: «M sã n ta be na yɩ tɩlɛ tɩ m ta Rom me.»
44019022	A tʋma Masedoan a sõangdba a yiibu, a Timote la a Erast; yẽ meng yaool n paa rasem a wãn Azi tẽn-peelmẽ.
44019023	Wakat kãnga, Sora poorẽ, tẽnga wa n dãmbame.
44019024	Ned a ye n da ya yõaka n boond tɩ Demetriyus. A ra yõgda ne wanzurfu a Artemis wẽnd doto. Woto a ra sõngda tẽnga rãmb wʋsgo ne nug tʋʋmde.
44019025	A tigsa yẽ sẽn kõ b rãmb tʋʋmna la neba a taab sẽn ya yõgs wa yẽnda n yeel-ba: «M zo-rãmba, tõnd sẽn vɩ tɩ d vɩɩma sakdẽ wã, y miime tɩ rẽ bela d tʋʋmnẽ wã.
44019026	La ade, wala y sẽn ne la y sẽn wʋmde Azi tẽn-peelma tõre, a Pol ne a saglsã woola neb ka tɛk a poorẽ sẽn maand tɩ wẽnd sẽn dõog ne nug, ka tõe n yɩ wẽnd ye.
44019027	Woto tõeeme tɩ b pa le ges tõnd tʋʋmna wa bũmb sẽn be võor ye, tõeeme tɩ b wa ges tõnd wẽnd poaka Artemis meng rooga wa zaalem, la rẽ fãa wat n baasa ne paoore, wẽnd ning Azi la dũni wã tõr sẽn waoogda paoore.»
44019028	Neba sẽn wʋm dẽ, b sũur puuga wʋsgo tɩ b tar kaasgo: «A Artemis, Efɛɛz rãmba wẽnda, yaa wẽn kãsenga!»
44019029	Waa n lebga tẽnga tõr n wulumdi. Fãa kaoogame n digd reema zĩigẽ al tɩ Masedoan rãmba, a Pol so-toaka neba, a Gayus ne a Aristark, kong n pʋg-ba.
44019030	A Pol da ratame n tɩ yãend buudã la karen-biisa ka sak ye.
44019031	Azi rãmb neb kẽer sẽn da ya a zo-rãmba, kos-a lame t'a ra koos a yõor ye, la a ra tag reema zĩigẽ ye.
44019032	Bãmb dãmb da yetame tɩ wãnda, tɩ bãmb dãmb yet tɩ woto. Tẽnga taoor dãmb mens ra ka mi b tigsga võor ye.
44019033	Zʋɩf rãmba da ratame t'a Aleksãndr yɩ b norɛɛsa, n yiisa sʋka. A kabsa ne nug n na n gome ne nebã.
44019034	La b sẽn bãng tɩ yaa Zʋɩf, b fãa lagma taab n kelemd wa nin-yende, na ta wakat a yiib pʋgẽ: «A Artemis, Efɛɛz rãmb wẽn poaka, yaa wẽn kãsenga!»
44019035	Bʋʋda taoor soab waa n tõogame tɩ b bas bʋʋre t'a yeele: «Efɛɛz rãmba, ãnda be dũni wã pʋga n ka mi tɩ tẽn kãnga n gũud wẽn kãsenga Artemis doogã la a menga nin-naand sẽn yi yĩngr n sigã?
44019036	No-koeemd sẽn ka be rẽ poorẽ wã, y tog n zĩnda sɩɩ n da wa maan kegr ye.
44019037	Yãmb sẽn tall-b rãmb n wa ka wã, b ka tʋʋs yãmb wẽndã, b ka paooga ye.
44019038	A Demetriyus ne a tʋmd-n-taaga sã n tar koɛɛg ne ba, bʋʋd daar beeme, bʋ-kaoodb beeme, b bool-b badaare.
44019039	Koɛɛg a to sã n beẽ n dat welgre, d tigsga sẽn tar raarã, d na ges rẽnna.
44019040	Bũmb ning sẽn maan dũnna wã tõeeme tɩ b yeel tɩ yaa tõnd n dãmbd tẽngã, tɩ d meng yaool n ka tar rũnna gũm taaba võor ye.»
44019041	A sẽn leok woto n sɛ, b fãa sẽegame.
44020001	Bʋʋra sẽn yõke, a Pol boola karen-biisã, n sagl-ba, n pʋʋs-b wẽnd na taas la a looga Masedoan.
44020002	A Pɩʋʋga tẽngã n kengd tẽedbã la a rigd Grɛs Tẽn-peelmẽ.
44020003	Kiis a tãab la b maan be. Segame t'a sẽn waa n dat n kẽ koglg n dig Siri la a Pol sẽn wʋm tɩ Zʋɩf rãmba gãnega bẽdg a yĩnga. Dẽ me la a yeel t'a na n gõdg n leba Masedoan.
44020004	A tũud-n-taas yi-la a Sopatros, a Pirus biiga, Bere tẽng neda; n paas a Aristark ne a Sekundus, Tesalonik rãmba; n paas a Gayus, Doberɛs neda, n paas a Timote la a Tisik, la a Trofim, Azi rãmba.
44020005	Bãmb denga taoore n tɩ gũ-d Troas.
44020006	Tõnd mens kẽe koglg n yi komber a Filip tẽnga. Bur ka lobd bɩlla poore, rasem a nu pʋgẽ, d tɩ paam-b la Troas la bee d paa rasem a yopoe.
44020007	Sibr daar zaabre, d da tigma taab bura kaoob yĩnga. A Pol sẽn da rat n loog vẽkẽmbeooga ra sõsda ne-ba. A gomame n tãag yʋn-sʋka.
44020008	B ra widga fitils rãmb wʋsgo yĩngr doog ning d sẽn da tigma.
44020009	Bi-bɩɩg a ye sẽn boond tɩ Eutik da zĩi rooga võorẽ. Gõeem sẽn ya gõeem meng wa n lub-a lame, dẽ t'a Pol ket n maanda a karengo. Gõeema yĩnga a yii rooga roglem-roglem a tãab soaba n lʋɩ tẽnga. B sẽn zẽk-a, b mikame tɩ yaa kũum.
44020010	A Pol sigame n zõond n ges-a, n dɩk-a a nusẽ la a yeelame: «Tõog-y y mense t'a nan pa ki ye.»
44020011	A leba yĩngri n tɩ kao burã n dɩ; a Gomame tɩ zĩig wa yẽege. Dẽ marsã la a yaool n dɩk a sore.
44020012	B talla bi-bɩɩga vɩɩga n tɩ kẽes a zakẽ la zaka rãmb sũ-noog ka yɩ bilfr ye.
44020013	Tõnd denga taoore. D teesa d koglga Asos tɩ be la d da tog n dɩk a Pol n kẽes koglga pʋga wala a meng sẽn da kaoole.
44020014	A sẽn paam tõnd Asos d kẽes-a la koglga pʋga n dig Mitilɛn.
44020015	D sẽn yi be d taa Kio vẽkembeoogo. Da-yɩten-daare d looga Samos n tek n yaas Trogiliõ la raar ninga sẽn pʋga wã beoog vẽk-d la Milɛt.
44020016	A Pol da yeelame t'a ka na n yeg kooma noore n pẽneg Efɛɛz t'a wat n dat n bʋdgame n ta Azi, tɩ kẽnda tadge. A ra yãgdame n dat n kẽ Zerizalɛɛm, Wẽnd sã n sake, Tigsga kibs raare.
44020017	A Pol zĩnda Milɛt n tʋm tɩ b bool Efɛɛz Tigenga nin-kẽemsã.
44020018	B sẽn ta, a yeel-b lame: «Yãmb fãa miime, al pipi raarã, m naoor sẽn tag Azi tẽng tɛka, m manesem ne yãmb sẽn yɩ a soaba.
44020019	M tʋma Soaala tʋʋma ne yam sulgri, ne nintãm, ne namsg ning Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn nams maam ne b no-baoorã.
44020020	Y mii tɩ m baoo sẽn wat ne yõod yãmb yĩnga. M pa tar n leb poorẽ n mong-y y sẽn da tog n wʋmb bũmb ninga bɩ y sẽn da tog n zãms bũmb ninga, y zagsẽ bɩ y sɛk zĩisẽ ye.
44020021	D kosa Zʋɩf rãmbã wala bu-zẽmbã, tɩ b teem zʋg Wẽnd taoore la b tẽ Soaal a Zezi Krista.
44020022	Marsã yaa Wẽnd Vʋʋsem n tusd maam tɩ m dabd Zerizalɛɛm la m ka mi yell ning sẽn na n pak-m be ye.
44020023	M sẽn yaool n wʋm Wẽnd nengẽ n ta marsã yaa tɩ m sẽn ta tẽng ning fãa yaa naong la pɛt bal n gũud maam.
44020024	Sã n ya ne maam, m yaool n ka get m vɩɩma wa bũmb sẽn tar yõod ye. Sẽn pak maam yaa m vɩɩma, yaa m tʋʋmda baas neere, tʋʋmd ning Soaala Zezi sẽn kõ-ma. La b tʋʋmna yaa m yɩ Wẽnd kũun kãsenga kaset soaba, b Koe-nooga moanda.
44020025	Marsã, ad-m sẽn mi bũmb ninga: y kõn le yãend m neng ye; yãmb fãa yaool n yãend-m la y sʋka tɩ m moond Wẽnnaam Rĩunga Koe-noogo.
44020026	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m tõe n togs, y fãa gill taoore: m zug roka ne yãmb ned kam fãa vɩɩm sãoong taale.
44020027	M sɩd mao ne bũmb fãa; m wilg-y-la Wẽnd sẽn dat tɩ yɛla fãa pids to-to.
44020028	Bɩ yãmb mens maan gũusgu la y gũ Wẽnd bãgr ning a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn gũnug yãmbã. Kɩɩm-y bãgr ning paoong sẽn tũ ne Biiga zɩɩma raagre.
44020029	M sẽn mi yaa tɩ m loogra poore digd-n-yĩidsi sẽn ya toose, ka na n bas bãgra ye.
44020030	M miime tɩ m loogr poore, neb n na n yik yãmb sʋka, n gom n tudug karen-biisã tɩ b yi tõnd poorẽ n tɩ kẽ bãmba.
44020031	Dẽ la m kot-y tɩ y maan gũusgu la y tẽeg tɩ yʋʋm a tãab tõre, wĩndg la yʋngo m yõka yãbre n wilg ned kam fãa a kongre.
44020032	Marsã m gũnugda yãmb ne Wẽnd la ne b Gomda kũuni: Gomd sẽn tõe tɩ rooga me n yalse, la a tõe tɩ Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb toora rɩ b yõodo.
44020033	M ka tʋlg yãmb ned ba a ye wanzurf bɩ a sãnem, bɩ a fuug ye.
44020034	Ad-y yaa m nus bãmba m kõ-m tɩ m yiis m meng la m tũud-n-taasa kom.
44020035	M kõ-y la kaset toor-toore, tɩ d tog n saka toogo n tõog n yols d taaba nimbãanega la m yeel-y lame tɩ y tẽeg Soaala meng sẽn yeele: sẽn kõt-a sũ-noog yɩɩda sẽn deegd-a.»
44020036	A sẽn gom woto, a yĩgimdame n pʋʋs ne nin-kẽemsã.
44020037	B fãa ninga nintãm la b gãda a Pol n tara yubla mogsgo.
44020038	La bũmb sẽn sãam b sũur wʋsgo, yaa Pol sẽn yeel-ba: y kõn le yãend m neng ye. Bãmb n yãag-a n tãag kooma koglgo.
44021001	D sẽn paam n fãagd d meng nin-kẽemsa nusẽ, d teesa Kos tɩrga. Vẽkembeoogo d taa Rod la Patara.
44021002	Be d paama koom koglg sẽn dabd Fenisi. D kẽeme n looge.
44021003	D yãenda Sɩpr yɩɩga tɩ d bas-a d goabga, n tees Siri la yaa Tir la d sig yã. Koglga ra tog n yalsa be n sik a zɩɩbo.
44021004	D mika karen-biis beelẽ la rasem a yopoe la d paa Tir. A Vʋʋsem Sõng vẽnega karen-biisa tɩ b yeel a Pol t'a ra kẽng Zerizalɛɛm ye.
44021005	Loogra sẽn ta d baas n loogame. B fãa ra yãagd-d lame, pagb la kamb fãa. D sẽn yi tẽngã d fãa yĩgimda mogra noor n pʋʋse.
44021006	D sẽn pʋʋs taaba, d kẽe koglgã. Bãmb me leba b tẽngẽ.
44021007	D sẽn yi Tir d baasa d kẽndã Ptolemayis. D pʋʋsa beelẽ saam-biisã la d paa ne b raar a ye.
44021008	Vẽkembeoogo d yiime n dig Sezare. D siga a Filip zakẽ; a ra moonda Koɛɛga be la a ra yaa Sõangdb a yopoe wã nin-yende.
44021009	A ra tara kom-pugli a naas sẽn nan pa kul sɩdb ye la sẽn da gomd bãngr goama.
44021010	D paa be rasem a wãna la bãngd sẽn boond tɩ Agabus yii Zɩɩde n wa.
44021011	A bʋʋga tõnd a Filip zakẽ la a rɩka a Pol sẽbdgã n kɩt tɩ b loe a karse la a nusi la a gomda: «Ad-a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn wilgdi: Rao ninga sẽn soa sẽbdg kãnga bãng tɩ Zʋɩf rãmba na n sẽb-a la woto Zerizalɛɛm n bas-a bu-zẽmba nusẽ.»
44021012	D sẽn wʋm dẽ, d naaga ne tẽnga rãmb n bõs a Pol t'a ra keng Zerizalɛɛm ye.
44021013	La ad-a sẽn leok-do: «Yaa bõe tɩ y yãbd n sãamd m sũuri? Ad-y Soaal a Zezi yʋʋr yĩnga m sakda kũum Zerizalɛɛm tɩ b pa gomda bas tɩ b sẽb-m ye.»
44021014	D sẽn mik tɩ d gomda vɩʋʋgẽ d basame n kong n yetẽ: «Bɩ Wẽnd maan b sẽn date.»
44021015	Dẽ poore, d sẽn waa n segl n sɛ, d dʋ Zerizalɛɛm.
44021016	Sezare karen-biis n yãag-do. B tɩ kẽes-d la a Mnason zakẽ, Sɩpr daoa la al sɩngrẽ karen-biiga.
44021017	D sẽn ta Zerizalɛɛm la saam-biisa sẽn deeg-d ne sũ-noogo.
44021018	Daar ning sẽn pʋgã, a Pol tũ-d lame n kẽng a Zak yiri tɩ yaa be la nin-kẽemsa tigim taaba.
44021019	D sẽn pʋʋs taab n sɛ, a Pol sɩngame n wilgd bal-bale a tʋʋmda sẽn yɩ a soab ne Wẽnd sõngr bu-zẽmba sʋka.
44021020	B sẽn wʋme b pẽga Wẽnde. B yeelame: «Gese, m saam-biiga, yaa Zʋɩf rãmb tus ka tɛka n lebg karen-biisi n yaool n da yaa a Moyiiz Noora tũudb akɩka.
44021021	La b wʋmame tɩ b gomd tɩ sã n ya fo nengẽ wã, fo tusda Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn vɩb ne bu-zẽmbã tɩ b lak ne a Moyiiz, n sagend-b tɩ b ra le kẽes b kamb bãongo la b ra le tũ rog-n-mika ye.
44021022	Bõe la d na maane? Yaa vẽnega tɩ zãma na n sũu taab n wa. F waoonga ka tõe n ling b ye.
44021023	Maan d sẽn na n yeel-fã: Neb a naase n pʋlme n be ka.
44021024	Tall-ba n looge, tɩ naag-ba n yɩlg f menga la sõng-b ne ligd ning b sẽn na n kɩs n paam b zuta põngre. Woto neba fãa na bãng tɩ b sẽn leok bũmb ning f poorẽ wã, ka sɩd ye, b na bãng tɩ fo me vɩɩma yaa ned sẽn tũud Noora vɩɩm.
44021025	Sã n ya bu-zẽmba sẽn sak-b tẽebã, d taas-b-la sẽn be nin-kẽemsa sebr pʋga: vẽ-y ne maand nemd, ne zɩɩm, ne gɩfo, ne yoobo.»
44021026	Vẽkembeoogo, a Pol sɩd looga ne neb a naasã n na n naag bãmb n yɩlge. A kẽe wẽnd doogẽ wã n wilg sẽn ya daar ning la yɩlgra na n baase tɩ b tall b kũuna n wa.
44021027	Rasem a yopoe yɩlgra ra sɛɛme la bala. Zʋɩf rãmb sẽn yit Azi n yaool n wa yãend-a wẽnd doogẽ wã, n dãmb nebã tɩ b yõk-a,
44021028	la b kaasdẽ: «Israyɛl kamba waa-y tao, ad-y yaa nin-kãnga n saad n wilgd neba zĩig zãnga tɩ b ra tũ a Moyiiz noorã, la a saad n gomd beedo wẽnd do-kãnga poorẽ.»
44021029	Ad-y b ra reng n yãenda a Pol ne Efɛɛz rao, a Trofim, tɩ b tũud taaba tẽnga pʋga. Dẽ la b ra tagsd t'a peeg-a lame n kẽ wẽnd doogẽ wã.
44021030	Tẽnga fãa rãmbame tɩ neba zoet zĩig zãng n watẽ. B gãda a Pol n tall-a n yiis wẽnd doogẽ wã, n lɛɛg n pag kʋɩlemsã.
44021031	B ra baoodame n na n kʋ-a, la tãb-biis kobs-yoob tãnsoaba waa n wʋma me tɩ b moonẽ: «Zerizalɛɛm zũndga zãnga.»
44021032	Tãnsoab kãsenga yiisa tãb-biisi la tãnsoab-bi tɩ b na n kẽ zãma wã. Neba sẽn yãend tãb-biisa ne b tãnsoaben-dãmbã ka le saag n wẽ a Pol ye.
44021033	Tãnsoaben-dãmba kãsma kolgame n gãd a Pol n kɩt tɩ b sẽb-a ne bãeens a yiibu n yaool n sok-a a sẽn ya a soaba la a sẽn maan bũmb ninga.
44021034	La neba leoob ra ka tũud taab ye, kẽer t'a maana wãnda, kẽer t'a maana woto. Bʋʋra yĩnga tãnsoaba ka tõog n wʋm gomd tirg ye t'a yet tɩ b kẽes a Pol tãnsoben-dooga pʋga.
44021035	Sẽn ta rʋʋba zĩigẽ, b kong n põka a Pol, neba tusga yĩnga.
44021036	Neba ra pʋgda zembala, n maanẽ: «Bɩ b kʋ-a.»
44021037	B sẽn ta n na n kẽes-a roogã la a Pol sẽn yeel tãnsoabã: «Y tõe n kõ-m la sor tɩ m leok koɛɛg bɩ?» T'a lɛɛg n sok-a: «Fo gomda grɛk laa?
44021038	Dẽnd ka foo la Ezipt rao ning sẽn woole, daar nan ka zãre, so-gɩtb na ta tus a naas n kẽ we-raoogẽ wã wɛ?»
44021039	T'a Pol yeele: «Maam la a Pol, m yaa Zʋɩf, m doga Tars, Silisi tẽn-peelmẽ. M sẽn ya tẽng ning tẽnga biiga yʋʋr yiime. M kot-f lame tɩ f kõ-m sor tɩ m gome.»
44021040	A sẽn paam sore, a Pol yalsa teedsa zug, n zẽk a nug n kabs zãma wã. A kõ-b la koɛɛg ne Ebre rãmb goama:
44022001	«M Saam-biisi la m ba rãmba m kot-y la sor marsã n wĩnig m bʋʋma sẽn yɛs zĩig ninga.»
44022002	B sẽn wʋm tɩ yaa ne Ebre rãmb goam la a leokd bãmbã, bʋʋra wooga zãnga, t'a sɩnge:
44022003	«M yaa Zʋɩf. M doga Tars, Silisi tẽn-peelmẽ; m yaool wuba tẽn-kãnga la ya a Gamaliyɛl n zãms maam neere d yaab rãmba noora reegre la mam me ra pida ne Wẽnd nonglem wa yãmb sẽn pid rũnna wã.
44022004	M namsa so-paalga tũudba n tol n yãk yõore. M kɩtame tɩ b balg bãeense la b kẽes roogo pagb la rapa.
44022005	Rũnda maan-kʋʋd kãsengã la nin-kẽemsa fãa tara rẽ kaseto. M pʋs n da tɩ reega sɛb bãmb nengẽ Damas saam-biisa yĩnga tɩ m da rabd n na n tɩ sẽb So-palga rãmb n tall-b n wa Zerizalɛɛm tɩ b nams-ba.
44022006	M da rɩka sore n kolgd Damas, la vugr bala, wĩnto-sʋka, vẽenem kãseng n tãoos yĩngri n bui maam.
44022007	M lʋɩɩ tẽnga la m wʋma koɛɛg sẽn da yet ma: ‹Sol, Sol, bõe yĩng la f namsd maam?›
44022008	M leokame: ‹Yãmb yaa ãnda, Soaala?› Dẽ la b leok ma: ‹Yaa maam, Nazarɛt Zezi wã, la f sẽn namsdã.›
44022009	Sẽn da tũud-b maama yãenda vẽenema, la b ka wʋm sẽn da gomda ne maama soab koɛɛg ye.
44022010	M le sokame: ‹Bõe la m tog n maane, Soaala?› La Soaala yeel-m lame: ‹Yiki! Kẽ Damas. Beelẽ b na wilg-f f sẽn tog n maan bũmb ninga.›
44022011	La vẽenema sẽn kiis m nini tɩ m da ka le neẽ wã, m tũud-n-taasa nus la m gãd yã n kẽ Damas.
44022012	Ned n da be Damas n boond tɩ Anani. A ra tũuda Wẽnd wala noora sẽn date la tẽnga Zʋɩf rãmb da pẽgd-a lame.
44022013	Yẽnda n waa n yãend maam, la d sẽn pẽneg taaba, a yeel-m lame: ‹Sol, m saam-biiga, bɩ f nina puki.› La wakat kãng bala m tõog n yãend-a lame.
44022014	La ad-a sẽn yeele: ‹D yaab rãmba Wẽnnaam yãka foom n na n wilg foom b raabo, n wilg foom b Nin-sõngã tɩ f wʋm b koɛɛgã f toore.
44022015	Fo tog n yɩ-la b kaset soab dũni wã rãmb fãa taoore, f sẽn wʋm la f sẽn yãenda kaset soaba.
44022016	Bõe la d le gũud yɛsa? Aya! Reeg soobo, tẽ b Yʋʋrã tɩ f yel-wẽna fãa yẽese.›
44022017	M sẽn lɛɛg n wa Zerizalɛɛm, daar a yembre, m sẽn waa n be wẽnd doogẽ n pʋʋsdẽ, m yama fʋsga m yĩngã.
44022018	M yãenda Soaala, la ad-b sẽn yeel-ma: ‹Maan yãgbo, yi Zerizalɛɛm tao-tao, tɩ kaset ning f sẽn na n kõ maam beelẽ wã, b pa na n deeg-a ye.›
44022019	Mam leok-b lame: ‹Soaala, b yaool n mii neere tɩ m da saadame n yõgd n kẽesd doogo la m pãbd ne kaase sẽn da kẽed-b yãmbã.
44022020	B sẽn wa n daagd y kaset soaba, a Etiyɛn, zɩɩm, yɩla m nifẽ, a kʋʋba ra tata m yam la maam la a kʋʋdba ra gũnug b futu.›
44022021	Tɩ Soaala na n yeel-m marsã: ‹Looge; yaa yɩɩga, yaa bu-zẽmba nengẽ la m na n tʋm-fo.› »
44022022	B ra tara a Pol kelegre la a sẽn waa n pʋd bu-zẽmbã yʋʋre, b fãa sɩnga kaasgo: «Kʋ-y ned a woto buudu! A pa tog n vɩɩnd ye.»
44022023	Da yaa pãrbo, tɩ kẽer lobd b futu, tɩ kẽer fẽed tom yĩngri.
44022024	Tãnsoaba kɩtame tɩ b kẽes a Pol tãnsoben-dooga pʋga n pãb-a ne kaase, n paam n bãng a sẽn maan bũmb ning tɩ neba kaasd woto a zugu.
44022025	B sẽn waa n sẽba Pol ne gãn tagdo n na n pãb-a la a sẽn yeel tãnsoab bilã: «Yãmb tara sore n pãb ne kaase Rom tẽnga biiga, n pa reng bʋ a bʋʋdo?»
44022026	Tãnsoab bila sẽn wʋm dẽ, a tɩ yãenda a naabã n wilg-a woto: «Bõe la f na n maanẽ? Nin-kãnga yaa Rom tẽnga biiga.»
44022027	Tãnsoaba waa n soka a Pol: «Togs-ma, fo sɩd yaa Rom tẽnga biiga?» T'a Pol leok tɩ: N-yẽe!
44022028	Tɩ tãnsoaba yeele: «M yiisa ligd wʋsgo n na n paam n lebg Rom tẽnga biiga.» T'a Pol leok-a: «Sã n ya maam, m doga ne.»
44022029	Tao bala sẽn da na n pãb-bã tarame n leb poorẽ. Tãnsoaba meng ra maanda rabeem, a sẽn ne tɩ yaa Rom tẽnga biiga la a ra kɩt tɩ b balg ne yãndo.
44022030	Beoog sẽn vẽege, tãnsoaba tʋlg n bãnga bõe taale taki la Zʋɩf rãmba tʋk a Pol zugu. A kɩtame tɩ b lood a bãeensã la a yeel maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmba la bʋ-kaoodbã, tɩ b tigim. A waa ne a Pol marsã tɩ b na n kao-a bʋʋdo.
44023001	A Pol gesa bʋ-kaoodba pem n wa yeel-ba: «M saam-biisi m pelga m pʋg m tũ Wẽnde n tãag rũnna.»
44023002	Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga, a Anani, wẽneg n yeela sẽn naag-b yẽnda n kaood bʋʋdã tɩ b va a Pol noore.
44023003	Dẽ me la a Pol yeel-a: «Yaa Wẽnd meng n na n va foo, ninsaan-kazukma! F zaoo bʋʋda zĩigẽ n na n bʋ-m wala Noora sẽn date, n yaool n yet tɩ b pãb ma tɩ Noora yaool n ka kõt foo so-kãng ye.»
44023004	Bʋ-kaoodb a taaba yeel-a lame: «Foo n saag n tʋʋsd Wẽnd maan-kʋʋd kãsenga.»
44023005	T'a Pol na n leok-ba: «M da ka mi tɩ yaa maan-kʋʋd kãseng a ye. M mii sẽn gʋls sebr sõngẽ: da saag n kãab beedo, f buuda kãsem ye.»
44023006	A Pol da miime tɩ bʋ-kaoodba welga sags a yiibu: ad Farizẽ rãmba, ad Saduseẽ rãmba. Dẽ la a tãs bʋʋda rãmba: «M saam-biisi, mam yaa Farizẽ, la Farizẽ biiga. Yaa tõnd sẽn saagd bũmb ningã, yĩnsa vʋʋgre, yaa rẽnd yĩng la b kẽes maam bʋʋdo.»
44023007	A ka yãee n gom n baase la zabr sẽn yik Farizẽ la Saduseẽ rãmba sʋka la neba welga taab sags a yiibu.
44023008	Saduseẽ rãmba sɩd yetame tɩ yĩns ka vʋʋgde, tɩ malɛk ka be, tɩ sɩɩg ka be. Sã n ya Farizẽ rãmba bãmb tẽeda rẽ faa.
44023009	Dɩlla bʋʋda wulumda ne bʋʋre. Sɛb gʋlsdb kẽer da yaa Farizẽ rãmba. Bãmb n yik n tãs ne pãnga: «Tõnd ka ne nin-kãnga kongr ye. Tõe tɩ sɩɩg bɩ malɛk n gom ne a.»
44023010	Zabra wa n wɩngdame n paasdẽ, tãnsoaba zoe-la b na n wa taa a Pol n tõse, t'a kɩt tɩ tãb-biisa sig n wa yiis a Pol sʋka, n tall-a n leb tãnsoben-dooga pʋga.
44023011	Zĩig sẽn sobge, Soaala bʋʋga a Pol be n yeel-a: «Keng f sũuri! Wala f sẽn yɩ m kaset soab Zerizalɛɛm f togame n yɩ m kaset soab Rom tẽng me.»
44023012	Beoog sẽn vẽege, Zʋɩf rãmba le yẽsa ne taaba la b kãaba b meng beedo tɩ rɩɩb bɩ koom kõn kẽ b noorẽ tɩ b pa reng n kʋ a Pol ye.
44023013	La sẽn gom-b woto wã ra yɩɩda neb pis naase.
44023014	Bãmb n tɩ yeel maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmba la nin-kẽemsã: «Tõnd kãaba d meng beedo tɩ bũmb kõn kẽ d noorẽ tɩ d pa reng kʋ a Pol ye.
44023015	Sẽn ket marsã yaa yãmb ne bʋ-kaoodba zems taaba la y wilg tãnsoabã t'a tog n waa ne a Pol tɩ y maneg n ges a yella neere. Sã n ya tõndo d mi d sẽn na n maanega n kʋ-a t'a nan ka ta y sʋk ye.»
44023016	Biig n yaool n wʋm bẽdgã. Bi-kãng yaa a Pol tão biiga, la yẽ n babs a Pol n wɩdg-a.
44023017	A Pol me boola tãnsoab bil a ye n yeel-a woto: «Tall bi kãnga n taas y naaba t'a tara bũmb n na n togs-a.»
44023018	Tãnsoab bila tall-a lame n taas naabã n yetẽ: «B sẽn kẽes a soab roogã, a Pol, n bool maam n kos tɩ m tall bi-kãnga n wa y nengẽ tɩ bũmb la a rat n wilg yã.»
44023019	Tãnsoaba gãda biiga nug n yi kɛɛnga n sok-a: «Yaa bõe la f rat n togse?»
44023020	T'a leoke: «Zʋɩf rãmba sedame n na n kos-f tɩ b tall a Pol beoogo n wa bʋʋda zĩigẽ tɩ b rat n maneg n baoo yella nao.
44023021	Da tẽ-b ye. Ad bãmb na ta pisnaase n gũusd-a n na n yõke. B kãaba b meng beedo tɩ b kõn dɩ la b kõn yũ bũmb tɩ b pa reng n kʋ a Pol ye. Fãa sẽn gũud marsã, yaa fo ye n sake.»
44023022	Tãnsoaba basa biiga t'a looge; a yeel-a lame bala: «Da togs ned ba a ye tɩ f wɩdg-m la bũmb ye.»
44023023	Naaba boola tãnsoaben-dãmb a yiibu n yeel-ba: «Segl-y n dɩk sor yʋnga bala, neba sẽn wat n kẽed gõeem, yãmb ne tãb-biis kobsi, wed-dʋʋdb pisopoe la kãna rãmb kobsi.
44023024	Wa-y ne wiidi me, n zombg a Pol, n tall-a ne bãane n taas naab a Feligs.»
44023025	Woto la a ninga sebrẽ:
