44023026	«A Klod Liziyas n pʋʋsd na-kãseng a Feligs!
44023027	Zʋɩf rãmba yõka nin-kãnga n da rat n kʋ-a, la mam taa ne m tãb-biisi n fãag-a, m sẽn wʋm t'a yaa Rom tẽnga biiga.
44023028	M tʋlg n bãnga b sẽn dõt-a ne bũmb ninga n kos tɩ buuda bʋ a bʋʋdo.
44023029	M yãeeme tɩ yaa b Noora No-koɛɛm la b lʋɩɩs taoore la bũmb ka be sẽn sek a sẽbr meng tɩ b pa gomd a kʋʋb ye.
44023030	M waa n wʋmame tɩ b yẽsa ne taab n baood a kũum. Dẽ me la m tʋm-a yãmb nengẽ n yaool n wilga rõatba tɩ b sã n tar bũmb n na n dogl a zugu, bɩ yɩ yãmb taoore.»
44023031	Tãb-biisa reega noore n tall a Pol ne yʋngo n kẽng Antipatris.
44023032	Vẽkembeoogo b basa a Pol ne wiidi wã rãmba n lɛɛg n wa b tãnsoben-doogẽ.
44023033	Wiidi wã rãmb sẽn ta Sezare, b kɩsa sebra naabã la b wilg-a-la a Pol.
44023034	Naaba me karma sebrã la a sokame n bãng a Pol sẽn yit baobg ninga. La a sẽn bãng tɩ yaa Silisi la a yita, a yeel-a lame:
44023035	«M na bool-f bʋʋdo, f bʋʋd-n-taasa me sã n wa.» A kɩtame tɩ b pag a Pol a Erod sikẽ.
44024001	Rasem a nu soaba, maan-kʋʋd Kãseng a Anani waa ne nin-kẽems kẽere n paas bʋʋd mita, a Tertulus. Bãmb n wa naaba taoore n na n boola Pol bʋʋdo.
44024002	A Pol sẽn wa, a Tertulus goma woto n na wilg a Pol a zugẽ yelle: «Fo maasem yĩnga, nin-sõngo Feligs, d zamaana gãee ne laafi zãnga la fo sẽn wa ne f no-paalã, fo manega d tẽnga maneg sõngo
44024003	tɩ d kokd dẽ, d zãng gilli, la zĩis fãa, ne bark pʋʋsgo.
44024004	D sẽn pa rat-f ne yaamsã, m kotame tɩ f kelg d bilf bala ne d sẽn mi-f ne sũ-bʋgsem ningã.
44024005	Tõnd gesa a Pol n tɩge, a yaa sabaabo. A sẽn ta zĩig ning fãa dũni wã Zʋɩf rãmba ka le tar laafi ye. A yaa Zʋɩf rãmb sull a ye taoor soaba, Nazarɛt daoã sẽn yals sull ningã.
44024006	A makame meng n na n dẽgem tõnd wẽnd doogã, tɩ tõnd yõk-a. Tõnd tʋlgame n kao bʋʋdo wala d noora sẽn yalse, [
44024007	la a Liziyas waa n fãag-a la d nusẽ ne pãnga, la a yeela tõnd, a bʋʋd-n-taasã, tɩ d wa yãmb taoore,]
44024008	la a meng tõee n wilgame tɩ d sẽn leok bũmb ninga yaa sɩda.»
44024009	Zʋɩf rãmba gõmsame n wilg t'a leoka sɩda.
44024010	A Pol paama naaba sore n na n gome la a yeelame: «Ade, kaoosame marsã, Feligs, y sẽn zao y naama zaoorẽ tõnd zamaanẽ; dẽ me la m sũur ya kɛgenga, sẽn ya yãmb taoor la m na n gom n yiis m meng yellẽ wã.
44024011	Y tõe n dɩɩ kaseto tɩ m sẽn wa Zerizalɛɛm, Wẽnd waoogra yĩng nan ka loog rasem piig ye.
44024012	Ned ba a ye kõn tõog n yeele t'a yãend-m la wẽnd doogẽ, bɩ pʋʋsg roogẽ, bɩ tẽnga pʋga tɩ m wẽed no-koeemd bɩ m dãmbda tẽnga ye.
44024013	B sẽn yet tɩ m maana bũmb ningã, b pa tara kaset ye.
44024014	M sẽn tar n na n togs-y la woto: B sẽn boond a soab tɩ So-paalã ka bũmb a to n zʋʋg Wẽnd tũudem sor ye. Yaa woto la m waoogd m yaab rãmb Wẽndã, la m gãda sẽn be Noora pʋga la bãngdba sɛba pʋgẽ.
44024015	Mam saagda wa bãmb fãa sẽn saagdã tɩ nin-sõma la nin-wẽns na n vʋʋgame.
44024016	Yaa rẽnd yĩng la m maood wakat buud fãa n na n yɩ ned sẽn ka tar rẽko, Wẽnd la ninsaalb taoore.
44024017	Maana yʋʋma tɩ m yaool n na n lɛɛg n wa Zerizalɛɛm n kɩs saam-biisã sẽn lob buuda yĩnga la m waoog Wẽnd ne m kũuni.
44024018	Yaa woto la b yãend-m wẽnd doogẽ. M wa n yɩlga m menga la tus taab ka zĩndi, bʋʋr ka zĩndi.
44024019	Yaẽ la Zʋɩf rãmb kẽer sẽn yi Azi, sãooẽ lame. Bãmb n da togẽ n bool m bʋʋdo yãmb taoore, b sã n da tarẽ la bũmb n na n dogl m zugu.
44024020	Sã n yaa m sẽn yɛs b rãmb taoorã, b kolg n togs b sẽn yãend-m ne yell ninga bãmb meng bʋʋd kãsenga roogẽ.
44024021	M ka ne bũmb n zʋʋg m sẽn moon b taoore tɩ yaa m sẽn gomd kũum vʋʋgra yelle la b bʋʋd-m dũnna.»
44024022	A Feligs ra mii So-paala yɛla neere, dẽ la a kʋʋg koɛɛga n yetẽ: «Tãnsoab a Liziyas sã n wa d na baas bʋʋdã.»
44024023	A yeela tãnsoaba t'a kell n bas a Pol roogo, la a ra yɩ toaag ne a ye, a bas a buuda neb tɩ b sõangd-a.
44024024	Sẽn maan dasem a wãna, a Feligs lɛɛg n waa ne a pag a Drusil. Da yaa Zʋɩf poaka. A kɩtame t'a Pol wa la a kelga a sẽn gomd a Zezi Krista tẽeba yell toto.
44024025	A Feligs sẽn mik t'a gomda sõmblem yelle, tõog-m-meng yelle, yaoolem bʋʋda yelle, a yɛɛsame la a yeel-a lame: «F tõe n leba f roogẽ dũnna, la m sẽn paam daar ninga m na le bool fo.»
44024026	A ra tẽedame t'a Pol na n kõ-a la ligdi; la bool a Pol t'a wa tɩ b sõsa waa n lebga pẽdgem-pẽdgem.
44024027	A Pol dooga waa n looga yʋʋm a yiibã ta ra ket be. A Feligs bas-a-la roogo n na n noog Zʋɩf rãmba sũuri. A Porsiyus Festus n waa n led a zĩiga.
44025001	A Festus sẽn ta Sezare tɩ rabitẽ, a yii n tuda Zerizalɛɛm.
44025002	A sẽn ta la maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmba la tẽnga nin-bɛdã sẽn yeel tɩ b boonda a Pol bʋʋdo yẽnda taoore. B sẽn wilg b raabã,
44025003	b kos-a lame wala bũmb sẽn na n yãng b zooda ne taaba, t'a sõng t'a Pol lɛɛg n wa Zerizalɛɛm. Ra yaa bẽdgo la b gãneg yã n na n paam-a n kʋ sorẽ.
44025004	A Festus leok-b lame t'a Pol tog n paa Sezare la yaa be la yẽ meng lebd mars-marsã.
44025005	A paasame: «Neb niyns sẽn tõe n kao bʋʋdo n be yãmb sʋka, wa tɩ d loog. B sã n yet tɩ yell be a zugu, b na bool-a bʋʋd Sezare.»
44025006	A Festus maana dasem a nii bɩ piig bala n yaool n leb Sezare. A sẽn vẽeg beoogo, a kẽe bʋʋda zĩigẽ la a kɩtame tɩ b bool a Pol.
44025007	A sẽn wa, Zʋɩf niyns sẽn yi-b Zerizalɛɛma gũbg-a lame n dogend a zugu, yɛl sẽn waooge la sẽn ya tagdo, b mens sẽn ka tar kaset t'a sɩd maaname ye.
44025008	A Pol da kɩɩsdame n yetẽ: «M ka ne m sẽn tõdg Zʋɩf rãmba noor ne bũmb ning ye, m ka paoog wẽnd doogã, m ka paoog Rom naaba ye.»
44025009	A Festus tʋlgame n noog Zʋɩf rãmba sũuri n leok a Pol woto: «Fo ratame n leb Zerizalɛɛm tɩ b kao rẽ fãa bʋʋd mam taoor bɩ?»
44025010	T'a Pol yeele: «Yaa Rom naaba bʋʋd la b na n bʋ maam; dẽn yĩnga yaa ka, pa Zerizalɛɛm ye. M ka maan bũmb sẽn wa ne Zʋɩf rãmba bõne, la y meng mii rẽ neere.
44025011	M sã n sɩd kongame, m sã n maana bũmb sẽn tog ne kũum, m saka kũum. La nin-bãmba sẽn togsda sã n ka sɩda, ned ka be sẽn tõe n dɩk maam n bas b nugẽ ye. Bɩ m bʋʋda yɩ Rom naab taoore!»
44025012	A Festus yãenda a sagendbã n yaool n yeel a Pol: «Ka Rom naab taoor la f rat tɩ b bʋ-f laa? Bʋʋda na yɩ Rom.»
44025013	Sẽn maan dasem a wãna, dĩma Agripa waa Sezare ne a paga, a Berenis, la a tɩ pʋʋsa a Festus.
44025014	A Festus sẽn paam tɩ dĩma kaoosd Sezare, a goma ne-a, a Pol yell woto: «Ned la a Festus bas bi-bees roogẽ ka.
44025015	M sẽn waa n be Zerizalɛɛm, maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb la nin-kẽemsã wilg-m lame t'a beegame la b kota a bʋʋd paalgre.
44025016	M wilg-b lame tɩ Rom dãmb ka minim n basd ned a bɛɛb nusẽ tɩ b ka reng n bool-a bʋʋdo, a bʋʋd-n-taasa taoore t'a gom n paam n yiis a meng yellẽ ye.
44025017	B tũu maam n wa ka, la m pa kaoos ye, vẽkẽmbeoog bala, m kẽ-la m bʋʋd doogẽ la m kɩtame ti b wa ne a Pol.
44025018	A sẽn ta a bʋʋd-n-taasa taoore, b pa saag n dogl a zugu, yell sẽn ya bedre wa ned fãa sẽn da tõe n tags ye.
44025019	B sẽn da tar ne a Pol yaa kɩɩs taaba b Wẽnda tũudem poorẽ, la sẽn yɩɩda, yaa nin-yend sẽn ki poorẽ t'a Pol wẽend t'a ket n vɩɩme, ya a Zezi poorẽ,
44025020	M da ka mi m sẽn na n maan yell a woto poorẽ ye. Dẽ la m wilg-a t'a leb Zerizalɛɛm tɩ bʋʋda tɩ kao be.
44025021	A Pol kosame t'a bʋʋda kao Rom na kãsenga taoore, dẽ la m yeel tɩ m na n kell n bas-a la roogo n ta wakat ning m sẽn na n taas-a Rom naaba.»
44025022	A Agripa yeela a Festus: «M me nongẽ lame n kelg nin-kãnga.» T'a yeele: «Beoogo f na kelg-a.»
44025023	Vẽkembeoogo a Agripa ne a paga ninga b fan teedo n wa bʋʋda roogẽ. Tãnsoaben-dãmba la tẽnga taoor dãmba tũume. A Festus kɩtame tɩ b wa ne a Pol,
44025024	la a yeelame: «Dĩma Agripa la yãmb fãa sẽn naag tõnd n zĩ ka, woto la rao ning Zʋɩf rãmba sẽn waa n kos-m ne bʋ-raase, Zerizalɛɛm wala kaalẽ menga, tɩ m da bas-a t'a vɩɩnd ne yõor ye.
44025025	Sã n ya maam sẽn gesã, m pa ne a sẽn maan bũmb ning tɩ sek a kʋʋb ye. La yẽ meng sẽn yeel tɩ b kao a bʋʋdã Rom tẽnga, m sakame n na n tʋm-a be.
44025026	M ka tar yell tik n na n gʋls Rom naab a poorẽ ye. Yaa rẽn yĩng la m wa ne a yãmb taoore, dĩma Agripa. A sẽn na n leok bũmb ning ka wã m na paam dẽ n gʋlse.
44025027	M ka rat n maan yalemdo n tʋm al Rom tẽnga, ned sẽn kẽ roogo, n pa naag n togs a sẽn maan bũmb ning tɩ ya wẽng ye.»
44026001	A Agripa yeela a Pol: «Fo tara sor n gom n yiis f meng yellẽ.» A Pol sẽn kabs nebã ne a nugu a sɩngame:
44026002	«M yetame tɩ m zug yaa noogo, dĩma Agripa, m sẽn paam n na n dok m zugẽ yella yãmb taoore.
44026003	M zu-noogã, yaa y sẽn mi Zʋɩf rãmba rog-n-mik la b no-koɛɛma. Dẽ me la m kot tɩ y bʋk y sũuri n kelg-ma.
44026004	Zʋɩf rãmba fãa tara m vɩɩma buka, m sẽn dog tɛk n tãag rũnna. B mii m vɩɩm sẽn yɩ a soab Zerizalɛɛm, m buuda sʋka.
44026005	B sẽn mi-m al daar zãrã, b tõeeme n kõ kaseto tɩ m vɩɩma yɩɩ Farizẽ vɩɩm, neb sẽn tũud Wẽnd ne b sũur zãnga.
44026006	B sẽn bool-m bʋʋd dũnna mengã, yaa m sẽn saagd tɩ Wẽnd na n pidsa b sẽn pʋlem d yaab rãmba.
44026007	Pʋlem noog kãng pidsgu la buuda sags piig la a yiiba sɩd gũud, wĩndg la yʋngo. Dɩlla ya m saagra yĩnga, dĩma Agripa, la Zʋɩf rãmba bool-m bʋʋdo.
44026008	Bõe la yãmb neb kẽer yet tɩ b kõn deeg bada tɩ Wẽnd na n vʋʋga kɩɩmsã?
44026009	M da waa n yeelame tɩ m na n maana m sẽn tõe n zab ne Nazarɛt dao, a Zezi, sora rãmba.
44026010	La sɩd yaa rẽ la m maan Zerizalɛɛm la mam meng m tore kẽesa nin-sõma wʋsg roogo, la yaa maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb n da kõ-m sore. B sẽn waa n kʋʋd-ba m da kõta kaseto tɩ m saka b kʋʋbo.
44026011	Naoor wʋsgo yaa pʋʋsga rotẽ la m da kẽeda, n na n modg-b ne kalwaas tɩ b tʋʋs Wẽnde, la m sũura sẽn yik yĩnga, m mii n babs-b la tẽn-zãorgẽ fãa.
44026012	Yaa woto la m paam maan-kʋʋdba kãsem-dãmb sɛba la b noore n kẽng Damas.
44026013	Sor zugu, wĩnto-sʋka, m dĩm sõngo, m yãenda vẽenem sẽn yɩɩd wĩntoog rẽnna sẽn yi yĩngri n wa bui maam ne m tũud-n-taasã.
44026014	D fãa gill lʋɩɩ tẽnga la m wʋma koɛɛg sẽn leok-m ne Ebre: ‹Sol, Sol, yaa bõe tɩ f namsd maam? Da zãgs n bao toog n paas toog ye.›
44026015	Tɩ mam leoke: ‹Yãmb yaa ãnda, m Soaala?› La Soaala yeelame: ‹Yaa maam a Zezi la f sẽn namsdã.
44026016	La yik n yals yĩngri. M sẽn lik-fa võor la woto: m datame tɩ f yɩ m sõgne la f kõ f sẽn yãend-m dũnna la f sẽn na n yãend-m beooga kaseto.
44026017	La yaa rẽnd me yĩnga la m na n fãag-f ne f buudã la ne bu-zẽmbã, m sẽn tʋmd foom b rãmb nengẽ.
44026018	M tʋmd-f lame tɩ f tɩ puk b nini, tɩ b yi b likẽ n wa vẽenemẽ; n yi Sʋtãan soolmẽ n kẽ Wẽnd dẽnnẽ, la b paam, b sẽn na n sak n tẽ maama yĩnga, b yel-wẽna sugri la nin-sõma wã pʋɩɩre.›
44026019	Sẽn yɩ woto wã, dĩma Agripa, m pa kɩɩs m sẽn wʋm ne yĩngr likra ye.
44026020	M pa zãgs ye: yaa Damas woo, yaa Zerizalɛɛm woo, yaa Zɩɩde bɩ bu-zẽmba tẽng woo, m mooname tɩ d tog n tedga zʋgo, n lɛɛg n kẽ d Wẽnde la d tʋm zʋg tekr tʋʋma.
44026021	Yaa rẽnd yĩng la Zʋɩf rãmba yõk-m wẽnd doogẽ n baood n na n kʋ-m.
44026022	Wẽnd sẽn sõng-m yĩnga, m talla Koɛɛga moonego n tãag rũnna, nin-bɛd wala nin-bõones taoore. M pa tẽed tɩ m paasa bõn-zɛreng meng sẽn ka be a Moyiiz la bãngdba sebrẽ ye. Sɛba yeta woto:
44026023	Krista na n namsame. Bãmb n na n vʋʋg pipi kɩɩms sʋka la bãmb Koɛɛgã n na n wa ne vẽenem a Israyɛl la bu-zẽmba yĩnga.»
44026024	A Pol taa zĩ kãngã t'a Festus zẽk a koɛɛg n yeele: «Pol, fo yika gãeemdo, f bãngr pidunga lebga f zugu.»
44026025	T'a Pol na n leoke: «Ad-y m pa gãeemd ye, nin-songa Festus, m goama yaa ned sẽn so a menga la sẽn baood sɩd goama.
44026026	La m sẽn gomd ne rĩm ninga tɩ m sũur pa kiuusdẽ wã zoe n mii yɛla fãa; bũmb ka be a sẽn ka vẽen ne ye, yaa vẽenemẽ la yɛla maan yã, ka maan pẽkẽ la likẽ ye!
44026027	Yãmb tẽeda bãngdba bɩ, dĩma Agripa? La m neeme tɩ y tẽedame.»
44026028	Dẽ la dĩma Agripa leok a Pol: «Kellẽ la bilf bala tɩ f kɩt tɩ b gesẽ maam wa Kristneda!»
44026029	T'a Pol yeele: «Kella bilf bɩ wʋsgo, Wẽnd na sõng dĩma Agripa la yãmb fãa sẽn kelgb maam dũnna wã, tɩ y wa lebg m sẽn yaa soabã, m bãeensa toog sẽn yãke.»
44026030	Dĩma yikame t'a Festus ne a Berenis la sẽn da zĩ-ba fãa me yiki.
44026031	B waa n yitame la b goamda: «Nin-kãnga ka maan bũmb sẽn tog tɩ b balga bɩ n kʋ-a ye.»
44026032	Dẽ la a Agripa yeel a Festus: «D da tõe n basẽ la nin-kãnga a sã n da ka kosẽ t'a bʋʋda kaoẽ Rom naaba taoore.»
44027001	Itali loogr raar sẽn yãke, b basa a Pol ne bi-bees kẽere, tãnsoab a ye nugẽ. Tãnsoaba ra boondame t'a Zuliyus, tɩ b tãnsoben-dooga boond tɩ Ogusta.
44027002	D kẽe koglg sẽn yi Adramisiom, n looge. Koglga da rabda Azi sẽnẽ. Masedoan dao a ye sẽn da kẽed Tesalonik n da naag tõndo.
44027003	Vẽkembeoogo d taa Sidõ t'a Zuliyus maan wa ninsaal sẽn mi a to waoogre n bas a Pol t'a sig n kaag a zo-rãmbã la a reeg b sõngre.
44027004	D sẽn yi be, d yega Sɩpr, sobga sẽn da wẽed lebend yĩnga.
44027005	D sẽn kẽn n loog Silisi la Pãnfili, dasem piig la a nu raare, d taa Mir sẽn be Lisi baobgo.
44027006	Tãnsoaba paama Aleksãndri koglg sẽn digd Itali la a kẽesd-d-la a pʋgẽ.
44027007	Maana rasem a wãna, kẽnda ra ka fɩɩd ye la tũu toogo tɩ d ta Knid. Sobga sẽn da ya lebend yĩnga d kong n yega Krɛt n tees Salmone.
44027008	D sẽn paam n yõsg be d ta zĩig a ye koom koglg sẽn tõe n tɩlg sobgo. Zĩ-kãng boondame tɩ Soondg zĩ-neeba la a ra pẽe ne Lasayia tẽnga.
44027009	Waa n kaoosa bilfu la kooma zug kẽnd waa n lebga rabeem. Sugr kosg no-loeera meng da zoe n lokame. A Pol da rat n wilga rẽnna n gom woto:
44027010	«M zo-rãmba, m neeme tɩ mogra rʋʋgr marsã tõe n waa ne sãoongo la bõne: koglga bõne, a zɩɩba bõne la tõnd mens bõne.»
44027011	Tãnsoaba ra kelgda koglga soaba la koglga rugsda n yɩɩd a Pol.
44027012	Koglga me tõog n paa a sẽn yɛs zĩig ninga yaa toogo, tɩ sobga yikda waood wẽnde. Woto wã b yeelame tɩ b na n makame n ta Fenigs n soond waooda be. Fenigs bee Krɛt tẽn-peelmẽ la kogenda soondg zĩig gõdg n teesa nin-taoore.
44027013	Sob-bil n waa n yik n fʋʋsd nug rɩtgo tɩ b tags tɩ b raaba tõe n pidsame. Woto b sɩnga kẽnde n yegd Krɛt tẽnga.
44027014	La ade, ka yãee n kaoose, nug goabg sob-raoog sẽn boond ti «Erakilõ» wẽneg n yikame.
44027015	Sobga fãaga koglgã a soaalba nusẽ tɩ d na n kong n tũ a raabo.
44027016	Tẽmbil sẽn puk koomẽ n boond tɩ Koda wa n wooga sobga pãnga tɩ d na n tõog n yiis koglg bilã.
44027017	D sẽn yiis koglg bila d maana d sẽn tõe fãa. D sẽba koglga sʋk ne wĩ la d loe ra-peg-yaleng a poorẽ n sõngd-a t'a ra lis ye, tɩ d da zoeta a na n wa tɩ pa Sirt sẽnẽ. Kẽnda yẽ lebga sobg sẽn teesẽ.
44027018	Beoog sẽn vẽege, d yãeeme tɩ sobga ket n yaa wʋsgo tɩ d sɩng teeda woogre.
44027019	Dasem sẽn maan a tãabo, koglga rãmb mens b toor n yogs wĩ wã la pɛɛlã.
44027020	Maana rasem a wãn tɩ b pa yãend wĩntoog la ãdg vẽenem ye. Sobga ra ket n fʋʋsda ne pãnga tɩ d yɛɛsdẽ la d pa le tẽed põasg ye.
44027021	D sẽn da paam n dɩ meng ra vẽsgame dẽ la a Pol yik n yaas b sʋka n yeele: «Y ra tog n kelg-m lame, m zo-rãmba, n da yiẽ Krɛt ye. Sãong la bõne kõn n zĩnnẽ ye.
44027022	La ba sẽn na n yɩ a soaba, m kotame tɩ y ra maan dabeem ye, tɩ yãmb ned ba a ye vɩɩm kõn tõsg ye, koglga bal n na n yɩ bõne.
44027023	Yʋngẽ bala Wẽnd ning m sẽn kẽ la m sẽn waoogd a soaba malɛk lika maam
44027024	la a yeel-m lame: ‹Da maan dabeem ye, Pol, ya tɩlɛ tɩ f bʋʋda kao Rom naaba taoore la fo yĩnga m basda ne vɩɩm sẽn be-b koglga pʋg ne fooma.›
44027025	Dɩlla, m zo-rãmba, keng-y y sũuri! M saagdame tɩ Wẽnd na n maana wala b sẽn togs-ma.
44027026	La tɩɩm ka be tɩ d ka pa tẽng a ye sẽn puk koomẽ ye.»
44027027	Wã n da tõkd d dasem piig la a naase, d sẽn be Adriatik mogra zug n lengdẽ. Yʋn-sʋka, ko-rugsdba bãngame tɩ d kolga tẽn koɛɛnga.
44027028	B sẽn mak kooma zulum b mikame tɩ yaa kãntɩɩs koabga; b sẽn ta taoor bilfu n le make, b paama kãntɩɩs pisopoe la a nu.
44027029	B zoe rabeem tɩ d na n wa teem sore n tɩ kẽ pĩisã, tɩ b lob ra-peg-yalens a naase, poorẽ, la b kot ne b sũur fãa, tɩ sõora puki.
44027030	Ko-rugsdba ra baoodame n na n zoe n loog. Dẽ la b ra baood n na n sik koglg bila koomẽ la b ra yagdame tɩ baood n na n gãda taoor da-peg-yalemsa tɩ koglga rɩk so-yɛnga la a ra le kẽn yaar ye.
44027031	A Pol yeela tãnsoabã la tãb-biisã: «Bãmba sã n ka pa koglga pʋga, y kõn põs ye.»
44027032	Woto wã tãb-biisa kʋʋsa koglg bila wĩ n bas-a t'a loog.
44027033	B ra gũuda sõora yẽegre la a Pol da sagend-b lame tɩ b bao rɩɩbo. A ra yetame: «Yaa rasem piig la a naas rũnna la y zĩi n gũudẽ, n pa rɩtẽ ye.
44027034	M sagend-y lame tɩ y bao rɩɩb n dɩ, tɩ ka rẽ y kõn põs ye. M le togsd-y lame yɛsa, yãmb sʋka, ned ba a ye zug zoobg kõn menem ye.»
44027035	A Pol sẽn gom woto, a rɩka buri, n pẽg Wẽnd b fãa taoore, n kaoog burã n sɩng wãbre.
44027036	Raood le kẽe nebã tɩ b fãa bao rɩɩb n dɩ.
44027037	Tõnd neb kobsi la pisopoe la a yoob n da be koglga pʋga.
44027038	Rɩɩba sẽn paam n dɩ, b bao koglga na lebg faasga n yiisd koodã n lobd koomẽ.
44027039	Zĩig sẽn yẽege, ko-rugsdba ra ka mi b sẽn beẽ ye. B ra nee mogra sẽn wõg n kẽ la sẽn gãneg bĩsri tɩ d da rat n tus koglgã n taas be, sã n tõe.
44027040	B looda ra-peg-yalemsã n bas koomẽ. B yolsa koglga wẽnemdega wĩ; b rʋʋsa taoor peend bilfã tɩ sobga tõog n tus koglgã n kolg kooma noorẽ, bĩsrã sẽn samẽ wã.
44027041	B taa zĩig a ye la b suda bĩisrẽ tɩ koglga wa gimb zãnga, a poorẽ, tɩ ko-wiisa pãb a taoorã n wesge.
44027042	Tãb-biisa sedame n na n kʋ bi-beesã tɩ b ra wa rug kooma n loog ye.
44027043	Tãnsoaba da rat n basa a Pol ne yõore, woto wã, a pa sak ye. Yẽ meng n kõ noor tɩ sẽn mi-b koom deng n looge n paam tẽn-koɛɛnga.
44027044	Sẽn ka mi-b kooma marsã na yi ne ra-pegdo bɩ ne bũmb ning fãa sẽn yi koglga pʋga. La yɩɩ woto la b fãa paam n ta tẽn-koɛɛnga tɩ bũmb ka maan-b ye.
44028001	D sẽn paam n põsa la d yaool n bãng tɩ tẽnga boondame tɩ Malt.
44028002	Tẽnga rãmb gesa d yell neere. Saag sẽn ni la sẽn ya waood yĩnga, b yõgna bugum la bugma waolgẽ la b reeg-do.
44028003	A Pol waa n wolga ribli n na n lob n yãng bugma. Bugma waolg yiisa põeere sẽn vil a Pol nug n wẽneg n be a kɛɛbẽ.
44028004	Tẽnga rãmb sẽn yãend waafã a nugẽ, b yeela taaba: «Yaa vẽnega, nin-kãnga yaa nin-kʋʋda; a paam n põsa mogra koom mars-marsã, tɩ Wẽnd ket n data vɩɩm n na n dok b sũuri.»
44028005	La a Pol mesga põeera bugmẽ. Bũmb ka tol n maan a Pol ye.
44028006	Neba yẽ ra tẽedame t'a nuga na n fɩɩgame t'a lʋɩ n kell n be kũum. B sẽn gũ n kaoos tɩ bũmb ka maan-a wã, b teema goama n yet tɩ nin-kãnga yaa wẽnde.
44028007	Tẽnga kãsem da boondame tɩ Publiyus. A da tara pʋʋgo. Nin-kãng n deeg tõnd n kõ-d doog da-yɩten-daare.
44028008	Segame t'a Publiyus ba ra gãee ne weoogo la ne sãb-noodre. A Pol tɩ pʋʋs-a la tarem, n yõk Wẽnd sɛɛg a yĩnga, a tẽega a nus a zugu, n sãoog-a zãnga.
44028009	Dẽ yĩng la tẽnga bãad-dãmb a taaba me wayã, la bãmb me sãoogame.
44028010	D paama waoogr buud fãa tẽnga rãmb nengẽ la d loogra sẽn waa n ta, b sõng-d la ne sor dɩɩbo.
44028011	Sẽn maan kiuus a tãabo, d paamame n kẽ koglg a to, sẽn yit Aleksãndri, la koglga gũudb yaa wẽnd-bi, a Kastor la a Polugs.
44028012	D sẽn ta Sirakuz, d paa be da-yɩten-daare.
44028013	D yii be n yegd kʋɩl kogrã n ta Reziom. Daar ninga sẽn pʋgã, sobg fʋʋsa nug rɩtgo; woto, d da-yɩten-daare, d taa Puzol.
44028014	D yãenda saam-biis be. La d zug yɩɩ noog tɩ d pa ne b rasem a yopoe. D sẽn yi be d kẽe Rom.
44028015	Beelẽ saam-biisa sẽn wʋm d waoongo, b waa n seg-d la a Apiyus raaga, zĩig ning sẽn pʋd tɩ Rã-rot-a-tã. A Pol sẽn yãend-ba, a pʋʋsa Wẽnd bark wʋsgo la a sũur le kengame.
44028016	Tõnd sẽn ta Rom, a Pol paama sore n na n zĩnd a sẽn datẽ, tãb-biig ning sẽn be ne a wã yee n da zãag ye.
44028017	Sẽn maan dasem a tãabo a Pol kosa Zʋɩf rãmba tɩ b seg taaba. B sẽn tigim taaba, a yeelame: «B yõk-m la Zerizalɛɛm n kɩs Rom dãmba tɩ m yaool n da ka beeg buudu la m ka tõdg d yaab rãmba dog-n-mik ye.
44028018	Rom dãmba sẽn sok n tɩge, b da rat n bas-m lame, tɩ b pa yãend bũmb sẽn sek m kʋʋb ye.
44028019	Zʋɩf rãmba yeelame tɩ rẽ ka tõe ye, dẽ la mam me gãd tɩ m bʋʋda kõn kao zĩig a to tɩ ka Rom naaba taoor ye. La rẽ ka rat n yeel tɩ m ningda m saam-biisa taal ye.
44028020	Ya rẽ yĩng la m tʋlg n seg-y la m taas-y m koɛɛga; bãng-y tɩ yaa Israyɛl sẽn saagd bũmb ninga poorẽ la m sog ne yãndo, n yɛsẽ.»
44028021	Zʋɩf rãmba leoka a Pol: «Sã n ya tõndo d ka paam Zɩɩde rãmb sebre la saam-biisa me sẽn yi be n wa wã ka leok bũmb f poorẽ sẽn ya wẽng ye.
44028022	D datame tɩ fo meng togs-d sẽn be f sũurẽ tɩ sã n ya So-paalã, yaa zĩig zãng la b kɩɩsda.»
44028023	B kõo taab raare n wa wʋsgo a Pol sikẽ wã. A goma ne ba Wẽnd Rĩunga yelle la a togsa bũmb ning fãa sẽn gʋls a Zezi poorẽ, a Moyiiz Noora sebrẽ la bãngdba me rẽnnẽ. La yɩɩ raara zãnga, yibeoog n ta zaabre.
44028024	Kẽer deega a goama, kẽer me zãgsame.
44028025	B ra waa n sẽegdame la b tar b no-koɛɛma t'a Pol leok-b woto: «Yaa sɩd bala la a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn togs y yaab rãmba ne bãngda Izayi noore:
44028026	‹Tɩ yãend buudã la f yeel-a: Y nong bɩ y kelge, y kõn wʋm fɩ y nong bɩ y gese, y kõn yãend fɩ.
44028027	Buud kãnga yama sobame, b tʋb pagame, b nin mumame, la yaa sẽn na yɩlẽ tɩ b nin da yãend ye la b tʋb da wʋm ye la b yam da vẽneg ye, la b ra teem zʋg ye. B ra tẽ tɩ b bãaga na sãoog koe!›
44028028	Bɩ y bãng tɩ fãagrã yaa bu-zẽmba la Wẽnd tool yã. Bãmb yẽ sẽ na kelge.» [
44028029	A Pol sẽn gom n sɛ, Zʋɩf rãmba me loogame la b tar no-koɛɛm ne taaba.]
44028030	Yaa yʋʋm a yi para la a Pol paa a sẽn sig zak ningã. A ra sõsda ne neb niyns fãa sẽn da wat-b a nengẽ.
44028031	A ra gomda Wẽnd Rĩunga yelle la Soaala Zezi Krista yelle. A ra gomda a yam la a ka yãend gɩdgr ye.
45001001	Maam, a Pol, n pʋʋsde; maam la Krist a Zezi sõgne, bãmb Tʋʋm-tʋmda, Wẽnd sẽn bool la b welg toore Koe-nooga mooneg yĩnga.
45001002	Koe-noog kãnga la sẽn da kãab al-pĩnd pĩnd ne bãngdba noor tɩ be Sebr sõng pʋgẽ.
45001003	Kãabga kãaba b Biiga poorẽ, biig ning sẽn yit a Daviid buudẽ sã n ya ne tẽng zug rogma,
45001004	n yaool n ya Wẽnd bi-roaka, rogm a to wã pʋgẽ, tɩ Sõmblem Vʋʋsma puk rẽ ne kaset sẽn tar pãnga, ne b vʋʋgr kɩɩms sʋka, bãmb la a Zezi Krista tõnd Soaalã.
45001005	Tũu ne bãmba tɩ d paam n lebg b tʋʋm-tʋmdã n na n moon la d bao b yʋʋra pẽgre, n wilg tɩ tẽeba yaa bũmb sẽn pake, la d taas-a bu-zẽmba fãa,
45001006	la d taas-a yãmba, tɩ y me paama a Zezi Krista boolle.
45001007	Bɩ Wẽnd kom-nongdsã sẽn be Rom tẽnga, Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb sõmblem welgrã paam kũun buud fãa la laafi, d Ba a Wẽnd la d Soaala Zezi Krista maasem yĩnga.
45001008	M na n deng n kudga Krista a Zezi kãntɩɩga tɩ b pʋʋs Wẽnd bark y yĩnga tɩ mooga tõr kilsda y tẽebo.
45001009	M sẽn waoogd Wẽnd ning m yamẽ la m moond b Biiga Koe-noogã, bãmb meng n ya m kaseto, tɩ m tẽegda y yelle wakat buud fãa,
45001010	la m kota m pʋʋsg pʋʋgẽ, n wa paam vɩʋʋg n ta y nengẽ, bãmb sã n data.
45001011	M rata ne m sũur fãa n yãend yã n paam n kõ-y ye Wẽnd kũun bilfu tɩ y tẽeba sĩdi,
45001012	la sẽn yɩɩda, m datame n le paas m daood yãmb nengẽ la yãmb sɛɛgẽ tɩ d fãa paam n gãda tẽeb a ye, yãmb wala maam.
45001013	M saam-biisi, m ka rat n solg yã tɩ yaa naoor yak la m tʋlg n wa y sʋka – la gɩdgr n zĩnd n ta marsã, – m saagdame tɩ yãmb me nengẽ m na paam bũmb sẽn be yõodo wala m sẽn paam bu-zẽmb a taaba nengẽ.
45001014	M tog n tʋma Grɛk rãmb yĩnga wa wetẽ dãmba yĩnga, zolg yĩng wa mit yĩnga.
45001015	Dẽ me yĩng la m data, Rom dãmba, n wa taas yãmb me Koe-noogã.
45001016	Yãnd ka tar-m ne Wẽnd Koe-nooga ye, a yaa Wẽnd pãnga n fãagd ned ning fãa sẽn tar-a tẽebo, Zʋɩf pipi tɩ sẽn ka a Zʋɩf yaool n pʋgda.
45001017	Koe-nooga kɩtdame tɩ tẽeb tũud tẽeb n pukd Wẽnd sõmblem wala sẽn gʋlse: Tẽeb n na n dɩlg nin-sõng vɩɩm.
45001018	Wẽnnaam beema sẽn sigd a soab zugu, yaa wẽn-kɩɩsa, sẽn nong-a wẽnga la sẽn baood-a zãmb loɛɛg n loe sɩda.
45001019	Wẽnnaam beelma kaset yaa vẽeneg ne-ba. Wẽnd ka solg-b fɩ.
45001020	Bũmb ning sẽn be Wẽnd nengẽ n solg al dũni sɩngrẽ, ninsaal tõe n yãend-a la ne a yam tɩ Wẽnd tʋʋma n pukd b pãnga la b wẽndlem, al tɩ f sã n yeel marsã tɩ f ka ne, yaa fo yelle.
45001021	Ad-y yaa b sẽn bãng Wẽnd sẽn ya a soaba la b ka pẽg-bã, la b ka pʋʋs-b barka wala sẽn segdã, ad-y yaa rẽ la b yam kɩdga sob zãnga.
45001022	B sẽn yeel tɩ b baooda bãngr zulunga yaa gãeemd la b paam yã.
45001023	Woto b rɩka Wẽnnaam ne b zɩɩrã la b sõmblema sẽn ka tɛkã, m mams-b ne bõn-yaals wẽnego, n tol n kõ Wẽnd sẽn ka kiidã ninsaal, luiila, rũnga, bɩ bõn-vuudr yĩn-kidgã.
45001024	Yaa rẽ yĩng la Wẽnnaam bas-b ne b sũura raab yaalse tɩ b lʋɩ yoob pʋgẽ n yaal b toorẽ yĩnga zãnga.
45001025	Wẽnnaam bas-b lame tɩ yaa bãmb n deng n bas Wẽnde, n dɩk Wẽnnaam sɩda n tek ne zirẽ-beedo, n lɛɛg n kẽ bõn-naands n waoog-ba, n yaool n bas Naanda sẽn tog ne pẽgr wakat buud fãa. (Ami!)
45001026	Dẽ n so tɩ Wẽnnaam bas-ba ne b minim wẽnse, al tɩ b pagba tek vɩɩm ning b sẽn da segdẽ n vɩɩnde, n sak sẽn kisi.
45001027	B rapa me basa sẽn ka kis bãmb ne b pagbã, n na n tʋlg taab ne raab kãsenga, n sak wɩɩbd ne taaba la b reega b tudgr kãng yaoodo, yaood sẽn da ka tõe n ka yao ye.
45001028	B sẽn pa modg n tall Wẽnd bãngr akɩka, wala bũmb sẽn be yõodo, Wẽnnaam bas-b lame ne yam kɩdga tɩ b maan sẽn ka segd.
45001029	B sũur sẽn pid ne bũmb ningã, yaa wẽnem buud fãa, fɩglem, raab wagla, pu-toogo; b sẽn mi yaa sũ-kiiri, taab yõor yãkre, zaba, zãmbo, taab bẽdgo; b nonga b taab yʋʋr sãoongo,
45001030	taab wɩdga. Bãmb la Wẽnd bɛɛba, mo-be-neba, zẽk-m-meng rãmba, wʋglem dãmba, sɩlem wẽns rãmba, kõn-sak-b-ba rãmba,
45001031	yam kaoolg rãmba, kõn-togs-m-pʋg rãmba, ka mi nimbãan-zoeer dãmba, ka mi sugr dãmba.
45001032	Ne b sẽn mi tɩ Wẽnd yeelame tɩ wẽng a woto buud maandb toga ne kũum, b ka baas n maandẽ bal ye, b le be tẽngre n pẽgd sẽn maand-b wẽnga menga.
45002001	F sẽn ya a soaba, f na n konga bʋʋm f sã n dat n bʋ f taaba. Fo sã n baood n na n ning f to taale, yaa f meng la f na n paalg, tɩ foo ne yẽ soab manesem yaa a ye.
45002002	D miime tɩ Wẽnd sã n kẽesd yell a woto rãmb bʋʋdo, b tũuda b sɩdã n bʋʋdẽ.
45002003	Dɩlla fo sã n maand wa f taaba n yaool n zĩ n kaood b bʋʋdo, fo tẽedame tɩ Wẽnnaam na bʋ foo n bas-f taal bɩ?
45002004	Da maan wa f sãbsda Wẽnnaam ne b sõmblema sẽn ka be tɛkã, ne b tõog-m-mengã, ne b kõt-yaara ye; ad-b sõmblema ratame tɩ f ning pãng n teem zʋgo.
45002005	F sã n kʋɩɩs f sũuri, f sã n zãgs tuubgu, Wẽnnaam beem la f samd f zugu, la b beema na n puka b bʋ tirsa kaoob raare,
45002006	raar ning b sẽn na n kõ ned kam fãa a tʋʋmda keoore.
45002007	Na n yɩɩ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ la b na n kõ neb niyns sẽn modg-b ne neer maanego, n baood pẽgre, waoogre, vɩɩm sẽn ka tar goalenga.
45002008	Neb niyns sẽn ya-b tõatba, sẽn kɩɩsd-b sɩda, n yaool n sakd wẽnga, Wẽnd sũ-puura na n dɩɩ bãmb dãmba, b na n paama Wẽnd zabre.
45002009	Ned ning fãa sẽn maand-a wẽnga, a pʋɩɩr na n yɩɩ pɛta la yɩɩre, Zʋɩf pipi, tɩ sẽn ka-a Zʋɩf yaool n pʋgd.
45002010	La sẽn maand-a neere, ziir la pẽgr n yɩt a pʋɩɩre, Zʋɩf pipi tɩ sẽn ka-a Zʋɩf yaool n pʋgd.
45002011	Wẽnd ka yɛs n get fo sẽn ya buud ninga ned ye.
45002012	Ade, neb niyns fãa sẽn maan-b yel-wẽnde, b na n dɩ-la b yel-wẽnda taale, ba b sã n ka Zʋɩf. Neb niyns sẽn mi-b a Moyiiz Noorã n maan wẽnga, bãmb dãmb bʋʋd na n yɩɩ wala a Moyiiz Noora sẽn yalse.
45002013	Ka sẽn mi-b noora la nin-sõma, Wẽnnaam taoor ye, yaa sẽn maand-b noora sẽn wilgã.
45002014	Bu-zẽmba sẽn ka mi-b Noorã n yaool n maand wala Noora sẽn datã, b bãng tɩ wakat kãnga b manes sõngã n lebg bãmb noore,
45002015	wakat kãnga b wilgdame tɩ noor n be n gʋls b sũurẽ la rẽ n so tɩ ned kam fãa wʋmd koɛɛg a pʋgẽ, la koɛɛg sẽn leokd d taab tʋʋma poorẽ, b sã n toga ne sãbsgo bɩ ne pẽgre.
45002016	Ad-y yaa sẽn maand-b Noora sẽn data bʋʋdo la Wẽnd na n tũ a Zezi Krista n bʋ sẽn solg fãa ninsaalb sũurẽ, wala m Koe-nooga sẽn wilgdã.
45002017	Fo sã n zẽkd f menga, f sẽn ya Zʋɩf yĩnga, fo sã n yet tɩ f yaa Wẽnd Noora biiga, tɩ Wẽnd la fo zu-zẽkre,
45002018	tɩ f mii b raabo, tɩ yaa sẽn be yõod la f mi la f pʋgda, tɩ f mii sor ning f sẽn tog n dɩke,
45002019	tɩ f nin pukame, al tɩ f tõe n wilg zoeens sore, tɩ f tõe n lebg sẽn kẽnd-b likẽ vẽenem,
45002020	n lebg zɩtba bãngre, n lebg sẽn ka mib neng karen-saamba, f sã n paam tɩ Wẽnnaam Noora tuk sɩd la bãngr sor n kõ-fo,
45002021	m na sok-f n gese, yaa bõe yĩng la f mi f taab zãmsgo n yaool n ka tõe n zãms f menga?
45002022	Bõe tɩ f zãmsd tɩ wagdem kisame la f zuuda? Ti yoob kisame, la f yooda? Bõe tɩ wẽn-naandsa yaand f sũuri tɩ f baas n kẽed b rotẽ n zɛɛdẽ?
45002023	Foo tɩ Wẽnnaam Noora bãngr la f zu-zẽkre, bãng marsã tɩ f sã n pa reegd-a, yaa Wẽnnaam meng la f paoogda.
45002024	La sɩd me wala sẽn gʋlse: Yaa yãmb yĩng la Wẽnnaam yʋʋra tar sãoong bu-zẽmba nengẽ n dabda.
45002025	Bãong kõom bee yõodo fo sã n deegd Wẽnnaam noore; fo sã n kẽ bãong la f ka reegd Wẽnnaam noore, foo ne sẽn ka kẽ-a bãong zem taaba.
45002026	Sẽn ka kẽ-a bãong sã n deegd Wẽnnaam noorã, a ka zem sẽn kẽ-a bãong sɩda?
45002027	Ne a sẽn ka kẽ bãongã, yaa yẽ n na n kao fo bʋʋdo; yẽ sẽn deegd Wẽnnaam noorã n na n bʋ foo, fo sẽn ya bãnkoanga la f mi Wẽnd noore la f baas n tõdgd-a.
45002028	Sẽn yaa Zʋɩf akɩk ka sẽn yaa Zʋɩf neb nifẽ bal ye, la bãong akɩk ka yĩnga sẽn kẽed a soaba ye.
45002029	Zʋɩf akɩk yaa Zʋɩf a sũurẽ la sẽn kẽed-a bãong akɩk yaa sẽn kẽed-a a sũurẽ. Sẽn be sũuri wã n yɩɩd sẽn gʋls sebrẽ. Ad-y yẽ soaba pẽgre ka na n yi ninsaal nengẽ, a na n yii Wẽnd nengẽ.
45003001	Yaa bõe pʋgẽ la Zʋɩf yɩɩd neb a taaba la bãong kõom yõod be-la a yɛ?
45003002	Ad-y yaa bũmb wʋsg pʋgẽ. Pipi, yaa Zʋɩf rãmba la Wẽnnaam kõ b koeese.
45003003	Kẽer yɩɩ tõatba, la rẽ maana bõe? Wẽnd zooda tũu rẽ n sãam bɩ?
45003004	Ka boto ye! Wala sẽn gʋlse, yaa tɩlɛ tɩ Wẽnd pa b sɩd zĩigẽ tɩ ninsaal pa a zirẽ-beedẽ; la rẽ me la lebg pakre tɩ f gom n yiis f meng yellẽ la f gom n yiis f meng bʋʋdẽ.
45003005	Tõnd wẽnema sã n pukd Wẽnd sõmblem, koe bʋg la d le tara? D na tõog n le yeel tɩ Wẽnd ka maan neere b sã n bas tɩ b sũ-puura yõog-do? Ad-y yaa ninsaal zʋbsgo la m na n zʋbse.
45003006	B sã n ka tõe n puug b sũuri, b na n yɩɩ wãn n wilg dũni wã a bʋʋm la a kongre?
45003007	La mam zirẽ-beed sã n kɩt tɩ m bãng n paase tɩ Wẽnnaam yaa sɩd soaba, tɩ Wẽnnaam pẽgr tũ rẽ n lebg wʋsgo, m sok n gese ned le tara sor n ges maam wa yel-wẽn-maand bɩ?
45003008	La woto wã, wala rõatb kẽer sẽn gomd tɩ yii tõnd noorẽ wã, d kõn maan wẽng tɩ neer wa tũ rẽ n zĩndi? M mi tɩ rõadg a woto buud yẽ toga ne sɩbgre!
45003009	Bõe la m na n yeele, tɩ tond Zʋɩf rãmbã n são bɩ? Lɛ-lɛ!
45003010	Wala m sẽn zoe n wilgã, Zʋɩf ne sẽn ka-a Zʋɩf naaga taab n ya yel-wẽnd yemse. Tẽeg-y b sẽn gʋlse: «Nin-sõng ka ye, ba a ye.
45003011	Yam soab ka ye, sẽn baood-a Wẽnnaam ka ye, ba a ye.
45003012	B fãa gill bʋdga sore, b fãa gill wegmame. Sẽn maand-a neer ka ye, ayo! Ba a ye.
45003013	B kokor yaa wa yaoog sẽn ka tar limdi, b zelemd wʋgda zãmb sʋndo. Wag-toaag zẽnem n bee b noorẽ
45003014	B noor yiisda gom-miisg la kãab beedo.
45003015	B nao tʋʋla ne wudg n daag zɩɩm.
45003016	B sor yaa sãoong la far sore.
45003017	B ka bãng yĩin-maasma sor n dɩk ye.
45003018	B nin zɩ n kabs Wẽnnaam dabeem yĩng ye.»
45003019	Ade, tõnd yaool n miime tɩ yaa Wẽnnaam sẽn kõ b rãmb noore la noora modgda; la b maana woto tɩ ned ba a ye ra tõog n yaag a noor ye, tɩ b paalg ninsaalba fãa b bʋʋdẽ.
45003020	Wẽnnaam taoore ned ba a ye ka na n tõog n kõ a meng bʋʋm b noya deegr poorẽ ye, tɩ Noor sẽn tõe ne bũmb ning yaa wa ne yel-wẽnd bãngr bala.
45003021	Dũnna-rũnna, ne noora sẽn teke, Wẽnnaam sõmblema ket n yaa vẽenega wala Noora la bãngdba zamaanẽ.
45003022	Neb niyns fãa sẽn tẽed-ba a Zezi Krista yãeta sõmblem kãnga – tɩ bũmb ba a ye ka teem bãmb nengẽ ye –
45003023	b fãa beega Wẽnde tɩ Wẽnd sẽn pid ne ziira zãag ne-ba.
45003024	La b sã n le paam b yell manegre tũu ne Wẽnd yamleoog la Krista maoonga yõodo.
45003025	Wẽnd yãk-b lame tɩ b lebg, ne b meng zɩɩm, sugr bũmb, tẽedba yĩnga; la rẽ yaa b sẽn dat n wilg b sõmblem la b bas yel-wẽn niyns sẽn maan pĩnda taale,
45003026	Wẽnd sũ-maasma wakato; la b sẽn dat n wilg rũnna tɩ b ket n zĩ b sõmblema zugu, yaa sẽn tẽed-ba a Zezi yelle la b manegda.
45003027	Sã n ya woto, fo tara sor n zẽk f meng bɩ? Ayoo, sor ka ye! La bõe tɩ sor kaẽ? Be f tʋʋmẽ wã bɩ? Ayoo! Yaa f manegrã sẽn ya tẽeba bũmbã. Sɩda d tagsdame tɩ ninsaal manegr yita a tẽebẽ. Ka tũud a sẽn deegd noora ye. Ka rẽ d yetẽ lame tɩ Wẽnd yaa Zʋɩf rãmb bal Wẽnnaam.
45003028	Sɩda, d tagsdame tɩ tẽeb fãagda neda tɩ ka tũ ne Noora reegr ye.
45003029	Ka rẽ d na kong n yeel tɩ Wẽnnaam ka bu-zẽmba Wẽnnaam ye, b yaa Zʋɩf rãmb Wẽnnaam bala. La d miime tɩ Wẽnd yaa bu-zẽmba me Wẽnde, tɩ b yaa Wẽnd a ye tãa.
45003030	B fãagda ned ning fãa sẽn tar-a tẽebo, sẽn kẽ-a bãongo wala sẽn ka kẽ-a bãongo.
45003031	Dɩlla tẽeb yãkda Noora bark bɩ? Ayoo! A kõt-a lame.
45004001	D na n yeelame tɩ bõe d yaaba Abraam poorẽ?
45004002	Sã n yaa Abraam tʋʋm sõma yĩng la a lebg nin-sõngo, a zug tõe n zẽkame, Wẽnnaam nengẽ wã la m ka mi.
45004003	Sebr sõng yetame tɩ bõe? A Abraam tẽe Wẽnnaam la rẽ n wa ne a yell manegre.
45004004	Ned sã n tʋm tɩ b kõ a yaoodo, ka kũun la b kõ a ye, yaa bũmb sẽn ya tɩlɛ ne-a.
45004005	La ned sã n ka teeg a tʋʋma n yaool n teeg ned ninga sẽn tõe tɩ nin-wẽng yell manegã, d yetame tɩ yaa tẽebã n sɩd maneg a yelle.
45004006	Pʋsẽ yaa rẽ yĩng la a Daviid boond tɩ zu-noog soaba ned ning Wẽnd sẽn maneg a soab yelle tɩ ka tũ ne a tʋʋm manesem:
45004007	Zu-noog rãmba la sẽn paam b beegre sugri la b yel-wẽna ludbu.
45004008	Zu-noog soaba la Wẽnd sẽn bas a soab taal zãnga.
45004009	B sẽn gomd zu-noog ningã, b gomd-a-la sẽn kẽ-b bãong yĩng bala bɩ yaa sẽn ka kẽ-b bãong me yĩnga? Sɩda d yetame t'a Abraam tẽebã n wa ne a yell manegre.
45004010	Manega wakat bʋgo, a sẽn waa n nan ka kẽ bãong bɩ a bãong kõom poore? Ka a sẽn lebg zũng poor ye, ya a sẽn waa n nan ka kẽ bãongo.
45004011	A bãonga lebga wa kaseto t'a sẽn waa n nan ka kẽ bãongo, a ra zoe n tara tẽeb ning sẽn manegda ned yellã. Dẽ n so t'a na n lebg buud a yiib ba. A yaa ba pipi, sẽn na n tẽ-ba n yaool n ka kẽ bãonga yĩnga, tɩ tẽeb n maneg bãmb dãmb yelle,
45004012	la a leb n yaa ba sẽn kẽ-b bãong yĩnga; b kẽe bãongo n yaool n ka get rẽ wa bũmb sẽn seke, n na n dɩk a Abraam tẽeba sore, tẽeb ning a sẽn da tare t'a nan ka kẽ bãongã.
45004013	Sɩda, a Abraam sẽn paam tɩ Wẽnd pids kãabg ning b sẽn da kãab-a, n yeel tɩ dũni wã na n yɩɩ yẽnda bɩ a kamb soolem, bãng-y tɩ ka tũ ne noor deegr ye. Tũu ne tẽeb yel-sõmde.
45004014	Sẽn paam-b pʋɩɩrã sã n da yaẽ la sẽn deeg-b noore, tẽeb yaẽ la zaalem la kãabga me yaẽ la belegre.
45004015	Noor yõod ya f tõdg-a tɩ Wẽnd puug b sũur ne fo; noor sã n kaẽ, tõdgr me ka ye;
45004016	Yaa rẽ la m yet tɩ tõnd zu-noogã, yaa tẽeb n wat ne-a, tɩ tẽeb la kũun akɩka la yaa tẽeb yĩng la Wẽnd pids b kãabg ne a Abraam yagens buud fãa: ka sẽn tũud-b noorã bala, yaa sẽn tar-b d fãa ba a Abraam tẽebo,
45004017	tɩ woto la b gʋls yã: M kɩtame tɩ f lebg neb ka tɛk saamba – tẽeb saamba – t'a tẽe Wẽnd ning sẽn tõe vʋʋg sẽn ki, la a tõe tɩ sẽn ka be, zĩndi.
45004018	A Abraam saaga a sẽn kõn saage, n tẽ Wẽnde; woto la a lebg neb ka tɛk saamba wala b sẽn yeele: F yagens na n yɩɩ ka tɛka.
45004019	A Abraam gesa ne tẽeb sẽn ka tõe n kɩlle a yĩnga kʋʋlem (a yʋʋma da zoe n pida koabga) n ges a Sara me kʋʋlem.
45004020	A sẽn ne Wẽnd kãabga yĩnga, a ka zoe rabeem ye, a tẽeb kõ-a-la pãnga t'a pẽg Wẽnde,
45004021	n mii tɩ Wẽnd sã n pʋlme b tõogd n pidsa b pʋlengo.
45004022	Yaa rẽ yĩng la a paam t'a yell manege.
45004023	La Sebr sõng sã n yet tɩ ya a Abraam tẽebã n maneg a yelle, ka yet tɩ yɩɩ yẽnda a yembr bal ye; goma tõnd me yelle,
45004024	tɩ tẽeb n sɩd maneg d yelle, tõnd sẽn tẽed Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋg a soab kɩɩms sʋka, tõnd Soaala Zezi Krista.
45004025	B ki-la d yel-wẽna yĩnga la b vʋʋga d yell manegr yĩnga.
45005001	Tẽeba sẽn maneg d yell yĩnga, d zĩi ne laafi Wẽnnaam taoore, la rẽ tũu ne tõnd Soaala Zezi Krista maasem.
45005002	Bãmb kɩtame tɩ d tũ tẽebo n paam kũun ning d sẽn zĩ ne a soabã; yaa kũun sẽn waoogd tõndo, t'a ka bũmb a to n zʋʋg Wẽnd ziira pʋɩɩr saagr ye.
45005003	Bõe la m na n paase? Ad-y d fara meng le yaa d zu-zẽkre tɩ d miime tɩ far yalsda ned yam zĩ yɛnga.
45005004	Ned sã n yals a meng zĩ yɛnga, a rɩkda tʋʋm sõma minugu la minim n tʋm neerã n wat ne saagre.
45005005	La sẽn saagd-a ka tõe n lʋɩ vɩʋʋgẽ ye tɩ Wẽnnaam kɩtame tɩ Vʋʋsem sõng ning d sẽn paama daagd Wẽnd nonglma tõnd sũurẽ.
45005006	Yaa tõnd sẽn dag n ka tõe n le maan fɩ wã wakato la Krista yãk b raare n ki wẽn-kɩɩsdba yĩnga.
45005007	– Daare ned tõe n sak n kii sẽn ka tar-a a toorẽ yelle yĩnga, n ki nin-sõng yĩnga, daare, rẽ tõeeme.
45005008	– Kaset ning d sẽn tare n mi tɩ Wẽnd nonga tõndã, yaa Krista sẽn ki d yĩnga tɩ d yaool n da ket n ya yel-wẽn-maandbã.
45005009	D miime tɩ marsã la d na n põs zabre d sẽn paam tɩ b raag b zɩɩm tɩ d yell tũ rẽ n maneg zãngã.
45005010	Beem sẽn waa n ket tõnd ne Wẽnd sʋka, Wẽnd Biiga kii tõnd yĩnga n kɩt tɩ d lebg Wẽnd zo-rãmba, tõnd sẽn lebg zood ne Wẽnda marsã d miime tɩ Wẽnd Biiga vɩɩm na tõog tɩ d yell le maneg n yɩɩg.
45005011	La ka rẽnd bal ye, bũmb n le kɩt tɩ d kɩdemd Wẽnnaam taoore, yaa Krista sẽn sõng tɩ d zoe n be manegr pʋgẽ dũnna-rũnna.
45005012	Ad-y yaa nin-yend n wa ne yel-wẽnd dũni pʋgẽ, tɩ yel-wẽnd me wa ne kũum, tɩ kũum me lebg neb fãa bũmbu tɩ yel-wẽnd me lebga neb fãa yel-wẽnde.
45005013	Wẽnnaam sẽn da waa n nan ka kõ b noora wakato, yel-wẽnd da bee dũni pʋgẽ, la wakat kãnga, Wẽnnaam noora sẽn da ka moon yĩnga, b ra basa yel-wẽnd taale.
45005014	Baasgo a Adem n ta a Moyiiz, kũum da rɩkdame, la sẽn pa beeg-ba a Adem beegr da kiidame; baad-y pipi Adema yaa Adem ninga sẽn pʋgda wã makre.
45005015	Kũun sẽn kõt to-to, la beegr sẽn beegd to-to ka a ye ye. Nin-yend beegr waa ne neb ka tɛk kũum, bãng-y tɩ Wẽnd kũuna b sẽn ning Krista b yembra nugẽ, kũun kãnga b sudg-a la zembala, ne yamleoogo, neb ka tɛk zutu.
45005016	Wẽnd kũuna sẽn wa ne bũmb ninga la nin-yend beegra sẽn wa ne a soaba me ka wẽnd taab ye. Yel-wẽnd a ye poore bʋʋd n bʋ la yɩɩ paalgr bʋʋdo la Wẽnd bas taala yɩɩ yel-wẽn ka tɛk bas taale.
45005017	Nin-yend yel-wẽnd waa ne kũum dũni pʋgẽ la kũum lebga naaba, nin-kãng manesem yĩnga, bãng-y tɩ sẽn paam-b nin-yend kũuni, tõnd Soaal a Zezi Krista manegrã, bãmb dãmb n na n yãmb moogo.
45005018	Nin-yend yel-wẽnd waa ne neb gill sɩbgre, tɩ nin-yend sugr kosg wa ne vɩɩm neb fãa yĩnga.
45005019	Nin-yend tõdgr kɩtame tɩ neb ka tɛk tũ rẽ n lebg yel-wẽn-maandba, ad-y nin-yend sakr n na n maneg neb ka tɛk yelle.
45005020	Sã n ya Noorã, yẽ waame tɩ yel-wẽnd tũ yẽ n wek balbo la a sẽn wek balb zĩig ninga, be la Wẽnd kũuna me yɩ ka tɛka.
45005021	Tũu ne yel-wẽnde tɩ kũum lebg naab dũni pʋgẽ la Wẽnd maag Krista sugri, b kõt yaara yĩnga, sõmblem zamaan na n yalsa vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ yĩnga.
45006001	M na n yeelame tɩ bõe? Tɩ d kell n pa yel-wẽnd pʋgẽ tɩ Wẽnnaam nimbãan-zoeerã tõog n yɩ wʋsgo d yĩnga? Ayoo!
45006002	Tõnd sã n lebg bõn-kɩɩms yel-wẽnd yĩnga, d na n yɩɩ wãn n le vɩɩnd a pʋgẽ?
45006003	Bɩ yãmb ka mi tɩ tõnd sẽn so Krist a Zezi soobã, yɩla b kũuma pʋgẽ la b lis tõndo?
45006004	Tõnd sẽn deeg soobã, tõnd naaga ne bãmba n mum yaoogẽ, sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ Krista sẽn vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka, Ba Pãng soaba maasem yĩnga, bɩ tõnd me paam n vɩɩnd vɩɩm paalga.
45006005	D sã n lebga bũmb a ye ne Krista, d kũuma sẽn wẽneg bãmb rẽnna, bɩ d bãng tɩ d na kell n wẽneg bãmba me ne vʋʋgr sẽn wẽnd bãmb dẽnna.
45006006	D bãng tɩ b naaga tõnd yĩn-kʋdrã n ka pik ne Krista, sẽn na n yɩlẽ n woog a wẽnema pãnga tɩ d da le yɩ yel-wẽnd yems ye.
45006007	Sẽn ki-a ka le ya yel-wẽnd yem-daoog ye.
45006008	La tõnd sã n naag Krista n ki, d tẽedame tɩ d naaga bãmb n vɩ.
45006009	Krista sẽn vʋʋgã, b ka tõe n le ki yɛs ye, kũum ka leb n tar b gaab yɛs ye.
45006010	B kũuma yɩɩ yel-wẽnd na menem zãng kũum; b vɩɩma yaa vɩɩnd ne Wẽnnaam vɩɩm.
45006011	Dɩlla yãmb me ges y meng marsã wa neb sẽn ka le kĩ ne yel-wẽnde, la y vɩɩnd Wẽnnaam kamb vɩɩm tõnd Soaala Zezi Krista maasmẽ.
45006012	Da sak-y tɩ yel-wẽnd le rɩ naam y yĩn-kiidga zug ye; da le sak yã a tʋls wẽnsa ye.
45006013	Da sak-y tɩ y yĩnga wils lebg yel-wẽnd zab-teed ye. Dɩk-y y mens n kõ Wẽnd tɩ y yaa bõn-kɩɩms sẽn lebg nin-vɩɩse. Dɩk-y y yĩnga wils n kẽ Wẽnd tãpẽ n zab sõmblem zabre.
45006014	Yel-wẽnd ka tog n le rɩ naam y zug ye tɩ y yii Noor zamaanẽ n kẽ sõmblem dẽnnẽ.
45006015	D na n maana bõe d sẽn paam tɩ b yiis-d Noor soolmẽ n kẽes-d sõmblem zamaanẽ, d tõe n le maana wẽng bɩ? Lɛ-lɛ!
45006016	Y ka mi tɩ y sã n bas tɩ ned kẽes y yembd pʋgẽ, y sɩd lebga yẽ yem-daoogo? Y sã n lebg wẽng yem-daado, y kũum la y bao yã, y sã n tũud Wẽnnaam, y manegr la y paam yã.
45006017	Wẽnd paam barka tɩ y sẽn da ya yel-wẽnd yembs pĩnda, y sakame n deeg zãmsg ninga b sẽn zãms yã,
45006018	n yi yel-wẽnd soolmẽ n kẽ sõmblem zamaanẽ.
45006019	Y yama sẽn pa waoog yĩnga m na n dɩka ninsaal makre. Wala y sẽn dɩk y yĩnga pĩnd n kẽes yel-wẽnd yembdẽ t'a yaal zãnga, woto-me bɩ y rɩk y meng rũnna n kõ neere n lebg sõma.
45006020	Yãmb sẽn waa n ya yel-wẽnd yem-daado, neer maaneg ra ka pak-y ye.
45006021	La m na n sok-y lame n gese, y paama bõe y tʋʋm kãensa pʋgẽ sã n ka y sẽn zĩ rũnna tɩ b yãnd tar-y wã? B ka tar yõod n zʋʋg kũum ye.
45006022	Rũnna y sẽn paam n yi yel-wẽnd yembdẽ n kẽ Wẽnnaam, bãng-y tɩ y womda sõmblem biisi la rẽ n na n kẽes-y vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ pʋgẽ.
45006023	Yel-wẽnd sẽn wat ne bũmb ninga yaa kũum bala; la Wẽnnaam kũuna sẽn wat ne a soaba, yaa vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ, tõnd Soaala Zezi Krista maasmẽ.
45007001	M sok n gese, m saam-biisi, la yaa waa m gomda ne neb sẽn mi noor sẽn ya a soab taki, m sok-y n gese, y ka mi tɩ yaa ned sẽn ket n vɩ la noor modgd sɩda?
45007002	Yaa a sɩd sẽn ket n vɩ noor la pʋg-kãad reegda; a sɩda sã n ki, a noor ka le modgd-a yɛs ye;
45007003	yaa sɩda sẽn ket n vɩ wakato t'a bas-a n kul dao a to la b na n bool-a tɩ kãad sãamda. A sɩd sã n ki, a yi-la a sɩd soolmẽ; dɩlla a sɩd kũum poore a sã n kul dao a to a ka sãamd kãadem ye.
45007004	Dẽ la m na n yeelyã, m saam-biisi, tɩ yãmb me sẽn naag Krista n ki wã y yii noora soolmẽ; tõnd bee ned a to soolmẽ: yaa sẽn vʋʋg-a kɩɩms sʋka soab soolmẽ la d be, la d na n woma bi-sõma n kõ Wẽnnaam.
45007005	Sɩda, d sẽn da waa n ket n vɩ d pĩnd vɩɩma, noora sõnga d yĩnga wilsi la d zʋg wẽnga tɩ d wom biis sẽn tak kũum n kõ-do.
45007006	Marsã noor ka le modgd tõnd ye, tõnd lebga noora bõn-kɩɩmse, n yi yembd buud faa pʋgẽ; d basa no kʋdra sẽn da gʋls bũmb ninga n pʋgd Wẽnd ne zʋg paalga.
45007007	Noor yaa wẽnga? M kõn yeel dẽ lɛlɛ, la sã n ya sɩda, yaa noor n kɩt tɩ d bãng yel-wẽnde. M tʋlla woto kõn waẽ m sũurẽ, noor sã n dag n ka yeelẽ lɛ-lɛ: da tʋlg ye!
45007008	Noora sẽn yet tɩ woto la woto kisame wã yĩnga, yel-wẽnd tũu rẽ n kẽes tʋlsem ka tɛk m sũurẽ. Noor sã n da kaẽ, yel-wẽnd me kaẽ ye.
45007009	Pĩnda noora sẽn waa n dag n nan ka kõ, m da yaa bõn-vɩɩga; noora waoong poore, yel-wẽnd n lebg bõn-vɩɩga,
45007010	tɩ mam põd n lebg bõn-kɩɩnga. Ade, noora sẽn da kõ maam vɩɩm yĩnga, a waa ne mam kũum.
45007011	Yel-wẽnd dɩka noora sẽn da kis bũmb ningã n belg maam n paam n kʋ-ma.
45007012	D sã n ges neere d mikdame tɩ noor yaa bõn-sõngo; m tõe n paasame t'a yaa bõn-neere, bũmb sẽn toge.
45007013	La bõn-sõng tõe n tiig n lebga kũum mam yĩng bɩ? Ayoo! Ka tõe ye. Ad-y yaa yel-wẽnd n tʋm dẽnna; sẽn na n yɩlẽ t'a wẽnema puk zãnga, yel-wẽnd dɩka bõn-sõng n kʋ maam. Yel-wẽnd tũu noor n wilg maam a wẽnema pãnga.
45007014	Sã n ya sɩda, sẽn tar-a yam la b kõt noore; mam yaool n tara yĩng sẽn lebg yel-wẽnd yem-daago.
45007015	M ka mi m sẽn maanda võor ye, m sẽn data ka rẽ la m maand ye, m sẽn pa rata la m maanda.
45007016	La m sã n maand m sẽn pa rata, m naaga Noorã n kõt kaseto t'a yaa sõmbo.
45007017	M sã n maan m sẽn pa rate, tʋʋmda ka le ya mam tʋʋmd yɛs ye, a yaa yel-wẽnd sẽn ti a roog mam pʋgẽ tʋʋmde.
45007018	M neeme tɩ bõn-sõng ba a ye ka be m nengẽ ye, ka be m yĩngẽ ye; neer tʋlsem ka toog ne maam ye, yaa maaneg n ya toog ne-ma,
45007019	dẽ n so tɩ m pa maand neere, m sẽn date, n yaool n maand wẽng m sẽn pa rate.
45007020	La m sã n maand m sẽn pa rate, dẽ ka le ya mam tʋʋmd ye, a yaa yel-wẽnd sẽn ti a roog mam pʋgẽ tʋʋmde.
45007021	Dɩlla noor n be m yĩnga tɩ m sã n dat fãa n maan neere, maan wẽngã n yɛs m taoore.
45007022	M sũura pʋgẽ Wẽnnaam noora noom-m-la al wʋsgo;
45007023	la m yĩnga wilsẽ, noora to n yɛse; la no-kãng yika zabre ne m sɩɩgã la a za-m la ne bãeense, yel-wẽnde sẽn be m yingẽ bãeense.
45007024	M yãbda m menga! Ãnd n na n fãag maam ne m yĩnga sẽn dat m kũuma?
45007025	Wẽnd paam pẽgr d Soaala Zezi Krista maasem yĩnga. Ad-y yaa maam bala n ne m yamẽ tɩ m tog n tũ Wẽnd sẽn yalse, n yaool n sakd m yĩngẽ wã, yel-wẽnd sẽn yalse.
45008001	Bãng-y tɩ sẽn be-b ne a Zezi marsã wã ka le zoet bʋʋd paalgr ye.
45008002	A Vʋʋsem Sõng noora n kõt vɩɩm a Zezi maasmẽ, la yẽ n fãag foom ne noor ninga sẽn wata ne yel-wẽnd la kũum.
45008003	Wẽnd pidsa a Moyiiz Noora sẽn da ka tõe bũmb ningã, ninsaal komslma sẽn mong-a bũmb ningã, n tõog yel-wẽnde ne ninsaal yĩnga. Ad-y b tʋma b meng Biiga sẽn wa ne yĩng sẽn wẽnd tõnd dẽnna n yaool n tar pãng n menesd yel-wẽnde.
45008004	Wẽnd maana rẽnna, tɩ d tõog n deeg Noorã, tõnd sẽn ka le vɩ wala d yĩnga sẽn datã, n vɩ wala a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn datã.
45008005	Sɩda neb niyns fãa sẽn tũud-b yĩnga raab baooda sẽn noom b yĩngã la neb niyns sẽn tũud-ba a Vʋʋsem Sõng raab baooda sẽn noom a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.
45008006	Bãng-y tɩ sẽn baood-a a yĩnga sẽn datã, baooda a kũum la sẽn baooda a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn datã, baooda a vɩɩm la laafi.
45008007	Yĩnga sẽn data baoob sẽn pak b rãmbã, lebgda Wẽnnaam bɛɛba, n pa rat n le reeg Wẽnnaam noor ye; b pʋs n ka tõe meng ye.
45008008	Yaa rẽ me yĩng la b ka tõe n ta Wẽnnaam yam ye.
45008009	Yãmb ka le ya neb sẽn tũud b yĩnga yamleoog ye, y pʋgda a Vʋʋsem Sõngo sẽn date, tɩ Wẽnd meng kõ yãmb a Vʋʋsem Sõngo. Sẽn ka tar-a Krista Vʋʋsma, Krista ka so yẽ soab ye.
45008010	La Krista sã n be ne yãmba, ba yel-wẽnd sã n da kɩt tɩ y yĩnga tog n ki, Vʋʋsma na n kõ-y-la vɩɩm, Wẽnd sẽn maneg d yell ne bãmba yĩnga.
45008011	Wẽnd Vʋʋsem ninga sẽn vʋʋga a Zezi Krista kɩɩms sʋka, sã n be ne yãmbã, ad-y b sẽn vʋʋga a Zezi Krista kɩɩms sʋka, b na kõ y yĩn-kiidgã vɩɩm, b Vʋʋsma sẽn be ne yãmba yĩnga.
45008012	M saam-biisi, pakr sã n beẽ me, kõn yɩ pakr bada tɩ d vɩɩnd wala d yĩnga sẽn data ye.
45008013	Yãmb sã n vɩ wala y yĩnga sẽn date, y na n kiime. La y sẽn paam Vʋʋsem ninga sã n kɩt tɩ y lak ne yĩnga raabo, y na n vɩɩndame.
45008014	Wẽnnaam Vʋʋsma sẽn be ne b rãmb fãa lebga Wẽnnaam kamba.
45008015	Vʋʋsem ning y sẽn paama ka bũmb sẽn kɩt tɩ y lebg yem-daado n zĩ ne rabeem ye; y lebga Wẽnd zak kamba al n tõe n bool Wẽnd Aba, dat n yeelame tɩ Ba.
45008016	A Vʋʋsem Sõng meng naaga tõnd n kõt kaset tɩ d lebga Wẽnnaam kamba.
45008017	La d sẽn ya Wẽnnaam kamba, d na paam pʋɩɩr ning b sẽn pʋlem b kamba; d na naag Krista n paam pʋɩɩr kãnga; d sẽn naag bãmb n namsã, d na naag bãmba n paam pẽgre.
45008018	M tagsdame tɩ zamaan kãnga namsgo ne rolb ninga sẽn na n yɩ tõnd dẽnd beoog raarã ka tõe n mak taab ye.
45008019	Bõn-naandsa fãa zĩ n gũuda ne yãgbo, Wẽnd kamba pẽgr sẽn na n puk raare.
45008020	Ninsaal tʋls yaalsã sã n tiig n kẽes bõn-naandsa fãa yembd pʋgẽ, d bãng tɩ ka tũ ne bãmb daab ye, tũu ne ninsaalb tʋʋmde la bãmb me saagdame
45008021	tɩ b yembdã sɛɛb bee raare, tɩ b yĩnga komsg sɛɛb bee raare, la b gũuda b sẽn na n paam soog-m-menga ne ziir ning Wẽnd sẽn kõt b kamba.
45008022	D mii vẽenega tɩ al n ta marsã bõn-naandsa fãa waasda rogem waasgo;
45008023	la ka bãmb bal ye, yaa tõnd me sẽn zoe n paam lɛng ninga a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn lemb tõndã; yaa tõnd fãa n naag n waasd d sũurẽ, n gũud d yĩnga fãagre.
45008024	Tõnd fãagra yaa bũmb d sẽn tõe n saag. La fo sã n ne f sẽn saagda soaba, dẽ ka le ya saagr ye. Fo na n yɩɩ wãn n ne bũmb la f le yet tɩ f saagda a yãeebo?
45008025	Saagr yaa fo sẽn ka ne bũmb ninga tɩ f kʋmb f yam n tar a gẽegre.
45008026	A Vʋʋsem sõng me wata d sõngre, tɩ d ka mi d sẽn na n kos bũmb ning taki tɩ d pʋʋsg yɩ neer ye, la ad-y yĩnsir tara a Vʋʋsem Sõngo tɩ b yõkd sɛɛg d yĩnga la b wiisd wiis toogo.
45008027	Bũmb-kõ-solg-m Wẽndã mi a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn dat d yĩnga la bãmb me sẽn yõkd sɛɛg Wẽnd kom-nongdsa yĩnga, zemsa ne Wẽnd meng raabo.
45008028	D miime tɩ Wẽnd sẽn nong b rãmbã, Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb toorã ne b raabo, b sõngda bãmb tɩ b yɛla fãa welg neere.
45008029	B sẽn welg b rãmb toor al pĩnd-pĩnda, b tʋlgame tɩ b rɩk b Biiga wẽnego la Biiga na n lebga kãsem sẽn tar yaop ka tɛka.
45008030	B sẽn pʋlem b rãmb neera la b bool yã. B sẽn bool b rãmba yell la b maneg yã, b sẽn maneg b rãmb yell la b pids ne ziiri.
45008031	Bõe la m na n le paas yɛsa? Wẽnd meng sẽn yaa d sõangdã d zabd-n-taag na n yɩɩ ãnna?
45008032	Wẽnnaam ka zoe b Biiga nimbãaneg ye, b sakame t'a ki d yĩnga; b Biiga yĩnga, bõe la b ka na n kõ-d marsã?
45008033	Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb toorã, ãnda n tõe n le kẽes-b bʋʋdo? Yaa Wẽnd n manegd ninsaal yelle.
45008034	Woto wã tõe n le yɩ-la a Zezi Krista sẽn ki tõnd yĩnga, n vʋʋge la b zĩ b Ba rɩtg n pʋʋsd d yĩnga tõe n le yɩɩ bãmb n na n kẽes tõnd bʋʋd bɩ?
45008035	Bõe n na n yiis tõnd a Zezi Krista nonglem pʋgẽ? Far bɩ, sũ-beed bɩ, namsg bɩ, kom la naong bɩ, bũmb sẽn tõe n yak yõor bɩ, sʋʋg bɩ?
45008036	Kõn le yɩ wa d sẽn karemd Sebr sõng pʋgẽ ye: Yaa yãmb yĩng la b tar tõnd n koot wa piisi wakat buud fãa, beoog sẽn vẽege.
45008037	Baad-y t'a Zezi nonglem yĩnga, tõnd n maand daoodo.
45008038	N-ye! M sũur kegmame tɩ bũmb ba a ye ka le tõe n zãag d ne Wẽnnaam nonglma, a Zezi Krista sẽn wa ne a soaba ye. Kõn yɩ kũum bɩ vɩɩm ye, kõn yɩ malɛk bɩ dũni soaal ye,
45008039	kõn yɩ rũnna bɩ beoog bũmb ye, kõn yɩ sẽn be sa-gãnẽ bɩ sẽn sud tẽng ye, kõn yɩ naand buud ba a ye.
45009001	Ne Krista m togsda sɩda, m ka yagd ziri ye, – a Vʋʋsem Sõng meng kaset la m tar m sũurẽ –
45009002	m togsdame tɩ sũ-sãang la toog n tar maam n namsd wakat buud fãa.
45009003	M tʋllẽ lame tɩ Wẽnnaam yãk m barka, m tʋllẽ lame n welg ne Krista, dẽ sã n tõe n nafẽ m saam-biisã,
45009004	sẽn ya-b bũmb a ye ne maam rogmẽ wã, sẽn ya-b Israyɛl kamba, Wẽnd kom-wubdsi, Wẽnd Ziira vẽenem sẽn bui b rãmba, Wẽnd sẽn yõg zood ne b rãmba, Wẽnd sẽn kõ b rãmb b noy, Wẽnd sẽn wilg b rãmb waoogr ning b sẽn dat ninsaalb nengẽ, Wẽnd sẽn kãab b rãmb noogo,
45009005	Wẽnd sẽn kãab b rãmb yaab sõma, yaab niyns sẽn dog Krista, sã n ya tẽng zug rogma, la Krista yɩɩda bũmb fãa, tɩ b yaa Wẽnd n tog ne pẽgr sẽn kõn sɛ. Ami!
45009006	Ka rat n yeel tɩ Wẽnd kãabga lʋɩɩ vɩʋʋgẽ ye. Y mens miime bala tɩ ka a Israyɛl kamba fãa la a Israyɛl ye.
45009007	Yaa wala y sẽn mi t'a Abraam yagensã fãa kaa Abraam sẽn dog a toor ye. Na n tũu ne a Izaak tɩ yagens kẽer na n ges foo wa b sɩgre,
45009008	dẽ rat n yeelame tɩ ka yĩnga sẽn dogd la Wẽnnaam kamb bal ye, kãabga kamb me yaa Wẽnd kamba.
45009009	Kãabga kãaba woto: Vẽer woto sasa, m na lɛɛg n wa, la a Sara na n doga biiga.
45009010	Ad bũmba to sẽn ya vẽenega n yɩɩda: a Rebeka waa n dɩka pʋga, d ba a ye maasmẽ, d ba a Izaak maasmẽ.
45009011	La a sẽn waa n nan ka rog a kinkirsã, tɩ kinkirsã me nan ka mi wẽng la neere,
45009012	sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ b bãng tɩ Wẽnd boolg tũuda ne Wẽnd raabo, la a ka tũud ninsaal tʋʋma, a Izaak wʋma b sẽn yeele: «Kãsma na n yɩɩ yao wã sõgne;»
45009013	la sɩda woto n be sebrẽ: «M nonga a Zakoob la m kisga a Ezayu.»
45009014	M yeelame tɩ bõe? Tɩ Wẽnd maanda sẽn ka zemsde? Ka boto ye.
45009015	B yeela a Moyiiz: «M zoeta m sẽn zoet a soab nimbãanega, m kũmda m sẽn kũmd a soaba.»
45009016	Ka sẽn nong-a, ka sẽn zoet-a n pʋgd Wẽnd pʋlengo n paamd-a ye, ya Wẽnd sẽn zoe a soab nimbãanega n paamd-a.
45009017	Ad sebra sẽn yet Ezipt naaba: M kõ-f la naama ne m daabo n na n tũ foo n wilg nebã m pãnga tɩ m yʋʋr paam pẽgr dũni fãa pʋgẽ.
45009018	Sɩda Wẽnd zoeta b sẽn dat a soab nimbãanega la b kidibda b sẽn dat a soab sũuri.
45009019	Fo na n yeel-m lame: «Yaa bõe la a le zĩi n sãbsdẽ yɛsa? Ãnda n tõe n kɩɩs Wẽnnaam daabo?»
45009020	Ninsaal biiga, foo la a bõe n na n wẽ no-koeemd ne Wẽnde? Ninsaal sẽn naan bũmb ninga na yik n yeel-a: «Bõe yĩng tɩ f naan m woto?»
45009021	Yagda ka tõe n dɩk yagd yɛnga n yag laok sẽn tar neerem n zems bala bɩ laok sẽn be neer wʋsg sɩda?
45009022	Ad-y yaa Wẽnd sẽn tʋlg n wilg tɩ ba b sũur puuda, b tara pãnga n tõe n yõk b menga ne lagd kẽer sẽn da yikd b sũuri n tog ne wãabo, n yaool n ka wã-b ye.
45009023	Ad-y yaa b sẽn dat n wilg b ziira la b pãnga, la lagd kẽer paam tɩ b kũm-b nimbãanegã n segl-b al pĩnda tɩ b ya ziir lagdo, lagd sẽn yag b pẽgr yĩnga.
45009024	La yaa woto la b maan ne tõnd, n sʋk-do Zʋɩf rãmba la bu-zẽmba sʋka.
45009025	Yaa woto la b gomd a Oze sebrẽ: «Sẽn da ka m buud neba la m na bool tɩ m buudu, la pʋg-beooga la m na n bool tɩ rʋmde,
45009026	b sẽn deng n wʋm zĩig ning tɩ b ka Wẽnnaam neba, zĩ kãng la b na n bool-b tɩ Wẽnnaam vɩɩga kamba.»
45009027	A Izayi yeela a Israyɛl poorẽ: «Ba a Israyɛl kamba sõor sã n da taẽ la bĩisri sẽn be mogr noore, ad-y yaa b sẽn kees b rãmba bala n na n fãage,
45009028	tɩ tao tao la vugr bala Wẽnnaam na n pidsa b kãabga tẽng zugu.»
45009029	Wala a Izayi sẽn pĩnd n yeele: «Tãnsoab a Wẽnd sã n da ka keesẽ buudu, tõnd lebgẽ la wala Sodom la Gomor.»
45009030	M na n kʋʋ m koɛɛga wãn wãna? Ade, Bu-zẽmba sẽn da ka baood sõmblem paam-a lame la yaa tẽeb sẽn wat ne sõmblem ningã.
45009031	A Israyɛl sẽn da tũud noorã n tẽed ta na kõ-a sõmblem, a raaba ka pids ye.
45009032	La yɩɩ bõe yĩnga? T'a basa a tẽeba teegre n teeg a tʋʋma. La woto b laka b lʋɩɩs kugri,
45009033	wala sẽn gʋlse: «Lakr kugr la m vigl Siõ pʋgẽ, m bẽd-y la ne pĩiga sẽn lubd neba, Siõ pʋgẽ; la ned ning sẽn yaool n dell-a pĩ-kãng kõn paam yãnd ye.»
45010001	M sẽn dat bũmb ning ne m sũur fãa la m sẽn pʋʋsd bũmb ning yĩnga, yaa m saam-biisa maan b sɩɩg fãagre.
45010002	M tõe n kõo kaset tɩ b ka tũud Wẽnnaam ne reem ye; bũmb sẽn be bala, yaa b yama n nan ka vẽneg tɩ seke.
45010003	B sẽn ka mi Wẽnd sõmblem sẽn ya a soaba, b ka bao-a ye, b bas-a lame n na n bao b toorẽ dẽnna.
45010004	B ka bãng tɩ Wẽnnaam kõ b noya tɩ b tall ninsaal n tãag Krista sẽn ya tẽed fãa manegd ye.
45010005	A Moyiiz gʋlsa noya sẽn wat ne manegr ninga poorẽ n yeel tɩ ninsaal sã n tũ-ba, b tõe n kõ-a la vɩɩm.
45010006	Tẽeb sen wat ne manegr ninga poorẽ, ad-a sẽn gʋlse: «Da yeel f sũurẽ: ãnda n tõe n dʋ yĩngri,» n dʋ yĩngr n sik Krista?
45010007	Bɩ ãnda n tõe n sig bʋg-tẽnga n yiis Krista kɩɩms sʋka.
45010008	Bõe la a pʋs n yeele? A yeelame: «Koɛɛga pẽ-f lame, a be f noorẽ, a be f sũurẽ,» yaa tõnd sẽn moond tẽeb ninga koɛɛga.
45010009	Sɩda, fo fãag n sɛɛme, f noor sã n togs t'a Zezi la Soaala tɩ f sũur deeg tɩ Wẽnd vʋʋg-b la kɩɩms sʋka.
45010010	Fo sẽn tẽed f sũurẽ n wat ne f manegre, la f noor toagsg wata ne f fãagre.
45010011	Ka sebr sõng n togsd tɩ ned ning fãa sẽn tẽed-a kõn paam yãnd bɩ?
45010012	Ad-y yaa rẽ yĩng la bũmb ka welg Grɛk ne Zʋɩf ye: b yiiba fãa tara Soaal a ye bala la Soaala kelgda neb niyns fãa sẽn yõkd b sɛɛga.
45010013	D karma sebr sõng pʋgẽ tɩ ned ninga sẽn na n yõka Soaala sɛɛga na n kẽe fãagr pʋgẽ.
45010014	B na n yɩɩ wãn n yõk Soaala sɛɛga tẽeb sã n ka reng n beẽ, la tẽeb na n yɩɩ wãn n zĩndi wʋmb sã n ka reng taoore, la b na n yɩɩ wãn n wʋm, koɛɛgã sã n ka reng n moone,
45010015	la koɛɛg na n yii yɛ sã n ka sẽn tʋm a soaba nengẽ, wala sebr sõng sẽn togsde: «Ad-y b sẽn tʋm b rãmb tɩ b saa n togs Koe-noogã, ad-b nao be neere.»
45010016	Da tẽ-y tɩ neba fãa n deeg Koe-nooga ye, t'a Izayi n yeele: «Ãnda n deeg d sẽn togs bũmb ningã?»
45010017	Sɩd yaa wilgri n dengd taoore tɩ tẽeb yaool n wa la wilgra yita Krista gomnẽ.
45010018	Bas-y tɩ m sok n gese, y tẽedame tɩ koɛɛga la b pa wʋme? Mooga tõr wʋma b rãamde la b gomda taa mooga yaanga.
45010019	Bas-y tɩ m le sok n gese, y tẽedame t'a Israyɛl ka wʋm bɩ? Bãng-y t'a Moyiiz reng n togsame: «M na n kɩtame tɩ buud sẽn ka bu-sõng yamleoog yõk yã; m na kɩt tɩ y wa sãbs buud a ye, a sẽn ka bãng yam yĩnga.»
45010020	A Izayi saag n le paasame: «Sẽn da ka baood-b maam, yãend-m lame, m lika m meng sẽn da ka sokd-b mam yelle.»
45010021	Ad-a sẽn leok a Israyɛl poorẽ: «M tuda m nug beoog sẽn wẽege, m tud-a la tõatba la tʋb-pa-wʋmdba.»
45011001	Dɩlla m sok n gese: Wẽnnaam yi-la b neba poorẽ bɩ? Ka boto ye. Mam meng ka Israyɛl ned laa, m ka a Abraam yageng laa, m ka rog a Bẽzamẽ buudẽ laa?
45011002	Wẽnd ka tõe n yeel tɩ b yii buud ning b sẽn welg toor al pĩnda poorẽ ye. Bɩ y yĩma sẽn gʋls a Eli poorẽ, a sẽn waa n gomd woto ne Wẽnnaam n baood n na n paalg Israyɛl kamba:
45011003	«Soaala, ad-y b kʋ-la y bãngdba, n sarm y maan-kuga; maam m ye n põse, tɩ b baas n dat n yãk m yõore!»
45011004	Yaa bõe la Wẽnd leok-a? «M keesa m yĩnga neb tus a yopoe sẽn ka yĩgimd a Baal taoor ye.»
45011005	Woto-me kell n kees rũnna la Wẽnd n welg-a toore ne b yamleoogo.
45011006	La sã n yet ne b yamleoogo, ka yet tɩ tũu ne ninsaal tʋʋmd ye, ka rẽ b kõn gom yamleoog yell ye.
45011007	D na n kʋʋga d koɛɛga wãn wãna? A Israyɛl sẽn bao bũmb ningã, a ka paam-a ne a toorẽ tʋʋm ye, tɩ Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb toora yaool n paam-a. Sẽn ket-bã, b basa b sũura tɩ kidbi;
45011008	wala sẽn be sebr sõng pʋga: «Wẽnd kõ-b-la yam sẽn suusdi la nin sẽn ka ne, la tʋb sẽn ka wʋmde, n tãag rũnna.»
45011009	A Daviid me ra yeela woto: «Kɩt-y tɩ b rɩɩb zĩig lebg b bẽdgo, n lebg b wĩir, n lebg kugr b sẽn na n lak n lʋɩ, tɩ rẽ yɩ b rolbo!
45011010	Bɩ b nin kẽ kõaada tɩ b ra le tõog n yãe ye, kɩt-y tɩ b po-raoog zõond n ka le roog ye!»
45011011	M le sok n gese: y tẽedame tɩ Zʋɩf rãmba lakame n na n lʋɩ lʋɩɩs meng bɩ? Ayoo! B lakr waa ne bu-zẽmba fãagre tɩ sũ-kiir na tũ rẽ n yõk-ba.
45011012	B lakra sã n wa ne dũni manegre, la b sõora woogr sã n wa ne bu-zẽmba nafre, b zãng gill sã n lɛɛg n wa, yita wãna?
45011013	Yaa ne yãmba, bu-zẽmba, la m togsda, m yaa yãmb tʋʋm-tʋmda, la m maanda m tʋʋmda neere,
45011014	la rẽ yaa m sẽn dat tɩ m saam-biisa yãende n yik sũ-kiiri tɩ m paam n fãag kẽere.
45011015	Wẽnd sẽn bas b rãmb kɛɛnga sã n wa ne dũni manegre, b sã n le bool-b sʋka na n yɩɩ bõe sã n ka kɩɩms vʋʋgre?
45011016	Kood dẽeng zom sẽn yãk n kõ Wẽnd sã n ket n ya sõmbo, bura zãng na n yɩɩ sõngo. Tɩɩga yẽgend sã n ya sõngo, wila me yɩta sõmbo.
45011017	Tɩ-sõnga wil sã n kʋʋse, tɩ fo sẽn ya tɩ zaal willã paam n sel b zugu n vʋʋg n paam sɩɩlem sõng n yũ,
45011018	da wa nand f meng n yɩɩd wil sõnga meng ye. Bɩ f sã n pẽgd f menga, da yĩm tɩ ka foo n zãad yẽgendã, yaa yẽgenda n zãad foo.
45011019	Fo na n yeelame: «B kɛɛ wila tɩ mam tõog n sel b zĩigẽ.»
45011020	Yaa sɩda, yaa b sẽn ka tar tẽeba yĩng la b kʋʋs-ba, la yaa fo tẽeba yĩng la f keta. Ne rẽ fãa da maan wilg-m-meng ye, maan dabeem n yɩɩda.
45011021	Wẽnd sã n kɩt tɩ b kʋʋs wil sẽn da be b zĩisẽ, fo me gũus tɩ b tõeeme n ka bas-f ye.
45011022	Bãng Wẽnd toolem la b nimbãan-zoeere. B yɩɩ toaag sẽn lʋɩ-ba yĩnga, n ya nimbãan-zoet ne foo, f sã n kell n pa b nonglma pʋgẽ; ka rẽ fo me yaa will sẽn na n kʋʋg.
45011023	Sẽn bas b rãmb kɛɛnga sã n yi b kɩɩsg pʋgẽ, b me na paam n le sel tɩɩg a to zug: Wẽnd tara pãng tɩ seka le sel b yɛsa.
45011024	Ade, b sã n kɛɛg foo tɩ zaalg zugu, la bee n da ya f zĩiga, n tɩ sel foo tɩɩg sẽn tũus zugu, la yaool n ka be la f zĩigã, fo zɩ tɩ b na lebs tɩ-sõnga wil n sel b zĩigẽ!
45011025	Bũmb n ket n nan ka puk d yĩnga la m pa rat n solg-y ye, m saam-biisi, tɩ y ra wa yet tɩ y sẽn mi wã sek-y lame ye; Israyɛl bogr kidba a sũuri al tɩ bu-zẽmba fãa wa sak tẽebo,
45011026	t'a zãng-zãnga yaool n paam n põse, wala sẽn gʋlse: «Fãagda na n yii Siõ, a na n peka a Zakoob rẽgda fãa.
45011027	La m sã n pek b yel-wẽna n sɛ, yaa zood la m na n yõg ne-ba.»
45011028	Zʋɩf rãmba sã n kɩɩs Koe-noogã n lebg Wẽnd bɛɛba, tɩ yãmb yell tũ rẽ n manege, ad-y Wẽnd boollã yĩnga, la b ba rãmb yĩnga, b ket n yaa Wẽnd zo-rãmba.
45011029	Wẽnd ka kõt n le reeg ye, Wẽnd ka boond n le yeel tɩ vẽ ye.
45011030	Yãmb n yɩ wẽn-kɩɩsdb pĩnda tɩ Wẽnd yik rũnna n maan-y nimbãan-zoeere, Zʋɩf rãmba tõdgr yĩnga.
45011031	Bãng-y tɩ yaa rẽnd me yĩnga la Zʋɩf rãmb me yik n lebg tõatba, n na n paam rũnna Wẽnd nimbãan-zoeerã.
45011032	Wẽnd kẽesa ninsaalb buud fãa kɩɩsg pʋgẽ sẽn na n yɩlẽ n wilg b fãa b nimbãan-zoeere.
45011033	Wẽnnaam, y arzɛka geels toɛ yã, y minim la y bãngr zulma! Ad-y ned ka tõe n bãng y sẽn pʋɩt y yɛla toto ye, ned ka tar y soy wã buk ye!
45011034	Ãnda n zoe n tõog n bãng Soaala tagsgo, ãnda n paam n yɩ b sagenda?
45011035	Ãnda n yɩ pipi n paam n kõ Wẽnde tɩ bãmb na n yaool n bao n lebse?
45011036	Fãa yita bãmb nengẽ, bãmb n maan fãa, fãa yaa b soolem. Bɩ b paam pẽgre sẽn ka be sɛɛbo. Amina!
45012001	Wẽnd sẽn ya nimbãan-zoeta yĩnga, m saam-biisi, m kota ned kam fãa t'a rɩka meng n kõ Wẽnde n lebg maoong vɩɩga, maoong sõmbo, maoong sẽn tat b yam: woto la y na n waoog Wẽnnaam ne waoogr akɩka.
45012002	Da wẽneg-y zamaana rãmb ye; modg-y n paam yam paale n tedg zãnga n tõog n bãng Wẽnnaam daabo, n bãng sẽn ya neere, sẽn ya sõmbo, sẽn ka tar goaleng ba bilfu.
45012003	M togsd-y la a yeyn-ye la y fãa gilli, ne Wẽnd sẽn maan-m nimbãan-zoeer ningã: ned ba a ye ra sak n pẽga meng tɩ loog ye. Ned kam fãa pa a zĩigẽ n zems tẽebã a sẽn paam Wẽnd nengẽ.
45012004	Tõnd ne d tar yĩng a ye wã, d yĩnga wils yaa kʋʋngo, la wilg fãa le tara a tʋʋmde.
45012005	Woto-me, tõnd ne d ya kʋʋngã, d naaga Krista n ya yĩng a ye; ned kam fãa yaa waa a to wilga.
45012006	Yaa kũun toɛ-toɛ la d paam Wẽnd nengẽ, dɩlla bɩ d modg tɩ sã n ya bãngr kũun la d paam yã bɩ d tʋm bãngr tʋʋmde wala d tẽeba sẽn tõe tɛka.
45012007	Sã n ya taab sõngre, bɩ d wɩng ne sõngre; sã n ya taab zãmsgo, bɩ d zãms-ba;
45012008	sã n ya taab saglgo, bɩ d sagl. Sẽn kõt-a kõ n da geel ye; sẽn deeg-a kãsengo maan moadg, sẽn kũmda a taab nimbãaneg yõgem a noore.
45012009	Modg-y tɩ belgr da zĩnd taab nonglma pʋgẽ ye, kisg-y wẽnga la tabend-y sẽn ya neer mepi!
45012010	Modg-y n nong taab wa ba-biisi la ned kam fãa ning a to sʋka.
45012011	Yɩ-y neb sẽn tʋmd n ka vʋʋsdẽ ye, neb sũur sẽn kɛɛd ne Soaala tũumde.
45012012	Y sũ-nooga yi y saagra pʋgẽ, y namsga wa ne y raoodo; y pʋʋsga ra yãk wakat ye,
45012013	nin-sõma wã yell gesg yɩ y tʋʋmd pakre, la sãamba fãa paam y gãag-sobendo.
45012014	Sẽn namsd-b yãmbã, kos-y tɩ Wẽnd bark sig b zugu; yeel-y tɩ Wẽnd na manege, da yeel-y tɩ Wẽnd na sãam ye.
45012015	Kɩdm-y sũ-noog ne ned ninga sẽn tar-a sũ-noogo; kiig-y nintãm ne sẽn yãbda.
45012016	Bʋk-y y sũur ne neba fãa gilli, kisg-y zẽk-m-menga; bao-y sulg-m-meng rãmba; da yeel-y tɩ y bãngra sekame ye.
45012017	Da maan-y wẽng n dol wẽng ye; bao-y neb fãa sẽn get wa bõn-sõng bala.
45012018	Modg-y wa y sẽn tõe tɛka tɩ y zĩnd-n-taar yɩ noog ne ned kam fãa.
45012019	Da kõ-y y meng bʋʋm ye, bas yã, m kom-sõma, tɩ b rɩ beem ne-yã, tɩ gʋlsa woto: Yaa maam n na n kao bʋʋdo, yaa maam n na n kõ rolbo.
45012020	N yɩɩd rẽ, f bɛ sã n yãbd kom bɩ f kõ-a t'a rɩ, ko-yũud sã n tar-a bɩ f kõ-a t'a yũ. F maan dẽ, yaa yãnd la f ningd-a.
45012021	Da bas tɩ wẽng tõog-f ye, la ning pãng n tõog wẽnga ne neer maanego.
45013001	Ned kam fãa sak taoor dãmbã. Ned ka so a to, Wẽnd sã n ka kõ a soab tõog ye. Tõog buud fãa yita Wẽnnaam nengẽ.
45013002	Ned ning fãa sẽn ka reegd a soaal noor, tõdgda Wẽnd noore la tõat fãa baooda a meng paalgre.
45013003	Ad-y d sã n maand neere, d ka tog n zoe bʋ-kaoodba ye; sẽn zoet-a bʋ-kaood yaa sẽn maanda wẽnga; fo sã n ka rat n dig rabeem sẽn so-b fooma taoore, bɩ f maan neere n paam b pẽgre.
45013004	Wẽnd datame tɩ ned sã n so a to bɩ a sõng-a ne neer maanego; f sã n maand wẽnga bɩ f maan dabeem; bãng tɩ sʋʋga sẽn be soaalba nugẽ ka zaalem yĩng ye; sʋʋga yaa sõng Wẽnd n kao bʋʋdo, n sɩbg bɛɛgd buud fãa.
45013005	Ad-y noora ka reegd sɩbgr dabeem yĩng bala, reegd-a lame tɩ y sũurẽ wã, koɛɛg n zoe n leokd boto.
45013006	M sok n gese, y sẽn yaood yõor yaoodã, ka y sẽn ne tɩ segdame sɩda? Rẽ me la Wẽnd yãk neb tʋʋmd kãng yĩnga.
45013007	Kɩs-y ned kam fãa a sẽn sokd-y bũmb ninga: yõora yaood, sã n ya rẽ la a sokda, raag ligdi, sã n ya raag ligdi; zoe-y y sẽn tog n zoe a soaba, waoog-y y sẽn tog n waoog a soaba.
45013008	Da rɩɩ-y ned ba a ye samde sã n ka nong taab samdã. Sẽn nong-a a to pidsa noora zãnga.
45013009	Noor ning sẽn yet tɩ f ra yo ye, ra kʋ ye, da zu ye, da tʋlg f to bũmbu, la sẽn ket-ba fãa, kʋmsame n lebg woto: nong f to n wẽnd f menga.
45013010	Sẽn nonga a to ka maand-a kegr ye. Taab nonglem pidsda noɛ a taaba fãa gilli.
45013011	Y mii tõnd sẽn vɩ zamaan ning pʋgẽ. Ad-y gõeema nekr taame, fãagra pẽneg-d la marsã n yɩɩd d sẽn paam tẽeba wakato.
45013012	Zĩig zʋʋgame. Beoog yaoome. D bas d likẽ tʋʋma la d yi vẽenemẽ ne d zab teedo.
45013013	D tall d meng ne waoogr wa sẽn segd wĩndga. D da yɩ rɩ-rɩtb la kokoraad ye. D bas yoob la yaoolg buud fãa. D bas zab la sũ-kiiri.
45013014	D yeelg Soaal a Zezi Krista wa fuugu la d da tags d yĩngã yelle n baood n na n pids a tʋls yooda ye.
45014001	Da bas-y ned kɛɛnga, a tẽeb sẽn pa sɩd yĩng ye la gãneg-y y no-koɛɛma.
45014002	Kẽer beeme n yet tɩ rɩɩb ka be bãmb sẽn kis ye, tɩ kẽer bee n yet tɩ bãmb a ka pãng rãmbã dɩta vãad bala.
45014003	Sẽn dɩt-a ra sãbs sẽn ka rɩt-a ye. Sẽn ka rɩt-a me ra sãbs sẽn dɩt-a ye, tɩ Wẽnd ka reega a soab wẽng ye.
45014004	Foom la a bõe tɩ f to sõgen sẽn maand pak-fo? A yɛs yĩngri bɩ a gãe tẽnga, dẽ paka a zu-soab bala. A pʋs n na n yalsa yĩngri tɩ Soaala pãng seka a yĩngr yalsgo.
45014005	Yõaa soab pẽgda daar a ye n yɩɩd a to, yõaa soab nengẽ daar fãa zema a to, ned kam fãa maan wa a sũur koɛɛga sẽn yet t'a gãd bũmb ninga.
45014006	Ned ninga sẽn welgd-a raar ne a to welgd-a-la Soaala yĩnga. Ned ninga sẽn dɩt-a, dɩta Soaala yĩnga n pẽgd Wẽnde. La ned ninga sẽn ka rɩt-a, yaa Soaala yĩng la a basd rɩɩbo la a pẽgda Wẽnde.
45014007	Tõnd sʋka, ned ka be sẽn vɩ-a a meng yĩng ye la ned me ka be sẽn kiid-a a meng yĩng ye.
45014008	D sã n vɩ d vɩɩ Soaala yĩnga, d sã n kiidẽ, d kiida Soaala yĩnga. D vɩ bɩ d kiida, Soaala n so-do.
45014009	Krista kiime n le vʋʋge, n na n lebg sẽn ki-b la sẽn vɩ-b Soaala.
45014010	Foo la a bõe n na n bʋ f to, foo la a bõe n na n sãbs f to? Wẽnd bal n na n kao d fãa bʋʋdo wala sẽn gʋlse:
45014011	M wẽenda (yaa Soaala meng n gomde) tɩ rũmd buud fãa na n yĩgimda m taoore la zelemd buud fãa na n pẽg-m lame.
45014012	Dat n yeelame tɩ bũmb ning sẽn ya d zugẽ yelle, yaa tõnd ned kam fãa n na n togs-a Wẽnde, d toore.
45014013	D vẽ d taab bʋʋdo. D bãng bal tɩ d ka tõe n dɩgl bũmb d to taoore t'a wa lak n lʋɩ ye.
45014014	M miime, la Soaala taoore m sũur pa kiuusd ye, m miime tɩ rɩɩb ka be n kis a meng yĩng ye, a kisa sẽn yet-a tɩ kisame wã yĩnga.
45014015	Ade, fo sã n sãamd f to sũur dɩɩb poorẽ, fo ka le maand taab nonglem sẽn dat ye; da sak-y tɩ y sẽn gomd rɩɩb ninga yellã wa ne a kũum ye, tɩ Krista zoe n kila a yĩnga.
45014016	Da bas-y tɩ b wa sãbs y zu-nooga sẽn kõ-y ye.
45014017	Wẽnd Rĩunga ka rɩɩb la rãam yell ye, a yaa sõmblem, laafi ne sũ-noog sẽn paamd a Vʋʋsem Sõng nengẽ.
45014018	Ned ninga sẽn baooda Krista woto, yẽ soab noogd-a Wẽnd sũuri la a paamda ninsaalb pẽgre.
45014019	Woto wã bɩ d pʋg bũmb ning sẽn kõt laafi la sẽn paasd daoodo.
45014020	Da saag n sãam Wẽnnaam tʋʋmd dɩɩb poorẽ ye. Dɩɩb ka be n ya yoog a meng yĩng ye, a sã ya yoogo yaa wala rɩ-rɩta tũu rɩɩbã n kʋɩɩb a taaba.
45014021	Sẽn be neere, yaa bas nemdo, rãam la bũmb fãa sẽn wat ne f taab lʋɩɩse, sẽn komsd f taaba pãnga.
45014022	Sõng n tall f tẽebã f sũurẽ la Wẽnd taoore. Pẽg-y ned ninga sẽn dengda n ges a tõeeme bɩ a ka tõe n yaool n sɩng bũmb maanego.
45014023	La yell na pak ned ninga sẽn ges-a rɩɩbo wa ka rɩɩb a sẽn tõe n dɩ n baas n dɩt-a; wakat kãnga a ka rɩ ne pʋ-peelem ye, la bũmb ning fãa sẽn ka maan ne pʋ-peelem yaa yel-wẽnde.
45015001	Yaa pakre ne tõnd a pãng rãmbã tɩ d sõng sẽn ka tar b tõnd pãngã; yaa pakr ne-do tɩ d bas d yamleoog maanego.
45015002	Ned kam fãa modg n noog a to sũuri tɩ rẽ la neere la rẽ n paasd a raoodo.
45015003	Krista ka pʋg sẽn noom-b ye, tɩ yaa woto la b gʋlsyã: «Sẽn tʋʋs-b yãmba long n tʋʋsa maam.»
45015004	Sɩda, bũmb ning fãa sẽn zoe n gʋlse, b gʋlsa la tõnd vẽnegr yĩnga. Sebr sõng paasda tõnd daoodo la a maagda d sũuri la rẽ kɩtame tɩ d zĩ ne saagre.
45015005	Tõe-m-meng soab Wẽndã la sẽn mi a ninsaal nintãm yẽesgã na sõng yãmb tɩ y sũk nonglem sũkr y taab yĩnga wa Krista sẽn maan d yĩnga.
45015006	Woto y na tõog n pẽg Wẽnnaam, tõnd Soaal a Zezi Krista Ba, ne sũur a ye la noor a ye.
45015007	Ning-y pãng n koll taab wala Krista sẽn koll-y, Wẽnnaam pẽgr yĩnga.
45015008	M le yet-y lame, tɩ sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ Wẽnd pids b sẽn kãab d yaab rãmba, Krista gesa sẽn kẽ-b bãong yelle,
45015009	al tɩ bu-zẽmba pẽgd b nimbãan-zoeere wala sẽn gʋls sebr pʋgẽ: «M na n pẽg-y la bu-zẽmba sʋka la m na n kilsa y yʋʋre.»
45015010	D le karemda zĩig a to: «Bu-zẽmba, naag-y m neba n kɩdme.»
45015011	Zĩig a to yɛsa: «Bu-zẽmba, pẽg-y Soaala la maan-y kibs b yĩnga.»
45015012	T'a Izayi na n paas woto: «A na n waame, a Zese biiga na n waame n kẽes bu-zẽmba a soolmẽ la b fãa na n dɩka b yɛlã n bas ne bãmba.»
45015013	D sẽn teeg Wẽnd ninga na pids yãmba, y tẽeba yĩnga, ne sũ-noog la laafi. Wẽnd na kɩt tɩ y saagra pids zãnga ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng pãnga.
45015014	M mii vẽenega, m saam-biisi, tɩ y sũur pida ne raab sõma la y yam pida ne bãngre al tɩ y tõe n sagl y taaba.
45015015	Baasgo m sã n gʋls yã al tɩ zĩis kẽer bɩ y tõe n yɛɛse, bãng-y tɩ yaa m sẽn dat n le nek y pʋtẽerã.
45015016	M dat n le tẽeg y lame tɩ Wẽnd yeel-m lame tɩ m yɩ wa maan-kʋʋd bu-zẽmba sʋka, Wẽnd Koe-nooga maan-kʋʋda, n kɩt tɩ bu-zẽmba lebg kũuni, kũuni a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn maneg tɩ tat Wẽnd yam.
45015017	Wẽnnaam sora tʋʋmd poorẽ, m tõe n zẽka m zugu, Krista maasem yĩnga.
45015018	M kõn saag n gom bũmb a to yelle sã n ka Krista sẽn sõng-m tɩ m kẽes bu-zẽmba, tẽeba sor pʋgẽ, ne m goam la m tʋʋmde,
45015019	ne wẽnd makr dãmba la bõn-bãna, ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng pãnga. Bãng-y tɩ bãmb maasem yĩnga, m saaga Zerizalɛɛm la Illiri zãnga, n moon Krista Koe-noogã.
45015020	La ade, m maana gũusgu; m sẽn kẽ tẽns niynsi, yaa zĩig ning b sẽn dag n nan ka pʋd Krista yʋʋr tɩ m da pa rat n me zĩig ning neda to sẽn dag n zoe n sɩng meeb ye.
45015021	M tʋlg n maana wa sẽn gʋls Sebr sõng pʋgẽ: B sẽn dag n zɩ n gom a soab yell ne b rãmbã na n yãend-a lame; neb niyns sẽn dag n zɩ n wʋm tɩ b gomd a yellã yam na n vẽnegame.
45015022	Ad-y yaa m tʋʋma n kɩt tɩ m nan ka tõog n ta y nengẽ ye.
45015023	La marsã m tẽedame tɩ m na yaa n tõoge. M sẽn dat n wa y sʋka raar yaa n vẽsgame; la kaalẽ, rũna-rũna, m ka le tar tʋʋmd ye.
45015024	M tẽedame tɩ m na tũ y nengẽ m sã n wa rabd Ispaniya. Sɩda, m saagdame tɩ d na yãend taaba n dɩ sõs ne taaba sũ-noogo, la m na paam y sõngre n tõog n ta Ispaniya.
45015025	Marsã m dabda Zerizalɛɛm n na n tɩ sõng m saam-biisã.
45015026	Masedoan la Akayi rãmb n tẽega b naonga yelle. B sõnga Zerizalɛɛm dãmb ne yamleoogo, yaa sɩda,
45015027	la mam yamẽ wã, b maana sẽn ya tɩlɛ ne-ba. Zerizalɛɛm sõnga bu-zẽmbã ne Soaala kũuni la yaa rẽ yĩng la m yet tɩ togame tɩ bu-zẽmba lebs-ba ne bãmb mens sẽn tar b nugẽ.
45015028	Dɩlla yell kãnga sã n welg n sɛ, m sã n ta m toor n kɩs ligdã, m na tũ yãmb tẽnga n yaool n ta Ispaniya.
45015029	Bãng-y tɩ m sã n poog y tẽngã, yaa Krista kũun buud fãa la m na n zã n wa kõ yã.
45015030	M saam-biisi, bũmb la m na n kos-y tõnd Soaal a Zezi Krista yĩnga la a Vʋʋsem Sõng nonglem yĩnga. M na n kos-y lame tɩ y sã n modgd n pʋʋsd m yĩnga,
45015031	bɩ y pʋʋs tɩ m põs wẽn-kɩɩsdba sẽn ket Zɩɩde tẽnga la m tõog n ta Zerizalɛɛm ne m kũuna n noog saam-biisa sũur be.
45015032	Woto m na lɛɛg n wa y sʋk ne sũ-noogo la m vʋʋs ne laafi, Wẽnd maasem yĩnga.
45015033	Laafi Naaba-Wẽnd zĩnd ne yã. Ami!
45016001	M kotame tɩ y sõng m tão nongr a Febe; a bee Sẽnkre, n ya be Tigeng sõangd poaka.
45016002	Krista yĩnga, reeg-y pʋg kãnga sãando wala sẽn segd ne nin-sõma. A sẽn tar bũmb ning fãa tʋʋmd tɩ y tõe n sõng-a bɩ y sõng-a ne. Bãng-y t'a kolla neere Krist neb wʋsgo, la mam menga.
45016003	M Pʋʋs-y sõnga maam Krista tʋʋmda pʋgẽ, a Priska ne a Akilas.

46004014	M ka gʋlsd woto n dat n ning y yãnd ye, m datame bal n sagl yã tɩ m nong-y la wʋsgo.
46004015	Ba y ya karen-biis sẽn tar neb ka tɛk sẽn get y yelle, Krista tũudma pʋgẽ, bãng-y tɩ y ka tar ba rãmb kʋʋng ye. Yaa maam bal n dog-y Krista buudẽ ne Koe-nooga moonego.
46004016	Dẽ la m kot-y tɩ y wẽneg maam.
46004017	La yaa rẽ me yĩng la m tʋm a Timote y nengẽ: a yaa m bi-nongre la a pelga a pʋg ne Krista tũudem. A na tẽeg-y m sẽn yals bũmb ninga Krista tũudma poorẽ, la m sẽn zãmsd Tigeng kamba fãa.
46004018	Kẽer tẽeme tɩ m ka na n wa y nengẽ n yik n tãoosd daoodo.
46004019	Yaool n ka na n le kaoos tɩ m ta y nengẽ, Wẽnd sã n sake. Wakat kãng la m bãngd b tɩtaama sã n yita b pãngẽ bɩ sã n teka noor goam bala.
46004020	Wẽnd Rĩunga ka goam bala, a naaga ne Wẽnd pãng tʋʋma.
46004021	Bõe la y nonga? M wa y nengẽ ne sãbse bɩ m wa ne nonglem la sũ-maasem?
46005001	D wʋmdame tɩ yoob goam bal n gomd yãmb sʋka la yoob buud meng sẽn ka yãet bu-zẽmba nengẽ; b gomdame tɩ yãmb nin-yend n tol n vɩ ne a ba paga.
46005002	Bõe tɩ y ket n wukd ne tɩtaam? Bõe tɩ y ka kelem kʋʋre la y kɩtẽ tɩ b yiis y sʋka, tʋʋm dẽgd a woto soaba?
46005003	Ade, m ka be y sʋk ne m yĩnga ye; m bee ne m yam la m zoe n kaoo yell a woto soab bʋʋdo wa m beẽ la y sʋka ne m yĩngã.
46005004	Togame tɩ Soaala Zezi yʋʋr yĩnga yãmb ne maam, tɩ m bee y sʋk ne m yama, ba sã n ka ne m yĩngã, togame tɩ d naag taab ne d Soaala Zezi pãnga,
46005005	n bas nin-kãnga ne Sʋtãan t'a sãam a yĩngã, t'a sɩɩga wa paam fãagre, Soaala raare.
46005006	Y zẽk-m-menga ka be zĩig ye! Y ka mi tɩ rabɩll bilfr bal tõeeme tɩ zoma fãa wuki?
46005007	Menes-y y rabɩll kʋdgã n lebg zom paalga, n tõog n yɩ bur sẽn ka lob bɩlle. Bãng-y tɩ Krista, tõnd Pak, kʋʋme.
46005008	Bɩ d kɩdem kibsa sũ-noogo la ra yɩ ne bur sẽn lob bɩll kʋdgã, ra yɩ ne d wẽnema la d pʋ-tooga rabɩlle, d kɩdem ne bur sẽn lob pʋ-peelem la sõmblem rabɩlle.
46005009	M sẽn yeel-y m sebra pʋgẽ tɩ y ra maan zĩnd-n-taar ne yoaadba,
46005010	ad-y m da ka gomd dũni wã yoaadba ye, m ka naagd raab waglã la fãadba ye, m ka naagd sẽn pʋʋsdb wẽn-faad ye. Sã n yaẽ la boto, yaẽ la tɩlɛ tɩ y fãa yiẽ dũniya.
46005011	M yeel-y lame bal tɩ y ra saag n maan zĩnd-n-taare ne ned sẽn yet t'a yaa yãmb saam-biiga a tẽeba pʋgẽ, n yaool n ya yoaada, yão-be-neda, wẽn-faad waoogda, n nong a taab paoogre, n woond arzɛgs n samdẽ. M yeelame menga tɩ y ra sak tɩ ned a woto yɩ y rɩt-n-taag ye.
46005012	Sẽn ka lagem-b tõnd ne tẽebo n yaa d saam-biisã, m yɩta wãn n kaood bãmb bʋʋdo? Ka sẽn be-b Tigenga pʋg bʋʋd la y bʋʋd laa?
46005013	Yɩng rãmbã, Wẽnd n kaood bãmb bʋʋdo. Wẽng ning sẽn be yãmb sʋka la y tog n menese.
46006001	Zabr sã n yik yãmb ne taab sʋka, bõe tɩ y boond taab bʋʋd bu-zẽmba taoore, n ka na n kẽng Wẽnd kamba taoore?
46006002	Bɩ y yĩmame tɩ yaa bãmb n na n kao dũni wã bʋʋdo? La sã n ya yãmb n na n kao dũni bʋʋdo, bõe tɩ y maand wa y ka tõe n bʋ yell faadã?
46006003	Y ka mi tɩ ba malɛgsã, tõnd n na n bʋ-b laa? Tɩ b pa gomd vɩɩm kãnga yɛlã!
46006004	Y sã n tar no-koɛɛm ne taab tẽng zug yɛla poorẽ, bõe yɩng la y paasdba na n yɩ Tigengu sẽn ka pẽgd b rãmba?
46006005	Ad-y m zoe n ningd-y la yãnde m sã n sok ned sã n ka be y sʋka n tar yẽesem n tõe n welg y yɛla,
46006006	tɩ y tat y saam-biis n dabd bʋʋd bu-zẽmba taoore!
46006007	Sɩd me, y sẽn tar bʋʋd ne taaba zoe n yaa y kongr kaseto. Y sẽn sakd n deeg kegr ka são? Y sẽn basd tɩ b fã-y ka são?
46006008	La ayɛy! Ka woto la y maand ye; yãmb n lɛɛg n maand y taab kɛga la y fãad-ba, la yaool n yaa y saam-biisi!
46006009	Y zɩ tɩ sẽn maand-b kɛg ka tar pʋɩɩr Wẽnd Rĩung pʋgẽ laa? Da belg-y y meng ye: yoaadba, sẽn waoogd-b bõn-naandse, dataase, sẽn nong-b wẽnga, sẽn maand-b wɩɩbdo,
46006010	wagdba, dat-wʋsg-rãmba, dã-yũud bɛda, sẽn paoogd-b taaba, fãadba, bãmb ned ba a ye kõn paam Arzãn Rĩung ye.
46006011	La ka y zãng me, yãmb wʋsg ra yaa boto. Marsã y pekame, y tara sõmblem, y paama fãagre, Soaal a Zezi Krista la d Wẽnnaama Vʋʋsem pãng yĩnga.
46006012	Neb kẽer n gomda: «M tõe n maana m sẽn dat fãa.» La m na leoke tɩ ka m sẽn tõe n maan fãa n ya yõod ne m ye. M tõe n maana fãa la m kõn saag n lebg m manesem yem-daoog ye.
46006013	Dɩɩb bee pʋg yĩnga, tɩ pʋg me be rɩɩb yĩnga la Wẽnd n na n sɛɛs b yiiba fãa. Yĩnga ka be yoob yĩng ye; yĩnga yaa Soaalã n so, la yĩnga me rɩta Soaala yõodo.
46006014	Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋg Krista na n vʋʋga tõnd me ne b pãngã.
46006015	Y zɩ tɩ y yĩnsa yaa Krista yĩnga wilsi? La maanda a wãna tɩ Krista yĩnga n wa lebg woto n ka bak ne pʋg-yoodr yĩnga? Dẽ ka tõe ye.
46006016	Y zɩ tɩ ned ning sẽn lagemd ne pʋg-yoodre lebgda yĩng a ye ne a? Woto la gʋls yã: B yiiba na n lebga yĩng a ye.
46006017	Sã n ya sẽn lagma ne Krista, yẽ soab me lebga yam a ye ne Bãmba.
46006018	Zoe-y yoobo! Yɛl a taaba ninsaal sẽn maand pa sog ne a yĩng ye la ned ninga sẽn maanda yoob maanda wẽng ne a yĩnga.
46006019	Sãnd y miime tɩ y yĩnga yaa a Vʋʋsem Sõng roogo? B bee ne yãmb la Wẽnd n kõ-b yãmba. Y zɩ tɩ y ka so y menga?
46006020	Ad-y yaa ligd la b kɩs n deeg yã! Modg-y tɩ y yĩnga pẽg Wẽnde.
46007001	Sebr ning y sẽn gʋlsã la m na n ges marsã. La y yeta y sebra pʋgẽ tɩ yaa sõmbo rao ne pag sã n zãr taaba.
46007002	La sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ y põs ne yɛl kɛga, bɩ rao tar paga, tɩ pag me tar sɩda.
46007003	Rao sak a paga tɩ paga me sak a sɩda.
46007004	Paga ka so a yĩng ye, yaa sɩdã n so. Botome raoa ka so a yĩnga, yaa pagã n so.
46007005	Da zãgs-y taab ye, sã n ka y seda rẽ, n na n maan pʋʋsgo. La rẽnd poore, bɩ y pa ne taaba tɩ Sʋtãan da wa bẽd y ka tõe y mensã, n kʋɩɩb-y ye.
46007006	M sẽn gom marsa wã yaa yãmb sẽn tõe bũmb ningã, la ka pakr ye.
46007007	M tʋllẽ lame tɩ y fãa yɩẽ wa maam; la m miime tɩ ned kam fãa paamda Wẽnd nengẽ kũun sẽn tog ne-a: yãoo soab wã, yãoo soab woto.
46007008	Neb niyns sẽn ka kẽ-b kãadem la pʋg-kõapa, m yet-b lame tɩ b sã n pa wa maam, yaa neere.
46007009	La b sã n ka tõe b mense, bɩ b kẽ kãadem tɩ rẽ n são bugum sẽn dɩt-b.
46007010	Sã n ya kãadbã, ad noore, la ka mam noore ye, yaa Soaala rẽnna: bɩ pag ra welg ne a sɩd ye,
46007011	-la-la welgr sã n kẽ sʋka, a ra le rɩk sɩda; ka rẽnn bɩ a leb a sɩd kʋdga nengẽ tɩ b le zems taaba. – Daoã me da yiis a pag ye.
46007012	Yɛla taab n kete, la ka Soaala n gomd ye, yaa maam: saam-biig sã n tar paga sẽn nan ka tar tẽebo la sẽn sak n na n zĩnd ne-a, bɩ a ra yiis-a ye.
46007013	Pag me sã n tara sɩda sẽn nan ka tar tẽebo la sẽn sakd n na n zĩnd ne-a, a ra bas-a ye.
46007014	Sɩda sẽn nan ka paam tẽebã sõmblem na n yi-la a paga nengẽ. Botome pag ning sẽn nan ka paam-a tẽebã sõmblem na n yi-la a sɩda nengẽ. Sã n da kaẽ boto, y kamba yaẽ la kom-dẽgdo la Wẽnd bark yaool n sig-b lame.
46007015	Ned ninga sẽn ka paam-a tẽebã sã n dat n loog bɩ a looge: sã n ya woto saam-biiga sẽn tẽedã yi-la a loɛɛgẽ. Wẽnd bool-y lame tɩ y vɩɩnd laafi vɩɩm.
46007016	Paga, f mi-la f na fãag f sɩda? Sɩda, f mi-la f na fãag f paga?
46007017	Sẽn paase, yaa ned kam fãa kell n vɩɩnd wa Wẽnd boolla sẽn mik-a zĩig ninga. Yaa woto la m zãmsd saam-biisa fãa Tigeng pʋgẽ.
46007018	Wẽnd boolla mik-f lame tɩ f ya zũnga, pa zũnga; boolla mik-f lame tɩ f ka kẽ bãongo, bas bãong kõom.
46007019	Kẽe bãong yaa zaalem, ka kẽ bãong me yaa zaalem; sẽn pak yaa Wẽnnaam noya reegre.
46007020	Bɩ ned kam fãa pa Wẽnd boolla sẽn tuk-a zĩig ninga.
46007021	Boolga wakat tɩ f ra yaa yamba, bɩ rẽ ra lebg f zu-loɛɛg ye. F sã n tõe n lebg burkĩnd me bɩ f bao n dɩ f yembda yõodo.
46007022	Ned ninga sẽn da yaa yamb a boolg wakata bãng t'a lebga Soaala burkĩna La sẽn da yaa burkĩna a boolga wakat lebga Krista yamba.
46007023	La sɩda, b raa yãmba! Da leb-y ninsaalb yembdẽ ye.
46007024	Bɩ ned kam fãa pa Wẽnd taoore wala Wẽnd boolla sẽn tuk-a.
46007025	Sã n ya kom-pugli sẽn nan ka kẽb kãadma poorẽ, m ka paam Soaala noor ye, m togsda m sẽn tagsde, wala Soaala nimbãan-zoeer sẽn sig a soaba t'a goam sek kelgre la reegre.
46007026	M tagsdame tɩ ned sã n pa wa m sẽn wilgã n sãoẽ, d sã n get d rũnna-rũnna pɛtã.
46007027	F kẽe kãadem ne paga, da bao welgr ye. F ka kẽ kãadem ne-a, ra bao kãadem ye.
46007028	La f sã n baood kãadem bɩ f ra tẽ tɩ f maana wẽng ye. La bi-pugl me sã n kẽ kãadem, a ka maand yel-wẽnd ye. Ya b sẽn na n yãe toog b yĩngẽ wã la m datẽ tɩ b tɩlgẽ dẽ.
46007029	Maam n yet yã, m saam-biisi: wakata ka zɛɛd ye. Sẽn tar-b pagb vɩɩnd wala b sã n da ka tarẽ ye.
46007030	Sẽn daagd-b nintãm wala b ka yãbd ye; sẽn langd-b sũ-noogo wala b ka kɩdemd ye; sẽn maand-b leebgo wa b pa tar fɩ ye;
46007031	sẽn dɩt-b zamaana yõodo wala b pa rɩt-a meng ye, tɩ y mi tɩ zamaana neng ka na n zɛ teoong ye.
46007032	M datẽ lame tɩ y zãrẽ ne yɩɩr buud fãa. Rao ning sẽn ka kẽ kãadem yaa Soaala yɛl la a lʋɩɩsd taoore, n gẽesd a sẽn na n yɩlẽ n ta b yam.
46007033	Sẽn kẽ-a kãadem sẽn lʋɩɩsd taoore yaa dũni wã yɛla, yaa a sẽn na n yɩlẽ n ta a pag yam,
46007034	la ad-a sẽn pʋɩ a yiibu. Pag sẽn ka tar sɩda, la pa-kuli, bãmb me lʋɩɩsda Soaala taoore; b naag n baooda b yĩnga la b sɩɩga sõmblem. Sẽn kul-a sɩd lʋɩɩsda rũnda vɩɩma taoore, n baood n na n noog a sɩd sũuri.
46007035	M gomda woto y sõngr yĩnga, ka bẽdg la m gãnegd-y ye, m datame tɩ y yama zẽk n tees sẽn ya neere la a tabend Soaala n ka pʋɩ zĩis a yiib ye.
