46007036	Fo maanda wa f sẽn date, kãadem goam sãn zoe n gomame tɩ foo ne bi-pugla nan ket n paoodẽ la f neeme marsã tɩ kãadma sã pa yi na yɩɩ toog ne foo, Fo tõe n kẽe kãadem la f ka maand yel-wẽnd ye.
46007037	La ned sũur sã n gãd kẽnkẽ, tɩ moadg ka lʋɩ sʋka, t'a sed ne yamleoogo t'a kõn yi kãadem ne biig ning a sẽn da pʋlem a menga, a maanda neere.
46007038	Dɩlla sẽn kẽeda kãadem ne bi-pugl ning a sẽn da pʋlem a menga, maanda neere, la sẽn ka kẽeda kãadma n maand neer n yɩɩda.
46007039	Pag bãng t'a sɩd sã n ket n vɩ a ka tõe n welg ne a ye. A sɩda sã n kaẽ la a tõe n kẽ ne a sẽn dat a soaba, la yɩta Soaala maasmẽ bala.
46007040	La sã n ya mam sẽn tagsde, a vɩɩm na yɩ-a noog n yɩɩda, a sã n pa wa a sẽn ya-lã. M me tẽedame tɩ m sẽn leok woto wã yaa ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsma vẽnegre.
46008001	Sɩda, sã n ya maanda sẽn kʋʋd wẽn-naandsa yĩnga, d fãa yetame tɩ d miime; m deegame. La ade, bãngr wata ne wilg-m-menga. To nonglem bal n zẽkd ninsaala.
46008002	Ned sã n yet t'a mii bũmbu, a bãng tɩ baasgo, ka waa a sẽn teeda zãng ye.
46008003	Sẽn nong-a Wẽnnaam, Wẽnnaam me mii yẽ soaba.
46008004	Dẽ wã, sã ya rũmsa nemd wãbre, rũms niyns sẽn kʋʋd bõn-naandsa yĩngã, d miime tɩ wẽn-naand yaa zaalem, dũni pʋgẽ, la Wẽnnaam b ye tãa la Wẽnde.
46008005	Ba bũmb sã n be yĩngri bɩ tẽng zugu tɩ b get-b wa wẽnde -la sɩda wʋsg beeme n boond tɩ wẽnd dãmba, n boond tɩ dũni soaalba –
46008006	tõnd nengẽ Wẽnd yaa b ye tãa, yaa Wẽnd Ba, bũmb fãa sẽn yit a soab nenge la d sẽn vɩ a soab yĩnga, la d Soaala me yaa a ye, a Zezi Krista, bãmb nengẽ la bũmb fãa yita la bãmb yĩng la tõnd be.
46008007	Ka neba fãa n tar bãngr ye. Ade, kẽer sẽn bas wẽn-naandsa pʋgb nan ka zãag ye; la woto b wãbda maanda nemdã n tẽrẽ tɩ rũmsa kʋʋ wẽn-naands yĩnga la b sɩɩga rẽgemdame, b sẽn nan ka wɩsga yĩnga.
46008008	Ka rɩɩb n tõe tɩ d kolg Wẽnd n paas ye. D ka rɩ, bũmb pa woogde, d rɩ yã, bũmb ka paasde.
46008009	Y sã n kõ y meng tɩ y tõeeme bɩ y pa tõe n dɩ, gũus-y bal tɩ y sẽn yalsã da wa ne koms rãmb lʋɩɩs ye.
46008010	Wala ned sã n yãend foo, foom a bãng-n-tɩgame soab, tɩ f rɩt wẽn-naands taoore, b waoogr zĩigẽ, nin-kãng sẽn nan ket n ya koamsã, a tẽebẽ wã, a ka na n tags t'a me tõe n wãba maand nemdo?
46008011	La woto wã, yaa fo bãngrã n lub koamsã yel-wẽndẽ. La yẽ me yaa f saam-biiga, la Krista ki-la a yĩnga.
46008012	Y saam-biisa sã n ket n ya koms rãmb b tẽebẽ tɩ yãmb manesma lub-b wẽng pʋgẽ, ad-y yaa Krista meng la y beg yã.
46008013	Woto wã m sã n ne tɩ rɩɩb na n luba m saam-biiga, m na bas nemd kãng zãng-zãnga, n da wa lub m saam-biiga ye.
46009001	Maam n pa so m meng bɩ bõe? Maam n pa Soaala tʋʋm-tʋmd bɩ bõe? Maam n pa yãend Soaal a Zezi bɩ bõe? M tʋʋmdã sẽn paam yõod Soaala nengẽ wã, ka yãmb laa?
46009002	M sã n ka tʋʋm-tʋmd neb a taab yĩnga, ne yãmb sẽ, m yaa tʋʋm-tʋmda, tɩ Soaala sã n baood m tʋʋmda kaseto, yaa yãmb la b ne yã.
46009003	M sẽn tar n na n leok sẽn dõt-b maama la woto:
46009004	d ka tar sor n dɩ la d yũ bɩ?
46009005	Sõangd poaka sẽn ya tẽeda n ka tar sor n yãag-do wala b sẽn yãagd tʋʋm-tʋmdb a taaba, Soaala saam-biisã, la a Kefas bɩ?
46009006	Bɩ yaa maam ne a Barnabe bal n ka tar sore n vʋʋs ne tʋʋmde?
46009007	Yaa ãnd n kẽed tãpo n le rɩt a meng ligdi? Ãnda n send tɩɩga tɩ b rigd a biis rɩɩbo? Ãnda n kɩɩmd rũmsi n ka rɩt b bĩisim?
46009008	La woto yaa ninsaalb n gomd bala, bɩ Noora me paasa bũmbu?
46009009	Yaa a Moyiiz Noora sebrẽ la b gʋls yã: «Naaf sã n tʋmd zɛɛgẽ bɩ f ra loe a noor ne yʋk ye.» La Wẽnd toog bee ne niisi?
46009010	Ka tõnd yĩng la a gomd sɩda? N-ye! Yaa tõnd yĩng la b gʋls yɛsa: Sẽn kood-a pʋʋg tẽeda bũmbu, tɩ sẽn pãbd-a ki zɛɛgẽ me tẽed a keoore.
46009011	D sã n bʋd yĩngr kũuna y sũurẽ, bõe n ka zemse d sã n tigsd sẽn wom y pʋtẽ?
46009012	Neb sã n beẽ n tar sor n dɩ y yõodo, ka tõnd n yɩɩde? D yaool n ka sak n maan boto ye. D sẽn mi yaa d sak toog buud fãa, tɩ d pa rat n kẽes gɩdgr Krista Koe-nooga moonegẽ ye.
46009013	Y zɩ tɩ wẽnd doogã n kõt a tʋʋm-tʋmdbã b rɩɩbo, tɩ maan-kugrã kõt a maan-kʋʋdba b rɩɩbo?
46009014	Woto-me, Soaala sẽn kõ b rãmb noor tɩ b moone Koe-noogã rɩta Koe-nooga sẽn kõt-b bala.
46009015	M yaool n ka rɩ b sẽn da segd n kõ-ma ye. La m ka gʋlsd-y wa m datame n paam n dɩ-y ye. Ayɛy! M sẽn kiid n são. Dẽ la m zu-zẽkre la ned kõn deeg-a n bas m zaalem ye.
46009016	Koe-nooga mooneg ne maam ka m zu-zẽkr bal ye, a yaa tʋʋm pakre n loe m zugu. N ye! Yell bela m zug, m sã n ka moon Koe-noogã!
46009017	Sã n yaẽ la maam la tʋʋmda zu-raoogo soaba m togẽ la ne rolbo; m sã n ka tar dolbã, dẽnd yaa zɩɩb la neda to zɩlg-ma.
46009018	Bõe n na n yɩ m dolbo? M tɛka yaa m paam n moon Koe-noogã tɩ ka tũ ne rolb ye, n ka reeg Koe-nooga sẽn tõe n kõ-m bũmb ning ye.
46009019	Ade, yãmb ned ba a ye ka ra maam waa a yamb ye la m sakame n lebg neba fãa yem-daoogo, sẽn na n yɩlẽ n wa paam bãmb ka tɛka.
46009020	M lebga Zʋɩf ne Zʋɩf rãmba, n na n paam Zʋɩf rãmba; m lebga Noora tũuda ne sẽn tũudb Noorã – la Noora tũub yaool n da ka le pak-m ye – n na n paam sẽn tũud-b Noora rãmba.
46009021	M lebga no-kɩɩsa ne Noora tõatba – m yaool n pa ned sẽn yiis a meng Wẽnd Noora tũudmẽ ye, tɩ m deegda Krista Noore – n na n paam sẽn ka tũud-b Noora rãmba.
46009022	M lebga koamsa ne koms rãmba n na n paam koms rãmba. M lebga neb fãa bũmbu, n na n fãag-ba, ba sã n ka b zãnga.
46009023	M maana rẽ fãa Koe-nooga yĩnga tɩ m me bũmb zĩnd sʋka.
46009024	Yãmb ka mi tɩ wags taaba zĩigẽ, zoetba fãa zoetame la yaa nin-yend bala n yɩt pipi? Yãmb me mao n lʋɩ taoore n wa paam dolbo.
46009025	Sẽn wagsd-b taaba tuuba bõn-nood wʋsgo la b tõee rẽnna. La yaool n yaa rolb sɛtga la b baooda. Sã n ya tõndo yaa rolb sẽn kõn sɛ.
46009026	Yaa woto la m wudgda, m pa zoet n tuumnẽ ye, m nug ka vaad vɩʋʋg ye.
46009027	M dɩdgda m yĩngã, m talld-a-la toogo tɩ m zoeta m na n moon m taab Koe-noogã n yaool n wa rõb vɩʋʋgẽ.
46010001	Ad-y m pa rata, m saam-biisi, tɩ y yĩm tɩ sawadgo n bui d yaab rãmba fãa la b fãa rʋʋga mogr a ye.
46010002	Wẽnd maag a Moyiiz, b reega soob sawadg tẽngr la Mogr pʋga.
46010003	B fãa rɩlga b mens ne yĩngr dɩɩb yɛnga.
46010004	B fãa yũu yĩngr bõn-yũudl a ye; yaa yĩngr pĩig koom la b ra yũuda la pĩiga ra yãagda bãmba la pĩ kãng ra yaa Krista.
46010005	La ne rẽ fãa sẽn ta-b Wẽnnaam yam sõor yɩɩ bilfu; la rẽ me la b kõaba sẽeg we-raoogẽ wã.
46010006	Yɛla reng n maana woto n na n nek d yam, tɩ da bas tɩ yamleed wẽnsã wa pid d sũur wa bãmb dẽnd ye.
46010007	Da waoog-y bõn-naands wa bãmb kẽer sẽn maane tɩ b kibara gʋls woto: «Zãma wã zĩndame n dɩ la a yũ, la a yikame n na n deem a reem.»
46010008	Da sak-y yoob wala bãmb kẽer sẽn sake, tɩ bãmb tus pisi la a tã na n ki daar a ye wã ye.
46010009	Da kʋɩɩb-y Soaala wa bãmb kẽer sẽn kʋɩɩb-ba tɩ wiis kɛ-b n kʋ wã ye.
46010010	Da guglem-y wala bãmb neb kẽer sẽn maane tɩ Tẽn-kũuma na n loog ne b fãa gilla ye.
46010011	Dẽ fãa maaname n na n nek d yam la rẽ fãa gʋlsa tõnd zãmsg yĩnga, tõnd sẽn pẽneg dũni wã sɛɛbã.
46010012	Dẽn yĩnga, sẽn yɛsa yĩngr n pẽgd a menga gũus n da wa lʋɩ ye.
46010013	Y nan pa seg kʋɩɩbgo sẽn zʋʋg ninsaal pãng ye. Wẽnd yɛsa b sɩd zĩigẽ la b kõn sak tɩ y paam kʋɩɩbg sẽn yɩɩd y pãng ye; kʋɩɩbg sã n wa, b na kõ-y dabaare tɩ y rig-a n zãage, b na kõ-y pãng tɩ y maan daoodo.
46010014	M kom-sõma, zãag-y y meng ne wẽn-naandsa waoogre.
46010015	M gomda ne yã wa neb sẽn tar yam. Wʋm-y m sẽn dat n togsã.
46010016	Laok ning d sẽn deeg la d pʋʋsd barkã ka Krista zɩɩm la d pʋɩt taab la? Burã d sẽn kaoodã, ka Krista yĩng la d lagem n dɩtẽ laa?
46010017	Wala bura sẽn yaa a ye wã, tõnd me ne d ya kʋʋma d yaa yĩng a ye tɩ d fãa rɩta bur yɛng kãnga.
46010018	Tẽeg-y d yaab a Israyɛl rooga kibare. Neb niyns sẽn da rɩt-b maandã, ka maan-kugra yõod la b da rɩt bɩ?
46010019	La rẽ rat n yeelame tɩ bõe? Tɩ maanda nemd bee yõodo? Tɩ maanda sẽn waoogd a soaba n tar yõodo?
46010020	Ka Sʋtãan yĩng la maanda kʋʋd laa, b ka kʋʋd bũmb sẽn ka Wẽnd yĩng laa? M yaool n pa rat tɩ y lagem ne sʋtãamb ye.
46010021	Yãmb pa tõe n yũ Soaala bõn-yũudem la y naag n yũ Sʋtãan dẽn ye, y ka tõe n dɩ Soaala rɩɩb la y le naag n dɩ Sʋtãan dẽn ye.
46010022	D dat n yika Soaala sũur bɩ d dat n maan-b la pãnga?
46010023	Neb n gomd woto: «M tõee fãa.» La d ka tẽed tɩ fãa yaa yõod ye. «M tõee fãa» la m pa tẽed tɩ fãa n wat ne manegr ye.
46010024	Bɩ ned ba a ye da bao sẽn manegd a meng ye; a bao sẽn manegd a taaba.
46010025	Wãb-y nemd ning fãa sẽn da koos-roogẽ, n da yɛs n sokd y sũurẽ sẽn ya bũmb ning nemd ye,
46010026	tɩ tẽnga ne a pʋgẽ teed fãa yaa Soaalã n so.
46010027	Bu-zẽnd sã n bool yãmb a zakẽ tɩ y sak n kẽnge, bɩ y rɩ a sẽn kõ-y bũmb ning fãa la y ra yɛs n sokd y menga: y tõeeme bɩ y pa tõe n dɩ ye.
46010028	Ned sã n yeel yã: «Ad-y nemda yaa maoong nemdo» bɩ y vẽ ne a wãbre, sẽn togsa yãmba yĩnga la a sũura koɛɛg sẽn leokd tɩ pa tõe n wãba yĩnga.
46010029	M sẽn gomd sũur koɛɛgã, m ka gomd yãmb dẽn ye, yaa to wã rẽnda; la sɩda, ned a to sũur koɛɛg yɩta a wãn n leok m yĩnga, m pa so m meng laa?
46010030	M sã n dɩt bũmb la m pẽgd Wẽnde, b na yɩɩ wãn n zab ma m sã n pẽgd m Soaala m sẽn paam dɩɩb yĩnga?
46010031	Woto wã, y rɩta, y yũuda, bɩ yaa bũmb a to la y maanda, bɩ fãa yɩ Wẽnnaam pẽgr yĩnga.
46010032	Gũus-y tɩ y manesem da wa ne ned lʋɩɩse, Zʋɩf rãmb sʋka, bɩ bu-zẽmba, bɩ Tigung kamb sʋk ye.
46010033	Sã n ya maam, m baood n na n zemsa ne y fãa gill, bũmba fãa pʋgẽ; m ka baood sẽn nafd m menga ye, yaa kʋʋnga nafr la m baooda n dat tɩ b fãa paam fãagre.
46011001	Yɩ-y mam togs-n-taase wa m meng sẽn ya Krista togs-n-taaga.
46011002	M pẽgd-y la y sẽn tẽeg m yell bũmba fãa pʋgẽ la y reeg m noya fãa wala m sẽn wilg-y.
46011003	M datame tɩ y bãng tɩ rao tara zu-soaba, yaa Krista; la pag me zu-soab la raoa, tɩ Krista Zu-soaba ya Wẽnnaam.
46011004	Dao sã n fõgen bũmb a zug n na n pʋʋs Wẽnd bɩ n na n togs b goama, a paoogda a zu-soaba.
46011005	La sã n ya pag n pʋʋsde bɩ a togsda Wẽnd goama t'a zug ka teeg bũmbu, yẽ me paoogda a zu-soaba. Yaa wala a sã n da põnga a zuga koeelle.
46011006	Pag sã n ka rat n teeg a zug peende bɩ a põng zuga zãnga. La a sã n get wa yãnd ne-a, a zoobd sẽn põng bɩ sẽn wõrse, bɩ a teeg peende.
46011007	Rao ka tog n teeg a zug bũmb ye, tɩ rao yaa Wẽnnaam ne b ziira wẽnego; sã n ya paga, yẽ la raoã ziiri.
46011008	Sɩd me, ka pag n deng taoore tɩ rao vɩɩma yi a nengẽ ye, yaa rao n denge.
46011009	Ka raoã la b naan n kõ pag ye, yaa paga la b naan n kõ raoa.
46011010	Yaa rẽ yĩnga, la malɛk rãmba waoogr yĩnga, pag zug tog n teeg bũmb sẽn wilgd t'a ka so a meng ye.
46011011	Soaala nengẽ pag yell ka gomd n zẽng rao ye, rao yell me pa gomd n zẽng pag ye.
46011012	Sã n ya ne rao la Wẽnd naan paga, yaa pag me n dogd daoa la b yiiba fãa yita Wẽnd nengẽ.
46011013	Yãmb me ges wɛ! Segdame sɩd tɩ pag pʋʋs Wẽnd n ka lud a zugu?
46011014	Ninsaalb nifẽ, rao ne zoob wogd ka yãnd bɩ?
46011015	La yaool n ka rẽ la pag zu-zẽkr bɩ? Wẽnd kõ-a la zoob wogd tɩ yɩ wala a zug peende.
46011016	Pʋs n seka woto, gomd n pa sɛtẽ soab sã n be y sʋka bɩ a bãng tɩ tõnd ka minim dẽ, la Wẽnd Tigenga me ka minim dẽ ye.
46011017	La m sẽn dat tɩ y maan gũusgã, m kõn solg-y tɩ m ka pẽgd y lagmen-taarã sẽn wat ne y bõne n yɩɩd a sẽn wat ne y yõodã ye.
46011018	M sẽn wʋm la woto, tɩ y sã n tigime y wẽnegd n welga taaba, la m tẽedame tɩ rẽ yaa sɩd bilfu.
46011019	Pʋs n segdame tɩ welegr zĩndi, segdame tɩ b tõog n bak sẽn sĩdb ne neera maanego, n bak-b ne neb a taaba.
46011020	Y sẽn mii n tigim taabã ka le ya Soaala rɩɩba yĩng ye.
46011021	Rɩɩba sã n na n sɩnge, ned kam fãa yiisda a sẽn wa ne; woto kẽer yãbda kom, tɩ kẽer yũud n gãeemdẽ.
46011022	Y ka tar zagse n na n dɩ la y yũ be laa? Bɩ yaa Tigengã la y sãbsda n dat n ning sẽn ka tar-ba yãnde? M na n yeel-y lame tɩ bõe? M pẽg yã? Dẽ wã yẽ m kõn saag n pẽg-y ye.
46011023	Sã n ya maam, ad-m sẽn paam Soaala nengẽ la yaa rẽ la m wilgd-y: yʋng ning b sẽn zãmb Soaal a Zezi wã, b rɩka buri,
46011024	la b sẽn pʋʋs bark n sɛ, b wesa burã n yeele: «Wã yaa mam yĩnga m sẽn kõ yãmba; maan-y woto n tẽeg m yelle.»
46011025	Dẽ poore, yaa yõg-laaga la b rɩk yã n yeele: «Wã yaa zood paalg sẽn yõg m zɩɩmẽ laaga; y sẽn na n tugla raar ning fãa bɩ y tẽeg m yelle.»
46011026	Ade, wakat ning fãa y sẽn dɩt bur kãngã la y yũud la-kãnga, yaa Krista kũum la y moonda la na n yɩɩ woto n tãag b waoongo.
46011027	Dẽ yĩnga, sẽn ka tog n dɩ-ɛ burã la a rɩtẽ, sẽn ka tog n yũ Soaala laaga la a yũud-a, yaa Soaala yĩnga taale, yaa Soaala zɩɩma taale la a rɩta, la a yũuda.
46011028	Bɩ ned kam fãa deng n tɩg a menga la a yaool n dɩ burã, la a yaool n yũ rãama.
46011029	Ned ning fãa sẽn dɩt-a bɩ sẽn yũud-a yaare, ya a meng bõne la a rɩta, ya a meng bõne la a yũuda.
46011030	Ad-y yaa rẽn yĩng la bãad-dãmb ne koms rãmb ya wʋsg y sʋka, tɩ wʋsg meng tol n maand yõore.
46011031	La tõnd sã n deng n tɩg d pʋga, d paalgr bʋʋd kõn kao ye.
46011032	Soaala nug sã n wa zɩsgd d zugu yaa d paam n tek tɩ b ra wa naag ne zamaana rãmb n paalg ye.
46011033	Dɩlla, m saam-biisi, y sã n mii n tigim taaba n na n dɩ Soaala rɩɩbo bɩ y maag y yĩng n gũ taaba;
46011034	sẽn data n dɩ n yiis a kom, tʋg n dɩ yiri n da wa bao yelle n kõ saam-biisa ye. Sẽn ketã, d na yãend taaba m sã n wa.
46012001	Sã n ya yĩngr kũna poorẽ, m saam-biisi, m pa rat tɩ y maan wa y ka mi ye.
46012002	Y sẽn waa n nan ka kẽ Soaalã, y mi tɩ yaa y wẽn-mugsã yamleoog n da tar-y n lengdẽ.
46012003	Marsa wã ad-m sẽn tõe n togs yã: Ned ka bee n paam a Vʋʋsem Sõng kũuna la a le tõog n yeel tɩ «Wẽn na sãam a Zezi ye.» Ned me ka tõe n yeel t'a «Zezi la Soaala» t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng ka vẽneg-a ye.
46012004	Yaa sɩda, a Vʋʋsem Sõng kũuna yaa toor-toore la yaa zĩ-yɛng la b yita.
46012005	Pʋɩɩba yaa toor-toore la Pʋɩta ya Soaal yɛnga,
46012006	tʋʋma yaa toɛ-toɛ la yaa Wẽnnaam b ye bal n tʋmd fãa d fãa pʋsẽ.
46012007	Yaa buuda zãng yĩnga la a Vʋʋsem Sõng pʋɩt b kũuna.
46012008	A Vʋʋsem Sõng kõta nin-yend t'a tõog n zulg gomde; n kõt a to t'a wegs n togs gomde;
46012009	nin-yend paamda tẽebo ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng pãnga, t'a to paamd bãas sãoogr kũuni Vʋʋsem Sõng yɛnga nengẽ.
46012010	Nin-yend paamda wẽnd makr dãmb kũuni, t'a to paamd beoog bãngr kũuni; nin-yend paamda a taab pʋg bãngre, t'a to ya goam buud toɛ-toɛ wɩlengo, t'a to ya b võor togsgo.
46012011	La rẽ fãa yaa Vʋʋsma a ye tʋʋmde, bãmb n pʋɩt b yam, ned fãa ne a rẽnna.
46012012	Wala ninsaal yĩnga sẽn yaa a yembr tãa n yaool n tar wils wʋsgo, tɩ wilsa ne b sẽn ya kʋʋma maand yĩng a ye tãa, woto-me Krista nengẽ.
46012013	Dẽ me la tõnd paam soob Vʋʋsma a ye pʋgẽ n lebg yĩng a ye, d ya Zʋɩf bɩ bu-zẽna, yamb bɩ burkĩna; Vʋʋsma a ye tãa la b yũnug tõndo.
46012014	Yĩnga ka wilg a ye ye, b yaa kʋʋma.
46012015	Naoor sã n da yetẽ: «Ka maam la nugu; dẽ yĩnga m ka naag ne yĩnga ye,» dẽ na kɩt t'a sɩd ka naag ne yĩngã?
46012016	La tʋbr sã n yetẽ: «M ka nif ye; dẽnd m ka yĩnga wilg ye,» dẽ na kɩt t'a sɩd kaẽ yĩnga wilga?
46012017	Yĩnga fãa sã n dag n yaẽ nifu, tʋbra yaẽ la bʋgo? Fãa sã n dag n yaẽ la tʋbr bala, bõe n yɩtẽ yõore?
46012018	Wẽnd n sel wilsã yĩngẽ, wala b sẽn tʋlge.
46012019	Yĩnga tõr sã n dag n yaẽ la wilg a ye, yĩnga wẽndẽ la bõe?
46012020	La ade, wilsa yaa kʋʋma, tɩ yĩnga yaool n yaa a ye.
46012021	Nif ka tõe n yeel nugu: «Ad-m ka tar f tʋʋmd ye.» Zug me ka tõe n yeel nao: «Ad-y m ka tar y tʋʋmd ye.»
46012022	Yɩɩd rẽ, b sẽn get wils niyns wa bõn-mɛdsã, bãmb me tara b tʋʋmde,
46012023	Wils niyns sẽn wẽnd-b pa togẽ ne waoogrã, bãmb la tõnd waoogd n yɩɩda; wils niyns gesg sẽn ya yãndã, bãmb la tõnd koagend n yɩɩda.
46012024	Sẽn sakd-b gesgã, bãmb ka le tar waoogr tʋʋmd ye. Wẽnd n sigl yĩnga woto, tɩ wilg ning sẽn ka wẽnd b na waoog-a wã paamd waoogr n paase.
46012025	Woto yĩnga wils zãaga taab ne welegre, tɩ wilg kam fãa be-la a to yĩng zãng-zãnga.
46012026	Toog n tar wilg a ye, wilsa fãa naagda yẽ n tar toogo; wilg a ye paama waoogre, yaa b fãa sũ-noogo.
46012027	Sã n ya yãmba, yãmb yaa Krista yĩnga la ned kam fãa yaa wilg n be a zĩigẽ.
46012028	Wẽnd sẽn yãk b rãmb Tigenga yĩnga, pipi yaa tʋʋm-tʋmdba, a yiib soaba, bãngdba, a tãab soaba, karen-saam-dãmba. B kõo kẽer tõog tɩ b maand bõn-bãna, kẽer yaa sãoogre, kẽer yaa naong rãmb yaoogre, kẽer kʋʋnga zãabo, kẽer goam buud toɛ-toɛ wɩlengo.
46012029	M sok n gese, yaa b fãa la tʋʋm-tʋmdb bɩ? B fãa la bãngdba? B fãa la karen-saam-dãmba? B fãa gill n maand wẽnd makr dãmba?
46012030	B fãa gill n tõe n sãoog bãase? B fãa gill n tõe n wɩlem bu-zẽnd goama? B fãa gill n tõe n yɩ bu-zẽnd no-rɛɛsa?
46012031	Bao-y kũun niyns sẽn ya-b sõmb n yɩɩdã. La bas-y tɩ m wilg-y sẽn be neer n yɩɩd wa fãa-fãa.
46013001	Ba mam wɩlemd ninsaalb buud fãa goama, n paas malɛgsa rẽnna, m sã n pa tar nonglem, m yaa wa lombr sẽn wẽde, bɩ waaga sẽn kãglemde.
46013002	Ba mam tar beoog yɛl bãngre, la m mi sẽn solg fãa, ba m yama vẽen ne bũmb fãa, ba m tẽeb pid zãnga tɩ sek a vigs tãmsã b zĩisẽ, m sã n ka tar nonglem kũuni, mam yaa zaalem.
46013003	Ba mam dɩkẽ m paoong fãa n sõng naong rãmba; ba mam sakẽ tɩ b los m yĩnga bugmẽ, m ka tar nonglem, m kõn yãend dẽ yõod ye.
46013004	Nonglem yaa maag-m-menga, nonglem yaa to sõngre, nonglem ka mi sũ-kiir ye, a ka wakr bɩ tɩtaam ye.
46013005	Nonglem ka tʋmd beed ye, a ka mi zoe-bõne, a ka mi sũ-puuri, a ka tẽegd beegr ye.
46013006	A ka kɩdemd a to bõne; a sũur nooma a puk sɩda.
46013007	A ka ningd ned ba a ye taal ye; a tẽeda fãa, a saagda fãa, a sakda fãa.
46013008	Nonglem bal n ka be sɛɛbo. Bãngr na n loogame, goam wɩleng na n loogame, yam vẽenem na n loogame.
46013009	D yam vẽenem pʋs n yaa sãoogo, d bãngr me yaa sãoogo, ka pid ye.
46013010	Sãooga fãa na n pida raar a ye, vẽenem la bãngr pidunga raare.
46013011	M sẽn waa n ya yãaga, m da gomda wa yãaga, m da tagsda wa yãaga; m sẽn lebg bi-kãsenga, m basa yãadre.
46013012	Tõnd sẽn ne bũmb ning marsa wã yaa wa ne nin-gɛtga; m sẽn mi marsa wã yaa bõn-wɛdga bala la m na yaool n wa bãnga zãnga, wala b sẽn mi maama.
46013013	Marsã bũmb a tãab n be: tẽebo, saagre la nonglem la sẽn yɩɩd yaa nonglem.
46014001	Bao-y nonglem la bao-y Wẽnd kũun a taaba me, sẽn yɩɩda bãngr kũuni.
46014002	Sẽn wɩlemda goam pa gomd ne ninsaalb ye, a gomda ne Wẽnde. Ned pa wʋmd a goama võor ye, a gomda goam bãna a yamẽ.
46014003	Ned ning sẽn yaool n togsda bãngr goam, gomda ne ninsaalba n manegd b yɛla, n sagendẽ la a yolsdẽ.
46014004	Ned ninga sẽn gomda goam zẽna, ya a meng yell manegre; sẽn gomda bãngr goam manegda a saam-biisa sẽn tigma.
46014005	M datame tɩ y wɩlem bu-zẽn goama la m nongame n yɩɩda tɩ y gom bãngr goama; sẽn gomda bãngr goam yɩɩda sẽn wɩlemda bu-zẽn goama. Bu-zẽn goama soab sã n ka pa poorẽ, yaa a sã n paam n togsa a goama võore, n tõe n naf kʋʋnga sẽn tigm a sɛɛgẽ.
46014006	Ges-y yã, m saam-biisi, mam sã n wa yãmb sʋk n gomd goam zẽna la m goama ka vẽnegd y yam, la b ka paasd y bãngre, la b ka zãmsd-y fɩ, dẽ nafda yãmb bɩ?
46014007	Yaa boto ne yʋʋmba wɩɩg bɩ pɛndga: b rãamda sã n pa sãta, m yɩta a wãn n bãng yɩɩn bʋg la b pebd bɩ b wẽeda?
46014008	Tõntõoga sã n peebd zabr yĩnga, t'a peebga pa sãta, ãnda n na n bob a zab-teedo?
46014009	Yãmb me, y zelemd sã n ka gomd n fasgdẽ, ãnda n wʋmd y sẽn yet bũmb ninga? Y gomda vɩʋʋgẽ.
46014010	D ka tar dũni wã goam buud toɛ-toɛ yã sõor ye la b tara võor ne b rãmba.
46014011	M sã n pa wʋmd ned goama, m yaa bu-zẽnd ne yẽnda; yẽ me sã n pa wʋmd m goama, a yaa bu-zẽnd ne maam.
46014012	Y sẽn baood Wẽnd kũuna, bao-y-b wʋsgo n tõog n naf sẽn be-b ne yãmbã.
46014013	Woto wã sẽn wɩlemda bu-zẽn goam pʋʋs Soaala n paam b võor n wilgi.
46014014	M sã n pʋʋsd ne bu-zẽn goama, m maanda pʋʋsgo la a võora la m ka tara.
46014015	M na n maana wãna? M na n maana pʋʋsgo la m na n bao-la a võore. M bark pʋʋsga yɩɩl na n yɩɩ yɩɩlle m sẽn wʋmd a võore.
46014016	Sã n ka boto, fo sẽn pẽgd Wẽnd ne bu-zẽn goama, sẽn ka paam-a kũun ning fo sẽn paama yɩta a wãn n deeg tɩ Wẽnd na paam pẽgre, a sã n ka mi fo sẽn gomd n lebdẽ.
46014017	F bark pʋʋsga yaa sõmb wʋsgo, yaa sɩda, la a yɩta a wãn naf yẽnda?
46014018	Wẽnd paam bark b sẽn kɩt tɩ m wɩlemd goam n yɩɩd y fãa!
46014019	La m gesame tɩ d sã n tigim taab pʋʋsg yĩnga, m sẽn na n yiis goam a nu m sẽn tar b võore, n tõog n zãms m taaba n são m sẽn na n yiis bu-zẽn goam biis tus piiga sẽn pa zãmsd fɩ.
46014020	M saam-biisi da yɩɩ-y wa kom-bõonese n ka mi sẽn segd tɩ y maan ye. Y sã n ya kom-kɩds n ka mi wẽnga, m saka rẽ; la sã n ya sẽn segd tɩ y maana pʋgẽ, paam-y nin-bɛd yam.
46014021	B gʋlsa Noor sebr pʋga: «Yaa ne bu-zẽmb la ne bu-zẽn dãmb noor la m na n gom ne nin-bãmba la ne rẽ fãa b kõn kelg-m ye. – Soaala n yete –»
46014022	Dẽn yĩnga bu-zẽn goama ka nafd tẽedba ye, a yaa yõod ne sẽn nan ka paam-b tẽebo; bãngr me kũun pa bu-zẽmba yĩnga, a yaa tẽedba yĩnga
46014023	wala Tẽedba sã n tigim, tɩ fãa gomd bu-zẽnd goama, tɩ seg sãan waoongo bɩ sega sẽn ka tar-a tẽeb waoongo, b kõn yeel tɩ yãmb zʋbsdame?
46014024	La sã n ya bãngr goam la y fãa gomda tɩ seg kẽed paalga bɩ bu-zẽn waoongo, ad-y b na naag taab n wilg-a sẽn be la sẽn segde;
46014025	b na puk sẽn solg a sũurẽ al t'a wa kɩ a neng tẽng n waoog Wẽnnaam la a moon tɩ b sɩd be-la y sʋka.
46014026	M saam-biisi, d na n baasa d saglga wãna? Y sã n tigim taaba ned kam fãa tõe n waa ne a yɩɩle, bɩ a zãmsgo, bɩ yell sãang pukri, bɩ goam zẽna, bɩ gomd zẽnd võor pukri. La rẽ fãa tog n waa ne sɩɩga nafre.
46014027	Bu-zẽn goam la b wɩlemda? Bɩ b yɩ b yiib bɩ b tãabo, la ra loog rẽ ye, la yɩ bal-bale, la ned zĩnd sʋka n wilgd b goama võore.
46014028	Sẽn na n wilg võora soab sã n ka beẽ bɩ b sĩndi; bɩ ned kam fãa gom ne a meng la Wẽnde.
46014029	Bãngdba ta b yiib bɩ b tãabo n gomda tɩ sẽn ket-ba kelgdẽ la b pẽgda.
46014030	Ned a to sã n yik n na n gom a bãngr goama, bɩ pipi soaba bas-a t'a gome.
46014031	Y fãa gill tõee, bal-bal, n yiis y bãngre n zãms la y wɩng y taab tẽebo.
46014032	Bãngdba ka yiisd b bãngra zond-yaar ye;
46014033	Wẽnd yaa laafi Wẽnnaam, b ka zũnd-zãnd Wẽnd ye. Wẽnd kamba sẽn tigimd taab zĩig ninga,
46014034	bɩ pagba ra yaag b noor ye. B ka tar sor n gom ye; bãmb sẽn tõe yaa sakr bala, la Noorã n dat rẽ.
46014035	B sã n dat n sok n bãng bũmbu, b gũ yir n sok b sɩdb rãmba. Ka tog tɩ pag gom kʋʋng sʋk ye.
46014036	Yaa yãmb nengẽ la Wẽnd gomda yi bɩ? Bɩ yaa yãmb y ye bal n paam-a?
46014037	Ned sã n beẽ n tagsdẽ t'a yaa bãngda, t'a paama a Vʋʋsem sõng vẽnegre, bɩ a reng n bãng tɩ m sẽn gʋls yãmb bũmb ningã yaa Wẽnd noore.
46014038	Sẽn pʋs n ka rat-a n bãng bɩ a ra bãng ye.
46014039	Woto wã, m saam-biisi, bao-y n paam bãngr kũuni, la y ra gɩdg bu-zẽn goam wɩleng me ye.
46014040	La modg-y tɩ bũmba fãa maan wa sẽn segde la ra yɩ yaar ye.
46015001	M le tẽegda yãmba, m saam-biisi, Koe-noogã m sẽn moon yãmbã; y reeg-a lame la y ket n tar-a-la sõmbo.
46015002	Yẽ n na n fãag yã, y sã n kell n tall-a neere wala m sẽn wilg-a yãmbã, ka rẽ y tẽeba wat n yɩɩ zaalem.
46015003	Yaa mam meng sẽn da reng n wʋm la m togs yã, tɩ Krista kii d yel-wẽna yĩnga, wa Sebr sõng sẽn togse,
46015004	tɩ b solg-b yaoogẽ, la rasem a tãab raare, b vʋʋgame, wala sẽn le gʋls yɛsa;
46015005	tɩ b lika b meng a Kefas la piig la a yiibã;
46015006	dẽ poore yaa saam-biis sẽn ta kobs-nu la b lik yã – bãmb wʋsg keta ne yõore, kẽer bal n ki –
46015007	tɩ b lika a Zak la tʋʋm-tʋmdba fãa.
46015008	Dẽ poor marsã la b yaool n lik maam me, maam b bõn-mɛdga.
46015009	Sɩda, maam la tʋʋm-tʋmdba fãa yao-zʋʋga; m da pa tog meng ne tʋʋm-tʋmd yʋʋr ye, tɩ m namsa Wẽnd Tigengu.
46015010	La Wẽnd bark kɩtame tɩ m ya m sẽn ya-lã la b barkã ka pa n ka wom a biis ye. M ka tõe n ka ges m meng wa tʋʋm-tʋmd ye, tɩ m tʋmame n yɩɩg b fãa; la yaool n ka maam n tʋm ye, yɩ Wẽnd kũuna b sẽn kõ-ma n tʋm b tʋʋmde.
46015011	Yaa bãmb woo, yaa maam woo, yaa woto la d moonda. La yaa rẽ me la y reeg yã.
46015012	La sã n moond tɩ Krista vʋʋga kɩɩms sʋka, maana a wãn tɩ yãmb neb kẽer yik n yet tɩ kũum ka vʋʋgde?
46015013	Kɩɩms sã n pa vʋʋgdẽ, dẽn Krista me ka vʋʋg ye.
46015014	La Krista sã n ka vʋʋge, tõnd zãmsga yaa zaalem la yãmb me tẽeba zãng lebga zaalem.
46015015	La tõnd n lebg Wẽnd kaset zirẽ-dãmba, d sã n wẽennẽ tɩ b vʋʋga Krista, tɩ b yaool n ka vʋʋg-ba, sã n ya sɩd tɩ kũum ka vʋʋgd ye.
46015016	Kɩɩmsa sã n ka vʋʋgde, dẽn Krista me ka vʋʋg ye.
46015017	La Krista sã n ka vʋʋge, y tẽeba yaa zaalem; y ka yi yel-wẽndẽ ye,
46015018	la sẽn ki-b Krista yĩngã, bãmb me yell sɛɛme.
46015019	Sã n ya tẽng zug vɩɩma yĩng bal la d del Krista, tõnd la dũni wã fãa zu-bʋk rãmba.
46015020	La ayoo! Krista vʋʋga kɩɩms sʋka, la bãmb n deng kɩɩmsa fãa.
46015021	Wala kũuma sẽn tũ nin-yend n wa dũni wã, kɩɩmsa vʋʋgra me na n tũu ne nin-yend maasem.
46015022	Wala d fãa sẽn tũud a Adem n bãng kũuma, woto me d fãa tũuda Krista n le vɩɩnde,
46015023	ned kam fãa ne a wakato: Krista n so taoore, tɩ bãmb la Bi-rẽenga. Bãmb poor marsã neb niyns sẽn ket n be bãmb soolmẽ, b waoonga raare.
46015024	Dẽ poore bũmb fãa na n yãe-la a baasgo la yaa Wẽnnaam Ba la Krista na n lebs b naama, b sẽn wat n lub na-rɩtba, la soaalba la pãn-dãmb buud fãa.
46015025	Y mi tɩ yaa tɩlɛ tɩ Krista rɩ naam n tãag wakat ning b naoã sẽn wat n palg b bɛɛba zãnga.
46015026	B yaoolem na-rɩta b sẽn na n lubi, yaa Kũum.
46015027	Yẽ lubr poore b sɩd na n paamame tɩ bũmb fãa yaa b soolem. Bãng-y tɩ sã n gʋls tɩ bũmb fãa sura b taoore, ka naag ne ned ninga sẽn sulg bũmb fãa b taoora ye.
46015028	La bũmb fãa sã n wa lebg bãmb soolem n sɛ, dẽ marsã la Wẽnd Biiga me na n lebg bũmb-fãa-Soaala-soolem, la woto la Wẽnd na n lebg fãa-fãa ned kam yĩnga.
46015029	Sã n dag n kaẽ boto, bõe la neb niyns sẽn sood-b kɩɩmsa yʋʋr yĩnga na n paamẽ ? Kɩɩmsa sã n ka na n vʋʋg lɛ-lɛ, bõe tɩ b sood kɩɩms yĩnga?
46015030	Bõe me yĩng la tõnd meng ka na n baoẽ yĩn-maasem n zãag d mens ne yɛl tooda sẽn lʋɩt d zug wakat buud fãa?
46015031	M bee kũum nugẽ beoog sẽn vẽeg fãa la rẽ yaa sɩda, m saam-biisi, sɩd wa y sẽn ya m zu-zẽkre d Soaala Zezi Krista taoore.
46015032	Sã n da yaẽ la ninsaal geels la m geel yã n zab ne Efɛɛz rãmba, b wẽn-naandsa poorẽ, m yõoda la bʋgo? Sẽn ki-ba sã n ka na n vʋʋge, bɩ d rɩ la d yũ tɩ beoogo d na n kiime.
46015033	Da belg-y y mens ye: Tũud-n-ta wẽnse n wat ne vɩɩma sãoongo.
46015034	M kos tɩ y wɩsg y meng tɩ rẽ n toge la y zãag y meng ne wẽnga. Wʋsg bee yãmb sʋka n ket n ka mi Wẽnd, la rẽ ka yãnd sɩda?
46015035	La f sã n soke: Sẽn ki-ba na n vʋʋga wãn wãna? Yĩin bʋgo la b na n le wa ne?
46015036	Ges wɛ, yalma, fo meng sẽn bʋtã ka lebgd bõn-vɩɩla t'a ka reng n ki ye.
46015037	Fo sẽn bʋta ka bũmb la f võogd n sel ye, yaa bõn-beelle, ka-beelle, bɩ bũmb a to.
46015038	Wẽnd n kõt yako wala b sẽn date, bõn-buud fãa ne a rẽnna.
46015039	Yĩnsa fãa ka a yembr ye: ninsaal yĩng toore, rũng yĩng toore, luiil rẽnd toore, kʋɩl-zẽoog me rẽnd toore.
46015040	Saag zug tara a bõn-yood, tɩ saag tẽngr me tar a rẽnna. Yĩngr teeda yãgbo ne tẽng zug rẽnna ka a ye ye.
46015041	Wĩntoog yãgb toore, kiuug me rẽnd toore, ãdsa me rẽnd toore. Ãdg a ye meng peelem bakda ne ãdg a to rẽnna.
46015042	Yĩnsa vʋʋgr me na n yɩɩ boto. Yaa bõn-põosg la b bʋta la yaa sẽn ka tõe n le põog n vʋʋgde.
46015043	Yaa bũmb sẽn ka tar waoor la b bʋta, la bũmb sẽn pid ne ziir n na n vʋʋge; faoor la b bʋta, la pãng n na n vʋʋge;
46015044	tẽng zug bũmb la b bʋta, la yĩngr dẽn n na n yi. Yĩng sẽn tõe n deeg tẽng zug vɩɩma sã n beẽ, yĩng sẽn tõe n deeg yĩngr vɩɩma me beemẽ.
46015045	Yaa rẽ la b gʋlsyã: Pipi Adma naaname t'a ya vɩɩm deegda, Adma a yiib soaba yaa vɩɩma kõata.
46015046	Ka sẽn kõt-a vɩɩma la pipi ye, sẽn deeg-a vɩɩma n deng taoore tɩ yẽ yaool n pʋge.
46015047	Pipi soaba yaa tẽng tom, tɩ tẽng tomẽ la a yita; a yiib soaba yita yĩngri.
46015048	Tẽng zug raoã sẽn yɩ a soaba, a kamb me boto, yĩngr daoã sẽn yɩ a soaba, a neba me boto.
46015049	Wala d sẽn wẽneg tẽng zug soabã, lebga pakre tɩ d wẽneg yĩngr soaba me.
46015050	Maam n yet-y, m saam-biisi, ka yĩn-kãnga sẽn ya neong la zɩɩma n na n kẽ Wẽnd Rĩungẽ ye, ka bõn-põosgã n na dɩ sẽn zɩ a põogra faad ye.
46015051	M na n wilga yãmb koɛɛg sẽn yɩɩd ninsaal bãngre: Kũuma, ad-y ka d fãa n na n ki ye; la d fãa yẽ sẽ, d na n tedgame.
46015052	Vugr bala, nif kamsg pʋgẽ, baorga sã n tãse, la sɩda baorg n na n peebe, kɩɩmsa fãa na n vʋʋgame n ka le bãng põogr lɛ-lɛ, la tõnd me, tõnd me na n tedgame.
46015053	Bala yaa tɩ-lɛ tɩ yĩn-kãnga sẽn ya bõn-põosgã tɩlg põogr zãnga la yĩn-kiidga tɩlg ne kũum zãnga.
46015054	Dɩlla mam yĩn-kãnga sẽn na n põogã sã n wa tɩlg põogr zãnga, la m yĩn-kãnga sẽn na n ki wã sã n wa tɩlg kũum zãnga, dẽ marsã la sebr sõng gomda na n taase: «Pãn-tõog tʋʋmd n tʋʋme n loog ne kũum zãnga.
46015055	Kũum, fo sẽn tʋm daood la bɛɛ? Kũum, fo zab-teed bɛɛ?»
46015056	Mik kũum zab-teed yaa yel-wẽnde la Noorã n kõt yel-wẽnda pãngã.
46015057	La Wẽnd paam bark tɩ bãmb n kɩt tɩ d lub yel-wẽnde, d Soaala Zezi Krista maasem yĩnga.
46015058	Dɩlla, m saam-biisi, modg-y tɩ y raooda ra woog ye la y rabs Soaala tʋʋmna taoore n miẽ t'a kõn yɩ zaalem ye.
46016001	Sã n ya ligda lobr nin-sõma sõngr yĩnga bɩ y tũ noor ning m sẽn kõ tẽedba fãa sẽn be Galasi.
46016002	Dasem a yopoe-poe wã pipi daare bɩ ned kam fãa kẽgs n bĩng ligd a nengẽ la y ra gũ tɩ m wa tɩ y yaool n sɩng n tigs ye.
46016003	M sã n ta, m na gʋls sebr tɩ yãmb sẽn tũus neb niynsa tall y kũuna n ta Zerizalɛɛm;
46016004	la sã n wẽnda m meng na kẽnge, d na tũ taaba.
46016005	M na ta y tẽngẽ, m sã n wa pɩʋʋg Masedoan; na n yɩɩ pɩʋʋgr bala.
46016006	Tõeeme me tɩ m yals y sʋk n kaoose, tõeeme n yɩ sẽooga tõre la m sẽn na n kẽng zĩig ning fãa, y na yãag-ma.
46016007	M yaool n ka rat tɩ d yãend taab yĩngr-yĩngr bal ye, m geenda m na kaoos y sʋka, Soaala sã n sake.
46016008	La sẽn ya a soab fãa, m na n paa Efɛɛz n ta Zãna kibsa,
46016009	tʋʋmda roog paka kẽoong n gũud-ma la bɛɛba me ka paood ye.
46016010	A Timote sã n wa, sõng-y tɩ bũmb da yɛɛs-a y sʋk ye, tɩ yẽ me tʋmda Soaala tʋʋmd wala maam.
46016011	Ned ba a ye da paoog-a ye; sõng-y yã t'a leb mam nengẽ ne laafi. D gũud-a lame, maam ne saam-biisa fãa.
46016012	Sã n yaa d saam-biig a Apolos, m wɩnga ne a t'a tũ saam-biisã n wa ges yã la a zãgsa fas; a yeelame t'a ka tõe marsa ye la a sã n wa paam sẽka, a na wa.
46016013	Maan-y gũusgu, tall-y y tẽeba kẽnkẽ, maan-y raoodo.
46016014	Sõng-y tɩ bũmb fãa tũ ne taab nonglem, y sʋka.
46016015	Ad-m koɛɛg a to, m saam-biisi: yãmb mi tɩ yaa a Stefanas ne a zak rãmb n yɩ Akayi pipi kristneb la bãmb n sõng d saam-biisa fãa gilli.
46016016	Bɩ y waoog neb a woto buudu la neb niyns fãa sẽn tʋmd-b la b namsd wa bãmba.
46016017	M sũur nooma a Stefanas, a Fortunatus la a Akayikus sẽn waa n ges-ma; b reega yãmb zĩig mam sɛɛgẽ,
46016018	la b maasa m sũuri wala b sẽn maas yãmb me rẽnna; dẽ me yĩng la m yet tɩ y waoog neb a woto buudu.
46016019	Azi saam-biisa Tigeng n pʋʋsde; a Akila la a Priska tɩ b pʋʋs-y neere ne Soaala pʋʋsem, bãmb ne neb niyns fãa sẽn tigemd-b b zakẽ.
46016020	D saam-biisa fãa tɩ b pʋʋs yã; pʋʋs-y taab neer n kõ-ma!
46016021	Maam a Pol n gʋlsd-y, ad-m meng nug tikri.
46016022	Sẽn ka nong-a Soaala fãa bɩ Wẽnd me lak ne yẽ soaba! Maran ata! Soaala, wa-y yã!
46016023	Soaala Zezi barka sig yãmba!
46016024	M nong-y la ne Krista a Zezi meng nonglem.
47001001	Maam, a Pol, a Zezi Krista Tʋʋm-tʋmd ne Wẽnd daabo, maam ne m saam-biig a Timote, tõnd n pʋʋsd Wẽnd Tigenga sẽn be Korẽnt la d saam-bi sõma wã fãa sẽn be Akayi tẽn-tõre.
47001002	Bɩ Wẽnnaam tõnd Ba la d Soaal a Zezi Krista sik y fãa zutu b bark la b laafi!
47001003	Bɩ Wẽnd la d Soaal a Zezi Krista Ba, nimbãan-zoeer Ba, toog buud fãa yoalsdã, paam barka!
47001004	Bãmb n maasd tõnd sũuri d namsga pʋgẽ, la b meng sẽn maasd d sũurã, bãmb n sõngd tõndo tɩ d me maasd d taab sũuri, b sẽn zĩ ne toog ning fãa.
47001005	Wala Krista namsga sẽn lebg yõod ka tɛk tõnd yĩnga, boto me, ne Krista maasem, d sũ-noog lebga zembala.
47001006	D sã n namsdẽ, yaa yãmb sũur bʋkr yĩnga la y fãagre. D sũura sã n bʋke, yãmb me rẽnda na bʋke tɩ y sak wakat fãa, namsg niyns tõnd me sẽn namsde.
47001007	La saagr bee wʋsgo tɩ y sẽn naag tõnd n namsã, y na naag n kɩdem sũ-noog ne do.
47001008	M saam-biisi, m ka rat n soolg-y ye: pɛt ning d sẽn paam Azi tẽng nams-d-la wʋsgo al tɩ d da pa tẽed tɩ yõor kõn yãk ye.
47001009	Sɩda tõnd meng d toore n sak tɩ b paalg tõnd d kũum bʋʋdo la woto d bãngame tɩ d ka tog n teeg d meng ye. Yaa Wẽnd la d tog n teeg tɩ bãmb n vʋʋgd sẽn ki.
47001010	Yaa bãmb n zãag tõnd ne kũum a woto buud dũnna, n na n le zãag-d beoogo.
47001011	Yãmb meng na sõngd ne y pʋʋsgo, woto yel-sõmda sẽn ya kʋʋng yel-sõmdã na tak neb ka tɛka tɩ b wa pʋʋs bark d yĩnga.
47001012	Bũmb n ya tõnd zu-zẽkre la yaa d sẽn pelg d pʋg n zã d meng zamaana pʋgẽ la yãmb sʋka ne sõmblem la sɩda sẽn ya Wẽnd kũuni. Ad-y rẽ ka tũ ne ninsaal sɩlem ye, a tũu ne Wẽnd sõngre.
47001013	Bũmb ka be tõnd sɛba pʋgẽ n zʋʋg yãmb sẽn karemd la y wʋmd bũmb ninga ye. M tẽed tɩ y na wʋm fãa –
47001014	tɩ m neeme tɩ y zoe n wʋma bilfu – m tẽed tɩ m na yɩ y zu-zẽkre wala yãmb me sẽn na n yɩ m zu-zẽkre Soaal a Zezi Krista raare.
47001015	Yaa m sũura sẽn da kegem woto la m da rat n deng n tũ y nengẽ n le paas y sũ-noogo.
47001016	M sã da yiẽ yãmb nengẽ m na n digẽ la Masedoan, n tɩ yi be n le wa y nengẽ, tɩ y yaoolẽ marsã n taas-m Zɩɩde.
47001017	M mii, m tagsame tɩ seke ne m kẽna sẽn sigl woto wã? M mii, m ka kelg m sũura sẽn ya ninsaal sũuri n mi N-yẽe rũnna n yik beoog n mi Ayoo?
47001018	Wala Wẽnd sẽn yɛs b sɩd zĩigẽ, tõnd goama ne yãmb ka naag n yɩ N-yẽe la Ayoo ye.
47001019	Maam, a Silvẽ la a Timote sẽn moon yãmb Wẽnnaam Biig a Zezi Krista, nin-kãng me pa naag n yɩ N-yẽe la Ayoo ye. Bãmb nengẽ yɩɩ N-yẽe bala.
47001020	Wẽnd sẽn kãaba fãa, bãmb n gõms ne b zugu tɩ yaool n yɩ, la yaa bãmb maasem yĩnga la b sã n yet tɩ Wẽnd paam pẽgre bɩ tõnd tõe n leok tɩ: Ami!
47001021	Wẽnd n vigl yãmb ne maam Krista maasmẽ la b taag tõnd ne b ka-sõngo.
47001022	Bãmb n ning b bãnd tõnd dĩirẽ la b pids tõnd sũuri ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng kũuni.
47001023	Wẽnd naag-m lame n ya kaseto tɩ yaa m sẽn pa rat gãgs ne yãmbã la m pa wa Korẽnt.
47001024	Ka yet tɩ d da ratẽ lame n dems y tẽeba ye. Ayoo! Y sũ-noog la d baooda; d miime tɩ sã n ya y tẽeba, y wɩk n yɛsa y nao zutu.
47002001	Maam bal n yeel m sũurẽ tɩ m pa na n leb y nengẽ y sũ-sãanga pʋgẽ ye.
47002002	Sã n ya maam n sãamd yãmb sũuri wilg-y m sẽn na n paam sũ-nooga zĩig ninga sã n ka m sẽn sãam b rãmb sũurã nengẽ?
47002003	M sã n gʋls-y y sẽn mi wã, yaa m sẽn pa rat tɩ m waoonga yɩ sũ-sãang ne neb niyns sẽn da tog n pids-m ne sũ-noogo; m mii vẽenega tɩ m sũ-noog yaa yãmb me rẽnda.
47002004	Sɩda, yaa ne yam-yoodre, ne sũ-weoogre, n paas nintãm la m gʋls yãmba la m da pa maan dẽ n na n sãam y sũur ye; yɩla y bãng nonglem kãseng ning sẽn be m sũurẽ y yĩnga.
47002005	Sã n ya ne ned ninga sẽn waa ne beegrã, ad-y ka maam bal la a beegr ye – la m kõn paas tɩ yɩɩg woto ye – a beega yãmb me.
47002006	Nin-kãng sẽn paam kʋʋnga sɩbgrã, sekame.
47002007	B sẽn pʋs n na n kõ-a sugr la raoodo n são, sã n ka rẽ a sũ-sãanga wat n loogame.
47002008	M kot-y lame tɩ y maan zood ne a n yɩɩge.
47002009	M gʋlsd-y la seb kãngã n na n dɩ kaseto, n na n bãng y sakra sẽn ta zĩig ninga.
47002010	Y sẽn kõ a soab sugrã, mam me kõn mong-a ye; la m sã n kõ-a sugr wala a ra tara m sugr tʋʋmde, yaa yãmb nonglem yĩnga la Krista sẽn be d sʋkã yĩnga.
47002011	D da bas tɩ Sʋtãan belg-do tɩ d mi a geelsa fãa.
47002012	M taa Troas n moon Krista Koe-noogã. M mikame tɩ Soaala paka kʋɩlensa yalengo n kõ-m be,
47002013	baasg fãa m sũura pa tol n gãand laafi tɩ m pa yãend m saam-biig a Tit ye. M pʋʋs-b lame n le wẽnemd n dɩk Masedoan tẽng sor.
47002014	Wẽnd paam barka! Bãmb tũnuga Krista n peeg tõnd tɩ d pʋgd d Tãnsoab sẽn tõog a bɛɛba la d yelgd zĩig zãnga bãmb bãngrã yũ-noogo.
47002015	Wẽnd nifẽ, tõnd sɩd yaa Krista yũ-noogo, sẽn paam b fãagra sʋka wa sẽn na n kong-bã.
47002016	Bogr a ye yĩnga yũuga yaa kũum yũugu n wat ne kũum. Bogra to wã yĩnga, yũuga yaa vɩɩm yũugu n wat ne vɩɩm. La ãnda n tõe tʋʋmd a woto?
47002017	Tõnd ka ya wa neb wʋsgo sẽn pund koom n paasd Wẽnd gomda ye, ayoo! D yaa neb sẽn pelg b sũuri, n gomd ne Krista sɩda, Wẽnd taoore, wa neb sẽn deeg b tʋʋmda Wẽnd nengẽ.
47003001	La d le sɩngdame n lʋɩɩsd d meng taoor bɩ bõe? Sãnd ka wẽnd yaa pakre ne-do, wa sẽn ya pakr ne neb kẽere, tɩ d yiis d tʋʋm-sõnga kaset sɛb n wilg yã, bɩ d deeg d tʋʋm-sõnga kaset sɛb yãmb meng nengẽ?
47003002	D tʋʋm-sõnga kaset sebr yaa yãmb mense, yaa sebr sẽn gʋls y sũurẽ, sebr ned fãa sẽn zãad la a karemnẽ.
47003003	Vẽeneg fas, yãmb yaa Krista sebre b sẽn kõ-do. Ka sebr sẽn gʋls wa sɛb a taaba ne gʋlsg ko-sablg ye, gʋlsa ne Wẽnd Vɩɩga Vʋʋsem; pa gʋls kug peesem zug ye, yaa yĩn-gãongẽ, yaa sũurẽ.
47003004	D sũura sẽn ya kɛgeng woto Wẽnd taoorã, yaa Krista yĩnga.
47003005	Tõnd meng ka tõe n yeel tɩ bũmb tol n beeme n yit tõnd nengẽ ye, ayoo! D tõog buud fãa yita Wẽnnaam nengẽ.
47003006	Wẽnd n kɩt tɩ d lebg b Zood paalga tʋʋm-tʋmda. Zooda yaool n ka zood ning sẽn tar-a a kaset sebr zuga ye, zooda yõga ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsem. Sebra waa ne kũum tɩ Vʋʋsma wat ne vɩɩm.
47003007	Zood ning sẽn tar-a a kaset kug peesem zug la sẽn waa ne kũuma, paamame t'a siginda yãend pẽgr kãsenga al tɩ Israyɛl kamba da pa tõe n ges a Moyiiz nenga sẽn da yãgd ne ziir ninga ye. A ziira yaool n da yaa bũmb sẽn ka na n kaoos n sɛ ye.
47003008	Zood ning sẽn yõg ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsma, zood kãng Siginda ziir kõn yɩɩg sɩda?
47003009	Tʋʋmd ning sẽn baas-a ne ninsaalb paalgrã sã n kõ a tʋʋm-tʋmda ziiri, sẽn tũ a soab wilgri tɩ zemsg zamaana yalsã, nin-kãng soab pẽgr kõn yɩɩg sɩda?
47003010	Ayoo! D kõn yals n mak b ziira ne taab ye tɩ pipi ziira pʋs n ka yɩ zɩɩr meng ye.
47003011	Bũmb sẽn ka na n kaoos n loog sã n puk ne ziiri, bũmb ning sẽn pa loogdã ziira kõn yɩɩg sɩda?
47003012	D sẽn paam saagr a woto fãa kɩtame tɩ d zĩi n ka bʋʋd fɩ.
47003013	D ka ya wa a Moyiiz sẽn da kong n bao peend n lud a nengã, n zoet tɩ Israyɛl kamb na n wa yãend sẽn ka tõe n ka sɛ wã sɛɛbo.
47003014	A Israyɛl kamba yama kell n paa lika. Al n tãag rũnda menga, f sã n karemd zood kʋdga sebre, f neeme tɩ peenda ket n ludame. A pa lak ye, tɩ Krista bal n lakd peend kãnga.
47003015	N-ye! Sẽn ta ne rũnna, a Moyiiz sebra kareng wakato, yaa wa peend la b gãnegd b sũurẽ.
47003016	Ya f sã n kẽ Soaala bal la peenda lakda.
47003017	Soaala la Vʋʋsem: tʋʋmd a ye; la Soaala Vʋʋsem sẽn be zĩig ninga, be la burkĩndlem be.
47003018	Tõnd fãa sẽn doog d neng t'a tʋʋsd Soaala pẽgrã wa nin-gɛtgã, tõnd lebga b wẽnego la d wẽnega pãng tara paasgo n dabda, ne Soaala Vʋʋsma.
47004001	Woto wã, tõnd sẽn paam tʋʋmd kãng ne Wẽnnaam nimbãan-zoeere sẽn maneg tõndo, tõnd ka mi tadgr ye.
47004002	D basda yãnd la zoe-nif buud fãa, n zoet zãmbo la zirẽ-beedo, Wẽnnaam Koɛɛgã mooneg pʋgẽ. D sẽn baood bala, yaa sɩda puki tɩ ned ning fãa sẽn yaa pʋ-peen-neda bãmb taoore bɩ a pẽg tõndo.
47004003	D sẽn moond Koɛɛg ninga sã n ket n ka vẽenega, yaa ne neb niyns sẽn kẽed-b moogã la a ka vẽenega.
47004004	Yaa pʋ-to-nebã: zamaana soaal sẽn sob b rãmb yama tɩ b pa ne Krista Koe-nooga sẽn yãgd ne ziir ningã.
47004005	D zãmsga pʋgẽ, ka tõnd menga yell la d goamd ye. Yaa Krista a Zezi sẽn ya Soaala la d wilgd yãmba; tõnd yẽ yaa yãmb sõgen-kamba, a Zezi yĩnga.
47004006	Wẽnd ning sẽn kõ noore, tɩ vẽenem pusg lik pʋga, yaa bãmb vẽenem n pusg tõnd sũya tɩ d tõe n wilg neb a taaba, Wẽnnaam pẽgr d sẽn yãend t'a yãgd ne Krista nenga.
47004007	D zɩta yõod a woto fãa ne d yĩn-koamsã, d yĩn-tãndã. Dẽ me n kɩt tɩ d mi vẽenega tɩ tõnd pãnga yita Wẽnnaam nengẽ, a ka tõnd meng pãng ye.
47004008	B tara tõnd n tabd zĩis fãa la d nan ka beds ye. D zĩime n tar saagre la d yam nan ka lak ne d meng ye.
47004009	B tara d yaoolgo la Wẽnd nan ka yi d poorẽ ye. B lub-d la tẽnga la b nan ka yiis-d moog ye.
47004010	Sẽn na n yɩlẽ t'a Zezi vɩɩma puk tõnd me yĩngẽ, tõnd me sakda zĩis fãa la wakat fãa a Zezi kũuma namsgo.
47004011	D nan pa ki ye, yaa sɩda, la yaa wakat fãa la b namsd tõnd a Zezi yĩnga la namsga seka a na kʋ-do. Yaa woto me la a Zezi vɩɩma pukd vẽenega tõnd yĩn-kiidgẽ.
47004012	Tõnd nengẽ kũuma tʋmda a tʋʋmde la yãmb nengẽ yaa vɩɩm n tʋmd a tʋʋmde.
47004013	Tõnd tara yam ning tẽeb sẽn kõt a soaba wala sẽn gʋlse: «M tẽeme, la yaa rẽnd yĩng la m gom yã.» Tõnd me tẽedame la yaa rẽnd yĩng la d gomda,
47004014	n miẽ tɩ sẽn vʋʋga Soaal a Zezi wã na n vʋʋga tõnd me ne bãmba la b yals tõnd ne yãmba b sɛɛgẽ.
47004015	La rẽ fãa yaa yãmb yĩnga, tɩ wʋsg gale ne Wẽnd kũuni, tɩ bark pʋʋsga gale neb wʋsg nengẽ, Wẽnd pẽgr yĩnga.
47004016	Yaa rẽnd me yĩng la d raooda ka boogd ye. Ayoo! Yĩnga pãng sã n tar boogre n dabda, d sɩɩga rẽnd tara paasg beoog-beoog fãa.
47004017	Daar a wãn namsg segenda tõnd yĩnga, pẽgr sẽn kõn sɛ, pẽgr sẽn zʋʋg saagre.
47004018	D sẽn saagd n yɩɩdã, ka nif sẽn tõe n yãend ye. Nif sẽn ne ka zɛɛd sɛɛb ye. Nif sẽn pa ne wã n ka sɛt lɛ-lɛ.
47005001	Tõnd sẽn mi, yaa tɩ zãnd ning tõnd sẽn be a soab tẽngrã, tẽng zug ka, sã n wa sirgi, doog a to n be arzãna, Wẽnnaam sẽn segl d yĩnga; roog sẽn kõn sirg abada, sẽn ka ninsaalb nug tʋʋmde la sẽn zao yĩngri.
47005002	D zĩi ne nintãm tẽng zug rooga pʋga n dat ne d sũur fãa tɩ yĩngr dooga me n dogl a zugu.
47005003	La rẽ yaa d sã n dat tɩ b wa mik tɩ d ka zĩ d zaala, d yera fuugu.
47005004	D zĩi d tẽng zug rooga pʋga n tar waasgo la yɩɩre; yaa rẽ me la d dat fuuga yeelgre n yɩɩd a yeegre; d datame n yeelg fuug a yiib soabã n bʋʋg pipi soabã, tɩ vɩɩma rɩ sẽn tõe n ki a soabã.
47005005	Yaa Wẽnd meng n togl tõnd so-kãnga tɩ bãmb meng n lembd tõnd a Vʋʋsem Sõng kũuni.
47005006	D sũur kegma, ba d sã n mi tɩ kaoos yɩnga ne yĩng ning d sẽn zĩ ne a soaba zãagda tõnd ne Soaalã.
47005007	D kẽnda ne tẽebo, ka ne d nina vẽenem ye.
47005008	Tõnd sũur kegmame tɩ d datẽ meng n bas d yĩn-kãnga n tɩ yegl Soaala.
47005009	Dẽ n so tɩ d vɩ ne d yĩngã bɩ d yeeg-a lame n base, d sẽn baood la Wẽnd daab maaneg bala.
47005010	D sẽn ya a soab fãa, d na n yaasa d kãre bʋʋda raare tɩ ned kam fãa reeg a tʋʋm keoore, tʋʋmd ninga a sẽn tʋme, a sẽn da waa n ket ne a yĩnga, a tʋʋm sõng wala a tʋʋm wẽnga.
47005011	D sẽn zoet tɩ d Soaala waoogr na n wa pa sãoog yĩnga, d modgdame tɩ ninsaalba reegd d saglgo. Sã n ya ne Wẽnde, d miime tɩ d yɛsa d kãr bãmb taoore la d tẽedame tɩ d sũura me rɩga pɛɛlg fas bãmb taoore.
47005012	Ka lʋɩɩs d meng taoorã la d rat n le sɩng ye, d wilgd-y lame bala bũmb ning sẽn be d nengẽ tɩ y zug tõe n zẽk ne tõndo la woto y na lub sẽn ka baood b meng pẽgre ne sẽn solg sũurẽ, n baood-a ne sẽn puk yɩnga.
47005013	Sɩda d sã n gomame waa d yika gãeemdo, yaa Wẽnd yĩnga; d sã n gomd tɩ tũudẽ, yaa yãmb yĩnga.
47005014	A Zezi Krista nonglem rɩdgd-d lame tɩ d tags tɩ nin-yend sã n ki neb fãa yĩngã, fãa n naag n ki.
47005015	B sẽn ki fãa gill yĩngã, yaa sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ sẽn vɩ-ba da le vɩɩnd d mens yĩng ye, b vɩɩnd sẽn ki-a la sẽn vʋʋg-a b fãa yĩnga.
47005016	Woto wã d ka le ne ned ba a ye ne ninsaal nif ye. Ba sã n da yaa ne d nin la d da bãng Krista, ka boto marsã la d le get-b ye.
47005017	Ned sã n kẽ Krista a lebga nin-paalle, nin-kʋdga menemame tɩ paalla led a zĩiga.
47005018	La fãa yita Wẽnd nengẽ, bãmb tũu Krista maasem n maneg tõnd yell ne bãmba la b kõ-d la maneg taab yell ne tʋʋmd ning d sẽn deeg b nengẽ wã.
47005019	Yaa Wẽnd meng n da tũ Krista n wẽnemd dũniya neng n le tees b menga; b basa ninsaal beegr taale la b kõ tõnd zelemd sẽn na n gom n maneg d taab yelle.
47005020	Tõnd tʋʋmd yaa d deeg Krista zĩiga. Yaa wa Wẽnd sagenda ne tõnd noore. Yaa rẽ la d kot-y, Krista yĩnga, tɩ y maneg y yell ne Wẽnde.
47005021	Ned ning sẽn ka maana yel-wẽndã, yẽ soab basame tɩ b tʋk-a yel-wẽnd zɩɩb, sẽn na n yɩlẽ bala tɩ Wẽnd tũ a maasem n pids tõnd ne b sõmblem.
47006001	Tõnd sẽn ya Wẽnd tʋʋm-tʋmdba, tõnd wɩngda ne yãmba tɩ y da sãam Wẽnnaam kũuna b sẽn kõ yãmba ye.
47006002	Yaa bãmb meng n yete: «Barka daare mam deega f kosgo, fãagra raare, mam sõnga foom.» Barka raar la rũnna, fãagra raar la rũnna.
47006003	Woto tõnd ka rata tɩ d manesem rɩgl kugr tɩ ned lak n lʋɩ tɩ b wa sãbs tõnd tʋʋmda ye.
47006004	D sẽn pa rat tɩ b sãbs-dã, d modgda d manesem fãa pʋgẽ, n wilg tɩ d yaa Soaala tʋʋm-tʋmdba. D modgdame n sak lengr daar fãa, n sak sũ-beedo la yɩɩre,
47006005	n sak pãbre, n sak roog kõom, n nams zab-kaoodb nusẽ, n sak yaamse, n bas gõeem, n bas rɩɩbo;
47006006	d modgda ne pʋ-peelem, ne bãngr baoobo, ne sũ-tõogo, ne taab sʋk ningri, ne yam sõng baoobo, ne taab nonglem akɩka,
47006007	ne sɩd togsgo, ne Wẽnd pãng bõsgo; d modgda ne sõmblem zab-teed baoobo, zab-teed sẽn zãad n digd bɛɛba, zab-teed sẽn zãad n ligind bɛɛba.
47006008	D sakda waoor wala paoore, yʋ-sõng wala yʋ-beedo. B rõt-d la zirẽ-beedo tɩ d yaool n togsd sɩda,
47006009	b get-d la wa neb sẽn ka yʋʋre, tɩ d yʋʋr yaool n sãt zĩig zãnga, wa neb kũum sẽn yãk raare tɩ d vɩɩma wɩɩd ne pãnga; wa neb sẽn tog ne kaase la d yaool n ka kiid ye;
47006010	wa neb sẽn zĩ ne sũ-sãamse, tɩ d noor yõgemd daar fãa; wa naong rãmba tɩ wʋsg yaool n tũud tõnd n lebgd arzɛk rãmba; wa nug sẽn ka zãad rãmba, tɩ d yaool n tar fãa.
47006011	D ka gom-y ne zoe-nif ye, Korẽnt dãmba, d laka d sũur zãng n wilg yã.
47006012	D sũurẽ wã weer be y yĩnga, ya y meng sũurẽ la weer paoogda.
47006013	Lebs-y tõnd d yel-sõmde; m gomda ne yãmb wala m kamba, m kot-y lame tɩ y pak y sũura yalengo.
47006014	Da lagem-y ne bu-zẽmbã n dɩk so-yɛng ye. Bõe n be sẽn baood-a sõmblem la sẽn baooda wẽng sʋka, vẽenem ne lik sʋka?
47006015	Sɛdg bʋg buud n tõe n sede Krista ne a Beliar sʋka? Sẽn tẽed-a la sẽn ka tẽed-a lagemda taab bõe yĩnga?
47006016	Wẽnd dooga maanda a wãn n wa lebg wẽn-naandsa rẽnna? Tõnd yẽne la Wẽnd vɩɩga roogo tɩ b meng n yeele: «M na n ti-la m doog bãmb sʋka la m na n zĩnd n paka bãmba. M na yɩ b Wẽnd tɩ bãmb yɩ m neba.»
47006017	Dɩlla welg-y mens ne nin-bãmba, bas-y-b kɛɛnga. Da sɩɩs-y bõn-dẽgd buud ye tɩ m zaka noor na pak y yĩnga.
47006018	M na yɩ Ba y yĩnga tɩ y me yɩ m kom-dibli la m kom-pugli – Pãng-Soaba-Wẽnd n yeele.
47007001	Tõnd sẽn paam kãab nood a woto fãa, m kom-sõma, d sõng tɩ d yĩnga la d yama lak ne rẽgd buud fãa, d zoe Wẽnnaam la d baas d tʋʋmna, d sõmblem baoob tʋʋmna.
47007002	Pak-y y sũurã d yĩnga. Ned ba a ye ka rɩ bõne d nengẽ ye. Ned ba a ye ka lebg naongo, tõnd ka rɩ ned ba a ye paoong ye.
47007003	M pa gomd woto n dat n ning y taal ye. M zoe n togs-y lame tɩ y vɩ bɩ y ki yã, y paada tõnd nonglem pʋgẽ.
47007004	D sũur kegma ne yã la d zug zẽka wʋsgo; y maasa d sũuri al tɩ ba ne d sen tar toogã, m sũ-nooga ket n pida zãnga.
47007005	D taa Masedoan la pems maasg ka wẽ d yĩnga ye. D yãee lengre zĩig zãnga. Yɩnga yɩɩ maoore tɩ pʋgẽ ya rabeem.
47007006	Wẽnd sẽn maasd nimbãan-dãmb sũuri, n maag tõnd dẽnna ne a Tit waoongo.
47007007	Ka a waoonga bal ye, yaa yẽ me sẽn leok t'a yãenda sũ-noog y sʋka. A wilg-d lame tɩ y gũud-d la ne y sũur fãa; a wilg-d lame tɩ y sũur sãama y sẽn ka yãend tõndã; a wilga y sẽn da rat neer ning fãa ne tõndo, la woto wã mam nengẽ yɩɩ sũ-noog ne sũ-noogo.
47007008	Sɩda m sebrã sã n sãam y sũuri me, ad-y rẽ pa sek mam lɛɛg n zab ne m meng marsa ye; tõe tɩ m zaba ne m menga a wakatẽ tɩ m mi tɩ sebrã kõ-y la sũ-sãanga, ba sũ-sãanga sã n ka kaoose.
47007009	La marsã m sũur noomame. Ka y sũ-sãangã n wa ne mam sũ-nooga ye, yaa m sẽn yãe t'a waa ne y tuubgu. Yãmb sũ-sãangã yaa Wẽnd sẽn dat a soaba buudu; tõnd ka maan bũmbu n wa ne-a ye.
47007010	Sũ-sãang wa Wẽnd sẽn dat a soaba buudu wata ne tuubgu n manegd yelle la woto wã a ka bõn-wẽng ye. Yaa sũ-sãang wa zamaana rãmb sẽn mi a soabã n wat ne kũum.
47007011	Ad-y y sũ-sãang sẽn naag ne tuubgã tʋma tʋʋm-sõma y sũurẽ. Ad-y y sẽn yãgd marsã n na n bao yella sore, – bõe la m gomd woto? – Ad-y y sẽn pa rat n dɩ a taale, n sãbsda wẽnem, ad-y y sẽn zoet rabeem ne a maanego; ad-y y sẽn tʋl m yãabo, ad-y y sẽn tʋl neere, ad-y y sẽn gẽesd sɩbg-sõngo. Y wilga sõmb-sõmbo tɩ yell kãnga pʋgẽ y ka lʋɩɩs y toog ye.
47007012	Dɩlla m sã n gʋls-y sebre, ad-y ka bɛɛgda, ad-y ka b sẽn beeg a soaba me yĩng ye. Yaa sẽn na n yɩlẽ bala tɩ y nonglem kãsenga ne tõnd puk Wẽnd taoore.
47007013	Yaa rẽ n maas d sũuri. La sũ-noog sẽn yɩɩd rẽ n waa n paase: ya a Tit sũ-noogã, t'a yama gãanda y fãa poorẽ.
47007014	M sã n saag, yẽ taoore, n pẽg m meng bifu yãmb poorẽ, dẽn ka bũmb sẽn wat ne m yãnd ye. M sẽn minim n togs sɩd bũmb fãa poorẽ, m sẽn togs bũmb ning a Tit poorẽ wã me yɩɩ sɩda.
47007015	La woto a nonglem ne yãmb le paasame t'a tẽega y fãa sakr sẽn yɩ a soaba, a tẽega y sẽn deeg-a ne rigbu la sulg-m-menga.
47007016	M sũur nooma m sẽn tõe n teeg-y bũmb fãa pʋgẽ.
47008001	M saam-biisi, d wilgd-y la kũun ning Wẽnd sẽn kõ Masedoan Tigengu.
47008002	Ne b namsga sẽn yɩ ka tɛka, b kɛ-la b sũ-noog kãsenga la b naonga sẽn yɩ naong menga pʋga n yiis b kõo-n-da-kees kũuni.
47008003	M kõta kaset tɩ b kõo ne yamleoogo wala b pãng sẽn tõe la sẽn yɩɩg b pãng menga.
47008004	Bãmb meng n kos tõnd ne dɩdgre tɩ bas-ba tɩ b naag n sõng nin-sõma wã.
47008005	B kõome tɩ yɩɩg d sẽn da tẽeda tɩ yaa b mens la b reng n dɩk n kõ Wẽnde, la tõnd me, Wẽnd poore, ne Wẽnd sõngre.
47008006	Dẽ n kɩt tɩ d kos a Tit t'a sõnge, tɩ kũm-taab-nimbãanega tʋʋmde a sẽn sɩng yãmb sʋka, baas neere.
47008007	Y sẽn wɩngd sõma ne bũmb faa wã: ne tẽebo, ne goam, ne bãngre, ne tʋʋmde, ne nonglem, wa tõnd sẽn wilg yãmb a soabã, bɩ y wɩng woto me ne taab sõngre.
47008008	Ka noor la m kõt-y ye, m datame bal tɩ y sẽn wɩngd ne taab sõngrã wilg tɩ y sɩd tara taab nonglem akɩka.
47008009	Yãmb mii neere Soaal a Zezi Krista ne b kõt yaarã. B sẽn da ya arzɛk soaba b lebga naong soab tõnd yĩnga la woto b naonga lɛɛg n pidsa tõnd ne arzɛka.
47008010	Dɩlla yaa saglg bala la m kõt yãmba la wã n tog ne yã tɩ yãmb n deng neba fãa rɩẽ, n tags tʋʋmd kãng yelle la y sɩng-a.
47008011	Baas-y tʋʋmda marsã wala y sẽn da rat ne sũur ningã la ne pãng ningã.
47008012	Fo sũura raab sã n pidi, f sẽn wat ne bũmb ning fãa yɩta bõn-sõngo tɩ ka fo sẽn ka tara la b na n ges ye, yaa fo sẽn tarã.
47008013	Pa yet tɩ y kõ y taab la y zĩnd ne naong ye; neera la ned fãa paoong zeng a to rẽnna.
47008014	Yãmb paoonga n dɩlgd bãmb naong rũnna, la raar a to tõe tɩ b me paoong wa lek yãmb sãoogo. Woto la zem-taab zĩndida.
47008015	Yaa woto la b gʋlsyã: Sẽn deeg-a wʋsgo ka paam tɩ yõsg ye, la sẽn deeg-a bilf me ka yãe tɩ paoog-a ye.
47008016	Wẽnnaam paam barka, bãmb sẽn yãnga a Tit nonglem ne yãmba!
47008017	A saka m boolle. A sũura nonglem sẽn kɛɛd n yɩɩd pĩnda, a kõ-la a meng yam n na n wa y nengẽ.
47008018	D yãka d saam-biig a ye t'a yãag-a; kristneba fãa pẽgda nin-kãng sẽn tʋm tʋʋmd ninga Koe-nooga yĩnga;
47008019	la ka rẽ bal ye, yaa kristneba fãa n yãk-a t'a yãag tõnd d so-toaka pʋgẽ, n naag n yãend y vaag-n-kõ zãnga sẽn wat ne Soaala pẽgr ninga la a naag n yãend tɩ yɛla me tũu wa d sẽn date.
47008020	D maana woto tɩ d ka rat tɩ ned wɩd tõnd ligd kãnga sẽn labsa poorẽ ye: sɩd lebga zɩɩb meng la b tʋk-do.
47008021	Ka Wẽnd taoor bal la d baood tɩ d yɛla tũ sor ye, yaa ninsaalba me taoore.
47008022	D saam-biig a to la d paas bãmb b yiibã; d yãenda naoor yaka la bũmb wʋsg pʋgẽ tɩ nin-kãng tara tʋʋmda sũuri; so kãngã, a le wɩsg a meng n yɩɩda, a pʋg sẽn peel ne-y yĩnga.
47008023	Sã n ya a Tit, yẽ yaa mam tũud-n-taaga la m sõangd yãmb sʋka; sã n ya saam-biis a taabã, yaa Tigengã, Krista zu-zẽkrã, n yãk-ba.
47008024	Wilg-y-ba, tẽedba fãa taoore, y nonglma sẽn ta zĩig ninga la sẽn tũ ne bũmb ning tɩ d tar zu-zẽkre y fãa gill poorẽ.
47009001	M pa na n nams n gʋls yãmb saam-biisa sõngra poorẽ ye.
47009002	M miime tɩ yaa ne y sũur fãa la y baood nin-sõma wã sõngre la m goma y yelle ne Masedoan dãmb n pẽg yãmba; m togsame tɩ yaa al dɩẽ woko la Akayi tẽng segl n sɛ. Yãmb modgra kõo neb wʋsg sũ-keelem.
47009003	M na n deng n tʋma m saam-biisã tɩ mam sẽn pẽg yãmba da wa yɩ zirẽ-beedo la b mik tɩ yãmb segl n sɛɛme wa mam sẽn yeelã.
47009004	Ka rẽ Masedoan dãmba sã n tũ maam n wa ling yãmba, m sẽn tãoosd raooda na n lebga yãnde; na yɩ yãmb dẽnd n yɩɩda.
47009005	Dẽ la m tʋlg yã tɩ d saam-biisa reng taoore tɩ y segl y sẽn dat n kɩs bũmb ningã tɩ beed ka naag ye, la b yãend tɩ y kõta ne y sũuri.
47009006	Gese, kʋɩɩm sã n zoe bʋdb toogo, a na n tigsa ka-faado la ned ning sẽn bʋta ne sũuri yaa bark buud fãa la a tigsda.
47009007	Bɩ yãmb ned kam fãa tũ a sũur yalem n kõ a sẽn tare la a ra maan wala a ka kõt ne yamleoog ye, wala yaa moadeg ye. Sẽn kõt-a ne yamleoog la Wẽnnaam nonga.
47009008	Bũmb zãnga Wẽnd meng tõeeme n pids yãmb ne sõm buud fãa, al tɩ y tar wakat fãa, la bũmb fãa pʋgẽ sẽn sek y vɩɩma n tol n kell, tɩ yãmb me rɩk rẽ n maan yel-sõmde.
47009009	Yaa woto la b gʋls yã: «Zĩis fãa b maanda sõm bala, b kõo naong rãmba, b sõmblem kõn sɛ abada.»
47009010	Wẽnd sẽn kõt ka-koaad ka buud sẽn na n bʋde, la bur sẽn na n dɩ, b na kõ yãmb a yiiba fãa, la y sõmblema na n woma biis zembala.
47009011	Y arzɛka sã n paase, y na tũ rẽ n lebg kõt yaar dãmba, la tõnd me na tũ y kõt yaarã n sõng tɩ neba fãa wɩng ne Wẽnd bark pʋʋsg kãsenga.
47009012	Ka nin-sõma wã bal nimbãaneg la y kũmd ne kũun-sõng a woto ye, kũuna le wata ne Wẽnd bark pʋʋsg neb ka tɛk nengẽ.
47009013	Kũuna wilgd-b-la yãmb sẽn ya neb niynsi la b pẽgda Wẽnnaam b sẽn bãng tɩ yãmb sɩd tũuda Krista Koe-noogã. B pẽgd-y lame yɛsa tɩ y sẽn kõt n pa keesdẽ wã, pukda y zood ne nin-sõma wã la ne tõnd me.
47009014	B sã n pʋʋsd yãmb yĩnga, lebga b me wilg b nonglem ne yãmba, b sẽn yãend bark ning Wẽnd sẽn sudg yãmbã.
47009015	Wẽnnaam paam barka tɩ b kõ-d la kũuni sẽn yɩɩd noor toagsg!
47010001	N-ye! Sẽn kot-a yãmbã, Krista sẽn bʋgs la b ya nin-noang yĩngã, yaa mam meng a Pol, rao ninga sẽn ka tar võore a sã n be yãmb sʋka, t'a sã n yaool n zãr bɩ a ya nin-toaaga,
47010002	maam n kot-y: sõng-y tɩ m sã n wa bɩ m da yik zʋg toaag ning m sẽn dat yik ne neb kẽera ye. Bãmb dãmb tẽedame tɩ m manesma tũuda ninsaalb rẽnna.
47010003	Tõnd vɩɩ dũni wã pʋga, yaa sɩda, la tõnd ka zabd ne dũni rãmba zab-teed ye.
47010004	N-ye! Tõnd zab-teeda ka zamaana rãmb dẽnd ye, Wẽnd n kõ-b tõndo, b meng yĩnga, la d tõe n tusa tãnsoben-doog buud fãa n lubi.
47010005	Sẽn maand-b wa b ka mi Wẽndã, tõnd n lubd bãmb dãmba sɩlem la b tɩtaam, tõnd n gõdgd yam buud fãa n loe ne Krista tẽebo.
47010006	Yãmb tũudma sã n lebg neer zãnga, d na yik n zab la d sɩbg kɩɩsd fãa.
47010007	Ade, ned sã n beẽ n tẽed tɩ Krista n so-a, a bãng rũnna la beoog tɩ Krista n so yẽnda, la Krista n so tõnd me.
47010008	Yãmb sõmblem paasg yĩnga, ka y bõna yĩng ye, d paama tõog Soaala nengẽ la d sã n pẽgd d meng tɩ loog, yãnd ka tar m ye.
47010009	M ka rat n maan wa m baood n na n fʋʋsa yãmb ne m sɛba ye.
47010010	B yetame tɩ m sɛba pʋga m yaa gãndaoogo la nin-toaaga la m sã n yɛs y taoore m ka tar yaoko la m ka mi goam ye.
47010011	Bãng-y nere tɩ d sẽn be yɩɩg n ya a soab ne d goama, d sã n pẽnege, yaa d tʋʋma n na n wilg tɩ d ka teem ye.
47010012	M pa kɩɩs tɩ m kõn saag n zeng m meng bɩ m mak m meng ne neb kẽer ye. Bãmb dãmb sẽn baood yaa b lʋɩ b taab taoore. B sẽn pa rʋʋsd ned a to n ta b sẽn yals b meng zĩig ningã, b yaa yalemse.
47010013	Tõnd yẽ kõn saag n pẽg d meng tɩ loog ye. Tõnd tũuda sor ning Wẽnd sẽn wilg tõnd tɩ d dɩk n ta yãmbã.
47010014	D ka na n tũ sor a to wala sor ning d sẽn dɩka ka taas tõnd yãmb nengẽ ye. D taame menga ne Krista Koe-noogo.
47010015	Tõnd pa na n pẽg d meng tɩ loog ne d taab tʋʋm ye la d saagdame tɩ y tẽeba sẽn yẽrgd n dabd taoorã, d na waa n lebg y zu-zẽkre wa sẽn yɩ zĩisa taabã.
47010016	D na n gãndga yãmb tẽngã n moon Koe-nooga zĩis a taaba, la kõn le yɩ ned a to toaagẽ, la kõn le yɩ ne neb a taab sẽn tʋʋm n dɩglẽ, la d na n pẽgd d meng ye.
47010017	Ned sã n baood a pẽgre, bɩ a bao-a Soaala nengẽ.
47010018	Ad-y ka ned ning sẽn pẽgd a meng n ya nin-kãseng ye, yaa Soaala sẽn pẽgd a soaba.
47011001	Y sã n tõe n sak tɩ m maan wa gãeeng bɩ y sak waare!
47011002	Mam sẽn nong yãmb ne sũ-kiir ningã, yaa ne Wẽnd meng nonglem; m dɩka yãmb n kõ sɩd a ye; m peega yãmb wa pug-bĩngri n tɩ kɩs Krista.
47011003	La rabeem tar-m lame, m zoeta y na n wa maan wa a Awa sẽn sak waafa sɩlem goama, tɩ y sũya wa rẽgem, tɩ y sãam y pʋ-peelem ne Krista.
47011004	M neeme tɩ ned ninga fãa sẽn wa-a yãmb nengẽ t'a na n wilga yãmb Zezi a to, sẽn ka tõnd sẽn wilg a soabã, bɩ a gom Vʋʋsem Sõng a to sẽn ka yãmb sẽn zoe n paam a soabã, bɩ a moon koɛɛg a to sẽn ka Krista rẽnna, yãmb deegda yẽ soab neere.
47011005	Mik m pa tagsd tɩ nin-bãmb sẽn tẽed tɩ b yɩɩda tʋʋm-tʋmdb a taabã, m pa tẽed tɩ b sãoo maam ye.
47011006	Ba mam sã n ka goam-goamda, ne bãngr yẽ sẽ, m ka paood ye; d wilg-y la y nifẽ, ne bũmb wʋsgo sẽn yɩ vẽenese.
47011007	Dɩlla m kongra bee yɛ? Mam sẽn moon yãmb Koe-noogã n pa tol n bao yõoda bɩ bõe? Bɩ mam sẽn sak n yaal m menga n na n zẽk yãmbã?
47011008	Yaa saam-biis a taab paoong la m deeg n dɩlg m menga, n tõog n sõng yãmba.
47011009	M sẽn ta y nengẽ tɩ bũmb paoog-ma m ka lebg yãmb ned ba a ye zɩɩb ye, yaa Masedoan saam-biisi n yaoog-m. M pa tʋlg, ba vugr menga, n kos yãmb sãando la m kõn saag abada.
47011010	Sɩd wa Krista sẽn ya m kasetã, m zug kõn sulg Akayi tẽn-tõre, yell kãnga poorẽ ye.
47011011	La rẽ ya m sẽn pa nong yãmba bɩ? Ayoo! Wẽnd mi tɩ ka boto ye.
47011012	M na kell n maan boto tɩ neb niyns sẽn baood-b n na n kõ b meng bʋʋm, n gomd tɩ b maana wa tõndã, bɩ b ra tõog n paam bʋʋm ye.
47011013	Nin-bãmb ka tʋʋm-tʋmdb akɩk ye, yaa rɩ baoodb sẽn belg tɩ b yaa Krista tʋʋm-tʋmdba.
47011014	La rẽ ka tog n yɛɛs-d ye tɩ Sʋtãan meng mi n wẽnda malɛk ne a vẽenem.
47011015	Dɩlla Sʋtãana neba sã n yet tɩ yaa Wẽnd sõmblema la b pʋgda, bɩ d da yɛɛs ye. D bãng bala tɩ b kũuma na n wẽnega b vɩɩma: bõn-wẽnga.
47011016	M le yet-y lame, da mams-y maam wa gãeeng ye; la rẽ sã n noom-y bɩ y bas tɩ m sɩd yɩ gãeenga n tõog n maan wakr bilfu.
47011017	M sẽn na n togsã, m ka na n togs-a ne Soaala yam ye, na n yɩɩ wa ne gãeemdo, tɩ m tara m sẽn na n pẽg m menga.
47011018	Neb wʋsg nagda ne zamaana yɛla. M me na maan wa bãmba.
47011019	Y moor nooma ne gãeemse la yãmb n yaool n get y mens wa neb sẽn tar b vɩɩma buka.
47011020	Yãmb sakdame tɩ b kẽesd-y yembdo, tɩ b rɩt yãmba, tɩ b fãad yãmba, tɩ b tar yãmb toogo, tɩ b tʋʋd yãmb, tɩ b laand-y pegse.
47011021	M togsda rẽ ne yãnde; d sɩd basa d meng yog-yoge. M me na n goma wa gãeenga la m yeel tɩ b sẽn lʋɩɩsd bũmb ning taoorã, ma me toe rẽnna.
47011022	B yet tɩ yaa Ebre rãmb buudu, maam me; tɩ b yaa Israyɛl kamba, maam me; tɩ b yaa Abraam yagense, maam me;
47011023	tɩ b yaa Krista Tʋʋm-tʋmdba, mam na gom wa gãeenga: maam n yɩɩd bãmba; m sẽn kẽ bi-bees roogẽ sõor yɩɩd-b lame, b sẽn pãb-m sõor yɩɩd-b lame; yɩɩ naoor yak la kellẽ bilf bal tɩ m kiẽ.
47011024	M sẽn deeg Zʋɩf rãmba nengẽ kaas pistã la a wɛ – a ye bal n ka pisnaase – yaa naoor a nu.
47011025	Sãbsa yaa naoor a tãabo; vugr la b lab-m ne kuga; d koglg sẽn paa koomẽ yaa naoor a tã; m tol n paa kooma zug wĩndg la yʋng tõre.
47011026	Sor zug yaams yɩɩ ka tɛka; ad kʋɩlsa gɩdgre, ad so-gɩtba, ad saam-biisi, ad bu-zẽmba, ad tẽng pugẽ yel-pakre, ad we-raoog rẽnna, mogr dẽnna, ad buuda neb zãmbo,
47011027	m kõn gom m tʋʋmde, m namsgo, gõeem kaalem, kom la ko-yũud yelle, kom-gãaga, fut sẽn na n yiis waood kaalem.
47011028	D kõn gom sẽn keta ye: m sẽn zĩ ne yɩɩr ning beoog-beoog fãa, Tigenga yɛl sẽn loe m zug yĩnga.
47011029	Ãnda la pãn-kaoolg soaba, tɩ m pa naag-a n ya koamsa? Ãnda n lʋɩte t'a lʋɩɩsa ka yõog-m wala bugum?
47011030	M sẽn tõe n zẽk m meng ne bũmb ning yaa m komsma.
47011031	Tõnd Soaala Zezi Krista Ba a Wẽnde – sẽn so bark yʋʋm tong taab n ka mi sɛɛbã – bãmb miime tɩ m pa yagd ye.
47011032	Damas tẽng naaba, a Aretas, kɩtame tɩ tãb-biisa gũbg tẽngã n baood n na n yõk-ma.
47011033	La yɩɩ peoog pʋga la b sagl maam n tũnug roog võore n sik-m lal-gũbra poore la woto la m tõog n põs-a.
47012001	Ka yaa zẽk-m-meng la y baood laa? (Rẽ yaool n pa segd ye) la bas-y tɩ m togs-y bũmb ning fãa Wẽnd sẽn wilg maam la m sẽn yãende.
47012002	M mii kristneda, yʋʋm piig la a naas rũnna (yaa ne a yĩnga, mam pa mi ye, Wẽnd n mi) b tall-a lame n dʋʋs arzãna.
47012003	La nin-kãnga sẽn dʋʋs arzãna, yaa ne a yĩnga, mam pa tõe n bãng ye, Wẽnd n mi.
47012004	Beene, yẽ soaba wʋma goama ninsaal sẽn ka tõe n le rɩk n togs ne ninsaal noor ye.
47012005	Nin-kãng yĩnga, mam da tõeeme n zẽk m menga, la sã n ya maam, m komsma bal la m na n lʋɩɩs taoore.
47012006	Mam sã n da tʋlgẽ n zẽk m meng dẽ yĩng me, kõn yɩẽ gãeemd ye, tɩ yaẽ la sɩda, la m kõn wɩɩg ye, ka rẽ neba wat n sãmbame tɩ m sõmblema yɩɩda bãmb sẽn ne wã, bɩ b sẽn wʋmdã.
47012007	Sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ m zu-nooga ra wa ne m nagre, m paama namsg sẽn wẽnd moog n sorg m yĩngã, wẽnd Sʋtãan n gõod n laand-m pegse – tɩ m da maan nagr ye!
47012008	Al naoor a tãabo mam yõka Soaala sɛɛga tɩ b fãag maam,
47012009	tɩ b leok maam: «Base, m sõngr kõn paoog f ye, m pãnga na keng f komsem.» Woto wã yaa ne sũ-noog kãseng la m lʋɩɩsd m komsma taoore tɩ Krista pãnga tõog n sig m zugu.
47012010	Yaa rẽ me yĩng la m pid ne sũ-noogo m sẽn sak Krista yĩnga, komsma, paoogrã, naongã, namsgã, yɩɩrã. La m sẽn waa n lebg koams zãnga la m lebg pãng soaba.
47012011	Y sẽn maana m ka lebg gãeenga! Yãmb n da togẽ n pẽg maam. Ne m sẽn ka fɩ wã, m ka ne yãmb sẽn boond b rãmb tɩ tʋʋm-tʋmdb bɛda sẽn yɩɩd-m ne bũmb ning ye.
47012012	Ad bũmb ning sẽn maand kaset tɩ f yaa tʋʋm-tʋmd tɩ neb fãa miẽ: sũ-tõog namsg pʋgẽ, wẽnd makr dãmba, yel-soalma, bõn-bãna.
47012013	Yaa bõe la tẽns a taaba Tigeng paamyã tɩ yãmb ka paame sã n ka mam meng sẽn pa reeg y bũmbã? La rẽ sã n ya zãmbo bɩ y kõ-m sugri.
47012014	M le segendame n na n wa yãmb nengẽ la woto n tõkd m naoor a tãab soaba la m kõn bõs y sãando, tɩ mam sẽn data, pa yãmb paoong ye, ya y mense. Yaa kamb n tigsd b ba rãmb yĩnga, bɩ yaa ba rãmb n tigsd b kamb yĩnga?
47012015	Sã n ya maam, m na n sɛ m pãng fãa yãmb sɩɩs yĩnga; yaa m nonglma sẽn paasdã n boogd yãmb dẽnd ne maam?
47012016	Beneere, nina na n yeelame tɩ mam pa rɩ yãmb ye, yaa sɩda, la m belg n dɩɩme tɩ m sɩlma yaa sɩlem baafo.
47012017	Yaa ne m tʋʋm-tʋmda bõe la m belg yãmb n dɩ?
47012018	A Tit la m modgr t'a wa, yẽ ne m saam-biig y sẽn mi neere. Dɩlla yaa Tit n belg yãmb bɩ? Tõnd d yiiba zʋgo n ka yɩ zʋg yɛng sɩda? D ka rɩk taab nao sɩda?
47012019	Al daar zãar menga yãmb da tõeeme n yõke tɩ tõnd dat n kõ-la d meng bʋʋm, yãmb taoore, baa fɩ! Tõnd gomda Wẽnnaam la Krista taoore la rẽ fãa yaa yãmb sõngr yĩnga, m kom nongedse.
47012020	M zoeta m na n wa tũ yãmb nengẽ n ka mik tɩ y yaa wa m sẽn datã, bɩ yãmb me mik tɩ m ka ya wa y sẽn data ye. M zoeta m wa mik tɩ ket n yaa zaba, sũ-kiiri, zoe-bõne, beem, wɩdga, gom yaalse, no-rɩkre, kalem-kalem bala.
47012021	M zoeta m na n wa y sʋka, tɩ Wẽnd ning-m yãnde, yãmb poorẽ, tɩ m wa kiigd nintãm, tɩ yell maandeb kʋdã kẽer ka sak n tuub b tʋʋm wẽna ye: b yoobã la b yell yooda taaba ye.
47013001	Woto n tõkd naoora tã marsã m sẽn wat y nengẽ. Koɛɛg buud faa ratame tɩ b welg-a ne kaset dãmb a yiib bɩ a tãabo.
47013002	M zoe n togsa yell mandeb kʋdã la sẽn wẽnd b bãmbã, la m le wilgd-b la rũnna yɛsa, tɩ m nan ket yɩɩga, wala m sẽn wilg-b m waoonga yiib soaba wakato: m sã n wa marsã sugr ka ye.
47013003	Yãmb dat n bãnga sã n yaa sɩd tɩ Krista gomda ne m noore? Bãmb yẽ la sẽn ka põnegd-y wã la, bãmb wata yãmb sʋk ne pãng la!
47013004	Yaa sɩda, b saka komslem, tɩ b ka-b pika la ne Wẽnd pãnga b ket n vɩɩme. Tõnd me boto. Tõnd me komsame, la Wẽnd ne b pãngã na kõ-d vɩɩm, d tʋʋmda pʋgẽ.
47013005	Kẽe-y y meng sũurẽ, bao-y n gese y sã n tara tẽebo. Sok-y y mense, y ka ne tɩ Krista be y pʋsẽ. Wẽnd na kɩt tɩ y menga sokr ra wa ne y bãon-lukr ye.
47013006	Wala m sẽn tẽedã, y kõn yãend tɩ d bãong lukr ye.
47013007	Tõnd pʋʋsda Wẽnd tɩ y ra maan wẽng ye. Tõnd pa rat n maan waa d yɩɩda d taab toog wakat ye, d datame n maan neere, ba neera sã n na n waa ne toogo.
47013008	Tõnd ka tar pãng n kɩɩs sɩd ye, d pãnga la d sõng sɩd bala.
47013009	D komsma sẽn ya a soab fãa, d bee sũ-noog pʋgẽ, d sã n ne tɩ yãmb wɩɩda pãnga. D sẽn kot bũmb ning d pʋʋsg pʋgẽ, yaa yãmb lebg sõma.
47013010	Yaa woto la m gʋls-y tɩ m ket yɩɩga tɩ d sã n wa pẽneg taaba bɩ d bas toolem ne yã; Soaal kõo tõnd pãng kãng manegr yĩnga, ka sãoong yĩng ye.
47013011	Dẽn yĩnga, m saam-biisi, noog-y y sũuri, bao-y sõmblem bala, sõng-taaba bala; yɩɩ-y sũ-yɛnga, vɩɩnd-y laafi ne taaba, la Wẽnd sẽn ya nonglem la laafi Naaba na zĩnd ne yã!
47013012	Pʋʋs-y taab neere. Saam-biisa fãa tɩ d pʋʋs y zãnga.
47013013	Soaala Zezi Krista barka, Wẽnnaam Ba nonglem la a Vʋʋsem Sõng zoodo lagem y ne taaba. Ami!
48001001	Maam a Pol, sẽn lebga Soaala tʋʋm-tʋmda tɩ pa tũ ne ninsaal pãnga bɩ a sõngre: tũu ne Krista a Zezi meng pãnga la ne Ba a Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋg-b kɩɩms sʋka.
48001002	Maam la saam-biisa sẽn be-b ne maama, tõnd n pʋʋsd Wẽnnaam Tigenga kamb fãa sẽn be Galasi.
48001003	Wẽnd na sudg-y b kũuna, n zĩndig-y ne laafi, d Ba a Wẽnd la d Soaal a Zezi Krista maasmẽ,
48001004	bãmb n kɩs b meng d yel-wẽna yĩnga, bãmb n kɩt tɩ d tɩlg dũnna zamaan wẽngã, wala d Ba a Wẽnd sẽn tʋlge.
48001005	B soog pẽgr yʋʋm sẽn kõn sɛ. Ami!
48001006	M yɛɛsa y sẽn yɩ tao-tao, n bas Wẽnd sẽn bool-y ne Krista sõngre, n na n deeg koe-noog a to,
48001007	wa Koe-nooga ya a yiibu; yaool n yaa neb bal n kẽ yãmb sʋka n baood n na n kẽes sãmbse y yamẽ, la b tedg Krista Koe-noogã.
48001008	Ade, tõnd meng bɩ malɛk sẽn yi yĩngri sã n saag n kõ yãmb koɛɛg sẽn ka tõnd sẽn zoe n wilg yãmb a soabã, bɩ Wẽnd yãk a soab barka!
48001009	Tõnd n yeele la rũnda menga tõnd n le togsde: ned ninga fãa sẽn saag-a n kõ yãmb koɛɛg sẽn ka yãmb sẽn zoe n paam a soabã, bɩ Wẽnd yãk a soab barka!
48001010	Togs sɩd sãn beẽ, yaa ninsaal yõod bɩ yaa Wẽnd dẽnna la mam baood marsã? Yaa ninsaal yamleoog la m tũuda? M sã n ket n baood n na n noog ninsaalb sũuri m ka le tõe n yɩ Krista sõgen ye.
48001011	Bãng-y, m saam-biisi, tɩ m sẽn kõ yãmb Koe-noog ningã ka tek ninsaal bãngra zulum sẽn tekẽ ye.
48001012	Ka ninsaal nengẽ la m deeg-a, ka ninsaal nengẽ la m zãms-a ye, ya a Zezi Krista meng n wilg-a maam.
48001013	Mam miime tɩ yãmb bãnga m vɩɩma sẽn yɩ a soab Zʋɩf rãmba sʋka, m sẽn waa n namsd Wẽnd Tigengu ne m pãng fãa, la m da sãamd-a sãang wẽnga,
48001014	y wʋma m sẽn da tũud m yaab rãmb sorã ne sũur ningã al tɩ sã n ya zĩ kãng bɩ m lʋɩt m dogd-n-taasa fãa taoore.
48001015	Ned ninga sẽn welga maam toor tɩ m nan ket m ma pʋgẽ la a bool-m ne a raabo,
48001016	yẽ soab n wilg maam b Biiga, n yet tɩ m wilg-a bu-zẽmbã. M ka le yaas n sok m doagdb la m buudu,
48001017	m ka kẽng Zerizalɛɛm n babs sẽn deng-b maam n ya Soaala Tʋʋm-tʋmdbã, ayoo! Yaa Arabi la m tees yã, n le lɛɛg n wa Damas.
48001018	Yʋʋm a tãab dẽ poor marsã la m kẽng Zerizalɛɛm n tɩ ges a Kefas la m zĩnda ne-a dasem piig la a nu;
48001019	m pa yãend Tʋʋm-tʋmdb a taaba sã n ka Krista saam-biig a Zak ye.
48001020	M wẽend ne Wẽnd tɩ m sẽn gʋls y woto wã, m ka yagd ziri ye.
48001021	Dẽ poor la m kẽng Siri la Silisi,
48001022	la rẽ tɩ Zɩɩde Tigenga kamb ra ka mi-m ye;
48001023	b ra wʋmdame bal tɩ b gomd tɩ bãmb pĩnd bɛyã yikame marsã n moond tẽeb ning yẽ meng sẽn da rat n sãama,
48001024	la b ra pẽgda Wẽnd m poorẽ.
48002001	Yʋʋm piig la a naas dẽ poore, mam le rʋʋ Zerizalɛɛm ne a Barnabe la m tũud-n-taag a Tit.
48002002	Tũu ne Wẽnd wilgri, la m sẽn wa be wã, m togs-b la Koe-noog ning m sẽn moond bu-zẽmbã – la yɩɩ maam ne kãsem-dãmba bala n zĩnd ne taaba – tɩ m zoe rabeem m tʋʋmda na n wa ka tũ sore.
48002003	M da tara tũud-n-taag sẽn ya Grɛk, a Tit, la b ka modg-a t'a kẽ bãong ye.
48002004	Neb kẽer bala n belg tɩ b yaa d saam-biisi n soos n kẽ sʋka n na n bãng tõnd sẽn lood d wĩ niyns n na n tũ Krista; bãmb dãmba ra baood n na n kẽes-d la b yembdo.
48002005	Tõnd pa sak n tũ b raabo, ba vugr menga, zoe-nif yĩng ye, tɩ d tʋlg n taasa yãmb Koe-noogã ne a sɩda zãnga.
48002006	Sã n kella sẽn mamsd-b mens ne nin-bɛdã – b sẽn yaa a soab taki dẽ ka pak m ye, tɩ Wẽnd ka welgd ninsaal ne a to ye – bãmb me pa yãend sãoog sẽn na n lek m Koe-nooga pʋgẽ ye.
48002007	B bãngame menga tɩ yaa Wẽnd n yãk maam tɩ m moon Koe-nooga nin-zẽmbã wala b sẽn yãk a Piyɛr Zʋɩf rãmb yĩnga.
48002008	Sẽn kõ-a a Piyɛr tõog Zʋɩf rãmba yĩngã, yẽ soab bala n kõ-m tõog kãnga bu-zẽmba yĩnga.
48002009	Sẽn waa n lebg vẽeneg ne-ba, tɩ Wẽnd bark la m paam yã, a Zak, a Kefas la a Zã, kãsem-dãmba la tẽn-kuga, bãmb me tuda b nug n maan zood ne maam la a Barnabe, la b wilg-d lame tɩ bãmb n na n ges Zʋɩf rãmba yelle tɩ tõnd ges bu-zẽmbã yelle.
48002010	D da tog n tẽega naong rãmba yelle; la rẽ me la m maan ne m sũur fãa.
48002011	A Kefas waa n pɩʋʋga Antiyos la m sãbsa a manesem neba fãa taoore, la yẽ n da kong bʋʋm.
48002012	Sɩd me, a Zak tũud-n-taasa sẽn waa n nan ka pooge, a Kefas ra rɩta ne bu-zẽmba. Bãmb waoonga poore, la a sẽn soos n leb kɛɛnga, sẽn kẽ-b bãonga rabeem yĩnga.
48002013	Zʋɩf rãmb a taaba me togs-a lame, al t'a Barnabe meng naag-ba n solge.
48002014	M sẽn mik tɩ b pa tũud sɩd sor ning Koe-nooga sẽn wa ne a soabã, m yeela a Kefas, neba fãa taoore: «Fo yaa Zʋɩf, n sak n bas Zʋɩf rãmba dog-n-mik n vɩ wala bu-zẽna, bõe tɩ fo rat n modg bu-zẽmbã tɩ b vɩɩnd wa Zʋɩf rãmba?»
48002015	Sã n ya tõndo, d doga Zʋɩf rãmb buudẽ, woto d ka kĩ ne bu-zẽmba sẽn ya yel-wẽn-maandba ye;
48002016	la baasgo d miime tɩ ninsaal pa teeg noya reegre n na n paam a yell manegr ne Wẽnd ye; ya a Zezi Krista tẽeb n wat ne rẽ. Yaa rẽ la tõnd me tẽ Krista, a Zezi, n na n paam d yell manegre, d pa teeg noya reegre, tɩ ned pa paamd a yell manegre ne noya reegr ye.
48002017	Dɩlla sã n ya Krista nengẽ la tõnd baood sõmblem la d ket n zĩ ne d yel-wẽna wala neb a taaba, Krista tʋʋmd ka lebg yel-wẽnd yaoogr marsã, la rẽ na yɩ sɩda?
48002018	Wala m sã n le maneg n me mam sẽn tus n lubi, ka maam n kõ kaset marsã tɩ m tus-n-lubã n yɩ wẽnga la m le lɛɛg n metẽ.
48002019	Sã n ya noora poorẽ, m lebga bõn-kɩɩng a yĩnga, sẽn na n yɩlẽ n tõog n vɩɩnd Wẽnd yĩnga. M naaga Krista n ka pika zugu.
48002020	Pa le ya mam meng n vɩ ye, yaa Krista n vɩ mam pʋgẽ, m sã n vɩ ne m yĩnga marsã, m tɛk yaa m tẽ Wẽnnaam Biiga sẽn nong maam, n dɩk b meng n kõ maama.
48002021	M pa kɩtd tɩ Wẽnd kũuna lebg zaalem ye; la sã n ya ne noor deegr la yell manegda, dɩlla Krista ki zaalem yĩnga.
48003001	Galat rãmb sẽn ka tar yam, ãnd n lebg y zutu. B wilga yãmb neere, Krista sẽn lebg bũmb ning pika zugu.
48003002	Sokr bala a ye la m na n sok yãmba: Yaa yãmb sẽn sak noora yĩng la y paam Wẽnd Vʋʋsem, bɩ yaa y sẽn tẽ Koe-nooga?
48003003	Yama paoog-y la sẽn ta woto fãa tɩ yãmb sɩng ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsem n na n baas ne y toorẽ pãnga?
48003004	Na n yɩɩ zaalem yĩng la y reeg kũuna woto fãa? Ad-y rẽ fãa na n sɩd yɩɩ zaalem bala!
48003005	Sẽn kõt-a yãmb a Vʋʋsem Sõng la a tʋmd tʋʋm bãna yãmb sʋka, a maanda rẽ y sẽn sakd noora yĩnga, bɩ yaa y sẽn deeg Koe-noogã?
48003006	Y mi t'a Abraam tẽe Wẽnde tɩ Wẽnd maaneg a yelle.
48003007	Bɩ y bãng tɩ neb niyns sẽn teeg-b tẽeb, yaa bãmb la a Abraam kamba.
48003008	Sebr sõng sẽn pĩnd n mi tɩ Wẽnd na n tũu tẽeb n fãag bu-zẽmbã, b pĩnd n togsa a Abraam kiba-noog kãngã: «Yaa fo maasmẽ la Adem biis na n paam barka.»
48003009	Dẽ n kɩt tɩ neb niyns fãa sẽn teeg-b tẽebo na n tũu tẽeba ba, a Abraam, n paam barka.
48003010	Neb niyns fãa sẽn yet-b tɩ yaa Noora bal la b tũuda, yaa kãab wẽng la b kãab bãmba, tɩ b gʋlsa woto: «Wẽnd na sãam ned ning fãa sẽn ka modga n deeg la a tũ sẽn gʋls fãa sebr sõng pʋgẽ.»
48003011	– Ad-y yaa vẽenega tɩ noora tũudem ka tõe n maneg ned yelle tɩ nin-sõng teeg-a a tẽebo n na n vɩɩnde.
48003012	Ka tẽebẽ wã la Noora yit ye la paka ninsaal t'a reeg sẽn be a pʋgẽ wã fãa n yaool n paam vɩɩm.
48003013	Krista sakame tɩ Noora kãab wẽnga leb bãmba, n kõ-d tɩlgre. Bãmb meng sak n yɩɩ ka bark soaba d fãa yĩnga; tɩ b gʋlsa woto: «Ka bark soab la sẽn yagla pika.»
48003014	La yɩɩ woto la a Abraam kãab nooga leb bu-zẽmbã; d sẽn paam tẽebã, d paama b sẽn da kãab tõnd a soabã: a Vʋʋsem Sõngo.
48003015	M saam-biisi, m na n kõ-y la ninsaal makre: Raboog welgr sebr sã n gʋls n sɛ, b pa le tõe n yẽes bũmb ye, b pa le tõe n paas bũmb ye, ba gʋlsga sẽn yaa ninsaal n gʋlsã.
48003016	Ad-y yaa Abraam ne a buudu la kãabga kãab yã. Sebr sõng pa yeel: a Abraam ne a buud kamb ye, wala yaa kʋʋng yell la b da rat n gom ye; goma nin-yend yelle, buuda nin-yende: Krista.
48003017	M sẽn dat n wilg-y bũmb ninga la woto: Wẽnd da yalsa kãabga yɛl fãa b zĩigẽ, woto noora sẽn wa yʋʋm kobs-naas la pistã kãabga poore, a ka tõe n woog a pãnga t'a lebg fãoog ye.
48003018	Sã n tũuda ne raboog welgr noy la ku-biig dɩt faado, yaa noor la tũuda, pa tũud kãabga ye. Mik a Abraam barka ka yi zĩig a to tɩ ka Wẽnd kãabga pʋgẽ ye.
48003019	Noora bee bõe yĩnga? A wa n paasame bala n na n wilg tɩ ninsaal mii kɩɩsgo. Noora ra kõome n gũud a Abraam yagenga waoongo tɩ yaa yẽnda la kãabga kãabyã. Noora yalsa ne malɛk rãmb toagsg la ne nin-yend sẽn lʋɩ sʋka.
48003020	Sã n ya kãabgã, Wẽnd yɩla b ye n kãabe, ned a to ka lʋɩ sʋk ye.
48003021	Noya sãama Wẽnnaam kãabg bɩ bõe? Abada! Tõnd sã n da paamẽ la noor sẽn tõe n kõ vɩɩm la d tõogdẽ n yeel tɩ noor deegr n wat ne manegre.
48003022	Sebr sõng paalga bũmba fãa yel-wẽnd soolmẽ, sẽn na yɩlẽ t'a Zezi Krista tẽedbã dɩ kãabga yõodo.
48003023	Tẽeb sẽn da waa n kaẽ, yaa wa b da rɩka tõnd n gũnug ne noya n gẽegd tẽebã waoongo.
48003024	Dẽ la Noor yɩ karen-saamba n tãag Krista sẽn waa n kɩt tɩ tẽeba wa ne yell manegrã.
48003025	La tẽeb sẽn wa, tõnd ka le baood karen-saamb yɛs ye.
48003026	Yãmb fãa sẽn kẽ Krista a Zezi wã, y lebga Wẽnnaam kamba.
48003027	Yãmb fãa sɩd tũu Krista n so soobo la y yeelg bãmb wa fuugu.
48003028	Tɩ m yaa Zʋɩf bɩ Grɛk, yamba bɩ burkĩna, pag bɩ raoa: rẽ ka le be ye; yãmb fãa lebga bũmb a ye a Zezi Krista pʋgẽ.
48003029	Y sẽn tabend Krista bala, yãmb lebga a Abraam yagense, yãmb bal n so kãabgã.
48004001	M gomda võor la woto: ku-bi-kẽeng sã n ket n ya yãaga, ad-y ne a sẽn so a ba laoga fãa, bũmb ka welg-a nanda ne yamb ye.
48004002	A tara gũuda la koagenda, n tãag a ba sẽn yals wakat ningã.
48004003	Tõnd me, d sẽn da waa n ya yãase d da yaa yem-daado, zamaana pãn-dãmba yem-daado.
48004004	La wakat sẽn waa n ta, Wẽnd tʋma b Biiga sẽn yɩ pag biiga la noora rɛɛgda,
48004005	sẽn na n yɩlẽ n tõog n fãag noora yemse, la a kɩt tɩ d lebg Wẽnd kom-wubdsi.
48004006	La kaset ning y sẽn tare n mi tɩ y lebga Wẽnd kamba, yaa Wẽnd sẽn ning yãmb sũurẽ bãmb Biiga Vʋʋsem sẽn tãsde: Aba! (M Ba!)
48004007	Woto fo ka le ya yem-daoog ye, f yaa zak biiga, la f sẽn lebg Wẽnd biiga, f lebga Wẽnd yõod dɩta.
48004008	Pĩnda, y sẽn waa n nan ka mi Wẽnnaama, yaa bõn-yaals sẽn ka wẽnde la yãmb da nok yã wala y wẽnde.
48004009	Marsã, yãmb sẽn bãng-ba, yɩɩd rẽ, bãmb sẽn bãng yãmbã, yãmb na n maana a wãn n leb y bõn-yaalsa nengẽ n tɩ soond bãmb wala pĩndã?
48004010	Yãmb ket n sõta dasma, kiisi, zĩ likri ne yʋʋma!
48004011	Ad-y y maandame tɩ m zoet-m na n wa nams zaalem bal y yĩnga.
48004012	M saam-biisi, m yõkda y sɛɛga, modg-y n wẽneg maam tɩ m maoome n na n wẽneg yãmba. Da tẽ-y tɩ y beeg-m lame ye.
48004013	Y mi tɩ bãag n wa ne m ka tɩ m paam n sɩng Koe-nooga mooneg y sʋka.
48004014	La ne m bãaga sẽn kɩt tɩ m lebg y zɩɩbo, y pa paoog-m ye, y pa sãbs-m ye; y kell n deega maam wala Wẽnd malɛka, wala Krista a Zezi menga.
48004015	Yãmb zoe n yĩma y sẽn da kilsd maam ne sũ-noog ninga laa? M meng tõe n kõo kaseto tɩ wakat kãnga, y sã n da tõee lame, y na kɩɩdẽ y nin-bɛɛl n kõ-ma.
48004016	La marsã m sẽn togs yãmb sɩda la m lebg y bɛya?
48004017	Neb kẽer zooda ne yãmb ka segd ye. B ratame bal n welg yãmb ne maam tɩ yãmb tabend bãmba.
48004018	Tʋlg-y neer maanego tɩ yaa sõmbo, la togame tɩ yɩ daar fãa, la ra yɩ m sẽn pẽ yãmba wakat bal ye.
48004019	M kom-bõonego, m sẽn le rogd ne waasgo, ad-y na n kell n yɩɩ boto n tãag y sẽn wat n dɩk Krista wẽnego.
48004020	M da paam n pẽẽ yãmba m na modgẽ tɩ d wʋm taaba tɩ marsã wã m ka mi m sẽn na m gom to-to ne y ye.
48004021	Aya! Yãmb sẽn yet tɩ y yaa Noora tũudbã, y tẽra sẽn togs noora sebrẽ bɩ?
48004022	Ad-y gʋlsame t'a Abraam doga kamb a yiibu: a ye yaa yem-poak biiga t'a to wã ya tom pag biiga.
48004023	Pʋg rɩkra biig doga wa kamb a taaba; tom paga biig rogma tũu ne kãabgo.
48004024	Ad-y yaa yelbũndi: pagb a yiiba makda zood buud a yiibu. Pipi zooda yõga Sinayi tãng zugu; zood kãng kamb yaa yem-daado, la b ma la a Agar.
48004025	(Sinayi tãnga bee Arabi soolmẽ) Yẽ makda dũnna Zerizalɛɛma, yẽ me yaa yem-poaka la a kamba me yaa yemse.
48004026	Zerizalɛɛm a to wã, sẽn yita Wẽnnaam nengẽ soaba, yẽ la tom paga la yẽ la tõnd ma.
48004027	Yaa woto la b gʋlsyã: «Bɩ f kɩdem, pʋg-kiiri sẽn pa rogde, kils sõmbo la f lang ne sũ-noogo fo sẽn zɩ n bãng rogem toogo; ad pʋg-beooga kamba sõor yɩɩda rʋmda rẽnna.»
48004028	M saam-biisi, bɩ y baad tɩ yãmb la zooda kamba wala a Izaak.
48004029	Biig ninga sẽn doga wa kamb a taabã da namsda biig ning rogem sẽn tũ ne kãabgã. Boto me n ket n maand marsã.
48004030	Yaa bõe la Sebr sõng togsda? «Bɩ f rig yem-poaka ne a biigã tɩ yem-poaka biig ka tog n naag tom paga biiga, a ba raboogẽ ye.»
48004031	Bɩ d bãnge, m saam-biisi, tɩ tõnd ka yem-poaka kamba, d yaa tom paga kamba.
48005001	Krista fãaga tõnd tɩ d kell n vɩɩnd ne d burkĩndlem; dɩlla bɩ d da bas raood ye la d da leb d pĩnd yemdẽ ye.
48005002	Maam a Pol n togsede: ad-y yãmb sã n sak bãong kẽesgo, Krista lebga zaalem yãmb yĩnga.
48005003	Maam n le togsde: ned ninga fãa sẽn sak-a bãong kõom, lebga modgr ne yẽ soab ta tũ noya fãa gill kɛpi!
48005004	Yãmb sẽn baood y yell manegr ne noor deegre, bãng-y tɩ yãmb welga ne Krista, la y konga b bark zãnga.
48005005	Sã n ya tõndo, yaa Wẽnd Vʋʋsem n kɩt tɩ d gũud tɩ tẽeb wa ne kũun niyns d sẽn saagde, d yella sẽn manegã.
48005006	Sɩd me, a Zezi Krista nengẽ ka be m kẽe bãong bɩ m ka kẽ bãong ye, yaa tẽeba bal n pake: tẽeb sẽn tʋmd nonglem tʋʋma.
48005007	Yãmb wudgra da paam n sɩnga neere, bõe n woogd y tĩiga marsã sɩda reegre pʋgẽ?
48005008	Gɛɛlg a woto pa yit sẽn boond-a yãmba nengẽ ye.
48005009	Rabɩll bilf bala n wukd zom nagdem.
48005010	Mam yẽ tẽedame tɩ yãmb sã n be ne Soaala, yãmb kõn tags bũmb a to ye, la ned ninga sẽn na n kɩt tɩ y maan sãmb-sãmbe, yẽ soab kõn põs Wẽnd bʋʋd ye, a sẽn ya a soab fãa.
48005011	Sã n ya maam, m saam-biisi, n ket n wɩngd-y tɩ y kẽ bãongo, bõe yĩng la b namsd-m yɛsa? Pika ne a pɛlen-yɩkã ka sɛ?
48005012	Sẽn kẽesd-b yãmb rabeema kõn fiuus b yĩnga wils fãa gilli!
48005013	Sã n ya yãmba, m saam-biisi ad-y b ratame tɩ y yɩ burkĩmbi, gũus-y bala tɩ y burkĩndlema da wa lebg yĩnga maan a sẽn dat ye. Y burkĩndlema waa ne to nonglem, n kɩt tɩ ned kam fãa sõngd a to.
48005014	Noya fãa pidsa noor a ye pʋgẽ: «Nong f to n wẽnd f menga.»
48005015	Yãmb sã n yĩid taab marsã la y wãbd taab wa baase, bɩ y gũus tɩ yaa y wãab n sɩnge.
48005016	Bɩ y sak tɩ Wẽnd Vʋʋsem gãd yãmba tɩ y na bas y yĩnga raaba pʋgbo.
48005017	Yãmb mi tɩ yĩnga maanda sũ-kiir ne Wẽnd Vʋʋsem tɩ Wẽnd Vʋʋsem me maand boto ne yĩngã; bãmb b yiiba zabda taaba; ya rẽ yĩng la yãmb pa tõe n tʋm y yam ye.
48005018	Sã n ya Wẽnd Vʋʋsem n kẽ yãmba, yãmb pa le tar noor tʋʋmd ye.
48005019	Yĩnga sẽn womd biis niynsã, y mi-b-la fãa: ad pagb yõgbo, yoobo, rataado,
48005020	wẽn-yaals pʋgbo, tɩt rɩɩbo, kisgu, mo-beedo, sũ-kiiri, sũ-puuri, zaba, zems-taab-kaalem, welegre,
48005021	to paoong tʋlsem, rɩt-n-pa yɛɛdẽ, yũud-n-pa-roogdẽ la yɛl a taab sẽn wẽnd rẽ – la m togsdame wa m sẽn zoe n togsã tɩ yel-maandb a woto buud ka paamd Wẽnd Rĩunga pʋɩɩr ye.
48005022	Ad Vʋʋsem sõng sẽn womd biis niynsi: to nonglem, sũ-noogo, laafi, sũ-tõogo, taab sõngre, kõt yaare, taab teegre,
48005023	sũ-bʋgsem, tõog-m-menga. Noor ka be n gɩdg bõn-sõma a woto ye.
48005024	Neb niyns fãa sẽn lebg-b Krista a Zezi soolem, bãmb dãmb rɩka b zʋg wẽngã n ka pik zugu ne a tʋls wẽnsa fãa.
48005025	A Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn ya tõnd vɩɩma, bɩ b sõng d me tɩ d tʋm.
48005026	D da bao yʋ-yaals ne wags taab ye, la d da maan sũ-ki-yaals ye.
48006001	M saam-biisi, yãmb sʋka nin-yend sã n tudgi, y sẽn tũud Wẽnd Vʋʋsma, bɩ y maag y yĩng n sõng-a. Fo meng maan gũusgu tɩ kʋɩɩbg tõeeme n wa lub foom me.
48006002	Sõng-y taab n zɩ y vɩɩma zu-loeese tɩ woto la y na n deeg Krista noore.
48006003	Ned sã n tẽed t'a yaa bũmbu, mik a ka fɩ, yẽ soab belgda a menga.
48006004	Ned kam fãa ges a sẽn vɩ to-to, a ges a tʋʋma n bao a zu-zẽkre be, a ra zẽka meng ne a taab tʋʋm ye.
48006005	Ad-y ned kam fãa tog n tʋka a zɩɩbo.
48006006	Bɩ karen-biig modg n sõng sẽn zãmsa yẽ karengã ne a paoong fãa.
48006007	Da belg-y y mens ye; ad-y ned ka laad Wẽnd ye. Ninsaal sẽn bʋd bũmb ning la a tigsda.
48006008	F sã n bʋd sẽn tog ne yĩngã, yaa yĩnga põosgo la f na n tigsi. Fo sã n bʋd sẽn tog ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo, yaa vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ la f tigsda.
48006009	Wa-y tɩ d da bas raood ne neer baoob ye, tɩ tigsg na n wala a wakato, tõnd sã n kell n maan daoodo.
48006010	Dẽnd yĩnga, d sẽn tõe wakat ning fãa, bɩ d maan neer ne neba fãa gilli, bũmb zãnga ne d saam-biisã, sẽn tar d tẽebã.
48006011	Ges-y bẽes bɛd niyns m nuga sẽn bẽes yãmb yĩnga.
