55004021	Ning pãng n wa tɩ waooda nan ka sɩng ye. A Ewubul tɩ m pʋʋs-fo, n paas a Pudẽns, a Lẽ, a Klodiya la d saam-biisa fãa.
55004022	Soaala zĩnd ne fo! Wẽnd bark sig yãmb fãa!
56001001	Maam a Pol n pʋʋsde. M yaa Wẽnd sõgne; m kẽe a Zezi Krista tʋʋmde n na n sõng tɩ Wẽnd sẽn welg b rãmb toorã paam tẽebo. B paam n bãng sɩda n lebg wẽn-pẽgdba.
56001002	B paam vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ saagre me. Vɩɩm kãng la Wẽnd sẽn ka mi zirẽ-beeda ra kãab tõnd al tɩ dũni nan ka naan ye.
56001003	B wakata sẽn ta, b pidsa b kãabgã ne b Koe-nooga moonego la maam la b kõ noor tɩ m maan tʋʋm-kãnga.
56001004	Dɩlla yaa maam a Pol n pʋʋsd a Tit, m bi-roak meng d fãa tẽeba pʋgẽ. Bɩ Wẽnd Ba nimbãan-zoeere la b laafi tũ Krista a Zezi, tõnd Fãagdã, n sig f zugu!
56001005	Mam sã n bas foo Krɛt tẽnga yaa sẽn na n yɩla tɩ f yõdg n sigl Tigenga n baase la f ning kãsem-dãmb tẽng-tẽnga wa m sẽn wilgi.
56001006	Kãsem-dãmba togame n yɩ neb sẽn ka tar yell b zugu; sã n ya kãadma, b kẽe-a la vugr bala la b kamb yaa tẽedba; b pa tõe n dõd-b ne wẽng ye, la b mii sakre.
56001007	A sẽn ya Wẽnd zag-gũuda, kãsem-soab tog n yɩɩ nin-tɩrga; a ka mi porbo, a ka mi zẽk-m-menga, a ka mi sũ-puuri, a ka rã-yũuda, a ka baood zaba, a ka baood arzɛk ne zãmb ye.
56001008	A mii gãag-sobendo, a nong n maana neere, a ka mi pir-pir ye, a mii zemsgo, a yaa wẽn-pʋʋsa, a tõe-la a menga.
56001009	A modgdame tɩ bũmb ra keoos a zãmsga pʋgẽ ye, a zãmsga tũudame. A tog n tõogame n sagl sagl tɩrse, n tõog n ning kɩɩsdba yãnde.
56001010	Neb wʋsg n be, la bãnkomsa sʋk la b be n yɩɩda, n ya tõatba, gom-faad-dãmba, la no-noom-dãmba.
56001011	Da bas-b tɩ b gom ye. Yaa neb sẽn wãad b taab roto, n togsd sẽn pa sõmbe n na n paam n dɩ bala.
56001012	Woto la b bãngd meng a ye togsd b poorẽ: «Krɛt tẽng rãmba, zirẽ-be-neb wakat buud fãa, ninsaan-yoodo, dɩt-n-pa-tʋmnẽ-dãmba.»
56001013	B bãngda toagsg yaa sɩda. Dẽnd yĩnga, togs-y bãmb vẽenega tɩ b ra bʋdg n bas tẽeb sɩdã.
56001014	B lak n bas Zʋɩf rãmba ne b soalma, n lak n bas sẽn wẽnemd-b kãar n tees sɩdã.
56001015	F ya pʋ-peen-neda, f yɛla fãa tũuda pʋ-peelem sore; f sã n ya nin-dẽgdo la f pa tar tẽebo, bõn-sõng me kõn zĩnd f yĩng ye. B yama la b pʋga zãng sobame.
56001016	B yetame tɩ b yaa neb sẽn mi Wẽnde, la bãmb meng n lɛɛg n kɩɩsd-b ne b vɩɩm: ad-y b yaa nin-yoodo, tõatba, neb sẽn ka tõe n maan bõn-sõng ba bilfu.
56002001	Sã n ya foo, modg tɩ f zãmsg tũ Zãms-sõngã.
56002002	Bɩ nin-kẽemba yɩ neb sẽn tõe b mense, neb sẽn tog ne pẽgre, maag-m-meng rãmba, n tar tẽeb sẽn kɩ yẽgna, n nong b taaba, n ka yɛɛd ne neer pʋgb ye.
56002003	Pʋg-yãansa me boto. B manesem yɩ pʋg-sõma manesem, b ra wɩd b taab ye, b ra yɩ rã-yũudba, b yɩ sagl-sõng rãmba.
56002004	Woto la b tõogd n zãms pʋg-bõonegã tɩ b nong b sɩdb rãmba la b kamba,
56002005	n vẽ ne yaare, ne yoodem, n mi b zak tallgo, n ka mi gãgs ye la b reegd b sɩdb rãmb noy; woto Wẽnnaam gomda kõn paam sãbsgo ned ba a ye nengẽ ye.
56002006	Sagl kom-bɩɩba neere tɩ b gũus ne yirgu buud fãa.
56002007	Fo meng nengẽ la b na n yãend vɩɩm sõng sor n dɩke, tɩ f zãmsg tũuda sɩda, tɩ f waoogda f menga,
56002008	tɩ f gomda ne gũusgu, tɩ bũmb ka keoosd f vɩɩmẽ ye; yaa woto la bɛɛba zĩ ne yãnde, n ka tõe n gom beed f poorẽ ye.
56002009	Bɩ yemsa sak b zu-soaben-dãmb bũmb fãa pʋgẽ. B bao n noog b sũuri, b ra kɩɩs b gomd ye.
56002010	B ra soos n zãmb-b ye, bũmb da woog b nonglem ne b ye. Woto b na yɩ neb niyns sẽn deegd Wẽnnaam d Fãagda gomdã.
56002011	Wẽnd nimbãan-zoeerã sẽn fãagd Adem biisa fãa puka zãnga.
56002012	A kɩtame tɩ d bãng tɩ d tog n basa bũmb ning fãa sẽn ka wat ne Wẽnd waoogre, n bas zamaana tʋls wẽnsã, n vɩɩnd marsã ne gũusgu, ne sõmblem, ne Wẽnd pẽgre.
56002013	D tog n gũu ne saagre, zu-noog wakat ninga d Wẽnnaam la d Fãagd a Zezi Krista, sẽn na n sig ne b pãng la ziiri.
56002014	Yaa bãmb n kõ b meng n fãag-do, n kɩt tɩ d tɩlg ne wẽng buud fãa, la b segl buud sõng n kõ b menga, buud sẽn wɩsg a menga n baood neere.
56002015	Yaa woto la f tog n gome, n sagle, n togs sɩda wa f sẽn tõe fãa. Bɩ ned da sãbs-f ye.
56003001	Tẽeg b fãa gilli tɩ b togame n sak tẽnga taoor dãmba la kãsem-dãmba, n deeg b goama, n sak n tʋm tʋʋmd sõng buud fãa.
56003002	B ra beeg ned ye, b bas zaba, b yɩ neb sẽn baood n na n noog b taab sũuri, b bʋk b sũuri ne neb fãa.
56003003	Ade, pĩnda tõnd me yɩɩ yalemse, kɩɩsdba; tõnd me ra bʋdgame; tʋls yood la sũ-nood yood n da balg tõndo tɩ d da vɩ ne yam wẽnga, ne sũ-kiiri, ne taab sãbsgo la taab kisgu.
56003004	Wakat n puki, yaa Wẽnnaam d Fãagda wakato, yaa b sũ-bʋgsem la b nimbãan-zoeer ne ninsaalb wakato.
56003005	B ka ges tʋʋm-sõma niyns d sẽn tʋma ye, yaa b nimbãan-zoeera bal n tus ba tɩ b na n fãag-do. Tũu ne koom soobo la rogem paalga ne a Vʋʋsem Sõngo pãnga.
56003006	B sudga tõnd Vʋʋsem kãnga n mabge, tõnd Fãagd a Zezi Krista pãng yĩnga.
56003007	Woto d sen paam tɩlgr ne bãmb kũuni, d na n tũu bãmb n dɩ Wẽnd yõodo, vɩɩm sẽn ka tar sɛɛb pʋgẽ.
56003008	Gomda yaa sɩd menga tɩ m dat wa fãa-fãa tɩ f bas sãmbse la f togs ne pãnga tɩ sẽn tẽed-b Wẽnda fãa wɩng ne neer maanego. Dẽ la sõmbo, dẽ n be yõod ninsaalb yĩnga.
56003009	Sã n kella vɛɛs yaalse, rogma sẽn tong zĩig ninga, Noora poorẽ zaba la no-koɛɛma, zoe-ba. B pa manegd fɩ, b pa wat ne yõod ye.
56003010	Ned sã n ya welgda, yãend-a tɩ ta naoor a yiibu, n wilg-a t'a maan gũusgu; dẽ poore lak ne ned a woto buudu.
56003011	Fo mi tɩ ned a woto buud bʋdga zãnga, n lebg yel-wẽn-maanda, n tʋk a meng taal a zugu.
56003012	M sã n wa tʋm f nengẽ a Artemas bɩ a Tisik, bãng tɩ f togame n wa bʋʋg-m Nikopolis tẽnga: yaa be la m na n zĩnd waooda wẽnde.
56003013	Pĩnd n ges bʋ-kaooda Zenas la a Apolos so-toaka yell neere, tɩ bũmb da wa paoog-b ye.
56003014	Tõnd neba me tog n wɩnga ne tʋʋm-sõma n paam n yiis b meng yell pakdem; b kõn zĩ woto tɩ b vɩɩm ka yõod ye.
56003015	Sẽn be-b ne maama fãa tɩ b pʋʋs-fo. Pʋʋs d saam-biisa sẽn nong-b tõnd, tẽeba pʋgẽ. Bɩ Wẽnd barka sig yãmb fãa!
57001001	Maam a Pol sẽn be roogẽ Krista yĩnga, ne m saam-biig a Timote n pʋʋsd d zoa la d sõangd a Filemo,
57001002	d tão sõnga Afia, d ba-biig la d tʋmd-n-taaga a Arkip la Tigenga kamb fãa sẽn segd taab a zakẽ.
57001003	Wẽnnaam d Ba la Soaala Zezi Krista sik y fãa zutu b bark la b laafi!
57001004	M tara Soaala bark pʋsgo f yĩnga la m tẽegda f yell m pʋʋsg pʋgẽ.
57001005	M wʋmdame tɩ b tar-f pẽgre. Yaa Krista a Zezi bɩ nin-sõma wã poorẽ, b pẽgda f nonglem la f tẽebo.
57001006	Wẽnd na kɩt tɩ f tẽeba yals foo sõng-taab-tʋʋmda zugu. Wẽnd na kɩt t'a vẽneg f yam zãnga tɩ f yãend bõn sõng ning fãa d sẽn tõe n maan Krista yĩnga.
57001007	La sɩda m paama sũ-noog kãsenga la m sũura gãandame, m sẽn wʋm f nonglma ne f taaba kibare; b yeel-m lame, m saam-biiga, tɩ f maasa nin-sõma wã sũuri.
57001008	Dẽ n so tɩ ne m sẽn tõe n soond Krista maasmẽ n gom-f vẽenega la m wilg-fu f sẽn tog n maane,
57001009	m baas n tʋlgame n lʋɩɩs nonglma taoore la m kos foom m kosgo. Sẽn na n goma wã, ya a Pol, yaa nin-kẽem a Pol, ya b sẽn balg a soab bãeens marsã, Krista a Zezi yĩngã.
57001010	M kosga yaa m biiga yĩnga, biig ning m sẽn dog m bãeensa roogẽ, t'a reeg yʋʋr a Be yõodo (Onezim).
57001011	Nin-kãng tʋʋmd ka naf-f pĩnd ye la marsã a na zĩnd yõodo, foo wala mam yĩnga.
57001012	M lebsd-a la f nengẽ la ad-a lebga m sũur neda.
57001013	M da nongẽ lame t'a pa m sɛɛgẽ n tʋm fo ziigẽ, m bãeensa roogẽ, tɩ f mi tɩ Koe-nooga yĩnga b balg-m lame.
57001014	La ad-m pa tʋlg n maan fɩ tɩ f zɩ tiir ye, tɩ m pa rat tɩ yel-sõmda tũ ne moadg ye; m datame t'a yɩ yamleoog bũmbu.
57001015	Tõeeme marsã t'a Onezim sẽn da zãag ne foom bilfr bala bɩ a lebg f soolem yʋʋm tõt sɛɛbo.
57001016	La kõn le yɩ wala f yem-daoog ye, a lebga f babi-nongre. A sẽn lebg mam bi-nongr mengã, zamaana rãmb nifẽ, wa Krista nifẽ, fo nengẽ wã na yɩɩg boto.
57001017	Bɩ f ges bũmb ning sẽn be tõnd d yiiba sʋka la f reeg-a wa mam menga.
57001018	Tõe t'a ra beeg-f lame bɩ a ra looga ne f bũmbu, bɩ f bas tɩ rẽ paka maam marsã.
57001019	Maam a Pol meng n lʋɩɩsd m toogo, n gʋlsd-f woto ne m nugu: maam n na n yao. La rẽ yaa m sẽn pa rat n gom samd ning f sẽn tog n yao-ma; yaa fo menga la f tog n dɩk n yao maam.
57001020	M saam-biiga, Soaala yĩng bɩ f ra zãgs m kosg ye; maag m sũur Krista yĩnga.
57001021	M gʋlsd-f la ne saagr kãsenga tɩ f mii noor deegre; m tara kaset meng tɩ f tõe n kõome tɩ yɩɩd m sẽn kot fooma.
57001022	M sẽn paasd yaa f segl m gãag roogo, tɩ ne yãmb pʋʋsgo, m na n leba y nengẽ.
57001023	A Epafras tɩ m pʋʋs-fo: m sẽn kẽ roog Krista a Zezi yĩngã, yẽ la m sõsd-n-taaga.
57001024	Sẽn sõngd-b maama tɩ m pʋʋs-fo: a Mark, a Aristark, a Demas ne a Luk.
57001025	Soaala a Zezi Krista bark zĩnd ne-fo!
58001001	Pĩnda Wẽnnaam yãka bãngdba n gom ne tõnd yaab rãmbã naoor yaka la ne goam buud toɛ-toɛ yã,
58001002	dũnna-rũnna, yaoolem wakatã, yaa ne bãmb Biiga la b gom ne tõndo. Yaa Bi-kãng la b yãkre t'a yaa b yõod dɩta la yaa ne yẽ pãng la yʋʋma tong taaba n ka tõe n sõde.
58001003	Bi-kãng n waa n puk b ziirã tɩ nin-kãng yaa b menga wẽnego, la b zãada dũnia ne b Gomda pãnga. Bãmb n yẽes yel-wẽnd buud fãa, n dʋ yĩngri n zʋʋg saaga, n tɩ zĩ Wẽnd sẽn pid ne ziira rɩtgo.
58001004	B zʋʋga malɛgsa fãa tɩ malɛgsa ka paam yʋʋr sẽn tõe n mak ne yʋʋr ning b sẽn pʋd bãmba ye.
58001005	Yaa malɛk bʋgo la Wẽnnaam tõog n yeele: «Fo yaa mam Biiga; maam n dog-f rũnna bala?» La ad-b sẽn le paase: «Mam na n yɩla a Ba, t'a yɩ m Biiga.»
58001006	B sẽn wa n dɩk b Bi-kẽengã n na n kõ dũnia, b yeelame yɛsa: «Bɩ Wẽnd malɛgsa wõgemd b taoore!»
58001007	Sã n yaool n ya ne malɛgsa la b gomda, b yeta woto: B kɩtame tɩ b malɛgsã wẽnd sobgo, n kɩt tɩ b sõgen-kamba wẽnd bugum sẽn tʋʋl ne rɩɩbo.
58001008	Sã n ya ne b Biigã b gomda woto: «Wẽnde, yãmb naama zaoor kõn vik abada; bɩ b yetame: y naama rasaar yaa zemsg-na-zĩnd dasaare.
58001009	Y nonga sõmblem, n zãgs Wẽnd paoogre, yaa rẽ yĩnga la Wẽnnaam y Wẽndã, welg-y toore n bao yũ-noog kaam n zɛyã.»
58001010	B yetame yɛsa: «Sɩngrẽ wã yaa yãmba, Soaala, n lugl tẽngã la y nug n yɛdg saagã.
58001011	La rẽ fãa na n loogame n menem, yãmb bala n na n kelle tɩ sẽn keta na n kʋdg wa fuugu.
58001012	Sẽn ketã na n kʋʋ n dɩgla wala fu-yorgo, n kʋ wala peende la b na n teemame. Yãmb bal n ka na n teem abada, y yʋʋm kõn ta b tɛk abada.»
58001013	Yaa malɛk a bõe la b tõog n yeele: «Zĩnd m dɩtgo tɩ m wa gãneg f bɛɛba f taoore tɩ f tab-b n zĩẽ?»
58001014	D sok n gese, b fãa ka yam dãmb sẽn deeg sõgen-kamb tʋʋmd bal laa? Ka sẽn na n paam-b fãagra yĩng la b tʋmd laa?
58002001	Woto wã d tog n gãdame la d maand gũsgu ne zãmsg ning tõnd sẽn wʋma n da wa kẽ tudgr pʋgẽ ye.
58002002	Malɛgsa sẽn deeg gomd ning n wilgã sã n ya gom-sɩdem al t'a kɩɩsgo bɩ a tõdgr paamd sɩbgr sẽn tog ne-a,
58002003	tõnd maanda a wãn marsã n põse d sã n ka kelg neere koɛɛg ninga sẽn wata ne fãagr mengã? Fãagr kãng la Soaala waa n moone, tɩ sẽn wʋm-ba fãa wa ne b kaseto.
58002004	Wẽnnaam naaga b kasetã ne yel-bãna la tʋʋm bãna, ne wẽnd makr buud toɛ-toɛ yã. A Vʋʋsem Sõng me waa ne vẽnegr kũuni la b pʋɩ-a-la wala b sẽn date.
58002005	Tõnd sẽn gomd beoog zamaan ning yellã, ka malɛgs la Wẽnd dɩk-a n kõ tɩ b soog ye.
58002006	Gʋlsa woto zĩig a ye: Ninsaal yaa bõe tɩ yãmb tẽegd a yelle? Bɩ: ninsaal biig zema bõe tɩ yãmb get-a ne waoogre?
58002007	Wakat n zĩndi tɩ yãmb sik ninsaal malɛk rãmb taoore; la yãmb n le wa kõ-a ziir la naam pugla,
58002008	yãmb kõ-a la bũmb fãa soolem. La b sẽn kõ-a bũmb fãa soolma, bõe n kelle t'a pa so? Tõnd yẽ nan ka ne zãnga t'a soo bũmb fãa ye.
58002009	Baasgo d neeme tɩ wakat ning b sẽn waa n sik a Zezi bilfu malɛk rãmb taoorã, wakat kãng la tõnd yãet-b ne ziir la pẽgr kãsenga, b sẽn sak kũuma yĩnga. Ne Wẽnd sõngre, b sɩd saka kũuma ne a tɩɩsma, ninsaalb buud fãa yĩnga.
58002010	Yaa Wẽnd n naan bũmb fãa tɩ bũmb fãa me be b yĩngã, la bãmb datame n kẽes b ziira pʋgẽ b kamb ka tɛkã. Ad-y da togame tɩ b paam ned sẽn na n sak ne a namsgo n tedg kambã zãnga la a kẽes-b fãagra sorẽ.
58002011	Ad-y sẽn kõta sõmbem la sẽn deegd-b sõmblema yaa rogem ne taaba, yaa rẽ la a tõe n bool-b tɩ saam-biisi tɩ yãnd pa tar-a ye.
58002012	Ad-a sẽn yeele: «M na n wilga y Yʋʋrã m saam-biisã, m na n yɩɩlame n pẽg-y m buuda neba fãa sʋka.»
58002013	B le paasa zĩig a to me: «Bãmb la m teegr zãng-zãnga.» N le paase: «Ad-ma, maam ne kamb niyns Wẽnd sẽn kõ-ma.»
58002014	Dɩlla ba-biisa sẽn ya neong la zɩɩm yɛngã ra togame tɩ sẽn wa-a ne fãagra me yɩ wa bãmba. B lebga boto n na n lub ne b kũuma ned ninga sẽn waa ne kũum dũnia: Sʋtãana,
58002015	la b fãag neb niyns sẽn da zĩ b yõor tɛka, ne kũum dabeem wala yem-daado.
58002016	Sɩda ka malɛk rãmb la b waa n na n sõnge, yaa Abraam yagense.
58002017	Dɩlla me la yɩ modgre t'a wẽneg a saam-biisã ne bũmb fãa, n wa yals bãmb ne Wẽnd sʋka wa maan-kʋʋd kãsenga la nimbãan-zoeta, n paam n yẽes buuda yel-wẽna.
58002018	Yẽ meng sẽn bãng namsg toolem, a tõeeme n sõng neb niyns me sẽn tar-b pɛta.
58003001	Dɩlla m saam-biisi, Krista nin-sõma, yãmb me sẽn paam n wʋm yĩngr boolle, maneg-y n ges tõnd tẽebã tʋʋm-tʋmda la maan-kʋʋd kãsenga: a Zezi.
58003002	B reega sẽn kõ-a bãmb tʋʋmda noor zãnga wala a Moyiiz ne a zak rãmba.
58003003	B pʋd n yeelame t'a toga ne pẽgr sẽn yɩɩd a Moyiiz rẽnna wala ro-met sẽn tog ne pẽgr n yɩɩd rooga menga.
58003004	Roog fãa yaa ned n me-a la sẽn me-a bũmb fãa wã yaa Wẽnde.
58003005	Sã n ya sɩda, a Moyiiz ne a rooga zãnga tũu Wẽnd daabo, a yɩɩ sõgne sẽn togs b sẽn yeel-a t'a togse.
58003006	Krista yɩɩ zak soab Biiga, n so zaka. La zaka la tõndo; la rẽ yaa d sã n yiis rabeem d sũurẽ n lɛɛg n pids-a ne saagra sũ-noogo.
58003007	Yaa rẽnd yĩnga la wala a Vʋʋsem Sõng sẽn yete: «Dũnna, y sã n wʋm b koɛɛgã,
58003008	bɩ y ra kidb y sũuri wala sẽn maan sɩlakra raare, fɛɛsga raare, we-raoogẽ wã ye.
58003009	Yãmb yaab rãmb fɛɛsame n na n bãng m pʋga. B yaool n da yãenda tʋʋm niyns fãa m sẽn tʋm,
58003010	yʋʋm pis naas tõrã. Dẽ me la m puug m sũuri ne bãmb, wakat kãnga n yeele: Daar fãa b sũur bʋdgda moogo, b pa yãend m sorã n dɩk ye.
58003011	M puuga m sũuri n yet tɩ m na bas-ba n ges b sẽn na n maan bũmb ninga n kẽ m vʋʋsga zĩigẽ.»
58003012	M saam-biisi, gũus-y tɩ ned da wa zĩnd yãmb sʋka t'a sũur pid ne pʋ-toogo, la wẽn-kɩɩsgo sẽn sek a wa lak zãnga ne Vɩɩm naab a Wẽnd ye.
58003013	Sagl-y taab beoog-beoog fãa tɩ sẽn nan ket n boond tɩ rũnna wã nan ya d dẽnna, woto ned ba a ye kõn bas tɩ wẽng tʋlsem wa kidb a sũur ye.
58003014	Ad-y tõnd naagda Krista n dɩt b yõodo, sã n yaa sɩda tɩ tõnd gãda kẽnkẽ n ka na n tol n bas d pipi teegrã t'a sãam ba bilfu.
58003015	B sẽn yeel woto: dũnna, y sã n wʋm b koɛɛg bɩ y ra kidb y sũuri wala pĩnd sɩlakra raarã,
58003016	m sok n gese, yaa nin-bʋse n wʋm koɛɛgã n baas n yɩ sɩlakr dãmba? B fãa gill ka yɩ neb sẽn yi Ezipt tẽng ne a Moyiiz pãng wɛɛ?
58003017	Yaa ne ãnd dãmb la Wẽnd sũur puugr yʋʋm pisnaas pʋgẽ fãa? Ka yɩ neb niyns sẽn tʋm b wẽnga tɩ weooga rɩ b fãa gilla bɩ?
58003018	Ãnd dãmb la b kãab wẽnga, n yet tɩ b kõn paam vʋʋsga tẽng n kẽ? Ka sẽn kɩɩs-ba wɛɛ?
58003019	D sɩd yãeeme tɩ b sẽn pa tõog n ta wã, yɩɩ b sẽn bas raooda yĩnga.
58004001	Wẽnd sẽn pʋlem tõnd vʋʋsgã, tɩ b kãabga ket n yɛsẽ wã, d maan dabeem, tɩ yãmb nin-yend na n wa yet tɩ b basa yẽ kɛɛnga.
58004002	Koe-noog sẽn wẽnd bãmb dãmb sẽn paama la tõnd me paam yã. La bãmb dẽnna ka naf-ba tɩ b ka paam tẽeb tɩ sek ye.
58004003	Tõnd yẽ sẽn tar tẽebã, tõnd yẽ na n kẽe vʋʋsga pugẽ, vʋʋsg ning b sẽn gom a soab yell woto: M wẽena ne sũ-puuri tɩ m na bas n ges b sẽn na n maanega n wa paam n kẽ m vʋʋsga pʋgẽ. Tẽeba sẽn wat ne vʋʋsg ninga yaa toore ne b sẽn vʋʋs a soab sɩngrẽ, dũni wã sẽn naan n sɛ wakatã.
58004004	Daar a yopoe soaba vʋʋsga yell goma woto: Wẽnd vʋʋsa rasem a yopoe daarã ne b tʋʋma.
58004005	Bõe yĩng marsã la b ket n gomd kaalẽ: M na ges b sẽn na n maanega n kẽ m vʋʋsga pugẽ?
58004006	Ad-y b sã n yeel tɩ neb n yɩ pipi n wʋm vʋʋsga kãab noogo n yaool n pa kẽ a pugẽ, la rẽ wã yaa b sẽn yɩ tõatbã, baasgo Wẽnd yalsame tɩ neb kẽer yẽ na kẽ.
58004007	Yaa rẽ me yĩng la Wẽnd leb n kõ raare: rũnna raare, n na n togs-do, ne a Daviid noore, a me wakato, wala sẽn togs al pĩndã: dũnna, yãmb sã n wʋm b koɛɛga bɩ y ra kidb-y y sũur ye.
58004008	La sɩda, a Zozuwe sã n da tõogẽ n kẽes a Israyɛl kamba vʋʋsga pʋgẽ b kõn le gomẽ daar a to yell ye.
58004009	Woto wã vʋʋsg daare, daar a yopoe soab vʋʋsgo, n kees n bĩng Wẽnd buudu.
58004010	Zozuwe ninga sẽn kẽ-a vʋʋsga zĩigẽ wã, yẽ me vʋʋsda ne a tʋʋma, wala Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋs ne b rẽnna.
58004011	Woto wã bɩ tõnd me maan yãgbo n kẽ vʋʋsg kãng zĩigẽ, la ned ba a ye da rɩk kɩɩsga sore n wa yɩ tõat ye.
58004012	Wẽnnaam Gomda sɩd yaa bõn-vɩɩga, n tar pãnga, n dɩt n yɩɩd sʋʋg buud fãa sẽn saas noy a yiibu; a sã n kõse, a kẽeda zulunga n sãagd n tat ninsaal yalẽ, n tat yĩnga sũgdsi la kõaba sɩɩlem, la a pukd ninsaal tagsgo la a pʋg zãnga.
58004013	Bũmb ka be n solg ne yẽ, fãa yaa bɩlgemde la kãre ne Ned ninga sẽn na n sok-a tõnd d vɩɩma yelle.
58004014	Woto wã tõnd sẽn paam maan-kʋʋd kãseng sẽn dʋ yĩngri n zʋʋg saaga, a Zezi, Wẽnnaam Biiga, bɩ d tall d tẽeb dɩm-dɩm.
58004015	D sẽn paam a soabã ka maan-kʋʋd kãseng sẽn ka tar gãbe n na n yols d naongã, yaa ned sẽn bãng kʋɩɩbg bũmb fãa pʋgẽ, wa tõnd fãa, la a ka maan yel-wẽnd ye.
58004016	Bɩ d kolg ne sũur sẽn ka kiuusdi b bark zaoorã, n deeg b nimbãan-zoeer la d paam sõngr sẽn segd ne-do.
58005001	Maan-kʋʋd kãseng fãa tũusda ninsaalb sʋka t'a sõng ninsaalba n maneg b yɛla ne Wẽnnaam; a maan wẽn-kosgo la a kʋ maando b yel-wẽna yĩnga.
58005002	Woto la a tõe n kũm sẽn ka mi-ba la sẽn tudg-ba, tɩ yẽ me yaa koamsa.
58005003	A sẽn ya koamsa yĩnga a togame n kʋ maand a meng yel-wẽna sugr kosg yĩnga, wa a sẽn maand buuda yĩnga.
58005004	Tʋʋmd a woto buudu, ka ninsaal n kõt-a a meng ye, yaa Wẽnd n boonde wala b sẽn maan ne a Aarõ.
58005005	Woto me, ka Krista n kõ b meng naam n na n lebg maan-kʋʋd kãseng ye. B sẽn deeg naama a soab nengẽ wã n yeel bãmba: «Fo yaa mam Biiga, rũnna la m dog foo.»
58005006	Zĩig a to me b le yeelame: «Fo yaa maan-kʋʋda, la fo maan-kʋʋra kõn sɛ abada, a wẽnda a Melkisedɛk rẽnna.»
58005007	Yaa Krista n yiki, b tẽng zugu vɩɩma wakato, n kelem ne pãnga la b yiis nintãm, n kos sugri la b yõk sẽn tõe n fãag-b ne kũuma soab sɛɛga; b sulg-m-menga yĩnga, b pʋʋsga reegame.
58005008	Woto, ne b sẽn ya Wẽnd Biigã, b zãmsa sakre ne b sẽn namsã.
58005009	B sẽn paam n pid sõmblem ne sõmblem, b lebga neb niyns fãa sẽn sakd b bãmba tɩlgr sẽn kõn sãam abada yẽgre.
58005010	Yaa Wẽnnaam meng n pʋd-b tɩ maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sẽn dɩt maan-kʋʋr naam sẽn wẽnd a Melkisedɛk rẽnna.
58005011	Yell kãnga poorẽ, tõnd na gom n yɛ; a toagsg meng ka naana ba bilfu tɩ y lebga maasg ne wʋmbo.
58005012	Sɩd me, kaoosg maaname al tɩ yaa n sek y bãng n togs y taab marsã, la ad-y sẽn ket n zĩẽ tɩ b sõng-y ne Wẽnd zãmsga sɩngre, n tol n wa lebg wa kom-peelse sẽn dat bĩisim, n pa rat rɩ-tagd ye.
58005013	Sɩda, biig sẽn nan yẽsemd tõe n bãnga koɛɛg sẽn ya sõmblem koɛɛg bɩ? A ket n yaa bi-bilf nanda.
58005014	Sã n ya rɩ-tagdã, bãmb la nin-kãseng rɩɩbo. Nin-kãsenga me la yam sẽn wɩsg a soaba t'a minim n bakd neer ne wẽnga.
58006001	Yaa rẽ yĩng la d basd zãms bõonesã, Krista bãngra sẽn sɩngd ne b rãmbã, n zẽkd d wilgrã n taasd a neerma zĩigẽ. D kõn tar poorẽ n leb n gom bũmb kẽer yelle, wa tʋʋm sẽn ka naag ne tẽeb n tʋme, wa tʋʋm kãens tuubgu, wa Wẽnnaam tẽebo,
58006002	d wa soobo, nus tikri, yĩns vʋʋgre, yaoolem bʋʋdo.
58006003	Ad-d sẽn na n maane, Wẽnd sã n sake.
58006004	Yaa toog ne neb niyns fãa sẽn paam-b Wẽnd vẽenema, sẽn lemb-b yĩngr kũuna, sẽn deeg-ba a Vʋʋsem Sõngo,
58006005	sẽn bʋgsd-b Wẽnd gomd noogã b yamẽ, sẽn wɩɩd-b ne zamaan ning sẽn wat beooga pãngã,
58006006	n baas n lʋɩ wã, yaa toog ne-ba tɩ b le lebg nin paalse ne tuubgu, tɩ bãmb meng b toore n leb n kaad Wẽnd Biiga pika la b kamsd d bɛɛba tɩ b le wa yaal-ba la b tʋ-ba.
58006007	Pʋʋg ninga sẽn paame tɩ sa-koom madg-a naoor wʋsgo t'a wom biisi wa a koadba sẽn date, pʋ-kãng paama Wẽnd barka.
58006008	Pʋʋga sã n yit gõose la yõeestabdo, b get-a-la wa pʋʋg sẽn ka yõodo, sẽn ka barka la b sẽn na n wa kong n yõog bugum.
58006009	Sã n ya yãmba, m kom-nongdse, ba m sẽn gom woto wã, m miime tɩ yãmb yalsa y mens zĩ sõngẽ, zĩig ning Fãagra sẽn na n yɩ naana ne yã.
58006010	Wẽnd pa mi zãmb ye. B yɩta a wãn n yĩm yãmb manesem la sõngr ning yãmb sẽn yaoog la y ket n yaoogd nin-sõma, bãmb yʋʋr yĩngã?
58006011	Tõnd sẽn datã, yaa yãmb ned kam fãa wɩng n paase ne tʋʋmd kãnga tɩ y saagra tar yãagre n dabda n wa tãag a tɛka.
58006012	Woto yãmb kõn maan kʋɩɩng ye, y na wẽneg neb niyns sẽn dɩt-b kãabga yõodo ne b tẽeb la b sũ-maasem.
58006013	Sɩda, Wẽnnaam sẽn waa n na n kãab a Abraam b kãab-noogã, b kong n wẽena ne b menga tɩ ned da ka be sẽn yɩɩd bãmba tɩ b nan wẽen ne yẽ soab ye,
58006014	b yeelame: «Sɩd ne sɩda, m na n ning-f la barka n sudgi, la m na n yalga f buuda zembala.»
58006015	Yaa woto la a Abraam sẽn gãd a tẽeb n pa viigã paam kãabga pidsgu.
58006016	Yaa ne sẽn yɩɩd-a la ninsaal wẽenda. Wẽeneg sã n lʋɩ ninsaal ne a to sʋka, no-koeemd sɛɛme.
58006017	Yaa woto la Wẽnd tʋlg n wilg sẽn dɩt-b bãmb kãabga yõodo, tɩ b raaba pa teem ye, n wẽen b wẽenego.
58006018	Ne bũmb a yiibã sẽn ka tõe n ka pidsã: kãabgã la wẽenegã, Wẽnd wilgame tɩ b yɛsa b sɩd zĩigẽ, tɩ tõnd sor bãmba n na n paam daoodo n saag sõmb-sõmbo, d sẽn tõe n saag bũmb ningã.
58006019	Saagr kãng yĩnga, yaa wa tõnd sɩɩga kɩɩ baare, baar sẽn ka kẽnkẽ n ka tõe n võoge, baar sẽn sãag n ka peen-lillã sẽn yag zĩig ningã.
58006020	A Zezi n deng pipi n kẽ peen-lilla poore, tɩ b lebga yʋʋm sẽn kõn sɛ yĩnga, maan-kʋʋd kãsenga, wala a Melkisedɛk.
58007001	Melkisedɛk yẽne yɩɩ Salɛm dĩma la Yĩngr Wẽnnaama maan-kʋʋd; yẽ n tɩ seg a Abraam a sẽn waa n zab n tõog dĩm dãmba n lebda tẽngẽ, la yẽ n ning-a barka,
58007002	t'a Abraam me sak n kẽ a paoongẽ n yãk a paoonga rʋr a ye piig fãa zugu, n kõ-a; a Melkisedɛk yʋʋra meng rat n yeelame tɩ Zemsg dĩma; yẽ me n le yaa Salem dĩma, dat n yeelame tɩ laafi dĩma.
58007003	Yẽnda ba yʋʋr ka pʋde, a ma yʋʋr ka pʋde, a yaab rãmb yʋʋr ka pʋde; b pa tar a yʋʋm sõore, b ka mi a rogem yʋʋmde, b ka mi a vɩɩma sẽn baas wakat ning ye; a wẽnda Wẽnd Biiga; Melkisedɛk kãng yaa maan-kʋʋd yʋʋm tõt sɛɛb yĩnga.
58007004	Ges-y wa nin-kãsenga ned ning a Abraam, buud kãsma, sẽn kõ a soaba a zu-noog pʋɩɩre, pʋɩɩr sẽn be yõodo.
58007005	Sɩda a Levi buud kamba sẽn lebgd maan-kʋʋdba tara tõogo n deeg bũmb neb a taaba nengẽ, dat n yeelame tɩ b saam-biis nengẽ, a Abraam yagense, wa bãmb mense.
58007006	Kaalẽ wã yaa ned sẽn da pa kĩ ne a Abraam n deeg pʋɩɩr a nengẽ, la a ning-a-la barka; yaool n da yaa yẽ zugu la Wẽnd kãab nooga sig yã.
58007007	La yãmb zɩ tɩ yaa kãsma n ningd yao barka?
58007008	Sẽn paase, ad-y yaa neb sẽn kiidi n deesd pʋɩɩr a ye piig zugã, la ka wã, b gomda ned sẽn vɩ daar fãa yelle.
58007009	La bũmb zãnga yaa waa a Levi menga, sẽn deesd-a pʋɩɩr a ye piig zugã, yaa wa yẽ n soola Abraam n kɩs a rẽnna;
58007010	tɩ yẽ sẽn ya yagenga, a da bee a yaab kãseng saagrẽ, wakat ning a Melkisedɛk sẽn seg a yaaba: a Abraam.
58007011	Buuda sẽn tũud Noor ninga gʋlsa a Levi sebrẽ; dɩll a Levi sẽn paam maan-kʋʋr ninga sã n da tõe n kõ sõmblem pidungu, yaa bõe yĩng tɩ b le baood maan-kʋʋr a to sẽn wẽnd a Melkisedɛk rẽnna, n ka na n baoẽ maan-kʋʋr sẽn yaa Aarõ rẽnna?
58007012	Ade, maan-kʋʋra sã n tedge, a noy wã me naagdame n tedge.
58007013	Sɩda, b sẽn gomd ned ning yellã yita sak a to sẽn ka a Levi dẽn ye, la sak kãng ned ba a ye zɩ n tʋm maan-kʋʋr tʋʋmd ye.
58007014	Tõnd fãa miime tɩ tõnd Soaala yita a Zɩɩda sakẽ la a Moyiiz sã n gomd maan-kʋʋdba yelle a zɩ n pʋd sak kãng yʋʋr ye.
58007015	Bũmb ning sẽn le vẽnegd tõnd n paasdẽ yaa b sẽn yeel t'a Melkisedɛk zĩigẽ, maan-kʋʋd a to n wa n wẽnd yẽnda.
58007016	La yẽ soaba sẽn lebg maan-kʋʋda, ka tũ wa ninsaal noor sẽn da yals ye, tũu ne vɩɩma ka be sɛɛba soaba pãnga.
58007017	Ad-b sẽn yeele: Fo reega maan-kʋʋr naam sẽn ka be sɛɛbo wala a Melkisedɛk rẽnna.
58007018	Yɩɩ woto la b menes pĩnd Noorã, a pãng la a yõod sẽn paoodã.
58007019	Sɩda Noora ka tõog n taas bũmb ba a ye a neerem zĩigẽ ye. Paam n kolg Wẽnd n yɩɩd pĩnda saagr ka tũ-a n wa ye.
58007020	Tũu ne wẽeneg la maan-kʋʋr naam paalga yalsyã. Maan-kʋʋdb a taaba reegda b tʋʋmde tɩ Wẽnd wẽeneg ka lʋɩ sʋk ye;
58007021	Krista naama kõo ne wẽenego. Sẽn kõ-a maan-kʋʋrã n yeele: «Soaala meng n wẽene la b kõn lebs b zelemd ye: fo lebga maan-kʋʋd yʋʋm tõt sɛɛb yĩnga.»
58007022	La rẽ me n kɩt tɩ zood ning a Zezi sẽn wa ne a soaba yõod yɩɩda.
58007023	N paasme, maan-kʋʋdba taaba sõor da yaa wʋsgo, tɩ kũum n da loogd ne-ba, tɩ b pa kaoosdẽ ye.
58007024	Sã n ya Krista, bãmb sẽn ya vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ naaba, b maan-kʋʋra naam me kõn sɛ abada.
58007025	Rẽ me yĩng la b tõe n fãag zãng-zãnga, sẽn tũud-b bãmba n kolgd Wẽnnaam, tɩ bãmb vɩɩ wakat fãa n tõe n yõk sɛɛga, b yĩnga.
58007026	Sɩda, yaa maan-kʋʋd kãsma woto la d da tog n paamẽ: nin-sõngo, ned sẽn ka tar a toorẽ yelle, wẽng sẽn pa pẽneg a soab lɛ-lɛ la sẽn welg marsã tɛka ne yel-wẽn-maandba, tɩ b zʋʋga saasã, n zao yĩngri.
58007027	Ka pakr ne yẽnda, wa maan-kʋʋdb a taaba, tɩ beoog sẽn vẽege, bɩ b reng n kʋ maand b meng yĩnga n yaool n kʋ buuda yĩng ye; b maana dẽ fãa vugr la tɛka ne b menga maoongo.
58007028	Noora sẽn da waa n ket n yɛsẽ, yaa koms-rãmba la b ra yãkd n kõt maan-kʋʋr naam; la wẽenega sẽn wẽene n pʋgl Noorã, yaa Biiga sẽn pid ne sõmblem n lebg maan-kʋʋd yʋʋm tõt sɛɛb yĩnga.
58008001	D goama fãa yẽgre yaa d tara maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sẽn zĩ yĩngri, naama goeela rɩtgo.
58008002	Bãmb n maan b tʋʋmde pʋʋsga zĩigẽ, zãnda tẽngre; zãn-kãng ka ninsaal n ti ye, yaa Soaala sẽn ti a soaba menga.
58008003	Maan-kʋʋd kãseng fãa tʋʋmde ya a kõ kũuni la a kʋ maando; woto wã yaa pakr ne-a t'a paam bũmb n kɩse.
58008004	D sã n togs sɩda, a Zezi sã n da yaẽ la tẽng zug neda, b kõon n yɩẽ maan kʋʋd me wee, tɩ tẽnga zoe n tara a maan-kʋʋdba sẽn kõt kũuni wala noora sẽn date.
58008005	Bãmb dãmb tʋʋmna yaa yĩngr soaba rẽnna wẽnego la a sulunsuku. Yaa rẽ la a Moyiiz bãngyã, a sẽn waa n na n ti Sɛka zãnde, tɩ Wẽnd waa n yeel-a lame: «Gese la f maan fãa tɩ tũ m sẽn wilg foo tãnga zugã.»
58008006	Marsã Krista paama tʋʋmde sẽn ya sõmbo n yɩɩda tɩ bãmb n yals sʋka tɩ b yõg zoodo la zood kãng tũu ne kãabdo sẽn yɩ sõmb n yɩɩda.
58008007	Pipi zooda sã n da yɩẽ la zood sẽn ka keoose, b kõn le yõgẽ zood a to n leda zĩig ye.
58008008	Sɩda Wẽnd sãbsa Israyɛl kamb n yeele: «Ad-y daar n wate – Soaala n yeele – tɩ m na n yõg zood paalga ne a Israyɛl roogo la a Zɩɩda roogo;
58008009	la kõn yɩ wala zood ninga m sẽn yõg pĩnda ne y yaab rãmba, m sẽn waa n gãd-ba n yiis Ezipt tẽnga ye; bãmb mens n ka pa m zooda pʋga tɩ mam me bas-ba: yaa Soaala n yeele.
58008010	La ad zood ninga m sẽn na n yõg ne a Israyɛl: Dasem kãens poore, – Soaalã n yeele – m na n ninga mam noya b yamẽ, mam na n gʋls-b-la b sũurẽ, mam na n yɩ bãmb Wẽnnaam tɩ bãmb yɩ mam neba.
58008011	Ned ba a ye kõn yik rẽ poore, tɩ yẽ n na n zãms-ba a tẽngen-bi-taaga bɩ a ma-biiga, n yetẽ: ‹Bãng Soaala,› tɩ b fãa na n bãnga maam, kom-kɩdsã, n tãag nin-bɛdã.
58008012	M na n kõ-la b beegra sugri, la m kõn le tẽeg b yel-wẽna yɛs ye.»
58008013	B sẽn yeele tɩ Zood paalgã, b kɩtame tɩ pipi soaba kʋdg zãnga; la bõn-kʋdgo, bũmb sẽn pid yʋʋma kolga loogre.
58009001	Pipi zooda me ra tara a noy sẽn sigl Wẽnd waoogr yĩnga n paas a pʋʋsg roogo sẽn ya tẽng zug rẽnna.
58009002	B ra tii zãnde n kẽe n pas-a pʋs ne peen-lilli. Pipi pʋga da reegda Fitil kãsenga, ne te-roagendga, tɩ bark bur dɩg a zugu, tɩ b ra boond zĩ kãng tɩ sõmblem zĩiga.
58009003	Peen-lill a yiib soaba poor zĩiga ra boondame marsã tɩ Sõmblem pid sõmblem zĩiga.
58009004	Maan-kugr n da be be n ya sãnem tɩ b yõogd wisdã a zugu. Sẽn le paas, yaa Zood kasetã Koglgo; yẽ me tablga sãnem la sãnem yubl n da be yẽ me pʋgẽ ne rɩɩb ninga sẽn da yit yĩngri n dʋʋgd tẽnga n boond tɩ maan; sẽn le paas yaa a Aarõ dasaar sẽn tob vãoogo. D da yĩm walsa yiibã tɩ bãmb zug n gʋls zooda siglgu.
58009005	Zood kaseta koglga limda zugu, malɛgs n da yɛdg b pɩgsa n maand maasem n kõt zĩig ning b sẽn da kʋʋd maand yel-wẽna sugr kosg yĩnga. La vẽ-y tɩ d da yaas n sõdg rẽ fãa a yeyn-ye kaalẽ ye.
58009006	Ya woto la bũmba fãa siglyã la maan-kʋʋdba kẽeda pipi zãnda, wakat fãa, n maand b waoogr tʋʋmde.
58009007	Sã n ya zãnd a yiib soabã, yaa maan-kʋʋd kãsma a ye tãa n kẽed be la rẽ me yaa vugr yʋʋmde la a zãada zɩɩm a sẽn na n daag buudã la a meng beegr sugr kosg yĩnga.
58009008	A Vʋʋsem Sõng wilgd-d la ne rẽ tɩ wẽnd doog a to wã kõn pake tɩ pipi zãndã ket a zĩigẽ ye.
58009009	Dẽ yaa makre, marsã zamaana yĩnga: kũuna b sẽn da kõtã la maandã b sẽn da kʋʋdã da ka tõe n paas sẽn waoogda Wẽnda sõmblem ye.
58009010	Yaa noy sẽn get yĩnga yɩlgre, rɩɩb bɩ bõn-yũudri yelle, noy sẽn get koom waasg yelle, noy sẽn ya tɩlɛ tɩ b tũ n gũud b tekre.
58009011	Sã n ya Krista, bãmb waame wa Zooda zamaana Maan-kʋʋd kãsenga, dẽ la b kẽ roog sẽn ya kãsenga la sẽn ya sõmb n yɩɩda, roog sẽn ka ninsaal nug n me, roog sẽn ka tẽng zug bũmb meng ye.
58009012	B kẽe ro kãng pʋga. B pa kẽ ne boees la lols zɩɩm ye, b kẽe ne b meng zɩɩm la woto b tõogame tɩ d tɩlg tɩlgr sẽn kõn sãam abada.
58009013	Sɩda, b sã n tõe n dɩk boees la lols zɩɩm, n paas nag-sɛdg tompɛglem n mes neb sẽn dẽgme tɩ b paam b yĩnga pekre,
58009014	y pa tẽed tɩ Krista sẽn tũ a Vʋʋsem Sõngo menga n dɩk b meng sẽn ka tol n dẽgma n kõ Wẽnde, y pa tẽed tɩ b zɩɩma na pek d sũurã ne a tʋʋm dẽgda fãa tɩ d me tõog n waoog vɩɩm Naaba?
58009015	Yaa rẽ me la Krista lʋɩ sʋka tɩ zood paalga tõog n yõge, la b kiime n na n yao samde: beegr ning sẽn beeg pipi zooda wakatã saamde; b kiime tɩ Wẽnd sẽn bool b rãmba tõog n dɩ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ pʋgẽ b sẽn kaab-b yõod ningã.
58009016	B sã n gomd raboog welgr yelle, yaa tɩlɛ tɩ b gom tɩ kũum n deng taoore.
58009017	Raboog welgr sebr ka be võore, kũum sã ka ki ye, sebra soab sã n ket n vɩ b ka tõe n yãg n tũ sẽn gʋls sebra zuga ye.
58009018	Dẽ n kɩt tɩ pipi zooda meng ka tõog n yõg tɩ zɩɩm ka reng n daag ye.
58009019	A Moyiiz sẽn wilg nebã Noora sẽn yet tɩ b reeg bũmb ninga fãa, n sɛ, a rɩka lol-bõonese la boees zɩɩm, a rɩka koom, n dɩk pe-kõbd sẽn ya moomde la tɩɩg sẽn tar yũ-noog vão killi, n mes Noora sẽn da gʋls bũmb ning zuga menga la a mes zãma wã.
58009020	A yeel-b lame: «Zɩɩm kãnga yaa yãmb ne Wẽnd zooda kaset zɩɩm!»
58009021	Dẽ poore yaa zãnda menga ne pʋʋsga teed fãa la a mes ne zɩɩm.
58009022	Dẽ pʋgẽ me, wa Noora sebr sẽn wilgdi, bũmb fãa la bala pekda ne zɩɩm, tɩ sugr kũun naagda ne zɩɩm daagre.
58009023	Dẽ n so tɩ wala arzãn yɛla sulunsugdu la b makre sẽn da tog n pek boto ne maand zɩɩm, woto me ne arzãn bũmba menga, la yaa ne maand sẽn tar pãng n yɩɩd tẽng zug maandã.
58009024	Krista sẽn be zĩig ninga ka ro-zaal sẽn me tẽng zug ye, a ka yĩngr dooga meng mamseg ye, yaa arzãn meng la b kẽ yã n na n yals Wẽnd taoor marsã n yõk sɛɛg n kõ-do.
58009025	B pa tɩ kõ b meng naoor yak wa pĩnd maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sẽn da maand yʋʋmd yʋʋmd fãa n kẽed pʋʋsga roogẽ ne zɩɩm sẽn ka a meng zɩɩma ye.
58009026	Ka rẽ yaẽ la naoor yak la b namsẽ, dũnia sẽn sɩng tɛka. La d neeme tɩ yaa marsã, yaoolem wakatã la vugr bala, la Krista lik yã n na n yẽes yel-wẽnd zãnga ne b maoong yɛngã.
58009027	Ninsaal kiida vugr bala t'a bʋʋd kao.
58009028	Wotome la Krista sẽn kõ b meng vugr bala n na n dol neb wʋsg yel-wẽna, na n le lɛɛg n waame, la kõn le yɩ yel-wẽnd yĩng ye, na n yɩla b wa fãag sẽn gũud-b bãmb waoongã.
58010001	Noora sẽn dat n kõ-d bũmb ninga yaa sẽn nan wat beooga sulunsugdu la b mamsega, ka bũmba meng ye; woto Noora ka tõe ba bilfu, tɩ sẽn baood-ba n na n pẽneg Wẽndã lebg sõma ne maand sẽn wẽnd taab daar fãa la sẽn ya pakre tɩ b kʋ rõanna n le kʋ vẽere.
58010002	Ka rẽ, sõmblema sã n da paamdẽ la vugri la tɛka, maan-kʋʋdba na vʋʋsẽ al daar zãra ne maand a woto buud kʋʋbo tɩ b mens ra ka na le neẽ b kongra sẽn yɛs zĩig ning ye.
58010003	Mik maand kãens kʋʋb ra tẽegd-b la yʋʋmd yʋʋmd fãa tɩ b yaa yel-wẽn-maandba.
58010004	Ka lolsa la boeesa zɩɩm n tõe n yẽes yel-wẽn ye.
58010005	Yaa rẽ yĩnga la Krista yeel yã, b sẽn waa n kẽed dũnia: «Yãmb pa tʋlg maoong bɩ yamleoog kũun ye, la y yaool n kõ-m la yĩnga.
58010006	Maandã sẽn yõogd tɩ bugum dɩ zãnga, maand sẽn kʋʋd yel-wẽna yĩnga, ba a ye yamleoog pa yõk-y ye;
58010007	yaa rẽ la m yeel yã: ‹Ade! M watame, tɩ yaa mam yell la b gomd sebra pʋgẽ, m watame n na n maan yãmb yam, m Wẽnnaam!› »
58010008	B sɩngame n yeele: maando la yamleoog kũuni, maand sẽn yõog bugmẽ, maand sẽn kʋʋd yel-wẽna yĩnga, yãmb tõdg-b lame, y pa reeg-b ye – mik maand kãens la Noora ra yals yã, –
58010009	dẽ yĩng la b yeel yã: Ade! M watame n na n maan yãmb yam. Dɩlla b waa ne zamaan paalga n na n sãam pĩnd soabã.
58010010	La yaa ne raab kãng pãng la tõnd paam sõmblem ne Krista a Zezi yĩnga maoong b sẽn kʋ vugri la tɛka.
58010011	Maan-kʋʋd tɛka yaa beoog sẽn vẽege bɩ a yɛs ne pʋʋsgo la a tar maand kʋʋbo, maand sẽn yaool n ka tõe n yẽes yel-wẽnd ba a ye.
58010012	Sã n ya Krista, b sẽn maan maoong yɛng yel-wẽna yĩnga, ad-b sẽn zĩ b Ba rɩtgo daar fãa marsã,
58010013	n gũud tɩ bɛɛba gãneg b taoore tɩ b palgd b nao n zĩi.
58010014	Ne maoon yɛng bala yaa sõmblem sẽn pid zãnga la sẽn kõn sãam abada la b paam n kõ-b sẽn maneg b rãmb yellã.
58010015	Mik yaa rẽ me la a Vʋʋsem Sõng kõt kaseto b meng b toore, b sẽn waa n yeele:
58010016	«Ad zood ninga mam sẽn na n yõg ne bãmba dẽ loogr poore, la woto la Soaala gom yã: Mam na n ninga mam noya b sũurẽ, mam na n gʋls-b la bãmb pʋtẽerẽ,
58010017	mam kõn le tẽeg b beegre bɩ b yel-wẽna abada.»
58010018	La yel-wẽn niyns sẽn zoe n paam-b sugrã, b ka le kʋʋd maand b yĩng ye.
58010019	Dɩlla m saam-biisi, marsã d bãng neere tɩ d tõe n taa arzãn pʋʋsg roogẽ ne a Zezi zɩɩm pãnga,
58010020	tɩ b tuka sor n kõ-do, so paale la vɩɩm sor sẽn sãag peen-lillã, – la peen-lilla yaa bãmb yĩnga makre.
58010021	D sẽn paam maan-kʋʋd kãsenga woto, Wẽnd sẽn dɩk n gũnug b roogo,
58010022	bɩ d kolg ne pʋ-peelem, ne sũur sẽn pid ne tẽebo la sẽn nedeg zãnga ne pʋ-toog buud fãa la ne yĩng sẽn pek ne ko-sõngo;
58010023	d tabend d sẽn teeg a soaba neere. Sẽn pʋlm-a tõndã yaa sɩd soaba;
58010024	d tẽeg taab yelle, la d yãng d nonglem ne taaba la d wɩng ne tʋʋm-sõma.
58010025	Bɩ y da vaal y lageng wala neb kẽere sẽn nong n maana ye; yãmb wee n kengd taab sũya, bũmb zãnga y sẽn ne tɩ Soaala waoong raar kolgame.
58010026	La sã n ya tõnd n sak tudgr ne yamleoogo la d yaool n da bãnga sɩda, ad-y maoong a to ka le be yel-wẽnd yĩng koe!
58010027	Bũmb ning sẽn be n ya yel-beed kãsenga, yaa bʋʋda kaoobo. Ad-y yaa bugum sẽn ka mi sugri, n na n dɩ wẽn-kɩɩsdbã.
58010028	Ned sã n da tõdg a Moyiiz Noore sugr da ka be yẽ soab yĩng ye; kaset dãmb a yiib bɩ a tãab sã n da be bala, b kʋʋda yẽ soaba.
58010029	La yãmb ka tagsd tɩ yaa sɩbgr sẽn ya toog n yɩɩd la b na n sɩbg sẽn tabd-b ne b nao, Wẽnd Biigã, n sɩbg sẽn ges-b wa bõn-yaalga, zooda zɩɩm sẽn kõ-b sõmblema, n sɩbg sẽn paoog-b a Vʋʋsem Sõngo, Wẽnd kũuna Kõatã?
58010030	Tõnd mii sẽn yeel-a: «Maam n so rok-m-sũuri, maam n so sɩbgre.» La zĩig a to yɛsa: «Soaala meng n na n kao b neba bʋʋdo.»
58010031	Yel-beed kãseng meng la b sẽn bas ninsaal Wẽnd nusẽ, Vɩɩm Naaba nusẽ!
58010032	Bɩ y tẽeg marsã pipi raarã yãmb sẽn paam y yam vẽnegre ne tẽebo, yɩɩ namsg wʋsgo la yãmb da sak yã.
58010033	Wakat kẽere yɩɩ yãmb meng la b yaal yã la b yãk y zak neb fãa nifẽ; wakat kẽere yɩɩ neb a taab la b maan woto tɩ yãmb kũm bãmb dãmba.
58010034	Sɩda, yãmb kũma sẽn da be-b bi-bees roogo la y sõng-b lame; yãmb sakame tɩ b maan y pãnga n deeg y paoong fãa; y ra miime tɩ b bĩnga yãmb arzɛk sẽn yɩɩd rẽ la sẽn kõn menem abada.
58010035	Dẽ yĩngã da bas-y y tẽeba teegr ye t'a dolb na n yɩɩ kãsenga, a na n dola y naongã.
58010036	Yaa sũ-keelem la y tog n maane tɩ y sã n tũud Wẽnnaam yam, y na tõog n paam b sẽn kãab yãmbã.
58010037	Keta bilfr bala, keta sẽn ka zem bũmbu, tɩ sẽn wat a soaba na n wa la kõn kaoos ye.
58010038	Mam nin-sõng tog n dɩla a tẽeb yõodo; la a sã n tar n leb poorẽ, mam yam na lak ne-a.
58010039	Sã n ya tõndo, tõnd ka neb sẽn lebd poorẽ n na n sãam d yelle, tõnd yaa neb sẽn teeg tẽebo n na n fãag d sɩɩga.
58011001	Tẽeb n kɩtd tɩ d saagd bõn-sõma paoongo la a kõt kaset tɩ bũmb n be n zʋʋg nif sẽn ne bala.
58011002	Tõnd yaab rãmba tẽebo n yɩ b vɩɩm sõnga kaseto.
58011003	Yaa tẽeb n wilgd tõndo tɩ dũni wã sigla ne Wẽnnaam gomde. Woto me la d mi tɩ d sẽn ne bũmb ningã yita d sẽn ka tõe n yãend a soaba nengẽ.
58011004	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Abɛl kõ Wẽnd maoong sẽn tar yõodo n yɩɩd a Kaẽ rẽnna. Rẽ me yĩng la Wẽnd puk a sõmblem; Wẽnd meng n kõ kaseto t'a kũuna yɩɩ kũun sõma. Leb n yaa tẽeba yĩnga la a ki yã t'a koɛɛg ket n sãta.
58011005	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Enok paam tɩ b yiis-a dũnia t'a pa bãng kũum ye; a waa n menema woto, tɩ Wẽnnaam n loog ne-a. A sẽn da waa n nan ka looge, a paama kaset t'a vɩɩma taa Wẽnnaam yam.
58011006	Ninsaal yaool n pa tõe n ta Wẽnnaam yam a sã n ka tar tẽeb ye. Ned ninga sẽn kolgda Wẽnnaam tog n deng n deegame tɩ b beeme. Bãmb n dond ned ning fãa sẽn baooda bãmba.
58011007	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Nowe paam Wẽnd vẽnegre n yãend a sẽn da pa tõe n yãende tɩ rabeem sõng yõk-a t'a yik n sɩng koglga kaabo n paam n fãag a zak rãmba; a tẽebã n kɩt t'a zãag a meng ne zamaana la a rɩɩ tẽeb sẽn wat ne sõmblem ninga yõodo.
58011008	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Abraam wʋm Wẽnnaam koɛɛg ninga sẽn yeel-a t'a yik n tees tẽng ning b sẽn kãab-a, t'a sɩd yik n dabd a sẽn pa miẽ ye.
58011009	Yaa tẽeb n kɩt t'a wa zĩnd kãabga tẽngẽ wala tẽn-zẽna, zãn tẽngr bala, yẽ ne a Izaak la a Zakoob sẽn naag b yẽ n dɩ kãabga yõodo.
58011010	A Abraam ra gũuda tẽng a to, Wẽnd sẽn sõoge la b me b toore.
58011011	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Sara meng ne a kʋʋlma tõog n dɩk pʋga; a reegame tɩ sẽn kãab-a yẽnd biigã yaa sɩd soaba.
58011012	Yaa woto la nin-yend sẽn da kʋʋle n ta a yõor menga tõog n dog kamb la yagens kõn-bãng-n sõde, wa saag zug ãdse bɩ mogr noorẽ bĩisri.
58011013	Yaa ne b tẽebo la d yaab rãmba fãa gãnd yã tɩ b nif pa yãend kãabga tẽng ye. B yaool n yãend-a la yɩɩga n bɛɛl-a la b maannẽ tɩ tẽng zug ka b ra yaa sãamba la so-toagdba.
58011014	Neb sẽn gom a woto wilga vẽenega tɩ yaa b ba-yir la b saad n baoodẽ.
58011015	La sã n da yaẽ la ba-yir ning b sẽn basã la b ra bolgda, b paama vɩʋʋg tɩ sek a lebẽ be.
58011016	B sẽn baood ba-yir ningã yaa ba-yir a to sẽn noom n yɩɩda: arzãn ba-yirã. Ya rẽ yĩng la Wẽnd pa zoe yãnde n pʋd b meng tɩ bãmb Wẽnnaam, la sɩda bãmb meng n segl tẽng kãng n bĩng-ba.
58011017	Wẽnnaam sẽn wa n tʋlg n bãng a Abraam pʋga, a Abraam tẽeba kɩtame t'a yõk a biig a Izaak, a bi-yende, n na n kʋ maoongo; yaool n da yaa bi-kãng zugu la kãabga fãa da yɛsa.
58011018	Yaa yẽnda poorẽ la b ra yeel yã: Yaa ne a Izaak la fo na n dog buudu.
58011019	Mik a Abraam tagsame tɩ Wẽnnaam pãnga tõeeme n vʋʋg kũum; la yaa rẽ me yĩng la Wẽnd le lebs-a a biiga la yell kãng me lɛɛg n yaa zãmsgo d yĩnga.
58011020	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Izaak ninga a Zakoob la a Ezayu barka, bark sẽn na n kɩt tɩ b poorẽ yɩ yalengo.
58011021	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Zakoob sẽn waa n na n looge, a ninga a Zozɛf kamb a yiiba barka; dẽ t'a wõgame n tikd a rasaarã.
58011022	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Zozɛf me sẽn waa n na n ki, a goma Israyɛl kamb Ezipt yiib yelle n wilg a sẽn dat tɩ b wa maan bũmb ning ne a kõabã.
58011023	Yaa b tẽeba yĩnga la a Moyiiz rogem wakato, a ba rãmb solg-a kiis a tãabo, b sẽn yãe t'a yaa bi-neere; b pa zoe naaba noor tõdgr ye.
58011024	Yaa a tẽeba yĩnga la a Moyiiz kos yã, a sẽn waa n lebg bi-kãsenga, tɩ b ra bool-a tɩ Ezipt naaba yageng ye;
58011025	a tagsame t'a sẽn naagd Wẽnnaam buudã n nams n são a sẽn na n bao yel-wẽnd ne a sũ-noogã sẽn pa zɛɛdã.
58011026	A tagsame tɩ sak namsgo Wẽnd Nedã yĩng bee yõodo n yɩɩd Ezipt tẽnga laog buud fãa; sɩda a nina ra zoe n ne-la a rolbo.
58011027	Tẽeb n kɩt t'a yi Ezipt tẽnga tɩ naaba sũ-puur dabeem da ka tar-a ye; a maana sũ-keelem wala a ra nee ned ning sẽn ka tõe n yãend ne nina.
58011028	Tẽeb n kɩt t'a maan pak kibsa la a bol zagsa ne zɩɩm tɩ malɛk ning sẽn wata ne tẽn-kũuma ra sɩɩs a Israyɛl kom dẽemsa ye.
58011029	Tẽeb n kɩt t'a Israyɛl kamb dʋʋg Mog-Miuugu wala b kẽnda tẽn koeeng zugu, tɩ kooma yaool n dɩ Ezipt neba sẽn mak-a rʋʋgre.
58011030	B tẽeba yĩng la Israyɛl kamba sẽn kẽne n gilg Zeriko dasem a yopoe, n lub a lalsã ne b bedrema fãa.
58011031	Tẽeb n fãag pʋg-yoodr a Raab; b pa naag-a ne kɩɩsdbã n kʋ ye, t'a reega lɩɩsdba sãando, laafi sãando.
58011032	M na n le paasa bõe? Sẽk bee m sẽn na n togs a Zedeõ kibare, n paas a Barak, a Sãmsõ, a Zefte, a Daviid ne a Samwɛl la bãngdbã?
58011033	Yaa b tẽeba yĩnga la b yalg b rĩungu ne nanamsa taab rẽnda. B tẽeba yĩng la b kao bʋ-tɩrse, la b paam Wẽnnaam sẽn kãab-ba fãa pidsgu; b tõog n paga bõnyẽes noore,
58011034	n sɛɛs bugum pãnga, n põs sʋ-rɩts noore; b ra yaa koms-rãmba la b lebga neb sẽn wɩɩd pãnga; b maana raood zabr zĩigẽ, b riga bu-zẽmba sẽn da wat n na n soog b tẽnga.
58011035	B vʋʋga kamba n lebs b ma rãmba. Bãmb neb kẽer sakame tɩ b nams-ba, la b zãgs fãagre, n wa tõog n paam vʋʋgre sẽn be yõod n yɩɩda.
58011036	Neb a taab sakame tɩ b yaal-ba, n bug b yĩinsa ne kaase, n balg-b bãeense, n kẽes-b roogo.
58011037	B laba kẽer ne kuga, n bees kẽer ne sʋʋs sẽn kɩ yẽna, n kood kẽere; b yeelga pe-gãndo la bʋ-gãndo; b kẽnga ka, n leb ka, tɩ naong tar ba, tɩ toog tar ba, tɩ pɛt tar ba.
58011038	Zamaana ra pa tog ne b ye tɩ b na n gilim weoogẽ, tãms zutu, tãms pẽgsẽ la tẽng bogdẽ.
58011039	Bãmb fãa paama pẽgre, b tẽeba yĩnga; b fãa yaool n pa rɩ kãabga yõod ye,
58011040	tɩ Wẽnd ra bĩnga tõnd zu-noog pʋɩɩr sẽn yɩɩde la b ra pa tog n ta sõmblema zĩigẽ tɩ tõnd ket poorẽ ye.
58012001	Tõnd sẽn zĩ marsã ne kaset dãmb kʋʋngo sẽn gũbg tõndo, ad-y d tog n sika zɩɩb ning fãa d sẽn tʋke la d lood yel-wẽnd gãda fãa la d wudg n da yalse, n ta b sẽn wilg tõnda tɛka.
58012002	D doog d neng n ges d tẽeba kõata la a bɩɩsda: a Zezi; b tõdga laafi n yãk pika namsgo la b tʋk-a lame n ka zoe a yãnd ye, la yaa rẽ la b sẽn zĩ marsã Wẽnnaam zaoora rɩtgo.
58012003	Tags-y namsg niyns fãa Krista sẽn paam yel-wẽn-maandba la kɩɩsdba nengẽ; woto yãmb me sɩɩs kõn bas raoodo n lʋɩ ye.
58012004	Ad-y sẽn ta marsã y nan ka teedg ne yel-wẽnde tɩ sek y zɩɩm daagr ye.
58012005	Yãmb yĩma Wẽnnaam sẽn sagend yãmb wala b kamba: «M biiga, ra tõdg Soaala sɩbgr ye; la b sã n wilgd foom f kongre, bɩ f ra bas raood ye.
58012006	Ned sã n nong Soaalã, Soaala sɩbgd-a lame; b sɩbgda biig ning fãa b sẽn nonge.»
58012007	Y sã n namsdẽ, yaa sẽn na yɩlẽ tɩ y tedg zʋgo; Wẽnd maanda woto ne yãmba wa ba sẽn maand ne a biiga. La bi-bʋg la a ba ka sɩbgde?
58012008	B sã n ka sɩbg yãmb wala b sẽn sɩbgd neba fãa, dɩlla yãmb yaa tãmpĩiba, y ka b kamb ye.
58012009	Tõnd paama neb sẽn sagl tõndo: yaa sẽn dog-b tõndã, la tõnd da kelgd-b la ne waoogre. Bõe yĩng marsã la d ka na n sulg d meng d yĩngr Ba wã taoore n paam vɩɩm?
58012010	Pipi ba rãmba sagla tõnd bilf bala la wala b sẽn da tagsde. D Ba a to wã sagend-d lame n dat-d ne neere, n dat tɩ d paam sõmblem.
58012011	Sɩda sɩbgr buud fãa yaa toog a wakato, n ka kõt sũ-noog ye, la sã n kaoos bilfu, dẽ poore, a sikda sẽn deeg-a wã sũurẽ laafi la sõmblem.
58012012	Dẽ yĩnga vʋʋg-y y nusa sẽn ki wã la y rũma sẽn komsã,
58012013	rems-y y soya goalma, soy niyns y sẽn tũuda goalma, la woto woabg kõn pogl n paas ye, a na paam sãoogre.
58012014	Bɩ y bao laafi ne neba fãa la sõmblem tɩ yẽ sã n ka be, ned pa tõe n yãe Soaala ye.
58012015	Gũus-y tɩ ned ba a ye ra kong Wẽnd sõngr ye; gũus-y tɩ yẽgend toaaga ra wa tob yãmb sʋk n wa ne sãoongo sẽn na n mad buuda zãng ye.
58012016	Gũus-y tɩ b ra yãend y sʋka yoaada bɩ neb sẽn ka pẽgd Wẽnd kũuna ye, wala a Ezayu sẽn dɩk a kãsengo n tek ne rɩ-yaalga.
58012017	Y bãngame tɩ rẽ poor marsã, a sẽn waa n kos a ba t'a ning-a barka, a ka paam ye, a ka tõog t'a ba yam tedge, ne a sẽn yõk sɛɛga ne nintãm.
58012018	Ad-y ka bũmb sẽn tar yaoko la yãmb paam n kolg ye. Yaa bug-witem, zĩ boogo, lika, sob-raoodo,
58012019	tõntõod bʋ-raase, koees sẽn sãte. Sẽn wʋm-b bʋʋrã ka le tulg n kelg koɛɛgã n paas ye.
58012020	B ra ka tõe n deeg sẽn togs woto wã ye: «Sẽn sɩɩs-a tãnga bɩ b lab-a ne kuga, ba a ya rũnga.»
58012021	A Moyiiz sẽn yãend bũmb sẽn yɩkd pɛlenga a woto fãa yeelame: «M yɛsa ne yɛɛsgo la rigbu.»
58012022	Sã n ya yãmba, yaa Siõ tãng la yãmb kolg yã, yaa Wẽnd vɩɩga tẽn nongre, yĩngr Zerizalɛɛm; yãmb kolga malɛk rãmb kõn-bãng-n-sõde, yãmb kẽla b tig-raag menga;
58012023	yãmb kolga neb niyns sẽn deng-b fãa n paam b yʋy gʋlsgo arzãna la y kolga Wẽnnaam, dũni bʋ-kaooda, y kolga nin-sõma sɩɩs sẽn pelg-b zãnga,
58012024	la y kolga a Zezi, d Wɛɛmba, sẽn wat ne zood paalga, ne b zɩɩm sẽn tar pekr pãnga, zɩɩm ne a koɛɛg sẽn sãt n yɩɩd a Abɛl dẽnna.
58012025	Dɩlla gũus-y n da wa zãgs sẽn gomda ne yãmbã kelegre ye. Y mi tɩ neb niyns sẽn ka kelg a Moyiiz sẽn da gomda ne bãmb tẽng zugã sã n ka põs sɩbgre, tõnd n yɩs kõn põse, tõnd sã n pa kelg sẽn gomda ne tõnd yĩngrã.
58012026	Ned ning koɛɛg sẽn tãs pĩndã tɩ tẽnga miima, yẽ soab n pʋlem tõndo n yet-do: «Bãng-y yɛsa tɩ ka tẽnga bala la m na n vik ye, yaa saaga meng marsã.»
58012027	La sẽn yeel tɩ na n le yɩɩ woto yɛsa, wilgame, tɩ bũmb niyns sẽn zoe n vigsã, na n teemame, tɩ b yaa bõn-naandse; sẽn na n kellã yaa bũmb niyns sẽn pa tõe n tedgã.
58012028	Woto wã tõnd sẽn lebg Rĩung sẽn kõn lʋɩ abada soaalba, bɩ d kell n tall Wẽnd kũuna neere n tõog n waoog-b ne waoogr sẽn tat b yam, n waoog-b ne waoogr ning sẽn tog ne Wẽnde la a wat ne gũusgu.
58012029	Tõnd Wẽnda yaa bugum sẽn dɩt n ka kẽesd bũmb ye.
58013001	Kell-y n nong-y taaba wa ba-biisi!
58013002	Da yĩm-y gãag-sobend ye tɩ yẽ n kɩt tɩ neb kẽer maan malɛk rãmb sãando n ka bãng ye.
58013003	Tẽeg-y sẽn be-b bi-bees roogẽ wala y me naagame n pag ne bãmba; tẽeg-y sẽn tar-b tooga yelle wala y me tara yĩnga.
58013004	Bɩ yikãadem paam waoogre y fãa gill nengẽ; bɩ y gãasa ra tol n dẽgem ye. Wẽnd n na n bʋ yoaadba la rataasã.
58013005	Vẽ-y ne m paoong kõn lʋɩ m to nugẽ; ges-y y sẽn tare wa bũmb sẽn seke tɩ Wẽnd meng n yeele: «M kõn daag foom n bas abada!»
58013006	Woto tõnd tõe n yeela ne sũur sẽn pa kiuusdi: «Soaala la m sõangda, bõe rabeem yɛsa, Adem biig tõe n maan-m la bõe?»
58013007	Tẽeg-y neb niyns sẽn ya-b taoor dãmba yelle, tɩ bãmb n kɩt tɩ y wʋm Wẽnnaam koɛɛga; ges-y b sẽn baas baas-neer ninga la togs-y b tẽebo.
58013008	A Zezi Krista bala n yɛse, zaamẽ, rũnna la beoog woko! B kõn tedg abada!
58013009	Da sak-y tɩ b wa tudg yã ne zãmsd sẽn ya toore la d sẽn ka mi tiir ye. Yĩngr kũuna sẽn na n keng d sũuri n são d sẽn na n keng-a ne rɩɩb niyns kẽer sẽn dɩ tɩ yõod yaool n pa zĩndã.
58013010	Tõnd tara maan-kugri, la sẽn da tʋmd-b maan-kʋʋr tʋʋmd pĩnd zãnda tẽngrã, ka tar sor n dɩ bũmb sẽn kʋ maan-kugr kãng zug ye.
58013011	Ad-y maan-kʋʋd kãsenga sã n da kood rũmsã, yaa b zɩɩma bal la a talda n kẽ pʋgẽ n kos yel-wẽna sugri; nemda meng ra yõogda bugum we-kɛɛnga.
58013012	Dẽ me la a Zezi sẽn da rat n kõ ninsaalb sõmblem ne b meng zɩɩm, bãmb me namsa we-kɛɛnga.
58013013	Dɩlla d sã n dat n bʋʋg ba bɩ d yi we-kɛɛnga la d sak n deeg yãnd wa bãmba.
58013014	Tõnd ka tar doog tẽng zug ka n na n kaoos a pʋgẽ ye; yaa beoog tẽn-noogã la d baooda.
58013015	Bɩ d tũ bãmba n kõ Wẽnnaam wakat fãa pẽgr maoongo, dat n yeelame tɩ d noor kils b yʋʋre.
58013016	Da yĩm-y taab sõngre la y paoonga lageng ye; tɩ yaa rẽ bala la maoong sẽn noom Wẽnnaam sũuri.
58013017	Sak-y yãmb kãsem-dãmba la y reeg b goama, ad-y yaa bãmb n gũud y sɩɩsã n miẽ tɩ Wẽnd na n wa sok-b lame. Woto wã, b maan b tʋʋmda ne sũ-noogo la ra yɩ ne sũ-sãang ye, tɩ rẽ ka nafd yãmb ye.
58013018	Pʋʋs-y tõnd yĩng me tɩ d me tẽedame tɩ d yaa pʋ-peen neba la d me maooda wakat fãa ne vɩɩm sõng baoobo.
58013019	M pʋs n kot-y lame tɩ y maneg n wɩng ne pʋʋsgo n paam tɩ m le wa y sʋk tao-tao.
58013020	Bɩ Wẽnd sẽn ya laafi kõata, bãmb sẽn vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka d Soaala Zezi Krista, n kɩt tɩ b lebg pe-yãansa pe-kɩɩm kãsenga, ne b zɩɩm b sẽn daag n tõog n yõg zood sẽn kõn sãam abada,
58013021	bɩ Wẽnd meng kõ yãmb sũuri tɩ y sak bãmb yam la y wɩng ne tʋʋm-sõma buud fãa, tʋʋm sẽn womd bi-sõma, sẽn noom bãmba, a Zezi Krista pãng la b maasem yĩnga; bãmb paam pẽgr sẽn kõn sɛ, marsã la daar fãa. Ami!
58013022	M saam-biisi, maam n yõkd-y sɛɛga, tɩ y reeg sagl kãensa neere; m gʋls-y la koɛɛg-koɛɛga.
58013023	Bɩ y bãng tɩ b yiisa d saam-biig a Timote roogo; a sã n paam n ta ka pĩnda, d na tũ taab n wa ges yãmb.
58013024	Pʋʋs-y kãsem dãmba la nin-sõma wã fãa. Rom dãmb tɩ b pʋʋs yãmba!
58013025	Wẽnd bark sig yãmb fãa. Ami!
59001001	Maam a Zak, Wẽnd la d Soaal a Zezi Krista sõgne, n pʋʋsd buuda sags piig la a yiiba kamba sẽn sẽeg Pa-weere!
59001002	M saam-biisi, ges-y wa sũ-noogo meng-menga, namsg ka tɛka sẽn lʋɩt y zugu.
59001003	Wala y sẽn mi, y tẽeba sã n pidi la y yɛs y zĩ-yɛnga.
59001004	Sẽn yɛs-a a zĩ-yɛng me tʋmda tʋʋmd sõngo, la yaa woto la y sõmblema na n pid zãnga, bũmb kõn pa sãoogo, bũmb kõn keoos ye.
59001005	Yãmb nin-yend sã n pa tar yam zulunga bɩ a pʋʋs n kos Wẽnd t'a na paame. – Wẽnd kõtame tɩ gale la ne yamleoogo.
59001006	Bɩ a modg n kos ne tẽebo, n ka sãmbdẽ ye; sẽn sãmbda wẽnda mogr koom, sobg sẽn zẽkd la a rãmbdẽ.
59001007	Ned a woto buud da tẽ t'a na n paama bũmb Soaala nengẽ ye,
59001008	t'a raaba teemdame, a soy wã yaa kʋʋma.
59001009	Saam-biiga sẽn yaa naong soab kɩdem t'a zug na n zẽkame;
59001010	arzɛk soaba me gũ a zug sulugri t'a na n looga wa mo-puugu.
59001011	Wĩndg puka ne a waolgo n kʋɩɩs moogo t'a puug sʋʋge, t'a neerma wẽneg n sãam. Boto me la arzɛk soab raab wagla na n sãam-a.
59001012	Zu-noog soaba la sẽn tõoga kʋɩɩbgo! A sã n tõog kʋɩɩbgo n puk a sõmblem, a paamda vɩɩm dolb ning Wẽnnaam sẽn kãab sẽn nong-b bãmba.
59001013	Kʋɩɩbg wakato bɩ ned ba a ye ra saag n yeele: yaa Wẽnd n kʋɩɩbd maam. Wẽnd pa baood wẽnga, Wẽnd pa kʋɩɩbd ned ye.
59001014	Yaa ned kam fãa raab wẽng n takd-a, n belgd-a.
59001015	Raab wẽnga sã n dɩk pʋga, yaa yel-wẽnd la a roagda, la yel-wẽnd sã n kũmd dogem, yaa kũum la a roagda.
59001016	Da kẽ-y moog ye, m neb sõma!
59001017	Kũun ning fãa sẽn be yõodo, kũun sẽn pid kũun fãa yita yĩngri soaba nengẽ; a yita d Ba ning sẽn pida ne vẽenema nengẽ. Bãmb pa mi teengo, bãmb pa mi tekre ba bilfu.
59001018	B tʋlg n doga tõnd ne b sɩd gomde, b tʋlgame tɩ d yɩ wa bõn-naandsa fãa bõn-dẽenga.
59001019	Ade, m saam-biisi, m sẽn nong wa fãa-fãa: bɩ ned kaam fãa modg n yɩ tʋʋlg ne kelgre la maasg ne leokre la sũ-fõore.
59001020	Ned sẽn basd a sũur tɩ fudgdẽ, ka maand Wẽnd sẽn dat ye.
59001021	Dẽ yĩnga zãag-y meng ne rẽgd buud fãa, ne wẽng buud fãa sẽn kell y sũurẽ, la sak-y n deeg Wẽnd Gomdã sẽn bʋd y sũurẽ n tõe n fãag y sɩɩse.
59001022	Tũ-y Gomda sẽn yet tɩ y maan a soaba. Da yɩɩ-y kelgdb bala n wa belg y mens ye!
59001023	Sẽn kelgd-a Gomdã n yaool n pa tũudĩ, wẽnda ned sẽn get a neng nin-gɛtgẽ.
59001024	A sẽn ges n loog la a sẽn wẽneg n yĩm a sẽn ya a soaba.
59001025	Ned ninga sẽn gãda la a tabend Noor ninga sẽn wata ne burkĩndlem menga, a sã n pa yĩmd-a, a sã n yik n tũud-a zãng-zãnga, yẽ soab na n yãee sũ-noogo.
59001026	Ned sã n tẽed t'a yaa Wẽnd tũud akɩka n yaool n ka loet a zelemde, a belgda a menga, la a tũudma pa tũudem ye.
59001027	Wẽnnaam d Ba wã tũudem akɩka la woto: kɩɩb bɩ la pʋg-kõap yell gesgo, la b zu-loees yolsgo n paas zãag-m-meng ne zamaana rẽgd buud fãa.
59002001	M saam-biisi, ad-y bak ned ne a to ka le tõe n zĩndi, d sã n tẽed Soaal a Zezi Krista ne pẽgr kãseng ning b sẽn paam a soaba ye.
59002002	D mak wala yãmb tigma taaba tɩ ned wa ta ne sãnem nug-bĩng a nugẽ la a yer karfo, tɩ naong soab me wẽneg n wa ne fu-kʋɩdse,
59002003	tɩ yãmb wudg n seg fu-neeba soaba, n yeel-a: «Yãmb wa zaoond ka, waoora zĩigẽ» n yaool n yeel naong saoba: «F rat bɩf yals yĩngri, f rat bɩ f zĩnd tẽng ka.»
59002004	Ka yãmb marsã n bakd ned ne a to la y tũud y tags-goalma?
59002005	Kelg-y, m saam-biisi m sẽn nong ne m sũur fãa, ka Wẽnd n tʋlg tɩ dũni wã sẽn boond tɩ naong rãmba lebg arzɛk rãmb b tẽebẽ la b lebg Arzãn Rĩunga yõod dɩtba wala Wẽnd sẽn kãab b zo-rãmba laa?
59002006	Sã n ya yãmba, yãmb pa nand naong rãmb ye! Mik-y yaa arzɛk rãmbã n namsd yãmba. Bãmb n vuud yãmb n digd bʋʋd zĩigẽ.
59002007	Bãmb n sãamd yʋ-sõng ning b sẽn pʋd yãmbã;
59002008	Bãng-y tɩ y sã n deegd noor ning b sẽn kõ yãmbã, tɩ Sebr sõng boond tɩ no-kãsenga: «Nong f to wala f menga, y maanda neere.»
59002009	La y sã n be tẽngre n bakd ned ne a to, y maanda yel-wẽnde, la y na n dɩɩ taale, tɩ y tõdgda Noorã.
59002010	Ned sã n deeg Noora zãng la bala, bũmb bilfr bal la a bas yã, ad-y yaa Noora zãng taal la a rɩ yã tɩ b na n sok-a.
59002011	Bãng-y tɩ yaa sẽn yeela: «Da rɩk f to pagã,» yẽ soab n yeele: «Da kʋ ned ye.» Fo sã n zãgs yoobo, n yaool n kʋʋda, f baas n yaa Noora tõata.
59002012	Gom-y la vɩɩnd-y wa ned sẽn ya burkĩna.
59002013	F ka zoet f to nimbãanega, b kõn zoe fo me nimbãanega n kao f bʋʋd ye; sẽn tara nimbãan-zoeere, b pa le kẽesd yẽ soab bʋʋd ye.
59002014	M saam-biisi, nin kãnga goama bee võor bi: «Ad-y m tara tẽebo,» n yaool n ka tʋʋm sõma neda; tẽeba a ye tõe n fãag-a lame bi?
59002015	Wala f saam-biiga, dao bɩ pag sã n zĩ a kãre, n ka tar fɩ n ningd a noorẽ,
59002016	tɩ yãmb nin-yend wa yeel-a: «Kul ne laafi, bao bugum n woode, rɩ n pid f pʋga» a sã n ka sõng a yĩnga ne a sẽn tar bũmb ninga tʋʋmna, a goama tara nao bi?
59002017	Tẽeba nengẽ me yaa boto. Tʋʋm-sõma sã n ka naage tẽeba yaa tẽeb kɩɩnga.
59002018	Yaa woto la d tog n gome: «Daoa, fo tara tẽebo tɩ mam ya tʋʋm-sõma neda, wilg maam f tẽeba sẽn ka naag ne tʋʋm-sõma wã, t:i sã n ya maam yaa m tʋʋm-sõma wã n pukd m tẽebo.
59002019	Fo tẽedame tɩ Wẽnnaam yaa b ye bala? F tẽeb yaa sõmbo, la bãng tɩ Sʋtãamba me tẽeda boto n baas n zĩ ne rigbu.
59002020	Yam-kaoolg soaba, f ratame n bãng tɩ tẽeb sẽn ka naag ne tʋʋm sõma yaa tẽeb faoogo?»
59002021	A Abraam, d fãa yaabã paamame t'a yell maneg ne bõe? Yaa a sẽn sak n dɩk a biig a Izaak n na n maan maoong n kõ Wẽnnaama.
59002022	Dɩlla a Abraam tẽeba ra naaga ne tʋʋm sõma la bãmb n kɩt t'a lebg sõng zãnga.
59002023	Yaa woto me la Sebr sõng gomda pid yã: a Abraam tẽe Wẽnnaam tɩ Wẽnd maneg a yelle, tɩ b na n bool-a tɩ Wẽnd zoa.
59002024	Y ne-la, yaa ne tʋʋm sõma la ninsaal paamd a yell manegre, ka ne tẽeb bal ye.
59002025	La pu-yoodr a Raab me, yaa tʋʋm-sõma n wa ne a yell manegre: a reega b sẽn tʋʋm b rãmbã la sõng-b-la ne sor a to tɩ b tũ n paam n põse.
59002026	Yaa wala yĩnga sẽn lebgd kũum sɩɩga sã n yi n bas-a. Yaa boto me ne tẽebo, tʋʋm-sõma sã n ka naage, yaa bõn-kɩɩnga.
59003001	Bɩ yãmb sʋka, sẽn dat-b n lebg karen-saam-dãmba sõor da yɩ wʋsg tɩ loog ye. Karen-saamba sẽn na n wa ne bũmb ning yaa paas d bʋʋda toolem bala.
59003002	D da yĩm tɩ d fãa gill beegdame ye. Ned sã n pa gomd n yõsda, yẽ la nin sõngo, yẽ soab tõe-la a yĩnga zãnga.
59003003	D sã n ningd salbr wiidi noore yaa sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ b mensa sak n tũ b sẽn datẽ.
59003004	Yaa boto me ne koom kogendã: b bedrema sẽn zem to-to, sobg ning sẽn tusd-ba sẽn ya to-to, yaa ne bũmb sẽn ya mɛdg bala la b soaalba tõe tɩ b kẽn tɩrga.
59003005	Zelemd me yaa bõn-mɛdga la a tõee yel-bɛda. Ya bugum sẽn paoode n yaool n tõe tɩ weooga fãa dɩ bõaga.
59003006	Zelemd yaa tõnd yĩnga wilga la a me yaa bugum n pid ne wẽnem. A rẽgemda tõnd yĩngã, a rɩta d vɩɩma zãnga la a moka a bugma bugum yiri.
59003007	Ninsaal ne a zelemda tõogame, la a ket n tõeeme n maan a sẽn dat ne we-rũmsi, bõn-yɩgdi, bõn-vuudi, koomẽ rũmsi.
59003008	Ya zelemd bal la ninsaal ka tõoge; a ka mi vʋʋs ne sãoong ye la a pida ne zẽnem sẽn ka mi sugr ye.
59003009	D sã n tar-a n pẽgd d Soaala la d Ba, d tar-a lame n tʋʋsd ninsaal sẽn tar Wẽnnaam wẽnego.
59003010	Zelemda naagame n yiisd pʋlem nood la kãab-wẽnse. Yaool n ka tog n yɩ boto ye, m saam-biisi.
59003011	Bõe ko-bunnem n naag n tãoosd zĩig a ye, ko-sõng la ko-beedo?
59003012	Kankang tõe n woma kɛgl bi: bugsuntung tõe n woma kankam bi? Yaa wa mogra ko-menesendã sẽn ka tõe n yɩ ko-noogã.
59003013	Ãnda n be yãmb sʋkã n yet t'a mi-la a menga la a mii gũusgu? A sẽn yet t'a vɩɩma yaa sõmbã, a wilg tʋʋm niyns a sẽn tʋme tɩ b kõt a tõog-m-menga la a sũ-bʋgsma kaseto.
59003014	A sũura sã n wɩka ne sũ-kiiri la zab-taasem bɩ a gũus n da wa sak wakre la zirẽ-beed ye.
59003015	Fo sã n yagd zirẽ n na n kõ f meng bʋʋm, bãng tɩ yam kãng ka yit yĩngri soaba nengẽ ye, a yaa tẽng zug yam, a yaa rũng bɩ Sʋtãan dẽnna;
59003016	Sũ-kiir la zab-taasem kedbda yɛla la b wata ne yel-wẽnde.
59003017	Fo sã n tar Yĩngr Soaba sẽn dat-f ne zʋg ningã, bɩf bao sɩd la laafi, sak n bas beegr taale, sak n yiis n kõ, sak n nong nimbãan-zoeere ne a tʋʋm sõma, sak n pʋɩ tɩ ned kam fãa reeg a rẽnna, sak vẽenem la f kisg lika.
59003018	Sẽn baood-a laafi soab pʋʋgẽ la b send sõmblem tɩɩga t'a womd biis b yĩnga.
59004001	Y sẽn be ne taab tɩ ya zab la mo-beedã, dẽ yita yɛ? Ka y zʋg wẽnga sẽn gudgd pʋgẽ wã laa?
59004002	Yãmb baoodame n yaool n ka paamnẽ ye, tɩ y yik n kʋʋda. Y neeme n data n ka soogd fɩ tɩ lebgd zaba la gãgs ne taaba. Bãng-y tɩ y sẽn pa tarã, yaa y sẽn pa kotã.
59004003	Y sẽn kot bũmb ning n pa paamnẽ wã, yaa y sẽn pa mi kosgã. Sẽn nafd y yĩnga bal la y kota.
59004004	Long rõaag, long sɩɩg kamba, yãmb pa mi tɩ zamaana nonglem yaa beem ne Wẽnd laa? Sẽn data n yɩ zamaana zoa lebgda Wẽnd bɛyã.
59004005	Y tẽedame tɩ yaa zaalem la Sebra yet woto: Wẽnd data ne raab kãsenga zʋg-sõng ning b sẽn pʋdg tõndã?
59004006	Yaa sẽn be yõod n yɩɩdã la b nong n kõtẽ, dẽ la Sebr sõng togdsda: «Wẽnd mongda b kũuna wilg-m-meng rãmba n yaool n kõta sulg-m-meng rãmba.»
59004007	Woto wã, sak-y Wẽnde la y tõdg Sʋtãana, t'a na zoe n menem.
59004008	Kolg-y Wẽnd tɩ bãmb me na yẽrg n kolg yãmba. Pek-y y nusi, yel-wẽn-maandba, pek-y y sũya, ka yɛs-b zĩ yɛng rãmba!
59004009	Ges-y y bʋkã, kelem-y kʋʋre, kɩt-y tɩ y laad lebg kũmkũm, tɩ nintãm deeg sũ-noog zĩiga.
59004010	Sulg-y mens Soaala taoore tɩ bãmb na roog yãmba.
59004011	Da wɩdi-y taab ye, m saam-biisi. Ned ninga sẽn wɩt-a a to, la a tagsd a soab wẽnga, yẽ soab wɩta Noorã la a tagsd Noora ne wẽnga. La fo sã n tasgd tɩ Noora yaa wẽnga, fo ka le ya Noora tũuda, fo lebga Noora sãbsda.
59004012	Ned ninga sẽn yiisa Noorã, yẽ soab n na kao bʋʋd Noora poorẽ. Yẽ soab n tõe n yiis bɩ a paalg bʋʋdo. Ka tõnd n na n kao taab bʋʋd ye.
59004013	Yãmb la m tat marsã, arzɛk rãmba. Y yetame: «Dũnna bɩ beoogo d na n taa Bõnd tẽnga, d na n zĩnda be yʋʋmda tõre, d na n maana leobgo n paam ligdi.»
59004014	Yãmb yaool n ka mi y vɩɩma sẽn na yɩ a soab beoog ye. Yãmb yaa waolg sẽn dukd yĩngr bilf bala n pa na n zɛ loogr ye.
59004015	Yãmb kisa y yeelẽ: «Wẽnd sã n sõnge d na vɩɩnde, d na maan woto la woto.»
59004016	La ade y basa rẽ goama n zĩi n tãoosd daoodo! Kato, wakr a woto buud fãa yaa wẽnga!
59004017	Ned ninga sẽn mi a neer maanego n ka maandẽ, a soab maanda yel-wẽnde.
59005001	Rakãagba, m le wata yãmba! Sɩng-y wiisgu la kũm-y tɩ yell n na n pak yã.
59005002	Y arzɛka põogame; y futã, zũnzuy wã zurb-b lame.
59005003	Y sãnema la y wanzurfa zoe n kẽe tẽngempiisem: ka tẽngempiisma n na n gom n sõng yãmb ye. Yẽ n na n wa rɩ y nemsã. Ad-y yaa bugum ra-giis la y tigsd n gũud beoog raara yĩnga.
59005004	Kelg-y rãamde: neb la yãmb dɩk yã tɩb wa tigs y koodo la y maana zãmbo n pa yao-b ye; ad-y yaa bãmb n kelemde la b kɛlenga sãag n lʋɩ Pãng Soaba tʋbrẽ.
59005005	«M yĩnga kõn yãe toogo, a na tɩg faongo» n yɩ yãmb vɩɩma tẽng zugu la y sɩd rɩ-la y pãngẽ, n nob wa rũng sẽn nobe, n gũud koos naaba.
59005006	Y sakame meng n paalg nin-sõng bʋʋdo la y kʋ-a lame t'a ka be pãng ye.
59005007	M saam-biisi, tõog-y meng n ta Soaala waoongo; Ges-y ka-koaada, a gũuda a tʋʋmda yõodo, n tẽed tɩ sa-koom na rʋʋg sig-noy n ta sẽooga tɛka.
59005008	Yãmb me yɩ tõog-m-meng rãmba la keng-y y sũya tɩ Soaala Waoong taame.
59005009	Da guglem-y ne taab ye, woto b kõn tags-y ne wẽng ye.
59005010	M saam-biisi, togs-y bãngdbã la ges-y-ba wa neb sẽn sak toogo, neb sẽn maan sũ-keelem Wẽnd yĩnga.
59005011	Ade tõnd meng pẽgda neb niyns sẽn ka basd-b sũ-keelem. Y pa wʋm a Zoob sũ-keelma kibare, y pa bãng Soaala sẽn da rat n puk bũmb ninga? Soaala yaa nimbãan-zoeta, Soaala kũmda b neba.
59005012	M saam-biisi, da wɩng-y ne wẽeneg ye. Da wẽen-y ne saaga, bɩ ne tẽnga bɩ ne bũmb a to ye. Y sã n tog n leok tɩ N-yẽe bɩ y yet tɩ N-yẽe! Sã n ya Ayoo, bɩ y yet tɩ Ayoo! Woto b kõn kẽes-y bʋʋd ye.
59005013	Ned sã n namsd yãmb sʋka bɩ a soab pʋʋse. Ned sã n kɩdemnẽ bɩ a pʋd yɩɩle. Ned sã n pa keeme,
59005014	bɩ a kɩt tɩ b bool Tigeng nin-kẽemsã tɩ b yals a zug n pʋʋs a yĩnga la b zɛɛ kaam, Soaala yʋʋr yĩnga.
59005015	Pʋʋsga sẽn maan ne tẽebã na n fãaga bãadã. Soaala na kɩt t'a tɩlge; a sã n maana yel-wẽnde, a na paam sugri.
59005016	Wilg-y taab y beegre fãa. Pʋʋs-y n kõ taaba tɩ y fãa paam sãoogre. Nin-sõng sã n yõk sɛɛga, wa a sẽn tõe tɛka, a tara pãnga.
59005017	A Eli da yaa ninsaal wa tõndo la a pʋʋsa ne tẽebo tɩ saag ra ni ye. La saaga ka tol n tosg tẽnga yʋʋm a tã la kiis a yoob ye.
59005018	A sẽn leb n pʋʋse, sa-koom dʋʋgame la tẽnga woma a biisi.
59005019	Ned sã n bʋdge n bas sɩd sore tɩ neda to le tall-a n wa,
59005020	yẽ soab bãnge t'a fãaga a sɩɩga kũum nugẽ la a na paam a yel-wẽn ka tɛk sugri.
60001001	Maam a Piyɛr, a Zezi Krista tʋʋm-tʋmda, n pʋʋsd Wẽnd kom-nongds sẽn vɩ-b wa sãamba la pa-weto: Põ, Galasi, Kapados, Azi la Bitini tẽnse.
60001002	Yaa Wẽnd Ba sẽn mi fãa wã n tũus yãmb al daar woko, t'a Vʋʋsem Sõng pids-y ne b kũuni, tɩ y na n pʋg a Zezi Krista la y sak tɩ b mes-y ne b meng zɩɩm. Bɩ Wẽnd nimbãan-zoeere la b laafi sig y zug zembala!
60001003	Soaala Zezi Krista Ba paam pẽgre! B nimbãan-zoeer n waooge tɩ b le kõ-d vɩm paalga, ne a Zezi Krista sẽn vʋʋg kɩɩms sʋka. Bãmb yĩng la y vɩ la y saagdẽ,
60001004	tɩ y na paam n dɩ b yõod sẽn kõn sɛ, sẽn kõn wooge menga, b sẽn bĩng yãmb b arzãnẽ.
60001005	Ad-y y tẽeba yĩnga, Wẽnd ne b pãnga segla y yĩnga fãagr sẽn na n puk a meng a toore yaoolem daarã.
60001006	Dẽ n kɩt tɩ yãmb kɩdemd sũ-noog marsã, ba y mi tɩ togame tɩ y kell n namse.
60001007	Y miime tɩ Wẽnd sã n mak yãmb ne namsgo, y tẽeba sẽn be yõodo n yɩɩd sãnem sẽn kalem dẽgdo tɩ b losda boaagẽ, y tẽeba na wa ne yãmb pẽgre la y zu-zẽkre Krista a Zezi waoong raare.
60001008	Bãmb la yãmb zɩ n yãe la y yaool n nongẽ, bãmb la y nif nan ka teege la y tẽeba kɩtame tɩ y zoe n kɩdemd y pẽgra sũ-noogo la y langdẽ.
60001009	Y miime tɩ y kõn kong y sẽn tẽedã: y sɩɩsa fãagrã ye.
60001010	Fãagr kãng poorẽ, bãngdba yõka vɛɛsgo la baoobo, bãngdb niyns sẽn gom Wẽnd sẽn bĩng-y kũun ninga yelle.
60001011	B baoome n na n bãng yaa wakat bʋgo la bõe taki la Krista Vʋʋsma b sẽn paama ra zoe n neẽ, bãmb sẽn waa n gomd Krista namsgã la pẽgr ning sẽn na n pʋgã.
60001012	Bãngdba bãngame tɩ ra ka bãmb yĩng la b ra gomd ye, b ra gomda yãmb yĩnga. Sɩd yaa ne yãmb la sẽn moond-b Koe-nooga gomda. B gomd-y-la ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng b sẽn zĩnd yĩngr n tool yãmbã; b gomdame al t'a yamleoog tar malɛgsa menga.
60001013	Dɩlla, nek-y y yam la yõk-y y mense. Maan-y saagre ne kũun ning sẽn na n sig y zutu ne Krista a Zezi Waoongo.
60001014	Wa kamb sẽn mi sakre, lak-y y yam ne pĩnd tʋls wẽns sẽn da be y sũurẽ, y sẽn waa n da ket likĩ.
60001015	La wala sẽn bool-a yãmbã sẽn ya Sõmblem naaba, y me yɩ sõma, y manesem fãa pʋgẽ,
60001016	tɩ yaa woto la b gʋlsyã: Yɩ-y sõma tɩ mam menga yaa sõngo.
60001017	Yãmb sã n boond tɩ y Ba, Wẽnd ninga sẽn ka bakd-a ninsaal ne a to, sẽn get-a ned kam fãa yel-manesem n na n kao bʋʋdo, bɩ y tall y meng ne rabeem, vɩɩm kãnga pʋgẽ t'a yaa pa-weer vɩɩm.
60001018	Bãng-y tɩ ka ne bõn-sãamdem, sãnem bɩ wanzurfu, la y paam n tɩlg vɩɩm yaalg ning y yaab rãmba sẽn kõ yãmba ye.
60001019	Yɩɩ ne zɩɩm sẽn tar yõodo, wa pe-bil sẽn ka tara toorẽ yelle, sẽn ka tar bãnd ba bilfu zɩɩm: yɩɩ ne a Zezi Krista zɩɩm.
60001020	Wẽnd n welg-b toore tɩ dũni nan ka naan ye, n yaool n puk-b marsã yãmb yĩnga.
60001021	Yaa ne Krista pãnga la yãmb tẽed Wẽnd sẽn vʋʋg b kɩɩms sʋka n kõ-b pẽgre; woto y tẽeb la y saagr bee Wẽnnaam b ye nugẽ bala.
60001022	Yãmb sẽn deeg sɩdã, yaa yãmb sɩɩs n paam sõmblem tɩ y na n nong taaba wala ba-biis bala; dɩlla bɩ y ra vʋʋs ye la nong-y taaba ne pʋ-peelem zãnga.
60001023	Sẽn le roga yãmbã ka ninsaal yĩng sẽn mi kũuma ye, yaa Wẽnd ne b gomd pãnga: bãmb n ka mi kũum, bãmb n tar vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ.
60001024	Ad-y yĩng neong yaa wa moogo: a neerma yaa wa puugu; moog kʋɩtame t'a puuda me sʋʋgdẽ.
60001025	Sã n ya Wẽnd Gomde, a bee daar fãa. Wẽnd Gomda la Koe-noog ning b sẽn taas yãmbã.
60002001	Woob-y pʋ-toog buud fãa ne zirẽ-beedo, zãmbo, sũ-kiiri, la tẽn-kãnem.
60002002	Tʋlg-y Wẽnd Gomdã wala kom-peelse sẽn tʋl bĩs-naare sẽn ka pul koom; yẽ n tõe n bɩɩs y yaoko tɩ y tʋm y fãagra tʋʋma.
60002003	La rẽ me yaa y sã n deng n lemba Soaala kũuna n mi tɩ bãmb n noom n yɩɩd fãa.
60002004	Bɩ y yẽrg n kolg bãmba tɩ bãmb la kugr vɩɩga ninsaalb sẽn daag n bas kɛɛnga tɩ Wẽnd yaool n yãk-a wa kugr sẽn tar neerem.
60002005	Yãmb me, yɩɩ-y wa kug vɩɩse la sak-y tɩ b rɩk yãmb n me Wẽnnaam doogo, tɩ b sɩng maan-kʋʋr sõng tʋʋmd a pʋgẽ n kõt Wẽnd maand sẽn ka tẽng zug rẽnna, la sẽn tat b yam, a Zezi Krista maasem yĩnga.
60002006	Ad-b sẽn gʋlse: Yaa Siõ tãng zug la m vigĩnd kuga ma, kugr m sẽn tũusi, kugr sẽn be neere la ned ninga fãa sẽn na n teeg kugr kãnga kõn yãe yãnd ye.
60002007	Yãmb tẽedba yĩnga a na wa ne y pẽgre; sã ya kɩɩsdbã, b bãng tɩ kugr ninga metba sẽn bas kɛɛngã, yẽ n lebg kuga ma,
60002008	a lebga lakr kugri, lak-n-lʋɩ pĩiga. Kɩɩsdba lakd-a lame tɩ b pa tẽ Gomda ye, la lakra la bãmb me pʋɩɩre.
60002009	La yãmba, yãmb yaa buud Wẽnd sẽn welg tore, buud sẽn paam maan-kʋʋr naam, buud sõngo Wẽnd sẽn tũus n na n kils Ned ninga sẽn yisa yãmb likĩ n kẽes-y vẽenem sẽn ka taar pʋgẽ.
60002010	Y buuda da ka buud ye la ad-y y sen lebg Wẽnd buud sõng marsã! Yãmb da ka paamd tɩ b kũm y nimbãaneg ye la ad-b sẽn zoe y nimbãanega marsã.
60002011	M sẽn nong b rãmb wa fãa fãa, maam n yõkd y sɛɛga, y sẽn ya sãamba la so-toagdba yĩnga, tɩ y zãag y mens ne y yĩnga tʋls wẽns sẽn sogd maoor ne y sɩɩgã.
60002012	Tall-y y mens neer bu-zẽmba sʋka tɩ ba b sã n wɩt yãmb wa nin-wẽnse, bɩ b yãend y tʋʋm-sõma. Rẽ n na n sõng ba tɩ b wa pẽg Wẽnnaam b waoonga raare.
60002013	Soaala yĩnga bɩ y sak tẽng zug naama ne a siglsã: sak-y dĩma sẽn ya fãa soaala,
60002014	sak-y b kombɛɛmba; b tʋʋmd yaa b sɩbg sẽn maand-b wẽnga la b pẽg sẽn maand-b neere.
60002015	Ad-y yaa Wẽnd n dat tɩ y maan neer woto, n pag gãeemsa la zɩtba noore.
60002016	Woto wã tʋm-y burkĩndlem tʋʋma. Da lʋɩɩs-y burkĩndlema taoore n dɩk menesg sor ye, yɩɩ-y Wẽnd tũudb bala.
60002017	Waoog-y neb fãa, nong-y y saam-biisi, zoe-y Wẽnde, la waoog-y dĩma.
60002018	Yãmba, zak kamba, sak-y y zu-soaben-dãmb ne rabeem menga, b tar bʋgsem, b yaa naana bɩ toose.
60002019	Ad-y yaa Wẽnd kũun la f paamyã, f sã n sak Wẽnd waoogr yĩnga n nams f sẽn ka tog n namse.
60002020	Bõe n sek pẽgre, f sã deeg toog sẽn ya f beegr sɩbgre? Sã n yaa y tʋʋm sõma yĩnga la y sakd namsgo, ad-y rẽ n be yõod Wẽnnaam nengẽ.
60002021	Mik b bool yãmb tɩ y wa namse; Krista me namsa y yĩnga n kõ y togs-n-taar n dat tɩ y pʋg bãmba.
60002022	La bãmb yaool n zɩ n maan wẽng ye – zirẽ-beed zɩ n yi b noorẽ abada.
60002023	B tʋʋs-b lame la b ka tʋʋs n lebs ye, b yãee toogo la b basa rẽ fãa ne ned ninga sẽn kaooda bʋʋd sɩda.
60002024	Pika zugu b meng tʋka d yel-wẽna, sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ tõnd me wa lebg bõn-kɩɩmse ne yel-wẽnd maanego la bõn-vɩɩse ne sõmblem baoobo. Bãmb sãmpogrã n wa ne yãmb sãoogre.
60002025	Yãmb da yaa wa pe-yãans sẽn kẽ weoogo la marsã y le leba y pe-kɩɩma la y sɩɩsa gũud nengẽ.
60003001	Yãmb me, pagba, sak-y y sɩdb-rãmba. Sɩdb-rãmba kẽer pa rat n deeg Koe-nooga ye la b pagba vɩɩm sõngã n na n tak-ba tɩ pa tũ ne b noor gomd ye.
60003002	Rẽ yaa b sã n ne tɩ y zãaga y mense ne yoob n tog ne waoogre.
60003003	Bɩ y faongã ra yɩ faong sẽn ne yɩng ye, faong sẽn baood ne zoobd pãnengo, sãnem teedo la fʋ-neeb ye.
60003004	Faongã tog n yɩɩ pʋgẽ faongo: yaa sũur sẽn ka sak wẽnga, n tar bʋgsem, n ka mi fudgr ye. Dẽ n be neer Wẽnd nifẽ.
60003005	Ya woto la pĩnd pʋg-sõma wã sẽn da tẽed-b Wẽndã ra baood b faong la b sakd b sɩdb-rãmba.
60003006	Woto la a Sara ra sakd a Abraam la a boond-a t'a zu-soaba. Yãmb me lebga yẽ kamba yãmb sã n baood neere n zĩ wɩsa n pa yɛɛsd bũmb ba a ye.
60003007	Sã n ya yãmba, sɩdb rãmba, zĩnd-y ne y pagba ne wʋm taab yam, wa ne zĩnd-n-taaga sẽn ka tar pãng wʋsg ye. Kõ y pagã a waoogr pʋɩɩre, wa neb sẽn naag taab n dɩt beoog vɩɩma yõodo. Woto bũmb kõn sãam yãmb pʋʋsg ye.
60003008	M sẽn kot bũmb zãnga, yaa y fãa yɩ yam yɛnga, ne taab kũmbu, ne taab nonglem, ne taab nimbãan-zoeere la ne yam-sulgri,
60003009	n ka lebsd wẽnga, n ka lebsd tʋʋr lɛ-lɛ. Yãmb yee n kãab noogo la y ra kãab beed ye, tɩ b welg-y la toore, sẽn na n yɩlẽ tɩ y wa rɩ pʋlemd nooga yõodo.
60003010	Sɩd me ned ninga sẽn baooda a yõore la a rat vɩɩm noogo, bɩ a paam-a, a yõk a zelemde la a vẽ ne goam wẽna la zirẽ-beedo.
60003011	A zãaga meng ne wẽnga la a maan neere, n bao laafi la a wɩng n wa paam-a.
60003012	Soaala neng togla nin-sõma la b tʋb kelgda b pʋʋsgo. Soaala nini yaool n gẽenda sẽn maand-b wẽnga.
60003013	Yell bʋg n tõe n pak yãmba, yãmb sã n baood neer ne y sũur fãa?
60003014	Ad-y y zug yaa noogo y sã n pʋs n namsdẽ y sõmblema na paas yĩnga; dɩlla da zoe-y rabeem ye la y ra bas tɩ sũur kiuus ye.
60003015	Y sẽn tog n maane, yaa waoogd Soaala, Wẽnd Nedã, y sũurẽ la rẽ tɩ y bob n yɛsame n na leok sẽn na n soka yãmbã: bõe saagr la y zĩi n saagdẽ?
60003016	Leok-y ne sũ-bʋgsem la waoog taab yam, wa neb sẽn mi tɩ b sũur ka kiuusd ye. Woto b sẽn wɩt yãmb bũmb ning poorẽ wã na n lɛɛg n pids ne yãnde neb niyns fãa sẽn sãbsd y vɩɩm sõngã, Krista tũudma pʋgẽ.
60003017	Maan neer tɩ b nams fo, Wẽnd sã n data, n são maan wẽnga n paam yĩn-maasem.
60003018	Krista meng kii vugri, yel-wẽna yĩnga. Sẽn ka tar-a yelle kii yell maandb yĩnga, sẽn na n yɩlẽ n tall-do n taas Wẽnde. B yĩngẽ wã la b lebg-bõn kɩɩnga, b sɩɩgẽ wã b kell n yɩɩ bõn vɩɩga.
60003019	B sɩɩgã n tol n taas Koe-noogã neb niyns sẽn da pag roogo.
60003020	Bãmb dãmb n zãgs tẽeb pĩnda, Wẽnd sũ-maasma wakato, a Nowe sẽn waa n kaad a koglga wakato, tɩ yaa koglg kãng pʋga la neb sẽn paoode, neb a nii bala, paam n dʋʋg kooma n põse.
60003021	Dẽ me n makd sooba sẽn fãagd yãmb me marsã. Ka yĩnga rẽgd la a pekd ye, a kɩtame tɩ ned kam fãa rɩk a menga n ko Wẽnd ne pʋ-peelem, A Zezi Krista sẽn vʋʋga yĩnga.
60003022	Bãmb n dʋ arzãna n zĩ b Ba rɩtgo la rẽ tɩ b reng n tõoga yĩngr Sõgen-kambã, yĩngr Kãsem-dãmbã, la Pãn-dãmba fãa.
60004001	Dɩlla Krista sẽn yãend toog woto, b yĩngẽ, bɩ tagsg kãnga wa kõ-y raoodo. Ned ninga sẽn yãenda toog a yĩngẽ, yẽ soab laka a meng ne yel-wẽnde;
60004002	n na n vɩɩnd tẽng zug vɩɩma marsã, wala Wẽnd sẽn date; ka na n le yɩ wa zʋg wẽnga sẽn dat ye.
60004003	Y sẽn yik pĩnd n tũ bu-zẽmba raabã, ka sek-y sɩda? Yãmb saka b yoobo, b yel-yoodo, b rã-tɩgre, b rɩ-bɛda, b yũud n pa roogdẽ, b bõn-naands waoog yoodo.
60004004	Ad-y yãmb sẽn pa le naag bãmba n dʋʋg kʋɩl ning sẽn na n dɩ-bã, b pa wʋmd a võor ye. Dẽ la b yik n tar yãmb paoogre marsã.
60004005	Mik rẽ fãa na n waa Bʋ-kaood yɛnga taoore, sẽn vɩ-b la sẽn ki-b Bʋ-kaoodã.
60004006	Ad-y yaa rẽnd yĩnga la kɩɩm-kulga meng paam tɩ b moon Koe-noogã, woto ninsaalb sẽn paalg b rãmb bʋʋd tẽng zugã tõog n paama yĩngr vɩɩma Wẽnd nengẽ.
60004007	Ad-y Dũni wã yikr kolgame; bɩ y yɩ neb sẽn tar gũusgu la y yõk y menga n tõog n pʋʋse.
60004008	Bũmb zãnga tall-y taab nonglem tɩ nonglem luta yel-wẽna.
60004009	Maan-y taab gãag-sobẽndo sẽn ka naag ne yẽgeng ye.
60004010	Bɩ ned kam fãa yik n sõnga taaba wala a sẽn paam tɛka, wala y lebga Wẽnd kũun ka tɛka pʋɩtb-a.
60004011	Ned sã n gomd bɩ a gom wa Wẽnd sẽn gomde. A sã n deeg taab sõngr tʋʋmde, a sõng wala Wẽnd n kõta noore. Woto bũmb fãa pʋgẽ Wẽnd na paam pẽgre, Krista a Zezi maasmẽ. Bãmb n so naam la ziir sẽn ka sɩng la sẽn kõn zĩnd sɛɛbo. Ami!
60004012	M kom-sõma, da yɛɛs-y bugum ninga sẽn wulumd yãmb sʋka wa bõn-lingdem ye tɩ yaa Wẽnd n dat n fɛɛs yãmba.
60004013	Y sã n naag Krista n namsdẽ bɩ y noog y sũuri tɩ b ziira pukr daare y na naag n lang la y kɩdem sũ-noogo.
60004014	Sã n ya Krista yʋʋr yĩng la b yaand yãmba, yãmb zug yaa noogo. Ad-y yaa Wẽnd Vʋʋsem ne b zɩiri, Wẽnd Vʋʋsem n sig yãmba.
60004015	Bɩ yãmb ned ba a ye ra wa namse, a sẽn ya nin-kʋʋd, bɩ wagdr, bɩ tẽn-wãad, bɩ tẽn-kãn neda yĩng lɛ-lɛ!
60004016	A sã n namsdẽ bɩ yɩ a sẽn tũud Krista yĩnga; a ra zoe yãnd ye la a pẽg Wẽnd tɩ b Yʋʋr n lebg yẽ me rẽnna.
60004017	Ad-y wakata taame tɩ bʋʋda na n sɩnge ne Wẽnnaam meng zaka neba; la sã n ya ne tõnd la bʋʋda na n sɩnge, sẽn tõdg b Wẽnnaam Koɛɛga reegrã, bãmb dãmb baasg na n yɩɩ wãna?
60004018	Nin-sõng paam n põs sã n ka naana, nin-wẽng la yel-wẽn-maand na n kẽe yɛ?
60004019	Dẽn yĩnga bɩ Wẽnd sẽn tʋlg b rãmb ne namsgo dɩk b mens n bas ne b Naanda la Sɩd Soaba la b wɩng ne neer maanego.
60005001	Ad-m koɛɛg marsã ne karen-saam-dãmba, sẽn be tõnd sʋka; mam meng yaa kãsem-soab wa bãmba la m yɩɩ Krista namsga fãa kaset soaba dẽ la m mi tɩ m na n paama bãmb pẽgre, a pukra raare.
60005002	M kotame tɩ y yɩ bãgr ninga Wẽnd sẽn gũnug yãmba pe-kɩɩmba. Gu-y piisã la ra yɩ rok-m-zug tʋʋmd ye, a yɩ yamleoog tʋʋmde wa Wẽnd sẽn date. Da yɩ rolb yooda yĩng ye, a yɩ taab sõngr yamleoog bala.
60005003	Da bao-y n dɩ naam neb zug ye. Bao-y bala n yɩ taoor dãmba sẽn wilgd piisa so-sõngo.
60005004	Wotoone, Pe-kɩɩm sõma naaba pukr daare y na reeg y pẽgr sẽn kõn sɛ pugla.
60005005	Woto me yãmba, kom-bɩɩba, reeg-y kãsem-dãmba goama; yɩ-y sulg-m-meng rãmba y taab taoore. Ad-y Wẽnd mongda wilg-m-meng rãmba n kõt yam-sulgr dãmba.
60005006	Dɩlla bɩ y sulg y mens Wẽnnaam taoore tɩ b tõog n zẽk yãmba, b raara sã n ta.
60005007	Bas-y y zu-loeesa fãa ne bãmba tɩ bãmb meng n na n ges y yelle.
60005008	Yɩ-y neb sẽn tõe b mense la maan-y gũusgu tɩ yãmb bɛyã, Sʋtãana, gilgdame n yãbd wa gɩgemde n baood a sẽn na n dɩ a soaba.
60005009	Tõdg-y Sʋtãana zãnga la y tall y tẽeb kẽnkẽ, n mi tɩ yaa namsg a woto buudu bala la saam-biisa namsd zĩig zãnga.
60005010	Y sã n paam n nams bilfu, ad-y Wẽnd sẽn ya kũuna fãa kõatã la bãmb n bool yãmb tɩ y wa rɩ vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ yõodo ne Krista a Zezi, Bãmb meng b toore n na n le yals yãmb y nao zutu la b kõ-y keelem la pãnga tɩ b mak y mimsg n konge.
60005011	B soog pãng la ziir daar fãa. Ami!
60005012	M kɩtame t'a Silvẽ gʋls-y sebr bil kãngã. Yẽ la m get wala m saam-biiga sẽn ka tol n bak ne m ye. M sagend-y lame la m wilgd-y lame tɩ kũun ning y sẽn paama, yẽ la Wẽnd kũun menga la tall-y kũun a woto buud neere.
60005013	Babilon Tigenga Wẽnd sẽn tũusi wala b sẽn tũus yãmbã tɩ b pʋʋs yãmba.
60005014	Pʋʋs-y taab ne saam-biis sẽn nong taab pʋʋsgo. Laafi zĩnd ne y fãa sẽn vɩ Krista maasmẽ!
61001001	A Zezi Krista sõgne la b tʋʋm-tʋmda, maam a Simo Piyɛr, n pʋʋsde. M pʋʋsda neb niyns fãa sẽn paam-b tɩ d Wẽnnaam la d Fãagd a Zezi Krista ko-b tẽeb sẽn be yõodo wala tõnd dẽnna.
61001002	Soaal a Zezi Krista bãngrã sudg-y bark la laafi zembala.
61001003	Wẽnd ne b pãnga kõo tõnd vɩɩnd-ne-bãmb la waoog-bãmb yamleoogo. B puka tõndo Ned ninga sẽn boola tõndo ne b pãng la b ziiri.
61001004	B kãaba tõnd kãab noodo la kãab bɛda: b kãab-d la b wẽndlema pʋɩɩre. La woto wã b zãaga tõnd ne dũni wã rẽgd la a tʋls wẽnse.
61001005	Rẽ me yĩng la y tog n modge tɩ y tẽeba naag ne vɩɩm sõngo, tɩ vɩɩm sõng naag ne bãngre,
61001006	tɩ bãngr naag ne tõog-m-menga, tɩ tõog-m-meng naag ne beoog beoog fãa modgre, tɩ modgra naag ne Wẽnd waoogre,
61001007	tɩ Wẽnd waoogr naag ne saam-biis nonglem, tɩ saam-biis nonglem naag ne Adem biig fãa nonglem.
61001008	Ade, dẽ fãa sã n beẽ, dẽ fãa sã n pida zãnga, y kõn zĩi n pa tʋmnẽ ye, n pa womd biisi sẽn ya tõnd Soaala a Zezi Krista bãngra ye.
61001009	Ned ning sẽn ka paama kũun kãensa lebgda zoanga, ned sẽn pa ne yɩɩga; sẽn yĩmd t'a paama a pĩnd dẽgda pekre.
61001010	Bɩ y le wɩng n paase, m saam-biisi, n kɩ yẽgna Wẽnd sẽn bool-y la b welg-y toora maasmẽ. Sã n ya woto rabeem ka be ne y raar a ye ye lʋɩɩs ye.
61001011	Yaa woto la b na n pids b kũuna zãnga n kẽes yãmb d Soaala la d Fãagd a Zezi Krista rĩung sẽn ka be sɛɛba pʋgẽ.
61001012	Yaa rẽ yĩng la m na n kell n tẽeg-y yell kãnga daar fãa, ba m sã n mi tɩ y ka yĩmi. Modg-y n vigl y mens sɩd kãnga pʋgẽ.
61001013	Mam tẽedame tɩ m sẽn nan ket m tẽng zug zãnda maasmẽ, segdame tɩ m sõng-y ne yell kãnga tẽegre tɩ y ra wa suus ye.
61001014	Soaal a Zezi Krista n zoe n wilg-m tɩ m mii tɩ loog n bas m zãnda wakat yaoome.
61001015	Woto wã mam me na n wɩngame, tɩ m loogr poore, bɩ yell kãensa kell n pa y pʋtẽerẽ.
61001016	Sɩd me, tõnd sẽn wilg yãmb bũmb ninga fãa, Soaal a Zezi Krista sẽn na n wa ne pãng ningã, ad-y ka solem-bãna bɩ yelbũna la d tão-y ye, yaa d sẽn deng n yãend bãmb meng ziirã ne d nifu.
61001017	Yaa Wẽnnaam Ba n kõ-b naam la waoogre. Bãmb n yiis b pãng la b naam gomd kãnga: «Ad-y yaa mam Bi-nongre, ad-y m yam kẽe-a la zãnga.»
61001018	Koe kãngã, d wʋm-a lame; a ra yita yĩngri d sẽn waa n be ne bãmba tãnga zugu.
61001019	Pʋs n yaa rẽ yĩnga la d gãd bãngdba goma sõmb-sõmbo. Y maanda neere, y sã n mams-b wala fitil bugum sẽn wɩt zĩ-sobdo n gũud beoog vẽegre la tõd-beoog ãdg pukri.
61001020	Reng-y n bãng-y tɩ bãngr gomd sẽn be sebrẽ, ninsaal ka bee n tõe, a menga toore, n wilg-a võor ye.
61001021	Bãngr gomd ka yit ninsaal sũurẽ ye; sẽn gom b rãmba goma Wẽnd zĩigẽ la ne a Vʋʋsem Sõng vẽnegre.
61002001	Neb n zĩndi buuda pʋga n yɩ zirẽ-be-bãngdba; la yãmb me sʋka zirẽ-be-neb n na n yik n yet tɩ b yaa karen-saam-dãmba; bãmb n na n wa ne welg yoodo; b na n basa Soaala sẽn fãag-bã la woto b ka na n kaoos n wã b mens ye.
61002002	Neb wʋsg na n kẽ-b lame n bʋdg moogo la b na n kɩtame tɩ sɩda sor sãame.
61002003	B sẽn dat tɩ b poorẽ yɩ yalengo, b na n yiisa goam noodo n belg yãmba, la bãng-y tɩ b bʋʋd zoe n kaoome la b wãab beoog zoe n vẽegame.
61002004	Wẽnd ka bas malɛgsa taale b yel-wẽnda poor ye. B pagb la namsg zĩigẽ la lik bog-zulungẽ tɩ b zĩ be n gũud Bʋʋda raare.
61002005	B ka bas tẽn-kʋdem wẽnnẽ dãmba taale, sã n ka neba nii, a Nowe sẽn paase, t'a Nowe n da wilgd-b tɩ b bas wẽnga. B kɩtame tɩ sa-kẽeng ni n sãam yel-maandba fãa.
61002006	B tʋlg n zãmsa yel-maandbã sẽn na n pʋga me, woto b kɩtame tɩ Sodom la Gomor tẽns rɩ bugum n sarem zãnga.
61002007	B fãaga nin-sõng a Lot t'a sũur da sãamda ne yoaadba manes wẽna;
61002008	– nin-sõnga Lot ra namsdame t'a sẽn da be bãmb sʋka, a ra neeme la a wʋmd b sẽn maand beoog beoog fãa –
61002009	Wẽnd maana boto n wilg tɩ b tõe n yolsa nin-sõma namsg buud fãa pʋgẽ n yaool n kees nin-wẽnsa n na n sɩbg-b Bʋʋda raare.
61002010	Sẽn na n paam-b sɩbgr n yɩɩda, yaa sẽn zĩb ne yoob tʋls wẽnse, sẽn tũud-b yĩnga raabo n sãbsd Ziira Naaba. Nin-wẽnsa tara wʋglem la tɩtaam; b pa zoet b na tʋʋs yĩngr dãmb mens ye.
61002011	Malɛgsa ne b sẽn yɩɩd-b ne pãng la tõogã, yaool n pa saagd n kãneg la b luk nin-bãmb bãong Soaala taoor ye.
61002012	Ad-y karen-saamb yooda wẽnda rũms sẽn ka tar yam tɩ b tɛk yaa yõk n kodg bala. Yaa bãmb n tʋʋsd-b sẽn ka mi la b me na n baasa baasg a woto buudu.
61002013	B wẽnema n wat ne b sɩbg wẽnga. Bãmb dãmb yaa m bao m sũ-noog tɩ wĩndg keta. Bãmb n dẽgem n sãam zãnga; b sũ-noog la b belg yãmba, n naagd yãmb n dɩt noodo.
61002014	B gesgo, bãng pʋg-yoodr gesgo; b sẽn pa tɩgd wẽngã, b kẽesda wẽng yamleoog sẽn pa tar-b pãnga sũurẽ; Wẽnd sẽn yãk b barkã, raab wagl bal n pid-ba!
61002015	B basa so tirg n kẽ weoog n menem wala a Balaam, a Bosor biiga, zãmb ligd yamleoog sẽn yõke.
61002016	Rẽ me n wa ne a kʋɩdgre, tɩ rũng sẽn ya mugtãa n yaag a noor n gom wa ninsaala n kiis bãngd kãng gãeemdo.
61002017	B sɩd yaa wa bul-kẽoodo, wa sob raoog sawadgo; b zĩig pida ne lik la lik bala.
61002018	Gom faad la b mi. Ne b tʋls wẽns la b yoob tʋʋma, b takda sẽn nan ka paam-b n zãag ne b pipi tudgrã.
61002019	B kãabda b taab soog-m-menga, la b mens balgame n zĩi ne wẽng yembdo. La sɩda bũmb sã n yɩɩd f ne pãnga, fo lebga bõn kãng yamba.
61002020	Neb sã n zoe n zãag ne zamaana rẽgdo, b sẽn bãng Soaala la Fãagd a Zezi Krista yĩnga la b lɛɛg n le lʋɩt a pʋgẽ, tɩ wẽnga le tõog-ba, ka bãmb yell n sãam n yɩɩd pĩnd sɩda?
61002021	B sã n da ka bãngẽ sõmblema sore n são b sẽn bãng la b baas n kɩɩs b sẽn taas-b no-sõng ningã.
61002022	Yaa woto la b yella lebg sɩda wa yelbũn kãnga: bãaga lɛɛg n vela a meng wʋbdo; bɩ wa b sẽn togs yɛsa: Kurkur yãanga, ka yãe n pek koom n lebd a begdẽ.
61003001	Yãmb ne la, m kom-sõma, ka wã la sebr a yiib soaba m sẽn gʋls yã? La yiiba fãa pʋgẽ, m maoome n yalg y pʋtẽer la m kõ-y bãngr sõngo.
61003002	Tẽeg-y bãngdb sõma sẽn wilgi la noor ning Tʋʋm-tʋmdba sẽn kõ yãmba, tɩ yaa d Soaala la d Fãagda meng noore.
61003003	Bɩ y bãng tɩ yaoolem wakatã neb sẽn nong b taab laado, neb sẽn mi b tab yaalgo n na n tũ b zʋg wẽngã n la yãmba.
