61003004	B na n saadame n maanẽ: «Ye! Soaala sẽn kãab tɩ b na n lɛɛg n waame wã bɛɛ? Yaab rãmba sẽn ki raar zãra, la fãa ket n yaa wa dũni wã sɩngrẽ.»
61003005	Ad-y b maanda wala b ka mi tɩ wakat n zĩndi tɩ Wẽnd gome tɩ saaga la tẽnga zĩndi; tɩ Wẽnd gome tɩ tẽnga sẽn da lis koomẽ wa n nug n yi;
61003006	tɩ Wẽnd gome tɩ koom dɩ wakat kãng dũniya.
61003007	Ad-y rũnna saagã la rũnna tẽngã, Wẽnd Gomd yɛnga bas-b la kɛɛnga, b bas-b-la bugum yĩnga, Bʋʋda raare la nin-wẽnsa wãab raare.
61003008	La bũmb n be, m kom-sõma tɩ y ka tog n yĩm ye: Soaala nengẽ daar a ye zema tusri la yʋʋm tusri me ka yɩɩd daar a ye ye.
61003009	Ad-y Soaala ka tadg b kãabga pidsgu, wala neb kẽer sẽn wɩt-ba n yet tɩ b pa yãgda ye. Yaa sũ-maasem la b maand ne yãmba, tɩ b sẽn datã ka ned ba a ye menengo, yaa b fãa paam vɩʋʋg n tuub b yel-wẽna.
61003010	Soaala daar yaool n na n tĩiga wa wagdre. Badaare yĩngr teeda fãa na n bõra zãnga, bõn-witi wã fãa na n yẽnegame la tẽnga ne a teeda fãa na n dɩɩ bugum kasi.
61003011	Bũmba fãa sẽn na n sʋʋgã, y zɩ marsã tɩ y tʋʋmd yaa vɩɩm sõngo la pʋʋsgo.
61003012	Yaa y segl n gũudĩ la y rabsd Soaala raare; baraare, saaga ne a bõn-yoodã na n wulumda ne bugum n sʋʋge, tɩ bõn-witsa fãa yẽneg n dʋʋge.
61003013	Ad-y yaa sa paalle la tẽn paalle la tõnd gũuda, wala b meng sẽn kãabe, la sõmblem n na n ti roog b pʋgẽ.
61003014	Woto wã, m kom-sõma, wɩng-y marsã ne y sũur fãa n yɩ sõma, la y rok yell buud fãa y zug tɩ b wa mik tɩ y sũur pida ne laafi.
61003015	Tags-y tɩ Soaala sũ-maasma ne yãmb yaa y sõngr yĩnga, wala d sam-biiga Pol me sẽn gʋls n togs-y ne yam ning Wẽnd sẽn kõ-a.
61003016	A sɩd wilgda rẽ ne sɛb niyns fãa a sẽn gʋls yãmbã. Zĩis kẽer meng wʋmb yaa toog tɩ zɩtba la yam yaals rãmb dat n lebg-b tulumdi – wa b sẽn nong n maan ne Sebr sõngo – la rẽ yaa b meng bõne la b baooda.
61003017	Sã n ya yãmba, m kom-sõma, y sẽn mi tiirã, bɩ y maan gũsgu. Da bas-y tɩ nin-yood wa tudg-y la b koms y pãng ye.
61003018	Yãmb wee n tar bɩʋʋng bal ne sõmblem la ne Krista a Zezi, d Soaala la d Fãagda bãngre. B pʋs n soog pẽgre, marsã n digd wakat sẽn kõn zĩnd sɛɛbo. Amina!
62001001	Yaa Gomd ning sẽn wata ne vɩɩma yell la d gʋlsd-y. Gomd kãng la sẽn dag n be-a al dũni sɩngrẽ, tõnd tʋbr wʋma b yelle, tɩ d nif yãend-ba, d paam n ges-b lame n tɩge, d nus sɩɩs-b lame,
62001002	– Vɩɩma sɩd pukame, tɩ d yãend-a la d kõt kaseto; Vɩɩm kãng ka be sɛɛb ye, tɩ d wat n na n wilg-a yãmba, a ra sɩng n bee ne Ba n yaool n wa lik a meng tõndo –
62001003	d sẽn yãend la d sẽn wʋme la d wilgd yãmba, tɩ yãmb me wa lagem ne tõndo. Tõnd sẽn lagem ne b rãmbã, yaa Wẽnnaam Ba la b Biig a Zezi Krista.
62001004	Yaa rẽ la d gʋlsd-y tɩ y sũ-nooga pid zãnga.
62001005	Ad-d sẽn wʋm b nengẽ n wat n na n wilg yã: Wẽnd yaa vẽenem, lik ka be b nengẽ ye.
62001006	Tõnd sã n kẽnd likẽ, n yaool n yet tɩ d lagma ne bãmba, d yagda zirẽ, d pa togsd sɩd ye.
62001007	La sã n yaa vẽenemẽ la tõnd kẽnda, b meng sẽn be vẽenemẽ wã, bãmb n lagemd tõnd ne taaba, la b Biiga Zezi zɩɩma n pekd tõnd yel-wẽnd buud fãa.
62001008	Tõnd sã n yeele: «D ka tar yel-wẽnd ye», d belgda d mense, sɩd ka be d pʋgẽ ye.
62001009	Tõnd sã n wilg d yel-wẽna, bãmb sẽn pidsd b kãabgo la b ya zemsg soaba, bãmb na n kõo d yel-wẽna sugri la b pek-do ne rẽgd buud fãa.
62001010	Tõnd sã n yeele: «D ka tar yel-wẽnd ye», tõnd kɩtdame tɩ b lebg zirẽ-be-neda la b Gomda ka na n pa ne d ye.
62002001	M kom-bõonego, m gʋlsd-y la woto tɩ y zãag ne yel-wẽnde. La ned sã n wa maan yel-wẽnde, bɩ a tẽeg tɩ d tara Wɛɛmba d Ba sɛɛgẽ: nin-sõng a Zezi Krista.
62002002	Yaa b maoongã n dond d yel-wẽna samde, la ka tõnd dẽnna bal ye, yaa dũni wã fãa yel-wẽna.
62002003	Ad bũmb ning sẽn wilgd tõndo tɩ d mi-b lame: b noya reegre.
62002004	Ned ninga sẽn yeela: « M mi-b lame» n yaool n ka reegd b noya, yẽ soab yaa zirẽ-be-neda, la a soab ka tar sɩd a pʋgẽ ye.
62002005	Ned ninga sẽn deegda b Gomdã, yaa yẽ soab pʋgẽ la Wẽnd nonglma paam n pid zãnga. Yaa rẽ n na n kɩt tɩ d bãng tɩ d lagma ne Bãmba.
62002006	Ned ninga sẽn yet t'a lagma ne bãmba, yẽ soab tog n vɩɩnda bãmb meng vɩɩm.
62002007	M kom-nongdse, ka no-paalle la m kõt-y ye, yaa no-kʋdgo, no-kãng la y paam al sɩngrẽ. No-kãng yaa koɛɛg ning y sẽn wʋma.
62002008	La m baas n le paasdame tɩ yaa no-paalle la m kõt yãmba, – la rẽ yaa sɩd ne yãmba, la ne Krista – tɩ lik wɩlgdame tɩ vẽenema meng zoe n yãgda.
62002009	Sẽn gomd-a t'a bee vẽenemẽ n yaool n ket n kis a saam-biiga, ket n bee likẽ.
62002010	Sẽn nong-a a saam-biig paada vẽenemẽ la bũmb ka bee n na n tus-a n lub ye.
62002011	Sẽn kis-a a saam-biig bee likẽ, a kẽnda likẽ, a ka mi a sẽn dabdẽ ye tɩ lika kiisa a nina.
62002012	Yaa yãmb la m gʋlsda, m kamba, tɩ y paama y yel-wẽna sugr, bãmb yʋʋr yĩnga.
62002013	M gʋlsd-y lame, ba rãmba, tɩ y paam n bãnga sẽn be-a al sɩngrẽ. M gʋlsd-y lame, kom-bɩɩba, tɩ y tõoga wẽnema naaba.
62002014	M gʋlsd-y lame, kom-bõonego, tɩ y mii Ba. M gʋls-y lame, ba rãmba, tɩ y mii sẽn be-a al sɩngrẽ. M gʋls-y lame, kom-bɩɩba, tɩ y tara pãnga, tɩ Wẽnd Gomda be-la y pʋgẽ, la yãmb tõoga Wẽnema naaba.
62002015	Da nong-y dũnia bɩ sẽn be a pʋgẽ ye. Ned sã n nong dũnia, a ka le nong Ba ye.
62002016	Sẽn be dũnia pʋga, – sẽn noom yĩngã, nina sẽn ne n tʋlla, arzɛk ne a sẽn dogd a soaba: wilg-m-menga – rẽ fãa ka yit Ba wã nengẽ ye, b yita zamaana pʋga.
62002017	Zamaana yaool n loogdame, ne a tʋls wẽnsã, la ned ninga sẽn maanda Wẽnnaam yam, yẽ soab paada daar fãa.
62002018	M kom-bõonego, yaoolem wakata taame, y wʋmame tɩ Krista bɛ n na n wa, ad-y yaa bãmb wʋsg meng n zoe n wa, la rẽ n wilgd tɩ yaoolem wakata taame.
62002019	Bɛɛba yii tõnd sʋk waare, la b ka tõnd neb ye. B sã n dag n yaẽ tõnd neba, b naan n paẽ ne tõndo. Da tog n wa vẽnegame tɩ b ra pa tõnd neb ye.
62002020	Sã n ya yãmba, yãmb paamame tɩ Wẽnd Neda taag y kaam la y lebga neb sẽn pid ne bãngre.
62002021	M gʋls-y lame, la ka wala y ka mi sɩd ye, ya y sẽn mi-a wã yĩnga, yaa y sẽn mi tɩ zirẽ-beed ka yit sɩd pʋgẽ wã.
62002022	Zirẽ-be-neda la ãndã, sã n ka sẽn kɩɩsda t'a Zezi la Wẽnd Nedã? Ad-y Krista bɛ la yẽ soaba! A kɩɩsda Ba la Biiga.
62002023	Sẽn ka mi-a Biiga fãa ka Ba wã ned ye. Sẽn tẽed-a Biigã yẽ soab bee ne Ba.
62002024	Sã n ya yãmba, modg-y tɩ y sẽn wʋm bũmb ning sɩngrẽ wã ra yi yãmb pʋtẽerẽ ye. Zãmsg ning y sẽn paam sɩngrẽ wã sã n pa-y y pʋtẽerẽ, yãmb me na lagem ne Biig la Ba.
62002025	B sẽn kãab yãmb bũmb ninga la woto: vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ.
62002026	Yaa rẽ me la m tʋlg n gʋlsyã sẽn dat-b n tudg yãmbã poorẽ.
62002027	Sã n ya yãmba, y ket n taaga Wẽnd Neda kaam la y pa le tar zãmsg tʋʋmd ye. La b meng sẽn zãmsd yãmb bũmb fãa wã n dat sɩda la b kis zirẽ-beedã, pa-y ne-ba, wa b sẽn wilgã.
62002028	N ye! M kom-bõonego, pa-y ne bãmba woto b sã n wa lik b menga d kõn sãmb ye la yãnd kõn yõk-do, wala d paam n zãaga ne bãmba b Waoonga raar ye.
62002029	Y sã n deeg tɩ b yaa sõngo, bɩ y bãng tɩ ned ning fãa sẽn baood sõmblem yita bãmb nengẽ.
62003001	Ges-y Ba sẽn wilg nonglem ning ne tõnd al tɩ d tõe n bool tɩ Wẽnnaam kamba, la d sɩd yaa Wẽnnaam kamba! Zamaana rãmb sã n ka mi tõndo, yaa b sẽn ka reng n bãng Krista.
62003002	M kom-nongdse, tõnd zoe n yaa Wẽnnaam kamba, yaa sẽn pʋgda bal la b nan ka wilg-du. D miime bala tɩ b Waoonga raare, d na n wẽnega bãmba, tɩ d na n yãend-b lame wa b sẽn ya-la.
62003003	Ned ning fãa sẽn teega bãmba, lebgda yɩlgemd wa Krista sẽn ya yɩlgemdã.
62003004	Sẽn maand-a yel-wẽnd maanda sẽn kisi, tɩ yaa maan sẽn kis la yel-wẽnde.
62003005	Y yaool n wʋmame tɩ b sẽn wa dũnia b waame n na n yẽes yel-wẽnde la bãmb meng ka maan yel-wẽnd ye.
62003006	Sẽn paada ne bãmb ka maand yel-wẽnd ye. Sẽn maanda yel-wẽnd ka yãend-b ye la a ka mi-b ye.
62003007	M kom-bõonego, da bas-y tɩ ned tudg-y ye. Sẽn maand-a neer yaa nin-sõngo wa Krista sẽn ya nin-sõngo.
62003008	Sẽn maand-a yel-wẽnde kẽe Sʋtãana tɩ Sʋtãan yaa yel-maand al sɩngrẽ. Yaa Sʋtãana tʋʋm yooda menesg yĩnga la Wẽnd Biiga wa yã.
62003009	Wẽnd sẽn dog a soab ka maand yel-wẽnde, tɩ yẽ soab tara b zʋgo; woto wã a ka tõe n maan wẽnga, Wẽnd sẽn dog-a wã yĩnga.
62003010	Ad bũmb ning sẽn bakd Wẽnnaam kamba la Sʋtãan kamba: sẽn ka maanda neere ka Wẽnd biig ye, wala sẽn kis-a a saam-biig me sẽn ka Wẽnd Biigã.
62003011	Ad koɛɛg ning y sẽn wʋm sɩngrẽ: d tog n nonga taaba.
62003012	D da saag n wẽneg a Kayẽ sẽn kẽ Wẽnema soab tãpẽ n kodg a yao wã ye. La a kodg-a la bõe yĩnga? Yaa a meng tʋʋm sẽn da ya tʋʋm yoodo, t'a yao wã rẽnd ya sõma.
62003013	Da yɛɛs-y ye, m saam-biisi, zamaana rãmb sã n kis-y ye.
62003014	Tõnd yẽ miime tɩ d yii kũumẽ n kẽ vɩɩmẽ, la rẽ yaa d sã n nong d saam-biisã.
62003015	Sẽn ka nong-a a saam-biig fãa yaa nin-kʋʋda; la y mi tɩ nin-kʋʋd ba a ye ka tar vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ ye.
62003016	Ad bũmb ning sẽn puk b nonglem: Bãmb dɩka b vɩɩm n kõ tõndo, la woto tõnd me tog n kõ d vɩɩm d saam-biisa yĩnga.
62003017	Ned sã n tar tẽng zug arzɛka n ne a saam-biig zu-loɛɛga la a maand wa a ka ne, Wẽnd nonglma yɩta a wãn n pa ne yẽ soaba?
62003018	M kom-bõonego, d nonglma ra yɩ bʋʋre la gom nood ye, nonglma yɩ sɩda, a tũ ne tʋʋmde.
62003019	Yaa rẽ n na wilg tɩ d bee sɩd pʋgẽ tɩ d sũur me gãe ne laafi,
62003020	ba d sũura sã da ratẽ lame n ning-d taale, tɩ Wẽnd yɩɩd-a lame, la b mii fãa.
62003021	M kom-nongdse, d sũur koɛɛg sã n ka ningd-d taale d zĩi ne sũ-keelem Wẽnd taoore.
62003022	D sẽn kos b bũmb ning fãa d paamd-a la bãmb nengẽ, d sẽn deegd b noe wã, la d maand sẽn tat b yama yĩnga.
62003023	B noora la woto: d tẽ b Biig a Zezi Krista yʋʋr yĩnga, la d nong taaba wala b sẽn zoe n togsã.
62003024	Sẽn deegda noor paada ne Wẽnd tɩ Wẽnd me paad ne a soaba; ad bũmb ning sẽn wilgd tõnd tɩ b bee ne do: yaa b Vʋʋsma b sẽn kõ tõndã.
62004001	M kom-nongdse, maan-y gũusgu ne neb kẽere, bãng-y b yama sã n sɩd yaa Vʋʋsem Sõng rẽnna, la tẽeg-y tɩ zirẽ-be-bãngdb ka tɛk n wa moogo.
62004002	Ad bũmb ning sẽn wilgd b bãngra sã n yita Wẽnd nengẽ: yaa reeg t'a Zezi Krista waa tẽng zugu ne ninsaal yĩnga.
62004003	Ned ning fãa sẽn kɩɩsd a Zezi, yẽ soab ka yit Wẽnnaam nengẽ ye; yẽ soab tara Krista bɛ wã yam. Yãmb wʋma b sẽn yeele tɩ bɛ wã na n waame, ade, marsã a zoe bee dũniya.
62004004	Yãmba kom-bõonego, yãmb yaa Wẽnnaam kamba, la yãmb n maan raoodo ne bɛɛbã. Yãmb sẽn tũuda soabã yɩɩda sẽn be-a dũni wã pʋgã.
62004005	Krista bɛɛba la zamaana rãmba; yaa rẽ me yĩng la b gomd wa zamaana rãmba tɩ zamaana rãmb kelgd-b.
62004006	Tõnd yẽ yaa Wẽnd soolem. Sẽn mi Wẽnd kelgda tõndo; sẽn ka mi Wẽnd ka kelgd tõnd ye; la wotome la d bakd sɩda ne zirẽ-beedo.
62004007	M kom-nongdse d nong taaba, tɩ nonglem yita Wẽnd nengẽ la ned ning fãa sẽn tar nonglem, yaa Wẽnd biiga, la a mii Wẽnde.
62004008	Sẽn ka tara nonglem ka bãng Wẽnd ye, tɩ Wẽnd yaa nonglem.
62004009	Ad Wẽnd sẽn puk b nonglma toto ne tõndo: Wẽnd tʋma b Bi-yenda tẽng zugu sẽn na n yɩla tɩ d paam vɩɩm bãmb nengẽ.
62004010	B nonglma sẽn tũ sor ninga la woto: ka tõnd n deng Wẽnnaam nonglem ye, bãmb n deng tõnd nonglem n tʋm b Biiga tõnd sʋka tɩ b wa ki d yel-wẽna yẽesg yĩnga.
62004011	M kom-nongdse, Wẽnd sã n nong tõnda woto segdame tɩ tõnd me nong taaba.
62004012	Ned nif zɩ n yãend Wẽnd ye. Tõnd sã n nong taaba Wẽnd bee ne do, b nonglma pida zãng ne tõndo.
62004013	Bũmb ning sẽn wilgd tɩ Wẽnd bee ne do tɩ tõnd me be ne bãmba: yaa b sẽn sudg tõnd b Vʋʋsem.
62004014	Sã n ya tõndo, d yãendame la d kõta kaseto tɩ Ba tʋma b Biiga, wala dũniya Fãagda.
62004015	Ned ning sẽn tẽed tɩ Krista yaa Wẽnnaam Biiga, Wẽnd bee ne yẽ soaba la yẽ soab me bee ne Wẽnde.
62004016	Sã n ya tõndo, tõnd bãnga Wẽnd nonglma ne tõndo la d tẽeme. Wẽnd yaa nonglem. Sẽn pida ne nonglem paada ne Wẽnd tɩ Wẽnd me paad ne yẽ soaba.
62004017	Nonglem pidsda a tʋʋmd zãng d pʋgẽ a sã n tõog tɩ d pa yɛɛsd Bʋʋda raare. A Zezi sẽn pa yɛɛsd bũmbã, tõnd me yaa boto dũni kãnga pʋga.
62004018	Nonglem ka naagd ne rabeem ye, nonglem sẽn pid zãagda rabeem buud fãa; sɩbgr la f yãeta n digd rabeem; dɩlla sẽn digda rabeem, ka tar nonglem pidung ye.
62004019	Sã n ya tõndo, d nong bãmba, tɩ bãmb n yɩ pipi n nong tõndo.
62004020	Ned sã n yeele: «M nonga Wẽnde» n yaool n kis a to, yẽ soab yagda ziri. Ade, f sã n ka nong f saam-biig f sẽn ne ne f nini, f yɩta wãn n nong Wẽnnaam f nif sẽn ka tõe n yãende.
62004021	D sẽn paam noor ning b nengẽ wã la woto: Sẽn nonga Wẽnd bɩ a nonga saam-biiga.
62005001	Ned ning sẽn tẽeda t'a Zezi yaa Krista yẽ soab dɩta rogem ne Wẽnde. La f sã n nong ned ba f nonga a sẽn dog biig ninga.
62005002	D bãngdame tɩ d nonga Wẽnnaam kamba d sã n nong Wẽnd menga n deegd b noore.
62005003	Wẽnd nonglma yaa bãmb noya reegre la noy wã ka zɩs ye,
62005004	tɩ Wẽnd sẽn dog a soab tõoga dũnia la ad-d sẽn tõog dũnia ne bũmb ningã, yaa d tẽebã.
62005005	Ãnda la sẽn tõoga dũniya, sã n ka sẽn tẽeda t'a Zezi Krista yaa Wẽnd Biiga?
62005006	Ya a Zezi Krista n wa ne koom la zɩɩm, la ka ne koom bal ye, yaa ne koom la zɩɩm. A Vʋʋsem Sõng n kõt kaseto, la Vʋʋsem Sõng kaset yaa sɩda.
62005007	Woto, kaseta rãmb yaa b tãabo:
62005008	a Vʋʋsem Sõngo n paas koom la zɩɩm, la b kaseta ka kɩɩsd taab ye.
62005009	D sã n deegd ninsaalb kaseto, Wẽnd dẽnd n yɩɩde. La yaool n yaa Wẽnd kaseta la d paam b Biiga poorẽ.
62005010	Ned ninga sẽn tẽed Wẽnd Biiga yẽ soab reegda kaset kãnga. Sẽn ka tẽed-a Wẽnde, geta bãmb wa zirẽ-be-neda, b pa tẽ kaset ning b sẽn kõ b Biiga ye.
62005011	La kaset kãng la woto: Wẽnd kõo tõnd vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ la vɩɩm kãng be b Biiga nengẽ.
62005012	Sẽn tara Wẽnd Biiga tara vɩɩm; sẽn ka tara Wẽnd Biiga ka tar vɩɩm ye.
62005013	Yaa yãmb sẽn tẽed Wẽnd Biiga yʋʋrã la m gʋls woto, tɩ y bãng tɩ y paama vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ.
62005014	D sũur kegma ne Wẽnde n mi tɩ d sã n kos b bũmbu wala b sẽn date, b kelgd-d lame.
62005015	D sã n mi tɩ Wẽnd kelgda, d kosg bud fãa, d miime tɩ d na paam d sẽn kos b bũmb ningã.
62005016	Ned sã n yãend a saam-biig t'a maand yel-wẽnde sẽn ka wat ne a kũum, a pʋʋse la Wẽnd na kõ saam-bi-kãng vɩɩm. Ka gomd neb niyns yel-wẽnd sẽn wat ne b kũuma ye, tɩ yel-wẽnd n be n wat ne kũum la ka yell kãng yĩng la m yet tɩ b tog n pʋsame ye.
62005017	Maan sẽn kis fãa yaa yel-wẽnde la yɛl kẽer n be n wat ne kũum.
62005018	D miime tɩ Wẽnd sẽn dog a soab fãa ka maand yel-wẽnd ye, tɩ Wẽnd Biig gũuda yẽ soaba la woto Wẽnema soab ka tar a gaab ye.
62005019	D miime tɩ Wẽnd n so tõndo, tɩ dũni wã tõr yaool n gãe Wẽnema soab soolmẽ.
62005020	D miime tɩ Wẽnd Biiga waame la b kõ-d la yam tɩ d tõog n bãng Sɩd soaba. Tõnd lagma ne Sɩdã soaba, ne b Biig a Zezi Krista. Bãmb la Wẽnd, Sɩd soabã, bãmb la vɩɩm sẽn ka be sɛɛbo.
62005021	M kamba, da saag-y n waoog wẽn-naandsa ye.
63001001	Yaa maam, nin-kẽema, n pʋʋsd Tigengu, m Pʋg sõngã, ne a kambã m sẽn nong ne nonglem menga, la ka maam bala n pʋʋsde, yaa neb niyns fãa sẽn bãng-b sɩdã.
63001002	Sɩd kãng yẽne pʋgẽ la d be la d na n kell n pa, n tãag vɩɩm sẽn ka be sɛɛbo.
63001003	D datame tɩ y kell n pid ne sõmblem, ne nimbãan-zoeere la laafi ning sẽn yit Wẽnnaam Ba nengẽ la a yit a Zezi Krista nengẽ, bãmb Biig, sẽn tar sɩda la nonglem.
63001004	M sũur yɩɩ noogo wʋsgo m sẽn yãend f kamb kẽer sẽn tũud sɩd wa Wẽnd Ba sẽn kõ-d noor ningã.
63001005	La marsã Pʋg sõngo, ad ka no paalg la m kõt-f ye, ayoo! Yaa noor ning d sẽn paam al sɩngrẽ, yaa nong taab noorã.
63001006	D nonglem ne Wẽnd yaa d deeg b noya. La y sẽn paam noor ning al sɩngrẽ wã yaa y vɩɩnd ne taaba, nonglem pʋgẽ.
63001007	Neb n yik zembala n tuut-b taaba n kɩɩsd t'a Zezi Krista lebga Neda: bãmb la Sʋtãana, bãmb la a Zezi Bɛ wã.
63001008	Bɩ y gũus tɩ y tʋʋma ra lebg tʋʋm faad ye, mao-y n dɩ b yõod pidingu.
63001009	Ned ning fãa sẽn yet t'a mii zãnga n yaool n basd a Zezi Krista zãmsgã, yẽ soab ka be ne Wẽnnaam ye. Sẽn gãda Krista zãmsgã n be ne Wẽnnaam Ba la b Biiga.
63001010	Ned sã n wat y nengẽ, n ka tar a Zezi zãmsgã, bɩ y ra reeg a soab y yir ye, da pʋʋs ned a woto buud ye.
63001011	Sẽn pʋʋs-a naag-a la a tʋʋm wẽngẽ.
63001012	M da rat n togs-y la koees wʋsgo la m pa tʋlg tɩ yɩ ne sebr ye tɩ m saagda m na paam n wa y nengẽ; m sã n wa, m na paam n togs-y rẽ fãa ne noore, tɩ d sũ-nooga pid zãnga.
63001013	Tigengã, f Tão sõnga kamb tɩ b pʋʋs-fo.
64001001	Yaa maam, nin-kẽema, n pʋsd a Gayus m sẽn nong ne nonglem menga.
64001002	M kotame, m zoa sõngo, tɩ Wẽnd kõ-f laafi zãnga, f yĩng la f sɩɩg laafi.
64001003	Kristneb n wa ka la b kõo f kaseto tɩ f vɩɩma tũuda tɩrga, m gomda a sẽn ka lak ne sõmblem la sɩd sorã, ad-m sũur yɩɩ noog al wʋsgo.
64001004	Ade, bũmb ka be n noogd m sũuri n yɩɩd m sẽn wʋmd tɩ m kamba tũuda sɩda sora ye.
64001005	M zoa nongre, f sɩd rɩka f meng zãng n kõ kristnebã ba b sã n ya bu-zẽmba.
64001006	B fãa pẽga f nonglma Tigenga taoore. Fo me na maan neere n sõng-b ne b so-toaka rɩɩbo wala Wẽnd sẽn date.
64001007	Yaa Krista yʋʋr yĩng bala la b rɩk sore n pa sak n deeg bũmb bu-zẽmba nengẽ ye.
64001008	D tog n deega neba woto buudu tɩ woto la d naagd-b n tʋm sɩda wilgr tʋʋmde.
64001009	M da paam n gʋlsa sebr n kõ Tigengã. La a Diotrefɛs, ned sẽn pid ne tɩtaam la a baood n na n yɩ taoor soaba, pa sak n deeg-d ye.
64001010	Woto wã, m sã n ta be m na tẽeg a sẽn maan fãa, n paas gom-beed niyns fãa a sẽn yelg tõnd poorẽ. Rẽ pa sek-a ye, t'a zãgs t'a meng kõn deeg saam-biisa sãando, la a gɩdgd sẽn dat-b n deeg-bã, n tol n yiisd-b Tigengu pʋgẽ.
64001011	M bi-nongre, da togs sẽn maand-a wẽng ye, togs sẽn maand-a neere. Sẽn maanda neer bee Wẽnd maasmẽ. Sẽn maanda wẽng ka mi Wẽnd ye.
64001012	A Demetriyus poorẽ neba fãa kõta kaset sõngo; Sɩd soaba meng naag n kõta kaseto. Mam meng kõta kaseto la fo mi tɩ m kaset yaa sɩda.
64001013	M da rat n togs-f la koees wʋsgo, la m pa tʋlg tɩ yɩ ne ribl bẽesgo, ribl ne gʋlsg sabl ye.
64001014	M saagdame tɩ m kõn kaoos n yãend-f ye; woto d na paam n sõs ne taaba.
64001015	Laafi zĩnd ne fo! F zo-rãmba fãa tɩ b pʋʋs-fo; fo me pʋʋs d zo-rãmbã n kõ-do; pʋʋs-ba a yeyn-ye, ned kam fãa ne a yʋʋre.
65001001	Maam a Zɩɩd, Krista a Zezi sõgne, a Zak saam-biiga, n pʋʋsd Wẽnd Ba sẽn nong b rãmbã, n bool-b la b bĩng-b toore Krista yĩnga.
65001002	Bɩ y paam zembala, Wẽnd nimbãan-zoeere, b laafi la b nonglem!
65001003	M kom-nongdse, m da tʋlla wʋsgo n gʋls yãmb bũmb a ye poorẽ, d fãa sẽn paam fãagra poorẽ. Waa n lebga pakre ne-ma tɩ m gʋlse n segl-y tɩ y zab tẽeba yĩnga, tẽeb ning nin-sõma wã sẽn deege la sẽn ka bõn-tɛɛmdgã.
65001004	Neb n soos n kẽ sʋka la bãmb dãmb poorẽ la b ra tog n yeel al daar zãra: Ad neb sẽn ka mi Wẽnd waoogre n teemd tõnd Wẽnda yel-sõmde t'a lebgd yoobo la b basd kɛɛnga d Zu-soab la d Soaala, a Zezi Krista.
65001005	M dat n tẽeg-y lame, yãmb sẽn mi yɛla fãa zãngã, tɩ Soaala sẽn fãag b neba n yiis-b Ezipt tẽnga, b lɛɛg n kʋʋ kɩɩsdbã.
65001006	Sã n ya ne malɛgs niyns sẽn bas-b tɩ b naama fãage, tɩ b kong n dig-ba n yiis b sẽn da beẽ, b bao zĩig n balg-b bãeens sẽn ka tõe n kao. B balg-b la likẽ n gũud bʋ kãsenga raare. Sã n ya malɛgs niyns sẽn bas-b tɩ b reeg b kãsengo tɩ b ka pa b naama zugu, b bĩnga bãmb bʋʋda ra-kãsenga yĩnga la b sẽb-b lame tɩ b be likẽ, wakat buud fãa.
65001007	Yaa yoob so-yɛng la Sodom la Gomor dãmba me rɩk yã, b me maan wɩɩbdo la b sɩbg-b lame, neb a taaba zãmsg yĩnga, ne bugum sẽn ka kiid lɛ-lɛ.
65001008	La ade, wala b yika gãeemdo, bãmb me rẽgemda b yĩnsi la b sãbsd yĩngr soaalba, yĩngr na-rɩtba.
65001009	Malɛk kãsm a Mikayɛl sẽn yik zabr ne Sʋtãan tɩ b maand no-koeemde a Moyiiz yĩnga poorẽ, a ka saag a paoogr ye. A yeelame bala: «M basd-f la ne Wẽnde!»
65001010	Bãmb yẽ paoogda-b sẽn ka mi, la b sẽn mi bũmb ningã b mi-a-la ne ninsaal yam bala, wala rũng sẽn mi, la rẽ ka wat ne bũmb a to tɩ ka b menesg ye.
65001011	La yell bee zirẽ-be-mitba zugu; b rɩka a Kaẽ sorã n kẽ moogo; b tudga a Balaam tudgrã, ligd daab yĩnga; b ki-la b tõdgr pʋgẽ wala a Kore.
65001012	B kɩtdame tɩ y sã n dat n lagem taab n dɩ bɩ ka baasd neer ye. B rɩta noogo tɩ yãnd ka tar-b ye, n pit b pʋse. Ad-y b lebga sawat faad sobg sẽn tar n looda. B lebga tɩɩs sẽn wom n sɛ, n ki b wilẽ la b kʋɩ b yẽgnẽ, n võ n dɩga.
65001013	Ad-y b yɛsa ne yãnde tɩ b na lɛɛg wʋb wa mogr pʋg sẽn dãmbe t'a wʋbd a ko-puudu. B wẽnda yĩngr ãds sẽn kẽnd yaare la sẽn lebg lik soolem yʋʋm tõt sɛɛb yĩnga.
65001014	Yaa bãmb fãa poorẽ la a Enok, d yaab a yopoe soab a Adem poorẽ, leok bãngr leokre: «Soaala waa ne b nin-sõma, zãma kõn bãng n sõde,
65001015	tɩ b na paalg nin-wẽnsa fãa b tʋʋm-wẽna yĩnga la b sẽn gom tɩtaam goama yĩnga.»
65001016	Yaa bãmb n tar gom-bi, n tar guglengu, n tũud b yĩnga yamleoogo, n gomd wilg-m-meng goama la b belgd neb n na n paam n dɩ.
65001017	Sã n ya yãmba, m kom-nongdse, tẽeg-y Soaal a Zezi Krista tʋʋm-tʋmdba sẽn wilg bũmb ningã.
65001018	B ra yet-y la woto: «Dũni wã sɛɛb wakato neb n na n zĩndi n mi b taab laado la b pʋgd b minim-wẽnse.»
65001019	Bãmb dãmb n wat ne welgre. B basa b yam sõnga pʋgbo n vɩ wa rũmsi.
65001020	Sã n ya yãmba, m kom-nongdse, keng-y taab pelse ne y tẽeb sõngo la a Vʋʋsem Sõng sɛɛg yõkre.

65001022	Neb niyns sẽn ket-b n zĩi n sãmbdẽ wã, sõng-y tɩ b tẽeba lebg kẽnkẽ.

66001001	Ad Krista a Zezi sẽn puk yɛl niyns sẽn da solg b nengẽ: Wẽnd n yeel-b tɩ b wilg b kambã bũmb ning waoonga sẽn zoe n seglã; b sõgna Zã nengẽ, la bãmb meng tʋm b Malɛka;
66001002	la sɩd yaa Wẽnd Koɛɛga ne Krista meng kaseto la a Zã paam yã ne a sẽn yãend bũmb ninga fãa.
66001003	Sũ-noog soab la ned ninga sẽn karm-a bɩ sẽn kelg-a goama sẽn ya bãngr goama la a bĩng-ba a sũurẽ; ad-y Soaala Waoong yaoome.
66001004	Maam a Zã n pʋʋsd Azi Tigengu sẽn sẽeg tẽns a yopoe wã. Bɩ y paam bark la laafi, Pĩnd ne Rũnda la Beoog soaba maasem yĩnga; malɛgs a yopoe, sẽn yeg-b zaoorã maasem yĩnga,
66001005	la a Zezi Krista maasem yĩnga; bãmb la kaset sɩd soaba, a Adem buud bi-kẽeng la dũni dĩm dãmb Dĩma: bãmb n nong-do, la b waas d yel-wẽna rẽgdo ne bãmb meng zɩɩm.
66001006	Bãmb n kɩt tɩ tõnd lebg maan-kʋʋdb buudu, b Wẽnnaam la b Ba yĩnga; bãmb bal n tar ziir la naam, marsã la daar fãa. Ami!
66001007	Ad-b sẽn wat sawadg zugu tɩ ned kam fãa na n yãend-ba, ba neb niyns sẽn kõs-b ne kãndã; Adem biis fãa na n kaasa b poorẽ. N-ye! Sɩd ne sɩda!

66001009	Maam a Zã, yãmb saam-biiga, sẽn naaga yãmb n nams a Zezi yĩnga, n nams b Rĩunga yĩnga, n ka bas raood ne bãmb pʋgbã,

66004001	Dẽ poore m sẽn yãe la woto. Noor n pak saag zugu la koɛɛg ning sẽn tãs wa baorgo tɩ mam wʋma, yeela maam: Dʋ yĩngr ka tɩ m wilg-f bũmb ning sẽn wate!
66004002	Wakat kãnga yɩɩ wa m yama fʋsga m yĩngã la ade, zaoor n da lugl saag zugu la Ned n da zao a zugu.
66004003	Sẽn da zĩ-a zaoorẽ wã ra tãoosda vẽenem wa kug peesem kẽer sẽn tãoosde vẽenem n ya kẽeg lima la moomd yʋdʋd; saag gomtɩʋʋg n tão gũbri n gilg zaoorã la a ra yaa kẽeg toenɛɛga.
66004004	Zaoora meng ra gũbga ne goeels pisi la a naase tɩ Nin-kẽems pisi la a naas da zĩ-b zutu ne fut sẽn ya wogd la peelse; Nin-kẽemsa zut ra fõga sãnem pugli.
66004005	Zaoora meng ra tãoosda sa-yagdo ne koees la sa-tãse; fitils rãmb a yopoe n da yõgne, zaoora taoore: bãmb la Wẽnnaam malɛgs a yopoe wã.
66004006	Zaoora taoor ra gãnega wa mogre sẽn yãgda la a pɩn wa kugr sẽn saas sõmb-sõmbo; Bõn-vɩɩs a naase n da gũbg zaoorã tɩ b mensa ya nin bala a yeyn-ye, poorẽ la taoore.
66004007	Pipi Bõn-vɩɩga ra wẽnda gɩgemde; Bõn-vɩɩg a yiib soaba da wẽnda loalga, a tãab soaba ra tara neng sẽn wẽnd ninsaal dẽnna, la a naas soaba da yaa sɩlga sẽn laand yĩngri.
66004008	La Bõn-vɩɩs a naasa fãa ra tara pɩgs a yoobe la b yĩnga da yaa nin bala zĩig zãnga, poorẽ la taoore; b da moondame, wĩntoog la yʋngo, n ka yalsdẽ ye: «Yãmb la Sõmblem, yãmb la Sõmblem, yãmb la Sõmblem! Bũmb fãa Soaala. Yãmb la Pĩnda, Rũnna la Beoog Soaba.»
66004009	La wakat ning fãa Bõn-vɩɩsa sẽn pẽg la b waoog, la b pʋʋs Ned ninga sẽn zĩ-a zaoorẽ wã n vɩ a vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ wã,
66004010	Nin-kẽems pisi la a naasa me da wõgemdeda a taoore n waoogd ka sɩng kõn zĩnd sɛɛbo Soabã la b ra lobda b sãnem pugli wã zaoora taoore n yetẽ:
66004011	«D Soaala la d Wẽnnaam, yãmb toga ne pẽgre la ne waoogre la ne ziiri, tɩ yãmb n naan dũniya la yaa ne yãmb pãnga la bũmb sẽn da ka be zĩnd yã.»
66005001	M yãeeme tɩ sẽn da zĩ-a zaoora zug ra zãada a rɩtg nugẽ sebr sẽn pili la sebra ra gʋlsa a nens a yiiba fãa la soagds a yopoe n da sog-a.
66005002	M yãee Malɛk sẽn wɩɩd pãnga sẽn moon ne koe kãsenga: «Ãnda n na n tõog n lak sebrã, n soka soagdsã?»
66005003	La ned ba a ye ra ka be, saag zugu, tẽng zug bɩ bʋg-tẽnga, sẽn tõe n lak sebrã la a karm-a ye.
66005004	La m kiiga nintãm tɩ b pa yãend ned sẽn da segd n lak sebrã la a karm-a ye.
66005005	Nin-kẽemsa nin-yend yeela maam: «Da yãb ye; ad-a Zɩɩda buudẽ gɩgemdã, a Daviid yagengã, tõeeme; yẽ n na n pilg sebrã la a sok a soagdsã a yopoe wã fãa.»
66005006	Zaoora yegende, Bõn-vɩɩs a naasã la Nin-kẽemba sʋka, m yãee Pe-bil sẽn yɛse tɩ yaa wa b kodg-a lame la a ra tara yɩɩl a yopoe la nin a yopoe; bãmb la Wẽnd tõogã, b yama sẽn tʋmd b tʋʋmda tẽng zugu, zĩis fãa wã.
66005007	Pe-bila kolga sẽn da zĩ-a zaoora n deeg sebrã a sẽn da zãad, a rɩtg nugẽ.
66005008	A sẽn deege la Bõn-vɩɩs a naasa sẽn wõgemd Pe-bila taoore; Nin-kẽems pisi la a naasa me wõgemdame, ned kam fãa ne a pɛndga, ne a sãnem laag sẽn nukd tɩdare bug-zõose: tẽedba pʋʋsg makre.
66005009	B pʋda yɩɩn paalle: «Yãmb sɩd togame, n deeg sebrã la y sogs a soagdsã tɩ yãmb la b kodg yã, la yaa ne yãmb zɩɩm la y reeg ninsaalba n lebs-b Wẽnnaam, bãmb ne b buud toɛ-toɛ yã, ne b goam, ne b rog-n-mik, ne b soolem.
66005010	Yãmb kɩtame tɩ b lebg d Wẽnnaama yĩnga, maan-kʋʋr nanams buudu, maan-kʋʋr naam sẽn dɩt tẽng zugu.»
66005011	M da ket n getame la ade, m wʋma rãamd kãsenga; Malɛk rãmb zãma n da gũbg zaoorã ne Bõn-vɩɩsã la Nin-kẽemsã. B sõora yaa tus kẽema belem tus kẽema n paam n zage. La b ra moonda ne koe kãsenga:
66005012	«Pe-bila sẽn kodgã n tog ne tõogo, ne Wẽndlem, ne bãngr pidungu, ne naam, ne waoogre, ne ziiri, ne pẽgre.»
66005013	Bõn-naand buud fãa sẽn be saag zugu, bɩ tẽnga, bɩ bʋg-tẽnga, bɩ mogrẽ, dũniya tõre, m wʋma b fãa sẽn moonde: «Sẽn zĩ-a a zaoorẽ wã la Pe-bila, paam pẽgre, waoogre, naam la ziiri yʋʋm sẽn kõn sɛ!»
66005014	Bõn-vɩɩs a naasa ra leokdame: «Ami!» Tɩ Nin-kẽemsa na n wõgemd tẽng n waooge.
66006001	M yaool n yãee Pe-bila t'a sokd pipi soagdga; tɩ pipi Bõn-vɩɩga koɛɛg na n tãs wa saaga: «Wa-y!»
66006002	M gesame la m yãee wed bolle; wedʋʋda ra zãada tãpo; b kõ-a-la naam pugla n le yet t'a yi n tɩ maan daoodo.
66006003	Pe-bila le soka soagdg a yiib soaba tɩ m wʋm Bõn-vɩɩg a yiib soaba kɛlenga: «Wa-y!»
66006004	Yɩɩ wed moomd menga n puki; wed-dʋʋda paama sore n na n menes laafi tẽng zugu, n bas tɩ ninsaalb kood taaba; b kõ-a-la zãngoogo.
66006005	Pe-bila sẽn sok soagdg a tãab soaba, mam wʋma Bõn-vɩɩg a tãab soaba sẽn kelme: «Wa-y!» La m yãee wed sablg sẽn yi t'a wed-dʋʋda zãad bũmb sẽn tar m magd zɩslem;
66006006	la m wʋma koɛɛg sẽn tãse, Bõn-vɩɩs a naasa sʋka, la a mooname: «Zom pɛɛlg wũmbl yaa wakɩ koɛɛnga, zom pugsg wũmbl a tãab yaa wakɩ koɛɛnga; sã n kella kaama la rãama, da paas-y bũmb ye.»
66006007	Pe-bila sẽn sok soagdg a naas soaba, m wʋma Bõn-vɩɩg a naas soaba sẽn kelme: «Wa-y!»
66006008	Ade, weef ning sẽn yi-a wã yaa kẽeg-toenoɛɛga tɩ wed-dʋʋda yʋʋr boond tɩ Kũum; la bʋg-tẽnga n da yãagd-a. B kõ-a-la tõogo t'a soog tẽnga boag a naasa bogr a ye, la a kʋ neba ne sʋʋga, ne kom, ne bã-longdem, ne we-rũmsi.
66006009	Pe-bila soka soagdg a nu soaba tɩ m tool n yãe b sẽn da kʋ b rãmba sɩɩse, sẽn da ki-b Wẽnnaam Gomda yĩnga la b kaseta yĩnga.
66006010	La bãmb me sɩnga kɛlenga ne b pãng fãa: «D Soaala, Sõmblem la Sɩd soaba, yãmb na n gũu wakat bʋgo n yaool n kao y bʋ-sɩdã la y rok y sũur ne tẽng zug rãmba sẽn daag d zɩɩma?»
66006011	Dẽ la b kõ ned kam fãa fu-wok pɛɛlga la b yeel-b tɩ b gãneg b yam bilf nanda tɩ b tũud-n-taasã la b ma-bi-taasã sẽn tʋm-b wa bãmba la sẽn tog n kood wa bãmba sõor lebg ka tɛka.
66006012	Mam leb n gesame: Pe-bila sẽn waa n sok soagdg a yoob soaba, tẽnga miima ne pãnga la wĩntoog sobgame n lebg wa vũundu, tɩ kiuug moog zãng wa zɩɩm.
66006013	Ãdsa fãa rʋʋga tẽnga wa sɩlmand sẽn wẽnend kankang wila n sʋʋgd a bi-kãse;
66006014	saaga pilga wa seb-vãoogo n menem, tãmsa ne tẽns niyns sẽn puk-b mogrẽ wã fãa vigsa b zĩisẽ.
66006015	Tẽng zug nanamse la nin-bɛdã ne tãnsoaben-dãmbã la rakãagba, la pãng rãmba, b fãa bala: yamb bɩ burkĩna, b zoeeme n soond tãmsã la pĩisã bogdẽ.
66006016	B ra yeta tãmsã la pĩisã: «Sirg-y n solg-y tõndo tɩ d põs sẽn Zao-a a zaoorẽ wã la d tɩlg Pe-bila beem.»
66006017	Dũnna la Wẽnd sũ-puur da-kãsenga, la ãnna n na n yalse?
66007001	Dẽ poore mam yãee malɛgs a naase sẽn yɛs tẽnga kɩrems a naasã; b ra gãda tẽnga sob-raad a naasã tɩ b ra fʋʋs tẽng bɩ mogre, bɩ tɩɩg meng ye.
66007002	Mam yãee malɛk a to sẽn lik Yaanga. Yẽ n wat n na n ning Vɩɩm naaba kamba makre; a kelmame n yeel malɛgs niyns sẽn da paam-b sore n na n dãmb tẽnga la mogrã:
66007003	«Da yãg-y nanda n dãmb tẽnga la mogre bɩ tɩɩse tɩ tõnd ka reng n ning makre d Wẽnda kamba fãa rĩirẽ ye.»
66007004	M bãnga neb niyns fãa sẽn paam-b makra sõore: tus koabg la pis naase la a naase a Israyɛl kambẽ.
66007005	A Zɩɩda roogẽ: tus piig la a yiib n paame; a Rubẽ roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Gad roogẽ: tus piig la a yi;
66007006	a Asɛr roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Neftali roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Manase roogẽ: tus piig la a yi;
66007007	a Simeõ roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Levi roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Isakar roogẽ: tus piig la a yi;
66007008	a Zabulõ roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Zozɛf roogẽ: tus piig la a yi; a Bẽzame roogẽ: tus piig la a yi n paame.
66007009	Dẽ poore m yãee zãma kõn bãng n sõde, tẽns toɛ-toɛ rãmba, buud toɛ-toɛ, rog-n-mik toɛ-toɛ, goam biis toɛ-toɛ; m yãend-b lame tɩ b yɛs yĩngri, zaoora taoore la Pe-bila taoore, n yer fu-wogd peelse la b zãad kãase la b moon ne koe kãsenga:
66007010	«Tõnd Wẽnnaam sẽn zao b zaoorẽ la Pe-bila soog waoogre!»
66007011	Malɛgsa fãa sẽn da gũbg zaoorã ne Nin-kẽemsã la Bõn-vɩɩs a naasã, b fãa wõgemd n waooga Wẽnnaam,
66007012	b ra maandame: «Sɩda tõnd Wẽnda toga ne pẽgre ne ziiri, b pida ne yam, b toga ne bark pʋʋsgo, ne waoogre, ne naam, ne tõogo tɩ yʋʋma tong taab koabg koabga n tõt sɛɛbo. Ami!»
66007013	Nin-kẽem a yembr yaool n sok-m lame: «Nin-bãmba sẽn yer fu wogd peelsã, fo mi b sẽn ya b rãmba, la b sẽn yitẽ?»
66007014	Tɩ mam leoke: «M Naa, yãmb n mi wɛ!» T'a yeele: «Yaa neb niyns sẽn tɩlg-b pɛt kãsenga; b pegsa b futu la b los-b la Pe-bila zɩɩmẽ tɩ b pelge.
66007015	Yaa rẽ yĩng la b yɛs Wẽnnaam zaoora taoore, n tʋmd b tʋʋma wĩndg la yʋngo, b roogẽ. Sẽn zao-a zaoorã na n kẽes-b-la a zãnd maasmẽ.
66007016	La bada! B kõn le nams kom bɩ ko-yũud ye, wĩndg bɩ pems tʋʋlg ye,
66007017	tɩ Pe-bila sẽn yɛs tẽnsʋka, zaoora taoore, yẽ n na n yɩ b Pe-kɩɩma la b taas b vɩɩm ko-bundem zĩigẽ, la Wẽnnaam na n yẽesa b nintãma fãa.»
66008001	Pe-bila sẽn sok soagdg a yopoe soaba la fãa sẽn yɩ sɩɩ saag zugu n kaoose, n ta wakat pʋɩ-sʋka.
66008002	M yaool n yãee malɛgs a yopoe wã sẽn yɛs-b Wẽnnaam taoorã la b kõ-b-la bard a yopoe.
66008003	Malɛk a to yaool n yaasa zaoora taoore ne sãnem kaorgo la b kõ-a-la tɩdar wʋsgo t'a naag ne nin-sõma wã pʋʋsgo n dɩgl sãnem maan-kugra zug, zaoora taoore;
66008004	la woto tɩdara bug-zõos ruka malɛka nugẽ n dʋ yĩngri, Wẽnnaam taoore, n naag ne Nin-sõma wã pʋʋsgo.
66008005	Malɛka leb n dɩka kaorgã n pids-a ne maan-kugra bugum; a fẽega bugma tẽnga la yɩɩ sa-tãs la bʋrga, ne sa-yãgdo la bũmb fãa miimame.
66008006	Malɛgs a yopoe ne bard a yopoe tɩ seglame n na n peebe.
66008007	Pipi baorga peebame. Yɩɩ sapɩlem ne bugum sẽn kalem ne zɩɩm n dʋʋg tẽng zugu la dũniya bogr a tãab soaba, tɩɩsa fãa bogr a tãab soaba, mo-maasa bogr a tãab soaba, fãa gill rɩɩ bugum.
66008008	Malɛk a yiib soaba peeba a baorgo. La bõn-kẽemde sẽn zem tãnga n wit wa bugum, yii yĩngri n lʋɩ mogrẽ la mogr a bogr a tãab soab lebga zɩɩm.
66008009	Mogra pʋgẽ bõn-vɩɩsa bogr a tãab soab kiime; koom kogenda bogr a tãab soab bõra koomẽ.
66008010	Malɛk a tãab soaba peebame. La ãd bedre sẽn dɩt wa bug-vɩlenga yii yĩngri n lʋɩ kʋɩlsa bogr a tãab soaba la ko-bundsa pʋga.
66008011	Ãdga yʋʋr la a «Tɩɩsem»; kooma bogr a tãab sob lebga tɩɩsga la neb wʋsg sẽn yũ kooma sẽn lebg toog liga kiime.
66008012	Malɛk a naas soaba peebame. Tɩ yell na n paam Wĩntoogo, kiuug la ãdsa bogr a tãab soaba. Wĩndga, kiuug la ãdsa vẽenem bogr a tãab soab n wooge; daara konga a vẽenema bogr a tãab soaba. Vẽenem ning sẽn mii n kees yʋngã, yẽ me bogr a tãab soabã n wooge.
66008013	La mam sẽn da ket n getẽ m wʋma sɩlg sẽn lug yĩngr-yĩngr sẽn kelem ne pãnga: «Bʋko, bʋk wɛɛ, bʋk bal ne dũni wã bõn-vɩɩse, bard a tãaba sã n wa tãse, bard niyns malɛgs a tãabã sẽn ket n zãad b nusẽ wã sã n wa tãse!»
66009001	Malɛk a nu soaba peebame. La mam yãee ãdg a yembre sẽn yi yĩngri n lʋɩ tẽnga la b kõ-a-la bul-zulunga kʋɩlen-bila.
66009002	A sẽn pak kʋɩlengã, bug-zõos n yi, wala wʋng kẽeng sẽn widg rẽnna – la a sobga wĩndga la zĩiga fãa.
66009003	Bug-zõosa pʋgẽ, sʋy n yɩke n lʋɩ dũniya zãnga; la b kõ-b-la zẽnem wala tẽng zug namsa rẽnna.
66009004	B kõ-b-la noor tɩ b bas pʋt la moog buud fãa, la tɩɩs buud fãa la b rɩ neb niyns bala sẽn da ka tar b Wẽnd makrã b rĩirẽ.
66009005	B da ka tar sor n kʋ neb ye, yaa b nams-b bal kiis a nu tõre; la b rũmba zabr da yaa wa nang rẽnna.
66009006	Dasem kãense, neb wʋsg na n baoo kũum n konge, b na n tʋlga kũum la kũum na n zoe n bas-b lame.
66009007	Mik fo sã n ges sʋya, b wẽnda wiidi sẽn bob zabre, b zuta fõga sãnem pugli tɩ b nens ya wa ninsaal nenga.
66009008	B zoobda yaa wa pagb rẽnna, tɩ b yẽna ya gɩgemd yẽna.
66009009	B da rɩka kut n pil b yãoogo la b pɩgsa rãamd da fõta wa bilim-bilm ka tɛk b sẽn sog wiidi n dabd zabre.
66009010	B zʋya nee wa nang zʋʋre, n tar kõse; yaa kiis a nu la b paam sore n na n nams ninsaalba.
66009011	B ra tara b naaba, yẽ la bul-zulunga dĩma, a yʋʋr ne Ebre rãmb goam la a Wãabo, a Abadõ, tɩ Grɛk rãmb boond-a tɩ Wãab naaba, a Apolliõ.
66009012	Bʋk a yembre ka looge t'a yiib nan pʋgda.
66009013	Malɛk a yoob soaba peebame. La m wʋma koɛɛga; a yii sãnem maan-kugra sẽn vigl Wẽnd taoora kɩrems a naasã;
66009014	la Koɛɛga yeela malɛk a yoob soaba sẽn zãad baorgo: «Lood Malɛgs a naasã b sẽn da loe Efrat kʋɩl kãsengẽ wã n base.»
66009015	La b basa malɛgs a naasã sẽn da yɛs n gũud wakatã, daarã, kiuugã la yʋʋmdã n na n kʋ ninsaalba fãa bogr a tãab soabã.
66009016	B tãb-biisa da yaa wed-dʋʋdb tus kẽems kobsi: woto la b sõorã b sẽn togs-ma.
66009017	Ad-y yaa woto la m yãend wed-dʋʋdba ne b wiidi wã: wed-dʋʋdba ra teega b yãoog ne kut sẽn wit bug-kẽega la bug-kõodre. Wed-bãmb zuta ra yaa wa bõnyẽeg rẽnna tɩ b noor pursd bugum, bug-zõose la kidbri.
66009018	Bugma, bug-zõosã la kidbrã wiida sẽn da pursd b noorẽ, kʋʋ ninsaalba bogr a tãab soaba zãnga.
66009019	Wed bãmb wẽnem da bee b noorẽ la b zʋʋrẽ me; zʋya ra baasda ne wiis zutu la rẽ la b ra tar n wɩɩbd ninsaalba.
66009020	Ne rẽ fãa neb niyns sẽn põs-b tẽn-kũuma ka lak ne b yel-wẽna ba bilfu. B ka vẽ ne b sʋtãamba waoogre, bõn-yood niyns sen naan ne sãnem, wanzurf, kugri, bɩ raoogo, bõn-yood sẽn ka nini, n ka tʋba n ka nao.
66009021	B ka vẽ ba bilfu ne b nin-kʋʋre, ne b tɩto, ne b yoobo la ne b wagdma ye.
66010001	Dẽ poore mam yãee malɛk a to sẽn tar pãng sẽn sigi; a menga zãng pila sawadgo, tɩ saag gomtɩʋʋg tão gũbri, a zugẽ, t'a nenga ya wa wĩntoog, t'a karsa wit bugum.
66010002	A da zãada a nugẽ, seb bil sẽn lake la rẽ t'a rɩtg naoor teega mogre, t'a goabg naoor teeg tẽn-koɛɛnga.
66010003	A kelma ne koe yaanga wa bõnyẽega. La rẽ poore sa-tãs a yopoe n gom b goama.
66010004	B sẽn gom n sɛ la m sẽn sɩng n na n gʋls, la koɛɛg n yi yĩngri n yeel-ma: «Bĩng sa-tãs a yopoe wã goama f yamẽ bala la f ra gʋls-b ye.»
66010005	La m sẽn da yãend malɛk ninga t'a teeg mogra la tẽngã n yɛsẽ wã zẽka a rɩtg n tees yĩngri,
66010006	la a wẽena ne Vɩɩm sẽn kõn sɛ Naaba, sẽn naana yĩngr ne a teeda fãa, sẽn naana tẽnga ne a teeda fãa, sẽn naana mogr ne a pʋgẽ teeda fãa, a wẽename n yeele: «Wakat taame!
66010007	Raar ning b sẽn na n wʋm malɛk a yopoe soabã, a baorga peebg raare, ba raare la Wẽnnaam yɛla fãa na n puk zãnga, wala b bãngdba, b sõgen-kamba, sẽn togs Koe-noog ningã.»
66010008	Dẽ poore, koɛɛg ning sẽn yi a yĩngr tɩ m wʋma le goma ne m yɛsa: «Kẽng n tɩ reeg seb bila malɛka sẽn zãad a nugẽ, malɛk ning sẽn teega mogra la tẽngã.»
66010009	La m kẽngame, n kos malɛka t'a kõ-m sebrã la a yeela maam: «Deeg la f vele; a na n pidsa f pʋga ne tɩɩsem la f noorẽ, a naa n yɩɩ noog wa sɩɩdo.»
66010010	La m deega seb bilã malɛka nugẽ la m vel-a lame; m noorẽ a ra yaa wa sɩɩdo, la m sẽn vel n sɛ, a taa m pʋgẽ n lebg toogo.
66010011	B le yeel-m lame: «Fo tog n le goma bãngr gom-beedo ne ninsaalb buud ka tɛka, ne tẽns ka tɛka, tɩ b zɛlma ya toore, tɩ b nanams me ya toore.»
66011001	Dẽ poore b kõ-m la moogo, mo-sĩdimdi wa ribla la b yeel-m lame: «Yik n tɩ mag Wẽnd doogã ne a maan-kugrã la bãng wẽn-pʋʋsdba fãa sẽn be a pʋgẽ sõore;
66011002	da mag yɩnga ye, tɩ rẽ basa ne bu-zẽmba la yaa kiis pis naase la a yiibu tõre la b na n saag Tẽn-Sõngã.
66011003	M na n kõ-la m kaset dãmb a yiibã noore tɩ b yeelg sũ-pa-noang futu n gom bãngr goam dasem tusr la kobsi la pisoob pʋgẽ.»
66011004	Bãmb makre la oliviye tɩɩs a yiib la fitils a yiiba sẽn be dũni Soaala taoore.
66011005	Ned sã n baood nin-bãmba namsgo, bugum n na n yi b noorẽ n dɩ b bɛɛbã. N-ye! Sẽn baood-a b namsg, yaa woto la yẽ soab na n ki.
66011006	B sã n yi n na n tʋm b tʋʋmna, b kõ-b la sore tɩ b pag saaga tɩ koom da tosg ye; b tara pãng me n tõe tɩ koom lebg zɩɩm la b tõe n bẽnega tẽnga tõrẽ ne yel-beed tusri, b sẽn dat wakat ning fãa.
66011007	La b sã n wa baas b wilgrã, bõn-ninda sẽn yi-a bul-zulungẽ wã n na n tak zabre ne-ba, n tõog-ba la a kʋ-ba.
66011008	B na n daaga b yĩnsã n bas yɩng woto dasem a tãabo la pʋɩ-sʋka, Tẽn-kãsenga pʋga, Sodom bɩ Ezipt, wala neb kẽer sẽn bɩnd n boondẽ, zĩig ning b sẽn ka b Soaala pika;
66011009	b na n daaga b yĩnsã n bas ninsaalb ka tɛka, nin-zẽmba, gãgnense, la tẽn-zãorgẽ dãmb nini, dasem a tã la pʋɩ-sʋka, la b ka tar sor n dɩk-ba n tɩ mum ye.
66011010	Adem biis fãa kɩdemdame la b pʋʋsd taab zu-noogo, n pʋʋsd taab ne kũuni, tɩ bãngdba a yiibã ra nams b la wʋsgo.
66011011	La dasem a tã la pʋɩ-sʋka sẽn looge, Wẽnnaam le kõo b bãngdba vɩɩm tɩ b le tik n yiki, tɩ sẽn get-ba yɛs marsã ne rabeem kãsenga.
66011012	La m wʋma koɛɛg kãseng sẽn yi yĩngri n bool-ba: «Dʋ-y yĩngr ka!» La b dʋʋ yĩngr ne sawadgo, tɩ b bɛɛba yɛs n getẽ.
66011013	La wakat kãnga tẽnga miima ne pãnga la na-tẽnga bogr piig soaba bõrame n lʋɩ, la rẽ waa ne neb tus a yopoe kaalem. Rabeem yõka sẽn põs-ba fãa tɩ b na n pʋʋs yĩngr Soaala barka.
66011014	Bʋk a yiib soaba ka looge, keta a tãab soaba!
66011015	Malɛk a yopoe soaba peebame. Yĩngri, yɩɩ koees n tãs woto: «Tõnd Soaala ne b Krista n so dũniya, b na n dɩɩ naam tɩ yʋʋma tong taab n tõt sɛɛbo!»
66011016	Nin-kẽems pisi la a naasã sẽn zĩ-b Wẽnnaam taoorã yika b goeelsa zutu la b wõgemdame n waoog Wẽnnaam woto:
66011017	«Tõnd pʋʋsda yãmb barka, Soaala-Wẽnnaam, bũmb fãa Naanda, yãmba, Zaamẽ la Rũnna la Beoog soaba, yãmb waa ne y pãn-kẽoongã n deeg y soolem zãnga n na n dɩ y naam.
66011018	Nin-zẽmba da yika ne sũ-puuri la yãmb me waa ne y rẽnna n taas sẽn kiba bʋʋda wakato, la y taas y rolba wakato y bãngdba, y sõgen-kamba yĩnga, y tʋʋm-tʋmdba, y nin-sõma yĩnga, neb niyns fãa, nin-bɛd la nin-bi sẽn waoogd-b yãmb yʋʋra yĩnga, la y taas y sɩbgra wakato tẽn-wãadba yĩnga.»
66011019	Wẽnd dooga noor yaool n paka yĩngri tɩ b na n yãend b zooda kaseto a pʋgẽ; la yɩɩ sa-yãgdo ne koeese ne sa-tãse, ne tẽng miuungu, ne sapɩlem sẽn dʋʋgd barar.
66012001	Yell bãnd kãsenga n puk yĩngri: pag sẽn yɛse tɩ wĩndga vẽenem buiid-a, t'a naoor tabg kiuugu, t'a zug teeg ãds piig la a yiibu.
66012002	A ra tʋtame n tol n kũmd rogum.
66012003	Dẽ poore yell bãnd a to n puk yĩngri: Wag-bãnde, moomde zãnga, ne zut a yopoe la yɩɩl piiga, tɩ zug fãa fõgen naam pugla.
66012004	A zʋʋra kãaga yĩngr ãdsa bogr a tãab tõre n dʋʋg tẽnga; a waa n yalsa paga sẽn kũmd dogma taoore n gũud t'a rog a biigã t'a rɩk n vele.
66012005	Paga roga bi-ribla la bi-kãng n na n dɩ naam bu-zẽmba zutu la a naama rasaar yaa kutu.
66012006	Biiga pɩsgame n ta Wẽnnaam nengẽ, zaoora taoore, tɩ paga zoe n dig weoogo n tɩ soond zĩig ning Wẽnnaam sẽn da segl a yĩnga la b rɩlg-a-la be dasem tusri la kobsi la pisoobe.
66012007	Dẽ marsã la zabr kaoog yĩngri: a Mikayɛl ne a malɛgs yika zabre ne Wag-bãndã tɩ yẽ me yi ne a malɛgse,
66012008	la bãmb n kong pãnga tɩ b rig-ba n yiis arzãna.
66012009	B teeba Wag-bãndã, wag kʋdrã, sẽn boond tɩ Sʋtãana, bɩ bɛyã, dũni belgda, b teeb-a B teeba Wag-bãndã, Wag-kʋdrã lame n fabg tẽnga, yẽ ne a malɛgsa fãa.
66012010	M wʋma koɛɛg sẽn tãs yĩngri: «Marsã tɛka tõnd Wẽndã n so tõogo, naam la ziiri, la b Krista zaoo bũmb fãa zugu, tɩ tõnd saam-biisa rõatã, sẽn da rõta bãmb Wẽnd taoor, wĩntoog la yʋngo, b lub-a-la tẽnga.
66012011	Bãmb tõog-a-la ne Pe-bila zɩɩma, ne b noor kaseto, n pa ges b vɩɩma wa bũmb la b sak kũum ye.
66012012	Dɩlla kɩdm-y sũ-noogo, yãmba, yĩngr kamba. Yãb-y, tẽnga la mogre, tɩ Sʋtãan siga yãmba la a sũura puudame, a sẽn mi t'a raara sõdame.»
66012013	La a sẽn mik tɩ b lub-a la tẽnga, Wag-bãndã yikame n na n bʋʋg pagã, bi-ribla ma wã.
66012014	Paga paama Sɩl-kãseng pɩgs a yiibu n yɩk n tud weoogo n paam n ta zĩig ning a sẽn na soond Wag-bãndã la a paam tɩ b rɩlg-a yʋʋmde n le paas yʋʋm a yi la pʋɩ-sʋka.
66012015	Waafa yaool n sẽnesa a kolkoodo tɩ lebg kʋɩlga n pʋgd pagã n na n dɩ-a.
66012016	Tẽnga fãaga pagã: a yaaga a noor n vel kʋɩlgã sẽn yi waafa noorẽ.
66012017	Waafa lɛɛgame t'a sũur kãbd ne pagã, t'a kong n na n tɩ maan zabre ne a kamb a taabã, kamb niyns sẽn da reeg-b Wẽnnaam noya la b paam a Zezi kasetã.
66012018	A waa n yalsa mogra noore.
66013001	La m yãenda Rũng sẽn puk koomẽ ne zut a yopoe la yɩɩl piiga; yɩɩl piiga da fõga naam pugli piiga la zut a yopoe wã ra gʋla zab yʋy sẽn tʋʋsd Wẽnde.
66013002	Rũnga ra wẽnda ãbga, t'a nao wẽnd tãntur nao, t'a noor wẽnd gɩgemd noore; Wag-bãnda kõ-a-la a pãnga la a naama zaoore, n kõ-a rĩung sẽn tar yalem.
66013003	Rũnga zug a ye ra nee wa a poglame n sek a kũum, la a poglgã sẽn da sek a kʋʋma wẽneg n sãoogame; dẽ la ãndũni rãmba yik n pʋgd-a ne pɛlen-yɩka.
66013004	B wõgemdame n waoog Wag-bãndã a sẽn dɩk a naama n kõ Rũngã, la b wõgemda Rũnga me taoore n yetẽ: «Ãnda n zem Rũngã la ãnd n tõe n tak zabr ne-a?»
66013005	Rũnga paamame n na n gom tɩtaam goama la a tʋʋs Wẽnde; a paamame n na n tʋm a tʋʋmde kiis pis naas la a yiibu.
66013006	T'a sɩd na n sɩng n tʋʋs Wẽnde, n tʋʋs b yʋʋre la b roogo la sẽn be-b arzãna fãa.
66013007	Rũnga paamame n na n maan beem ne nin-sõma la a tõog-ba; a paama tõog ninsaalb fãa zugu, tẽns toɛ-toɛ rãmba, tɩ b goam la b rog-n-mik ya toɛ-toɛ yã.
66013008	Ada sẽn na n paam waoogr neb niyns nengẽ: yaa sẽn wa-b moogo n yaool n ka paam, dũni sɩngra wakato, tɩ b yʋʋr gʋls vɩɩm sebra pʋgẽ, Pe-bil ning b sẽn kodgã vɩɩma sebr pʋgẽ.
66013009	Sẽn tar-a tʋb bɩ a kelg!
66013010	B balg bãnga sẽn toga ne bãnga! B kʋ ne sʋʋga sẽn toga n kʋ ne sʋʋga! Woto wã, nin-sõma wã maanda sũ-keelem la b zĩ ne saagre.
66013011	Ad-y m yãee Rũng a to sẽn yi tẽngã ne yɩɩl a yiibu wa Pe-bila dẽnna t'a koɛɛg ya wa Wag-bãnda koɛɛg.
66013012	A reega a tʋʋmna pipi Rũnga nengẽ, la a saa n vigla a naama zaoor zĩig zãnga n kɩt tɩ dũnia tõre ne a neba ka tɛkã waoog pipi Rũngã, rũng ning zug a ye sẽn pogle n wẽneg n sãoogã.
66013013	A maana tʋʋm bãna sẽn yɩkd pɛlense; a tol n kɩtame tɩ saag bugum sig tẽnga neb fãa nifẽ.
66013014	La a sẽn kẽ pipi Rũngã, rẽ tudga tẽnga rãmba n ning b yamẽ tɩ b maan nin-naande, Rũng ning sʋʋga sẽn pogle tɩ nodra wẽneg n maaga soab nin-naande, n tar n waoogdẽ.
66013015	B kõ-a-la tõogo t'a kɩt tɩ Rũnga nin-naand lebg wa bõn-vɩɩg menga n gomda, la a modg tɩ b kʋ neb niyns fãa sẽn na n zãgs a waoogre.
66013016	A na n kɩtame tɩ rĩm biis wa talse, rakãagb la naong rãmba, yamba la burkĩna, wa reeg a makrã b nug-rɩtg bɩ b rĩir zugu.
66013017	Ned ba a ye kõn le paam sore n kẽ raagẽ n da rɩɩbo bɩ a koos bũmbu, b sã n ka reng n mak-a ne Rũnga yʋʋr menga bɩ ne Rũnga sõadg yʋʋre.
66013018	Yaa sõdba zĩigẽ la geel mitba na n yõs taaba: Yʋʋra yaa rao yʋʋre, yʋʋra yaa 666, kobs-yoob la pisoob la a yoobe.
66014001	La ad-m sẽn leb n yãe: Pe-bil sẽn yɛs Siõ tãnga zugu ne a neb tus koabg la pis naas la a naase n tar b rĩirẽ a yʋʋre la a Ba wã me yʋʋre.
66014002	La m wʋma rãamde sẽn yi yĩngri wala kʋɩl kãseng rãamde, bɩ wala sob-raoog sẽn fõta; m tagsa pɛnds wẽedb sẽn zĩ n wẽed b pɛndga.
66014003	B yɩɩnda yɩɩn paalle, Zaoora taoore ne Bõn-vɩɩs a naasã la Nin-kẽemsã; ned da ka tõe n zãms yɩɩlã sã n ka bãmb tus koabg la pis naas la a naasã sẽn põs tẽnga velbo.
66014004	Bãmb dãmb zɩ n lagem ne pagb ye, yaa zɩ n lagem pagb zãnga; bãmb n pʋgd Pe-bila a sẽn tʋgdẽ fãa; ninsaalba sʋka, bãmb la Wẽnd la Pe-bila kood-rẽems.
66014005	Zirẽ-beed zɩ n yi b noorẽ ye; b yaa zɩ yell dãmba.
66014006	Mam yãee malɛk a ye sẽn yɩgd yĩngri. Yaa koɛɛg sẽn ya noogo n na n kell n yɩ noogo la a wat n na n wilg tẽng zug rãmba, ned kam fãa ne a buudu, ne a goam, ne a tẽnga.
66014007	A ra moonda ne koe-kãsenga: «Zoe-y Wẽnde, la pẽg-y ba; ad-y bʋʋda wakat taame; waoog-y sẽn naana yĩngr la tẽnga ne mogre la ko bundem fãa.»
66014008	Malɛk a to, malɛk a yiib soaba, n pʋg-a, a me tar kɛlenga: «A lʋɩɩme yee! Na-tẽnga sẽn boond tɩ Babilon Kãsengã! Yẽ bal n belg ninsaalb buud fãa n yũnug-b ne Wẽnd sɩbgr dãam.»
66014009	Malɛk a to, a tãab soaba, n le pʋg-a; a me kelma ne koe-kãsenga: «Ned ning fãa sẽn na n waoog-a Rũnga ne a nin-naandã la a reeg-a makre a rĩirẽ bɩ a nugẽ,
66014010	yẽ soab na yũ Wẽnd sũ-puura rãam, rãam sẽn ka pul koom n tẽg ne b sũ-puura wamde. Yaa ne bugum la kidbri la b na n nams-a, Malɛgs sõma la Pe-bila nifẽ.
66014011	La ad-b namsga bug-zõos sẽn dukd yĩngri yʋʋm sẽn kõn sɛ. Sɩda, sugr kõn zĩndi, wĩndg bɩ yʋngo, ne neb niyns sẽn waoog-b Rũngã ne a nin-naandã, la b reeg a yʋʋra makrã.»
66014012	La rẽ me yĩng la nin-sõma wã maand sũ-keelem, neb niyns sẽn deeg-b Wẽnnaam noya la b tar a Zezi tẽebã.
66014013	M wʋma koɛɛg sẽn zĩnd yĩngr n yeel-ma: «Gʋlse: Sũ-noog rãmba la sẽn kiid-b ne Soaala barka. N-ye! Marsã tɛka – ya a Vʋʋsem Sõng n gomde – bɩ b vʋʋse ne b zaamẽ yaamse tɩ b tʋʋm sõma yãagd-b lame.»
66014014	La ad-m sẽn le yãe: Sawad-pɛɛlg n puki tɩ m ne wa ninsaal Biiga sẽn zao a zugu, b fõgna naam pugla n zãad goeoog b nugẽ, goeoog sẽn dɩte.
66014015	Malɛk a to yii wẽnd doogẽ la a tool n tãsa ne pãnga sẽn da zĩ a sawadgẽ wã n yeel-a: «Lob f goeoogã la f wʋre tɩ tigsig taame, dũniya kood bɩɩme.»
66014016	Sẽn da zi-a sawadgẽ wã loba a goeoog dũniya la dũniya kood tigsame.
66014017	Malɛk a to n le yi wẽnd dooga yĩngri, a me zãad goeoog sẽn dɩte.
66014018	Malɛk a to me n yi maan-kugrã zugu: yẽ la maan-kugra bugma gũuda, la a tool n tãsa sẽn da zãada goeoogã, n yeel-a: «Lob f goeoogã la f tigs tẽnga bugsuntung sõng biisi tɩ bɩɩme.»
66014019	Malɛka loba a goeoog dũni wã pʋga la a tigsa bugsuntung biisi la a rʋʋga fãa Wẽnnaam sũ-puura koglgẽ, koglg kẽengo.
66014020	La b yii ne-a, tẽnga kɛɛnga, n tɩ wẽk a biisa koom; la yɩɩ zɩɩm n daage n zẽk n tat weoof zãndlem, la yaa madgr meng la a madg zĩigã.
66015001	M leb n yãee yel-bãnd yĩngri. Yaa yel kãsenga sẽn yɩkd pɛlenga: Malɛgs a yopoe n zãad tẽn-kũum a yopoe; bãmb n na n baas Wẽnnaam sũ-puura tʋʋmde.
66015002	M yãenda mogr sẽn pɩnd wa nin-gɛtga tɩ bug-witem zomb-a; n paas neb niyns sẽn tõog-b Rũngã, n tõdg a nin-naanda waoogre, n bãnga yʋ-sõtra võore, tɩ b yɛs yĩngr, mogra yegende. B yɛs n wãagda ruuds
66015003	la b yɩɩn Wẽnd sõgen a Moyiiz yɩɩn noogo la Pe-bila me rẽnna: «Yãmb tʋʋma labsa la b bee neere, Wẽnnaam, bũmb fãa Soaala; y sẽn tũud soy niynsa yaa tɩrse, Adem biis Rĩma! Ãnd n be, Soaala, n ka rigd-a la a tõt yãmb yʋʋra pẽgre?
66015004	Yãmb bal n tar Sõmblem, yãmb bal n pid ne Sõmblem; la bu-zẽmba fãa na n wa wõgemda yãmb taoore, tɩ y yikame n dok y sũur la y sɩbg-ba, tɩ b neẽ.»
66015005	Dẽ poore m le gesame, la ade: Yĩngri wẽnd doogã, sɛka zãnda lakame,
66015006	la be la tẽn-kũum a yopoe Malɛgs a yopoe wã yi yã; b ra yera beren-dɩgr gĩ-bãanes fu-neeba la sãnem sẽbdse n da be b sɛɛgẽ.
66015007	Bõn-vɩɩs a naasa nin-yend kõo malɛgs a yopoe wã sãnem laase. Laasa ra pida ne Vɩɩm sẽn ka be sɛɛba soab sũ-puuri.
66015008	Wẽnd dooga wulumda ne bug-zõose: yaa Wẽnd ziira ne b pãnga kaseto. La woto ned ka le tõog n kẽ rooga pʋga, tɩ Malɛgs a yopoe wã ka reng n sɛɛs b tẽn-kũum a yopoe wã zãng ye.
66016001	M wʋma koɛɛg sẽn tãs wẽnd dooga pʋga n yeel Malɛgs a yopoe wã: «Aya! Saag-y tẽngã n daal Wẽnnaam sũ-puura sẽn pid y laasã.»
66016002	Pipi malɛka tɩ ralga a rẽnna tẽng zug la neb niyns sẽn deeg-b Rũnga makre la b wõgemda nin-naanda taoore bẽe nod-tãoodi toose.
66016003	A yiib soaba tɩ ralga a rẽnna mogra zugu: yɩɩ zɩɩm – wa ned la b kodg yã – la mogra bõn-vɩɩl fãa kiime.
66016004	A tãab soaba ralga a rẽnna kʋɩlsa la ko-bundsa fãa zugu tɩ fãa lebg zɩɩm.
66016005	M wʋma malɛk ning sẽn da gũud kooma sẽn yeele: «Yãmb yãee neere, Zaamẽ la Rũnna soaba, Sõmblem naaba, y sɩd bãnga sɩbgr sẽn toge.
66016006	B daaga nin-sõma la bãngdba zɩɩm, dẽ me la yãmb yũnug-b zɩɩm, la rẽ n segde.»
66016007	Koees n zĩnd maan-kugra tẽngr n deese: «Sɩda Soaala-Wẽnnaam, bũmb fãa Naanda, yãmb sɩbgr tũuda sɩda la zemsgo!»
66016008	Malɛk a naas soaba ralga a rẽnna wĩntoog zugu la wĩntooga bugum paama tõogo n na n dɩ ninsaalba.
66016009	La waoolg sẽn ka bilfu n sɩd yõog ninsaalbã. Ne rẽ fãa b zãgsa b yel-wẽna tuubgu la Wẽnd pẽgre, n na n tʋʋs-ba, b sẽn tõe n yiis tẽn-kũum a woto buud yĩngã.
66016010	A nu soaba ralga a rẽnna Rũnga zaoor zugu la a soolma fãa lebga lik tam t'a neba noor vam ne sũ-toogo.
66016011	La ninsaalba zãgsa b bas b tʋʋm wẽna n le yik ne yĩngr Wẽnda tʋʋre, b namsgã la nod-tãoodra yĩnga.
66016012	A yoob soaba ralga a rẽnna kʋɩl kãseng sẽn boond tɩ Efrat zugu. A kʋɩɩ zãnga n bas sor tɩ Yaang nanams tũud n loaada.
66016013	Dẽ poore, m yãee sẽn yit Wag-bãnda noorẽ, Rũnga noorẽ la zirẽ-be-bãngda noorẽ, sʋtãan dẽgd a tãabo, sẽn wẽnd loms buudu;
66016014	– la sɩd me yaa sʋtãamba sẽn tõe tʋʋm-bãna, n yi n na n saag n tigs dũniya tõr dĩm dãmba. Yaa tigs-ba n wa tõog n zab ne bũmb fãa Soaala, b ra-kãsenga raare.
66016015	(Ad-m sẽn wat wa wagdre: sũ-noog soab la sẽn gũusd m waoongo, n kell n yeelg fuugu, n ka kẽnda kãre tɩ b yãet a yãnd ye.)
66016016	B kɩtame tɩ dĩm dãmba tigim taab Megido tãnga, zĩig ninga sẽn boond tɩ Armagedõ ne Ebre rãmb goama.
66016017	Malɛk a yopoe soaba fẽega a rẽnna yĩngri la koɛɛg n zĩnd wẽnd doogẽ wã n tãse: «Sɛyã!»
66016018	La yɩɩ sa-yãgdo la sa-tãse, la tẽng miuung kãsenga; sɩda ninsaalb sẽn wa tẽng zug tɛka, b zɩ n yãend a taar ye!
66016019	Na-tẽng kãsenga wãa boag a tã; bu-zẽmba tẽns rʋʋga zãnga; la Babilon, na-tẽn-kãsengã, Wẽnd tẽega a yelle n yũnug-a ne b sũ-puura rã-toose.
66016020	Tẽns niyns fãa sẽn puk-b mogra zug menemame, la tãmsa fãa sirgame.
66016021	Sapɩlem bɛd-bɛd sẽn zem yɩga, yii yĩngri n lab ninsaalba; tɩ ninsaalb na n tʋʋs Wẽnnaam, sapɩlma sẽn lebg tẽn-kũuma yĩnga, tɩ sɩda, a waa ne tẽn-kũum kãsenga.
66017001	Malɛgs a yopoe wã sẽn tar sãnem laasa sʋka nin-yend n yeel maam: «Wa tɩ m wilg-f pʋg yoodr kãsenga, pag ning sẽn zĩ kʋɩl kãsenga noore, wa tɩ m wilg foom a bʋʋda sẽn yɩ a soaba.
66017002	Yaa ne yẽnda la dũni dĩm dãmba yo yã, a tɩgsa dũnia neba ne a rãam, a yooba.»
66017003	Malɛka tall-m lame n kẽng weoogẽ – yɩla m sɩɩgã – la be, m yãee pag sẽn zomb Rũn-moomde, t'a yĩnga zãng gʋls zab yʋya, n tar zut a yopoe la yɩɩl piiga.
66017004	Paga da yera murfu la nufa, n yãgd sãnem yãgbo n yãgd lʋlʋʋgo la muizãan neeb yãgbo; a ra zãada a nugẽ sãnem laaga sẽn da pid ne a yooba rẽgdo la a tʋʋm-wẽna waoosa.
66017005	A yʋʋr da gʋlsa a rĩirẽ, yʋ bãnde: «Babilon, na-tẽng kãsenga, dũnia pʋg-yoaad wẽna fãa fãa ma.»
66017006	La mam nifẽ, paga ra tɩgsda a meng ne zɩɩm, ne nin-sõma wã zɩɩm, ne sẽn ki-ba a Zezi yĩnga zɩɩm. M sẽn yãend woto, m yɛɛsa wʋsgo.
66017007	Tɩ Malɛka na n yeel-ma: «Bõe yĩng tɩ fo yɛɛsd woto? Bas tɩ m wilg-f pʋg kãnga sẽn ya a soab taki, la m wilg-f Rũngã a sẽn zombã, Rũnga sẽn tar zut a yopoe la yɩɩl piigã, sẽn ya a soaba.
66017008	Rũn kãng ra beeme la marsã a ka ye; a na n yii bul-zulungẽ wã la na n yɩ-la a bõne; neb niyns faa sẽn ka paam tɩ b gʋls b yʋy al dũni sɩngrẽ, vɩɩm sebra pʋgẽ, bãmb fãa pɛlens na n yɩka Rũngã poorẽ, a sẽn da beẽ, n wa kaẽ, n na n le wa pukã.
66017009	Yaa marsã la yam dãmb la sɩlem dãmb na n paam taaba! Zut a yopoe wã yaa tãn-bi a yopoe tɩ paga zao b zugu.
66017010	Leb n yaa dĩm dãmb a yopoe la a makda; a nu zoe n loogame, t'a yembr be marsã, t'a to nan watẽ. A sã n wa, a na n kaoosa bilfu bala.
66017011	Sã n kella Rũnga sẽn da be la a ka marsã, yẽ n tõkd a nii, n yaool n ya a yopoe wã nin-yende; baad-y a rigda a yõor yãkre.
66017012	Yɩɩl piiga yaa dĩm dãmb piiga; b nan ka paam naam ye la b na n wa naaga Rũngã n dɩ naam wakat a ye bala.
66017013	B fãa gesame tɩ segdame tɩ b lebs Rũngã b naama la b tõogo.
66017014	B na n taka zabre ne Pe-bila la Pe-bila n na n tõoge t'a yaa soaalba Soaala la dĩm dãmba Dĩma, ye ne a poorẽ dãmba, Wẽnd sẽn bool b rãmba, Wẽnd sẽn tũus b rãmba, Wẽnd tẽedba.»
66017015	Malɛka le paasame: «Kʋɩl kãseng ning Pʋg-yoodrã sẽn zĩ a soab noorã makda Adem biisa ne b zãma, tɩ b tẽns ya toor-toore, tɩ b goam ya toor-toor e.
66017016	Yɩɩl piigã ne Rũngã menga na n dɩɩ beem ne Pʋg-yoodrã, b na n yeesa a futu, n fʋk-a a zãnde, n dɩ a nemdã la b yõog-a bugum.
66017017	Soaala meng n ning dĩm dãmba yamẽ tɩ b pids bãmb a Wẽnd daabo la b sed ne taaba n lebs b naama fãa Rũnga nugẽ n tãag Wẽnd gomda pidsg raare.
66017018	Paga la tẽn-kãsengã sẽn dɩt naam dũni dĩm dãmba zutã.»
66018001	Dẽ poore m yãee Malɛk a to sẽn yi yĩngr n sigd ne pãn-kãsenga; a vẽenema bui tẽnga tõre.
66018002	A kelma ne a pãng fãa: «A wãame! Babilon na-tẽn-kãsenga wãame! A lebga sʋtãamb doogo, yam yood dãmb soondg zĩiga, lʋɩɩn-dẽgd la lʋɩɩn-yood buud fãa tʋɩ-la b tʋgd a pʋgẽ.
66018003	Ninsaalb buud fãa waame t'a tɩgs-b ne a rãama, a yoobã. Dũniya rãmb gãanda ne-a; dũniya tẽnse ne b dĩm dãmb yoo ne-a, la yaa a arzɛka sẽn labsã la a fẽeg dũniya toandba fãa.»
66018004	M wʋma koɛɛg a to sẽn zĩnd yĩngri n yeele: «Yii-y tẽn-kãnga pʋgẽ, m neba, n da wa reeg a yel-wẽna taale t'a sɩbgra me lʋɩ y zug ye.
66018005	A tʋʋm beeda samame n tãag saaga; Wẽnnaam le tẽega a yel-wẽna.
66018006	Bɩ y sɩbg-a waa a sẽn sɩbg a taaba, bɩ y lebs-a a tʋʋm wẽna naoor a yiibu. Kalem-y naoor a yiibu rẽgd ning a sẽn da pidsd a wamdã n lebs-a!
66018007	Kɩt-y t'a sɩbgra zeng a nagrã la a tɩtaama. Ka yẽ n gomd ne a meng woto: ‹Ad-ma! M ka rĩm-poak bɩ? M yaa pʋg-kõor laa? M kõn yãb kʋʋr abada.›
66018008	Yaa rẽ yĩng la raar a ye bala yel-beed na n yẽeg-a: kũum, nintãm la kom, tɩ bugum yet tɩ b bas n kõ yẽ. A bãng tɩ Soaala Wẽnd sẽn kao a bʋʋdã sɩd yaa Pãng soaba.»
66018009	B na n wiisame, b na n kũmame, dũniya dĩm dãmb sẽn naag-b yẽ n vɩɩnd faong la yoob vɩɩma, b sã n wa yãend a bugma bug-zõose.
66018010	B na n tara yɩɩg n get a sɩbgra ne rabeem la b maanẽ: «Kato, kato, Babilon, tẽn-kãseng a woto, na-tẽng a woto! Babilon sẽn ka tar mak-n-taaga! Wakat yɛng bala tɩ fo bʋʋd zoe n kao!»
66018011	Tɩ dũniya toandba na n sɩng wiisgu la kũmbu tɩ ned ka le be n daad b koom kogend teed ye.
66018012	Bõe n da ka be b kogendẽ: ad sãnem, wanzurfu, lʋlʋʋgo, muizãan neeba, peen-neeba, peen-gʋnem, murfu la nufa, ra-nɛɛb buud toor-toore. Ad wob-yẽn sẽn maneg n peese, ad raad sẽn tar keglem la neerem, n paas yõg-teed buud fãa, kutu la zũudu, n paas kug sẽn yãgd wa nin-gɛtse.
66018013	Ad zẽed noosd toor toore, ad yũ-noodo la ka-noodo buud toor toore, ad tɩdare. Ad rãam la ka-rɩtem, zom pɛɛlga, zom pugsgu, koodo. Ad niigi, piisi, wiidi ne b bilim-bɩlm. Ad yem-daad la ninsaalb sẽn lebg bõn-koosem.
66018014	Fo sẽn da geend yõod ninga, fãa menemame n bas foom; f faongã, ne f ziira, fãa sɛɛ sõmpi!
66018015	Ad toandba sẽn da maand leebg ne foo n dɩt-b rɩɩbã, fo sɩbgra na n kẽes-b la rabeem tɩ b tar yɩɩg n yãbd nintãm la b wiisdẽ:
66018016	«Kato, kato! Tẽn-kãseng a woto fãa sẽn yer futu sẽn wʋg ne gɩ-bãanese, n yer murfu la nufa, n nags ne sãnem la lʋlʋʋgo la muizãan neeba!
66018017	Ad wakat a ye bal n sek faonga woto fãa sãango!» Koom kogenda gɛtba, neb niyns fãa sẽn togd soɛ koom zugu, sẽn dɩt-b mogra yõodo, fãa da yɛsa yɩɩga
66018018	n get bugma bug-zõosã la b maanẽ: «Bõe n da zem tẽn-kãseng kãngã?»
66018019	B ra yugda b zut tom, la b yãbda la b wiisd n yetẽ: «Kato, kato! Tẽn-kãseng a woto fãa! Yẽ faong n da rɩlgd mogra zug kogenda soaalba, ges-y wakat a ye bal sẽn wa ne a wãabo!»
66018020	Arzãn dãmb fãa, kɩdm-y sũ-noogo, nin-sõma, tʋʋm-tʋmdba, bãngdba, bɩ y la n kaase tɩ Wẽnnaam sẽn paalg-a bʋʋdã yaa yãmb la b kõ bʋʋm.
66018021	Malɛk a ye n yaool n tebg ne a pãn-kẽengo kugri sẽn zem neere, n lob-a mogrẽ n yetẽ: «Yaa woto, vugr bala la b na n lobg Babilon, tẽn-kãsengã, la ned nif kõn le yãend-a.
66018022	Fo nengẽ b kõn le wʋm ruudsã ne yʋʋmbã, wɩ-pɛɛbdba la tõntõoda abada. Tʋʋm-tʋmd ba a ye kõn le tag f pʋgẽ t'a rabda tʋʋmd ye; neer rãamde kõn le wʋm f pʋgẽ ye;
66018023	fitil vẽenem kõn le yãend f pʋgẽ abada; b kõn le wʋm kãad paal sẽn gomd ne pʋg paal abada! Toandba da yaa dũniya dĩm dãmba la fo manesma n kẽes b gill moogo.»
66018024	La yaa fo tẽn-peelmẽ la b raag zɩɩm, bãngdba, nin-sõma la b sẽn kood b rãmb fãa tẽng zuga zɩɩm.
66019001	La rẽ poore m wʋma rãamde wa zãma kãseng rãamde sẽn yi yĩngri la sẽn maamde: «Alleluia! Tõnd Wẽnnaama reeg waoogre, pẽgre la naam!
66019002	B bʋʋd tũuda sɩda la zemsgo; b bʋʋ Pʋg-yoodr kãsenga sẽn da sãamd dũniya ne a yoob tʋʋma la b roka b sũuri t'a raaga b sõgen-kamba zɩɩm.»
66019003	La b fãa le reegame: «Alleluia! N-ye, a bug-zõos ruk yʋʋm kõn zĩnd sɛɛbo!»
66019004	Wakat kãng la Nin-kẽems pisi la a naasã la Bõn-vɩɩs a naasã wõgemd tẽnga n waoog Wẽnnaam sẽn zĩ b zaoorẽ n yeele: «Ami! Alleluia!»
66019005	Koɛɛg n zĩnd zaoorẽ wã n yeele: «Pẽg-y tõnd Wẽnnaam, yãmb fãa sẽn nong-ba la sẽn zoet-b bãmba, talse la na-biisi!»
66019006	La m wʋma zãma kãseng rãamde, rãamd wa kʋɩl-kãseng sẽn fõt bɩ saag sẽn tãsd ne pãnga; b ra maandame: «Alleluia! Soaala bũmb fãa Naanda sɩnga a naam dɩɩbo.
66019007	Bɩ d lang sũ-noogo la d pẽg Wẽnnaam tɩ yaa Pe-bila, Wẽnd Biiga, kãadem la pʋg paala ninga a fan teedo;
66019008	yaa gĩ-bãaneg fu-pɛɛlg fadadad la b kõ-a t'a yeelge; gĩ-bãanega makda nin-sõma yel-sõma.»
66019009	Koɛɛgã n yeel maam: «Gʋls woto: Sũ-noog rãmb la b sẽn bool b rãmba Pe-bila, Wẽnd Biiga, yikãadem. La a le paasame: Wẽnd gom-kãensa yaa sɩda.»
66019010	M wõgemdame n me na n waoog sẽn gomda soabã la a yeela maam: «Ayo, vẽ! Ad mam me yaa Wẽnd yamb wa foo la m wẽnda fo saam-biisa fãa sẽn tar-b a Zezi kaseto. Yaa Wẽnnaam la fo tog n waooge.» Tõog tɩ Krista kaseta pid bala n tog n be bãngd yamẽ.
66019011	M yãeeme tɩ yĩngr pakame la wed-boll n yi, la wed-dʋʋda yʋʋr da pʋda woto: «Ra-Teem-Dĩma» la a «Sɩdyɛsa»; a kaooda bʋʋdo la a maanda zabre ne a sẽn tog n zab ne b rãmba.
66019012	A nina zirda wa bugum. Naam pugli n lagem n fõg a zugã la b gʋlsa a yʋʋre, yẽnda a ye bal sẽn mi.
66019013	Fuug ning a sẽn yerã losa zɩɩm la ad wed-dʋʋda yʋʋre: Wẽnd Gomde.
66019014	Yĩngr tãb-biisa ka tɛk ra pʋgd-a lame, n zao wed kaala la b yer gĩ-bãanes futu sẽn ya wogd la sẽn ya peels fadadad;
66019015	sʋʋg sẽn dɩte la a ra rũm a noorẽ la yẽ la a na n tall n kɛ bu-zẽmbã; yaa ne naam dasaar sẽn ya kutu la a na n legl bu-zẽmbã; leb n yaa yẽ n na n kẽ koglgã n fẽd bugsuntunga biisi la a yoog Wẽnnaam, bũmb fãa Soaala, sũ-puura rãam, b sũ-puur sẽn dɩt wa bugma rãam.
66019016	Yʋʋr n gʋls a fuuga zugu la a gera zugu: dĩm dãmba Dĩma, la soaalba fãa Soaala.
66019017	Dẽ poore m yãee malɛk a yembre sẽn teeg Wĩntoogo n yɛsẽ; a tãsame n yeel luiili wã fãa sẽn yɩgd yĩngrã: «Wa-y, kõ-y taab sɛk Wẽnd kibs kãseng rɩɩba zĩigẽ.
66019018	Yaa dĩm dãmb nemdo la y na n vele, n paas tãnsoaben-dãmb nemdo, gãndaad nemdo, wiidi ne b wed-dʋʋdb nemdo, yem-daad la burkĩn-bi, tals la na-biisi nemdo!»
66019019	La m wẽneg n yãee Rũnga ne dũniya dĩm dãmb la b tãb-biisi sẽn tigimd taaba n na n tak zabre ne Wed-dʋʋdã la a poorẽ dãmba.
66019020	Yaa Rũnga ne a zirẽ-be-bãngda la b yõk yã; zirẽ-be-bãngd kãng n da kẽ Rũnga tãpẽ la a maand bõn-bãna n tudgd neb niyns sẽn deeg-b Rũnga makre la b waoogd a nin-naandã. B losa bãmb b yiib fãa vɩɩse bugmẽ, kidbri bugum sẽn da yɛdg wa kʋɩlga.
66019021	Sẽn ket-ba fãa, yaa Wed-dʋʋda sʋʋg n kood-b: sʋʋg ning sẽn da be malɛka noorẽ wã. Ad-y luiili wã tɩga b nemdo.
66020001	Dẽ poore m yãee, yĩngri, malɛk a yembre sẽn sigd la a zãad Bul-zulunga kʋɩlen-bila ne bãn-soagdg sẽn ya bedre;
66020002	A luba Wag-bãndã, Wag-kʋdrã, Sãamdã, Sʋtãan mengã, la a balg-a la bãng yʋʋm tusr yĩnga.
66020003	A lob-a-la Bul zulungẽ wã n page n tol n sog bãeensã la a ning makre; la woto Rũnga kõn le tõog n bels ninsaalba, yʋʋm tusr sã n ka loog ye; dẽ poore b na yaool n bas-a wakat fĩifu.
66020004	M yãenda neb sẽn wa n zaoond goeels zutu tɩ b kõ-b bʋʋda kaoobo. M yãenda neb sẽn le vʋʋge n na n dɩ naam ne Krista yʋʋm tusri: yaa b sẽn fiuus b rãmb zut a Zezi kaset yĩnga la Wẽnd Gomda yĩnga, yaa sẽn zãgs-b Rũnga waoogre, n zãgs a nin-naanda waoogre, n zãgs tɩ b kõn deeg a makrã b rĩrẽ bɩ b nugẽ.
66020005	Bãmb n yɩ pipi n vʋʋge. Kɩɩms a taaba kõn tõog n vʋʋge, tɩ yʋʋm tusra ka pids ye.
66020006	Sũ-noog la bark soaba la sẽn paam-a pipi vʋʋgrã; kũum a yiib soaba ka le tar bãmb gaab ye; bãmb n na n yɩ Wẽnd la Krista maan-kʋʋdba n dɩ naam ne bãmba, yʋʋm tusri.
66020007	Yʋʋm tusra sã n looge Sʋtãan na n le paama a menga,
66020008	a na n yiime n le sɩng ninsaalb belgre dũniya kɩrms a naasã: Gog la Magog; a na n tigsa a zabr yĩnga tãb-biis ka tɛka, wa bĩisr sẽn be mogr noore.
66020009	B yii b tẽnga tõre n wa gũbg nin-sõma wã sika, bark tẽngã. La bãng-y tɩ bugum yi yĩngri n dɩ-b zãnga.
66020010	B loba Sʋtãana, kʋɩɩbdã, kidbra bugmẽ t'a tɩ naag ne Rũngã ne a zirẽ-be-bãngda n nams be wĩntoog la yʋngo n poog zamaan ne zamaan ka tɛka.
66020011	Dẽ poore mam yãee naam zaoor sẽn ya pɛɛlga la kãsenga; a soaba ra zao a zugu. Yĩngr la tẽnga yõbga a taoore n menem zãnga.
66020012	M yãee kɩɩmsa fãa, bɛd la bõonese, sẽn yɛs zaoora taoore; b talla sɛb n wa lagse, b waa ne vɩɩm sebrã me, la kɩɩmsa bʋʋd kaoome, ned kam fãa ne a sẽn maane, wa sẽn da be sɛba pʋga.
66020013	Mogra me yiisa kɩɩmsa sẽn da gãe a pʋgẽ; kũum la bʋg-tẽnga me yiisa b rẽnna la ned kam fãa bʋʋd kaoome, ned kam fãa ne a yɛla.
66020014	B yaool n tusa kũum la bʋg-tẽng n lub kidbra bugmẽ sẽn tond wa kʋɩlgã. Kʋɩl kãng bugma la kũum a yiib soaba.
66020015	Ned ning fãa yʋʋr sẽn ka gʋls vɩɩma sebrẽ, yẽ soab lobda bug-kãng pʋga.
66021001	Dẽ poore m yãee sa-paalle la tẽn-paalga, tɩ pipi saaga la pipi tẽnga da menemame la mogra ra fẽbgame.
66021002	M yãee bark tẽnga, m yãee Zerizalɛɛm paalga sẽn yit arzãna, Wẽnnaam nengẽ, n sigda; a ra manega a meng neere wa pʋg-paal sẽn manegd a menga a sɩd yĩnga.
66021003	M wʋma koɛɛg sẽn yi zaoorẽ wã n moone: «Ad Wẽnd zak sẽn ti ninsaalb sʋka; Wẽnd waa n mee bãmb sʋka, tɩ b na n lebg Wẽnd kamba tɩ Wẽnd-be-ne-ba na n legb bãmb Wẽnde.
66021004	B na n yẽesa nintãm buud fãa la b kõn le wʋm kũum yelle ye; yãbre bɩ kɛlenga, bɩ sũ-sãang me kõn le zĩnd ye tɩ dũni kʋdga menema zãnga.»
66021005	La sẽn da zĩ-a zaoorẽ wã gomame: «Ade, m le sigla dũni paalle!» A le yeelame: «Gʋls tɩ Gom-kãnga yaa sɩda la sɩd menga!»
66021006	A le paasame: «N-ye! Maam la A la O, Sɩngre, la Baasgo, Tʋɩɩsgo la Kʋʋbo; ko-yũud sẽn tara soab bɩ a wa tɩ m na kõ-a vɩɩm kooma t'a yũ zaalem.
66021007	Sẽn maan-a raood fãa pʋɩɩr na n yɩɩ woto; M na yɩla a Wẽnnaam tɩ yẽ yɩ m biiga!
66021008	Sã n kella rabɛɛmbã, zãmb dãmb la nin-yoodã, nin-kʋʋdba la yoaadba, bagba la sẽn waoogd-b naande, zirẽ-be-rãmba, bãmb dãmb pʋɩɩr bee bugma kʋɩlgẽ, kʋɩlg ning sẽn kɛɛd ne kidbr bugum, la rẽ la kũum a yiib soaba.»
66021009	Malɛgs a yopoe wã sẽn da zãad-b tẽn-kũum a yopoe wã nin-yend wẽneg n yeela maam: «Wa tɩ m wilg-f Pe-bila, Wẽnd Biiga, sẽn kẽed kãadem ne a soaba, m wilg fu b pʋg-paala.»
66021010	A kɩtame tɩ mam dʋ ne m yam tãn lug-lug a yembr zugu t'a wilg-m bark tẽnga, Zerizalɛɛm sẽn yit yĩngri, Wẽnnaam nengẽ, n sigda.
66021011	A waa ne Wẽnnaam meng pẽgre, al t'a yãgbã da yɩɩd kug-neeba buud fãa yãgbo.
66021012	A da gũbga ne lal-gũbri sẽn zãnde, n tar rɩgnoy piig la a yiib sẽn gũnug malɛgs piig la a yiibu, la sẽn da gʋls yʋya, a Israyɛl dot piig la a yiiba yʋya.
66021013	Yaang yaa noy a tãabo; goabg noy a tãabo; rɩtg noy a tãabo; nin-taoor yaa noy a tãabo.
66021014	Lal-gũbra meeb sɩnga ne kug ma rãmb piig la a yiibu, sẽn gʋls Pe-bila Tʋʋm-tʋmdba piig la a yiiba yʋya.
66021015	Sẽn da gomda ne maama ra zãada sãnem rasaar magdga n na n mag tẽngã ne a noya la a lalgã.
66021016	Tẽnga sõoga tɩrga, a ka maka, a ka goalenga, t'a woglma ne a yalma zem taaba.
66021017	A maga tẽnga lal-gũbrã ne dasaarã la yɩɩ magb tɛka; malɛka sẽn zãad magdg ninga ne ninsaal dẽnd da ya a ye.
66021018	– Lal-gũbra meng ra mee ne kug sẽn yãgd b toore, n ya kõaada, la tẽnga tõr mee ne sãnem yulli sẽn pɩnd wa nin-gɛtga.
66021019	Lal-gũbra mee rũnug rũnuga la rũnug fãa kug yaa toore. Pipi rũnuga kug yaa kõada, a yiib soaba togsda salsang kõbgo; a tãab soaba yaa miuug sẽn lʋʋs kẽega; a naas soaba: kẽeg toenɛɛga.
66021020	A nu soba: sɩɩga; a yoob soaba: miuug yʋdʋd; a yopoe soaba: rõodo; a nii soaba: kẽeg sẽn lʋʋs sabla; a wɛ soaba: kõodr sẽn liʋʋs moomde; piig soaba: kẽeg pespele; piig la a ye soaba: miuug sẽn lʋʋs sabla; piig la a yiib soaba: mismiuugu.
66021021	Rignoy piig la a yiibã da pagda ne kug sẽn saase n pɩnd wa muizãanfo, noor fãa ne a rẽnda. Tẽnga sõasg zĩig da yaa sãnem yull bala, neer wa nin-gɛtga.
66021022	M ka yãend Wẽnd doog be ye; Soaala-Wẽnnaam pãng soaba meng n da yaa b roogo, bãmb ne Pe-bilã.
66021023	Tẽnga ra pa tar wĩntoog ne kiuug vẽenem tʋʋmd ye tɩ Wẽnnaam pẽgra vẽenem n da buiid-a, la Wẽnd Pe-bila n da ya a bugum.
66021024	A vẽenema n na n wilg bu-zẽmba sore la dũniya dĩm dãmb na n waa ne b arzɛka.
66021025	Noya na n paka wakat fãa tɩ beelẽ yʋng ka ye.
66021026	Be la ninsaalb fãa na n wa ne b laogo la b naam teedo.
66021027	Bõn-dẽgd kõn tõog n kẽ be abada; d kõn gom sẽn tʋmd-b tʋʋm wẽna la tʋʋm beeda ye; neb nins yʋy sẽn gʋls Pe-bila vɩɩm sebra pʋgẽ bala n na n kẽ be.
66022001	Dẽ poore malɛka wilga maam vɩɩm kʋɩlga; a yaa pɛɛlg wa nin-gɛtga la a ra bunda Wẽnd la Pe-bila zaoora tẽngre.
66022002	Yaa tɩɩs sẽn kõt vɩɩm la b ra sel tẽnga tẽnsʋka, kʋɩlga foole; tɩɩsa ra womda naoor piig la a yiibu; kiuug fãa pʋgẽ b ra womdame; b vãada ra tõe n sãooga bu-zẽmbã.
66022003	Kãab-wẽng kõn le kãab be ye; Wẽnd ne Pe-bila zaoor na n lugla tẽnga sʋka tɩ b kamba wat be n waoogd-b.
66022004	Kamba nif na n teega Wẽnde; Wẽnd yʋʋr na n gʋlsa b rĩirẽ.
66022005	Lik kõn le zĩndi; b ka le tar wĩntoog bɩ fitl vẽenem tʋʋmd ye; Soaala Wẽnd vẽenema n na n bui-ba la b na n dɩɩ naam sẽn kõn sɛ.
66022006	Malɛka yeela maam: «Gomd bãmba yaa sɩd menga; yaa Soaala-Wẽnd menga, yaa bãngdba sẽn deegd-b bãngrã a soab nengẽ wã, bãmb n tʋm tɩ b wa wilg b yemsã bũmb ning sẽn yao waoongo.
66022007	Ade, m waoong yaoome; sũ-noog soab la sẽn deeg-a bãngra goama sẽn gʋls seb kãnga pʋga.»
66022008	Maam a Zã n da ne la m da wʋmd woto fãa; la m sẽn deeg dẽ fãa n sɛ, m wõgemda malɛka sẽn wilga maam woto fãa wã taoore tɩ m na n waoog-a,
66022009	la a yeel-m lame: «Ayoo! Gũus tɩ mam me yaa Wẽnd yamba wa foo la bãngdbã, f ma-bi-taasã; m yaa wa neb niyns sẽn deeg-b sebr kãnga goama. Yaa Wẽnnaam bal n tog ne waoogre.»
66022010	La a le paasame: «Da solg bãngra goam sẽn be sebr kãnga pʋgẽ wã ye, sɩd ne sɩda, wakat yaoome!
66022011	Yel-wẽn maand nong bɩ a tʋm wẽnga la nin-dẽgd nong bɩ a pa ne a rẽgdo; nin-tɩrg yee n wɩng ne a pʋ-peelem tɩ nin-sõng me mao ne a sõmblem.
66022012	Ade, m lebgr wakat yaoome, la m wata ne ned kam fãa yaoodo la yaooda zemsda ned kam fãa ne a tʋʋmde.
66022013	Maam la A la O, maam la Pipi soaba la Yaoolem soaba, Tʋɩɩsgo la Kʋʋbo.
66022014	Sũ-noog rãmb la sẽn pegs-b futu; bãmb n na n soog vɩɩm tɩɩgã, bãmb n tũud dignoya n kẽed bark tẽnga.
66022015	Yãmb fãa gilli, ba-raado, tɩt rãmba, yoaadba, nin-kʋʋdba, sẽn waoogd-b naande, neb niyns sẽn dat-b wẽnga, pa-y yɩnga!
66022016	Maam a Zezi n tʋm m malɛk t'a wa togs bũmb ning sẽn wat beoog Tigenga yĩnga; m ya a Daviid yagenga, yibeoog ãdg pɛɛlga.»
66022017	Wẽnd Vʋʋsem la pʋg-paala yeta me: «Wa!» Sẽn tar-a tʋb n kelgdẽ me yetame: «Wa!» Bɩ ko-yũud sẽn tar a soab fãa kolge; sẽn dat-a n deeg vɩɩm kooma n yũ, a wa reeg-a zaalem, n ka yiis lagf ye.
66022018	Maam n yete: ned ning sẽn kelga bãngr goama sẽn be seb kãnga pʋga la a saagame n paas bũmb be, bɩ Wẽnd tʋka zugu, yel-beeda fãa sẽn gʋls a pʋgẽ.
66022019	Sẽn saag-a me n yiis bũmb be, bɩ Wẽnd me yiis bũmb a pʋɩɩrẽ, vɩɩm tɩɩga la bark tẽnga sẽn kõt bũmb ning tɩ b gomd sebr kanga pʋga.
66022020	Sẽn kɩt-a tɩ goam kãensa fãa tar kaset sɩdã n yeele: «Sɩda, m waoong yaoome!» N-ye! Soaal a Zezi, wa-y wɛ!
66022021	Soaal a Zezi barka sig y fãa gilli. Ami!
